# ENGLISH-CHINESE VOCABULARY OF THE VERNACULAR OR SPOKEN LANGUAGE OF SWATOW

ENGLISH-CHINESE  
VOCABULARY  
OF THE  
VERNACULAR  
OR  
SPOKEN LANGUAGE  
OF  
SWATOW


SWATOW:  
ENGLISH PRESBYTERIAN MISSION PRESS.  
1883.

------

[Rudolf Lechler](https://en.wikisource.org/wiki/Author:Rudolf_Lechler)*,* [Samuel Wells Williams](https://en.wikisource.org/wiki/Author:Samuel_Wells_Williams)*,* [William Duffus](https://en.wikisource.org/wiki/Author:William_Duffus)

## PREFACE.

This vocabulary is based on a manuscript work prepared about thirty years ago by the Rev. R. Lechler of the Basel Mission, Hongkong, who was the first Protestant Missionary resident in this part of China. Mr Lechler's vocabulary was founded again on one by Dr. S. Wells Williams.

A purpose having been formed to copy Mr Lechler's MS. for personal use, with no further thought regarding it, the suggestion was made to have it printed in the Mission press, and so made available for general use. Hence its appearance in this form.

No time has been taken, because none could be spared, to do much more than rapidly write a copy for the press, making such additions and alterations as were attainable in the circumstances.

From many varieties of dialect found in the Swatow region that has been chosen which is spoken in the city of Ch'ao-chow-foo; and no words or phrases not current there have been knowingly admitted. By this rule many expressions are excluded which must be amongst the most familiar to persons acquainted with the general speech of the Swatow people.

The vocabulary makes no pretension to completeness in any sense. Very many words and idiomatic phrases are omitted; comparatively few of the terms given have been strictly defined and discriminated; for which reason the contents must be used with cautious regard to distinctions of meaning and usage. Years of labour and a very complete knowledge of the unwritten speech of the country would be necessary to make a work of this kind what it ought to be; and the difficulty is immensely increased by the absolute non-existence of native books in the vernacular. The exception of two or three broadsheets of proverbs and ballads is not worth mentioning. But if it be clearly understood that the present vocabulary is merely a collection of useful words, tolerably correct (it may be hoped) so far as it goes, but not by any means a work judged ready for publication, it may escape undue severity of criticism and prove of some service to those who make use of it.

When it is stated that the type-setting and printing have been done by two young men who do not know a word of English, and have not even been trained in the art of printing; and further, that the work has sometimes been hampered by scarcity of type, a kind indulgence will be extended to any typographical shortcomings.

Whatever errors may be found to exist in the vocabulary, it is quite certain that their number would have been much greatter but for the kind assistance of Miss C. M. Ricketts and the Rev. H. L. Mackenzie in correcting the proof sheets; and the Medical terms owe very much to their revision by Dr Alexander Lyall.

While any benefit to be derived from the vocabulary must be credited to its original author, Mr Lechler, enough has been changed and added to remove from him all responsibility for its mistakes and faults.

It may be confessed that one motive for printing this vocabulary was the hope of raising some funds for the support of the Mission Press, most of its work being unremunerative.

*English Presbyterian Mission,*⁠William Duffus.


## REMARKS.

There are many matters which it would be interesting and useful, and even indispensable, to set forth in the introduction to a complete Dictionary of this language, but from causes already referred to, most of them cannot even be touched upon here. A few notes, however, are imperatively necessary.

|   |                                                                          |    |    |   |                              |
|---|--------------------------------------------------------------------------|----|----|---|------------------------------|
|a ⁠|                                pronounced                                |like|*a* |in |            *far*             |
| e |                                    „                                     | „  |*e* | „ |            *bed*             |
| i |                                    „                                     | „  |*ee*| „ |           *seen*.            |
| o |                                    „                                     | „  |*aw*| „ |*saw*, but a little more open.|
| u |                                    „                                     | „  |*u* | „ |        *put*, *rude*.        |
| ṳ |nearly as *u* in lowland Scotch *abune*;  <br/>⁠or *eu* in French *heure*.|    |    |   |                              |

ai, au, oa, oai, oi, ou, ua, ui. In all these each vowel is pronounced with its own proper sound.

The consonants are nearly all as in English.

ch0ch is pronounced as in *church*.

ch0g is always hard as in *go*; never as in *gin*.

ch0h is always sounded except when final.

ch0j is pronounced as in *jet*.

ch0ng, as in *sing*, *ring*.

ch0s, always as in *so*, *sing*; never as in *lose*.

ch0z, always as *ds* or *da*; never as in *zeal*, *zone*.

k and t as finals are so much alike as to be scarcely distinguishable.

m and ng will be found written without any vowel (e.g. n̂g, m̃); often also preceded by a consonant (e.g. hm̄, sńg, kng, hñg). "The nature of these syllables without a distinct vowel becomes at once unmistakable in singing, as at such a word all vocal sound at once ceases, and nothing is heard but a dull nasal murmur.

"The aspirated consonants are a very remarkable feature in all the languages of China, and require very special attention. They are kh, th, ph and chh. The sounds are the same as those indicated by the same notation in the languages of India, being formed by a real distinct aspiration pronounced after the respective consonants......The sounds are almost the same as those often used by Irishmen when pronouncing with a strong brogue such words as *come*, *pig*, *&c*; they are also often heard in the mouths of the Scottish Highlanders.

"kh may be thus described:— Pronounce....*look here!* rapidly and clearly, cut off *loo*- and -*re*, and you have the Chinese 'khi'."<sup><a href="https://en.wikisource.org/wiki/English-Chinese_Vocabulary_of_the_Vernacular_Or_Spoken_Language_of_Swatow#cite_note-1">[1]</a></sup> The other aspirated consonants might be illustrated in a similar manner.

[ch is *not* an aspirated consonant — see above.]

Any attempt to write the colloquial language of Swatow without indicating the tones carries its condemnation on the face of it. It is utterly impossible to speak intelligibly while disregarding this essential feature.

There are *four* great classes of tones—1st, Phêⁿ *(*or, Pêⁿ*)*; 2d, Siãng; 3d, Khṳ̀; 4th, Ji̍p. In the Swatow Colloquial *eight* separate tones are distinguished from one another:—

|      |            |      |                  |
| ---- | ---------- | ---- | ---------------- |
| 1.   | chiēⁿ-phêⁿ | *as* | saⁿ, *a coat*.   |
| 2.   | ẽ-phêⁿ     | „    | nâng, *a man*.   |
| 3.   | siãng-siaⁿ | „    | hái, *the sea*.  |
| 4.   | chiēⁿ-khṳ̀  | „    | sì, *the world*. |
| 5.   | ẽ-khṳ̀      | „    | lĩ, *profit*.    |
| 6.   | khṳ̀-siaⁿ   | „    | bō, *a cap*.     |
| 7.   | chiēⁿ-ji̍p  | „    | pat, *to know*.  |
| 8.   | ẽ-ji̍p      | „    | pa̍t, *another*.  |

In combinations of two or more syllables, very important modifications occur in the tones. A learner is apt to think tliat, the tone of a word having been once fixed, he will find it the same in all circumstances, and to be surprised when he hears familiar words pronounced in quite another tone. It would be difficult, and is quite unnecessary, to describe here the characters of the various tones and the changes which they undergo in combination, as they can be most easily and correctly learnt by listening to the speech of a native.

A small ⁿ written above the line at the end of a syllable indicates that the whole syllable becomes nasal. In words beginning with m, n, and ng this symbol has been in some cases omitted where it ought to have been written.

The general idea involved in the use of hyphens is to link together those syllables which are so closely connected that the tones of certain of them are affected by the connexion. This principle, however, is not carried out to the full extent, because in many cases the words thus influencing one another would be too numerous to link together in this manner.

A double hyphen implies that the word preceding it retains its own proper tone in full force, and that the word or words following it are either enclitic or unaccented, and as far as possible deprived of distinctive tonal character.

The use of hyphens, though most essential, is yet difficult to regulate by any stringent law, and much must be left to discretion.

## ERRATA

On the next page are a few errors, chiefly misprints, which have been observed. It would be too much to hope that many more will not appear afterwards.

## VOCABULARY OF THE SWATOW COLLOQUIAL LANGUAGE.

### A

**a**, che̍k-kâi(一個); che̍k-chiah(一隻); &c.

**aback**, pùe-ãu(背後). *taken aback at meeting one*, ngõ--tie̍h uak--chē-kiè(遇着斡些叫).

**abacus**, sǹg-pûaⁿ(算盤). *to work the*, kiah-sǹg-pûaⁿ(揭算盤); khà-sǹg-pûaⁿ(扣算盤).

**abaft**, *the foremast*, thâu-ûi-ãu(頭圍後).

**abandon**, pàng-tiāu(放掉); ka̍k-tiāu(捔掉); sek-tiāu(擲掉); lī-khui(離開); màiⁿ(勿).

**abase**, kàng-khip(降級).

**abash**, sit-nâng kâi-thí-mīn(失人个體面). *abashed*, tshâm-khũi(慚愧); kièn-siàu(見笑); siáu-lí(少禮); siu-chhí(羞恥).

**abate**, kiám(減); chié(少). *the price*, sǹg-kiám(算減); tṳ̂-kiám(除減); khà-kiám(扣減); khà-tṳ̂(扣除); kiám--chē(減些); chié--chē(少些).

**abbess**, *(Buddhist)*, sṳ-hũ(師父); hûe-siēⁿ-phûa(和尚婆); nîⁿ-kou-phûa(尼姑婆).

**abbot**, *(Buddhist)*, sṳ-hũ(師父); hûe-siēⁿ-thâu(和尚頭); tang-ke(東家).

**abbreviation**, sié-siá(小寫). *a compendium*, tãi-lia̍k(大略).

**abdicate**, siā-cheh(謝職); sî-kuaⁿ(辭官). *of a sovereign*, siā-ūi(謝位); thò-ūi(退位).

**abdomen**, tóu(肚); tóu-pak(肚腹).

**abduct**, kuái-tô(拐逃); thau-kiau(偷驕); thau-kāng-tsáu(偷共走).

**abet**, pang-tsõ(幫助); pang-ak(幫惡).

**abhor**, lóu(惱); ù(惡); lóu-hṳ̃n(惱恨).

**abide**, kṳ-tsũ(居住); khiã-khí(徛起); tiū(住).

**abject**, hiã-tsūaⁿ(下賤); hiã-liû(下流).

**ability**, lêng-kàng(能幹); pún-sṳ̄(本事); pún-niáⁿ(本領); tshâi-chhêng(才情); tshâi-lêng(才能). *have not the ability to do*, bô-lêng-ûi(無能爲).

**abjure**, chiù-tsūa bô-chí-kâi-sṳ̄(咒誓無此個事). *one’s religion*, húan-kà(反教); pũe-kà(背教).

**able**, lêng(能); õi(會); miâⁿ-ke(名家); ũ-lêng-ûi(有能爲). see **ability**.

**ablution**, sói-chheng-khih(洗清潔); sói-chheng(洗清); sói-sin(洗身); sói-e̍k(洗浴).

**aboard**, tõ-tsûn(在船); tsûn-téng(船頂); lo̍h-tsûn(落船).

**abolish**, tṳ̂-tiāu(除掉); hùi-tiāu(廢掉).

**abominable**, khó-ù(可惡); tshūa-nâng-lóu(𤆬人惱).

**abominate**, ù(惡); lóu(惱); kĩ(忌).

**aborigines**, thóu-jîn(土人); pńg-tī-nâng(本地人[訓]).

**abortion**, lo̍h-sié-súaⁿ(落小產); lo̍h-sin(落身); phah-tó a-nôuⁿ(拍倒阿孥). *to produce by medicine*, ēng-ie̍h lo̍h-tiāu a-nôuⁿ(用藥落掉阿孥).

**abound**, hoh-tsōi(酷㩼); tōa-bó-mue̍h(大母物); tsōi-tsōi(㩼㩼); sẽng(盛); mõng-sẽng(茂盛); hong-sẽng(豐盛); tshù-tshù to-tsōi(處處多㩼).

**about**, tsha-m̄-to(差毋多); kâi-pan-bó(个班母); lím-lím(凜凜); ũ chí-kâi-pān(有此個辦); tsáu-tsua̍h bô-ki(走絀無幾); chìn-thò ũ-hãn(進退有限).

**above**, tõ-téng(在頂); tõ-chiēⁿ(在上); tõ-mīn-chiēⁿ(在面上).

**abrade**, siah--tie̍h(削着); phoi--tie̍h(批着); phiù-phûe(漂皮).

**abridge**, séⁿ-iak(省約); tiah-iàu(摘要); tiah-chhiet-iàu(摘切要); káng-séⁿ(簡省); tiah-tshut káng-iàu(摘出簡要).

**abroad**, tõ-gūa(在外); tshut-tshù(出厝); tshut-gūa(出外). *to go*, kùe-huan(過番); kùe-kok(過國).

**abruptly**, hut--chē-kiè(忽些叫); tu̍t-jiên(突然); hut-jiên(忽然).

**abscess**, seⁿ-thûe(生㿗); seⁿ-mue̍h(生物); seⁿ-eng(生癭); pũ-lâng-tshng(胕膿瘡).

**abscond**, tô-tsáu(逃走); tsáu-khṳ̀-tiàm(走去坫); tô-pī(逃避); thau-tsáu(逃走).

**absence**, m̄-tõ(毋在); *of mind*, sim m̄-tõ(心毋在); sim-hûn m̄-tõ(心魂毋在).

**absolute**, tsṳ̃-tsú(自主).

**absolve**, kói-tsũe(改罪); sià-tsũe(赦罪); sek-pàng(釋放).

**absorb**, sò-ta(疏大). *water*, sò-tsúi(疏水). *all one’s energies*, ēng-chĩn-la̍t(用盡力). *entirely absorbed in any thing*, ji̍p-sîn(入神).

**abstain**, kài(戒). *from liquor*, kài-chiú(戒酒). *from lust*, kài-io̍k(戒慾).

**abstemious**, tsat-ēng(節用); kúaⁿ-io̍k(寡慾); ũ-tsat-tōu(有節度).

**abstraction**, *in a state of (Buddhist)*, tsõ-siên(坐禪); ji̍p-tẽng(入定).

**abstruse**, chhim-àu(深奧); àu-biāu(奧妙).

**absurd**, thèng-tàⁿ(聽呾); bô-iáⁿ-chiah(無影跡); hó-chhiè(好笑).

**abundant**, see **abound**.

**abuse**, mēⁿ(罵). *filthy abuse*, mēⁿ kàu chhi-gî(罵到淒疑); tshou-tshùi-mēⁿ(粗喙罵).

**abutment**, *of bridge*, kiê-tún(橋墩).

**abyss**, chhim-thâm(深潭); chhim-chhim(深深); bô-tói(無底); bô-tói chhim-kheⁿ(無底深坑).

**academy**, tsṳ-īⁿ(書院); *imperial (at Pekin)*, hâng-lîm(翰林).

**accelerate**, tshui-pek(催迫); tshui-méⁿ(催猛).

**accede**, zún-na̍p(允納); hàuⁿ(好); khéng(肯); tsún(准); na̍p-ì(納意).

**accent**, siaⁿ-im(聲音); siaⁿ-kháu(聲口).

**accept**, siũ(受); siu(收); chiap-na̍p(接納); na̍p-siũ(納受).

**access**, lōu-mn̂g(路門); lōu-mn̂g hó-chiũ(路門好就). *increase*, thiⁿ-ke(添加); thiam-ke(添加).

**accession**, *to the throne*, seng-ūi(升位).

**accessory**, pang-tsõ(幫助).

**accident**, ì-gūa kâi-sṳ̄(意外个事); liāu-m̄-kàu kâi kéng-ngõ(料毋到个境遇). *accidental*, ngóu-jiên(偶然); tsõu-jiên(偶然).

**acclivity**, suaⁿ kiã-kiã(山崎崎); pho-lo-sia(陂咯斜).

**accommodate**, *others*, pang-tsõ(幫助); chieh-ēng(借用). *oneself to others*, tshông-khûan(從權); sûi-nâng-ì(隨人意). *able to accommodate oneself to circumstances*, ũ-pièn-thong(有變通); ũ-khuân-pièn(有權變).

**accompany**, tâng-kiâⁿ(同行); tsò-pû-kiâⁿ(做包行); pûe-sàng(陪送); sie-phũaⁿ(相伴).

**accomplice**, tâng-táng(同黨); tâng-pang(同幫).

**accomplish**, tsùn-kang(竣工); sêng-kong(成功); uân-kang(完工); tsò-chiâⁿ(做成). *one’s desire*, tit-ì(得意). *to fulfil*, sîn-ngiām(先驗); èng-ngiām(應驗).

**accord**, hûa(和); hûa-ha̍h(和合); siang-ha̍h(相合); hûa-míⁿ(和美); siang-hûa(相和); hûa-mo̍k(和睦).

**accordance**, sie-tùi(相對); sie-tâng(相同); siang-ha̍h(相合).

**according**, chiè(照); chiè-iēⁿ(照樣). *to one’s wishes*, zû-ì(如意). *to order*, zû-mẽng(如命).

**account**, siàu-ba̍k(數目). *book*, siàu-phõu(數簿). *to enter*, chiẽⁿ-siàu(上數); lo̍h-siàu(落數); kì-siàu(記數). *settle*, hôiⁿ-siàu(還數); siàu-ba̍k chheng-tshó(數目清楚). *owe*, khiàm-siàu(欠數). *square*, ap-siàu(押數). *collect*, thó-siàu(討數). *manage*, hūaⁿ-siàu(捍數). *make up*, sǹg-siàu(算數). *on account of*, in-ũi(因爲). *on no account*, būan-būan put-khó(萬萬不可); tùan-tùan m̄-hó(斷斷毋好). *cannot account for*, put-kói(不解); siẽⁿ-m̄-phùa(想毋破); siẽⁿ-m̄-tshut(想毋出). *give an account of any event*, o̍h pun-nâng-thiaⁿ(學分人聽); kāng-nâng-tàⁿ(共人呾).

**accumulate**, tun-chek(屯積); chek-thiok(積蓄). *wealth*, tun-kim chek-ge̍k(屯金積玉). *merit*, chek-tek(積德); chek-kong(積功).

**accurate**, bô-tsáu-tsua̍h(無走絀); siâng-sòi(詳細); sòi-siâng(細詳); chin-chiàⁿ(真正).

**accusation**, phah-kuaⁿ-si(拍官司); kò-tsn̄g(告狀); ji̍p-tiâⁿ(入呈); sie-kò(相告).

**accuse**, kò(告). *accuser*, ngûan-kò(原告). *accused*, pĩ-kò(被告).

**accustom**, kùan(慣); kùan-tsò(慣習); kùiⁿ-sìⁿ(慣勢); se̍k(熟); se̍k-chhiú(熟手).

**ache**, thiàⁿ(痛); sng-thiàⁿ(痠痛).

**achieve**, sêng-kong(成功); sêng-chiũ(成就); tsò-chiâⁿ(做成).

**acid**, sng(酸); sng-bī(酸味).

**acknowledge**, jīn(認); sêng-jīn(承認).

**agreeable**, ha̍h-ì(合意); zû-nguãn(如願); sûi-nguãn(隨願); thiàng-huâi(暢懷); thiàng-ì(暢意); tshù-bī(趣味); sũi-sim(遂心). *as companion*, ha̍h-su-kah(合舒合). *in conversation*, ha̍h-phue̍h(合詖).

**aloud**, tōa-siaⁿ(大聲); khui-siaⁿ(開聲). *to cry*, tshut-siaⁿ(出聲).

**alphabet**, jī-bó(字母).

**also**, iā(亦); kiam(兼); íⁿ-ki̍p(以及); iā-sĩ(亦是); kiam-kũa(兼跨); siãng-chhiáⁿ(尙且).

**altar**, tôaⁿ(壇); chì-tôaⁿ(祭壇); hieⁿ-tôaⁿ(香壇); hieⁿ-uàⁿ(香案).

**alter**, kói(改); kói-pièn(改變); kói-uāⁿ(改換); kói-e̍k(改易); kói-chiàⁿ(改正); chhiâⁿ-kói(正改).

**altercation**, cheⁿ-lũn(爭論); sie-à(相詏); sie-jiáng(相嚷); sie-cheⁿ(相爭); khau-peh(摳掰).

**alternate**, sie-lûn(相輪); sie-lûn-liû(相輪流); lûn-liû(相輪); sie-thòi(相代).

**alternative**, nõ-kiãⁿ suán-che̍k(兩件選一). *no*, bô-nãi-hô(無奈何); bô-khóu nãi-hô(無苦奈何); bô-ta-uâ(無奈何); put-tit-íⁿ(不得已).

**although**, sui(雖); sui-jiên(雖然); sui-chiet(雖然); sui-sĩ(雖然). *although ...... still*, sui-jiên ...... huân-liáu(雖然......還了).

**altogether**, hâm-kâi(咸個); hãm-kâi(含個); che̍k-khài(一概); che̍k-tsôi(一齊); che̍k-chhiet(一切); hãm-pa-lan(含巴攏); lóng-tsóng(攏總); tsn̂g-kâi(整個); tshuân(全).

**alum**, pe̍h-huân(白矾).

**always**, siêⁿ-sî(常時); sî-sî(時時); pâi-sî(排時); múeⁿ-múeⁿ(每每); kú-kú(久久); ē-ē(下下); lú-lú(屢屢).

**am**, *I*, úa sĩ(我是). *I am the man*, úa chiũ-sĩ(我就是). *I am sick*, úa ũ-pēⁿ(我有病). *I am cold*, úa õi-chhìn(我會凊).

**amanuensis**, thòi-siá(代寫); thòi-pit(代筆); thòi-tsṳ(代書).

**amass**, tun(堆); chek(積); tun-chek(堆積); chek-lúi(積累); chek-tsũ(積聚); lúi-chek(累積). *wealth*, huat-tshâi(發財); chek-tshâi(積財).

**amazed**, hãi-ĩ(駭異); khî-ĩ(奇異); tōa-khî-ĩ(大奇異).

**ambassador**, khim-chhe(欽差); sài-chhîn(使臣); tshut-sài(出使); khim-sài(欽使).

**amber**, hóuⁿ-phek(琥珀).

**ambiguous**, kâm-kôu(含糊); sang-kuan liáng-ì(雙關兩意); sang-thám(雙探); lóng-thóng(籠統); m̄-hun-mêng(毋分明).

**ambitious**, tsṳ̃-tsun(自尊); tsṳ̃-tōa(自大); ũ-tãi-chì(有大志); chì tōa(志大); chì-khì kau(志氣高); chì-liãm kûiⁿ(志念危).

**amble**, tsho̍k(戳); tsho̍k-tsho̍k-thiàu(蜀蜀跳).

**ambush**, ho̍k-piaⁿ(伏兵); tshâng-piaⁿ(藏兵); mâiⁿ-ho̍k(埋伏).

**amend**, kói-kùe(改過); kói-chiàⁿ(改正); chhiâⁿ-kói(正改); chhiâⁿ-hó(成好); kói-hó(改好). *one’s ways*, kui-chiàⁿ(規正); kói-ak kiâⁿ-siẽn(改惡行善).

**America**, A-múiⁿ-lĩ-kia(阿美利加); Múiⁿ-kok(美國); Hue-kî-kok(花旗國).

**amiable**, khó-ài(可愛); hó-sieh(好惜); tshūa-nâng-sieh(𤆬人惜); un-hûa(溫和); un-jiû(溫柔).

**amicable**, hûa(和); hûa-mo̍k(和睦); hûa-míⁿ(和美). *very*, hûa-hûa míⁿ-míⁿ(和和美美).

**amid**, tìn-tang(鎮中); tong-kan(中間); tong-iang(中央); lãi--tang(內中); lãi-tói(內底).

**amiss**, tshò(錯); ũ-kùe(有過); kùe-sit(過失); tshò-sit(錯失); tshò-gōu(錯誤); sit-tshò(失錯); m̄-tie̍h(毋着).

**ammunition**, kun-tsuang(軍裝); húe-ie̍h chhèng-chí(火藥銃子); tsu-ie̍h(珠藥); în-ie̍h(鉛藥).

**amnesty**, tãi-sià(大赦); ṳn-chiè(恩照); hí-chiè(喜詔); sià-chiè(赦詔).

**among**, see **amid**.

**amount**, kāng-kòi(共計); tsóng-kat(總結); kāng-tsóng(共總); ha̍h-kāng(合共). *what*, jie̍h-tsōi(若㩼).

**ample**, khuah-tōa(闊大); khuan-khuah(寬闊); khuan-khuàⁿ(寬寬); khùaⁿ-chhēng〔〕. *means*, pù-tsok(富足).

**amputate**, kuah-tiāu(割掉); tsám-tiāu(斬掉); kṳ̀-tiāu(鋸掉); tok-tiāu(斫掉).

**amulet**, hieⁿ-húe-lâng(香火籠); hieⁿ-húe-tō(香火袋). *to wear*, kùa-hieⁿ-húe(掛香火).

**amusement**, sie-sńg(相耍); thit-thô(佚佗); iû-la̍k(遊樂). *amusing*, tshù-bī(趣味). *ramble about for amusement*, iû-nguán(遊玩); nguán-la̍h(玩獵).

**analyse**, tshat-si̍t(察實); kháu-kiù(考究).

**anarchy**, bô-pẽ bô-kun(無父無君); huán-luãn(反亂); luãn-tsa̍p(亂雜).

**ancestors**, soiⁿ-tsóu(先祖); tsóu-kong(祖公); tsóu-tsong(祖終); kong-má(公媽). *ancestral hall*, sṳ̂-tn̂g(祠堂); tsong-sṳ̂(終祠). *tablet*, sîn-tsú(神主); sîn-tsú-pâi(神主牌); ke-sîn(家神); ba̍k-tsú(木主).

**anchor**, tèng(椗). *one*, che̍k-mn̂g-tèng(一門碇). *to cast*, pha-tèng(拋椗). *to weigh*, khí-tèng(起碇); khieh-tèng(牽碇); chhia-tèng(車碇); chhiû-tèng(揪碇). *anchorage*, hiah-tsûn kâi-ūi-tshṳ̀(歇船个位處). *anchorage (a port)*, pou-thâu(埠頭).

**ancient**, kóu(鼓). *times*, kóu-sî(古時); kóu-tsá(古早). *men*, kóu-nâng(古人[訓]). *doctrines*, kóu-kà(古教).

**and**, pẽng(並); íⁿ-ki̍p(以及); kiam(兼); kah(佮); kũa〔〕; kāng(共); iũ(又). *tell him to come and I will pay him*, hàm-i-lâi(喊伊來), uá chiũ àiⁿ-hôiⁿ--i(我就愛還伊). *you must speak the truth and then people will believe you*, lṳ́ tie̍h tàⁿ-si̍t-ūe nâng chiàⁿ-ũ-sìn--lṳ́(汝着呾實話人正有信汝).

**anecdote**, kóu-sṳ̄(古事); kóu-gṳ́(古語). *to relate anecdotes*, káng-kóu(講古); phue̍h-kóu(詖古); thâm-kóu(談古); o̍h-kóu(學古); phue̍h-tshù-bī(詖趣味); phue̍h-chhiè-thâm(詖笑談).

**angel**, thien-sài(天使); sîn-sài(神使).

**anger**, khì(氣); náuⁿ(惱). *angry*, seⁿ-khì(生氣); siũ-khì(受氣); huat-náuⁿ(發惱); náuⁿ-khì(惱氣).

**angle**, *the hook*, tièⁿ-kau(釣鉤). *to angle*, tièⁿ-hṳ̂(釣魚). *angle rod*, tièⁿ-ko(釣竿). *a corner*, kak(角). *angle of a house*, tshù-kak-thâu(厝角頭).

**animal**, khîm-siù(禽獸); seⁿ-kháu(牲口). *domestic*, cheng-seⁿ(眾牲). *wild*, iá-siù(野獸).

**animate**, kóu-bú(鼓舞); kóu-kah(鼓合).

**aniseed**, poih-kak-hieⁿ(八角香); tōa-hûe(大茴). *(fennel or coriander)*, sié-hûe(小茴).

**ankle**, kha-ma̍k(骹目).

**annals**, sṳ́-chheh(史冊); le̍h-tō sṳ́-kàm(歷代史鑑); sṳ́-kì(史記).

**annex**, chiap(接); tah(貼); tùe(綴).

**annihilate**, mi̍t-bûang(滅亡); chĩn-mi̍t(盡滅); mi̍t-bô(滅無).

**announce**, pò(報); pò-tsai(報知); pín-kàu(稟到); pín-tàu(稟報); pò-sie-sit(報消息); pò-sìn(報信); thong-ta̍t(通達); thong-thûan(通傳); thong-tsai(通知); thong-pín(通稟).

**annoy**, kiáu-jiáu(攪擾); jiáu-hũn(擾混); tshok-nōⁿ(觸惱); phièn-nâng-khì(騙人氣).

**annual**, nîⁿ-nîⁿ(年年); múeⁿ-nîⁿ(每年); pâi-nîⁿ(排年); le̍h-nîⁿ(曆年).

**annul**, hùi(廢); tṳ̂(除); khṳ̀-tiāu(去掉).

**anoint**, buah-iû(抹油); hú-iû(敷油); buah-ko(抹膏).

**anomalous**, khî-kuài(奇怪); koh-iēⁿ(各樣); bô-lí(無理); bô-lí-lōu(無理路); bô-chhêng-lí(無情理).

**anon**, chiet-khek(即刻); lîn-sî(臨時); liên-sî(連時); sûi-sî(隨時); sûi-chiet(隨即); chí-tsûn(此陣).

**anonymous**, *placards*, bô-thâu-thiap(無頭帖); bô-miâⁿ-thiap(無名帖).

**another**, pa̍t-kâi(別个). *matter*, pa̍t-sṳ̄(別事). *man*, pa̍t-nâng(別人). *one more*, ke--kâi(加个).

**answer**, ìn(應); tap(答); ìn-tap(應答); tùi-tap(對答). *written*, hûe-jī(回字); hûe-sìn(回信); ho̍k-jī(覆字).

**ant**, hiã(蟻); káu-hiã(狗蟻). *white*, pe̍h-hiã(白蟻). *nest*, hiã-siū(蟻岫); hiã-tàu(蟻竇); hiã-hua̍t(蟻穴); hiã-khang(蟻空). *hill*, hiã-èng(蟻壅). *covered way of white ants*, hiã-lōu(蟻路).

**antagonist**, tùi-thâu(對頭); uan-ke(冤家); chhiû-ke(仇家); te̍k-chhiú(敵手); tùi-te̍k(對敵).

**anterior**, tshông-tsôiⁿ(從前); tsṳ̃-soiⁿ(自先); tsṳ̃-tsá(自早).

**anticipate**, ṳ̃-pĩ(預備); soiⁿ-pān(先判); soiⁿ-liāu(先料); ṳ̃-liāu(預料); ṳ̃-pān(預判).

**antidote**, kói-ta̍k(解毒); siau-ta̍k(消毒); hùe-ta̍k(化毒).

**antipathy**, lóu-hṳ̃n(惱恨); uàn-hṳ̃n(怨恨); chhim-ù(深惡); ke̍k-ù(極惡); ke̍k-hṳ̃n(極恨).

**antique**, *curiosities*, kóu-tóng(古董); kóu-nguán(古玩). *antiquity*, kóu-tsá(古早); kóu-sî(古時). *in remote*, siãng-kóu tiâng-sî(上古當時).

**antithesis**, tùi-kù(對句); si-tùi(詩對). *(antithetic scrolls)*, tùi-liên(對聯).

**anvil**, thih-tiam(鐵砧).

**anus**, pùn-mn̂g-kháu(糞門口).

**anxiety**, khùa-lṳ̃(掛慮); huân-ló(煩惱); khùa-sim(掛心); iu-ut(憂鬱); ut-būn(鬱悶).

**any**, *one*, put-lũn tî-tiâng(不論底誰); huâm-sĩ-mih-nâng(凡是乜人). *where*, put-lũn hô-tshù(不論何處); put-lũn tî-kò(不論底塊). *is there any more*, huân-ũ a-bô(還有亞無). *is there anybody in*, ũ-nâng-tõ--bô(有人在無). *anyhow*, sûi-piẽn(隨便); sûi-sûi piẽn-piẽn(隨隨便便).

**apart**, keh-pie̍t(隔別); kak-pie̍t(各別); lî-khui(離開). *how far*, siang-lî jie̍h-hñg(相離若遠).

**apartment**, pâng(房); pâng-koiⁿ(房間). *female*, chhim-kui(深閨); kui-pâng(閨房); chhim-kui tièⁿ-lãi(深閨帳內).

**apathy**, bô-sim(無心); néⁿ-ì(冷意); néⁿ-tãⁿ(冷膽); tãⁿ-tãⁿ(淡淡).

**ape**, kâu(猴).

**aperture**, khang(空); phāng(縫).

**apex**, téng(頂).

**apology**, jīn-kùe(認過); jīn-tsũe(認罪); khiû-sù(求恕); khiû-khuan(求寬).

**apostasy**, puãn-tãu(叛道); pũe-kà(背教).

**apothecary**, ie̍h-tshâi-kheh(藥材客); khui ie̍h-tshâi-phòu(開藥材舖); ie̍h-phòu tshâi-tsú(藥舖財主).

**apparel**, i-ho̍k(衣服); ho̍k-sek(服飾); sin-chhēng(身穿); saⁿ-khòu(衫褲); kûn-saⁿ(裙衫).

**appear**, huat-hīn(發現); tshut-hīn(出現); lòu-tshut(露出); hién-lòu(顯露); tù-hīn(著現); lòu-hīn(露現); hién-hīn(顯現); hién-mêng(顯明). *appearance*, hêng-iông(形容); mīn-mãuⁿ(面貌); gūa-mãuⁿ(外貌); hêng-tsuãng(形狀); tsuãng-mãuⁿ(狀貌).

**appease**, khǹg-sek(勸息); khǹg--nâng màiⁿ-khì(勸人勿氣); sái--nâng sek-khì(使人息氣); sái--nâng hûe-sim(使人回心). *appeased*, sek-náuⁿ(息惱); sèⁿ lo̍h(性落); siẽⁿ-tńg(想轉); siẽⁿ-khui(想開).

**appellation**, hãu(號); miâⁿ-jī(名字).

**append**, kùa(掛); tah(貼); chiap-so̍k(接續); chiap-búe(接尾). *appendix*, chiap-ngân(接言); póu-ngân(補言).

**appertain**, so̍k(屬); ũ-kan-sia̍p(有干涉).

**appetite**, siẽⁿ-chia̍h(會食); tóu iau sṳ-chia̍h(肚枵思食); siẽⁿ-àiⁿ-chia̍h(想愛食). *no*, chia̍h-m̄-lo̍h(食毋落); ūi-kháu sat(胃口虱); ūi-kháu m̄-khui(胃口毋開). *to tempt the*, õi-khui ūi-kháu(會開胃口).

**applaud**, o-ló(呵咾); chheng-tsàn(稱讚). *in a loud voice*, tuah-tshái(喝彩); háu-siaⁿ o-ló(吼聲呵咾).

**apple**, phîn-kúe(蘋果).

**apply**, *the mind*, ēng-sim(用心); tsuan-sim(專心). *applicable*, kah-ēng(合用); ha̍h-ēng(合用); kah-tit-lo̍h(合得落).

**appoint**, siet-li̍p(設立); hun-phài(分派); hong-kuaⁿ(封官). *a time*, tiāⁿ-khî(定期); ieh-khî(約期). *appointment*, cheh-jĩm(職任); cheh-hūn(職分). *to receive*, siũ-thoh(受託); sêng-thoh(承託). *at the appointed time*, kàu-khî(到期).

**apprehend**, *a person*, lia̍h(掠). *meaning*, hiáu--tit(曉得); mêng-pe̍h(明白); thiaⁿ-mêng(聽明); thiaⁿ pat-kò-khṳ̀(聽識過去). see **fear**.

**apprentice**, thû-tĩ(徒弟); sai-kiáⁿ(師囝); tĩ-tsṳ́(弟子).

**approach**, kiâⁿ-bûa(行埋); lâi-kṳ̃n(來近); kṳ̃n-bûa(近埋); chiũ-kṳ̃n(就近); kṳ̃n-tsôiⁿ(近前); kṳ̃n-piⁿ(近邊); chìn-bûa(進埋).

**approbation**, huaⁿ-hí(歡喜); zua̍t-ì(悅意).

**appropriate**, ha̍h-sek(合適); kah-ēng(合用); siang-ha̍h(相合); kah-kah(合合).

**approve**, tsún(准); huaⁿ-hí(歡喜); zua̍t-ì(悅意); kùe-ì(過意); ha̍h-ì(合意).

**apron**, *to wear an*, hâ-ie-pòu(縖腰布); ûi-ie-kûn(圍腰裙).

**apt**, ha̍h(合); õi(會). *to get angry*, kōi-seⁿ-khì(易生氣).

**aqueduct**, ín-tsúi-tsô(引水槽); tsúi-làu-kau(水澇溝); tsúi-kau(水溝).

**arbiter**, kong-chhin(公親).

**arbitrary**, tsṳ̃-tsú(自主); chip-phiah(執癖); chip-sèⁿ(執性); kuai-phiah tsṳ̃-sĩ(乖僻自是).

**arch**, *of bridge*, kiê-chiu(橋周); kiê-chiu-mn̂g(橋周門). *arched door*, uân-mn̂g(圓門).

**archer**, keng-chìⁿ-piaⁿ(弓箭兵). *archery*, tau-keng siā-chìⁿ(兜弓射箭).

**architecture**, khí-tshù-huap(起厝法).

**archives**, sṳ́-kàm(史鑑); kok-kí(國紀); kok-sṳ́(國史); sṳ́-kì(史記); sṳ́-chheh(史冊).

**ardent**, chhiet(切); jie̍t(熱); zua̍h(熱); lie̍t(烈); kip(急); jie̍t-sim(熱心); sèⁿ-chhêng kín-kip(性情緊急); sim-sèⁿ pek(心性迫).

**area**, tiêⁿ(場). *in front of house*, tiâⁿ(埕). *inner*, thien-chéⁿ(天井).

**argue**, piẽn-lũn(辯論); piẽn-poh(辯駁); poh-mn̄g(駁問).

**arid**, kan-ta(乾灱).

**arise**, khí(起); heng(興); khí--lâi(起來); peh-tsáu-khí(百走起).

**aristocracy**, kong-kheng tãi-hu(公卿大夫).

**arithmetic**, sǹg-huap(算法); kui-tṳ̂ sêng-pun(規除乘分).

**arm**, chhiú(手). *clasp in the arms*, lám(攬); phõ(抱). *cross the arms*, tsha-chhiú(叉手).

**arms**, *weapons*, kun-khì(軍器); piaⁿ-khì(兵器); kan-kho(干戈); piaⁿ-kah(兵甲); ke-húe(家伙).

**armour**, chièn-phâu(戰炮); chièn-kah(戰甲); thâu-khue chièn-kah(頭盔頭甲); thih-kah(鐵甲). *armoury*, piaⁿ-khòu(兵庫); bú-khòu(武庫); kun-tsuang-ke̍k(軍裝極).

**armistice**, sek-chièn(飾戰); sek-chièn-pài(息戰拜).

**army**, tãi-kun(大軍); kun-sṳ̃(軍事); tãi-piaⁿ(大兵); piaⁿ-tsut(兵卒); iâⁿ-ngóu(營伍). *to lead an*, tòa-piaⁿ(帶兵).

**aromatic**, phang(芳); bī-sòu phang(味素芳). *spices*, hieⁿ-liāu(香料).

**around**, chiu-ûi(周圍); chiu-ûi sì-phìⁿ(周圍四片); sì-ûi(四圍); che̍k-ûi(一圍); tsôiⁿ-ãu(前後).

**arouse**, *from sleep*, kiè-chhéⁿ(叫醒); hàm-chhéⁿ(喊醒). *the mind*, kak-ngõ(覺悟); chhéⁿ-ngõ(醒悟); that-chhéⁿ(踢醒).

**arraign**, tòa-sím mn̄g-keng(帶審問經); tiàu-sím(吊審).

**arrange**, an-pâi(安排); uaⁿ-pâi(安排); pâi-pí(排比); sṳ̃-lí(伺理); liāu-lí(料理); chiáⁿ-tũn(整頓). *well arranged*, chiám-tso̍ih(斬截); tsôi-chiáⁿ(齊整).

**arrest**, lia̍h(掠); siu-kam(收監); khu-ah(拘押); ah-kuán(押管).

**arrive**, kàu(到); lâi-kàu(來到); kiâⁿ-kàu(行到).

**arrogant**, kiau-ngãu(驕傲); tsṳ̃-tōa(自大); tsṳ̃-sĩ(自私); tsṳ̃-tsun(自尊).

**arrogate**, tsṳ̃-tsuaⁿ tsṳ̃-múaⁿ(自專自滿); chhiàm-hūn(僭分); m̄-tsṳ̃-liãng(毋自量).

**arrow**, chìⁿ(箭). *to shoot*, siā-chìⁿ(射箭). *head*, chìⁿ-ne̍k(箭肉).

**arsenal**, piaⁿ-khòu(兵庫); bú-khòu(武庫); kun-khòu(軍庫); kun-tsuang-ke̍k(軍裝極).

**arsenic**, sìn-chie̍h(信絕).

**arts**, chhiú-gōi(手藝); peh-gōi(百藝); tshâi-gōi(才藝); kĩ-gōi(技藝); kang-gōi(工藝). *military*, bú-gōi(武藝). *literary*, bûn-gōi(文藝).

**artery**, kṳn-me̍hⁿ(筋脈); hueh-me̍hⁿ(血脈).

**artful**, káu-kuài(搞怪); hue-niau pe̍h-chi̍h(花猫白舌); kan-tsà(奸詐); kan-káu(奸狡); tsōi-sim-sṳ̄(㩼心事).

**articles**, mue̍h-kiãⁿ(物件). *three*, saⁿ-kiãⁿ(三件). *of commerce*, hùe-mue̍h(貨物).

**articulate**, *well*, tàⁿ-ūe liáu-liãng(呾話嘹亮); tàⁿ-ūe hiáng-liãng(呾話響亮); jī-ngán chheng-tshó(字眼清楚); tàⁿ-ūe hīn-hīn(呾顯). *badly*, tàⁿ-ūe hâm-hû(呾話含糊); jī-ngán kâm-kôu(字眼含糊).

**artificial**, m̄-sĩ seⁿ-jiên(毋是生然); seⁿ-tsõ(生做); tsãu-tsak(造作); nâng-chhiú só-tsõ(人手所造).

**artillery**, tōa-phàu(大砲).

**artist**, ūe-ūe sin-seⁿ(畫畫先生).

**artlessly**, tong-ti̍t(忠直); bô-nõⁿ-sim(無兩心); bô-ngũi(無僞); láu-si̍t(老實).

**as**, zû(如); chin-chhiẽⁿ(真像); àn(按); chiè(照). *as to*, lũn-ki̍p(論及); lũn-kàu(論到); tàⁿ-kàu(呾到); chì-kàu(至到). *as before*, jiông-kū(仍舊); jêng-kū(仍舊); i-kū(依舊); i-ngûan(依原); chiè-kū(照舊); zû-kū(如舊). *as you say*, chiè-lṳ́-tàⁿ(照汝呾). *as soon as*, che̍k-ē ... chiũ(一下...就). *as he grew up he gradually changed to evil*, i khuaⁿ-khuaⁿ-tōa chiũ chiãm-chiãm pièn-ak(伊看看大就漸漱變惡).

**ascend**, chiẽⁿ(上); khí(起); teng(登); seng(升).

**ascertain**, chèng mêng-pe̍h(證明白); chhê-mêng(查明); kháu-kiù mêng-pe̍h(考究明白); chieh-mn̄g tiāⁿ-tie̍h(借問定着); húang-mn̄g(訪問).

**ashamed**, siáu-lí(少禮); kièn-siàu(見笑); tshâm-khũi(慚愧).

**ashes**, húe-hu(火烌).

**ask**, *a question*, mn̄g(問); chieh-mn̄g(借問). *for anything*, khiû(求); khṳt(乞); thó(討). *leave of absence, as mandarin*, kò-kè(告假).

**asleep**, tõ-u̍t(在夗); tõ-gu̍t(在夗); gu̍t--khṳ̀-liáu(夗去了).

**aspect**, hêng-iông(形容); iông-mãuⁿ(容貌); mīn-sek(面色); mīn-mãuⁿ(面貌).

**asperity**, kín-sèⁿ(緊性); tshou-siap(粗澀); oh-thì-thâu(僫剃頭); tò-thì(倒剃).

**asperse**, húiⁿ-pãng(誹謗); pãng-húiⁿ(謗誹); tsham-húiⁿ iâu-pãng(讒誹謠謗); pãng nâng-miâⁿ-sek(傍人名色).

**ass**, lṳ̂(驢).

**assail**, kong(攻); kong-khek(攻擊); kong-phah(攻拍).

**assassin**, àm-chẽⁿ thâi-nâng(暗靜刣人); kiâⁿ-tshǹg(行剌); àm-hāi(暗害).

**assault**, khek-phah(擊拍); kong-khek(攻擊). *a city*, phah-siâⁿ(拍城).

**assay**, chhì-thóiⁿ(試睇); chhì-tsò(試做); thèng-tsãu-hùe(聽造化). *metal*, chhì-kim(試金).

**assemble**, chi̍p-hũe(集會); tsũ-chi̍p(聚集); hũe-chi̍p(會集); tsũ-hũe(聚匯); chi̍p-bûa(集埋).

**assent**, tsún(准); zún-na̍p(允納); khéng(肯); hàuⁿ(好); na̍p-ì(納意).

**assert**, tàⁿ-sĩ(呾是); chèng-ngẽ(證硬); ngẽ-chèng(硬證).

**assess**, tiāⁿ-hiàng(定餉); tiāⁿ-niêⁿ(定糧); khue-phài(科派).

**asseverate**, *on oath*, chiù-tsūa(咒誓); kiè thiⁿ-tī tsò-chèng(叫天地做證); tng-thiⁿ mêng-sī(當天明示).

**assiduity**, tsuan-sim(專心); khṳ̂n(勤); khṳ̂n-kang(勤工); ēng-kang(用工); siêⁿ-sim(上心).

**assign**, tiāⁿ(定); li̍p(立); phài(派); kau-thoh(交託); hù-thoh(付托).

**assimilate**, sái--i pêⁿ-iēⁿ(使伊平樣).

**assist**, pang-tsõ(幫助); siang-pang(相幫); sie-hũ(相輔); hũ-tsõ(輔助); pang-chhiú(幫手); pang-la̍t(幫力). *with a gift*, pang-tsān(幫贊).

**associate**, ṳ́-nâng uáng-lâi(予人往來); kāng-nâng lâi-uáng(共人來往); kau-tshap(交插); kau-chiap(交接). *as partner*, tsò-húe-kì(做伙記).

**assort**, thia̍p-kui-lūi(叠歸類); siu-kui kak-lūi(收歸各類).

**assuage**, *grief*, kói-iu(解憂). *thirst*, chí-âu(止喉); kói-khuah(解渴).

**assuredly**, tiāⁿ-tie̍h(定着); mién-gî(免疑).

**asthma**, he-ku-thiu(嘿龜抽); he-tshúan(嘿喘); he-khì(嘿氣).

**aster**, *(China)*, kek-hue(菊花).

**astonish**, khṳt--nâng hãi-ĩ(乞人駭異); sái-nâng khî-ĩ(使人奇異); hãi-ĩ nâng kâi zṳ́-ma̍k(駭異人个耳目).

**astounded**, kiaⁿ-kàu hua̍k--chē-kiè(驚到喝些叫); kiaⁿ-kàu hehⁿ--chē-kiè(驚到赫些叫); kiaⁿ-kàu ngo̍h-ngo̍h(驚到愕愕); kiaⁿ-kàu kông-kông(驚到戇戇).

**astray**, tsáu-tshò-lōu(行賺路); kiâⁿ-tāⁿ lōu-thû(行差路塗).

**astride**, khiâ-tsõ(騎坐); khiâ-bé-tsõ(騎馬坐); thí-kha-tsõ(體骹坐).

**astringent**, tau-tsũ(兜住); chí-sià-ie̍h(止瀉藥); siu-liám(收斂).

**astrologer**, lo̍h-ngóu-chheⁿ(落五星); khùaⁿ-miāⁿ(看命).

**astronomer**, kuan-thien-bûn(觀天文); thien-bûn-sṳ̃(天文士). *Imperial*, khim-thien-kàm(欽天鑑).

**astronomy**, thien-bûn(天文).

**asunder**, tñg(斷); keh-tñg(隔斷); keh-khui(隔開); pun-khui(分開); pie̍t-khui(別開).

**asylum**, *for infants*, io̍k-eng-tn̂g(育嬰堂); iáng-io̍k-tn̂g(養育堂). *for old people*, ku-láu-īⁿ(孤老院); iáng-chì-īⁿ(養濟院). *for lepers*, thái-ko-liâu(癩哥寮).

**at**, kàu(到); chì(至); tõ(在); kṳ̃n(近).

**athwart**, hûeⁿ(橫); *obliquely*, ka-lak-siâ(交落斜).

**atlas**, tī-tôu(地圖); tī-lí-tôu(地理圖).

**atmosphere**, *(weather)*, thiⁿ-khì(天氣).

**atom**, che̍k-tiám-kiáⁿ(一點囝); se-su-kiáⁿ(些須囝).

**atone**, so̍k-tsũe(贖罪); so̍k-tńg tsũe-kùe(贖轉罪過).

**atrocious**, hiong-ak(兇惡); hiau-hiông(梟雄).

**attach**, tah(貼). *a seal*, khap-ìn(蓋印).

**attachment**, siang-ài(相愛). *great*, sieh-tsãi lī-m̄-khui(惜知離毋開); lân-íⁿ kuah-siá(難以割捨); lân-íⁿ kuah-ài(難以割愛).

**attack**, kong-khek(功擊). *a city*, kong-siâⁿ(功城); phah-siâⁿ(拍城).

**attain**, tit(得); tit--tie̍h(得着); kàu(到); ki̍p(及). *attain literary rank*, tit-kong-miâⁿ(得功名); ji̍p-o̍h(入學). *the various degrees*, ji̍p-siù-tsâi(入秀才); tèng-kṳ́-jîn(中舉人); tèng-chìn-sṳ̃(中進士); tiám-hân-lîm(點翰林).

**attempt**, chhì-tsò(試做); chhì-thóiⁿ(試睇); thèng-tsãu-hùe(聽造化); thèng-hiau-hẽng(聽僥倖).

**attend**, *mind*, ēng-sim(用心); liû-sim(留心). *to business*, pōiⁿ-sṳ̄(伴事); lí-sṳ̄(理事). *upon somebody*, ho̍k-sṳ̃(服事); sṳ̃-hāu(伺候); kṳn-sûi(跟隨); tsáu-tãng(走動); teng-tùe(盯綴). *on sick person*, teng-tùe(盯綴); khâng-khiâ(捧擎).

**attendants**, kṳn-pan(跟班); kṳn-sûi(跟隨).

**attentive**, ēng-sim(用心); sié-sim(小心); liû-sim(留心); tsuan-sim(專心).

**attest**, tsò-chèng(做證); tsò-chèng-kṳ̃(做證據).

**auction**, *to sell by*, pie-mue̍h-kiãⁿ(標物件); khà-lõi-lang(扣黎郎).

**aunt**, *paternal*, a-kou(阿姑). *maternal*, bó-î(母姨). *aunt’s husband*, a-tiẽⁿ(阿丈); kou-tiẽⁿ(姑丈).

**audacious**, káⁿ-táⁿ(敢膽); tōa-táⁿ(大膽); káⁿ-tsak káⁿ-ûi(敢作敢爲).

**audience**, *to have a large*, tsōi-tsōi-nâng lâi-thiaⁿ(㩼㩼人來聽). *with a king*, chhiâu-kìⁿ(朝見); chiẽⁿ-chhiâu(上朝); kìⁿ-huâng-tì(見皇帝).

**auspicious**, kit(吉); siâng(祥); kit-tiãu(吉兆); siâng-sũi(祥瑞).

**austere**, tsang-ngiâm(莊嚴); ngiâm-sok(嚴束); kùe-ngiâm(過嚴); ngiâm-khek(嚴刻).

**authentic**, chin(真); chin-si̍t(真實); ũ-phêng-kṳ̃(有憑據); ũ-khak-kṳ̃(有確據); si̍t-tsãi(實在).

**author**, tù-tsṳ(著書); tù-tsṳ li̍p-sueh(著書立說).

**authority**, khûan(權); khûan-lêng(權能); khûan-pèⁿ(權柄); khûan-sì(權勢); chèng-pèⁿ(政柄).

**authorize**, úi-khûan--pun-nâng(委權分人); tsún(准); jîm(壬).

**autumn**, chhiu(秋); chhiu-thiⁿ(秋天).

**auxiliaries**, pang-piaⁿ(幫兵). *to engage*, chhiáⁿ-huan-piaⁿ(請番兵); chhiáⁿ-pang-piaⁿ(請幫兵); chieh-piaⁿ(借兵).

**avail**, *oneself of opportunity*, sêng-ki-hũe(乘機會); sêng-piẽn(乘便).

**avaricious**, *covetous*, tham-sim(貪心); tham-chîⁿ(貪錢); àiⁿ-chîⁿ(愛錢); hàuⁿ-chîⁿ(好錢); tham-khok(貪酷). *niggardly*, kien-liẽn(慳吝); tham-liẽn(貪吝); khek-po̍h(刻薄); kien-siap(慳澀); liẽn-siap(吝嗇).

**avenge**, pò-chhiû(報仇); pò-uan(報冤); sin-uan(伸冤).

**avenue**, chhiū-im kâi-lōu(樹陰个路); chhiū-nâⁿ-tói kâi-lōu(樹林底个路).

**average**, thuaⁿ-pêⁿ(攤平); thua-tn̂g póu-tó(拖長補短).

**averse**, m̄-hàuⁿ(毋好); m̄-ha̍h-ì(毋合意); tõaⁿ(惰); m̄-ngũan(毋願); m̄-khéng(毋肯).

**avert**, *the face*, ut-tńg-thâu(斡轉頭); tńg-sin(轉身). *calamity*, pī-tsai(避知); pī-hũa(避禍).

**aviary**, chhī-chiáu-koiⁿ(飼鳥間); chhī-chiáu-pâng(飼鳥房).

**avoid**, pī(弊); tô-pī(逃避); mién(免); tsáu-khṳ̀-tiàm(走去坫); kiâⁿ-khui(行開); pī-bûa(避埋).

**await**, thãi(待); tán(等); thẽng-hāu(等候); thẽng(停); hāu(候); hāu-thãi(候待).

**awake**, chhéⁿ(醒); gu̍t-chhéⁿ(夗醒); chhéⁿ--khí-lâi(醒起來). *wide awake*, lêng-cheng(靈精). *awaken*, hàm-chhéⁿ(喊醒); kiè-chhéⁿ(叫醒). *the world*, chhéⁿ-sì(醒世). *awakening words*, chhéⁿ-sì-gṳ́(醒世語).

**aware**, thâu-soiⁿ-tsai(頭先知); ṳ̃-pĩ(預備); ṳ̃-tsai(誤知); soiⁿ-tsai ṳ̃-pĩ(先知預備). *before one is aware*, put-kak(不覺).

**away**, lî-khui(離開); lî-khṳ̀(離去). *gone*, khṳ̀--liáu(去了).

**awe**, ùi(畏); ùi-kũ(畏懼). *dignity*, ui-hong(威鋒). *awe-inspiring*, ui-hong lím-lím(威風凜凜); ui-hong hek-hek(威風赫赫). *awful*, khó-ùi(可畏); khó-kèng-ùi(可敬畏); hó-kiaⁿ-ùi(好驚畏); tit-nâng-ùi(得人畏); tshūa-nâng-ùi(𤆬人畏). *put on an awe-inspiring appearance*, tién-ui(展威); théng-ui(挺威); chín-ui(震威).

**awhile**, siap-sî(霎時); khùn-kiáⁿ(頃囝).

**awkward**, tshou(粗); tsuat(拙); ngô-tsuat(吾拙); lõu-tsuat(陋拙); kông(戇); m̄-hiáu lói-siàu(毋曉理數); khong-khong-tiaⁿ(空空撞); thèng-tshùang(呾闖). *with one’s limbs*, kha-chhiú khie̍h bô-kò-khṳ̀(骹手挈無塊去).

**awl**, tsǹg-kiáⁿ(鑽囝); keng-tsǹg(經鑽); tsam-tsǹg(針鑽).

**awn**, chhek-mêⁿ(粟毛).

**awning**, pòu-phâng(布帆); liâng-phâng(涼滂); buan-thien-pòu(帆天布); chia-ji̍t-pòu(遮日布).

**awry**, tshúa(歪); m̄-chiàⁿ(毋正); uai-tshúa(歪歪); uai-siâ(挖斜); khi-siâ(欺斜).

**axe**, póu-thâu(斧頭).

**axle**, hûeⁿ-taⁿ(橫擔).

**azure**, tshang(蔥); chheⁿ(青); tshùi-lâm(脆藍). *the azure heaven*, tshang-thiⁿ(蒼天); chheⁿ-thiⁿ(青天).

### B

**babble**, thèng-tàⁿ(聽呾).

**babe**, nôuⁿ-kiáⁿ(孥囝); sòi-kiáⁿ(細囝); eng-jî(嬰兒); eng-hâi(嬰孩); hâi-jî(孩兒). *babyish*, a-nôuⁿ-kiáⁿ tsò-sṳ̄(阿孥囝做事); a-nôuⁿ-kiáⁿ-khúan(阿孥囝款); nôuⁿ-kiáⁿ-tsōng(奴囝狀).

**bachelor**, būe-tshūa-chhin(未娶親); bô-bóu-ko(無婦哥).

**back**, ãu(後); pùe-ãu(背後); ãu-mīn(後面). *turn back*, hûe-tńg(回轉). *come back*, hûe--lâi(回來); tńg--lâi(轉來). *the back*, ka-chiah(尻脊). *behind one’s back*, ka-chiah-ãu(膠脊後). *drum on the back*, *as barber*, tûi-ie(捶腰); phah-pho̍k(拍噗). *pinch the back for rheumatism*, lia̍h-pùe-kṳn(掠背根). *backdoor*, aũ-mn̂g(後門). *backroom*, ãu-pâng(後房). *backside*, ãu-pôiⁿ(後爿). *of cloth*, pòu-phak(布趴). *of paper*, tsúa-phak(紙趴); tsúa-pùe(紙背). *of a hill*, suaⁿ-pùe(山背); suaⁿ-ãu(山後).

**backbite**, húiⁿ-pãng(誹謗); pùe-ãu mēⁿ-nâng(背後罵人); pùe-ãu ngí-lũn(背後議論).

**backbone**, ie-kut(腰骨); ie-lêng-kut(腰龍骨); ie-chiah-kut(腰脊骨). *lower part of*, búe-lûn-kut(尾輪骨). *hunch-backed*, ku-ie(佝腰); ie hau-hau(); hau-ie(). *(more slight)*, ie hâu-hâu().

**backslide**, pũe-kà(背教); pũe-sìn(背信); tò-thò(倒退).

**backward**, tùi-ãu(對後); hiàⁿ-ãu(向後). *walk*, tò-kiâⁿ(倒行). *slow*, mān(慢). *slow (dull and stupid)*, chhi-ko(痴哥). *shy*, m̄-káⁿ kìⁿ-nâng(毋敢見人); ùi-nâng(畏人).

**bacon**, húe-ne̍k(火肉); chit-ne̍k(熾肉).

**bad**, ak(惡); pháiⁿ(痞); m̄-hó(毋好). *bad man*, àu-nâng(爛人). *good and bad*, hó-khiap〔〕; hó-tái(好痞); siẽn-ak(善惡).

**badge**, hō(號); jī-hō(字號). *secret*, àm-hō(暗號).

**baffle**, phùa-kòi(破計).

**bag**, tō(袋); láng(囊); pòu-tō(布袋).

**baggage**, hêng-lí(行李); hêng-tsuang(行裝); pau-ho̍k(行包袱李); pau-kó(包裹).

**bail**, tam-sêng(擔承); tam-pó(擔承); pó-niáⁿ(保領).

**bait**, jī(餌); hṳ̂-jī(魚餌); hiang-jī(魚餌); tièⁿ-jī(魚餌). *lay a bait*, pàng-jī(魚餌). *take the bait*, chia̍h-jī(魚餌).

**baize**, *red*, âng-phek-ki(紅劈基). *green*, chheⁿ-phek-ki(青劈基).

**bake**, pūe-piáⁿ(焙餅); hang-piáⁿ(烘餅). *baking oven*, piáⁿ-lôu(餅爐); húe-lôu(火爐). *baker*, pūe-piáⁿ sai-pẽ(焙餅司阜); tsò-pau sai-pẽ(做包司阜).

**balance**, *an account*, chheng-siàu(清數); tí-tṳ̂ chheng-tshó(抵除清楚).

**balances**, thien-phêng(天平).

**bald**, la̍h-chie̍h-thâu(蠟石頭); thâu-khak kng-kng(頭殼光光); thâu kng-nñg(頭光卵).

**bale**, *of goods*, khún(捆); tōa-khún(大捆). *out water*, ié-tiāu-tsúi(舀掉水).

**bamboo**, tek(竹). *pole*, tek-ko(竹篙). *mat*, tek-chhie̍h(竹蓆). *chair*, tek-íⁿ(竹椅). *shoots*, tek-sún(竹笋). *grove*, tek-nâⁿ(竹籃). *slips for wicker-work*, tek-bi̍h(竹篾). *scrubbing brush*, tek-tshóiⁿ(竹筅). *raft*, tek-pâi(竹牌). *beat with bamboo*, phah-póiⁿ-kiáⁿ(拍板囝). *beat with bamboo (in schools)*, phah-tek-póiⁿ(拍竹板).

**bank**, *river embankment*, toi(堤). *river bank*, hô-kîⁿ(河墘). *sand bank*, sua-phiâⁿ(沙坪); sua-pà(沙埧). *money*, ngṳ̂n-hâng(銀行); ngṳ̂n-tiàm(銀店); chîⁿ-tiàm(錢店); kheng-si-phòu(卿司舖). *notes*, ngṳ̂n-toaⁿ(銀團).

**bankrupt**, tó-tièⁿ(倒賬); phùa-ke(破家).

**bear**, *carry*, taⁿ(擔). *endure*, jím-nãiⁿ(忍耐); khat-nãiⁿ(刻耐); lún(忍). *cannot*, nãiⁿ-m̄-khṳ̀(耐毋去). *with people*, iông--nâng(容人); khuan-iông(寬容); ũ-tōu-liãng(有度量). *hunger*, nãiⁿ-gō(耐餓). *cold*, nãiⁿ-chhìn(耐凊). *heat*, nãiⁿ-pha̍k(耐曝). *hard to*, lân-nãiⁿ(難耐). *children*, seⁿ-kiáⁿ(生囝); kàng(降); kiau(邀). *in the womb*, huâi-tho(懷胎). *fruit*, seⁿ-kúeⁿ-chí(生果籽); kat-kúeⁿ(結果); kit-chí(結子); kat-si̍t(結實); kit-si̍t(結實).

**beat**, phah(拍). *one another*, sie-phah(相拍). *with bad language*, sie-mēⁿ sie-phah(相罵相拍). *beat the watch*, khà-khok sûn-keⁿ(扣柝巡更). *the time*, khà-pán(扣板); khà-chiauh(扣雀). *a drum*, phah-kóu(拍鼓). *to beat the bamboo in fishing*, khà-kou(扣罛). *one's own head*, phah-thâu phah-hia̍h(拍頭拍額). *the breast*, phah-sim-kuaⁿ(拍心肝); tûi-heng(捶胸). *clothes, in washing*, tûi-saⁿ-khòu(捶衫褲). *rice*, phah-tiũ(拍稻). *beat out fire*, phah-húe(拍火); kiù-húe(救火). *beat one with the hand in the face (a slap)*, piang(鞭). *beat one with the hand in the face (a blow)*, òng〔〕. *beat against the wind*, khau-huang〔〕. *excel*, iâⁿ(贏); iâⁿ-kùe(贏過). *to be beaten*, su(輸).

**beau**, hàuⁿ-phâi-chhiâng(好排場); hàuⁿ-ngiá(好雅); hàuⁿ-hue-liú(好花柳); hàuⁿ-he̍hⁿ(好赫).

**belong**, so̍k(屬). *belongs to you*, sĩ lṳ́-kâi(是汝个). *he belongs to Swatou*, i sĩ Sùaⁿ-thâu-nâng(伊是汕頭人). *this affair does not belong to me*, chí-kiàⁿ-sṳ̄ ṳ́-uá bô-kan(只鏡事予我無干); kāng-uá bô-kan-sia̍p(共我無干涉).

**beloved**, tit-nâng-sieh(得人惜); tshūa-nâng-sieh(𤆬人惜).

**below**, tõ-ẽ(在下); tõ-tói(在底); ẽ-mīn(下面). *on the ground*, tõ-thôu-ẽ(在塗下). *below the ground*, tõ-thôu-tói(在塗底). *below the sky (the world)*, thiⁿ-ẽ(天下). *below others*, tõ-nâng-ẽ(在人[訓]下).

**belt**, tòa(住).

**bemoan**, thiàⁿ--tie̍h(痛着); khàu(哭); thiàⁿ-khàu(痛哭).

**bench**, íⁿ-tiâu(椅條); tn̂g-íⁿ(長椅). *magistrate's*, kong-ùaⁿ(公案); ùaⁿ-tshn̂g(案床).

**bend**, uan(彎); uan-khek(拗彎). *the back*, phak-ku(趴佝); phak-ie(拗彎). *the body forward*, thâu-khek phak-kẽ(頭曲趴下). *the head backwards and look up*, tièⁿ-khí-thâu(脹起頭); thâu-khak tièⁿ taⁿ-taⁿ(頭殼脹擔擔); thâu tièⁿ-ngiáng(頭脹仰); ngiáng-mīn(拗彎). *the arms behind the back*, póiⁿ-káu-chhiú(板狗手). *a branch*, tau--lo̍h-lâi(兜落來); peⁿ--lo̍h-lâi(平落來).

**beneath**, ẽ(下); tõ-ẽ(在下); ẽ-tói(下底); ẽ-pôiⁿ(下爿); ẽ-mīn(下面).

**benediction**, tsok-hok kâi-ūe(祝福个話).

**benefactor**, ṳn-jîn(恩人); ṳn-tsú(恩主).

**beneficial**, ũ-iah(有益); ũ-lĩ-iah(有利益); ũ-kong-hāu(有功效).

**benefit**, *to*, sái ũ-iah(使有益); si-ṳn(施恩); lĩ(利); lĩ-iah(利益).

**benevolence**, jìn-ài(盡愛); jîn-tek(仁德); ṳn-hũi(恩惠); jîn-tshṳ̂(仁慈); jîn-ṳn(仁恩); ṳn-chhêng(恩情). *to shew*, kiâⁿ-tek(行德); si-hũi(施惠); si-ṳn(施恩).

**benignity**, tshṳ̂-ài(慈愛); jîn-tshṳ̂(仁慈); un-hûa(恩化).

**bent**, *the body*, sin phak-ku(身趴佝); ie tàm-ku(腰髧龜). *anything*, khiau-hie̍h(翹葉); uan-khek(彎曲); khiau-khek(翹曲).

**benumbed**, *with cold*, kûaⁿ kàu sin ngẽ(寒到身硬). *fingers*, chhiú ngẽ(手硬).

**bequeat**, zũi-lo̍h(遺落); thûan-lo̍h(傳落).

**beseech**, khṳ́n-khiû(懇求); koh-lô(閣羅); khṳ́n-chhêng(懇情).

**beset**, ûi--tie̍h(圍着); ûi-tsũ(桅住); ûi-miⁿ(圍免); sì-mīn ûi-tsũ(四面桅住).

**beside**, tsò-pû(做包). *on one side*, tõ-phâng-piⁿ(在旁邊); tõ-che̍k-pôiⁿ(在一爿); kṳ̃n(近).

**besides**, lêng-gūa(另外); têng-ūaⁿ(另換); tṳ̂-tshṳ́(除此); hûan-liáu(還了); siãng-chhiáⁿ(尙且); khùang-chhiáⁿ(況且).

**besiege**, ûi-siâⁿ(圍城); ûi-khùn(圍困); khùn-siâⁿ(困城).

**besmear**, kôu(糊); buah(抹); tôu(圖); hú(敷); zṳ́〔〕; phia̍k(抹); hún(粉); kài〔〕.

**besom**, sàu(掃); sàu-siú(掃帚); sàu-chiú(掃酒); sàu-soi(掃帚). *soft one*, mâng-hue-sàu(忙灰掃); nn̍g-sàu-siú(軟掃手).

**bespeak**, tsham-siàng(摻信); tàⁿ-tiāⁿ-tie̍h(呾定着); soiⁿ-tàⁿ(先呾).

**best**, siãng-hó(上好); chì-hó(至好); siãng-téng-hó(上頂好); it-hó(一好); ke̍k-hó(極好). *it would be best*, put-zû ...... kèng-hó(不如......更好); put-zû(不如).

**bestir**, *oneself*, khat-khóu(刻苦); tshut-la̍t(出力); lâu-sim(留心); khṳ̂n-la̍t(勤力); mién-la̍t(勉力).

**bestow**, sṳ̀(四); si(絲); siéⁿ(賞); sàng(送); pun(分); khṳt(乞); ṳ́(予).

**bestride**, khiâ(騎). *a horse*, khiâ-bé(騎馬).

**bet**, sie-su(相輸); sie-tóu(相肚). *fond of betting*, hàuⁿ-sie-su(好相輸). *to make a* , lo̍h-tóu(落肚).

**betel**, *leaf*, láu-hie̍h(荖葉). *nut*, pin-nôⁿ(檳榔).

**betimes**, tsá(早).

**betray**, *a prince*, khi-kun bōi-kok(欺君賣國). *one's country*, hièn-kok bōi-siâⁿ(獻國賣城). *one's village*, thàu-tsúi ji̍p-tsûn(透水入船). *a trust*, sit-sìn(失信). *a secret*, sia̍p-lāu(洩漏); phùa-tiãⁿ(破綻).

**betroth**, hṳ́-chhin(許親); kat-hun(結婚); kit-hun(結親); tiāⁿ-hun(定婚); sàng-phiàⁿ(送聘); phiàⁿ-tiāⁿ(聘定); tsò-chhin-chiâⁿ(做親成). *betroth a girl to any one*, tsò--pun-nâng(做分人); phiàⁿ--pun--nâng(聘分人). *betrothal presents*, phiàⁿ-lói(做親).

**better**, kèng-hó(更好); zú-kèng-hó(愈更好); hó--kùe(好過); iâⁿ--kùe(贏過); kiêⁿ--kùe(強過); sèng--kùe(勝過). *he is better today*, kim-ji̍t iáu-hó(今日猶好); iáu-tsua̍h(要絀). *you had better*, put-zû(不如); m̄-pí(毋比); m̄-chhin-chhiẽⁿ(毋親像).

**between**, tang(中); tìn-tang(鎮中); tong-iang(中央); tong-sim(中心); tong-kan(中間); lãi(內).

**bewail**, ai-khàu(哀哭); thòng-khok(痛哭); thiàⁿ-khàu(痛哭).

**beware**, kṳ́n-sín(謹慎); thî-huâng(提防); kṳ́n-kù(謹顧); kṳ́n-huâng(謹防).

**bewidered**, hũn-sim(渾心); kông-kông(戇戇).

**bewitch**, iau-su̍t mîⁿ-nâng〔〕. *bewitched*, pĩ iau-su̍t só-mîⁿ〔〕; bua̍h--tie̍h〔〕; chhek--tie̍h〔〕.

**beyond**, tõ-gūa(在外); gūa-pôiⁿ(外爿). *the time*, kùe-hãn(過限); kùe-khî(過期).

**bezoar**, gû-n̂g(牛黃).

**bias**, phien-sim(偏心); sim-kuaⁿ phõ-che̍k-pôiⁿ(心肝抱一爿); tōa-sòi-sim(大小心).

**bib**, *a*, ãm-ûi(頷圍).

**Bible**, Siàⁿ-kiaⁿ(聖經); Siàⁿ-tsṳ(聖書).

**biche-de-mer**, hái-siam(海參).

**bicker**, kháu-kak(口角); kak-kháu(角口); ũ-ūe(有話); sie-à(相詏); khau-peh(摳掰).

**bid**, hun-hù(吩咐); hàm(喊); sái(使). *a price*, tshut-kè(出價). *adieu*, chiãm-pie̍t(暫別); sî-pie̍t(辭別).

**bier**, kuaⁿ-tshâ-íⁿ(棺柴椅).

**big**, tōa(舵); tãi(大).

**bigot**, chip-thì(執滯); thì-nĩⁿ(剃奶); chip-ì(執意); chip-phiah(執癖).

**bile**, táⁿ(膽); táⁿ-tsap(膽汁); n̂g-thâm(黃痰).

**bilge**, *water*, tiam-lāu(沾漏); sia̍p-tsúi(涉水).

**bill**, toaⁿ(端); hùe-toaⁿ(貨單); ngṳ̂n-toaⁿ(銀單). *make out*, khui-toaⁿ(開單). *of bird*, chiáu-tshùi(鳥喙).

**billhook**, liâm(鐮); liâm-to(鐮刀).

**billet**, tsṳ-sìn(書信); kò-jī(告字); sòi-huang-sìn(細風信). *of wood*, kò-tshâ(告柴).

**billow**, éng(湧); tsúi-eng(水英); hái-éng(海湧).

**bind**, pa̍k(縛); hâ(縖); khún-pa̍k(捆縛); khún(捆); tîⁿ(纏). *book*, kap-chheh(合冊). *feet*, tîⁿ-kha(纏骹).

**bird**, chiáu(鳥). *cage*, chiáu-lâng(鳥籠). *lime*, chiáu-thi(). *nest*, chiáu-siū(鳥岫); chiáu-tàu(鳥竇). *edible bird's nest*, ièn-o(燕窩); ièn-tshài(燕菜).

**birth**, seⁿ(生); tshut-sì(出世). *birth-place*, ngûan-chiã(原籍); kū-chiã(舊籍); pńg-chiã(本籍); pńg-tshù(本處).

**birthday**, seⁿ-ji̍t(生日); siū-tàng(壽誕). *keep one's*, kāng-i-tsò seⁿ-ji̍t(共伊做生日).

**bistre**, tṳ-kuaⁿ-sek(豬肝色); tsang-sek(棕色); ou-âng-sek(豬肝色).

**bit**, *of anything*, che̍k-tiám(一點); tiám-kiáⁿ(點囝); kò-kiáⁿ(塊囝). *boring*, tsǹg-kiáⁿ(鑽囝). *horse's*, bé-hâm-thih(馬銜鐵).

**bitch**, káu-bó(狗母).

**bite**, kã(咬). *bite off*, kã-tñg(咬斷). *as pepper*, soh--tie̍h chi̍h(索着舌); soh-tshùi soh-chi̍h(索喙索舌).

**bitter**, khóu(苦). *in life*, khóu-tshó(苦楚); sin-khóu(辛苦).

**bitumen**, chie̍h-iû(石油).

**black**, ou(烏); hek(黑). *black and blue*, ou-chheⁿ(烏青).

**blackguard**, láu-kiáⁿ(漏囝); iá-kiáⁿ(野囝); pháiⁿ-kiáⁿ(痞囝).

**blackbird**, peh-chi̍h-chiáu(百舌鳥); peh-lêng(百靈).

**blacking**, *shoe*, sueh-ôi kâi-ba̍k-tsúi(刷鞋个墨水).

**blacksmith**, phah-thih sai-pẽ(拍鐵司阜).

**bladder**, jiē-pha(尿脬); tsúi-pha(水脬); phâng-kuang(水脬).

**blade**, to-ne̍k(刀肉). *of grass*, tsháu-keⁿ(草更); tsháu-sún(草筍); che̍k-ki-tsháu(一枝草). *"ilka blade o' grass keps its ain drap o' dew"*, ki-tsháu tiám-lōu(枝草點路).

**blame**, hiâm(嫌); cheh-hiâm(責嫌); cheh-mēⁿ(責罵); cheh-pĩ(責備). *it is my*, sĩ uá kâi-kùe-sit(是我个過失). *worthy of*, khó-cheh(可責); hó-hiâm(好嫌); m̄-tùi-sṳ̄(毋對事); m̄-tie̍h(毋着); ũ-phāng(有縫); ũ-khiah(有隙).

**blameless**, bô-hó-hiàm(無好嫌); bô-phāng hó-cheh(無縫好責); bô-ũ hó-ngí(無有好議); bô m̄-tie̍h--tshù(無毋着處).

**bland**, un-jiû(溫柔); un-hûa(溫和). *but with hatred in the heart*, kháu bi̍t pak kiàm(口蜜腹劍); chhiè-lí tshâng-to(笑裏藏刀).

**blanket**, chiⁿ-tiâu(氈條).

**blaspheme**, siet-to̍k Siãng-tì(褻瀆上帝); mēⁿ-thiⁿ chiù-tī(罵天咒地); chiù-thiⁿ mēⁿ-tī(咒天罵地).

**blast**, *wind*, che̍k-tsūn-huang(一陣風). *rocks*, ēng húe-ie̍h sie-chie̍h pit-tsò-pôiⁿ(用火藥相石筆做爿); ēng húe-ie̍h sie-phùa-chie̍h(用火藥相破石); éng húe-ie̍h lâi kek-phùa-chie̍h(湧火藥來激破石).

**blaze**, húe-iām(火焰); húe-iãm(火炎); húe uak-uak-kiè(火焜焜叫); húe uāng-uāng-kiè(火旺旺叫).

**bleach**, piè-pe̍h(漂白).

**bleareyed**, mîⁿ-ma̍k-kîⁿ(棉目墘).

**bleat**, iêⁿ mehⁿ-mehⁿ-kiè(羊哞哞叫).

**bleed**, *a patient*, pàng-tshut-hueh(放出血); thie-hueh(流血); tshn̍g-hueh(床血). *wound*, tshut-hueh(流血); lâu-hueh(流血).

**blemish**, ũ-hiâ--tshù(有瑕疵). *on one's reputation*, miâⁿ-sek tiam-u(名色玷污).

**blend**, sie-tsham(相參). *metal*, tsò-pû-iêⁿ(做包羊).

**bless**, tsok(祝); tsok-hok(賜福). *as God*, sṳ̀-hok(賜福); kàng-hok(賜福); hṳ́-hok(賜福).

**blessedness**, hok(福); hok-khì(福氣); hok-che̍k(福澤).

**blight**, *in grain*, m̄-kit-chí(毋結子); m̄-kat-si̍t(毋結實). *by frost*, khṳt sng-soh tàng-sí(乞霜雪凍死).

**blind**, chheⁿ-mêⁿ(青盲); sit-mêng(失明).

**blindfold**, ma̍k-chiu aⁿ-miⁿ(目睭掩眯); ma̍k-chiu pa̍k-miⁿ(目睭縛眯).

**blind man's buff**, lia̍h-hṳ̂(掠魚); mông-hṳ̂(蒙瞎).

**blinds**, *of door*, mn̂g-liâm(門簾). *venetian*, hāu-peh-chheh(鱟伯策).

**blink**, nihⁿ-ma̍k(聶目).

**blister**, phã(泡). *to rise in blisters*, phok-phã(起泡); phah-phòng-phã(拍碰泡); phok-kóng(仆起). *with medicine*, buah-phã(抹泡).

**blithe**, sóng-khuài(爽快); chhiè-mīn(笑面); muáⁿ-mīn hí-iông(滿面喜容).

**bloated**, tièⁿ(脹); chéng(腫); hap-hap(合合).

**block**, *for chopping meat*, tiam(砧); tshâ-tiam(柴砧). *large lump of wood*, tshâ-thâu(柴頭). *printing*, ìn-póiⁿ(印板). *to cut*, khek-ìn-póiⁿ(刻印反); kuah-ìn-póiⁿ(割印反).

**blockade**, kìm-kháu(禁口); kìm-káng(禁港).

**blockhead**, lú-tũn(魯鈍); ngûi-phûe(危皮); tshâ--kâi(柴个).

**blood**, hueh(血). *vessel*, hueh-me̍hⁿ(血脈); hueh-lōu(血路). *to pass*, pàng-hueh(放血); pàng-âng(放紅). *to let*, pàng-tshut-hueh(放出血). *curdled*, kit-hueh(結血).

**bloody**, ũ-hueh(有血); lâu-hueh(流血). *all over*, che̍k-sin-hueh(一身血).

**bloodshot**, *eyes*, ma̍k-chiu pãu-thiàⁿ(目睭暴痛); chhiẽⁿ-âng-kṳn(象紅筋); ma̍k-chiu âng(目睭紅); ma̍k ham-ham-âng(目蚶蚶紅).

**bloodthirsty**, hàuⁿ-suah(好殺); suah-lo̍k tãng(殺戮重); tshâng-pãu(藏暴); pãu ngia̍k(暴瘧).

**blossom**, khui-hue(開花). *bud and blossom*, kit-lúi khui-hue(結蕊開花); phah-lúi khui-hue(拍蕊開花).

**blot**, *out*, hú-tiāu〔〕; khou-tiāu(箍掉). *of ink*, tih--tie̍h ba̍k(滴着墨); tshak--tie̍h ba̍k(擦着墨).

**blotch**, *from drinking*, chiú-mo̍hⁿ(酒膜).

**blotting-paper**, sò-tsúa(疏紙).

**blow**, *a*, phah che̍k-ē(拍一下). *up a vessel*, pàng-húe-ie̍h kún-tiāu-tsûn(放火藥滾掉船). *wind*, huang tshue(風吹). *high wind*, thàu-huang(套風). *flute or pipe*, tshue-siau(吹簫); pûn-hûeⁿ-te̍k(歕橫笛); pûn-ti-tâ(歕嘀嗒). *out (as lamp)*, pûn-kùe(歕過). *the fire*, pûn-húe to̍h(歕火着); hut-húe(弗火). *the nose*, hnghⁿ-phīⁿ(哼鼻); sàng-phīⁿ(送鼻). *blow pipe*, húe-kóng(火管).

**blubber**, *jelly-fish or medusa*, thē(蜇); hái-thē(海蜇); tsúi-bó(水母).

**bludgeon**, ba̍k-káng(木槓); ba̍k-thûi(木槌); tshâ-thûi(柴槌).

**blue**, lâm(藍); chheⁿ(青). *vitriol (sulphate of iron; copperas)*, chheⁿ-hûan(生矾); táⁿ-hûan(膽煩).

**blunder**, tshò(錯); m̄-tie̍h(毋着).

**blunt**, *edge*, tun(鈍); bõi-lāi(袂利). *point*, lu(夵); bõi-chiam(袂尖). *of a man*, tun-kùe tṳ̄-thâu(鈍過箸頭). *outspoken*, thóu-ti̍t(土直).

**blurred**, *printing*, ìn-póiⁿ sie-hũn(印板相混); ìn-póiⁿ kôu-kôu(印板糊糊).

**blush**, siẽⁿ-tie̍h siáu-lí(想着少禮); siáu-lí kàu mīn âng-âng(少禮到面紅紅).

**boar**, tṳ-ko(豬哥).

**board**, pang(枋); póiⁿ(反). *on board ship*, tõ tsûn-téng(在船頂). *the six Boards*, la̍k-põu(六部). *Civil office*, lī-põu(吏部). *Punishment*, hêng-põu(刑部). *Revenue*, hõu-põu(戶部). *Rites*, lí-põu(禮部). *War*, piaⁿ-põu(兵部). *Works*, kang-põu(工部). *to board at an inn*, hiah-tiàm(歇店); suah-hiah(宿歇). *wages and board*, thàn-kang-chîⁿ chia̍h tshâi-tsú(趁工錢食財主).

**boast**, tsṳ̃-khua(自誇); khua-kháu(誇口); la-kè〔〕; tàⁿ-tōa-ūe(呾大話); sueh-huáng(說謊).

**boat**, tsûn(船); tsûn-kiáⁿ(船囝); théng-kiáⁿ(艇囝); sam-pán(舢板). *passage*, tōu-tsûn(渡船). *ferry*, kùe-khoi-tōu(過溪渡); hûeⁿ-tōu(橫渡). *boatman*, kuâⁿ-tsûn--kâi-nâng(寒船个人). *head ditto*, tãi-kong(舵工).

**body**, sin(身); sin-thói(身體); sin-hūn(身分); ne̍k-sin(肉身).

**bodyguard**, *imperial*, gṳ̄-lîm-kun(御林軍); sĩ-ũe(侍衛).

**bog**, che̍k-phiâⁿ-tsúi liù-liù-ku̍t(一坪水溜溜滑).

**Bohea**, *hill*, Bú-î-suaⁿ(武夷山).

**boil**, *rice*, tsṳ́-pn̄g(煮飯); pû-pn̄g(煲飯). *tea*, pû-tê(煲茶). *fish*, sa̍h-hṳ̂(煠魚). *a fowl*, tũn-koi(燉雞). *egg*, sa̍h-nñg(煠卵). *half-boil*, sa̍h-thn̄g-sim(煠湯心). *thoroughly*, sa̍h-se̍k(煠熟); sa̍h-thàng-sim(煠通心); pû-mîⁿ-mîⁿ(煲糜糜); pû-lok-lok(煲漉漉). *the rice is not yet boiled*, pn̄g būe-se̍k(飯未熟). *rice boiled but not very soft*, pn̄g khiū(飯糗). *boil water*, pû-tsúi(煲水). *boiling water*, kún-tsúi(滾水). *boiler*, ue(鍋); pn̄g-ue(飯鍋); tê-ue(茶鍋); tâng-ue(銅鍋).

**boil**, *a*, che̍k-lia̍p-thûe(一粒㿗); zua̍h-pauh(熱癤); pùi kat(沸結). *on buttocks*, tsõ-póiⁿ-tshng(坐板倉).

**boisterous**, *wind*, huang mé(風猛); huang tōa(風大); khûang-huang tãi-tsak(狂風大作).

**bold**, káⁿ(敢); táⁿ(膽); káⁿ-káⁿ(敢敢); káⁿ-ûi(敢爲); ũ-táⁿ-la̍t(有膽力); ũ-táⁿ-lia̍k(有膽略); mùiⁿ-sí(免死).

**boletus**, ba̍k-zṳ́(木耳).

**bolster**, tn̂g-chím-thâu(長枕頭); zo̍k(褥).

**bolt**, *of door*, mn̂g-tshùaⁿ(門閂); mn̂g-chhēng(門拴); mn̂g-tshùan(門串). *iron bolt or wedge for boring stones*, tsãm(鏨). *thunder bolt*, lûi-tsãm(雷鏨). *bolt a door*, tshùaⁿ-mn̂g(閂門); chhēng-mn̂g(穿門); kueⁿ-mn̂g(關門); tshùan-mn̂g(串門). *bolt out*, tshùaⁿ--tshut-khṳ̀(閂出去); kueⁿ-tiāu(關掉). *grain*, thai(篩). *bolter*, bí-lô(米籮); bí-thai(米篩).

**bolus**, ie̍h-îⁿ(藥丸); tōa-ie̍h-îⁿ(大藥丸).

**bombastic**, lō-ho〔〕; tàⁿ-tōa-ūe(呾大話).

**bombazine**, ú-lẽng(羽令); ú-tn̄g(羽緞); ú-se(羽紗).

**bond**, *contract*, ieh-toaⁿ(約單); ieh-jī(約字); ha̍p-tâng(合同); khòi(契).

**bondman**, po̍k(僕); nôuⁿ-po̍k(奴僕); ke-po̍k(家僕); po̍k-jîn(僕人).

**bone**, kut(骨); kut-thâu(骨頭). *after death*, kut-hâi(骨骸). *out of joint*, kut tshut-khũ(骨出臼). *to set, after dislocation*, kut tàu-tńg(骨鬥轉); kut tàu-lo̍h-ngám(骨鬥落眼).

**bonnet**, bō(帽). *one*, che̍k-téng-bō(一頂帽). *to put on*, tì-bō(戴帽).

**bonze**, hûe-siēⁿ(和尚).

**book**, tsṳ(書); chheh(冊); tsṳ-chheh(書冊). *one volume*, che̍k-pńg-tsṳ(一本書). *whole work*, che̍k-pang〔〕. *binding*, kap-chheh(合冊); tèng-chheh(釘冊). *case*, tsṳ-tû(書櫥). *cover*, chheh-phûe(冊皮). *learning*, ha̍k-mn̄g(學問). *seller*, bōi-tsṳ-chheh tshâi-tsú(賣書冊材子). *stand*, tsṳ-chheh-kè(書冊價); tsṳ-kè(書架). *worm*, chheh-hṳ̂(冊魚); pe̍h-gôu-hṳ̂(白吳魚). *worm (metaphor)*, khṳ̂n-tha̍k(勤讀); tsṳ-tsù(書蠹). *read one silently*, thóiⁿ-tsṳ(睇書). *read one audibly, as in study*, tha̍k-tsṳ(讀書). *compose or write one*, tù-tsṳ(著書). *classical books*, kiaⁿ-tsṳ(經書). *quote a book phrase*, ín-tsṳ-kù(引書句). *recite ad aperturam*, tshoh-liām〔〕. *bookish*, hàuⁿ-tha̍k-tsṳ(好讀書).

**boon**, ṳn-sṳ̀(恩賜).

**boor**, hieⁿ-ẽ-nâng(鄉下人); kṳ-hieⁿ-nâng(居鄉人[訓]); tshou-hu(粗夫); tshân-peⁿ-ko(田平哥). *boorish*, tshou-so̍k(粗俗); so̍k-hu(俗夫).

**boots**, ôi(鞋); hia(靴). *boot-straps*, hia-tòa(靴帶). *boot-tree*, hia-hùn(靴楦).

**booth**, tsháu-liâu(草寮).

**bootless**, *vain*, bô-ēng(無用); bô-iah(無益); bô-kong-hāu(無功效).

**booty**, tsng-mue̍h(贓物); tsha̍t-tsng(賊贓); chhiéⁿ-kiap mue̍h-kiãⁿ(搶劫物件).

**borax**, phêng-sa(硼沙).

**border**, kéng-kài(境界); kau-kài(交界). *bordering*, sie-kiam-kài(相兼界).

**bore**, tsǹg(鑽). *a hole*, tsǹg-khang(鑽空); sú-khang(暑空). *borer*, tsńg-kiáⁿ(指囝); keng-sú(經暑).

**born**, seⁿ(生); seⁿ-tshut-sì(生出世); tshut-sì(出世). *again*, têng-seⁿ(出世).

**borrow**, chieh(借); chhia(賒).

**bosom**, huâi(懷); sim-huâi(心懷); sim-kuaⁿ(心肝); heng-huâi(胸懷).

**botany**, hue-tsháu tsóng-lũn(花草總論).

**both**, nõⁿ-kâi(兩個); sang-kâi(雙個); liáng-kâi(兩個); jī-ke(二家); liáng-ke(兩家); liáng-pôiⁿ(兩爿).

**bottle**, po-lî-tsun(玻璃樽); kuàn(罐); tãng(筒). *ink-bottle*, ba̍k-tsúi-kuàn(墨水罐); ba̍k-tsúi-tãng(墨水甔); ba̍k-tsúi-hû(墨水壺). *bottle-gourd*, hôu-lôu(葫蘆).

**bottom**, tói(底); ẽ-tói(下底). *to the bottom*, kàu-tói(到底); tîm-tah-tói(沉到底). *of the heart*, sim-tói(心底); sim-tī(心地). *bottomless*, bô-tói(無底); chhim-bô-tói(深無底).

**bough**, ki(枝); chhiū-ki(樹枝); chhiū-kàng(樹幹); chhiū-pà(樹欛).

**bounce**, *against*, tsuãng--tie̍h(撞着).

**boundary**, kau-kài(交界); kéng-kài(境界); tī-kài(地界); kài-hãn(界限).

**boundless**, bô-hãn(無限); sǹg m̄-pat tò-khṳ̀(算毋判倒去); bô-pān(無辦); bô-liáu(無了).

**bounty**, ṳn-hũi(恩惠). *bountiful*, si-hũi(施惠); sṳ̀-ṳn(賜恩); tōa-pù-si(大佈施).

**bow**, *to*, ip-tsã〔〕; tsak-ip(作揖). *to the ground*, khàu-thâu(叩頭); khap-thâu(蓋頭); khàu-siú(叩首); kiâⁿ-tōa-lói(行大禮).

**bowels**, tn̂g(腸); tóu-tn̂g(肚腸); tãi-chhiâng(大腸); siáu-chhiâng(小腸). *obstruction of*, tãi-piẽn kâi-lōu m̄-thong(大便个路毋通); tãi-piẽn pĩ-kat(大便閉結). *inflammation of*, tn̂g seⁿ-húe(腸生活); tóu-lãi huat-húe(肚內發火); tóu-lãi zua̍h(肚內熱).

**bowl**, uáⁿ(碗); au(甌). *large*, uáⁿ-kong(碗公). *one bowl of rice*, che̍k-uáⁿ-pn̄g(一碗飯). *of a lamp*, teng-tsúaⁿ(燈盞).

**bowlegged**, tháng-khou-kha(桶箍骹).

**box**, sieⁿ(箱); a̍p(匣); che̍k-kha-sieⁿ(一骹箱); sieⁿ-láng(箱囊). *packing-box*, tsuang-sieⁿ(裝箱). *to box*, phah-khûn-thâu(拍拳頭). *boxer*, khûn-thâu sai-pẽ(拳頭司阜).

**boy**, a nôuⁿ(阿孥); nôuⁿ-kiáⁿ(孥囝). *is this a boy or a girl*, sĩ ta-pou a-sĩ tsṳ-niêⁿ(是大夫亞是諸娘). *boy approaching manhood (14 or 15)*, nôuⁿ-kiáⁿ-thûn(奴囝豚).

**bracelet**, chhiú-huân(手環).

**brackish**, kiâm(鹹); se-su-kiâm(些須鹹); kiâm-chhi̍h kiâm-chhi̍h(鹹彳鹹彳); kiâm-siam(鹹參); pùaⁿ-kiâm-tãⁿ(半鹹淡); pùaⁿ-kiâm-chiáⁿ(半鹹䭕).

**brain**, thâu-khak-tshúe(頭殼髓); náuⁿ-tshúe(惱髓).

**brand**, chhiah-jī(刺字); chhih-jī(彳字); ù-jī(惡字). *a*, hō(號); jī-hō(字號).

**brandish**, *a sword*, mõng-kiàm(舞劍); bú-kiàm(舞劍).

**brass**, tâng(銅); n̂g-tâng(黃銅). *brass-leaf*, tâng-po̍h(銅薄).

**brave**, ióng-káⁿ(勇敢); káⁿ-sí(敢死); ũ-táⁿ(有膽); ũ-táⁿ-lia̍k(有膽略); ũ-táⁿ-la̍t(有膽力); ũ-táⁿ-liãng(有膽量). *a brave*, ióng-tsàng(勇壯).

**brawl**, uan-ke lâ-chè(冤家朥債); sie-jiáng(相嚷); tshàu-nãuⁿ(臭惱); ki-ka bó-jiáng(幾家母嚷).

**bray**, lṳ̂ kiè(驢叫).

**brazier**, phah-tâng sai-pẽ(拍銅司阜). *brazen*, tâng--tsò(銅做). *brazen-faced*, mīn-phûe-kãu(面皮厚); m̄-sieh thí-mīn(毋惜體面); put-kù liâm-chhí(拍銅司阜).

**breach**, *of wall*, phah-phùa-siâⁿ(拍破城). *of friendship*, nâng-chhêng tñg(人情斷); nâng-chiâⁿ tñg(人成斷); tso̍h-kau(絕交). *of promise*, sit-sìn(失信); sit-ieh(失約); chia̍h-ngân(食言); m̄-sĩ tshùi-chi̍h(毋是喙舌). *of chastity*, sit-chiet(失節). *of contract*, sit-ieh(失約); pũe-ieh(背約); ûi-ieh(違約).

**bread**, mīⁿ-pau(麵包). *toasted*, pek-mīⁿ-pau(迫麵包).

**break**, khà-phùa(扣破). *asunder*, chi̍h-tñg(折斷); chi̍h-tsò-hue̍h(折做血). *a branch*, á-chi̍h(掗折). *break off a marriage*, thò-chhin(退親). *break to pieces*, phùa-tshùi(破碎). *one's word*, sit-sìn(失信); sit-ieh(失約). *break open*, peh-khui(掰開). *break the law*, hũam-huap(犯法). *a bone*, chi̍h-kut(折骨). *wind*, pàng-phùi(放開). *into a house*, tōng-mn̂g(撞門). *out of prison*, tsáu-kam(走監); pũan-kam(叛監).

**bream**, *to*, nãⁿ-húe(南火). *a boat*, nãⁿ-tsûn(南船); uãng-tsûn(旺船).

**breast**, sim-kuaⁿ-thâu(心肝頭); heng-tsôiⁿ(胸前). *breasts*, nõⁿ-lia̍p-niⁿ(心肝頭); nĩⁿ-pâng(奶房); nĩⁿ-phè(奶帕). *abscess in female breast*, niⁿ-hóuⁿ(奶虎). *breastbone*, heng-tsôiⁿ-kut(心肝頭). *breastplate*, chia-heng-thih(心肝頭).

**breath**, nâng-khùi(人氣); phīⁿ-khang-huang(鼻空風); u-khip(呼吸). *to hold in one's breath*, khip-khùi(吸氣); kìm-khùi(禁氣).

**breeches**, khòu(褲); tó-khòu(短褲); khòu-kue̍h(褲橛).

**breeze**, huang(風). see **wind**.

**brethren**, hiaⁿ-tĩ(兄弟).

**bribe**, iũ(賄); iũ-lũ(賄賂); kiâⁿ-iũ(行賄); sái-chîⁿ iũ-kuaⁿ(使錢賄官); soih-kha(細骹); sái-soih(使細); sái-ēng(使用). *receive*, siu-iũ(收賄).

**brother**, *older*, hiaⁿ(兄). *younger*, tĩ(弟). *brothers*, hiaⁿ-tĩ(兄弟). *one's own*, chhin-hiaⁿ-tĩ(親兄弟). *in-law (wife's brother)*, chhi-kũ(妻舅); *(sister's husband)*, a-nn̂g(阿郎); ché-hu(姐夫); mūeⁿ-sài(妹婿). *your brothers (polite)*, khun-tõng(坤重).

**buckwheat**, saⁿ-kak-be̍h(三角麥).

**bud**, *a*, gê(芽); sún(筍); hue-lúi(花蕊). *to*, huat-gê(發芽); huat-sún(發笋); phah-lúi(拍蕊).

**Buddha**, Hu̍t(佛); Hu̍t-tsóu(佛祖). *Buddhism*, Hu̍t-kà(佛教). *Buddhists*, Hu̍t-ke(佛家); pài-Hu̍t kâi-nâng(拜佛个人). *priests*, hûe-siēⁿ(和尚).

**buffalo**, tsúi-gû(水牛); suaⁿ-gû(水牛).

**bug**, ba̍t-sat(木虱); ba̍k-sat(木虱).

**build**, *a house*, khí-tshù(起厝); kiẽn-ok(建屋). *walls, of concrete*, cheng-chhiêⁿ(鐘牆). *of stones*, kih-chhiêⁿ(砌牆). *loosely with stones*, lúi-chie̍h(壘石). *ship*, tsõ-tsûn(造船); tèng-tsûn(釘船).

**bulb**, kṳn-thâu(筋頭). *of taro*, ōu-thâu(芋頭). *of lotus*, nôiⁿ-kãu(蓮厚).

**bulge**, thóu-tshut(凸出). *inwards*, thap-ji̍p(塌入).

**bulky**, lô-ho(羅呵); tōa(舵).

**bull**, gû-kóu(牛牯). *young*, gû-kóu-kiáⁿ(牛牯囝).

**bullet**, în-chí(鉛子); chhèng-chí(銃子); seⁿ-tsu(生珠).

**bullion**, bûn-ngṳ̂n(紋銀); uâng-pó(王寶); ngṳ̂n-piáⁿ(銀餅); ngṳ̂n-tiâu(銀條); khiau-thâu-si(蹺頭司).

**bully**, tsò-hûeⁿ(做橫); tsò-chhiàu(做笑); tsò-khiâng(做強).

**bulrush**, teng-sim-tsháu(燈心草).

**bulwarks**, *of city*, siâⁿ-chhiêⁿ(城牆). *of ship*, tsûn-po(船坡).

**bunch**, *of flowers*, che̍k-pé-hue(一把花); che̍k-pà-hue(一葩花); che̍k-tẽⁿ-hue(一捏花). *of grapes*, che̍k-tô(一朵). *of plantains (whole large bunch)*, che̍k-pà keng-chie(一葩弓蕉); che̍k-keng(一弓). *of plantains (portion of large bunch)*, che̍k-siu(一收).

**bundle**, pau(包); siáu-pau(小包); pau-kó(包裹). *of grass*, che̍k-pé-tsháu(一把草). see **fagot**.

**bung**, tháng-that(桶塞). *hole*, tháng-khang(桶空).

**bungle**, gōu(誤); tshou-kang(粗工); thèng-tsò(聽做); chhìn-tshái-tsò(凊彩做). *an affair*, gōu-sṳ̄(誤事).

**bunting**, ú-pòu(羽布); ú-se(羽紗). *flags*, kî(旗). *display of*, kat-tshái(結彩).

**buoyant**, phû-tsúi(浮水); bõi-tîm(袂沉). *in health*, khin-sang(輕鬆).

**burden**, che̍k-tàⁿ(一擔). *carry a*, taⁿ-tàⁿ(擔擔); taⁿ-mue̍h(擔物).

**burdensome**, tãng(重); chhin-chhiẽⁿ taⁿ-tãng-tàⁿ(親像擔重呾); lân-tng(難當); lân-nãiⁿ(難奈); kan-khóu(艱苦); teh tõ-sim-lãi(壓在心內); tam tõ-sim-lãi(湛道心內).

**bureau**, toh-kūiⁿ(桌櫃); tshn̂g-kūiⁿ(床櫃); siá-jī-tshn̂g(寫字床).

**burglar**, tsha̍t(賊); tshuan-chhiêⁿ liú-piah tsha̍t(穿牆㧕壁賊).

**burial**, kuaⁿ-ba̍k sàng-chiẽⁿ suaⁿ-thâu(棺木送上山頭); tsǹg-kuaⁿ-tshâ(葬棺柴); sàng-tsǹg(送葬).

**burn**, sie(燒); húe sie(火燒). *up*, sie-tiāu(燒掉). *a*, sie--tie̍h(燒着); húe thǹg--tie̍h(火燙着); húe chhih--tie̍h(火炙着).

**burnish**, bûa-kng(磨光); chhiù-kng(漱光).

**burrow**, liú-thôu-khang(㧕塗空); ku̍t-thôu-khut(掘塗窟); púe-khang〔〕; tshuan-khang(穿空); tshuan-hua̍t(穿穴).

**burst**, phùa-khui(破開); pit-khui〔〕; kek-phùa(激破); piàⁿ-li̍h(拚裂). *burst out laughing*, tōa-chhiè(大笑); ha-ha-chhiè(哈哈笑); tshâu-tshàu-chhiè(嘈嘈笑). *bonds*, tñg-soh(斷索).

**bury**, tsǹg(葬); tsǹg-suaⁿ(葬山); mâiⁿ-tsǹg(埋葬); tsǹg-mâiⁿ(葬埋); kám-lo̍h-thôu(感落塗); iám-thóu(堰土). *burying place*, phûn-suaⁿ(墳山). *public*, ngĩ-thóng-pou(義塚埔). see **burial**.

**bush**, che̍k-tsâng chhiū-kiáⁿ(一叢樹囝).

**bushel**, táu(斗).

**busy**, ũ-sṳ̄(毋閒); m̄-ôiⁿ(毋閒). *very*, che̍k-sin chẽng-sĩ-sṳ̄(一身淨是事); sṳ̄-bũ tsōi-tsãi(事務㩼在). *business*, sṳ̄(事); sṳ̄-bũ(事務); thâu-lōu(頭路). *business (mercantile)*, seng-lí(生理). *business (official)*, kong-sṳ̄(公事).

**busybody**, hàuⁿ-seⁿ-sṳ̄(好生事).

**bustle**, lāu-jie̍t kip-pek(鬧熱急迫).

**but**, tãn-sĩ(但是); nâⁿ-sĩ(難是); tsóng-sĩ(總是); iā-sĩ(亦是).

**butcher**, thâi-tṳ sai-pẽ(刣豬司阜); thâi-gû sai-pẽ(刣牛司阜).

**butler**, sĩ-tsái(侍仔).

**butt**, sie-tak(相觸).

**butter**, gû-nĩⁿ-iû(牛奶油); gû-nĩⁿ-lâ(牛奶油).

**butterfly**, búe-ia̍h(尾蝶); hû-tia̍p(尾蝶); hia̍p-tia̍p(葉鍱).

**buttock**, kha-tshng(尻川); kha-tshng-póiⁿ(尻川爿).

**button**, niúⁿ(紐); saⁿ-niúⁿ(衫紐). *made of cloth*, tsó-niuⁿ(組紐). *gold*, kim-khàu(金扣); kim-niúⁿ(金紐). *hole*, niúⁿ-phàng(紐判). *on a cap, common*, bō-tsu(帽珠). *mandarin*, lia̍p-téng(粒頂).

**buttress**, chhiêⁿ-tú(牆堵); chhiêⁿ-tún(牆盾). *of bridge*, kiê-tún(橋盾).

**buy**, bói(買). *oil*, tò-iû(倒油). *rice*, tia̍h-bí(糴米); niêⁿ-bí(糧米). *wine*, kou-chiú(沽酒). *cloth*, ka-pòu(鉸布). *fowls*, lia̍h-koi(掠雞). *pork*, kuah-tṳ-ne̍k(割豬肉); phah-tṳ-ne̍k(拍豬肉). *fish*, téng-hṳ̂(頂魚). *and sell*, bói-bōi(買賣).

**buzz**, ng-ng-kiè(哼哼叫); hng-hng-kiè(哼哼叫).

**by**, *I was cheated by him*, uá pĩ-i-tshuah(我被伊絀); pun-i-tshuah(分伊絀); khṳt-i-tshuah(乞伊絀). *by (along) the shore*, în-hái-kîⁿ(沿海墘). *by weight*, chiè-khin-tãng(照輕重); chiè-chhìn-chheⁿ(照秤星); chiè-tshâ-chhìn(照柴秤). *by no means*, būan-put-khó(萬不可); tiāⁿ-tie̍h m̄-sĩ(定着毋是). *by day*, ji̍t--kùa(日旰); ji̍t--tsṳ́(日子). *by night*, meⁿ--tsṳ́(夜子); mêⁿ--kùa(夜旰). *by himself*, sai-khia-ẽ(私奇下); ka-kī(家己); toaⁿ-nâng(單人). *by chance*, tú-ngõ(睹遇); ngóu-jiên(偶然). *by good luck*, tsãu-hùe(造化); hẽng-tit(幸得). *by the way*, tõ-lōu-chiēⁿ(在路上). *by sea and land*, tsúi-le̍k(水力). *by way of a place*, tshông(從); tùi(對). *year by year*, nîⁿ-kùe-nîⁿ(年過年); che̍k-nîⁿ kùe-che̍k-nîⁿ(一年過一年). *man by man*, che̍k-nâng che̍k-nâng(一人一人). *little by little*, chiãm-chiãm(漸漸); mān-mān(慢慢); khuaⁿ-khuaⁿ(寬寬). *to pay by the day*, lũn-ji̍t hôiⁿ--nâng(論日還人); chiè-ji̍t--sǹg(照日算). *to lead by the hand*, khan-chhiú(牽手). *by the pattern*, chiè-iēⁿ(照樣). *by stealth*, thau(偷). *by turns*, sie-lûn(相輪). *by and by*, khuaⁿ-khuaⁿ(寬寬); tán--siap-sî(等霎時); mān--chē(慢些); ke--khùn-kiáⁿ(加頃囝); ke--khùn(加頃); ke-bô-kú(加無久).

**bygone**, íⁿ-keng-kùe(已弓過); kì-uáng(記枉); soiⁿ-ji̍t(先日).

**byname**, pie̍t-hō(別號); thóu-hō(土號). *to give*, tsò-pie̍t-hō(做別號).

**bypath**, lōu-kèⁿ(路徑); sié-lōu(小路); sòi-lōu(細路); phâng-kèⁿ(旁徑).

**bystander**, tõ-phâng-piⁿ kâi-nâng(在旁邊个人).

**byword**, so̍k-gṳ́(俗語).

### C

**cabal**, táng(董). *to cabal*, kat-táng(結黨); àm-mông(暗蒙); im-nâng(陰人[訓]).

**cabbage**, *white*, pe̍h-tshài(白菜).

**cabin**, kuaⁿ-tshng(官艙); kuaⁿ-thiaⁿ(官廳). *in stern*, tsûn-búe-lâu(船尾樓); bâ-lî(巴籬); mâ-lî(麻籬).

**cabinet**, *the*, lãi-koh(內閣).

**cable**, *anchor*, tèng-soh(椗索); tōa-tèng-soh(大纜索). *chain*, thih-tèng-soh(鐵釘索).

**cackle**, koi-bó kiè-ko̍k-ke(雞母叫谷家). *as hen about to lay*, khou-toaⁿ(枯端).

**cactus**, sien-nâng pa-chiéⁿ(仙人[訓]巴掌); hue-uãng(灰王).

**cadence**, siaⁿ kûiⁿ-kẽ(聲懸下).

**cadet**, *(military)*, o̍h-bú(學武).

**cage**, *bird*, chiáu-lâng(鳥籠). *for criminals*, chhiû-lâng(囚籠).

**cajole**, so-lua̍h〔〕; so--nâng lua̍h--nâng〔〕; moⁿ-so〔〕; phièn kàu-i-hàuⁿ(騙到伊好).

**cake**, piáⁿ(餅); kúe(粿); ko(糕). *sponge-cake*, koi-nñg-ko(雞卵糕). *bean*, khou(箍).

**calabash**, hôu-lôu(葫蘆); hôu-lôu-pû(葫蘆瓠).

**calamity**, m̄-tsãu-hùe(毋造化); seⁿ-hũa(生禍); hũa-huãm(禍患); tsai-hũa(災禍); tsai-lān(災難); huãm-lān(患難); tshou-khóu(粗苦).

**calamus**, chhiang-phû(昌蒲).

**calculate**, phah-sǹg(拍算); pheⁿ-phah(斟酌); sǹg(算); tá-sǹg(打算); tshâi-ta̍t(才達); tshâi-chiak(才酌).

**calculus**, *in bladder*, suaⁿ-lîm(山淋); chie̍h-lîm(石淋).

**caldron**, tōa-tiáⁿ(大鼎). *for boiling sugar*, thn̂g-tiáⁿ(糖鼎).

**calendar**, la̍h-ji̍t(曆日); thong-tsṳ(通書).

**calender**, ta̍h-pòu(踏布); khoih-pòu(夾布). *calender-stone*, ta̍h-pòu-chie̍h(踏布石); ta̍h-chie̍h(夾布). *the pin*, pòu-te̍k(夾布).

**calf**, gû-kiáⁿ(牛囝). *calf of leg*, kha-tn̂g-tóu(骹腸肚). *to calve*, gû seⁿ-kiáⁿ(牛生囝).

**calibre**, *of gun*, chhèng-kháu(銃口); chhéng-khang(稱空).

**calico**, pòu(布).

**call**, kiè(叫); hàm(喊); chie(招). *out*, khui-siaⁿ(開聲). *call to mind*, siẽⁿ-khí-lâi(想起來); siẽⁿ-tie̍h(想着); liãm-tie̍h(念着). *call on anyone*, pài-hāu(拜候); sie-sûn(相巡). *what is he called*, i kiè-tsò sĩ-mih-miàⁿ(伊叫做是乜名). *to call animals*, khou(呼).

**calling**, *occupation*, sṳ̄-ngia̍p(事業).

**callous**, lang(郎); seⁿ-lang(生郎); chhiẽⁿ-lang(象郎). *heart*, sim ngẽ(心硬); sim zû-thih-chie̍h(心如鐵石); o̍h kàu-kang-ngẽ(學到工硬).

**calm**, bô-huang(無風); tiām-huang chẽⁿ-nn̄g(恬風靜浪). *taking things calmly*, tshông-iông(從容); tshông-tshông iông-iông(從從容容).

**calumniate**, húiⁿ-pãng(誹謗); pù-lũ〔〕; pù-lũ miâⁿ-sek〔〕.

**camel**, lo̍h-tho̍h(駱駝).

**camellia**, tê-hue(茶花).

**camlet**, ú-se(羽紗); ú-tn̄g(羽緞); ú-môⁿ(羽毛).

**camomile**, *flowers*, kam-kek-hue(甘菊花); pe̍h-kek-hue(白菊花); iá-kek-hue(野菊花); suaⁿ-kek-hue(山菊花).

**camp**, iàⁿ-pûaⁿ(營盤); piaⁿ-iâⁿ(營盤); iâⁿ-chē(營盤). *to camp*, phah-iâⁿ-pûaⁿ(拍營盤); tshàng-iâⁿ(創營); hiã-chē(營盤).

**camphor**, chieⁿ-ló(樟栳). *(Baroos camphor)*, piaⁿ-phièn(冰片). *tree*, chieⁿ-chhiū(樟樹). *wood*, chieⁿ-tshâ(樟柴).

**can**, lêng(能); õi-tit(會得). *you can, or may, do so and so*, tsò-tit(做得); khó-íⁿ(可以). *can you do this*, lṳ́ pat-tò-tsò, mé(汝識倒做咩); lṳ́ tsò pat-tò-khṳ̀(汝做識倒去), a-m̄-pat(阿毋識). *cannot*, bõi-tit(袂得); bõi(袂); put-lêng(不能); bô-lêng-ûi(無能爲). *cannot but...*, put-tit put(不得不)...; put-tit-íⁿ tie̍h(不得已着)....

**canal**, káng(港). *the great canal*, tōa-káng(大港).

**canary**, n̂g-chiáu(黃鳥).

**cancel**, khou-tiāu-jī(枯掉字); kau-tiāu-jī(交掉字).

**cancer**, *disease*, ta̍k-tshng(毒瘡); huang-ta̍k phùa-mūaⁿ(風毒破滿); *of breast*, niⁿ-iong(奶癰); niⁿ-ngâm(奶癌).

**candareen**, hun(分). *two mace and one candareen*, nõⁿ-chîⁿ che̍k-hun(兩錢一分).

**candid**, chiàⁿ-ti̍t(正直); sêng-si̍t(誠實); láu-si̍t(老實). *I tell you candidly*, kāng-lṳ́ tàⁿ mêng-pe̍h(共汝呾明白); si̍t-ūe kāng-lṳ́-tàⁿ(實話共汝呾); sêng-si̍t tàⁿ(誠實呾).

**candidate**, *for office*, hāu-sùan(候選); hāu-póu(候補); hāu-khueh(候缺). *for first degree*, thông-seng(童生).

**candle**, chek(燭). *wax*, la̍h-chek(蠟燭). *candle-stick*, chek-ti̍h(燭碟); chek-tâi(燭檯). *candle-shade*, teng-tsa̍h(燈閘).

**cane**, tek-ko(竹篙); tek-tshûe(竹箠); khue-tîn(科藤); tîn(藤). *cane-chair*, tîn-íⁿ(藤椅). *sugar-cane*, chià(蔗).

**cangue**, kê(枷). *wear*, taⁿ-kê(擔枷). *to put on for an example*, phah-kê sī-chèng(拍枷示眾).

**canister**, *tea*, tê-bí-kùan(茶米罐).

**cannibal**, chia̍h-nâng-ne̍k(食人肉); chia̍h-nâng(食人).

**cannon**, tōa-phàu(大砲); tōa-chhèng(大銃). *ball*, tōa-chhèng-chí(大銃子). *to fire*, pàng-phàu(放砲); pàng-tōa-kòng(放大槓); khui-phàu(開砲).

**cannoneer**, phàu-siú(炮手).

**cannot**, bõi(袂); bõi-tit(袂得); bõi-tit-tie̍h(袂得着); bô-lêng-ûi(無能爲); put-lêng(不能); m̄-tsò-tit(毋做得). *cannot but*, put-tit-íⁿ(不得已); bô-nãiⁿ-hô(無奈何); bô-khóu-nãiⁿ-hô(無苦奈何); put-tit put(不得不).

**canon**, tién(典); huap-lu̍t(法律).

**canonize**, thek-hong(剔封); hong-tsò siàⁿ-nâng(封做聖人).

**canopy**, tsṳ́-thâi(子臺).

**contharides**, pn-ngiau(斑貓); tāu-bâ(豆蟲).

**canthus**, *of eye*, ma̍k-thâu ma̍k-búe(目頭目尾); ma̍k-tshṳ̂(目眥).

**Canton**, *province*, Kńg-tang-séⁿ(廣東省); Ua̍t-tang(粵東). *Canton and Kwang-si*, liáng-kúang(兩廣); liáng-ua̍t(兩粵). *city*, Kńg-tang séⁿ-siâⁿ(廣東省城); Iêⁿ-siâⁿ(羊城); ngõu-iêⁿ-siâⁿ(五羊城); ua̍t-siàⁿ(粵聖); thô-siâⁿ(桃城). *go to Canton*, lo̍h-séⁿ(落省); chìn-séⁿ(進省).

**canvas**, phâng-pòu(帆布).

**cap**, bō(帽). *one*, che̍k-téng-bō(一頂帽). *summer*, sú-bō(暑帽). *winter*, kûaⁿ-bō(寒帽). *put on*, tì-bō(戴帽). *take off*, pak-tiāu-bō(剝掉帽). *red tasselled cap*, âng-eng-bō(紅纓帽). *the common round cap*, káⁿ-náⁿ-kue̍h-bō(橄欖橛帽).

**capable**, ũ-lêng-ûi(有能爲); ũ-pún-niáⁿ(有本領); ũ-tshâi-chhêng(有才情); õi(會); ũ-lêng-kàng(有能幹).

**capacious**, khuah-tōa(闊大); khuah-khn̍g(闊曠); khùaⁿ-chhēng〔〕.

**capacity**, *ability*, tshâi-chhêng(才情); pún-niáⁿ(本領); pún-sṳ̄(本事); lêng-kàng(能幹).

**cape**, suaⁿ-thâu(山頭).

**caper**, tsho̍k-tsho̍k-thiàu(蜀蜀跳).

**capital**, pńg-chîⁿ(本錢). *lent*, bó-chîⁿ(母錢). *capital and interest*, bó-thâu lāi-sek(母頭利息); bó-lāi(母利). *crime*, sí-tsūe(死罪). *city*, kiaⁿ-siâⁿ(京城); kiaⁿ-sṳ(京師); kiaⁿ-tou(京都).

**capitulate**, kàu mién-chièn-pâi(到免戰排); tâu-hâng(投降); hâng-ho̍k(降服).

**capon**, iam-koi(醃雞).

**capricious**, bô-tsú-ì(無主意); húan-tshut húan-ji̍p(反出反入); bô-tiāⁿ bô-tie̍h(無定無着).

**capstan**, ká-pûaⁿ(攪盤). *for heaving anchor*, ká-tèng-soh kâi-pûaⁿ(攪釘索个盤).

**capsule**, *of leguminous plants*, khak(殼).

**captain**, *of foreign ship (owner)*, tsûn-tsú(船主). *of native vessel*, tãi-kong(舵工).

**care**, liû-sim(留心); sié-sim(小心); tsṳ́-sòi(仔細); ēng-sim(用心); kṳ́n-sin(謹身); tsham-chhim(參深); tham-chhim(貪深). *anxiety*, khùa-lṳ̃(掛慮); huân-ló(煩惱); khùa-sim(掛心); khùa-liãm(掛念); khùa-huâi(掛懷); huân-sim(煩心). *take care of*, chiàu-kù(照顧); thóiⁿ-kù(睇顧); kuan-kù(觀顧). *not to care*, bô-kài-ì(無介意); bô-chhiet-iàu(無切要); bô-siang-kan(無相干); m̄-tshái(毋采). *what care I for that matter*, hṳ́-kâi-sṳ̄ kāng-uá ũ-sĩ-mih kan-sia̍p(彼個事共我有是乜干涉). *I do not care to go*, uá bô-mih àiⁿ-khṳ̀(我無乜愛去); uá bô-mih nguãn-khṳ̀(我無乜願去).

**careless**, ló-tshó(潦草); chhìn-tshái(凊彩); bô-sié-sim(無小心); hut-lia̍k(忽略); thèng-lâi(聽來).

**case**, a̍p(盒). *type*, jī-pûaⁿ(字盤). *fan*, sìⁿ-tō(扇袋). *instrument*, ke-húe-a̍p(家伙盒). *bow*, keng-chìⁿ-sieⁿ(弓箭箱). *condition*, kuang-kéng(光景); kéng-ngõ(境遇); chhêng-hêng(情形). *case in law*, uàⁿ-kiãⁿ(案件). *in case*, zû-jia̍k(如弱); khióng-ùi(恐畏).

**charge**, *order*, hun-hù(吩咐). *entrust*, kià-thoh(寄託); thoh(托). *to an account*, chiẽⁿ-siàu(上數). *price*, thó-kè-chîⁿ(討價錢). *in battle*, tshong-tīn(衝陣); ke-húe sie-chih(家伙相接); kong-khek(攻擊). *with an offence*, kò(告).

**charger**, chièn-bé(戰馬).

**chariot**, bé-chhia(馬車). *to drive*, sái-chhia(駛車); gṳ̃-chhia(御車). *charioteer*, chhia-hu(車夫).

**charges**, *expenses*, só-hùi(所費).

**charity**, jîn-àiⁿ(仁愛); jîn-tshṳ̂(仁慈); jîn-tek(仁德); tshṳ̂-pui(慈悲); tshṳ̂-sim(慈心); hó-sim(好心); siu-sim(修心). *almsgiving*, si-chì(施濟); chín-chì(賑濟); kiàⁿ-tek(驚德); kiâⁿ-jîn-tek(行仁德); chì-phîn(濟貧); pù-si(佈施).

**Charles'-wain**, *or Ursa Major*, pak-táu(北斗); pak-táu-chheⁿ(北斗星).

**charm**, hû(符); phek-siâ-hû(僻邪符); phêng-an-hû(平安符); pó-sin-hû(保身符). *to write a*, ūe-hû(話符). *to put up*, tah-hû(貼符); kôu-hû(糊符). *to wear*, kùa-hû(掛符); kũaⁿ-hû(摜符). *charms and incantations*, hû-chiù(符咒). *a charm of invisibility*, siám-sin-hû(閃身符).

**chart**, tī-tôu(地圖); hái-tôu(海圖).

**charter**, *a ship*, sùe-tsûn(稅船); pa̍k-tsûn(縛船); tsou-tsûn(租船).

**chase**, tui(追); jiāu(趭); chẽng〔〕. *away*, jiāu-tsáu(趭走); chẽng-tsáu〔〕. *the chase*, phah-la̍h(拍獵).

**chasm**, tī pit-khui(地筆開); tī li̍h-khui(地裂開); tī hām(地陷).

**chaste**, cheng-chiet(精節); siú-chiet(守節); tsat-lie̍t(節烈). *archway in memory of chaste widow who remains unmarried*, chiet-hũ-têng(節婦藤).

**chat**, tàⁿ-ôiⁿ-ūe(詖閒話); phue̍h(詖); phue̍h-ūe(詖話); phi̍t-phue̍h〔〕; thâm-lũn(談論); thâm-ngân(談言).

**chattels**, ke-si la̍k-thiok(家伙六畜); ke-tsṳ(家資); ke-húe(家伙).

**chatter**, chiau̍h-chiau̍h-kiè(雀雀叫); ki-ki-kiè(基基叫). *with cold*, chhìn kàu pōu-sou ou-tāu(凊到步蘇烏豆); chhìn kàu khí tõ-tiē(親到起在地).

**cheap**, phiⁿ(便); pân-gî(便宜); kiám-kè(便宜). *dog-cheap*, pân-gî kui-tsūaⁿ(便宜歸賤); tsūaⁿ-kè(便宜). *cheap enough, do not beat it down more*, pân-gî m̄-hó tsài-tshú(便宜毋好載處).

**cheat**, phièn(騙); khi-phièn(欺騙); láu-phièn(老騙); kuang-láu(誆老); kuang-phièn(誆騙); tshuah(掇).

**check**, tsó-chí(阻止); at-chí(遏制); at-taīm(壓擔); tsó-keh(阻隔); iak-sok(約束); tsũ(住); at-tsũ(壓罪). *oneself*, at-chí ka-kī(遏制家己). *pain*, chí-thiàⁿ(止痛). *diarrhoea*, chí-sià(止瀉); tsũ-sià(住瀉).

**cheek**, kih-kau(頰溝).

**cheer**, uaⁿ-ùe(安慰); khǹg-kòi(勸戒); kāng--nâng khui-sim(共人開心). *cheerful*, hí-iông(喜佣); sóng-khùai(爽快).

**cheese**, gû-nĩⁿ-piáⁿ(牛奶餅).

**cherish**, bú-iáng(撫養). *in the mind*, khǹg tõ-sim-lãi(囥在心底).

**chess**, chhiẽⁿ-kî(象棋). *play*, teh-kî(壓棋). *(move)*, kiâⁿ-kî(行棋). *(to consider before moving)*, keng-kî(經棋). *men*, kî-chí(棋子). *board*, kî-pûaⁿ(棋盤).

**chest**, *box*, sieⁿ(箱). *one*, che̍k-kha-sieⁿ(一骹箱). *of drawers*, kūiⁿ(櫃). *with many drawers, as druggist's*, peh-chí-sieⁿ(百子箱). *the chest*, sim-kuaⁿ-thâu(心肝頭).

**chestnut**, kãu-la̍k(侯栗).

**chew**, pōu(哺); kã(咬). *the cud*, huan-tsháu(反草); húan-tsháu(反草).

**chicanery**, tsōi-sim-sṳ̄(㩼心事); sim-sṳ̄ tsōi(心事㩼); kan-tsà(奸詐); ngũi-kòi(偽計).

**chicken**, koi-kiáⁿ(雞囝). *pox*, tshut-tāu(出痘); tsúi-tsu(水珠). *hearted*, bô-táⁿ(無膽); bun-táⁿ(蚊膽).

**chide**, mēⁿ(罵); tok-cheh(督責); cheh-pĩ(責備); kùe-cheh(過責); cheh-hiâm(責嫌).

**chief**, thàu-nâng(透人); thâu-ma̍k(頭目). *chiefly*, thâu-che̍k-kâi(頭一個); tãi-sì(大世); tōa-pùaⁿ(大半).

**chilblain**, kûaⁿ-tàng(寒凍); tòng-tshng(凍瘡); tàng-tshng(凍瘡).

**child**, a-nôuⁿ(阿孥); nôuⁿ-kiáⁿ(孥囝); kiáⁿ(囝). *childhood*, tsò-sòi-kiáⁿ--sî(做細囝時); iùⁿ-nîⁿ(幼年). *childless*, bô-kiáⁿ(無囝); bô-kiáⁿ bô-jî(無囝無兒). *childish*, nôuⁿ-kiáⁿ-khuán(孥囝款); nôuⁿ-kiáⁿ-iēⁿ(孥囝樣). see **infant**.

**chill**, chhìn(凊); kûaⁿ(寒).

**chillies**, kim-kaⁿ-náⁿ(金橄欖).

**chimney**, in-tâng(煙筒); húe-hun-tâng(火薰筒).

**chin**, ẽ-hâi(下頦).

**China**, Tong-kok(中國); Tong-ngûan(中元); Tong-hûa(中華); Tn̂g-suaⁿ(唐山). *China proper*, tsa̍p-poih-séⁿ(十八省). *Chinese Empire (the Manchoo synasty)*, tãi-chheng-kok(大清國). *Chinaman*, Tn̂g-nâng(唐人); Tong-kok-nâng(中國人); Hàn-jîn(漢人); Hûa-jîn(華人). *Chinese language*, Tn̂g-nâng-ūe(唐人話). *china-aster*, kek-hue(菊花). *china-root*, thóu-ho̍k-lẽng(土茯苓); thóu-ho̍k(土茯); ho̍k-lẽng(茯苓). *china ware*, hûi(缶); jiâu-khì(窯器).

**chink**, phāng(縫). *to chink dollars*, pu̍ah-ngṳ̂n-siaⁿ(跋銀聲).

**chintz**, ìn-hue-pòu(印花布); hue-pòu(花布).

**chip**, phùa-khui-tshâ(破開柴); siah-tshâ(削柴). *chips*, tshâ-tshùi(柴碎).

**chirp**, *bird*, chih-chiau̍h-kiè(折哳叫). *crickets*, tek-sut kiang-kiang-kiè(竹蟀腔腔叫); tiang-tiang-kiè(叮叮叫).

**chisel**, tsha̍k-kiáⁿ(鑿囝). *stonecutter's*, tsãm(鏨); chie̍h-tsãm(截斬).

**chloranthus**, *(chloranthus inconspicuus)*, koi-kha-lân(雞骹蘭).

**choice**, *select*, chì-hó(至好); siãng-hó(上好); tsùe-hó(最好); tśng-hó(總好); it-hó(一好); súan-hó--kâi(選好个).

**choke**, kéⁿ--tie̍h(鯁着); kéⁿ-tie̍h-âu(鯁着喉). *to death*, kéⁿ-sí(鯁着).

**cholera**, thòu-sià(吐瀉); sî-lẽng thòu-sià(時令吐瀉); khak-luãn thòu-sià(殼亂吐瀉); khong-thûi-ùaⁿ(空槌案).

**choleric**, kip-sèⁿ(急性); sèⁿ kín(性緊); kōi-seⁿ-khì(易生氣).

**choose**, suán(選); suán-to̍h(選擇); kóiⁿ-to̍h(揀擇); to̍h(擇); kóiⁿ(揀); púe-to̍k(撥著).

**chop**, tso̍ih(截); tok(剁). *mark*, jī-hō(字號). *dollars*, tèng-hō(釘號). *chopping-block*, tiam(砧). *knife*, tshài-to(菜刀); tshài-iang-to(菜央刀); pang-to(方刀). *mutton-chop*, pâi-kut-ne̍k(排骨肉).

**chopsticks**, tṳ̄(箸). *to hold*, sái-tṳ̄(使箸); khiâ-tṳ̄(騎箸). *lift with*, koih(箸).

**chord**, *of musical instrument*, hîⁿ-sùaⁿ(弦線). *of an arc*, keng-hîⁿ(弓弦).

**Christ**, Ki-tok(基督). *Christianity*, Iâ-sou kà(耶穌教). *Christians*, Iâ-sou mn̂g-thû(耶穌門徒).

**chronic**, *disease*, kú-pēⁿ(久病); kú-tn̂g-pēⁿ(久長病); tn̂g-nîⁿ sì-tshun pẽⁿ(長年四季病); sì-khùi-pēⁿ(四季病); lãu-mâuⁿ(老毛); kú-chi̍t(久疾); kū-pēⁿ(舊病).

**chronicles**, kok-sṳ́(國史); kang-kàm(工監); sṳ́-kì(史記).
