**chronometer**, sî-pie(時鏢); sî-cheng(時鐘).

**chrysalis**, thâng-kóiⁿ(蟲繭). *of silk-worm*, tshôiⁿ-kóiⁿ(蠶繭).

**chrysanthemum**, kek-hue(菊花).

**chuckle**, khih-khih-chhiè〔〕; chhih-chhih-chhiè(彳彳笑).

**chunam**, hue(灰). *floor*, hue-tiâⁿ(灰埕). *walls*, hue-chhiêⁿ(灰牆). *road*, hue-lōu(灰路).

**Church**, *members*, Siàⁿ-hũe(聖會); Kà-hũe(教會). *building*, hũe-tn̂g(會堂); lói-pài-tn̂g(禮拜堂). *to enter the*, ji̍p-Siàⁿ-hũe(禮拜堂).

**churlish**, sèⁿ-chhêng m̄-hó(性情毋好); kou-ta̍k-sièⁿ(孤獨相); kou-phiah(孤僻).

**cicatrix**, hûn(痕); sieⁿ-hûn(傷痕); phùa-kiàⁿ(破鏡); khieh-kóiⁿ(挈襇).

**cigar**, hun(薰); jiàu-a-hun(繞阿薰). *Manilla*, Lṳ̃-sòng hun(呂宋薰).

**cimeter**, uan-to(彎刀); uan-kiàm(彎劍).

**cincture**, tòa(住).

**cinder**, *of wood*, tsàu-khang-thùaⁿ(灶空炭); húe-tshâ-thùaⁿ(火柴炭). *from red hot iron*, thih-sái(鐵屎).

**cinnabar**, tsu-sa(硃砂). *(vermilion)*, ngṳ̂n-tsu(銀硃). *in sticks*, ngṳ̂n-tsu-tiâu(銀珠條).

**cinnamon**, ne̍k-kùi(肉桂).

**circle**, khou(箍); îⁿ-khou(圓箍); khuan(圈); îⁿ-khuan(圓圈).

**circular**, *a*, tsham-jī(參字).

**circulate**, chiu-liû(周流); lûn-tńg(輪轉). *blood*, kiâⁿ(行); ūn-kiâⁿ(運行).

**circumcise**, kuah-iâng-phûe(割陽皮). *circumcision, as a rite*, kuah-lói(割禮).

**circumference**, îⁿ-îⁿ(圓圓). *three feet in c*, chiu-ûi saⁿ-chhieh(周圍三尺).

**circumjacent**, tsôiⁿ-ãu(前後); lîn-kṳ̃n(鄰近).

**circumlocution**, tàⁿ-lâi tàⁿ-khṳ̀(呾來呾去); hông-hun thoh-gue̍h kâi-ūe(紅薰托月个話).

**circumspect**, kiãⁿ-kiãⁿ tsṳ́-sòi(件件仔細); kṳ́n-sín(謹慎); tsò-sṳ̄ ũ-chim-chiak(做事有斟酌).

**circumstance**, *a*, sṳ̄(事); che̍k-kiãⁿ-sṳ̄(一件事). *circumstances*, ngûan-iû(原由); chhêng-iû(情由); chhêng-hêng(情形); sṳ̄-si̍t(事實); lâi-le̍h(來歷). *of one's condition*, kuang-kéng(光景); kéng-ngõ(境遇); kéng-khùang(境況); khùang-kéng(況境). *prosperous*, sũn-kéng(順境), tsu-sṳ̄ sũn-ì(珠事順意); sũn-thû(順途). *adverse*, nge̍k-kéng(逆境); tsu-sṳ̄ bô-hièⁿ-sũn(珠事無向順). *able to accommodate oneself to*, ũ-pièn-thong(有變通); khûan-pièn(權變).

**citadel**, tōa-phàu-thâi(大砲臺); siâⁿ-lâu(城樓).

**cite**, tiãu-chiẽⁿ-tn̂g(兆上唐). *an author*, ín-tsṳ(引之); ín-tsṳ tsò-chèng(引之做證).

**citron**, hieⁿ-n̂g(香黃); hu̍t-chhiú(佛手).

**city**, siâⁿ(城); siâⁿ-ip(城邑). *city walls*, siâⁿ-chhiêⁿ(城牆). *Capital*, Kiaⁿ-siâⁿ(京城). *Provincial*, Séⁿ-siâⁿ(省城). *District*, Kūiⁿ-siàⁿ(縣城).

**civil**, ũ-lói(有禮); hiáu-lí(曉理); hiáu-chhêng-lí(曉情理). *civility*, lói-siàu(禮數); lói-mãuⁿ(禮貌); lói-ngî(禮儀). *civil and military*, bûn-bú(文武). *civil-officer*, bûn-kuaⁿ(文官).

**claim**, thó(討). *money*, thó-chîⁿ(討錢). *unjustly*, âⁿ(佔); cheⁿ(爭); chiàm(佔); mãuⁿ-jīn(貌認).

**clamber**, *up a tree*, peh-chiẽⁿ-chhiū(百上樹); soh-chiẽⁿ-chhiū(索上樹).

**clammy**, ũ-ka-liâm〔〕; liâm-nîⁿ tha-thi〔〕.

**clamorous**, kā-kā-kiè(咳咳叫); sie-jiáng(相嚷); kā-kā-jiáng(咬咬嚷).

**clamp**, ka-sut〔〕; hôu-khî-tah〔〕.

**clan**, *of the same*, tâng-sèⁿ(同姓); tâng-tso̍k(同族).

**clandestine**, sai-khia-ẽ(私奇下); sai-ẽ(私下); àm-chẽⁿ(暗靜); thau(偷).

**clap**, *the hands*, phah-pa-chiéⁿ(拍巴掌). *of thunder*, lûi tâng leh-leh-kiè(雷銅叻叻叫); lûi phek-le̍k(雷霹靂). *clap-boards*, kak(角); êⁿ-kak(楹角); po̍h-póiⁿ(薄板); póiⁿ-kiáⁿ(板囝).

**clarionet**, ti-tâ(嘀嗒).

**clarify**, *by straining*, tè(笮); tè-chheng(笮清).

**clash**, sie-tsũang(相撞); tiaⁿ-tsũang--tie̍h(撞撞着); sie-kha̍p(相磕); sie-cheng sie-kha̍p(相爭相磕).

**clasp**, *a*, kau-tah(交搭). *in the arms*, chhiú phõ(手抱); chhiú lám(手攬).

**class**, téng(頂); lūi(類); iēⁿ(樣); khí(起); pan(班); chéng(種). *classify*, kui-lūi(歸類).

**classics**, kiaⁿ(經). *the five Chinese classics*, ngóu-kiaⁿ(五經). *classical expression*, tién-kù(典故); kiaⁿ-tién(經典).

**clatter**, kit-ko̍k-kiè(結谷叫); chhit-tshok-kiè(七促叫); khit-khok-lo̍k-kiè(屈哭柝祿叫).

**claw**, jiáu(爪).

**clay**, nîⁿ(泥); thôu-nîⁿ(塗泥); liâm-nîⁿ(廉泥). *for pottery*, hûi-thôu(缶塗).

**clean**, chheng(清); kng(光); mêng(明); pe̍h(白); mêng-pe̍h(明白); thêng-chheng(澄清). *water*, tsúi chheng-chheng(水清清). *weather*, thiⁿ chêⁿ(天晴); thiⁿ-sî chêⁿ(天時晴). *(cloudless)*, liâu-liãng(嘹亮). *clear up after rain*, hõu chêⁿ(雨晴). *clear up doubts*, kói-gî(解疑). *an account*, chheng-siàu(清數); siàu-ba̍k chheng-tshó(數目清楚). *sighted*, ma̍k-chiu kng(目睭光).

**clearance**, *ship's*, tsûn-pâi(船排).

**clearly**, mêng-mêng(明明); hīn(現); mêng-hīn(明現); mêng-pe̍h(明白).

**cleave**, phùa-khui(破開). *wood*, phùa-tshâ(破柴). *cleave to*, liâm-tùe(廉綴); tah-tùe(搭綴); tùe-kín(綴緊); zû-ka zû-tshat(如膠如漆); kuah-siá m̄-khui(割捨毋開).

**clemency**, khuan-iông(寬容); tsuṳ̂-sim(慈心); ṳn-hũi(恩惠); tshṳ̂-pui(慈悲).

**clerk**, tsṳ-phōiⁿ(書辦). *in civil court*, a-pún(阿本). *military*, kó-kong(稿公); siàng-kong(相公).

**clever**, lêng-lāi(伶俐); tshong-mêng(聰明); gâu(賢); miàⁿ-ke(名雞); õi(會); ũ-lêng-kàng(有靈降); ũ-tshâi-chhêng(有才能); ũ-tshâi-lêng(有才靈); mién-chia̍p(敏捷); lêng-tõng(靈動); ũ-pún-sṳ̄(有本事); ũ-tì-sek(有智識); ũ-ki-tì(有機智); ua̍h-phuah(活潑).

**clew**, *of thread*, che̍k-kiû-sùaⁿ(一球線). *to wind into a*, în tsò-che̍k-kiû(演做一球). see **clue**.

**click**, *with the tongue*, tok--chē-kiè(督舌叫).

**client**, sṳ̄-tsú(事主).

**cliff**, kiã-piah(崎壁); suaⁿ-kiã(山崎); suaⁿ-ngâm(山巖).

**climate**, tsúi-thóu(水土); tī-khì(地氣). *could not bear the climate*, chia̍h-m̄-tie̍h tsúi-thóu(食毋着水土).

**climb**, peh-chiẽⁿ(爬上). *over a wall*, pûaⁿ-chhiêⁿ(盤牆).

**clinch**, *or clench*, *the fist*, lĩm-khûn-thâu-bó(斂拳頭母). *a nail*, teng-búe tò-tah(釘尾倒貼); tûi-kâi-lo̍ih tò-ngám-tńg(捶个笠倒眼轉).

**cling**, phõ-kín(抱緊); lám-kín(攬緊); khîⁿ(纏); khîⁿ-kín(纏緊). *to one's opinion*, chip-ì(執意).

**clip**, ka(咖); ka-tó(鉸刀); chién-tó(剪刀). *clippings*, pòu-tshùi(布碎).

**cloak**, tōa-phâu(大袍); muaⁿ(滿).

**clock**, sî-cheng(時鐘); sî-sîn-cheng(時辰鐘). *what o' clock*, kúi-tiám-cheng(幾點鐘). *9 o'clock*, káu-tiám-cheng(九點鐘). *striking*, cheng hiáng(睜響).

**clogged**, sat-miⁿ(蝨眠); m̄-thong(毋通).

**clogs**, *wooden shoes*, tshâ-ôi(柴鞋); kia̍h(屐).

**cloister**, am(庵); Hu̍t-am(佛庵); hûe-siēⁿ-am(和尚庵).

**close**, *letter*, huang(封); huang-sìn(封信). *door*, kueⁿ-mn̂g(關門). *without fastening*, hõiⁿ-mn̂g(闔門). *the eyes*, ma̍k-chiu ha̍p-miⁿ(目睭合眠); ma̍k-chiu tièⁿ-miⁿ(目睭脹眠). *the market*, siu-tiêⁿ(梳場). *all shops in protest against injustice*, pã-chhĩ(罷市). *close or end*, tsong(蹤); uân(緣); hiah(歇). *close-fisted*, khiãm-siap(儉濕); kien-liẽn(慳吝). *weather*, hip-zua̍h(翕熱). *texture*, ba̍t-ba̍t(密密); ba̍t-tsa̍t(密實). *application*, tsuan-sim(專心); ēng-kang(用工); khṳ̂n(勤). *close to*, siang-kṳ̃n(相近). *follow closely*, tùe-kín(綴緊); sûi-tie̍h-kha(隨着骹).

**compare**, pí(比); siang-pí(相比); pí-pẽng(比並); pí-pn̄g(比飯). *not to compare with him*, m̄-hó pí-i(毋好比伊); tsò-káⁿ-pí(做敢比); m̄-chhin-chhiẽⁿ(毋親像). *comparison*, phì-zũ(譬如); pí-zû(比如); pí-huang(比方); khó-pí(可比).

**compatible**, ha̍h(合); siang-ha̍h(相合). *with reason*, ha̍h-lí(合理). *with one's station*, siú-pńg-hūn(守本分); siú-hūn(守分).

**compendious**, kâng-lia̍k(共略); káng-séⁿ(簡省). *compendium*, iak-ngân(約言); tiah-iàu(摘要); káng-iàu(簡要); tshái-iàu(採要).

**complete**, sêng(成); sêng-chiũ(成就); tsò-hó(做好); tsò-uân(做完); sêng-kong(成功); tsò-chiâⁿ(做成); uân-pi̍t(完畢). *all complete*, kũ-kàu(俱到); tsôi-pĩ(齊備); tshuân-pĩ(全備); kũ-pĩ(具備). *completely*, tshuân(全); tsa̍p-tshuân(十全).

**complexion**, mīn-sek(面色).

**complicated**, hũn-tsa̍p(混雜); huân-tsa̍p(煩雜); úi-khiok tsâng-chih(偉曲叢接).

**compliment**, chheng-hu(稱呼); o-ló(呵咾). *send compliments*, mn̄g-hāu(問候); chhiáⁿ-uaⁿ(請安). *compliments*, lói(禮); lói-mãuⁿ(禮貌). *return*, ho̍k-lí(服理); ho̍k-lói(服禮); pò-ho̍k(報服); tap-lói(答禮).

**contaminate**, ùe--tie̍h lâm-sap〔〕; mak--tie̍h nah-sap(衊着垃圾); jiám--tie̍h(染着); hú--tie̍h(腐着); hìⁿ-tie̍h(鼾着); u-ùe--tie̍h(污穢着).

**cousin**, *of same surname*, chek-peh hiaⁿ-tĩ(叔伯兄弟); thâng-hiaⁿ-tĩ(堂兄弟). *of same surname (more remote)*, tsõng-hiaⁿ-tĩ(從兄弟). *of different surname*, pié-hiaⁿ-tĩ(表兄弟). *of different surname (children of two sisters)*, î-pié hiaⁿ-tĩ(姨表兄弟). *of different surname (children of brother and sister)*, kou-pié hiaⁿ-tĩ(姑表兄弟).

**cove**, hái-ò(海澳).

**covenant**, ieh(約). *make*, li̍p-ieh(立約); kat-ieh(結約). *break*, sit-ieh(失約); bûang-ieh(忘約); pũe-ieh(背約).

**cover**, khàm(蓋); chia(遮). *the face*, chia-mīn(遮面); iám-mīn(掩面). *a book*, kap-tsṳ-chheh(夾書冊). *of a book*, tsṳ-chheh-ko̍ih(書冊夾); chheh-phûe(冊皮). *cover with earth*, kám-thôu(䃭塗); kám tõ-thôu-tī(感道塗地). *covered with mud*, che̍k-sin kôu-tie̍h-thôu(一身糊着塗). *covered with wounds*, thong-sin sieⁿ-kháu(通身傷口). *mat cover on a boat*, phâng-kám(帆䃭).

**coverlet**, phũe(被); phũe-toaⁿ(被單); phũe-mīn(被面).

**covert**, àm-chẽⁿ tī-hng(暗靜地方); hó-tiàm kâi ūi-tshṳ̀(好坫个位處). *secret*, àm-chẽⁿ(暗靜); sai-ẽ(私下); sai-khia-ẽ(私奇下).

**covet**, tham(貪); tham-àiⁿ(貪愛); tham-siẽⁿ(貪想). *covetous*, tham-sim(貪心); tham-lĩ(貪利); tham-tshâi(貪財); tham-chîⁿ(貪錢); tham-tshâi tõng-lĩ(貪財動利); thóiⁿ-chîⁿ tōa-kâi(睇錢大个).

**cow**, gû(牛); gû-bó(牛母). *common*, n̂g-gû(黃牛); chhiah-gû(赤牛). *water-buffalo*, tsúi-gû(水牛). *cowherd*, chiéⁿ-gû(掌牛). *cowhouse*, gû-koiⁿ(牛間); gû-pâng(牛房).

**coward**, bó-táⁿ(無膽); táⁿ khiap(膽怯); táⁿ sòi(膽細); sòi-táⁿ(細膽), bun-táⁿ(蚊膽).

**coxcomb**, hàuⁿ-tsuang-hûang(好裝皇); hàuⁿ-iâu-pái(好搖擺); hùuⁿ-thì-tsò(荒剃做); hàuⁿ-tsuang-tsò(好裝做).

**coy**, *modest*, ũ-liâm-chhí(有廉恥). *bashful*, ùi-siáu-lí(畏少禮); m̄-káⁿ kìⁿ-nâng(毋敢見人).

**cozen**, kuang-phièn(誆騙); khi-phièn(欺騙); mûaⁿ-phièn(鰻騙).

**crab**, hõi(蟹); phâng-hõi(帆蟹); môⁿ-hõi(毛蟹); chhi̍h(蠘); pê-khî(爬蜞); to̍k-kha-khî(毒骹蜞).

**crabbed**, *look*, àu-mīn(懊面); mīn àu-àu(面懊懊); mīn pũ-àu pã-àu(面哺懊罷懊).

**crack**, li̍h(裂); phùa(破); phùa-li̍h(破裂); li̍h-phùa(裂破); pit(筆); pit-li̍h(筆裂). *a crack*, pit-hûn(筆痕); li̍h-hûn(裂痕); hûn-chiah(痕跡); hûn-phāng(痕縫). *crackers*, phòng-phiẽ(碰鰾). *to fire off*, phah-phòng-phiẽ(拍碰鰾).

**crackle**, pit-piak-kiè(畢逼叫).

**cradle**, iê-nâⁿ(搖籃).

**craft**, chiú-gōi(酒藝); kĩ-gōi(技藝). *craftsman*, sai-pẽ(司阜).

**crafty**, kan-tsà(奸詐); kan-káu(奸狡); kan-hiông(奸雄); tsà-ngũi(詐僞); kan-ngũi(奸僞); ũ-tì-hũi(有智慧); ũ-sim-sṳ̄(有心事).

**cram**, teh-tsa̍t(壓實); ji̍h-tsa̍t(揤實).

**cramp**, thiu-thiàⁿ(抽痛). *in the legs*, thiu-kha-kṳn(抽骹筋).

**crane**, pe̍h-liãu-si(白鷺鷥). *for lifting weights*, chhia(車).

**crape**, jiàu-se(縐紗).

**crave**, khiû(求); khṳ́n-khiû(懇求); koh-lô(閣羅). *craving for food*, tóu iau(肚枵). *for opium*, a-phièn-ngièn(鴉片癮). *for liquor*, chiú-ngièn(酒癮).

**crazy**, siáu(少); huat-siáu(發痟); huat-khûang(發狂); huat-tien(發癲); khûang-lũan(狂亂); sim m̄-tiāⁿ(心毋定); sim-sîn m̄-tiāⁿ(心神毋定).

**creak**, i̍hⁿ-ua̍ihⁿ-kiè(軋軋叫); i̍hⁿ-a̍ihⁿ-kiè(軋軋叫).

**crease**, niàuⁿ-hûn(皺痕); chih-hûn(折痕); chih-tsūe(摺襊).

**create**, tshàng-tsãu(創造).

**credentials**, bûn-phêng(文憑); bûn-pêng(文憑); úi-pâi(委牌).

**creek**, káng(港); sié-khoi(小溪); sòi-khoi(細溪); thong-kà(通教).

**creep**, *pê*, so(逡). *creep up*, pê--khí-lâi(爬起來). *through a hole*, bùn-khang(糞空); nn̍g-khang(兩空). *under the bedclothes*, nn̍g--ji̍p phũe-tói(鑽入被底). *stealthily along*, níhⁿ-kha-kiâⁿ(軟骹行).

**crescent**, *moon*, gue̍h-bâi(月眉); sin-gue̍h(新月); ngô-bâi-gue̍h(娥眉月).

**crop**, *of field*, nîⁿ-tang(年冬); nîⁿ-chhêng(年情); hìⁿ-tang〔〕; tang-chhêng(冬情). *two crops a year*, che̍k-nîⁿ siu-nõⁿ-tang(一年收兩冬). *take in*, kuah-tiũ(割稻); siu-tang(收冬); kuah-chhek(割粟). *bird's crop*, kui(胿). *to fill crop of fowl with sand &c*, kuàn-kui(灌胿).

**cross**, *the*, tsa̍p--jī kè(十二駕). *to make or write a*, phah-tsham-chhe(拍參差); phah-tshãm-sia(拍杉斜).

**cross**, *to*, kùe(過). *a river*, kùe-khoi(過溪). *cross-wise*, hûeⁿ(橫). *to be cross with one*, hia̍p-hiâm(協嫌). *peevish*, tshou-siap(粗澀); kia̍p-khak(夾殼); tò-thì(倒剃); m̄-sóng-khùai(毋爽快). *cross-bar*, mn̂g-tshùaⁿ(門閂); hûeⁿ-tshùaⁿ(橫閂). *cross-bow*, nãuⁿ(鬧). *cross-examine*, poh-mn̄g(駁問); mn̄g-lâi mn̄g-khṳ̀(問來問去); kháu-piẽn(口辯). *cross-eyed*, siâ-chiáu-ma̍k(斜朝目); tsho̍h-ma̍k〔〕; ma̍k-chiu tsho̍h-tsho̍h〔〕. *cross-legged*, phûan-khí-kha(盤起骹); phûan-thúi-tsõ(盤腿坐). *both legs crossed*, sang-kha phûan-khí(雙骹盤起). *cross-way*, hûeⁿ-lōu(橫路).

**croton**, *oil*, pa-tāu-iû(巴豆油).

**crouch**, phak(趴); khu(嶇); tshn̂g(床). *as tiger*, phak-tī(伏地).

**crow**, ou-a(烏鴉); ou-a-chiáu(烏鴉鳥). *cockcrow*, koi thî(雞啼). *the second*, koi thî jī-lo̍h(雞啼字落).

**curiosity**, mih-sṳ̄ àiⁿ-tsai(乜事愛知); hàuⁿ-thiaⁿ ôiⁿ-ūe(好聽閒話); hàuⁿ-kiú-tîⁿ(好究纏); kiú-tîⁿ-mn̄g(究纏問); tîⁿ-mn̄g(纏問). *curiosities*, kóu-ngúan(古玩); kóu-tóng(古董); thih-thô-mue̍h(鐵桃物).

**customer**, bói-kheh(買客). *to be a*, kau-kuan(交關); bói-bōi(買賣).

**cut**, kuah(割); tso̍ih(截); tok(剁); phoh(劈); tsám(斬); phoi(批). *off, as branch*, tsám-tiāu(斬掉); siah-tiāu(削掉). *to pieces*, tok tshùi-tshùi(斫碎碎). *in two*, kuah-tñg(割斷); tok-tñg(斫斷); tok-tsò-kue̍h(斫做橛); tso̍ih-tñg(截斷). *(on a slant)*, phoh-tñg(劈斷). *(split)*, lòi-tsò-pôiⁿ(𠠍做爿). *out clothes*, ka-saⁿ(鉸三). *away*, kuah--khṳ̀(割去); kuah-tiāu(割掉); tsám-tiāu(斬掉). *the hair*, chién-môⁿ(剪毛); ka-môⁿ(鉸毛). *a pencil*, phoi-pit(批筆). *down*, *as a tree*, tsám-tiāu(斬掉); khám-tiāu(砍掉). *thing across in a slanting direction*, phoi gû-tâng-tshùi(批牛筒碎); phoh-sia(劈斜). *cut the throat*, kṳ̀-âu(鋸喉). *cut grain*, kuah-tiũ(割稻). *grass*, kuah-tsháu(割草). *cut a friend*, nâng-chhêng kuah-tñg(人情割斷); tso̍h-kau(絕交); kuah-chhie̍h(割蓆); tso̍ih-tñg kau-chhêng(截斣交情). *cut away a mast*, tsám-ûi(斬圍). *cut a road*, khui-lōu(開路). *through a hill*, tsha̍k-suaⁿ-lōu(鑿山路). *cut wages*, khà-tṳ̂ kang-chîⁿ(扣除工錢); tṳ̂-kiám nâng-kâi-chîⁿ(除減人个錢). *cut-purse*, chién-niúⁿ(剪紐), kuah nâng hō-pau(割人荷包). *cut-throat*, hiong-chhiú(兇手).

**cutaneous**, to(刀); kiàm(劍).

**cutler**, phah-to sai-pẽ(拍刀司阜). *cutlery*, lāi-khì(利氣).

**cuttle-fish**, ba̍k-táu-hṳ̂(墨斗魚); ba̍k-táu(墨斗).

**cuttings**, ka-tshûn kâi pòu-tshùi(鉸賰个布碎); ka-sīn kâi-pòu-tshùi(鉸剩个布碎). *of sugar-cane*, chià-tsai(蔗渣). *of sweet potatoes*, tsṳ̂-tsai(薯渣).

**cycly**, *of 60 years*, la̍k-tsa̍p kah-tsṳ́(六十恰仔).

**cymbals**, khãm(鈸); chhẽ(鑔); khõm-chhẽ(欽鑔).

**cypress**, chek-peh-chhiū〔〕.

### D

**dabble**, *in water*, mak-tsúi(衊水); sn̍g-tsúi(算水). *learn superficially*, ēng m̄-kàu-kang(用毋夠工); chhién-ha̍k(淺學); tshó-lia̍k pat-lân-ló(草略八欄惱).

**dagger**, tó-kiàm(短劍).

**daily**, ji̍t-ji̍t(日日); múeⁿ-ji̍t(每日); pâi-ji̍t(排日); siêⁿ-ji̍t(常日); che̍k-ji̍t kùe-che̍k-ji̍t(一日過一日). *to make daily progress*, ji̍t kìⁿ-ji̍t-chìn(日見日進).

**dainties**, tien-siu peh-bī(點梳爬味).

**dam**, *water*, tsúi-tsa̍h(水閘). *to dam*, tsoh-toi(作堤).

**damage**, hāi(害); hāi--tie̍h(害着); hùi-hāi(毀害); hām-hāi(陷害); mue̍h-tiāu(物掉); sún-hāi(損害); sún--tie̍h(損着); sieⁿ-sún(傷損). *damaged goods*, tie̍h-tsúi-hùe(着水悔). *damaged in ship's hold*, ù--tie̍h pũn-tói(惡着笨底); tsṳ̀--tie̍h pũn-tói(漬着笨底).

**damask**, tōa-hue-tn̄g(大花緞).

**dame**, ke-bó(家母); lãu-bó(老母); a-náiⁿ(阿奶); a-niêⁿ(阿娘).

**damp**, ip-chi̍p(浥集); tâm(㴷); tâm-sip(澹濕); lùn-lùn(嫩嫩); tâm-lùn(濕嫩). *dampness*, sip-khì(濕氣).

**damsel**, kui-nn̍g(閨女); tsṳ-niêⁿ-kiáⁿ(諸娘囝); a-niêⁿ-kiáⁿ(阿娘囝); chhim-kui nn̍g-tsṳ́(深閨女子).

**dance**, *(and gesticulate)*, thiàu-bú(跳舞).

**dandle**, *(up and down)*, õng(擁). *(sideways)*, phõ-tõ-iê(抱在搖).

**dandruff**, thâu-khiú(頭垢).

**danger**, hong-hiám(風險); huang-hiám(風險); ngûi-hiám(危險). *come into danger*, lîm-ngûi(臨危); hiám-hiám-hāi(險險害); lím-lím-hāi(凜凜害). *dangerous person*, lĩ-hāi(厲害); iá(野).

**dangle**, iâu-tõng(搖動); tín-tãng(振動). *dangling down*, sûi-lo̍h(隨落).

**dare**, káⁿ(敢); káⁿ-tsò káⁿ-ûi(敢做敢爲); m̄-phàⁿ seⁿ-sí(毋怕生死). *how dare*, tsò-káⁿ(做敢); tsò-káⁿ-tng(做敢當). *I daresay*, káⁿ-sĩ(敢是). *daring*, ũ-táⁿ(有膽); ióng-káⁿ(勇敢); ũ-táⁿ-liãng(有膽量).

**dark**, àm(暗); ou-àm(烏暗). *it is getting dark*, ji̍t àiⁿ-àm(日愛暗); ji̍t àm(日暗). *dark night*, mêⁿ ou-àm(夜烏暗). *dark moonless night*, gue̍h-àm-mêⁿ(月暗夜). *dark clouds*, ou-hûn(烏雲). *dark mind*, sim àm(心暗). *colour*, chhim-sek(深色). *dark complexion*, mīn-sek ou(面色烏).

**darling**, *my*, uá-kâi-ne̍k(我个肉); uá-kâi sim-kuaⁿ(我个心肝); uá-kâi-miāⁿ(我个命); sieh-ne̍k(惜肉); sieh-miāⁿ-miāⁿ(惜命命).

**dart**, tó-chhieⁿ(短槍). *throw*, sái-tó-chhieⁿ(使短槍). *to dart out*, huh--chē-kiè tshut--lâi(欻些叫出來); thuh--chē-kiè tshut--lâi(腯些叫出來).

**dash**, *against*, tsuãng--tie̍h(撞着). *dash to pieces*, tsuãng-phùa(撞破); tsuãng-hāi(撞害). *on the ground*, kuàn--lo̍h-khṳ̀(摜落去); sek-tõ-tī(擲在地). *dash in the face*, tsuah i-kâi-mīn〔〕; phuah i-kâi-mīn(潑伊个面). *dash out writing*, tiám-tiāu-jī(點掉字).

**dastard**, bô-táⁿ(無膽); tò-thò-táⁿ(倒退膽); táⁿ khiap(膽怯); bun-táⁿ(蚊膽).

**date**, ji̍t-chí(日子); nîⁿ-ji̍t(年日). *to date a letter*, siá-ji̍t-chí(寫日子).

**date**, *fruit*, tsó(棗); pe̍h-tsó(白棗); âng-tsó(紅棗); ou-tsó(烏棗). *dried*, tsó-kuaⁿ(棗官).

**daub**, *with mud*, kôu-thôu(糊塗). *writing*, tôu-buah(塗抹); tôu-tiāu(塗掉); buah-tiāu(抹掉); tiám-tiāu(點掉).

**daughter**, tsṳ-niêⁿ-kiáⁿ(諸娘囝); tsáu-kiáⁿ(走囝); nn̍g-tsṳ́(女子). *your daughter (polite)*, lẽng-ài(走囝); tshoiⁿ-kim(走囝). *my daughter (polite)*, sié-nn̍g(小女). *in law*, sim-pũ(新婦). *daughter's husband*, kiáⁿ-sài(囝婿). *daughter's chidren*, gūa-sun(外孫). *his daughter is betrothed*, i kâi tsṳ-niêⁿ-kiáⁿ íⁿ-keng tsò-sêng--liáu(伊个諸娘囝已經做成了). *marry one's d. to anyone*, tsṳ-niêⁿ-kiáⁿ kè--pun-nâng(諸娘囝嫁分人).

**daunt**, phièn-nâng-kiaⁿ(騙人[訓]驚); heh(嚇); kiaⁿ-heh(驚嚇); heh-kiaⁿ(嚇驚).

**dawn**, thiⁿ kng(天光); tang-pôiⁿ pe̍h(東爿白); tang-pôiⁿ tsò-sek(東爿作色); thiⁿ lâ-lân〔〕; thiⁿ lâ-lân-kng〔〕.

**day**, ji̍t(日); thiⁿ(添). *first day of month*, chhiu-it(初一). *15th day*, tsa̍p-ngõu(十五). *another day*, ẽ-ji̍t(下日); ãu-ji̍t(後日). *every*, ji̍t-ji̍t(日日); múeⁿ-ji̍t(每日); siêⁿ-ji̍t(常日); pâi-ji̍t(排日). *day and night*, ji̍t-mêⁿ(日夜). *all day*, tsong-ji̍t(終日); thàng-ji̍t(通日). *day before yesterday*, tso̍h--ji̍t(昨日). *one day earlier still*, tōa-tso̍h--ji̍t(大昨日). *day after tomorrow*, ãu--ji̍t(後日). *today*, kim-ji̍t(今日); kiáⁿ-ji̍t(今旦日); hīn-ji̍t(現日); pn̍g-ji̍t(憑日). *day by day*, che̍k-ji̍t kùe-che̍k-ji̍t(一日過一日); liên-ji̍t(連日). *to make progress day by day*, che̍k-ji̍t kìⁿ-ji̍t-chìn(一日見日進). *to wait day after day*, che̍k-ji̍t mōⁿ-che̍k-ji̍t(一日望一日). *day-time*, ji̍t--kan(日間); ji̍t--kùa(日旰); pe̍h-ji̍t--kan(白日間); ji̍t--tsṳ́(日子). *several days*, kúi-ji̍t(幾日); sù-ji̍t(四日); kúi-uã-ji̍t(幾外日). *within these few days*, chí-kṳ̃n-ji̍t(此近日); chí-kṳ̃n-ji̍t-lãi(此近日內). *day-labour*, lũn-ji̍t-kang(論日工). *day-book*, ji̍t-to̍k-phõu(日讀簿). *day-break*, see **dawn**. *to select a lucky day*, thóiⁿ-ji̍t(睇日); to̍h-ji̍t(擇日); suán-ji̍t(選日); pua̍h-ji̍t(跋日). *lucky day*, kit-ji̍t(吉日); siãng-ji̍t(上日). *unlucky*, hiong-ji̍t(凶日). *good-day(at meeting)*, hó-ngõ(好日). *good-day(at parting)*, chhiaⁿ(請).

**dazzle**, ji̍t-kuang iàng-ma̍k(日光映目); kng chhiēⁿ-ma̍k(光搶目). *the lamp-light dazzling the eyes*, teng-kng chhiēⁿ-ma̍k(燈光搶目). *dazzling*, tāng-tāng-kng(洞洞光); ia̍p-ia̍p-sih(灼灼熠).

**deacon**, chip-sṳ̄(執事).

**dead**, sí(死). *man*, sí-nâng(死人). *body*, sin-si(身屍); si-hâi(屍骸); si-siú(屍首). *he is dead*, kùe-sì--liáu(過四了); sî-sì--liáu(時四了); sí--khṳ̀(死去). *dead tree*, chhiū kou-ta(樹枯灱). *dead drunk*, tsùi kàu--mîⁿ-mîⁿ(醉到糜糜); tsùi kàu hun-hun mîⁿ-mîⁿ(醉到昏昏糜糜). *among the dead*, im--kan(陰間); àm--thâu(暗頭). *deadly poison*, ta̍k(毒); ta̍k-sí-nâng(毒死人). *deadly hatred*, put-kāng tài-thiⁿ kâi-chhiû(不同戴天之讎).

**deaf**, hĩⁿ lâng(耳聾). *slightly*, hĩⁿ se-su-kiáⁿ-lâng(耳些輸囝籠). *deafening*, hĩⁿ-khang-kúi ōng-ōng-kiè(耳空鬼訇訇叫). *pretend to be deaf and dumb*, tèⁿ-lâng tèⁿ-é(詐籠詐啞); tsuang-lâng tsuang-é(裝籠裝啞); tèⁿ-tsò thiaⁿ-m̄-kìⁿ(詐做聽毋見); tèⁿ-lâng tèⁿ-sat(詐籠詐蝨).

**deal**, *trade*, bói-bōi(買賣); tsò-seng-lí(做生理); kau-e̍k(交易); kau-kuan(交關). *a good deal*, hoh-tsōi(酷㩼). *deal well with any one*, hó-khúan-thãi(好款待); kãu-thãi(厚待). *a deal board*, che̍k-kò-pang(一塊枋); che̍k-phièn-pang(一片枋); che̍k-liàm-pang(一捻枋).

**dear**, *expensive*, kùi(貴); ta̍t-chîⁿ(值錢); kau-kè(高價); kûiⁿ-kè(懸價). *dear friend*, siãng-hó kâi-phêng-iú(上好个朋友); sim-pak kâi-phêng-iú(心腹个朋友); ti-kí kâi-phêng-iú(知己个朋友); ti-sim kâi-phêng-iú(知心个朋友).

**dearth**, ki-hng(饑荒); bí kùi(米貴); nîⁿ--tang m̄-hó(年冬毋好).

**death**, sí(死). *life and death are decreed*, seⁿ-sí ũ-mẽng(生死有命). *near death*, lîm-tsong(臨終); kṳ̃n-sí(近死); chiang-sí(將死); chiang-kṳ̃n àiⁿ-sí(將近愛死); lîm-sí(臨死). *on one's deathbed*, tó-tshn̂g(倒床). *death-like*, chhin-chhiẽⁿ sí-nâng kâi-iēⁿ(親像死人个樣).

**debar**, kìm-chí(禁子); kìm-kài(禁戒); tsó-chí(阻止); m̄-tsún(毋準); put-hṳ́(不許).

**debark**, chiẽⁿ-suaⁿ(上山); khí-tsúi(起水); chiẽⁿ-tsúi(上水).

**debase**, *oneself*, tshap-ji̍p hiã-liû(插入下流); kàng-lo̍h hiã-liû(降落下流); u-tsūaⁿ hiã-liû(污賤下流).

**debate**, ngí-lũn(議論); piẽn-lũn(辯論); piẽn-poh(辯駁). *in one's own mind*, pheⁿ-phah(斟酌); chim-chiak(斟酌); tsham-siâng(參詳).

**debauch**, tiam-u(沾污); îm nâng chhi-nn̍g(淫人痴女); îm nâng bóu-kiáⁿ(淫人牡囝).

**debauchee**, chiú-sek tsṳ-thû(酒色之徒). *debauchery*, chia̍h-pua̍h-phiâu(食跋嫖).

**debility**, hṳ-jia̍k(虛弱); nn̍g-jia̍k(軟弱); khùn-jia̍k(困弱); hṳ-khùn(虛困); sin-hūn phàⁿ(身分冇); hueh-khì put-tsok(血氣不足); hueh-khì sue-jia̍k(血氣衰弱).

**debt**, chè(債); chîⁿ-chè(錢債). *to be in debt*, khiàm-chîⁿ(欠錢); khiàm-chè(欠債); khiàm-siàu(欠數). *to pay debts*, hôiⁿ-chè(還債); hôiⁿ--nâng(還人). *debtor and creditor*, chè-kiáⁿ chè-tsú(債囝債主). *collect debts*, thó-siàu(討數). *absconding debtor*, tô-chè(逃債); pī-chè(避債); tsáu-chè(走債). *bad debts*, phàⁿ-siàu(怕數).

**decade**, sûn(旬). *first 10 days of month*, tsho-sûn(初旬); chhiu--sûn(秋旬); *second ditto*, tong-sûn(東旬); tsa̍p--sûn(十旬). *third ditto*, hiã-sûn(下旬); ji̍h--sûn(廿旬).

**decalogue**, tsa̍p-tiâu-kài(十條戒).

**decamp**, chhien-iâⁿ(遷贏); î-iâⁿ(移贏); súa-iâⁿ(徙營). *run away*, tô-tsáu(逃走); thau-tsáu(逃走).

**decanter**, *po-lî-tsun*, po-lî-kùan(玻璃罐).

**decapitate**, thâi-thâu(刣頭); tsám-thâu(斬頭); tsám-siú(斬首); tshú-tsám(取斬).

**decay**, sue(衰); sue-mûiⁿ(衰微). *rot*, àu(懊); àu-tshàu(懊臭). *decayed tooth*, tsù-khí(蛀起).

**decease**, kùe-sì(過世); kùe-sin(過身). *deceased parents*, kháu-pí(口比). *my deceased father*, lẽng-soiⁿ-kháu(令先口); lẽng-soiⁿ-tsun(令先尊).

**deceit**, kan-tsà(奸詐); khũi-kòi(詭計); kan-kòi(奸計); khũi-phièn(詭騙); kuang-phièn(誆騙). *(in trade)*, tshuah(絀). *deception*, ké-sṳ̄(假事); mûaⁿ-mâng-ma̍k(瞞盲目); iám-sek(掩飾).

**decency**, ha̍h-lí(合理); ha̍h-sek(合適). *decent*, hiáu-lí(曉理).

**decide**, kuat-tùan(決斷); tiāⁿ-tie̍h(定着); tsú-ì(主意); li̍p-tiāⁿ tsú-ì(立定主意). *decided*, kuat-ì(決意); che̍k-kuat(一決); kuat-tùan(決斷); ũ-tsú-ì(有主意); ũ-tsú-kièn(有主見); ũ-tiāⁿ-kièn(有定見); ũ-pá-thî(有飽啼). *legal decision*, kuat-tùan ùaⁿ-kiãⁿ(決斷案件).

**decimate**, tsa̍p-hūn thiu-che̍k(十分抽一).

**deck**, *ship's*, tsûn-mīn(船面); pũn-mīn(笨面). *adorn*, siu-tsuang(修裝); tá-pàn(打扮); tsuang-sek(裝飾); tsuang-tshái(裝彩); pái-tshái(擺彩); tsuang-pái(裝擺). see **decorate**.

**declaration**, *official*, hiáu-zũ(曉諭); kò-sī(告示).

**declare**, káng-mêng(講明); tàⁿ-mêng-pe̍h(呾明白).

**decline**, *sun to West*, ji̍t siâ-sai(日斜西). *grow weaker*, sue-mûiⁿ(衰微); khuaⁿ-khuaⁿ sue-jia̍k(寬寬衰弱). *refuse*, m̄-tsún(毋準); tho-khui(推開); tho-sî(推辭); m̄-ngũan(毋願); put-hṳ́(不許). *invitation*, chhiáⁿ-sî(請辭); sî-siā(辭謝); kiong-sî-siā(恭辭謝). *a present*, piah-siā(劈謝). *receiving visitors*, sî-m̄-kìⁿ(時毋見); sî-m̄-kìⁿ-mīn(時毋見面). *receiving visitors (not "at home")*, tho-m̄-tõ(叨毋在).

**declivity**, pho-lo-sia(陂咯斜).

**decoct**, pû-ie̍h(煲藥); chien-ie̍h(煎藥). *decoction*, ie̍h-thng(藥湯); ie̍h-tê(藥茶).

**decorate**, tá-pàn(打扮); siu-tsuang(梳妝); siu-si̍p phâi-chhiâng(收拾排場); siu-si̍p hó-thóiⁿ(收拾好睇); siu-si̍p-ngiá(收拾雅); siu-si̍p kuang-tshái(收拾光彩); iām-lĩ(豔麗). see **deck**.

**decorous**, tuan-chiàⁿ(端正); hẽng-chí tuan-chiàⁿ(行止端正); ũ-thí-mīn(有體面). *decorum*, lói-ngî(禮儀); kui-kṳ́(規矩).

**decoy**, *ín-iú; iú-ho̍k*, phièn nâng ji̍p-io̍k(騙人入慾); iú-phièn(誘騙). *decoy-bird*, chiáu-bûe(鳥媒). see **abduct**.

**decrease**, húan-kiám(反減); chiãm-chiãm-kiám(漸漸減); siau-si̍h(消蝕); sue-mûiⁿ(衰微).

**decree**, mẽng-lẽng(命令). *Emperor's*, siãng-zũ(上諭). *heaven's*, thien-mẽng(天命). *issue a decree*, tshut-zũ(出諭); thûan-mẽng(傳命).

**decrepit**, khì-hueh sue(氣血衰); kiu tsò-che̍k-tu(龜做一坨); sok tsò-che̍k-pé(束做一把).

**dedicate**, hõng(奉); kèng-hõng(敬奉). *an idol*, an-sîn(安神); uaⁿ-sîn(還神); uaⁿ-sîn-ūi(還神位); an-kham(庵堪).

**deduce**, tshui-lũn(推論); tshui zṳ̂-lũn--tsṳ(推挐論姿).

**deduct**, khà-tṳ̂(扣除); khà-kiám(扣減); tṳ̂-kiám(除減).

**deed**, *action*, sṳ̄(事); hêng-ûi(行爲); kiâⁿ-sṳ̄(行事). *written*, khòi(契).

**deem**, siẽⁿ(想). *to deem it insufficient*, thóiⁿ-tsò m̄-kàu(睇做毋夠); íⁿ-ûi put-tsok(以爲不足).

**deep**, chhim(深); chhim-tîm(深沉). *the deep*, chhim-uan(深灣); chhim-thâm(深潭). *deep thought*, chhim-sṳ(深思); chhim-siẽⁿ(深想). *deep colour*, chhim-sek(深色); sek-tsúi chhim(色水深). *dig deep*, liú-chhim(㧕深). *deeply learned*, ha̍k-mn̄g chhim(學問深); tsṳ-lí chhim(書理深). *deep voise*, siaⁿ lô-lô(聲囉囉); tàⁿ-ūe o-o-kiè(呾話嘔嘔叫). *deeply absorbed in anything*, ji̍p-sîn(入神). *a deep and dangerous fellow*, im-thim-hāi〔〕.

**deer**, te̍k(鹿). *sinews*, te̍k-kṳn(鹿筋). *horns*, te̍k-zông(鹿茸). *musk-deer*, siā-káu(麝狗).

**deface**, mue̍h-tiāu(物掉); tôu-tiāu(塗掉); buah-tiāu(抹掉); kôu-tiāu(糊掉).

**defalcation**, khui-khòng(開空); sái-khòng(使空).

**defamation**, pù-lũ〔〕; húiⁿ-pãng(誹謗); bû-lūa(誣賴); u nâng miâⁿ-sek(污人名色).

**default**, sit-tshò(失錯); kùe-sit(過失); khiàm-khueh(欠缺); tshò-gōu(錯誤); khueh-hua̍t(缺乏).

**despond**, sit-mōⁿ(失望); sit-chì(失志).

**destined**, tiāⁿ-tie̍h(定着); ṳ̃-soiⁿ tiāⁿ-tie̍h(預先定着); ũ-thien-mẽng(有天命); ũ-mẽng(有命).

**destiny**, *miāⁿ*, miāⁿ-ūn(命運); seⁿ-sêng(生成). *evil*, khóu-miāⁿ(苦命).

**destitute**, lo̍h-po̍h(落薄); khueh-hua̍t(缺乏); phîn-hua̍t(貧乏); bô-chia̍h bô-chhēng(無食無穿); kêng(窮); phîn-khiông(貧窮); khiau(磽); khiau-kêng(磽窮).

**destroy**, pāi-hũai(敗壞); pāi-hāi(敗害); hùi-tiāu(廢掉); hùi-hũai(毀壞); húiⁿ-tiāu(毀掉); hùi-tũi(廢墜); tshau-mi̍t(抄滅). *destruciton*, mi̍t-buâng(滅亡); pāi-buâng(敗亡).

**detach**, thiah-khui(拆開). *(as different persons to different pieces of work)*, hun-buah(分抹).

**detain**, lâu(留); tau-lâu(逗留); lâu-tsũ(留住); lâu-kiâⁿ(留行); tam-koh(耽擱). *as guest*, lâu--nâng chia̍h-pn̄g(留人食飯); lâu-nāⁿ-kò chia̍h〔〕. *by force*, khiâng-lâu(強留); ngẽ-lâu(硬留).

**detect**, thóiⁿ-phùa(睇破); tshūe--tie̍h(覓着); siau--tie̍h(消着); chhê--tshut(查出); lia̍h(掠).

**deter**, tuah-thò(叱退); kéng-kài(警誡); kìm-kài(禁誡); kàu-kài(告誡); tsó-chí(阻止); tsó-têⁿ(阻瞪). *(by threats)*, heh-thò(嚇退).

**determine**, tsú-ì(主意); li̍p-sim(立心); li̍p-ì(立意); li̍p-tiāⁿ tsú-ì(立定主意); tiāⁿ-chì(定志); tiāⁿ-tie̍h(定着).

**detest**, lóu(惱); ù(惡); chhim-lóu(深惱). *detestable*, khó-ù(可惡).

**develope**, huat-hīn(發現); lòu-hīn(露現); khai-huat(開發).

**deviate**, kiâⁿ-tshúa(行歪); tsáu-tsua̍h(走絀); sit-gōu(失誤); kiâⁿ-tāⁿ-lōu(行賺路). *from right principle*, lī-khui chiàⁿ-tãu(離開正道).

**device**, kòi(計); sim-sṳ̄(心事); kòi-chheh(計策). *devise*, siet-kòi(設計); phah-sǹg(拍算).

**devil**, môⁿ-kúi(魔鬼); kúi(鬼).

**devious**, kiâⁿ-tāⁿ-lōu(行賺路); tsáu-tshò-lōu(走錯路).

**devoid**, bô(無). *of reason*, bô-chhêng-lí(無情理); bô-tõ-lí(無道理).

**devoted**, tsuan-sim(專心); zua̍h-sim(熱心). *to duty*, chĩn-tong(盡忠); tong-ngĩ(忠義).

**devour**, *thun*, thun-chia̍h(吞食).

**dial**, ji̍t-kui(日規).

**dialogue**, mn̄g-tap(問答); phue̍h-ūe(詖話). see CONVERSATION.

**diameter**, tong-sùaⁿ(中線); thàu-tong ti̍t-sùaⁿ(透中直線).

**diamond**, sūan-chie̍h(鏇石). *a glazier's*, sūan-pit(鏇筆).

**diaphanous**, kuang thàu-tit-kùe(光透得過).

**diarrhoea**, sià-tóu(瀉肚); làu-tóu(澇肚); làu-sái(澇使); tóu m̄-hó(肚毋好); pàng-tóu(放肚). *and vomiting*, thòu-sià(吐瀉).

**diary**, hêng-ûi-phõu(行爲簿); ji̍t-kì-lo̍k(日記錄).

**dice**, tâu-kiáⁿ(骰囝); kut-tâu(骨骰). *dice box*, tâu-kiáⁿ-a̍p(骰囝盒). *gamble with dice*, pua̍h-tâu-kiáⁿ(跋骰囝). *loaded dice*, kùan-în-tâu(罐鉛骰).

**dictate**, hun-hù(吩咐); mẽng-lẽng(命令). *write to my dictation*, uá-liām lṳ́-siá(我念汝寫).

**dictionary**, jī-tién(字典); jī-lūi(字類). *rhyming*, si-ūn(詩韻); kiám-ūn(減韻).

**die**, *to*, sí(死); kùe-sì(過世); sī-sì(去世); khùi tñg(氣斷); lãu--khṳ̍(老去); tsak-kóu(作古). see **decease**. *by one's own hand*, tsṳ̃-shĩn(自盡). *of disease*, pēⁿ-sí(病死). *of hunger*, gō-sí(餓死). *of cold*, kûaⁿ-sí(寒死).

**die**, *a*, chîⁿ-bôu(錢模); jī-bôu(字模).

**diet**, *to*, *as sick person*, khiēⁿ-tshùi(疆喙); kài-kháu(戒口).

**differ**, ũ-hun-pie̍t(有分別); õi-koh-iēⁿ(會各樣); m̄-sie-tâng(毋相同); m̄-pêⁿ-iēⁿ(毋平樣); m̄-che̍k-iēⁿ(毋一樣); m̄-chhin-chhiẽⁿ(毋親像). *slightly*, tsua̍h-m̄-ũa(差毋嘩); tsua̍h-m̄-hñg(差毋恨); tsua̍h hun-hun(絀紛紛); tãi-tâng siáu-ĩ(大同小異); tsha-m̄-to(差毋多). *to quarrel*, seⁿ-hiâm-khiah(生嫌隙); kāng-nâng ũ-ūe(共人有話). *make up a difference*, thiâu-ti̍t(調直); thiâu-hûa(調和).

**difficult**, oh(僫); lân(攔); kan-khóu(艱苦); bô-hièⁿ-kōi(無向易). *there are no difficulties in the world if you are only in earnest*, thiⁿ-ẽ bô-lân-sṳ̄(天下無難事), chí-phàⁿ sim-put-tsuan(只怕心不專).

**diffidence**, sim gî(心疑); m̄-káⁿ-sìn(毋敢信).

**diffuse**, *spread*, kúang-pù(廣佈); kúang-pùa(廣播); pùa-iâng(播揚); suang-iâng(宣揚); suan-pù(宣布). *not concise*, khui-khuah(開闊); seⁿ-ūe-sái(生話駛); seⁿ-ūe-phûe(生話皮); tàⁿ-ūe seⁿ-ki seⁿ-hie̍h(呾話生枝生葉); seⁿ-ūe-ki(生話枝); seⁿ-ūe-tsat(生話節); ūe seⁿ-ki-tsat(話生枝節); huàm(泛).

**dig**, ku̍t(掘); liú(㧕); ku̍t-thôu(掘塗).

**dignity**, ui-hong(威風); ui-hong lím-lím(威風凜凜).

**dilatory**, tũaⁿ(惰); mān(慢); în-tîⁿ(延停); kau-tîⁿ-lâi kau-tîⁿ-khṳ̍(交纏來交纏去); thû-mān(遲慢).

**diligent**, ēng-kang(用工); khṳ̂n-kang(勤工); khṳ̂n(勤); tsuan-kang(專工); la̍t-kang(力工); tshut-la̍t(出力).

**dill**, sié-hûe(小茴); hûe-hieⁿ(茴香). *water*, hûe-hieⁿ-tsúi(茴香水).

**dilute**, thàu-po̍h(透薄); thàu-tsúi(透水); tshong-tsúi(沖水); tshong-po̍h(沖薄).

**dim**, àm(暗); sit-kng m̄-hīn(息光毋現); bū-bū(霧霧). *dim-sighted*, ma̍k-chiu hue(目睭花); ma̍k hue(目花); ma̍k bū(目霧). *grow dim*, *as picture*, hùe--khṳ̍(化去). *dimly seen*, ṳ́n-ṳ́n iak-iak(隱隱約約).

**diminish**, kiám(減); tṳ̂-kiám(除減); khà-kiám(扣減); kiám-chié(減少). *the population, as epidemic*, kiám-nâng-kháu(減人口).

**dimity**, siâ-bûn-pòu(斜紋布).

**dimple**, *in chin*, ẽ-hâi-tsuh(下頦嘬). *in cheeks*, chiú-tsuh(酒窩).

**din**, *of gongs and drums*, kong-kuang-kiè(公光叫); kong-kong-kiè(公公叫).

**dine**, chia̍h-tōa-tn̍g(食大場); chia̍h mêⁿ-àm-pn̄g(食暗夜飯). *at noon*, chia̍h-ji̍t-tàu(食日晝).

**dip**, *into water*, ùn-tsúi(揾水); ùn-tâm(揾濕). *hot iron in water*, chhih-tsúi(彳水). *dip up water (with ladle)*, ēng-pû-hia lâi-ié-tsúi(用煲桸來舀水). *dip up water (from well)*, ēng pua̍h-tháng lâi kũaⁿ-tsúi(用跋桶來摜水). *dip up water (with bucket & well-sweep)*, ēng tiàu-o lâi-tiàu-tsúi(用吊嘔來吊水). *dip up water (with ladle having long handle)*, ēng hòu-táu lâi-hòu-tsúi(用戽斗來戽水). *a dipper*, tsúi-kóng(水管).

**diploma**, bûn-phêng(文憑); bûn-pêng(文憑).

**direct**, ti̍t(直); ti̍t-ti̍t(直直). *direct route*, ti̍t-lōu(直路). *directly*, khùn-kiáⁿ(頃囝); sûi-sî(隨時); sûi-chiet(隨即). *I will come directly after you*, úa sûi-ãu chiũ-lâi(我隨後就來). *to direct*, chí-ín(指引). *order*, hun-hù(吩咐); mẽng(命). *control*, kúan-lí(管理); kúan(管). *a letter*, siá-huang-phûe(寫方皮). *directions*, mẽng-lẽng(命令); kui-tiâu(規條).

**dirt**, nah-sap(垃圾); lâm-sap〔〕. *dirty*, nah-sap(垃圾); nah-sap-sièⁿ(垃圾相); o-tso(污糟); u-ùe(污穢); m̄-chheng-khih(毋清潔); m̄-chheng-kiet(毋清潔); o-lâm o-lī〔〕. *to dirty*, mak--tie̍h nah-sap(衊着垃圾); hú--tie̍h nah-sap(拊着垃圾).

**disabled**, hùi-chi̍t(廢疾); phùa-sièⁿ(破相); hùi-jîn(廢人).

**disadvantage**, si̍h-pńg(蝕本); m̄-piẽn(毋便); m̄-sũn(毋順); bô-iah(無益); siũ-khui(受虧).

**disagree**, m̄-hûa(毋和); m̄-ha̍h(毋合); m̄-siang-ha̍h(毋相合); m̄-tùi(毋對). *the climate disagrees with me*, m̄-ho̍k tsúi-thóu(毋服水土); chia̍h-m̄-tie̍h tsúi-thóu(食毋着水土). *disagreeable*, bô-mih tshù-bī(無乜趣味); tshūa-nâng-lóu(𤆬人惱). *disagreeable (unsociable)*, kou-ta̍k(毋合). *disagreeable (sensation)*, kãu-ue̍h(垢穢).

**disappear**, m̄-kìⁿ(毋見); sit-lo̍h(失落); bô--khṳ̀(無去).

**disapprove**, m̄-huaⁿ-hí(毋歡喜); m̄-ha̍h-ì(毋合意); m̄-tsún(毋準).

**disaster**, hiong-sṳ̄(凶事); tsai-iang(災殃); hũa(禍); tsai-hũa(災禍); hũa-tsai(禍災); bô-tsãu-hùe(無造化).

**disburse**, tshut-chîⁿ(出錢).

**discard**, m̃-ēng(毋用); pàng-tiāu(放掉); sî-tiāu(辭掉); sî-tù(辭著).

**discern**, thóiⁿ-tshut(睇出); thóiⁿ-tit-tshut(睇得出). *discernment*, tì-hũi(智慧); tì-sek(知識); kièn-sek(見識); tshong-mêng(聰明). *quick*, ũ-mién-tshâi(有敏才).

**discharge**, *servant*, sî(時); màiⁿ(勿); m̃-ēng(毋用); keh-tiāu(革掉). *a prisoner*, sek-pàng(釋放). *cargo*, khí-hùe(起貨). *duty*, chĩn-pńg-hūn(盡本分). *an account*, khou-tiāu-siàu(箍掉數).

**disciple**, mn̂g-seng(門生); ha̍k-seng(學生); tĩ-tsṳ́(弟子); mn̂g-thû(門徒).

**disclaim**, m̃-jīn(毋認); tho-m̄-tsai(叨毋知). *praise*, khiam-sî(謙時).

**disclose**, lòu-tshut(露出); sia̍p-lāu ki-kuan(洩漏機關); tshut-phùa(出破).

**discoloured**, sek m̄-tsâ(色毋巢)u; lo̍h-sek(落色); thò-sek(退色); sit-sek(失色); sek lut(色脫); sià-sek(褪色).

**discomfort**, m̄-khùaⁿ-ua̍h(毋寬活); kãu-ue̍h(垢穢); m̄-uaⁿ-sim(毋安心); sim-tang khau-peh(心胸嘔白).

**discontented**, m̄-kùe-î(毋過怡); m̄-tsai-tsok(毋知足); uàn-miāⁿ-khiap(怨命怯); uàn-miāⁿ-po̍h(怨命薄).

**discontinue**, hiah(歇).

**discord**, m̄-hûa(毋和); m̄-thiâu-hûa(毋調和); bô-siang chia̍h-chi̍h(無相食折); bô-chiap-chi̍h(無接折); m̄-hûa-mo̍k(毋和睦).

**discount**, póu-ngṳ̂n-tsúi(補銀水); thiap-ngṳ̂n-tsúi(貼銀水); khà-lāi-chîⁿ(扣裡錢). *(brokerage)*, thiu-thâu-ngṳ̂n(抽頭銀). *for ready money*, hīn-chîⁿ kiám-kè(現錢減價).

**discourage**, phièn nâng sàng-táⁿ(騙人喪膽); hāi nâng sàng-táⁿ(害人送膽). *discouraged*, sàng-táⁿ(喪膽); bô-táⁿ(無膽); siẽⁿ-tie̍h ià-ià(想着厭厭); siẽⁿ-tie̍h ià-sîn(想着厭神).

**discourse**, káng-lũn(講論); káng-tãu(講道).

**discourteous**, bô-lói(無禮); m̄-hiáu chhêng-lí(毋曉情理).

**discover**, chhê-tshut(查出); thóiⁿ-tshut(睇出); thóiⁿ-phùa(睇破); phùa-sṳ̄(破事); tshūe--tie̍h(覓着); chhîm--tie̍h(尋着). *have a clue to*, ũ-sùaⁿ-soh(有線索).

**discreet**, ũ-kièn-sek(有見識); kṳ́n-sín(謹慎); kṳ́n-sim(謹心); tsṳ́-sòi(仔細); sié-sim(小心); ũ-tì-hũi(有智慧); tîm-tieh(沉着).

**discriminate**, hun-pie̍t(分別); hun-lūi(分類); sòi-siâng hun-pie̍t(細詳分別).

**discuss**, piẽn-lũn(辯論); ngí-lũn(議論); káng-lũn(講論); thâm-lũn(談論); lũn-sṳ̄(論事); káng-kiù(講究).

**disdain**, thóiⁿ-khin(睇輕); thóiⁿ-m̄-chiẽⁿ(睇毋上); miáuⁿ-sĩ(渺視); thóiⁿ-m̄-chiẽⁿ-ma̍k(睇毋上目); lia̍h--nâng iàm-khì(掠人厭棄). *disdainful*, thóiⁿ-nâng m̄-tõ-ma̍k(睇人毋在目); ma̍k-khang khuah(目空闊).

**disease**, pēⁿ(病); mâuⁿ-pēⁿ(毛病); pēⁿ-thiàⁿ(病痛); pēⁿ-chèng(病症). *chronic*, kú-tn̂g-pēⁿ(久長病); kú-chi̍t(久疾). *have disease*, ũ-pēⁿ(有病); tì-pēⁿ(致病); phùa-pēⁿ(破病). *cure*, ui-pēⁿ(醫病). *diagnosis of*, jīn-pēⁿ(認病). *eye-disease*, ma̍k-chiu thiàⁿ(目睭痛).

**disembark**, chiẽⁿ-suaⁿ(上山); khí-tsúi(起水); chiẽⁿ-tsúi(上水).

**disembogue**, thàng-hái(通海).

**disencumber**, kói(解). *of burden*, hiah-tàⁿ(歇擔). *of clothing*, thǹg-tiāu(褪掉).

**disengaged**, bô-sṳ̄(無事); ôiⁿ(閒).

**disentangle**, kói(解); kói-kat(解結).

**disgorge**, thòu(吐); thòu--tshut(吐出).

**dollar**, ngṳ̂n(銀). *Spanish*, hu̍t-thâu(佛頭); hu̍t-ngṳ̂n(佛銀). *Mexican*, chiáu ngṳ̂n(鳥銀); chhì-kiû-chiáu(刺球鳥). *one*, che̍k-kâi-ngṳ̂n(一個銀); che̍k-khou ngṳ̂n(一箍銀). *$10,000*, che̍k-būan-ngṳ̂n(一萬銀); che̍k-tsháu-ngṳ̂n(一草銀). *$̃0*, che̍k-huang-ngṳ̂n(一風銀).

**dolt**, ngâ nâng(呆人); chhi-ko(痴哥); khòng-ngōng(悾戇).

**domestic**, ke-lãi(家內). *servants*, ke-jîn(家人); kṳn-pan(跟班). *animals*, cheng-seⁿ(眾牲). *affairs*, ke-bũ(家務). *circumstances*, ke-sṳ̄(家事); ke-chhêng(家情).

**domesticate**, chhī-se̍k(飼熟); chhī-sûn-se̍k(飼馴熟).

**dominoes**, kut-pâi(骨牌).

**done**, tso hó(做好); hó--liáu(好了). *exhausted*, liáu(了); ēng-liáu(用了). *done with a meal*, chia̍h-pá--liáu(食飽了).

**doom**, tiaⁿ-tsũe(定罪); sún-tùan(損斷); ngí-tiāⁿ tsũe-miâⁿ(議定罪名).

**door**, mn̂g(門). *bolt*, mn̂g-tshùaⁿ(門閂). *bolt the door*, tshùaⁿ-mn̂g(閂門), pi mn̂g(埤門). *shut the door*, kueⁿ-mn̂g(關門). *not quite close*, mn̂g hoiⁿ(門開). *door-bar*, mn̂g-chhēng(門拴). *keep a door*, chiéⁿ-mn̂g(掌門); siú-mn̂g(守門); kuan-mn̂g(關門); pé-mn̂g(把門). *door-posts*, mn̂g-thiãu(門柱). *door-frame*, mn̂g-khuan(門框). *lintel*, mn̂g-bâi(門楣). *socket*, mn̂g-khũ(門臼). *handle*, mn̂g-tsu(門珠). *threshold*, mn̂g-tõiⁿ(門第).

**dose**, che̍k-thiap-ie̍h(一帖藥); che̍k-ho̍k-ie̍h(一服藥).

**dot**, che̍k-tiám(一點).

**dotard**, láu-kàu-ngo̍h(老到愕); láu-kàu-thūe(老到退).

**dote**, ne̍k-ài(溺愛); liẽn-sieh(憐惜).

**double**, sang(雙). *to double*, kia-pũe(加倍). *folds of cloth*, sang-têng(雙重). *to double up, as cloth*, chih--khí-lâi(折起來). *double-chin*, ẽ-hâi thō-thō(下骸佗佗); ẽ-hâi lô-tō lô-tō(下骸羅袋羅袋). *double-dealer*, che̍k-mīn-to nõⁿ-mīn-sái(一面刀兩面使). *double-meaning*, sang-thám-ūe(雙貪話); sang-kuan liáng-ì(雙關兩意). *double price*, ke-che̍k-ûe-chîⁿ(加一半錢). *double-barrelled gun*, sang-hiáng-chhèng(雙響銃).

**doublet**, sin-tói-saⁿ(身底衫); kín-sin-saⁿ(緊身衫).

**doubt**, gî(疑); gî-tshai(疑猜); tshai-gî(猜疑); gî-thûan(疑團). *doubtless*, mín-gî(免疑); tiāⁿ-tie̍h(定着); kúaⁿ-jiên(果然). *doubtful*, bô-tiāⁿ-tie̍h(無定着); húang-hut bô-tiāⁿ(恍惚無定).

**dough**, mīⁿ-kàⁿ(麵酵); kàⁿ-mīⁿ(酵麵). *to knead*, chhi̍p-mīⁿ〔〕; na̍k-kàⁿ(搦酵).

**doughty**, ióng-káⁿ(勇敢); ũ-táⁿ-la̍t(有膽力); eng-hiông(英雄); hó-hàn(好漢).

**dove**, hún-chiáu(粉鳥); kũ-ku(咕咕). *dovecot*, hún-chiáu-tàu(粉鳥竇).

**dovetail**, kau-chí-sún(交指筍); tāu-sún(豆筍).

**dowdy**, tshou-hũ(粗婦); lah-tah tsṳ-niêⁿ(邋遢諸娘).

**down**, hiã(下); lo̍h(落); kẽ(下). *down on the ground*, tõ-thôu-ẽ(在塗下). *down-stairs*, lâu-ẽ(樓下). *down-hill*, lo̍h-suaⁿ(落山). *down below*, tõ-ẽ-pôiⁿ(兜下平). *go far down*, lo̍h kẽ-kẽ(落下下). *fall down*, pua̍h-lo̍h(跋落). *fall down (as wall)*, pang(枋). *down-stream*, lo̍h-lâu(落樓). *in price*, lo̍h-kè(落價); iáu-phiⁿ(僥平).

**down**, *(feathers)*, zông(絨). *goose-down*, gô-zông(鵝絨).

**dowry**, kè-tsng(嫁妝); sûi-liâm(隨奩); tsng-liâm(妝奩).

**doze**, tak-sut-gu̍t(觸蟀夗); tak(觸); tak-ma̍k-u̍t(觸目夗).

**draft**, *money*, ngṳ̂n-toaⁿ(銀端). *of letter*, sìn-kó(信稿).

**drag**, thua(拖); thua-túi(拖縋); khan(牽). *cart*, thua-chhia(拖車). *for shells*, tah-sap(搭颯); pê-sap(爬颯).

**dragon**, lêng(龍); kau-lêng(蛟龍). *to paddle dragon-boat*, phẽ-lêng-tsûn(扒龍船).

**dragonfly**, sua-meⁿ(沙蜢); chheng-thêng(蜻蜓). *(small)*, sua-meⁿ-niêⁿ(沙蜢娘).

**dragoon**, bé-piaⁿ(馬兵); khiâ-piaⁿ(騎兵).

**drain**, tsúi-kau(水溝); sái-kau(屎溝). *drain a place*, làu-tiāu-tsúi(澇掉水). *off water as through strainer*, tè-tsúi(滯水).

**drake**, ah-hêng(鴨雄).

**draught**, see **draft**. *of fish*, che̍k-mãng-hṳ̂(一網魚). *of wind*, thong-huang(通風). *in a draught*, tng-huang-lōu(當風路).

**draw**, thua(拖); po̍ih(拔); túi(挽). *water*, kũaⁿ-tsúi(摜水); pua̍h-tsúi(跋水). *out*, po̍ih-tshut(拔出); mán-tshut(挽出); thua-tshut(拖出). *teeth*, khieh-khí(拔起). *a sliding window*, thuah〔〕. *a sword*, po̍ih-kiàm(拔劍); po̍ih-to(拔刀). *poison*, po̍ih-ta̍k(拔毒). *a bow*, khui-keng(開弓); mán-keng(挽弓). *oneself together in a heap*, kiu-kiu niuⁿ-niuⁿ(勼勼扭扭). *draw up one's legs*, kha kiu--khí-lâi(骹勼起來). *draw breath (also, to sigh)*, tháu-khùi(㪗氣). *opium-smoke*, kuh-hun(嗝薰); po̍k-hun(曝薰). *lots*, khieh-khau(挈口); po̍ih-chhiam(拔簽); thiu-chhiam-kiáⁿ(抽簽囝). *a carriage*, thua-chhia(拖車). *nails*, po̍ih-teng(拔燈); kiãu-teng(撬釘). *a net*, po̍ih-mãng(拔網); chhiû-mãng(揪網). *draw near*, túi-bûa(挽埋). *near (approach)*, kiâⁿ-bûa(行埋); chiũ-kṳ̃n(就近); kṳ̃n-bûa(近埋). *attention*, ín-tõng nâng-sim(引動人心); tõng nâng-sim-ma̍k(動人心目). *up a line of battle*, pâi-tīn(排陣). *a list*, khui-mêng kak-mue̍h(開明角物); kiám-tiám(檢點). *as loadstone*, hiap-bûa〔〕. *out of the water*, liâu〔〕; kou〔〕. *a splinter*, liàm-tshut(捻出); túi-tshut(挽出). *a splinter (with a needle)*, thie-tshut(挑出). *blood*, lâu-hueh(流血); pàng-tshut-hueh(放出血). *money from bank*, khṳ̍-ngṳ̂n-hâng khie̍h-ngṳ̂n(去銀行挈銀); tùi-ngṳ̂u(對牛). *a curtain*, liâm sa-khui(簾沙開); liâm kiáu-phû(簾攪浮). *draw away*, ín-tshūa(引𤆬). *entice*, ín-iú(引誘); iú-ho̍k(誘惑). *draw on stockings*, chhēng-bue̍h(穿襪). *draw back*, tò-thò(倒退); thò(退); thò-pōu(退步).

**draw**, *pictures*, ūe-ūe(畫畫); ūe-ang-kiáⁿ(畫尪囝); ūe-sièⁿ(畫像). *a line*, ūe-hûn(畫痕); phah-keh(拍格). *a landscape*, ūe-suaⁿ-tsúi(畫山水). *a map*, ūe-tôu(畫圖). *one's portrait*, ūe-sièⁿ(畫像); ūe-hí-sîn(畫喜神); ūe-siáu-iáⁿ(畫小影).

**drawbridge**, tiàu-kiê(吊橋).

**drawer**, keh(格); tshn̂g-keh(床格); kūiⁿ-keh(櫃格). *open a drawer*, khui-keh(開格). *bureau with many drawers*, peh-chí-keh(百指格).

**drawers**, sin-tói-khòu(身底褲). *short drawers, as for bathing*, khòu-kue̍h(褲橛); tsúi-khòu(水褲).

**drawing-room**, khah-thiaⁿ(客廳); kheh-thiaⁿ(客廳).

**drawl**, tàⁿ-ūe mān-mān(呾話慢慢); tàⁿ-ūe zūn-pōu zūn-pōu(呾話閏步閏步); tàⁿ-ūe zūn-zūn(呾話閏閏).

**dread**, ùi(畏); kiaⁿ(驚); kiaⁿ-kũ(驚懼). *dreadful*, khó-ùi(可畏); tshūa-nâng-ùi(𤆬人畏).

**dream**, māng(夢); mêⁿ-māng(夜夢); ki-kuan(機關). *have a dream*, tit-che̍k-māng(得一夢); māng-che̍k-māng(夢一夢). *dream anything*, māng-kìⁿ(夢見). *interpret*, piẽn-māng(辨夢); piẽn-māng-tiãu(辨夢兆). *by a dream, e.g. to teach one*, thoh-māng(託夢).

**dreary**, ou-àm(烏暗); kan-ta(乾灱); sok-liau(寂寥).

**dredge**, chhip(緝). *to dredge for fish and shrimps*, oi-hṳ̂-hê(挨魚蝦).

**dregs**, phoh(粕); tsa(渣); tsa-tsái(渣滓). *of distilled liquor*, chiú-tsau(酒糟). *of tea*, tê-tsa(茶渣).

**drenched**, pun-tsúi chìm(分水浸). *with rain*, khṳt-hõu ak(乞雨沃); ak kàu-lok-lok(沃到漉漉); tsâng kàu-thúe-thúe(叢到體體).

**dress**, tá-pàn(打扮); ho̍k-sek(服色); chhēng-saⁿ(穿衫); i-ho̍k(衣服); sin-chhēng(身穿). *fine dress*, tá-pàn phâi-chhiâng(打扮排場). *to shew off*, tsuang-pàn iâu-pái(裝扮搖擺). *a wound*, pa̍k-bûa(縛埋); ūaⁿ-pòu-liâu(換布撩). *the feet of women*, tîⁿ-kha(纏骹); ūaⁿ-kha(換骹). *the hair*, siu-thâu(收頭); siu-thâu-môⁿ(梳頭毛); lua̍h-thâu(辣頭). *food*, tsṳ́-chia̍h(煮食); pa-lói-chia̍h(巴禮食); sṳ̃-lí-chia̍h(伺理食). *skins*, se̍k-phûe(熟皮). *stone*, phah-chie̍h(拍石); chie̍h khieh-kng(石挈光). *with flags, as ship or street*, kat-tshái(結彩). *dressing-gown*, siu-thâu-saⁿ(梳頭衫). *dress-case*, kiàⁿ-thâi(鏡臺); kiàⁿ-thâi-keh(鏡臺格). *dress-table*, siu-tsng-thâi(收妝臺). *dress-room*, siu-thâu-pâng(梳頭房).

**dribblets**, lân-su(零輸); lân-ló(零些).

**dried**, ta(灱); khùa-ta(掛灱). *fruits*, kuaⁿ(乾). *dates*, tsó-kuaⁿ(棗乾). *fish*, hṳ̂-póu(魚脯). *duck*, ah-póu(鴨脯).

**drift**, phiau-liû(漂流). *boat, to leeward*, kài(界). *meaning*, ì-sṳ̀(意思); tãi-ì(怠意); tói-tsṳ́(底子); tãi-lia̍k(怠略).

**drill**, *a*, tsǹg-kiáⁿ(鑽囝). *to*, tsǹg-khang(鑽空). *to drill soldiers*, tshau-piaⁿ(操兵); tshau-liēn(操練); tshau-în(操鉛); kà-tshau(教操).

**drink**, ím(飲); chia̍h(食); lim(啉). *tea*, chia̍h-tê(食茶); ím-tê(飲茶). *liquor*, chia̍h-chiú(食酒); ím-chiú(飲酒); lim-chiú(啉酒). *food & drink*, ím-chia̍h(飲食). *craving for*, chiú-ngièn(酒癮); chiú-ín(酒癮).

**drip**, tih(滴); tih--lo̍h-lâi(答答滴); ta̍p-ta̍p-tih(答答滴).

**drive**, *a carriage*, sái-chhia(駛車); gṳ̃-chhia(御車). *in a carriage*, tsõ-bé-chhia(坐馬車). *a flock of ducks*, hâⁿ-ah(懸壓). *away*, jiāu-tiāu(尿掉); kúaⁿ-tiāu(趕掉); chẽng-tiāu(淨掉); to̍k-tiāu(逐掉). *drive against*, tsũang--tie̍h(撞着).

**drivel**, lâu-nũaⁿ(流涎).

**drizzle**, hõu-kiáⁿ(雨囝); hõu-mûiⁿ-kiáⁿ(雨微囝); hõu-kiáⁿ êng-êng(雨囝延延); hõu-kiáⁿ sa̍p-sa̍p(雨囝閘閘).

**droll**, *humorous*, hàuⁿ-sńg(好耍); hàuⁿ-chhiè(好笑); hàuⁿ-tshu-chhiè(好趣笑); hàuⁿ-niap-kuài(好捏怪); tshu-sńg(趨耍). *laughable*, hó-chhiè(好笑); khó-chhiè(可笑); tshūa-nâng-chhiè(𤆬人笑).

**droop**, sàng-sim(喪心). *wings*, thu̍t-si̍t(脫實). *flower*, hue sià(花謝). *leaves*, hie̍h hûiⁿ-hûiⁿ(葉懸懸).

**drop**, *of water*, che̍k-tiám-tsúi(一點水); tih-kiáⁿ-tsúi(滴囝水). *to*, tih--lo̍h-lâi(滴落來); ta̍p-ta̍p-tih(答答滴). *anything from the hand*, ka-lau̍h--lo̍h-lâi(鉸落落來); liù-ka-lau̍h(溜鉸落); phiù-chhiú(失手). *anchor*, pha-tèng(拋椗). *cease*, hiah(歇).

**dropsy**, tsúi-hap(水合); chéng-hap(腫合); phòng-hap(膨合); n̂g-chéng-hap(黃腫合). *in the legs*, kha-khì(骹氣). *in the abdomen*, kóu-chèng(鼓脹).

**dross**, thih-sái(鐵屎); lôu-tói-sái(爐底屎).

**drought**, ũaⁿ(旱); thiⁿ-sî ũaⁿ(天時旱); khàng-ũaⁿ(亢旱); kan-ũaⁿ(乾旱); ũaⁿ-ta(旱灱); bô-hõu(無雨).

**drown**, pun-tsúi kek-sí(分水激死). *oneself*, khṳ̀ thiàu-tsúi(去跳水); thiàu-hái(跳海); thiàu-khoi(跳溪).

**drowsy**, phî(疲); phî-kũan(疲倦); ma̍k siap(目澀).

**drudge**, lâu-khóu(勞苦); khóu-kang(苦工); bûa-khóu(磨苦); bûa-le̍k(磨力).

**drugs**, ie̍h(藥); ie̍h-tshâi(藥材); ie̍h-liāu(藥料). *druggist*, ie̍h-phòu tshâi-tsú(藥舖財主); ie̍h-kheh(藥客).

**drum**, kóu(鼓). *beat*, phah-kóu(拍鼓); lûi-kóu(雷鼓). *stick*, kóu-thûi(鼓槌).

**drunk**, chia̍h-chiú-tsùi(食酒醉); tsùi-chiú(醉酒); tsùi-thûi(醉腿). *drunkard*, hàuⁿ-chia̍h-chiú(好食酒); hàuⁿ-chiú(好酒); chiú-thû(酒徒).

**dry**, ta(灱). *in the sun*, pha̍k-ta(曝灱). *in the air or wind*, lā-ta(晾灱); khau-ta(摳灱); tshue-ta(吹灱). *at the fire*, pūe-ta(焙灱). *season*, *as wood*, khùa-ta(掛灱). *wipe dry*, chhit-ta(拭灱).

**dubious**, khó-gî(好疑); hó-gî(好疑); bô-tiāⁿ-tie̍h(無定着).

**duck**, ah(鴨); ah-bó(鴨母). *wild*, tsúi-ah(水鴨). *dried*, ah-póu(鴨脯). *duckweed*, phiê(萍).

**duct**, *lachrymal*, ma̍k-khang(目孔); ma̍k-tsap-khang(目汁空).

**ductile**, zūn(韌); hó-túi-tn̂g--kâi(好拖長个).

**dudgeon**, mīn pìⁿ-pìⁿ(面變變); pìⁿ-mīn(變面); seⁿ-khì(生氣).

**due**, khiàm(欠); pńg-téng(本頂); eng-kai(應該). *what is due anyone*, só eng-kai-hôiⁿ--i(所應該還伊); só-tng-hôiⁿ--i(所當還伊); só-khiàm--i(所欠伊). *arrived in due time*, khṳ̀-kàu hù-hù(去到付付); lâi-kàu bõi-khah-mān(來到袂較慢); tùi-sî-hāu(對時候); hù-sî-hāu(付時候). *pay customs dues*, la̍p-hiàng(納餉).

**dull**, tun(鈍). *stupid*, lú-tũn(魯鈍); che̍k-tóu ṳ̀-sat(一肚淤塞); ṳ̀-sat put-thong(淤塞不通). *colour*, chhién-sek(淺色); tîm-sek(沉色). *fire*, húe bô-hièⁿ-jie̍t(火無向熱); húe khah-nńg〔〕. *day*, ou-im(烏陰). *of hearing*, hĩⁿ lâng(耳聾). *of vision*, ma̍k-chiu bū(目睭霧); ma̍k hue(目花).

**dumb**, é(啞); é-kháu(啞口); bõi-tàⁿ-ūe(袂呾話).

**dumpish**, ut-tsu̍t(鬱卒); iu-ut(憂鬱); sim-thâu thiàⁿ(心頭痛).

**dumpling**, *(native)*, lo̍h-thng-chî(落湯糍); mûaⁿ-chî(鰻糍).

**dun**, tshui(催); tshui-pek(催逼); thó-chîⁿ kín-kín(討錢緊緊); chiéⁿ-thó(掌討).

**dunce**, tsṳ-tai(書呆); bô-ēng-nâng(無用人); bô-lōu-ēng(無路用); bô-mih tshâi-chhêng(無乜才情); bô-ki-khiàu(無機竅).

**dung**, pùn(糞); pûi(肥); tshou(粗). *to dung*, lo̍h-pûi(落肥); èng-pûi(壅肥). *to dung (liquid)*, phuah-pûi(潑肥).

**dungeon**, lô-ge̍k(牢獄); hiu-ge̍k(幽獄); kam(監). *to put in*, hiu-kìm(幽禁).

**dupe**, *to*, tshuah(掇); mûaⁿ(鰻); phièn(騙).

**duplicate**, têng-siá(重寫); têng-kià(重寄).

**duplicity**, nõⁿ-sim(兩心); sie-phièn(相騙); che̍k-mīn-to nõⁿ-mīn-sái(一面刀兩面使).

**durable**, *nãiⁿ-kú; kien-kù; tōiⁿ*, khiàng(勥). *this cloth is very*, chí-kâi-pòu siãng-nãiⁿ-chhēng(此個布上耐穿).

**duration**, kú(久); kú-tn̂g(久長); chhiâng-kú(長久). *endless*, ióng-kú(永久); ióng-ién(永遠); kú-uán(久遠); kú-ién(久遠); bõi-liáu(袂了).

**durian**, *fruit (jack-fruit)*, po-lô-bi̍t(菠蘿蜜).

**during**, *the night*, mêⁿ--kùa(夜旰). *the year*, nîⁿ--kan(年間). *the hot weather*, zua̍h-gue̍h tiâng-sî(熱月當時). *dinner*, tõ-chia̍h-pn̄g kâi-sî-hāu(在食飯个時候).

**dusk**, mêⁿ-hng(夜昏); háⁿ-hun(黃昏); siè-siè-àm(褪褪暗); siè-siè thóiⁿ-m̄-kìⁿ nâng-mīn(褪褪睇毋見人面); háⁿ-hun-kiáⁿ(黃昏囝); háⁿ-bu(黃晡).

**dust**, thôu-êng(塗煙); thôu-hún(塗粉); tîn-êng(塵煙); sua-êng(沙煙); sua-thôu(沙塗). *dusty*, seⁿ-thôu-hún(生塗粉). *raise*, eng(煙); kiauh-sua(攪沙); iauh-sua〔〕. *beat off*, pũaⁿ-tiāu sua-êng(拂掉沙煙). *shake off*, hĩⁿ-tiāu thôu-hún〔〕. *to**dust*, tshóiⁿ-tiāu tîn-ai(筅掉塵埃). *duster (of feathers)*, koi-môⁿ-tshóiⁿ(雞毛筅). *dust-pan*, pùn-táu(糞斗). *dust-basket*, pùn-ki(糞箕).

**dutiful**, kiâⁿ-hàu(行孝); hàu-tsṳ́(孝子); chĩn-pńg-hūn(盡本分); hàu-sũn(孝順); sũn-tshông(順從).

**duty**, cheh-hūn(職分); pńg-hūn(本分); cheh-jĩm(職任); hūn-lãi kâi-sṳ̄(份內个事); só eng-kai-kiâⁿ(所應該行). *perform one's*, chĩn-pńg-hūn(盡本分); chĩn-cheh-hūn(盡職分).

**dwarf**, ói(矮); ói-jîn(嶁岣); nâng ói-ói(人矮矮); ói-sòi(嶁岣). *trees*, kóu-sông(嶁岣).

**dwell**, khiã-khí(徛起); kṳ-tsũ(居住); hiah-tshù(歇厝); tiū(住). *dwelling*, tshù(厝); kuán(管); tshù-ok(厝屋).

**dwindle**, chiãm-sue(漸衰); chiãm-chiãm-sòi(漸漸細); chiãm-chiãm-sán(漸漸㾪); sue-mûiⁿ(衰微); sue-jia̍k(衰弱); siau-si̍h(消蝕); siau-sòi(消細).

**dye**, jiám-sek(染色); níⁿ-pòu(染布); î-sek(移色); làm-pòu(藍布). *stuff*, sek-liāu(色料). *stuff (indigo)*, tōiⁿ(靛). *dyer*, níⁿ-pòu sai-pẽ(染布司阜). *frame used by dyer*, pha̍k-pòu-pêⁿ(曝布棚).

**dying**, chiang-sí(將死); àiⁿ-sí(愛死); kṳ̃n-sí(近死); chiang-kṳ̃n àiⁿ-sí(將近愛死); lîm-sí(臨死).

**dynasty**, chhiâu(朝). *the present*, chheng-chhiâu(清朝); pńg-chhiâu(本朝).

**dysentery**, lī(痢); lī-chi̍t(痢疾); pàng-âng(放紅); thâm-thūi(痰墜); thì-khì(滯氣); hueh-lī(血痢); pe̍h-lī(白痢).

**dyspepsia**, m̄-siau-hùe(毋消化); put-síau-hùe(不消化); chia̍h chek(食積); ím-chia̍h chek-tsũ(飲食積滯).

**dyspnoea**, tshúan(喘); khùi tōa(氣大); khùi kip(氣急); tshúan-kip(喘急); khì tshúan(氣喘); he̍hⁿ-he̍hⁿ-tshúan(赫赫喘). *infantine*, niⁿ-he〔〕; niⁿ-tshúan〔〕.

**dysury**, siáu-piẽn m̄-kiâⁿ(小便毋驚); sié-piẽn m̄-thong(小便毋通).

### E

**each**, kak(各); múeⁿ(每); pâi(排). *man*, kak-nâng(各人). *day*, múeⁿ-ji̍t(每日); pâi-ji̍t(排日). *year*, múeⁿ-nîⁿ(每年); nîⁿ-nîⁿ(年年); pâi-nîⁿ(排年). *each one*, kak-kâi(各個); kak-kak(各各). *each other*, siang(相); jī-ke(二家). *help each other*, jī-ke sie-hũ(二家相護). *scold each other*, sie-mēⁿ(相罵). *each end*, liáng-thâu(兩頭); nõⁿ-thâu(二頭). *side*, liáng-pôiⁿ(兩爿); liáng-ke(兩家).

**eager**, pek-chhiet(迫切); jie̍t-sim(熱心); méⁿ(猛); méⁿ-lie̍t(猛烈); kín-kip(緊急).

**eagle**, eng-chiáu(鷹鳥).

**ear**, hĩⁿ(耳). *orifice of*, hĩⁿ-khang(耳空). *earlap*, hĩⁿ-tûi(耳捶). *ear-brush*, hĩⁿ-tshóiⁿ(耳箲). *ear-pick*, hĩⁿ-pê(耳扒). *ear-wax*, hĩⁿ-sái(耳屎). *ear-ring*, hĩⁿ-kau(耳鉤); hĩⁿ-hûan(耳環); hĩⁿ-thūi(耳墜). *ear-drum (tympanum)*, hĩⁿ-kiàⁿ(耳鏡). *pierce the ear*, tshng-hĩⁿ(穿耳). *whisper in one's ear*, phak-tõ hĩⁿ-khang-kháu tàⁿ(趴在耳空口呾); hĩⁿ-piⁿ tàⁿ-ūe(耳邊呾話). *ear-witness*, chhin-hĩⁿ thiaⁿ-kìⁿ(親耳聽見). *ear of rice*, chhek-sūi(測穗).

**early**, tsá(早). *in the morning*, mn̂g-khí-tsá(眠起早); tsá-sîn(早晨). *very*, tsá-tsá(早早). *too*, khah-tsá(較早). *still*, hûan-liáu-tsá(還了早); iáu-tsá(猶早). *early and late*, tsá-mńg(早晚); tsá-àm(早暗); tsá-ùaⁿ(早晏). *in early times*, kóu-tsá(古早). *as early as possible*, kúaⁿ-tsá(趕早); thàu-tsá(透早).

**earn**, thàn(趁); thó-thàn(討趁). *money*, thàn-chîⁿ(趁錢). *one's living*, thàn-chia̍h(趁食). *much*, tōa-thàn(大趁). *easily*, kōi-thàn(易趁).

**earnest**, *tsuan-sim; chhiet-chhiet; pek-chhiet; sim kien*, ì chhiet(意切); tsuan-it(專一); jie̍t-sim(熱心). *speak in*, tàⁿ-si̍t-ūe(呾實話). *earnest money*, tiāⁿ-ngṳ̂n(定銀); tiāⁿ-chîⁿ(定錢); tiāⁿ-thâu(定頭); tǹg(當). *accept earnest money*, siu-tiāⁿ(收定).

**earth**, tī(地); thôu(塗); thóu(土). *the earth*, tī-kiû(地球). *heaven and earth*, thiⁿ-tī(天地). *on the earth*, tõ-tī-mīn(在地面上); tõ-thóu-ẽ(在塗下). *the whole earth*, phóu-thiⁿ-ẽ(普天下); thong thiⁿ-kha-ẽ(通天骹下). *garden-earth*, hn̂g-thôu(園塗). *earth-nut*, tī-tāu(地豆). *earth-worm*, kãu-ún(蚯蚓). *earth-quake*, tī chín(地震); tī tín-tãng(地振動); tī-gû ūaⁿ-koiⁿ(地牛換肩). *earthenware*, hûi-khì(缶器); jiâu-khì(窯器); au-úaⁿ pûaⁿ-ti̍h(烏碗盤碟).

**ease**, phêng-an(平安); uaⁿ(安); khùaⁿ-ua̍h(寬活); tsṳ̃-tsãi(自在); uaⁿ-jiên(安然); uaⁿ-chẽⁿ(安靜). *pain*; chí-thiàⁿ(止痛). *as rope*, pàng-sang(放鬆); pàng-lēng(放冗). *easy*, kōi(易); iông-kōi(容易); iông-ĩ(容易); bõi-oh(袂惡); put-lân(不難). *manner, not hurried*, khuaⁿ-chiâⁿ khuaⁿ-chiâⁿ(寬成寬成); tshông-iông(從容). *to recognize*, kōi-jīn(易認). *to learn*, kōi-pat(易識).

**easel**, ūe-ūe-kè(畫畫架).

**east**, tang(東); tang-pôiⁿ(東爿). *eastward*, tùi-tang(對東); niàⁿ-tang(向東); hiàng-tang(向東).

**eat**, chia̍h(食). *to the full*, chia̍h-pá(食飽). *cannot*, chia̍h-m̄-lo̍h(食毋落); bõi-chia̍h(袂食). *I have eaten*, chia̍h--liáu(食了). *I have eaten the whole of it*, chia̍h-liáu--liáu(食了了); chia̍h-uân--liáu(食完了). *eaten by rats*, khṳt niáu-tshṳ́ kã(乞鳥鼠咬); khṳt niáu-tshṳ́ khòi(乞鳥鼠喫). *by white ants*, pe̍h-hiã tsù(白蟻蛀). *by birds*, chiáu toh(鳥啄). *eat at one's own expense*, chia̍h-ka-kī(食家己). *at employer's expense*, chia̍h-tshâi-tsú(食齋主); tshùi-chia̍h gūa(喙食外). *eatable*, hó-chia̍h(好食); õi--nîn chia̍h-tit〔〕. *not very nice to eat*, bô-ūi-tàu(無胃竇). *eating-house*, tiàm-phòu(店舖).

**eaves**, lîm-chîⁿ(臨錢). *eaves-dropper*, thau-thiaⁿ(偷聽); thàm-thiaⁿ(探聽); àm-chẽⁿ-thiaⁿ(暗靜聽); phak-hĩⁿ thiaⁿ(趴耳聽).

**ebb**, khó(洘). *tide*, khó-lâu(洘流); tsúi thò(水退); lâu lo̍h(流落); pak-lâu(北流). *low*, khó-ta-ta(洘灱灱).

**ebony**, ou-tshâ-ba̍k(烏柴墨).

**eccentric**, kùai-phiah(怪癖); kóu-kuài(古怪); kú-kùai(古怪).

**echo**, tâng-siaⁿ siang-ìn(銅聲相印); hûe-siaⁿ ìn-tap(回聲印答); ìn-siaⁿ hûe-tap(印聲回答); tõu-kiàng-kúi ìn(肚見鬼應). *among hills*, suaⁿ siang-ìn(山相應).

**eclipse**, ji̍t si̍h(日蝕). *lunar*, gue̍h si̍h(月蝕). *beginning of*, tsho-si̍h(初蝕). *maximum*, ke̍k-si̍h(極蝕). *end of*, ho̍k-îⁿ(覆圓).

**economy**, tsat-ēng(節用); khiãm(儉); khieh-si̍p(挈拾). *in food and clothes*, khiãm-chia̍h khiãm-chhēng(儉食儉穿). *political*, kok-chèng kâi-sṳ̄(國政个事).

**ecstasy**, put-seng tsṳ-hí(不生歡喜); huaⁿ-hí ke̍k(歡喜極).

**eddy**, tsúi ká-tsn̄g(水攪旋); tsúi ká-pn̄g(水攪飯).

**edge**, piⁿ(邊); kîⁿ(墘). *of knife*, to-tshùi(刀喙); to-kháu(刀口). *teeth on edge*, khí nńg(起軟); khí sng-nńg(起酸軟).

**edict**, kò-sī(告示); hiáu-zũ(曉諭). *issue*, tshut-kò-sī(出告示); tshut-sī-zũ(出示喻). *imperial*, siãng-zũ(上諭). *The Sacred*, Siàⁿ-zũ(聖諭).

**edify**, kiẽn-tek(建德).

**edit**, kháu-chèng(考正).

**educate**, kà(教); kà-hùe(教化); kà-hùn(教訓); kà-tãu(教導); kà-tha̍k(教讀); kà-tsṳ(教書).

**eel**, siẽn-hṳ̂(鱔魚); mûaⁿ-hṳ̂(鰻魚).

**efface**, kôu-buah(糊抹).

**effect**, *to*, sêng(成); sêng-sṳ̄(成事); sêng-kong(成功); sêng-chiũ(成就); tsò-chiâⁿ(做成); sái-kàu(使到). *take effect, as medicine, prayer &c*, hāu-ngiām(效驗); ũ-kong-hāu(有功效).

**effeminate**, nńg-jiû(軟柔); jiû-nńg(柔軟); tsṳ-niêⁿ-iēⁿ(諸娘樣). *manner of walking*, ûe-ûe tsũn-a-tsũn(微微捘阿捘).

**effervesce**, kún--khí-lâi(滾起來).

**efficacy**, khì-la̍t(氣力); kong-hāu(功效); sîn-hāu(神效); èng-ngiām(應驗); hāu-ngiām(效驗).

**efficient**, tsò-sṳ̄ tsò-tit-chiâⁿ(做事做得成).

**effigy**, nâng-iēⁿ(人樣); nâng-sièⁿ(人像).

**effluvia**, tshàu(臭); tshàu-bī(臭味); tshàu-hièn(臭憲); ùe-khì(穢氣).

**effort**, tshut-la̍t(出力); khṳ̂n-kang(勤工); khat-khóu(刻苦); khṳ̂n-khóu(勤苦).

**effulgence**, kng(光); hâu-kng(豪光); kuang-mêng(光明); kuang liãng-liãng(光亮亮).

**egg**, nñg(卵). *fowl's*, koi-nñg(雞卵). *to lay*, seⁿ-nñg(生卵). *boil*, sa̍h-nñg(煠卵). *shell*, nñg-khak(卵殼). *yolk*, nñg-jîn(卵仁). *white of*, nñg-chheng(卵清). *embryo egg*, nñg-toaⁿ(卵丹). *three eggs*, saⁿ-lia̍p-nñg(三粒卵). *cockroach eggs*, ka-tsua̍h-sieⁿ(虼蚻鞘). *egg-plant (brinjal)*, kiê(簥).

**eight**, poih(八). *eighteen*, tsa̍p-poih(十八). *eighty*, poih-tsa̍p(八十). *eighth*, tõiⁿ-poih(第八).

**either**, *you may have either you pleas*, sûi-suán(隨選); jîm-suán(任選); sûi-lṳ́-súan(隨汝選); zuãn--tî-kâi hó pun-lṳ́-suán(任底个好分汝選). *either way will do*, sûi-piẽn(隨便); sûi-piẽn-hó(隨便好); sûi-sûi piẽn-piẽn(隨隨便便); chièⁿ-seⁿ iā-hó(此樣生也好); hièⁿ-seⁿ iā-hó(彼樣生也好). *any way will do*,  tou-hó(都好). *on either side*, liáng-pôiⁿ(兩爿). *either....or*, ho̍k....ho̍k(或...或).

**eject**, to̍k-tshut(逐出); kek-tshut(激出); jiāu-tshut(趭出); chhek-to̍k(斥逐); khu-tshut(驅出); kúaⁿ-tshut(趕出). *from mouth*, phùi--tshut-lâi(呸出來). *from stomach*, thòu--tshut-lâi(吐出來).

**eke**, chiap(接); chiap-tn̂g(接長); sùa-tn̂g(紲長); póu(補).

**elaborate**, kang-hu(工夫); tsò-lâi zû-zû(做來如如); kang-hu iùⁿ-sòi(功夫幼細).

**elapse**, *fifty years have elapsed*, kàu-taⁿ íⁿ-keng-kùe ngõu-tsa̍p-nîⁿ--liáu(到担已經過五十年了).

**elastic**, nńg(軟); õi-tshun õi-kiu(會伸會球); õi-sin õi-sok(會伸會縮).

**elbow**, chhiú-thñg(手肘). *elbow room*, ũ-kò hó-tshun-lûn〔〕. *to elbow*, thńg--nâng〔〕; thñg--nâng〔〕.

**elder**, lãu-tōa(老大); chiáng-láu(長老). *he is my elder*, i tōa--uá(伊大我). *elder brother*, a-hiaⁿ(阿兄).

**eldest**, siãng-tōa(上大). *son*, tōa-kiáⁿ(大囝); tōa-tau-kiáⁿ(大頭囝); chiáng-tsṳ́(長子). *brother*, tōa-hiaⁿ(大兄).

**elect**, suán(選); suán-to̍h(選擇); kóiⁿ-to̍h(揀擇); kóiⁿ-suán(揀選).

**elegant**, iông-mãuⁿ(容貌); ngî-iông(儀容). *composition*, bûn-ngiáⁿ(文雅). *scholar*, ũ-tshâi-ha̍k(有才學).

**elements**, ngóu-hêng(五行); kim(金), ba̍k(木), tsúi(水), húe(火), thôu(土).

**elephant**, chhiẽⁿ(象). *tusks*, chhiẽⁿ-gê(象牙). *elephantiasis*, tōa-kha(大骹).

**elevate**, kṳ́(舉); kṳ́-khí(舉起); khí-kûiⁿ(起懸); kau-kṳ́(高舉). *elevated*, kûiⁿ(懸).

**eleven**, tsa̍p-it(十一). *eleven o'clock*, tsa̍p-it tiám-cheng(十一點鐘).

**elf**, sien(仙). *malignant*, iau-chiaⁿ(妖精); iau-kuài(妖怪).

**elope**, tùe-nâng-tsáu(綴人走).

**eloquent**, ũ-kháu-tshâi(有口才); ũ-kháu-lẽng(有口令); õi-tàⁿ-ūe(會呾話); miâⁿ-ke tàⁿ-ūe(名家呾話).

**else**, *somewhere else*, tõ-pa̍t-kò(在別塊). *has any one else come*, hûan-ũ pa̍t-nâng lâi a-bô(還有別人來亞無). *I have nothing else to say*, úa bô pa̍t-kâi-ūe hó-tàⁿ(我無別个話好呾).

**elucidate**, kói-mêng(解明); káng-kiù(講究); sueh-mêng(說明); kói-thiah(解拆).

**elude**, pī(避); tô-pī(逃避); siám-pī(閃避); tô-siám(躲閃); tô-pī tsáu-siám(逃避走閃); tô-tsáu(逃走); pī-bûa(避埋); tiàm-bûa(坫埋); pĩ-khui(避開).

**elysium**, sien-kéng(仙境).

**emaciated**, sáu(嫂); sán-sòu(㾪小); sán-kut lo̍h-ne̍k(㾪骨落肉). *(skin & bone)*, têng-phûe nêⁿ-têng-kut〔〕.

**emanate**, *from*, lâu-tshut(流出); huat-tshut(發出); liû-thûan(流傳); tshông-tõ hṳ́-kò khí(從在許塊起).

**embalm**, ēng-hieⁿ-liāu lâi liãm-si(用香料來念詩); tieⁿ-liãm(恬念).

**embankment**, toi(堤); hô-toi(河堤); toi-hūaⁿ(堤捍).

**embargo**, *on ship*, huang-tsûn bô i tshut-kháu(封船無伊出口).

**embark**, lo̍h-tsûn(落船); chiẽⁿ-tsûn(上船); tah-tsûn(搭船).

**embarrassed**, chìn-thò liáng-lân(進退兩難); m̄-káⁿ kìⁿ-nâng(毋敢見人). *embarrassing*, thām-thūi(失墜).

**embers**, húe-hu(火烌).

**embezzle**, thau-àm-chîⁿ(偷使錢); àm-chîⁿ(暗錢); àm-thun(暗吞); sai-ēng(私用); sai-tshú(私取).

**emblem**, piáu-iēⁿ(表樣); kì-hō(記號).

**embrace**, phõ(抱); sie-phõ(相抱); lám(攬). *opportunity*, sêng-sì(乘勢); sêng-ki-hũe(乘機會).

**embrasure**, tōa-phàu-khang(大炮空); tōa-chhèng-khang(大銃空).

**embroider**, chhiah-hue(刺花); siù-hue(繡花); thie-hue(刺花); thie-siù(刺花).

**embroil**, seⁿ-sṳ̄(生事); tsak-lũan(扎亂).

**embryo**, hâi-thai(孩胎).

**emerge**, phû--tshut-lâi(浮起來); phû--khí-lâi(浮起來); huat-hīn(發現).

**emergency**, kín-kip kâi-sṳ̄(緊急个事). *able to act in an*, ũ-khûan-pièn(有權變); ũ-pièn-thong(有變通).

**emetic**, huat-thòu-ie̍h(發吐藥); thòu-ie̍h(吐藥).

**emigrate**, î-kṳ(移居); chhien-kṳ(遷居); súa-kṳ(徙居); tshut-tsóu(出祖); chhien-súa(遷徙); khṳ̀-pa̍t-kò khiã-khí(去別塊徛起). *abroad*, kùe-huan(過番).

**eminent**, thiàu-khûn(超群); tshut-chèng(出眾); tshut-thoh(出色); thiàu-thut(跳脫); kùe-nâng(過人). *physician*, tshut-miâⁿ sin-seⁿ(出名先生); hién-miâⁿ sin-seⁿ(顯名先生); kau-miâⁿ sin-seⁿ(高名先生).

**empire**, kok(國).

**employ**, ēng(用); sái(使). *employer*, thâu-ló(頭腦); tshâi-tsú(財主). *of teacher*, tong-ke(東家); tong-tsú(東主). *employment*, sṳ̄(事); sṳ̄-ngia̍p(事業). *without*, bô-sṳ̄ hó-tsò(無事好做). *help one to get*, khan-kũaⁿ(牽摜); khan-sêng(牽成); thî-pua̍t(提拔).

**empoison**, lo̍h-hãn-ie̍h(落限藥); lo̍h-ie̍h(落藥); lo̍h-ta̍k(落毒).

**empower**, hù-thoh(付托); úi(委); thoh(托); pun-khûan-jĩm khṳ̃-i(分權任許伊).

**empty**, khang(空); khang-khak(空殼); khang-hṳ(空虛); khang-phàⁿ(空冇). *handed*, khang-chhiú(空手). *to empty out*, tò-tiāu(倒掉). *empty from**one vessel to another, backwards and forwards*, tò-kùe-lâi tò-kùe-khṳ̀(倒過來倒過去); piâⁿ-lâi piâⁿ-khṳ̀〔〕. *empty show*, hṳ-hua(虛花).

**emulate**, o̍h(學); o̍h-iēⁿ(學樣); hãu-o̍h(效學); hãu-huap(效法).

**enact**, *a law*, li̍p-huap(立法); siet-li̍p tiāⁿ-lī(設立定例).

**enamel**, *glazing on dishes*, thn̄g(搪). *to enamel*, lâm-thn̄g(藍搪); kài-thn̄g(蓋搪).

**encamp**, tì-iâⁿ(置營); pha-iâⁿ-pûaⁿ(拋營盤); kiẽn-iâⁿ(建營); li̍p-iâⁿ(立營); kak-iâⁿ(結營); tshàng-iâⁿ(創營). *encampment*, iâⁿ-pûaⁿ(營盤).

**enchant**, mîⁿ(迷); miⁿ-ho̍k(迷惑). *enchantment*, siâ-su̍t(邪術); bû-su̍t(巫術); siâ-huap(邪法); tshái-chheⁿ-huap(彩青法). *enchanter*, sái-siâ-su̍t(使邪術); tsò-bû-su̍t(做巫術).

**enchase**, *inlay with jewels*, sieⁿ-ge̍k(鑲玉). *adorn with figures*, tiau(雕); kuah(割); khek(刻); tiau-hue kuah-chiáu(雕花割鳥); tiau-hue khek-chiáu(雕花刻鳥); tiau-kuah hue-chiáu(雕割花鳥).

**enclose**, pau(包); huang(封); huang tõ-hṳ́-tói(封在許底). *a letter*, huang-tsṳ-sìn(封之信).

**encumber**, thua-thūi(拖墜); tsó-gāi(阻礙); hûang-gāi(妨礙).

**end**, tsong(終); búe(尾); suah-búe(煞尾); kiáu-búe(繳尾). *of road*, lōu-búe(路尾). *of year*, nîⁿ-búe(年尾). *both ends*, thâu-búe(頭尾); sang-thâu(雙頭). *I do not know what the end of this affair will be*, m̄-tsai chí-kâi-sṳ̄ kàu-búe-ke̍k sĩ-tsò-nîⁿ(毋知此個事到底是怎呢). *in the end*, kàu-búe(到尾). *to end*, ûan(完); tsò-chiâⁿ(做成); sêng-kong(成功); tsò-kàu-liáu(做到了); tsò-kàu chhêng-tshó(做到情楚). *a speech*, tàⁿ-ūe-hiah(呾話歇). *one's life (voluntarily)*, tsṳ̃-chĩn(自盡); ka-kī khṳ̀-sí(家己去死). *attain one's end*, tit-ì(得意). *to what end is this*, chí-kâi-sṳ̄ ũ-sĩ-mih lĩ-iah(此個事是有乜利益). *what end has he in view*, i ũ sĩ-mih ì-sṳ̀(伊有是乜意思). *endless*, bô-liáu(無了); bõi-uân(袂完); kú-kú bõi-hiah(久久袂歇); bô-kat-suah(無結煞). *end of the world*, sì--kan kâi mu̍at-ji̍t(世間个末日). *no more of this! let the matter end!*, pã--liáu(罷了).

**endeavour**, chhì(試). *to do any thing*, chhì-thóiⁿ(試睇); thèng-tsãu-hùe(聽造化). *do one's best endeavour*, chĩn-la̍t(盡力); tshut-la̍t(出力).

**endow**, sṳ̀(賜); kien-ngĩ-tsou(堅義租). *natural endowments*, tshâi-chhêng(才情); pún-sṳ̄(本事); pún-niáⁿ(本領). *good ditto*, sèⁿ-chieh hó(姓借好); hó-tshâi-chhêng(好財情).

**endure**, nãiⁿ(耐); khat-nãiⁿ(刻耐); lún(忍); khat-khóu-lún(刻苦忍). *cold*, nãiⁿ-chhìn(耐凊); lún-chhìn(忍凊). *hunger*, lún tóu khùn(忍肚困); lún-ki lún-gō(忍飢忍餓). *affliction*, nãiⁿ-kan-khóu(耐艱苦). *patient endurance*, jím-nãiⁿ(忍耐). *cannot endure*, nãiⁿ-m̄-khṳ̀(耐毋去); jím-put-tit(忍不得); lân-nãiⁿ(難耐). *not to be endured (scolding)*, put-kham(不堪).

**enemy**, chhiû(仇); chhiû-te̍k(仇敵); te̍k(敵); te̍k-chhiú(敵手); tùi-thâu(對頭); uan-ke(冤家); chhiû-ke(仇家). *to become an enemy to anyone*, kāng i kat-chhiû(共伊結仇); kāng i tsò-chhiû-te̍k(共伊做仇敵); kat-uan-ngia̍p(結冤業).

**energy**, khì-la̍t(氣力); sim-la̍t(心力); kúaⁿ-kuat(果決); ióng-lie̍t(勇烈).

**enervated**, bô-khì-hueh(無氣血); bô-hueh-khì(無血氣); nńg-jia̍k(軟弱); bô-sîn-khì(無神氣); n̂g-sng sòu-sán(黃酸㾪㾪).

**enforce**, mién-kiáng(免強); khiâng-pek(強迫); ngẽ-lia̍h(硬掠).

**engage**, *in business*, tsò-seng-lí(做生理). *in an affair*, tshap-sṳ̄(插事). *workmen*, kòu-sai-pẽ(雇司阜); hàm-sai-pẽ(喊司阜). *a teacher*, chhiáⁿ-sin-seⁿ(請先生). *a boat*, kòu-tsûn(雇船). *a chair*, kiè-kiē(叫轎); kòu-kiē(僱轎); hàm-kiē(喊轎). *a passage*, tah-tsûn(搭船). *in conversation*, phue̍h-ūe(詖話). *engaged*, ũ-sṳ̄(有事); m̄-ôiⁿ(毋閒). *engagement (promise)*, ieh(約). *enter into*, li̍p-ieh(立約); kat-ieh(結約). *break*, sit-ieh(失約). *engagement (battle)*, kau-chièn(交戰); sie-thâi(相刣); ke-húe sie-chih(家伙相接). *engaging*, khó-ài(可愛); tshù-bī(趣味); tshūa-nâng-sieh(𤆬人惜); tit-nâng-sieh(得人惜).

**enter**, ji̍p(入); chìn(進); chìn-ji̍p(進入). *the house*, ji̍p-tshù-lãi(入厝內); ji̍p-lãi(入內). *account*, chiẽⁿ-siàu(上數). *office*, tsò-jīm(做任); chiẽⁿ-jīm(上任). *Buddhist monastery*, tshut-ke(出家). *the world (be born)*, tshut-sì(出世). *a petition*, ji̍p-pín(入稟); jip-tiâⁿ(入場). *a port*, ji̍p-káng(入港). *one's name*, kì-miâⁿ(記名); lo̍h-miâⁿ(落名); kì-lo̍k nâng-miâⁿ(記錄人名). *an association*, ji̍p-hũe(入會); pài-hũe(拜會). *a religion*, ji̍p-kà(入教).

**enterprising**, káⁿ-pàng-táⁿ(敢放膽); ũ-táⁿ-lia̍k(有膽略).

**ephemeral**, *insects*, chiau seⁿ mõⁿ sí kâi-thâng(朝生暮死个蟲).

**equal**, pêⁿ-iēⁿ(平樣); pêⁿ-téng(平等). *in size*, pêⁿ-tōa(平大). *in number*, pêⁿ-tsōi(平齊); pêⁿ-ke(平加). *two highland leagues are equal to three*, suaⁿ-lãi lōu-tsãm(山內路站), nõⁿ-phòu tǹg-saⁿ-phòu(兩舖當三舖). *having no equal*, bô-pí(無比); bô-hó-pí(無好比). *equally*, tsôi-tsôi(齊齊); tsâu-tsâu(足足). *equalize*, thuaⁿ-pêⁿ(勻平); thuaⁿ-ûn(勻勻). *equals*, tâng-téng(同等); tâng-lūi(同類).

**equator**, chhiah-tãu(赤道).
