**equinox**, ji̍t-mêⁿ pêⁿ-pun(日夜平分). *vernal*, tshun-hun(春分). *autumnal*, chhiu-hun(秋分).

**equip**, *an army*, phài-kip kun-tsuang(派給軍裝); niáⁿ-kun-tsuang(領軍裝).

**equipage**, *imperial*, lêng-chhia(靈車); gṳ̄-chhia(御車). *mandarin's*, tōa-kiē chip-sṳ̄(大轎執事).

**equitable**, kong-tãu(公道); kong-phêng(公平); kong-ngĩ(公義); kong-chiàⁿ(公正); kuaⁿ-chiàⁿ(官正).

**equivalent**, tùi-uāⁿ(對換); tùi-táu(對倒).

**equivocal**, sang-kuan liáng-ì(雙關兩意); che̍k-sṳ̂ liáng-ngĩ(賊事兩義).

**eradicate**, po̍ih-kṳn(拔根); pi̍t-po̍ih-tiāu(畢拔掉); tín-túi-tiāu(振挽掉); tsám-tsháu tṳ̂-kṳn(斬草除根).

**erase**, *writing*, khoi-tiāu-jī(揩掉字); kueh-tiāu-jī(刮掉字).

**erect**, *to*, khiã--khí-lâi(徛起來); kiẽn(建); khí(起). *adjective*, ti̍t(直); chiàⁿ(正).

**err**, kiâⁿ-tshò(行錯); ũ-kùe-sit(有過失); sit-tshò(失錯); sit-gōu(失誤). *miss the way*, kiâⁿ-tāⁿ(行賺); kiâⁿ-tāⁿ-lōu(行賺路). *errata*, tāⁿ-jī(賺字). *in printing*, khek-tāⁿ(刻賺); ìn-tāⁿ(印賺). *in writing*, siá-tāⁿ(寫賺); siá-tshò(寫錯); gōu-siá(誤寫).

**errand**, *send on an*, kià-thoh(寄託); hù-thoh tàⁿ-ūe(咐託呾話); kià-siaⁿ(寄聲); sái(駛).

**erroneous**, tshò(錯); tāⁿ(賺); m̄-tie̍h(毋着). *expression*, tàⁿ-tāⁿ(呾賺).

**error**, tshò(錯); sit-tshò(失錯); tsha-tshò(差錯); tshò--tshù(錯厝). *confess*, jīn-tshò(認錯).

**eructation**, phah-oh(拍呃). *sour*, phah-tshàu-oh(拍臭呃); eh-sng-oh(呃酸呃); áu-sng-oh(嘔酸呃).

**eruption**, *on skin, from heat*, zua̍h-pùi(熱痞); seⁿ-pùi(生痞).

**escalade**, peh-chiẽⁿ siâⁿ-téng(爬上城頂). *(scaling ladders)*, hûn-thui(雲梯). 

**escape**, tsáu(走); tô-tsáu(逃走); pī-tsáu(避走); pī-bûa(避埋); tsáu-tshut(走出); thut-sin-kòi(脫身計). *secretly*, thau-tsáu(偷走). *from prison*, tsáu-kam(走監).

**escort**, *sàng*, sàng-kiâⁿ(送行). *a criminal*, ah-sàng(押送); ah-kòi(押解). *military*, piaⁿ-bé sàng-kiâⁿ(兵馬送行); piaⁿ-teng hũ-sàng(兵丁護送).

**especial**, *chì-chhiet; chhiet-iàu*, te̍k-te̍k(特特); tsuan-tsuan(專專).

**essay**, *to*, chhì--chē(試些); chhì-thóiⁿ--chē(試睇些); thèng-tsãu-hùe(逞造化).

**essay**, *an*, bûn-chieⁿ(文章). *write*, tsò-bûn-chieⁿ(做文章); tsò-bûn(做文). *a moral*, siẽn-tsṳ(善書). *a moral tract*, khǹg-sì-bûn(勸世文).

**essence**, pńg-chie(本招); ngûan-khì(元氣).

**essential**, chhiet-iàu(切要); put-khó-bô(不可無); bõi-tit-mién(袂得免); pit-pit tie̍h-ũ(必必着有).

**establish**, li̍p(立); siet-li̍p(設立); kiẽn-li̍p(建立); tshàng(創); tshàng-siet(創設); tì(置); tì-tshàng(置創); tshàng-li̍p(創立); khai-tshàng(開創). *an ordinace*, li̍p-tiāⁿ-lī(立定例). *a family*, tì-ke(置家). *a proposition*, chèng-kṳ̃(證據); piáu-kṳ̃(表據).

**estate**, *landed*, tī(地); tī-hng(地方); tshân-tī(田地). *house*, tshù(厝); tshù-the̍h(厝宅). *general*, ke-sṳ̄(家事); ke-tshâi(家財); ke-ngia̍p(家業); ke-tsṳ(家資). *arrived at man's estate*, tōa--liáu(大了); chiáng-sêng(長成).

**esteem**, *a person*, kèng-tõng(敬重); tsun-tõng(尊重); kùi-tõng(貴重); thóiⁿ-tõng(睇重). see CONSIDER.

**estimate**, *price or value*, kóu-kè(估價); kóu-ta̍t(估值); phah-kè(拍價); pān(判); iak-pān(約判); phah-pān(拍判); phah-sǹg(拍算); chhek-ta̍t(測值); tshui-chhek(推測).

**estranged**, jī-ke siang-gūa(字家相外); lî-sim(離心).

**eternal**, ióng(永); ióng-ién(永遠); ióng-kú(永久); kú-kú bô-liáu(久久無了); bô-sí bô-tsong(無死無終). *eternity*, ióng-sì(永世); sì-sì bô-liáu(世世無了).

**ethics**, lûn-lí(倫理); lûn-siêⁿ(倫常).

**etiquette**, lói(禮); lói-siàu(禮數); lói-mãuⁿ(禮貌). *attend to*, kiâⁿ-lói(行禮).

**etymology**, káng-jī-thói(簡字體).

**eulogy**, tsàn(讚); lêng-seng(靈聖). *to write*, tsò-tsàn(做讚); tôi-tsàn(題讚).

**eunuch**, thài-kàm(太監); iam-huãn(閹宦); huãn-kuaⁿ(宦官); zṳ̃-jîn(女人).

**Europe**, Au-lô-pa(歐羅巴); tōa-sai-iêⁿ(大西洋). *the continent of*, Au-lô-pa chiu(歐羅巴州).

**evacuate**, *a place*, thò--tshut-khṳ̀(退出去); thò-piaⁿ(退兵). *the bowels*, chia̍h-sià-ie̍h(食瀉藥); tshut-kiong(出恭); teng-chhè(登廁); chiẽⁿ-chhè(上廁); tãi-piẽn(大便); kiâⁿ-tãng(行動); pàng-sái(放屎).

**evade**, mién(免); tô(逃); pī(避); pī-bûa(避埋); siám(閃); siám-pī(閃避). *a question, command or invitation*, tshui-úi(推委); tho-sî(推辭).

**evaporate**, pha̍k-ta(曝灱); tsáu-ta(走灱); tshut-khì(出氣); sùaⁿ-khì(散氣); hiàⁿ-khì〔〕; sia̍p-khì(洩氣); hia̍p-huang(熁風).

**even**, pêⁿ(平); pêⁿ-tsôi(平齊); bô-tn̂g-tó(無長短). *is 110 an even or an odd number*, peh-it sĩ sang a-sĩ khia(百一是雙抑是奇). *even if*, tsòng(縱); tsòng-jiên(縱然); tsòng-sái(縱使); sui-jiên(雖然). *even to*, chì-kàu(至到). *even his enemies do not blame him*, kũa i kâi chhiû-te̍k tou bô-hiâm--i(伊个仇敵都無嫌伊). *has he 100 dollars! why, he hasn't even 100 cash*, màiⁿ-tàⁿ i bô che̍k-peh-ngṳ̂n(勿呾伊無一百銀), liên-kũa che̍k-peh-chîⁿ--tou-bô. *he beats even his own parents*, kũa ka-kī kâi-pẽ-bó iā-káⁿ-phah(貫家己个父母也敢拍). *even so far as to...*, sĩm chì-kàu(甚至到).... *evenly arranged*, pâi-tsôi(排齊); pâi-tsâu(排齊); tsôi-chiáⁿ(齊整).

**evening**, ji̍t lo̍h-suaⁿ(日落山); mêⁿ-hng(夜昏); mêⁿ-hng-kiáⁿ(夜昏囝); ji̍t àm(日暗); mêⁿ àm(夜暗). *to-morrow*, mùaⁿ-mêⁿ-hng(滿明昏). *yesterday*, tsa-mêⁿ-hng(昨夜昏).

**event**, sṳ̄(事); che̍k-kiãⁿ-sṳ̄(一件事). *joyful*, âng-sṳ̄(紅事); hí-sṳ̄(喜事); kit-sṳ̄(吉事). *mournful*, pe̍h-sṳ̄(白事); sng-sṳ̄(喪事); hiong-sṳ̄(凶事).

**ever**, *always*, siêⁿ-siêⁿ(常常); sî-sî(時時); kú-kú(久久). *have you ever been there*, lṳ́ pat-kàu hṳ́-kò, méⁿ(汝曾到許塊咩). *ever and anon*, jie̍h-kú jie̍h-kú(若久若久). *I shall come as soon as ever I can*, uá méⁿ-méⁿ chiũ-lâi(我猛猛就來). *for ever*, ióng-kú(永久).

**everlasting**, ióng-kú(永久); kú-tn̂g(久長); ióng-ién(永遠); bô-liáu(無了). *life*, ióng-seⁿ(永生); siêⁿ-seⁿ(常生); chhiâng-seⁿ put-láu(長生不老); chhiâng-seⁿ put-sí(長生不死).

**every**, kak(各). *body*, kak-nâng(各人[訓]); nâng-nâng(人[訓]人[訓]); mih-nâng(乜人[訓]). *day*, múeⁿ-ji̍t(每日); ji̍t-ji̍t(日日); pâi-ji̍t(排日). *one*, kak-kak(各各); kak-kâi(各個); kâi-kâi(個個). *where*, kak-tshù(各處); kak-kò(各塊); múaⁿ-tî-kò(滿底塊); múaⁿ-kò(滿塊); múaⁿ-sì-tshù(滿四處). *thing*, kak-kiãⁿ(各件); kiãⁿ-kiãⁿ(件件); put-lũn sĩ-mih-mue̍h(不論是乜物); huâm-sĩ-mih-mue̍h(凡是乜物). *every tenth man*, tsa̍p-nâng tshú-che̍k(十人[訓]取一). *every four years*, sì-nîⁿ che̍k-pái(四年一擺). *every fall of rain will make it cooler*, pàn-hõu pàn-liâng〔〕.

**evidence**, phêng-kṳ̃(憑據); pêng-kṳ̃(憑據); chèng-kṳ̃(證據). *in court*, tn̂g-keng(堂供); kháu-keng(口供). *to recant*, húan-kháu-keng(反口供); húan-keng(反供).

**evident**, mêng(明); mêng-pe̍h(明白); hién-hīn(顯現); hīn(現).

**evil**, ak(惡); hiong-ak(兇惡). *misfortune*, hũa(禍); tsai-hũa(災禍). *good and evil*, siẽn-ak(善惡). *evil-minded*, ak-sim(惡心). *evil-speak(惡)ing*, húiⁿ-pãng(誹謗); pãng-húiⁿ(謗毀). *to look on one with an evil eye*, kòu-kĩ(妒忌).

**ewe**, iêⁿ-bó(羊母).

**ewer**, tsúi-kùan(水罐).

**exact**, *demand*, thó(討). *exact what is not due*, le̍k-sok(勒索); pak-le̍k(剝勒); khek-pak(刻剝). *hard and exacting*, khek-po̍h(刻薄). *accurate*, sòi-siâng(細詳); siâng-sòi(詳細); tsṳ́-sòi(仔細); kang-hu(工夫); cheng-sòi(精細); sié-sim(小心); miⁿ-ba̍t(密密); sòi-ba̍t(細密). *exactly*, bô-tshò(無錯); tie̍h(着); tùi-tùi(對對). *just exactly*, nẽⁿ tùi-tùi〔〕.

**exaggeration**, tàⁿ-ūe khah-kùe-ûi(呾話較過圍); tàⁿ khah-kùe-sĩm(呾較過甚); tàⁿ khah-kùe-tōu(呾較過度). *(fabulous stories)*, huang-thâng(荒唐).

**exalt**, kṳ́(舉); kṳ́-khí(舉起); kau-kṳ́(高舉). *oneself*, tsṳ̃-kau(自高).

**examine**, chhê(查); húang-mn̄g(訪問); sím-mn̄g(審問); séⁿ-tshat(省察); kàm-tshat(監察); sòi-thóiⁿ(細睇); kháu-kiù(考究). *goods*, chhê-hùe(查貨). *a witness*, mn̄g-keng(問經). *literary examination*, kháu-kà(考教); kháu-chhì(考試); kháu-tsṳ(考書); kháu-mn̄g(考問).

**example**, iēⁿ(樣); môⁿ-iēⁿ(模樣); piáu-iēⁿ(表樣). *for example*, phì-zũ(譬喻); phì-zû(譬如).

**exasperate**, kek-nâng-khì(激人氣); sái-nâng-khì(使人氣); lõng-nâng-khì(弄人氣); tshok-nâng-khì(觸人氣).

**excavate**, liú-khang(㧕空); khui-khang(開空); ku̍t-khang(掘空).

**exceed**, kùe(過). *bounds*, kùe-hūn(過分); kùe-liãng(過量); kùe-tōu(過度). *exceedingly*, siãng(上); tsa̍p-hun(十分). *exceedingly (after the qualified word)*, tsãi(在). *excessively*, khah-kùe-tōa(較過大); khah-kùe-thâu(較過頭); khah-kùe-sĩm(較過甚); khah-thài-kùe(較太過).

**excel**, iâⁿ(贏); iâⁿ--kùe(贏過); kiêⁿ--kùe(強過); hó--kùe(好過). *excellent*, siãng-hó(上好); múiⁿ(美). *Your Excellency*, tãi-jîn(大人); tōa-lãu-iâ(大老爺); thài-iâ(太爺).

**except**, tṳ̂(除); tṳ̂-gūa(除外). *none except this man came*, chheng tshṳ́-nâng lâi, ãu bô-nâng-lâi(清此人來，後無人來). *all are come except so & so*, lóng-tsóng kàu--liáu toaⁿ móng-nâng būe-kàu(攏總到了單某人未到).

**exchange**, uāⁿ(換); tùi-uāⁿ(對換); sie-uāⁿ(相換); kau-uāⁿ(交換); thiâu-uāⁿ(調換). *places*, sie-uāⁿ-ūi(相換位). *money*, táu-chîⁿ(討錢).

**excise**, hiàng-sùe(餉稅); hiàng-ngṳ̂n(餉銀).

**excite**, *people*, tõng-nâng-sim(動人心); kám-tõng(感動). *excite and draw upon oneself, as trouble*, jiá(惹); ín-jiá(引起). *instigate*, kòiⁿ-so(間唆); kà-so(教唆); kà-lā(教唆). *an enemy to battle*, jiá-chièn(惹戰). *cause excitement*, seⁿ-sṳ̄(生事). *public excitement*, nâng-sim iâu-tõng(人心搖動).

**exclaim**, hàm(喊); kiè(叫); khui-siaⁿ(開聲); tōa-siaⁿ-tàⁿ(大聲呾); jiáng(嚷).

**exclude**, tṳ̂(除); to̍k-tshut(逐出); kek-tshut(激出); bô-i-ji̍p(無伊入); khì-tõ-gūa(棄在外). *exclusive of*, tṳ̂-hui(除非); tṳ̂-gūa(除外); màiⁿ-sǹg(勿算); lêng-gūa(另外).

**excoriate**, lṳ̀-phùa-phûe〔〕; lṳ̀ kàu-phiù-phûe〔〕; phiù-phûe〔〕.

**excrement**, pùn(糞); sái(駛).

**exculpate**, kàu-sù(告訴); ín-chèng piáu-mêng(引證表明).

**excuse**, sṳ̀(事). *please excuse me*, chhiáⁿ-sù--chē(請恕些); sià-tsũe(赦罪); sù-tsũe(恕罪); chhiáⁿ-sî(請辭). *faults*, thóiⁿ-phùa(睇破); sià-tsũe; khuan-iông(寬容).

**execrable**, khó-ù(可惡); khó-hṳ̃n(可恨).

**execute**, tsò(做); tsò-chiâⁿ(做成); khîⁿ--tshut-lâi〔〕. *put to death*, thâi(刣). *execution*, sí-hêng(死刑). *execution ground*, kah-tiêⁿ(割場). *executioner*, khùai-tsṳ́-chhiú(刽子手); khùai-tsṳ́-siú(刽子手); suah-siú(殺手); tng-âng-kî(當紅旗).

**executor**, siũ-hù-thoh kâi-nâng(受付託个人). *(guardian)*, thoh-kou kâi-nâng(託孤个人).

**exemplary**, kṳ́-tõng tuan-chiàⁿ(舉動端正); hó-iēⁿ(好樣); hó-pun-nâng tsò-iēⁿ(好分人做樣).

**exempt**, bô-tō-lāi(無待來); tõ-gūa(在外). *from taxation*, mién-na̍p-hiàng(免納餉).

**exercise**, *take*, khṳ̀-thit-thô(去佚佗); kiâⁿ-tsáu ua̍h-tõng(行走活動); kiâⁿ-sóng-khùai(行爽快); khṳ̀-siau-iâu(去蕭謠). *literary*, tsò-bûn(做文); tsò-bûn-chieⁿ(做文章); bûn-gōi(文藝). *soldiers*, tshau-piaⁿ(操兵); tshau-liēn(操練). *learn military*, o̍h-bú(學武). *exercise in*, liēn(練); ha̍k-si̍p(學習); o̍h(學).

**exert**, *oneself*, tshut-la̍t(出力); khat-khóu(刻苦); tie̍h-la̍t(着力); tie̍h-khṳ̂n(着勤); ēng-sim(用心). *one's voice*, khui-tōa-siaⁿ(開大聲). *one's influence*, sái-sì(使勢).

**exhale**, huat-khì(發氣); tshut-khì(出氣). *exhalation*, khì(氣). *from water*, tsúi-khì(水氣). *damp*, sip-khì(濕氣).

**exhaust**, chĩn(盡); khiông(窮); liáu(了); hùi(費); ēng-chĩn(用盡); ēng-liáu(用了); phùa-chĩn(破盡). *strength*, la̍t hùi-chĩn(力費盡). *money*, chîⁿ-sái-uân(錢使完). *food*, bí-niêⁿ chia̍h-liáu(米糧食了). *exhausted (wearied)*, he̍k(乏); phì-kũan(疲倦); khùn(睏); khùn-siên(睏𤺪).

**exhibit**, hién-mêng(顯明); huat-hīn(發現). *goods*, pái-lie̍t(排列); pái-siet(擺設); phou-pâi(鋪排). *in competition*, sài(賽).

**exhilarated**, khin-sang(輕鬆); thiàng-khùai(暢快).

**exhort**, khǹg-kòi(勸戒). *to peace*, khǹg-hûa(勸化). *tracts exhorting to virtue*, khǹg-sì-bûn(勸世文).

**exigency**, kín-kip kâi-sṳ̄(緊急个事); kín-iàu kâi-sṳ̄(緊要个事). *from the exigency of the case*, bô-khó nãi-hô(無可奈何).

**exile**, see BANISH.

**exist**, ũ(有); tõ(在). *still in existence*, huân-tshûn--tõ-kò(還存在塊).

**exit**, tshut(出); tshut--khṳ̀(出去). *end*, tsong(終). *door*, lōu-mn̂g(路門).

**exonerate**, huan-ùaⁿ(翻案). *exonerated*, thut-tsũe(脫罪).

**exorbitant**, keh-gūa(格外); thài-sĩm(太甚); thài-kùe(太過). *price*, kùi-tsãi(貴在); khah-kùi(較貴).

**exorcise**, liām-chiù to̍k-kúi(念咒逐鬼); khṳ̀-siâ(去邪); phek-siâ(辟邪); khu-tṳ̂ iau-môⁿ(驅除妖毛).

**exotic**, pa̍t-kò-chéng(別塊種).

**expand**, khui-khuah(開闊); pàng-khui(放開); tièⁿ-tōa(展大). *expanse of heaven*, thiⁿ-khong(天空); chheⁿ-thiⁿ(青天); chheⁿ-khong(星空). *expansive*, kúang-khuah(廣闊).

**expect**, mōⁿ(望); hi-mōⁿ(希望). *(erroneously)*, kâu-kiè(猴叫).

**expectorate**, khak-thâm(殼痰); thòu-thâm-nũaⁿ(吐痰涎); phùi-nũaⁿ(呸涎).

**expedient**, ha̍h(合); piẽn(便); sũn-piẽn(順便).

**expedition**, *military*, khṳ̀-gūa sie-thâi(去外相刣); tshut-chièn(出戰).

**expeditious**, méⁿ(猛); khùe(快); méⁿ-méⁿ(猛猛); khùe-khùe(快快); kín-kín(緊緊).

**expel**, to̍k-tshut(逐出); kek-tshut(激出); khu-to̍k(驅逐); jiāu-khṳ̀〔〕.

**expend**, sái(使); sái-ēng(使用); phùa(破); hùi(費); hùi-ēng(費用). *expenditure*, só-hùi(所費); hùi-ēng(費用). *daily*, ji̍t-ēng(日用). *travelling*, lōu-hùi(路費); pûaⁿ-tîⁿ(盤纏).

**expensive**, kùi(貴); ke-chîⁿ(加錢); ta̍t-chîⁿ(值錢). *living*, só-hùi tōa(所費大).

**experience**, liēn(練); liēn-ta̍t(練達). *experienced*, ũ-liēn(有練); liēn-se̍k(練熟); se̍k(熟); se̍k-chhiú(熟手); kùan-liēn(慣練); kùan-se̍k(慣熟); kùiⁿ-sìⁿ(慣勢); keng-le̍h(經曆).

**experiment**, chhì(試); chhì-thóiⁿ(試睇); chhì-ēng(試用); chhì-thóiⁿ tsãi-seⁿ(試睇在生); thèng-tsãu-hùe(聽造化).

**expert**, se̍k-chhiú(熟手); ki-khá(機巧); õi(會); gâu(賢); khî-khiáu(奇巧); kuai-khiáu(乖巧); kha-chhiú õi(骹手能).

**expiate**, so̍k-tsũe(贖罪).

**expire**, tñg-khùi(斷氣); khùi tñg(氣斷); nâng kùe(人過). *time*, kàu-khî(到期); ji̍t-khî íⁿ-múaⁿ(日期已滿); kùe-khî(過期).

**explain**, kói(解); kói-mêng(解明); sueh(說); kói-sueh(解說); káng-kói(講解); tàⁿ-phùa(呾破); chí-phùa(指破); káng-pe̍h(講白); káng-lũn(講論). *explanation or commentary*, tsù-kói(注解).

**expletive**, hṳ-jī(虛字).

**explicit**, mêng-pe̍h(明白).

**explode**, kek-li̍h(激裂); kek-phùa(激破). *as gunpowder*, húe-ie̍h to̍h-húe(火藥着火); húe-ie̍h kún-phùa(火藥滾破).

**exploit**, kong-lâu(功勞); tōa-kong-lâu(大功勞).

**explore**, *places*, *for amusement*, iû-kuan(遊觀); iû-ngúan(遊玩). *search*, chhîm-tshūe(尋覓); thàm-chhîm(探尋). *with a clue*, thàm-soh(探索).

**export**, *to*, tsài-hùe tshut-kháu(載貨出口). *exports*, tshut-kháu kâi-hùe-mue̍h(出口个貨物).

**expose**, lòu-tshut(露出). *one's life*, piàⁿ-miāⁿ(拚命); tì-miāⁿ(致命); m̄-kù sèⁿ-miāⁿ(毋顧性命); put-sieh sin-miāⁿ(不惜身命). *criminals' heads*, hiau-siú sī-chèng(梟手示眾). *oneself to the sun*, pha̍k-ji̍t(曝日). *people's motives*, sueh-phùa nâng-sim(說破人心).

**expostulate**, khóu-khǹg(苦勸); la̍t-khǹg(力勸); chhiet-khǹg(切勸); hiâm(嫌); cheh-khǹg(責勸); khǹg-kài(勸戒).

**expound**, see EXPLAIN.

**express**, tàⁿ(呾); tàⁿ-tshut(呾出); káng-tshut(講出); sueh-tshut(說出). *one's opinion*, tàⁿ-tshut ì-kièn(呾出意見). *purpose*, piáu-mêng ì-sṳ̀(表明意思). *juice*, tẽⁿ-tsap(捏汁); liū-tsap(鎦汁). *juice of sugar cane*, ká-thn̂g(絞糖). *an express*, tsuan-sái kâi-nâng(專使个人); pò-bé(報馬). *government express*, tshoiⁿ-lí-bé(千里馬). *express purpose*, tõu-tsuan-ài(肚專愛).

**expression**, jī-ma̍k(字目); che̍k-kù-ūe(一句話); ūe-kù(話句). *of face*, mīn-sek(面色). *sad expression*, mīn-sek hûan-ló(面色煩惱).

**expressly**, tsuan(專); te̍k-te̍k(特特); ũ-ì(有意); chhiet-chhiet(切切).

**expunge**, kôu-buah(糊抹); tiám-tiāu(點掉); khou-tiāu(箍掉); hú-tiāu〔〕. *(as useless words or sentences)*, san-tiāu(刪掉); kau-tiāu(交掉).

**exquisite**, tsa̍p-hun-hó(十分好); chĩn-hó(盡好); siãng-iùⁿ(上幼); siãng-kang-hu(上工夫); chin-ngiá(真雅); chì-ngiá(至雅); siãng-múiⁿ(上美).

**extempore**, *speech*, sũn-tshùi-káng(順喙講); chiũ-sî-tàⁿ(就時呾). *composition*, phah-sim-kó(拍心稿).

**extend**, *spread widely*, iâng(揚); pùa(播). *stretch out*, tshun(伸). *extend to*, chì-kàu(至到); phóu-ki̍p(普及). *everywhere*, bô-só put-chì(無所不至). *extensive*, khuah(闊); kúang-khuah(廣闊); khùaⁿ(寬). *what is the extent of it*, ũ-jie̍h-tōa(有若大); ũ-jie̍h-khuah(有若闊).

**exterior**, gūa-mīn(外面); gū-mãuⁿ(外貌); gūa-thâu(外頭); gūa-phûe(外皮); gūa-pôiⁿ(外爿).

**exterminate**, mi̍t-tso̍h(滅絕); tu-mi̍t(誅滅); tshau-mi̍t(操滅); tṳ̂-mi̍t(除滅); thâi-chĩn(刣盡).

**external**, see EXTERIOR.

**extinct**, mi̍t-buâng(滅亡); bô--liáu(無了). *posterity*, bô-aũ(無後); tso̍h-sṳ̂(絕嗣).

**extinguish**, mi̍t(滅). *fire*, phah-húe kùe(拍火過); mi̍t-húe(滅火); phah-mi̍t(拍滅); kiù-húe(救火). *lamp*, pûn-kùe(歕過); iãⁿ-kùe(贏過); phuah-kùe(潑過).

**extirpate**, tshau-mi̍t(操滅); po̍ih-kṳn(拔根); tñg-kṳn(斷根); pi̍t-po̍ih-tiāu(畢拔掉); mán-chĩn(滿盡).

**extol**, tsàn-múiⁿ(讚美); sõng-tsàn(頌讚); chheng-tsàn(稱讚); chheng-sõng(稱頌); sõng-múiⁿ(頌美); o-ló(呵咾).

**extort**, *a false confession*, khut-phah sêng-chiau(屈拍成招). *extortion*, le̍k-sok(勒索); khek-pak(刻剝); pak-le̍k(剝勒); khiâng-tshú khiâng-to̍h(強取強奪).

**extract**, po̍ih(拔); khie̍h-tshut(挈出); thiu-tshut(抽出); túi--tshut(挽出). *from a book*, ín-tsṳ-kù(引字句); lo̍k-tsṳ(錄字); ín-lo̍k(引錄).

**extraordinary**, khî-sṳ̄(奇事); khî-ĩ(奇異); tshut-khî(出奇); hui-siêⁿ(非常); koh-iēⁿ(各樣); chié-ũ(少有); hán-tit thóiⁿ--kìⁿ(罕得睇見); hán-ngõ(罕我). *extraordinarily good*, khî-hó(奇好); hó kàu-koh-iēⁿ(好到閣樣).

**extravagant**, hua-hùi(花費); lãm-ēng(濫用); thèng-ēng(逞用); chhia-chhí(奢侈); chhia-hûa(奢華); phah-phún-sái(拍糞屎); thài-kùe(太過); hàuⁿ-sái(好屎); káⁿ-sái-chîⁿ(敢屎錢).

**extremely**, ke̍k-kàu-ke̍k(極到極); ke̍k--tshù(極厝); kàu-chì-ke̍k(到至極); chì(至); tsa̍p-hun(十分); tsãi(盡); siãng(上). *extremely ugly*, iá-iēⁿ-tsãi(野樣在). *good*, ke̍k-hó(極好); chì-hó(至好). *use extreme measures*, ēng-kàu-ke̍k kâi-huap(用到極个法). *two extremities of anything*, thâu-búe(頭尾). *utmost extremity of misery, &c*, ke̍k-mn̂g(極門).

**extricate**, kiù-tshut(救出); kói-thut(解脫); kói-tshut(解出).

**exuberant**, *foliage*, mõng-sẽng(茂盛); heng-sẽng(興盛); phò-phò〔〕; ap-ap〔〕.

**exude**, *perspiration*, huat-kūaⁿ(發汗); lâu-kūaⁿ(流汗); piáu-kūaⁿ(表汗). *walls*, chhiêⁿ chhiẽⁿ-ĩm(牆向陰). *plants*, tshut-tsap(出汁); tshut-nîⁿ(出年).

**exult**, tōa-tōa huaⁿ-hí(大大歡喜); huaⁿ-hí kàu-thiàu(歡喜到跳); huaⁿ-hí chì-ke̍k(歡喜至極).

**exuviae**, tsûa pak-khak(蛇剝殼); thâng pak-khak(蟲剝殼).

**eye**, ma̍k(目); ma̍k-chiu(目睭). *sharp*, ma̍k-chiu lêng(目睭靈); ma̍k-chiu lêng-lāi(目睭靈利). *dim*, ma̍k-chiu hue(目睭花); ma̍k mông-bū(目蒙霧); ma̍k bū(目霧). *sore*, ma̍k-chiu thiàⁿ(目睭痛). *open*, ma̍k peh-kim(目睜金); ma̍k khui-khui(目開開). *close*, ma̍k ha̍p-miⁿ(目合眠); ma̍k miⁿ-miⁿ(目眠眠). *red*, ma̍k-kṳn âng(目根紅). *inflamed*, ma̍k seⁿ-húe(目生火); ma̍k âng(目紅); ma̍k pãu-thiàⁿ(目曝痛). *turn up the white of*, ma̍k póiⁿ-pe̍h(目反白). *wink*, nihⁿ-ma̍k(眨目); ma̍k-chiu khap-khap-nihⁿ(目睭怯怯眨). *as signal*, su̍h-ma̍k(箭目). *squint*, siâ-chiáu-ma̍k(斜朝目); tshúa-ma̍k(歪目). *near-sighted*, kṳ̃n-sĩ-ma̍k(近視目). *wide and staring, as thief's*, ma̍k kok-kok-kim〔〕. *pupil of*, thông-jîn(瞳仁); sien-nâng-thâu(仙人頭). *brows*, ma̍k-bâi(目眉). *ball*, ma̍k-chiu-jîn(目睭仁). *white of*, ma̍k-pe̍h-jîn(目白仁). *lashes*, ma̍k-chhì-môⁿ(目刺毛). *lids*, ma̍k-kha-phûe(目骹皮); ma̍k-pau(目包). *inner corner*, ma̍k-thâu(目頭). *outer corner*, ma̍k-búe(目尾). *eye-hollow*, ma̍k-khóng(目孔); ma̍k-khuang(目眶); ma̍k-úaⁿ(目碗). *sight*, ma̍k-chiu kng(目睭光). *eye-glass*, ma̍k-kiàⁿ(目鏡). *eyeless*, sit-mêng(失明); chheⁿ-mêⁿ(青盲); hak-ngán(瞎眼). *medicine*, ma̍k-ie̍h-tsúi(目藥水). *salve*, ma̍k-ie̍h-ko(目藥膏). *eye-witness*, chhin-ma̍k thóiⁿ--kìⁿ(親目睇見). *of spectacles*, ma̍k-kiàⁿ-jîn(目鏡仁); ma̍k-kiàⁿ-ne̍k(目鏡肉). *of needle*, tsam-phīⁿ(針鼻); tsam-khang(針空). *bull's-eye*, pá-sim(飽心). *to hit it*, tòng-âng-sim(凍紅心). *please the eye*, ha̍h-ma̍k(合目); zua̍t-ma̍k(悅目). *make the eyes smart (as pepper)*, soh--tie̍h ma̍k(索着目). *get a mote in the eye*, ma̍k eng--tie̍h(目煙着). *before the eyes of all*, tõ-chèng-nâng mīn-tsôiⁿ(在眾人面前). *great in one's own eyes*, ka-kī tsṳ̃-sĩ tsò-tōa(家己自視做大);  tsṳ̃-tsun(自尊). *wise in one's own eyes*, tsṳ̃-gâu(自賢); tsṳ̃-hiên(自懸). *fix the eyes on one*, ma̍k kim-kim tõ-thóiⁿ(目金金在睇).

### F

**fable**, phì-zũ(譬喻). *to use a*, chieh-phì-zũ(借譬喻); siet-phì(設譬). *fabulous*, hṳ-tãng(虛重); buáng-tãng(妄重); bô-iáⁿ-chiah(無影跡).

**face**, mīn(面); mīn-mãuⁿ(面貌); mīn-sek(面色). *before one's*, mīn-tsôiⁿ(面前); tng-mīn(當面); tùi-mīn(對面). *face to face*, tùi-mīn(對面); tng-mīn(當面). *meet face to face*, hũe-mīn(會面). *shape of*, mīn-hêng(面行); mīn-bé(面馬). *long-faced*, mīn-bé tn̂g-tn̂g(面馬長長). *skin of*, mīn-phûe(面皮). *pallid*, mīn n̂g-sng(面黃酸). *cloth for washing face*, mīn-pòu(面布). *brazen-faced*, mīn-phûe kãu(面皮厚). *facing the south*, niàⁿ-nâm(向南); hiàⁿ-nâm(向南北); hiàng-nâm(向南); chhiâu-nâm(朝南). *face round*, hûe-thâu(回頭); u̍t-tńg-thâu(夗轉頭); hui-tńg-thâu(回轉頭). *facing one another*, siang-tùi(相對); siang-tùi-mīn(相對面).

**facetious**, *hàuⁿ-tàⁿ-sńg; hàuⁿ-tàⁿ-khá*, hàuⁿ-tàⁿ tshù-bī(好呾趣味); hàuⁿ-tshu-chhiè(好趣笑); hó-chhiè(好笑).

**facile**, kōi(易); sũn-nâng-chhêng(順人情); sũn-nâng-ì(順人意); hàuⁿ-khiâ sũn-huang-kî(好騎順風旗).

**fact**, si̍t-sṳ̄(實事); si̍t-chhêng(實情). *facts of the case*, sṳ̄-chhêng(事情); chhêng-iû(情由); sṳ̄-si̍t(事實); si̍t-chiah(實跡).

**factor**, *agent*, thòi-phōiⁿ(代辦); thòi-pōiⁿ(代辦); thòi-lí(代理).

**factory**, *large mercantile house*, hâng(行); hâng-kháu(行口).

**fade**, *flower*, sià(瀉). *colour*, thò-sek(褪色). *grow smaller*, sue-mûiⁿ(衰微).

**faculty**, tshâi(才); tshâi-chhêng(才情); tshâi-lêng(才能); pún-sṳ̄(本事).

**fagot**, *of wood*, khún-tshâ(捆柴); pé-tshâ(把柴); che̍k-pé ta-chhiū-ki(一把大樹枝).

**fagged**, khùn(睏); he̍k(乏); khùn-tõaⁿ(睏惰); khùn-siên(睏𤺪); siên(𤺪).

**fail**, sit(失); sit-sṳ̄(失事); gōu-sṳ̄(誤事). *of promise*, sit-sìn(失信); sit-ieh(失約); chia̍h-ngân(食言). *in business*, tó-tièⁿ(倒賬); hiah-sṳ̄(歇事). *failing or fault*, kùe-sit(過失).

**fain**, *to do anything*, àiⁿ-tsò(愛做); huaⁿ-hí-tsò(歡喜做); kho-leng-àiⁿ(苛燈愛).

**faint**, *exhausted*, khùn-tõaⁿ(睏惰). *to*, sit-hûn(失魂); m̄-tsai-nâng(毋知人); m̄-hiáu-nâng(毋曉人); kông-kông(戇戇); ka-tsua̍h-hîn(膠絀眩); hûn put-hù-thói(魂不復體); hûn sùaⁿ(魂散). *faint-hearted*, sàng-sim(散心); sàng-táⁿ(散膽). *colour*, chhién-sek(淺色); tãⁿ-sek(淡色).

**fair**, *beautiful*, múiⁿ(美); ngiá(雅). *woman*, múiⁿ-jîn(美人); múiⁿ-mãuⁿ(美貌); kia-jîn(佳人); ge̍k-jîn(玉人). *complexion*, ne̍k-sek soh-soh-pe̍h(肉色雪雪白). *weather*, chêⁿ-thiⁿ(晴天); thiⁿ chêⁿ(天晴). *price*, kuaⁿ-chiàⁿ bói-bōi(官正買賣). *wind*, sũn-huang(順風); huang-mīn hó(風面好). *prospect*, hó-kuang-kéng(好光景). *a fair*, hṳ(墟); chhĩ(市). *go to the*, tàu-hṳ(鬥墟); tàu-chhĩ(鬥市).

**fairy**, see ELF. *fairy-land*, sien-kéng(仙境).

**faith**, sìn(信); siang-sìn(相信). *reliance*, sìn-kõu(信靠); íⁿ-kõu(椅靠). *fidelity*, sìn(信); sìn-tek(信德); tong-sìn(忠信); sìn-si̍t(信實); hó-siang-sìn(好相信). *faithful*, tong-kãu(忠厚); tong-hõu(忠厚); tong-sìn(忠信); bô-nõⁿ-sim(無兩心). *having faith*, ũ-sìn(有信); sìn(信); sièn(煽). *strong faith*, chhim-sìn(深信); kãu-sìn(厚信); tok-sìn(篤信). *faithless*, pũe-sìn bô-ngĩ(背信無義).

**falcon**, eng-chiáu(鷹鳥).

**fall**, pua̍h(跌); lo̍h(落); ka-la̍u(倒落); kau-la̍uh(交落). *fall as house*, tó(倒); tó--lo̍h-lâi(倒落來); pang(崩). *fall in*, tha̍p(塌). *fall down (as person)*, pua̍h--tie̍h(跋着); pua̍h-lo̍h(跌落); tie̍h-pua̍h(着跋). *fall down (as thing)*, ka-la̍u(倒落)h. *fall into a snare*, lo̍h-khuan-thàu(落圈套). *fall in with*, ngõ--tie̍h(遇着). *to pieces*, sùaⁿ(散); sùaⁿ-tiāu(散掉). *leaves*, lo̍h-hie̍h(落葉). *as landslip*, suaⁿ pang, tī hām(地陷); pang-hām(崩陷). *rain*, lo̍h-hõu(落雨). *dew*, lo̍h-lōu-tsúi(落露水). *heavy fall of dew*, lōu-tsúi tãng(露水重); lōu-tsúi kãu(露水厚). *empire*, kok bûang(國亡). *flowers*, hue sià(花謝). *at any body's feet*, phak tõ-kha-ẽ(伏蹠骹下); phak-lo̍h-tī(伏落在). *fall upon (as enemy)*, kong-phah(攻拍); kong-khek(攻擊). *fall into one's hands*, pĩ-lia̍h(被掠). *price*, lo̍h-kè(落價); thu̍t-kè(脫過); tie̍t-kè(跌價). *fall away*, lī-khui(離開). *from religion*, pũe-kà(背教). *on one's neck*, phõ-ãm(抱頷); lám-kín-ãm(攬緊頷). *tide*, khó-lâu(洘流); lâu khó(流洘). *waterfall*, pha̍k-pòu-tsûaⁿ(瀑布泉). *(a rapid) waterfall*, thuaⁿ(灘). *falling star*, pue-chheⁿ(飛星); liû-chheⁿ(流星); chheng-sîn kùe-tōu(星辰過度). *falling-sickness*, see EPILEPSY.

**fallible**, õi-tshò(會錯).

**fallow**, *ground*, tshân-tī phau-hng(田地拋荒).

**false**, ké(假); hṳ-ké(虛假); ngũi(偽); tsà-ngũi(詐僞); hue-niauⁿ(花貓). *money*, ké kâi-ngṳ̂n(假个銀). *falsehood*, ké-ūe(假話); hṳ-ké kâi-ūe(虛假个話); phièn-nâng kâi-ūe(騙人个話); hue-tshùi hue-chi̍h(花喙花舌). *witness*, ké tsò-chèng-kṳ̃(假做證據). *charge*, bû-lūa(誣賴); bû-kò(誣告); bû-khòng(誣控); niap-kò(捏告). *purpose, intention*, ké-ì(假意). *falsely pretend not to know*, ké-tsò m̄-tsai(假做毋知); tèⁿ-tsò m̄-tsai(挺做毋知); iâng-ûi put-tsai(陽爲不知); tèⁿ-chhi(佯痴). *false goodness, hypocrisy*, ké-hó(假好). *falsely use another man's name*, ké nâng-kâi-miâⁿ(假人个名); mãuⁿ-miâⁿ(冒名).

**falter**, huan-ho̍k bô-tiāⁿ(翻覆無定).

**fame**, miâⁿ(名); miâⁿ-siaⁿ(名聲); siaⁿ-bũn(聲聞). *famous*, tshut-miâⁿ(出名); hién-miâⁿ(顯名); miâⁿ-siaⁿ pùa-iâng(名聲播揚). *famous fame(polite phrase)*, bûn-miâⁿ(文名).

**familiar**, siang-se̍k(相熟); sie-pat(相識). *most familiar friend*, chì-se̍k kâi phêng-iú(至熟个朋友); sù-se̍k kâi phêng-iú(素熟个朋友).

**family**, ke(家); ke-kùan(家眷); ke-hõu(家後); ke-so̍k(家屬). *whole*, ha̍p-ke(合家); hãm-ke(憾家); thong-ke(通家); che̍k-ke(一家); tshûan-ke(全家). *clan*, sèⁿ(姓); tso̍k(族). *property*, ke-sṳ̄(家事); ke-ngia̍p(家業); ke-tshâi(家財); ke-tsṳ(家資); ke-húe(家伙). *discipline*, ke-kà(家教); ke-kui(家規). *state of family as regards behaviour and prosperity*, ke-sì(家世). *to manage the*, hūaⁿ-ke(捍家); lí-ke(理家). *ruin*, phùa-ke(破家). *unbroken family*, che̍k-ke thûan-thûan-îⁿ(一家團團圓).

**famine**, ki-hng(饑荒).

**famish**, gō(餓). *thin and famished*, gō-sán(餓㾪). *to death*, gō-sí(餓死).

**fan**, sìⁿ(扇). *one*, che̍k-ki-sìⁿ(一支扇). *to use*, khie̍h-sìⁿ(挈扇); khiâ-sìⁿ(騎扇); lĩm-sìⁿ(臨扇); phuah-sìⁿ(潑扇); phuah-huang(潑風); iãⁿ-sìⁿ(向扇); iãⁿ-huang(向風). *beckon one with*, ia̍h-sìⁿ(葉扇). *for winnowing grain*, pùa-ki(簸箕). *for winnowing grain (fanners)*, huang-kūiⁿ(風櫃). *to extinguish a lamp with a fan*, iãⁿ-kùe teng-húe(向過燈火).

**fancy**, *I fancy he will not come*, úa phah-sǹg i m̃-lâi(我拍算伊毋來). *fancy articles*, thit-thô-mue̍h(佚佗物).

**fang**, *tooth*, tōa-gê(大牙).

**far**, hñg(遠); iâu-ién(遙遠). *and near*, hñg-kṳ̃n(遠近). *far greater*, tōa tsōi(大㩼). *far different*, tsua̍h hñg(絀遠); tsua̍h tsōi(絀㩼); tōa-tsua̍h(大絀); tōa-ē m̄-sie-tâng(大下毋是同); tōa-ē tsáu-tsua̍h(大下走絀).

**fare**, *boat*, tsûn-tsou(船租); tsûn-hùi(船費).

**farewell**, *bid*, kāng nâng tsak-pie̍t(共人作別); sàng-pie̍t(送別). *a farewell feast*, chién-kiâⁿ kâi-toh-sia̍h(餞行个桌席).

**farm**, tshân(田); tshân-tī(田地); tshân-hn̂g(田園). *farmer*, tsoh-tshân-nâng(作田人); lông-jîn(農人); lông-hu(農夫); keⁿ-hu(耕夫). *do farm work*, tsoh-tshân(作田); keⁿ-tsoh(耕作); chèng-tsoh(種作); tsoh-si̍t(作實).

**farrier**, ui-gû-bé sin-seⁿ(醫牛馬先生).

**farrow**, *to*, tṳ-bó seⁿ-tṳ-kiáⁿ(豬母生豬囝).

**fascinate**, mîⁿ-ho̍k(迷服). *fascinating*, iau-jiâu(妖嬈); zua̍h-sí-nâng(熱死人); kuah-tiàu-nâng(割吊人).

**fashion**, sî-heng(時興); sî-siãng(時尚). *new*, sin-iēⁿ(新樣); sin-khuán(新款); sin-sî-heng(新時興). *fashionable*, ha̍h-sî-heng(合時興); ha̍h-sî-phài(合時派); tng-sî(當時). *person*, hàuⁿ-sin-khuán(好新款). *doctor*, kiâⁿ-sî ui-seng(行時威風); sî-kiâⁿ sin-seⁿ(時行新聲).

**fast**, méⁿ(猛); khùe(快). *boat*, khùai-théng(快艇). *bound*, pa̍k-kín(縛緊). *colour*, bõi-lo̍h-sek(袂落色); lân-lo̍h-sek(藍落色). *asleep*, gu̍t kàu-tsùi-tsùi(夗到醉醉); gu̍t kàu-chhim-chhim(夗到深深). *hold*, lia̍h-kín(掠緊); chip-kín(執緊); lĩm-kín(臨緊). *to fast*, kìm-chia̍h(禁食); chia̍h-che(食齋).

**fasten**, pa̍k(縛). *to anything*, pa̍k-tùe(縛綴). *door*, tshùaⁿ-mn̂g(閂門).

**fastidious**, oh-huaⁿ-hí(惡歡喜). *about food*, hiâm-chia̍h(嫌食); õi-kóiⁿ-chia̍h(會揀食); póiⁿ-khóiⁿ-chia̍h(反蓋食).

**fat**, pûi(肥). *(more polite of a person)*, tshâi-khì(財氣). *of meat*, pe̍h-ne̍k(白肉). *lard*, lâ(朥).

**fatal**, kau-kùa sèⁿ-miāⁿ(交掛性命); tì-miāⁿ(致命); tì-sí(致命). *disease*, sí-chèng(死症); ngẽ-chèng bô-ui(硬正無醫).

**fate**, miāⁿ(命); miāⁿ-ūn(命運); sî-ūn(時運). *murmur at*, chiù-sin mēⁿ-miāⁿ(咒身罵命).

**father**, pẽ(父); lãu-pẽ(老父); pẽ-chhin(父親); a-tia(阿爹); a-pa(阿爸). *your father*, nín tōa--náng(恁大人); lẽng-tsun(令尊). *your late father*, lēng-soiⁿ-tsun(令先尊); lẽng-soiⁿ-ong(令先翁). *my father*, ke-hũ(家父); ke-tsun(家尊). *my late father*, uá soiⁿ-hũ(我先父). *wife's father*, tiẽⁿ-nâng(丈人); nga̍k-pẽ(岳父); tiẽⁿ-nâng-kong(丈人公). *husband's father*, ta-kuaⁿ(大家). *one's own*, seⁿ-pẽ(生父); seⁿ-sín tsṳ-pún(生身之本). *sort of adoptive father*, ngĩ-pẽ(義父); khòi-pẽ(契父). *step-father*, iáng-pẽ(養父); kì-pẽ(繼父); ãu-pẽ(後父). *fatherless*, bô-pẽ kâi-kiáⁿ(無父个囝); kou-tsṳ́(孤子).

**fathom**, *water*, thàm-thóiⁿ tsúi jie̍h-chhim(探睇水若深). *one fathom*, che̍k-chhíⁿ(一齒); che̍k-siâm(一尋). *fathomless*, m̄-hó chhek-ta̍t(毋好測度); chhim-bô-tói(深無底).

**fatigue**, he̍k(乏); phî-kũan(疲倦); kha sng(骹酸); siên(𤺪); khùn-siên(睏𤺪). *fatigue oneself*, lâu-la̍t(勞力); bûa-lâu(磨勞).

**fault**, kùe(過); kùe-sit(過失); tshò(錯); m̄-tie̍h(毋着); tshò-gōu(錯誤); put-si(不是). *fault-finding*, hàuⁿ-hiâm nâng m̄-tie̍h(好嫌人毋着); hàuⁿ ngí-lũn-nâng(好議論人); hàuⁿ phoi-tso̍ih-nâng(好批截人). *faultless*, bô-hó-hiâm(無好嫌); bô-hó-hiâm--tshù(無好嫌厝); bô-m̄-tie̍h(無毋着); bô-kùe-sit(無過失); bô-hiâ-tshṳ̂(無瑕疵).

**favour**, ṳn(恩); ṳn-tién(恩典); ṳn-ài(恩愛); ṳn-hũi(恩惠). *confer a favour*, si-ṳn(施恩); kiâⁿ-nâng-chhêng(行人情); tsò-chhêng(做情). *ask favour or pardon for another*, khiû-chhêng(求情); khí-nâng-chhêng(起人情). *thankful for*, kám-ṳn(感恩); liãm-ṳn(念恩). *forgetful of*, bûang-ṳn(忘恩); bûang-ṳn hũ-ngĩ(忘恩負義); hiau-hũ ṳn-chhêng(僥負恩情). see PARTIAL.

**favourable**, *auspicious*, kit(吉); che̍k-kìⁿ tãi-kit(一見大吉); siâng(祥); kit-siâng(吉祥); siâng-sũi(祥瑞). *wind*, sũn-huang(順風). *tide*, ha̍h-lâu(合流). *circumstances*, hó-ki-hũe(好機會); tú-tit-tie̍h(睹得着); kak-sṳ̄ bô-tsó-keh(各事無阻隔); kak-sṳ̄ sũn-sũn(各事順順); kak-sṳ̄ zû-ì(各事如意).

**favourite**, tit-nâng-sieh(得人惜); ha̍h-sim(合心); ha̍h-ì(合意); tit-sim(得心); tit-ì(得意). *book*, siãng-ha̍h-thóiⁿ(上合睇).

**fawn**, see FLATTER. *young deer*, te̍k-kiáⁿ(鹿囝).

**fear**, kiaⁿ(驚); ùi(畏); kiaⁿ-ùi(驚畏); phàⁿ(怕); khióng-ùi(恐畏); khióng-phàⁿ(恐怕); kiaⁿ-kũ(驚懼); tie̍h-kiaⁿ(着驚); hâi-phàⁿ(駭怕). *God*, kèng-ùi Siãng-tì(敬畏上帝). *death*, ùi-sí(畏死); phàⁿ-sí(怕死). *fearful*, khó-ùi(可畏); tshūa-nâng-ùi(𤆬人畏); kiaⁿ-nâng(驚人); kiaⁿ-sí-nâng(驚死人). *fearless*, m̄-ùi(毋畏); bõi-kiaⁿ(袂驚); ũ-táⁿ(有膽).

**feasible**, tsò-tit-lâi(做得來); tsò-tit-khṳ̀(做要去).

**feast**, toh(桌); toh-sia̍h(桌席). *eat*, chia̍h-toh(食桌). *wedding*, sin-hun-toh(新婚桌). *make*, tsò-toh(做桌); khui-toh(開桌); siet-sia̍h(設席); hũe-kheh(會客); chhiáⁿ--nâng chia̍h-chiú(請人食酒); chhiáⁿ-chiú(請酒).

**feather**, môⁿ(毛). *fowl's*, koi-môⁿ(雞毛). *bird's*, chiáu-môⁿ(鳥毛).

**features**, mīn-mãuⁿ(面貌); siàng-mãuⁿ(相貌); mīn-siàng(面相); mīn-sièⁿ(面像).

**fecundity**, seⁿ-tsōi(生㩼); õi-seⁿ(會生); mõng-sẽng(茂盛); seⁿ-khṳ̀ kãu(生去厚).

**fee**, kui-ngṳ̂n(規銀). *fee to teacher*, sok-kim(束金); sok-siu(束收); tsṳ-kuan(書關). *fee to teacher (extra presents at terms)*, sàng-tsoih(送節). *fee to doctor*, huang-pau(封包); âng-pau(紅包); bé-kè(馬價); kiē-kè(轎價). *fee to write*, pit-kim(筆金); pit-tsṳ(筆書); pit-tsṳ-ngṳ̂n(筆書銀). *fee to letter-carrier*, chiú-chîⁿ(酒錢).

**feeble**, nńg-jia̍k(軟弱); sue-jia̍k(衰弱); bô-la̍t(無力).

**feed**, chhī(飼); iáng(養); pun-i-chia̍h(分伊食).

**feel**, *by touch*, mông(摸); thãng(動). *the pulse*, phah-me̍hⁿ(拍脈); hūaⁿ-me̍hⁿ(捍脈); chién-me̍hⁿ(診脈); àn-me̍hⁿ(按脈); thóiⁿ-me̍hⁿ(睇脈); mông-me̍hⁿ(摸脈); tẽⁿ-me̍hⁿ(捏脈); me̍hⁿ-thóiⁿ(脈睇). *pain*, tsai-thiàⁿ(知痛). *afraid*, tsai-kiaⁿ(知驚). *ashamed*, tsai-siáu-lí(知少禮). *obliged*, kám-ṳn(感恩); kám-ṳn tài-tek(感恩戴德); tsai-chhêng(知情); tsai i-kâi nâng-chhêng(知伊个人情). *one's way with a stick*, tsang-ki-tshûe tõ-lã-lōu〔〕. *a feeling man*, ũ-nâng-chhêng(有人情); ũ-tshṳ̂-sim(有慈心). *hurt feelings*, sieⁿ-sim(傷心); sim-thâu thiàⁿ(心頭痛); sim-lãi pãu-pek(心內暴迫).

**feign**, ké-tsò(假做); tsuang-tsò(裝做); tèⁿ-tsò(詐做). *illness*, ké-tsò ũ-pēⁿ(假做有病); tsà-pēⁿ(詐病); tèⁿ-pēⁿ(詐病); ké-pēⁿ(假病). *death*, tèⁿ-sí(詐死). *madness*, tèⁿ-siáu(詐小); tèⁿ-kông(佯戇); tèⁿ-tien(詡顛); tsuang-siáu(裝小); ké-siáu(假小).

**felicity**, hok-khì(福氣); hok-che̍k(福澤); khùai-la̍k(快樂).

**fell (cruel)**, tshâng-hāi(殘害); tshâng-jím(殘忍); pãu-ngia̍k(暴虐). *trees*, tsám-chhiū(斬樹).

**fellow (companion)**, tâng-phũaⁿ(同伴). *commen*, so̍k-jîn(俗人). *mean*, siáu-jîn(小人). *fellow-officer*, tâng-în-kuaⁿ(同寅官); tâng-liâu(同僚). *fellow-student*, tâng-theng(同窗); theng-iú(窗友); tâng-o̍h(同學); o̍h-iú(學友); tsò-pû tha̍k-tsṳ(做伴讀書). *fellowship*, tâng-sim(同心); siang-kau(相交); siang-kau-tshap(相交插); kau-ṳ́(交語); kau-pûe(交陪). *felo-de-se*, tsṳ̃-chĩn(自盡).

**felon**, hũam-jîn(犯人); tsũe-jîn(罪人); kam-hũam(監犯).

**felt**, chiⁿ(氈). *hat*, chiⁿ-bō(氈帽); chiⁿ-zúan(氈轉). *carpet*, tī-chiⁿ(地氈); chiⁿ-tiâu(氈條). *to make*, ié-chiⁿ(舀氈); tsò-chiⁿ(做氈).

**female**, *of human beings*, nńg(女); tsṳ-niêⁿ(諸娘); tsa-bóu(諸婦); hũ-jîn(婦人); hũ--nâng(婦人); a-má-nâng(阿媽人[訓]); a-má-siàu(阿媽少). *children*, nńg tsṳ́(女子); tsṳ-niêⁿ-kiáⁿ(諸娘囝). *male and*, lâm-nńg(男女); ta-pou tsṳ-niêⁿ(丈夫諸娘); im-iâng(陰陽). *of beasts*, bó(母); phín(牝); láng〔〕. *of birds*, bó(母); tshṳ̂(雌). *female and male (beasts)*, phín-móuⁿ(牝牡); láng-kóu〔〕. *female and male (birds)*, bó-kak(母角); tshṳ̂-hiông(雌雄). *female apartments*, kui-pâng(閨房); chhim-kui tièⁿ-pâng(深閨帳房). *attendants*, tsáu-kúi(走鬼); chhiah-kha(赤骹); nńg-pĩ(女婢).

**fence**, *a*, hn̂g-lî(園籬); tek-lî(竹籬); tek-ûi(竹圍); tek-tsa̍h(竹柵); chhì-nâⁿ(刺籃); tek-nâⁿ(竹籃); chhì-phè(刺帕). *to, with swords*, mõng-kiàm(舞劍); bú-kiàm(舞劍); pí-kiàm(比劍). *fencing-master*, khûn-thâu sai-pẽ(拳頭司阜); khûn-thâu sṳ-hũ(拳頭師傅).

**festivity**, lāu-jie̍t(鬧熱); hí-sṳ̄(喜事).

**feud**, uan-ke(冤家). *to have, with anyone*, kāng-nâng tsò-uan-ke(共人做冤家); ũ-uan-ke(有冤家).

**fever**, sie-jie̍t(燒熱); huat-jie̍t(發熱); huat-sie(發燒); jie̍t-pēⁿ(熱病); jie̍t-chèng(熱症); sieⁿ-huang(傷風); ngia̍k-pēⁿ(瘧病). *(feverish)*, la-jie̍t(拉熱). *fever and ague*, kûaⁿ-jie̍t(寒熱); pak-kûaⁿ(拍寒); huat-sie(發燒); ùiⁿ-chhìn(畏凊); kûaⁿ-pēⁿ(寒病). *fever and ague (slightly feverish)*, kiâm-siam-kûaⁿ(鹹參寒); mahⁿ-mohⁿ mahⁿ-mohⁿ(茫茫茫茫). *quotidian ague*, ji̍t-ji̍t-kûaⁿ(日日寒). *tertian*, làng-ji̍t-kûaⁿ(零日寒); kòiⁿ-ji̍t-kûaⁿ(間日寒). *quartan*, saⁿ-ji̍t-kûaⁿ(三日寒). *to remove*, thò-jie̍t(退熱). *to abate*, jie̍t thò(熱退).

**few**, chié(少); lân-ló(零些); kúi-kâi(幾個); bô-ũa〔〕; bô-mih-tsōi(無乜㩼); bô-hièⁿ-tsōi(無向㩼); bô-jie̍h-tsōi(無若㩼); bô-ki(無幾). *a few people*, lân-nâng(零人); kúi-nâng(幾人); sù-nâng(數人).

**fib**, ké-ūe(假話); la-kè〔〕; la-san〔〕. *don't*, màiⁿ-la〔〕.

**fibre**, *vegetable*, si(絲).

**fickle**, bô-tiāⁿ(無定); sim kōi-î-e̍k(心易移浴); saⁿ-keⁿ-siẽⁿ pùaⁿ-mêⁿ-húan(三更想半夜反); húan-ho̍k bô-siêⁿ(反覆無常); ũ-thâu bô-búe(有頭無尾); î-î e̍k-e̍k(移移易易); húan-húan ho̍k-ho̍k(反反覆覆).

**fiction**, *works of*, siáu-sueh(小說). *fictitious*, ké(假); bô-iáⁿ-chiah(無影跡); bô-chin-si̍t(無真實).

**fiddle**, hîⁿ(弦). *with two strings*, jī-hîⁿ(字弦). *to play the*, kṳ̀-hîⁿ(鋸弦). *bow,* hîⁿ-keng(弦經). *string*, hîⁿ-sùaⁿ(弦線). *to tune*, hûa-hîⁿ(和弦). *fiddler*, hîⁿ-kha(弦骹).

**fidelity**, see FAITHFUL.

**fidget**, tòng-tòng-tsáu(動動走); bô-sî-tiām(無時恬).

**field**, *cultivated and irrigated*, tshân(田); tshân-bóu(田畝). *cultivated but not irrigated*, hn̂g(園). *wet or dry*, tshân-hn̂g(田園). *to cultivate*, tsoh-tshân(作田); chèng-tsoh(種作); keⁿ-tsok(耕作). *plough*, lôi-tshân(犁田). *to irrigate*, kùan-tshân(灌田); im-tshân(蔭田). *field mouse*, tshân-tshṳ́(田鼠). *boundary*, tshân-hūaⁿ(田捍). *battle-field*, chièn-tiêⁿ(戰場). *field-piece*, tōa-phàu(大炮).

**fiend**, kúi(鬼); môⁿ-kúi(魔鬼); siâ-kúi(邪鬼); ak-kúi(惡鬼); iau-kúi(妖怪).

**fierce**, pãu-sèⁿ(暴性); pãu-pek(暴迫); pãu-tshàu(暴躁); méⁿ-lie̍t(猛烈); pãu-lie̍t(暴烈).

**fife**, ti-tâ(嘀嗒); siau(簫); ki-kû(嘰咕). *to play*, pûn-ti-tâ(歕嘀嗒).

**fifty**, ngõu-tsa̍p(五十).

**fig**, ngõu-tsa̍p(無花果).

**fight**, sie-thâi(相刣); kau-chièn(交戰); hãi-tòu(亥鬥); sie-phah(相拍).

**figure**, hêng(形); hêng-iēⁿ(形樣); hêng-siãng(形像); hêng-sièⁿ(形像); hêng-tsuãng(形狀); iēⁿ-sièⁿ(樣像); hêng-thí(形體). *figures(numerals)*, bé-kiáⁿ(碼囝). *figured cloth*, hue-pòu(花布).

**filch**, thau-khie̍h(偷挈). *rice*, thau-tshah-bí(偷竊米); thau-lap-bí(偷套米).

**file**, tshò(銼). *iron filings*, thih-tshùi(鐵碎); thih-hu(鐵夫); thih-sut(鐵屑).

**filial**, kiâⁿ-hàu(行孝). *son*, hàu-tsṳ́(孝子).

**fill**, *with water*, tsúi tò-kàu-tĩⁿ(水倒到漲). *a room*, nâng ji̍p kàu che̍k-koiⁿ tsa̍t-tsa̍t(人入到一間實實); kàu che̍k-koiⁿ-nâng nẽⁿ tĩⁿ-tĩⁿ(到一間人軟定定). *an office*, seng-jīm(生任); chiẽⁿ-jīm(上任). *up with earth*, thūn-tī(遁地); thūn-thôu(遁塗). *a hole*, sat-khang(塞空). *to eat one's*, chia̍h kàu-pá-pá(食到飽飽). *filler, for pouring water*, tsúi-làu(水漏); khuah-tshùi-làu(闊喙漏).

**fillet**, tòa(住).

**fillip**, *with finger-nail*, tuāⁿ(彈); tuāiⁿ(撢).

**film**, mo̍hⁿ(膜); mo̍hⁿ-mo̍hⁿ(膜膜); po̍h-mo̍hⁿ(薄膜); phûe-mo̍hⁿ(皮膜).

**filter**, *to*, tè(笮). *filter water*, tè-tsúi(笮水); tsúi tè-chheng-khih(水笮清潔). *a filter*, tsúi-tè(水笮). *a filter (made of sand)*, sua-làu(沙勞).

**filthy**, nah-sap(垃圾); u-ùe(污穢); chhi-gî(淒疑). *abuse*, iá-siaⁿ-mēⁿ(野聲罵); tshou-siaⁿ-mēⁿ(粗聲罵); tshou-siaⁿ iá-tshùi(粗聲野喙); mēⁿ kàu-chhi-gî(罵到淒疑); tshou-lâm iá-tshùi〔〕.

**fins**, hṳ̂-si̍t(魚翼); hṳ̂-chhì(魚翅). *sharks'*, sua-hṳ̂-si̍t(沙魚翼).

**final**, *a particle*, suah-kha hṳ-jī(煞骹虛字). *conclusion, expressed in a word*, tsóng zṳ̂-ngân--tsṳ(總而言之); tàu-tí(到底). *finally*, tsong(終); suah-búe(煞尾); kàu-búe(到尾); kiáu-búe(繳尾); pi̍t-kéng(畢竟).

**find**, *find by search*, tshūe--tie̍h(覓着); chhîm--tie̍h(尋着); chhê--tie̍h(查着). *find by search (in a book)*, chhê-tit-tshut(查得出). *find by search  (in a book or mixed mass)*, púe--tie̍h(撥着). *meet with*, ngõ--tie̍h(遇着); tú--tie̍h(睹着); hông--tie̍h(逢着). *to find anything by chance*, khieh--tie̍h(挈着); to̍h-tie̍h(掇着).

**fine**, *in quality*, iùⁿ(幼); iùⁿ-sòi(幼細). *reasoning*, tõ-lí sòi-mûiⁿ(在理細微); cheng-mûiⁿ(精微); cheng-sòi(精細). *in fine*, tàu-tí(鬥抵). *weather*, hó-thiⁿ(好天); thiⁿ-sî chêⁿ(天時晴).

**fine**, *to*, hua̍t(罰). *to (money)*, hua̍t-ngṳ̂n(罰銀). *to (a play)* hua̍t-hì(罰戲); hua̍t-tsúa-iáⁿ(罰紙影). *to (crackers)*, hua̍t-phòng-phiẽ(罰碰鰾).

**finger**, chhiú-tsóiⁿ(手指). *1st or thumb*, tsńg-thâu(指頭); tsńg-thâu-kong(指頭公). *fore*, koi-tsóiⁿ(鷄指). *middle*, tang-tsóiⁿ(中手指). *the ring-finger*, hôu-lâi-tsóiⁿ(狐狸指). *the little*, búe-tsóiⁿ(尾手指); chhiú-tsóiⁿ-kiáⁿ(手指囝); búe-tsńg-kiáⁿ(尾指囝). *reckon on fingers*, khut-tsóiⁿ sǹg(屈手指算). *point with*, chhiú kí(手指); tsang-tsńg-thâu kí(將指頭指). *finger-ring*, see RING. *to take up between the finger and thumb*, nueh--khí-lâi(挼起來). *a pinch so taken*, che̍k-nueh-kiáⁿ(一挼囝). *finger-post*, lōu-pi(路碑); lōu-ín(路引). *finger-nails*, tsńg-kah(指甲). *finger-nails (long)*, chhiú-jiáu(手爪); jiáu-kah(爪甲).

**finish**, tsò-chiâⁿ(做成); tsò-sêng(做城); tsò-ûan(做圓); sêng-kong(成功); pi̍t(畢). *a meal*, chia̍h-pá(食飽). *finished*, uân(完); hó(好); hiah(歇); liáu(了); pi̍t. *have you finished*, hó--būe(好未).

**finite**, ũ-hãn-tiāⁿ(有限定).

**fir**, sêng-peh-chhiū(松柏樹); sam(杉). *needles*, sêng-peh-chhiu(松柏秋). *cones*, sêng-peh-lûi(松柏蕾).

**fire**, húe(火). *set fire to*, pàng-húe(放火). *make a*, khí-húe(起火). *put fuel on the*, hiâⁿ-húe(燃火). *light a*, to̍h-húe(著火). *strike*, phah-húe(拍火). *extinguish*, kiù-húe(救火); phah-kùe-húe(拍過火); mi̍t-kùe-húe(密過火). *extinguish (with water)*, tsâng-kùe-húe(藏過火). *gone out*, húe kùe--khṳ̀(火過去). *fire-place*, tsàu(灶); húe-lôu(火爐); chhiêⁿ-lôu(牆爐). *fire-engine*, kiù-húe kâi tsúi-chhia(救火个水車). *fire-arms*, chhèng-phàu(銃砲). *fire-arrows*, húe-chìⁿ(火箭). *fire-crackers*, phòng-phiẽ(碰鰾). *fire-crackers (large)*, tōa-lîn-kòng(大連槓). *fire-crackers (a long string)*, tshùan-phàu(串砲). *fire-rocket*, húe-su̍h〔〕. *warm oneself at the*, chieh-húe(借火). *flame of*, húe-iãm(火炎); húe-chi̍h(火舌). *fire-fly*, húe-mêⁿ-kou(火芒龜); iông-húe(陽火). *ignis fatuus*, kúi-húe(鬼火). *to fire a gun*, khui-chhèng(開銃); pàng-chhèng(放銃); phah-chhèng(拍銃); sià-chhèng(射銃). *fire-brands (partly burnt)*, tshâ-tsau(柴糟).

**firm**, kien-kù(堅固); kien-tōiⁿ(堅𠕆); kien-tsàng(堅壯); ún-tǹg(穩當); thó-tàng(妥當). *purpose*, kien-sim(堅心); kien-ì(堅意); kien-ì put-tshông(堅意不從); sim kien(心堅), ì chhiet(意切). *a firm in business*, hâng(行); kong-si(公司). *name of such*, hâng-miâⁿ(行名); phòu-hō(舖號).

**firmament**, chheⁿ-thiⁿ(青天); thiⁿ-chiēⁿ(天頂). *(not quite colloquial)*, thiⁿ-khong(天空).

**first**, tõiⁿ-it(第一); thâu-che̍k-kâi(頭一個). *first...then*, soiⁿ...ãu(先...後). *first-moon*, chiaⁿ-gue̍h(正月). *first-born*, tsho-seⁿ(初生); thâu-tho(頭胎); thâu-seⁿ(頭生); khí-thâu-seⁿ(起頭生); tah-thâu-seⁿ(貼頭生). *first son*, tōa-tau-kiáⁿ(大頭囝); chiáng-tsṳ́(長子). *first-fruits*, tsho-se̍k kâi-kúeⁿ-chí(粗熟个果子). *first year of reign*, ngûan--nîⁿ(元年). *first time*, thâu-che̍k-hûe(頭一回); thâu-pái(頭擺); khí-tsho--che̍k-hûe(起初一回); tsùe-soiⁿ--che̍k-hûe(最先一回). *from first to last*, tsṳ̂-thâu kàu-búe(薯頭到尾); tsṳ̃-sí kàu-tsong(自始到終); tshông-thâu kàu-búe(從頭到尾). *at first*, khí-thâu(起頭); tsho-ē(初下). *in the first place*, thâu che̍k-kiãⁿ(頭一件); khî-it(其一).

**fish**, hṳ̂(魚). *one fish*, che̍k-búe-hṳ̂(一尾魚). *salt fish*, kiâm-hṳ̂(鹹魚). *dried fish*, hṳ̂-póu(魚脯). *catch fishes(various methods)*, lia̍h-hṳ̂(掠魚); pha-hṳ̂(拋魚); mãng-hṳ̂(網魚); khiâ-hṳ̂(騎魚); áu-hṳ̂〔〕; tièⁿ-hṳ̂(釣魚); jī-hṳ̂〔〕; khan-hṳ̂(牽魚); tsa̍h-hṳ̂(閘魚); thó-hái(討海); lo̍h-khoi(落溪). *fish-pond*, hṳ̂-tî(魚池). *fish-hawk*, hṳ̂-a(魚鴉); hṳ̂-tèng-chiáu(魚碇鳥). *fish-hook*, tièⁿ-kau(釣鈎). *fish-maw*, hṳ̂-tõu(魚肚); hṳ̂-phiẽ(魚鰾). *fish-spear*, hṳ̂-pie(魚鏢). *fish-scales*, hṳ̂-lâng(魚籠). *roe or spawn*, hṳ̂-tshun(魚春). *roe or spawn (deposited)*, hṳ̂-nñg(魚卵). *fishing-rod*, tièⁿ-ko(釣糕). *fish-line*, tièⁿ-si(釣絲). *fisherman*, lia̍h-hṳ̂ kâi-nâng(掠魚個人); hṳ̂-ong(魚翁); thó-hái-nâng(討海人).

**fissure**, li̍h(裂); phùa-li̍h(破裂); pit-khui(筆開).

**fist**, khûn-thâu(拳頭). *to clench*, lĩm-khûn(臨拳); lĩm khûn-thâu-bó(臨拳頭母). *fisticuffs*, phah-khûn-thâu(拍拳頭).

**fit**, *a*, sit-hûn(失魂); hun-kông(昏戇). *fall down in*, hun-tó(昏倒). *epileptic*, tie̍h-iêⁿ-tshái(着羊癇); iêⁿ-kueh-tshái(羊角瘋). *of anger*, che̍k-tsūn-khì(一陣氣).

**fit**, *(adjective)*, ha̍h(合); kah(合); kah-ēng(合用); ha̍h-ēng(合用); kah-tit-lo̍h(合得落). *well (as clothes)*, kah-chhēng(合穿). *to do anything*, tsò-tit-lâi(做得來).

**five**, ngõu(五).

**fix**, tiāⁿ(定); tiāⁿ-tie̍h(定着). *a day*, tiāⁿ-ji̍t(定日); tiāⁿ-khî(定期). *fixed*, tiāⁿ-tie̍h(定着); ngẽ--liáu(硬了); ngẽ-tiāⁿ--liáu(硬定了); ngẽ-hóuⁿ(硬虎); ngẽ-ngẽ hóuⁿ-hóuⁿ(硬硬虎虎). *by fate*, seⁿ-sêng(生成); tsú-tiāⁿ(主定). *price*, tiāⁿ-kè(定價); ngẽ-kè(硬價). *choice upon*, suán-tiāⁿ(選定).

**flabby**, ne̍k chhieh(肉尺); nńg-nap(軟肭).

**flaccid**, jiâu-jiâu(縐嬈); hoih-hoih(咳咳).

**flag**, kî(旗). *staff*, kî-kuaⁿ(旗杆). *to hoist*, liū-kî(㨨旗). *flag-stone*, tī-póiⁿ-chie̍h(地反石); koi-lōu-chie̍h(雞路石).

**flagitious**, hiã-liû(下流); bô-chhí kâi siáu-jîn(無恥个小人); tsa̍p-ak(十惡); khiông-hiong kék-ak(窮兇極惡).

**flagon**, chiú-pân(酒便); tsúi-kùan(水罐).

**flail**, kéⁿ(骾).

**flake**, che̍k-phièn po̍h-po̍h(一片薄薄).

**flambeau**, húe-pé(火把); húe-nāⁿ(火爁).

**flame**, húe-iãm(火炎); húe-chi̍h(火舌). *up*, húe-chi̍h kia̍h-phû(火舌劇浮).

**flanks**, liáng-e̍k(兩腋); liáng-hia̍p(兩脅).

**flannel**, nîⁿ(呢). *(woollen material in general)*, nîⁿ-ú(呢羽).

**flare**, *up*, húe-chi̍h ti̍t-chiẽⁿ(火舌直上); húe-chi̍h kia̍h-phû(火舌劇浮). *in anger*, sim-húe huat(心火發). *soon flaring up*, ũ-húe-sèⁿ(有火性).

**flash**, *of lightning*, ia̍p-che̍k-sih(灼一熠); ia̍p-chē-sih(灼些熠); ia̍p-ia̍p-sih(灼灼熠).

**flask**, *oil*, iû-pân(油瓶); iû-tsun(油樽). *powder*, gû-kak-tâng(牛角銅).

**flat**, pêⁿ(平); píⁿ(扁); pién(扁); pêⁿ-tháng(平桶). *country*, pêⁿ-pou pêⁿ-tī(平坦平地). *in taste*, bô-bī(無味). *flatten*, teh-bih(壓癟); phah-pêⁿ(拍平). *to tell him flatly*, ti̍t-ti̍t-tàⁿ(直直呾).

**flatter**, thiám-mĩⁿ(諂媚); pong-song(奉送); hông-ngêng(逢迎); i-o hông-ngêng〔〕. *fond of praise and flattery*, hàuⁿ khṳt-nâng phùn-tsúi(好乞人噴水); hàuⁿ-tì kau-bō(好帝交帽); hàuⁿ-lap húe-thùaⁿ-lam(好套火炭籠).

**flatulence**, seⁿ-huang(生瘋); tóu tièⁿ-huang(肚脹風). *to dispel*, siau-huang(消風).

**flaunt**, iâu-pái(搖擺); iâu-iâu pái-pái(搖搖擺擺); hàuⁿ-pái-ngiá(好擺雅); hàuⁿ-tsuang-pàn(好裝扮).

**flavour**, khì-bī(氣味); bī(味); bī-sòu(味素). *strong*, bī tãng(味重); bī kãu(味厚).

**flaw**, hiâ(瑕); tiám(點). *without*, pe̍h-ge̍k bô-hiâ(白玉無瑕). *well arranged so that no flaw*, chiu-ba̍t(周密).

**flax**, tiũ(苧). *fine*, iùⁿ-tiũ(幼苧).

**flay**, pak-phûe(剝皮).

**flea**, ka-tsáu(虼蚤).

**fledged**, huat-môⁿ(發毛).

**flee**, tsáu(走); tô-tsáu(逃跑); phun-tsáu(奔走); pī-tsáu(避走).

**fleet**, méⁿ(猛); sok-sok(速速). *of ships*, che̍k-tūi-tsûn(一隊船).

**flesh**, ne̍k(肉); bah(肉). *fleshy*, ũ-ne̍k(有肉); pûi(肥). *colour*, chhiah-se̍k(赤色). *proud*, ṳ̀-ne̍k(淤肉). *putrid*, àu-ne̍k〔〕; hu-ne̍k(腐肉). *the flesh(in moral sense)*, sṳ-io̍k(私慾); ne̍k-io̍k(肉慾).

**flexible**, nńg(軟); kōi-uan(易彎); hó-á-uan(好拗彎); hó-ut-uan(好斡彎); hó-tshâu-uan(好移彎); hó-khut-uan(好屈彎).

**flight**, *of an army*, pāi-tsáu(敗走). *of steps*, che̍k-tieⁿ-thui(一張梯). *of arrows*, chìⁿ lũan-siā(箭亂射). *flighty*, sim bô-tiāⁿ-tsú(心無定主); sim-sèⁿ phû-tshàu(心性浮躁).

**flimsy**, nńg-jia̍k(軟弱); bô-la̍t(無力); bô-khì(無氣); lám〔〕; lẽ-ké〔〕.

**flinch**, thò-sok(退縮); kiu-thò(勼退); lîm-tīn thò-sok(臨陣退縮); kiu-tsáu(勼走).

**fling**, ka̍k(捔). *away*, ka̍k-tiāu(捔掉); sek-tiāu(擲掉); hám-tiāu(撼掉).

**flint**, húe-chie̍h(火石). *flinty-hearted (also, decided and firm)*, thih-chie̍h sim-kuaⁿ(鐵石心肝).

**flippant**, khin-phû(輕浮); phû-tshàu(浮臭); m̄-kṳ́n-ngân(毋近顏); tàⁿ-ūe m̄-kṳ́n-sín(呾話毋謹慎).

**flit**, pûe(飛). *remove*, puaⁿ-tshù(搬厝); súa-the̍h(徙宅); chhien-kṳ(遷居); î-kṳ(移居).

**float**, phû-tsúi(浮水); phiau-phû(飄浮). *a float*, sam-pâi(杉排).

**flock**, khûn(群). *a whole*, chiâⁿ-khûn(成群). *of sheep*, che̍k-khûn-iêⁿ(一群羊).

**flog**, phah(拍). *severely*, phah-thiám-thiám(拍忝忝); thiám-phah(忝拍); tãng-phah(盪拍). *with rod*, phah-tek-tshûe(拍竹箠); phah-tek-pì(拍竹比). *with large heavy rod*, phah-tek-póiⁿ(拍竹板). *till severely injured*, phah-kàu lok-lok(拍到落落); phah mîⁿ-mîⁿ(拍棉棉).

**flood**, *deluge*, tōa-tsúi(大水); âng-tsúi(紅水). *flooded*, pun âng-tsúi im--khṳ̀(分紅水淹去). *tide*, lâu tĩⁿ(流漲); nâm-lâu(南流); ji̍p-lâu(入流). *gate*, tsúi-tsa̍h(水閘).

**floor**, thôu-ẽ(塗下). *wooden*, lâu-pang(樓棚); tī-póiⁿ-pang(地板棚). *brick*, âng-tsng(紅磚). *lime*, hue-tiâⁿ(灰埕). *to lay a wood floor*, kek-tī-póiⁿ(格地板). *to lay a brick floor*, phou-tsng(鋪磚). *to lay a lime floor*, phah-hue-tiâⁿ(拍灰埕).

**florid**, kuang-tshái(光彩); hua-múiⁿ(花美). *complexion*, mīn-sek kuang-tshái(面色光彩); mīn-sek âng-zũn(面色紅潤); mīn-sek âng(面色紅).

**floss**, zông(絨).

**flour**, hún(粉). *wheaten*, mīⁿ-hún(麵粉); mīⁿ-tshòi(麵粞). *potatoe*, tsṳ̂-hún(薯粉). *rice*, tshòi(粞).

**flourish**, *to*, heng-sẽng(興盛); heng-uãng(興旺); hong-sẽng(豐盛); lāu-jie̍t(鬧熱); uãng-khì(旺氣). *and decay*, heng-sue(興衰).

**flout**, ki-chhiè(譏笑); ki-chhiáu(譏嘲); chhiáu-chhiè(嘲笑).

**flow**, lâu(流). *ebb and*, lâu khó-tĩⁿ(流洘漲). *around*, chiu-liû(周流). *over-flow*, lâu--tshut(流出); iah--tshut(溢出); múaⁿ--tshut(滿出); e̍k--tshut(液出). *till dry*, lâu-kàu-ta(流到灱).

**flower**, hue(花). *to*, khui-hue(開花). *bush*, che̍k-tsâng-hue(一叢花). *one sprig*, che̍k-ki-hue(一枝花). *a bouquet of*, che̍k-pa̍k-hue(一縛花); che̍k-pé-hue(一把花). *bud*, phah-lúi(拍蕾). *half-blown*, hue hâm-hâm(花含含); hue-pùaⁿ-khui(花半開). *full-blown*, khui-khṳ̀-phàu(開去砲). *fade*, hue sià(花謝). *quite faded and done*, tshâng(藏). *flower-vase*, hue-pân(花瓶); hue-kan(花缸); chéⁿ-kan(井缸). *flower-pot*, hue-puah(花缽); hue-phûn(花盆). *flower-garden*, hue-hn̂g(花園). *flowered cloth*, hue-pòu(花布). *work with needle*, see EMBROIDER.

**fluctuate**, bô-tiāⁿ-tie̍h(無定着); e̍k-lâi e̍k-khṳ̀(亦來亦去); î-î e̍k-e̍k(移亦亦亦); chhien-kói bô-tiāⁿ(遷改無定).

**flue**, in-tâng(煙筒). *(of furnace)*, tsàu-tshue(灶炊).

**fluent**, tàⁿ-ūe liù-liù-ku̍t(呾話溜溜滑); khî-tshùi zû-kuah-tsúa-to(其喙如刮紙刀); ũ-kháu-lẽng(有口令); ũ-kháu-tshâi(有口才).

**fluid**, tsúi-tsúi(水水); chhieh-chhieh(淖淖); iêⁿ-iêⁿ(洋洋). *(different degrees)*, ko-ko(糕糕).

**flush**, mīn âng--khí-lâi(面紅起來).

**flute**, hûeⁿ-te̍k(橫笛). *to play*, pûn-hûeⁿ-te̍k(歕橫笛).

**fly**, pue(飛). *run away*, tsáu(走); tô-tsáu(胡蠅); pī-tsáu(胡蠅). *a kite*, pàng-huang-khîm(放風禽).

**fly**, *a*, hôu-sîn(胡蠅). *a cloud of*, che̍k-tīn hôu-sîn(一陣胡蠅). *fly-catcher (spider)* hôu-sîn-hóuⁿ(胡蠅虎).

**foam**, *from mouth*, tshùi-nũaⁿ(喙涎); thâm(痰). *on water*, tsúi-phue̍h(水沬).

**fodder**, niêⁿ-tsháu(糧草).

**foe**, chhiû-te̍k(仇敵); tùi-thâu(對頭).

**fog**, in-bū(煙霧); mông-bū(蒙霧); mông-in(濛煙); hûn-bū(雲霧). *foggy weather*, thiⁿ-sî huat-mông(天時發蒙).

**foil**, *frustrate a plot*, phùa-kòi(破計); chiang-kòi chiū-kòi(裝計就計). *tin-foil*, siah-po̍h(錫薄).

**fold**, *sheep*, iêⁿ-nûaⁿ〔〕; iêⁿ-lô(羊牢).

**fold**, *to*, chih(折). *how many times shall I fold it*, áiⁿ-chih-tsò jie̍h-tsōi-chih(愛折作若㩼折); àiⁿ-chih-tsò jie̍h-tsōi-tsâng(愛折作若㩼層); àiⁿ-chih-tsò kúi-ē(愛折做幾下). *plait three folds*, pĩⁿ-saⁿ-kóu(辮三股). *as of paper*, têng(重). *to make folds or plaits on dress*, nia̍p-kóiⁿ(捻襇); khieh-kóiⁿ(挈襇). *fold the hands and salute one*, kióng-chhiú tsak-ip(拱手扎揖). *the arms*, tshah-chhiú(插手). *fold the hands and salute one (less complete, hands together on the breast)*, tsha-chhiú(差手). *two-fold*, kia-pũe(加倍); ha̍p-pũe(合倍). *manifold*, ke-ke-pũe(加加倍).

**foliage**, chhiū-hie̍h(樹葉). *dense*, chhiū-hie̍h mõng-sẽng(樹葉茂盛); ba̍t-tsa̍t(密實); tsa̍t-tsa̍t(實實); ap-ap〔〕; im-im(蔭蔭).

**follow**, tshông(從); tùe(綴); kṳn-sûi(跟隨). *as successor*, chiap(接); chih(接). *one's example*, o̍h-iēⁿ(學樣); tùe-iēⁿ(綴樣); chiè-iēⁿ(照樣); hāu-o̍h(效學). *in one's steps*, tùe i kâi-kha-pōu(綴伊个骹步). *one's advice*, thiaⁿ nâng khn̍g-kòi(聽人勸戒); thiaⁿ-nâng-tàⁿ(聽人呾). *one's own inclination*, jĩm-ì(任意); jĩm ka-kī kâi-ì(任家己个意). *customs*, tshông-so̍k(從俗); tshông-sì-so̍k(從世俗). *follower or disciple*, mn̂g-jîn(門人); mn̂g-seng(門生); mn̂g-thû(門徒).

**folly**, ngà-sṳ̄(㦙事).

**fomentation**, ù-sie(焐燒); tah-sie(搭燒).

**fond**, thiàⁿ-sieh(痛惜); hàuⁿ(好). *(to excess)*, ne̍k-ài(肉愛). *fond of wine*, hàuⁿ-chiú(好酒).

**food**, chia̍h(食); chia̍h-mu̍eh(食物); kháu-chia̍h(口食); bí-niêⁿ(米糧); kháu-siâm〔〕.

**fool**, ngà(㦙); ngà-nâng(㦙人); chhi-ko(痴哥); chhi-chhi ngâi-ngâi(痴痴呆呆).

**foot**, kha(骹). *sole of*, kha-tói(骹底). *barefoot*, thn̍g-chhiah-kha(褪赤骹); pak-chhiah-kha(剝赤骹). *walk on*, pōu-kiâⁿ(步行); kiâⁿ(行). *trample under*, ta̍h-tiāu(踏掉). *of hill*, suaⁿ-kha(山骹). *foot-ball*, that-kiû(踢球). *foot-path*, lōu-kiáⁿ(路囝); sié-lōu(小路). *foot-step (as seen)*, kha-chiah(骹跡). *foot-step (as heard)*, kha-pōu(骹步). *foot-stool*, kha-ta̍h(骹踏); ta̍h-póiⁿ-íⁿ(踏反椅). *measure*, chhieh(尺). *a foot and a half long*, chhieh-pùaⁿ-tn̂g(尺半長); tn̂g chhieh-pùaⁿ(長尺半).

**fop**, bàuⁿ-phâi-chhiâng〔〕; hàuⁿ-pâi-chhiâng(好排場).

**for**, *in place of*, thòi(代). *sell for ready money*, bōi-hīn-chîⁿ(賣現錢). *on account of*, in-ũi(因爲); ũi-tie̍h(爲着); uân-khî(緣其). *buy it for me*, kāng-uá-bói(共我買); kiau-úa-bói(邀我買). *this is for you*, chí-kâi sĩ àiⁿ-pun-lṳ́(此個是愛分汝). *repeat correctly word for word*, niām-lâi jī-jī bõi-tshò(念來字字袂錯). *I bought this chair for dollars*, chí-chiah-íⁿ úa bói sì-kâi-ngṳ̂n(此隻椅我買四個銀). *how much will you take for it*, lṳ́ àiⁿ sĩ-mih-kè(汝愛是乜價); lṳ́ àiⁿ jie̍h-tsōi-chîⁿ(汝愛若㩼錢). *set out for the Foo city*, khí-sin àiⁿ-khṳ̀ Hú-siâⁿ(起身愛去府城). *as for*, lũn-ki̍p(論及). *what for*, tsò-nîⁿ(怎呢); sĩ-mih uân-kù(是乜緣故). *for life*, che̍k-sì-nâng(一世人[訓]); che̍k-seⁿ(一生). *for the future*, tshông-kim íⁿ-ãu(從今以後); tsṳ̃-tshṳ́ íⁿ-ãu(自此以後). *for ever*, ióng-ién(永遠); ióng-kú(永久).

**forage**, niêⁿ-tsháu(糧草). *to*, chiũ-tī tshú-niêⁿ(就地取糧). *plunder*, khiâng-to̍h(強奪).

**forbear**, jím-nãiⁿ(忍耐); lún(忍); jím(忍); jím-khì(忍氣); lún-khì(忍氣); khuan(寬); khuan-iông(寬容); iông(容); pàng-khuan(放寬).

**forbid**, kìm(禁); kìm-chí(禁子); kìm-kài(禁戒); put-tsún(不准); hàm-i-màiⁿ(喊伊勿); tsó-chí(阻止).

**force**, la̍t(力); sì-la̍t(勢力); khì-la̍t(氣力). *to*, mién-kiáng(勉強); khiâng-pek(強迫); ngẽ-lia̍h(硬掠). *take by*, khiâng-to̍h(強奪); khiâng-chhiéⁿ(強搶); khiâng-thun(強吞). *a woman*, khiâng-kan(強姦). *one's way in through a crowd*, chìⁿ--ji̍p-khṳ́(擠入去); ngẽ-chìⁿ--ji̍p-khṳ́(硬擠入去).

**forceps**, thih-khîⁿ(鐵鉗); thih-kîⁿ(鐵鉗). *small*, koih-kiáⁿ(夾囝); kia̍p-kiáⁿ(夾囝).

**ford**, *to*, ẽ-kùe-khoi(下過溪); ẽ-khoi(下溪).

**fore**, soiⁿ(先); tsôiⁿ(前). *feet*, tsôiⁿ-kha(前骹).

**forearm**, chhiú-pì(手臂).

**foreboding**, ki-tiãu(機兆); hũa-ki(禍機).

**forecastle**, tsûn-thâu(船頭).

**forecast**, ṳ̃-ta̍t〔〕; ṳ̃-pān(預判); lṳ̃(慮); mông-lṳ̃(謀慮); phah-ke̍k〔〕; phah-sǹg(拍算); tá-sǹg(打算).

**forefathers**, soiⁿ-tsóu(先祖); tsóu-tshong(祖宗); tsóu-kong(祖公); tsóu-pẽ(祖父); kong-má(公媽).

**forego**, put-tshú(不取); m̃-tshú(毋取); chhìn-tshái-hiah(凊彩歇); pàng-tiāu(放掉). *humbly one's right*, khiam-jiãng(謙讓); chiãm-jiãng(暫讓); siũ-khui(受虧).

**forehead**, hia̍h(額); hia̍h-thâu(額頭); hia̍h-mn̂g-sîn(額門神). *(higher)*, hia̍h-sìn(額囟). 

**foreign**, huan(番); iêⁿ(洋). *country*, huan-pôiⁿ(番爿); huan-pang(番邦); huan-kok(番國); gūa-kok(外國). *go to*, kùe-kok(過國); kùe-huan(過番); tshut-gūa(出外). *goods*, iêⁿ-hùe(洋貨); iêⁿ-mue̍h(洋物). *cloth*, iêⁿ-pòu(洋布); huang-pòu(風布). *person*, huan-nâng(番人); gūa-kok-nâng(外國人); î-jîn(夷人). *language*, gūa-kok-ūe(外國話).

**foreknow**, soiⁿ-tsai(先知); ṳ̃-tsai(預知); liāu-tsai(料知).

**forelock**, lâu-môⁿ-sûi(流毛隨). *(only on girls)*, lâu-hia̍h-pìn(留額鬢).

**foreman**, thâu-nâng(頭人); sai-pẽ-thâu(司阜頭); tok-kang kâi-nâng(督工个人).

**foremast**, thâu-ûi(頭圍).

**foremost**, thâu-tsôiⁿ(頭前); siãng-soiⁿ(上先).

**forenoon**, chiēⁿ-kùa(上午); chiēⁿ-ngóu(上午).

**forerunner**, tsôiⁿ-khu(前驅).

**foresail**, thâu-phâng(頭帆).

**foresee**, soiⁿ-kièn(先見); soiⁿ-kak(先覺); soiⁿ-tsai(先知); ṳ̃-liāu(預料); ṳ̃-pī(預備).

**forest**, chhiū-lîm(樹林); chhiū-nâⁿ(樹籃).

**foretell**, soiⁿ-tàⁿ(先呾); ṳ̃-ngân(預言); ṳ̃-soiⁿ-tàⁿ(預先呾).

**forewarn**, ṳ̃-soiⁿ kéng-kài(預先警戒).

**forfeit**, hu̍at-ngṳ̂n(罰銀). *one's life*, tì-sí(致命). *money to government, e.g. bail*, siau-ji̍p kuaⁿ-khòu(銷入官庫).

**forge**, *metal*, tuãn-liēn(鍛鍊). *name*, ké-miâⁿ tshut-toaⁿ(假名出單); ké-pit-chiah(假筆跡). *a will*, ké-li̍p zũi-tsok(假立遺囑); ngũi-li̍p zũi-tsok(僞立遺囑).

**forget**, m̄-kìⁿ-tit(毋見得); m̄-kièn-tit(毋見得); buâng-kìⁿ(忘見); buâng-tiāu(忘掉). *forgetful*, bô-kì-tshâi(無記才); bô-kì-tî(無記持); bô-kì-sèⁿ(無記性).

**forgive**, sià(赦); sià-mién(赦免); sià-tsũe(赦罪). *mutually*, siang-sù siang-sià(相恕相赦).

**fork**, chhe(叉). *forked*, a-chhe(阿叉); khui-a(開阿); kâu-kê(猴枷).

**forlorn**, kou-to̍k(孤獨); bô hó-uá-pn̄g(無好我飯); bô hó-íⁿ-kõu(無好椅靠); bô-nâng hó-kau-tshap(無人好交插).

**form**, iēⁿ(樣); môⁿ-iēⁿ(毛樣); hêng(形); hêng-siãng(形像); hêng-tsuãng(形狀); hêng-sièⁿ(形像); hêng-mãuⁿ(形貌); hêng-iông(形容); hêng-thói(形體); khuán(款); khuán-sek(款式). *according to*, chiè-iēⁿ(照樣); chiè-thói-sek(照體色). *to form*, tsò(做); tsãu(造); tshàng(創); sêng(成). *a resolution*, li̍p-ì(立意); li̍p-tiāⁿ tsú-ì(立定主意). *seed*, kat-chí(結子); kit-chí(結子). *a friendship*, kat-iú(結友); kau-iú(交友); kat-kau(結交). *a conspiracy*, kat-táng(結黨). *a plot*, siet-kòi-mông(設計謀).

**formality**, lói(禮); lói-siàu(禮數); lói-bûn(禮文). *empty*, hṳ-lói(虛禮); hṳ-bûn(虛文); chip-gūa-lói(執外禮).

**formerly**, tshông-tsôiⁿ(從前); soiⁿ-tsôiⁿ(先前); tsôiⁿ-sî(前時); tsá-sî(早時); tsá-ji̍t(早日); tsá-tiâng-sî(早日時); tsôiⁿ-ji̍t(前日); soiⁿ-tiâng-sî(先當時); soiⁿ-tsá(先早).

**formidable**, khó-ùi(可畏); hó-ùi(好畏); lĩ-hāi(厲害); hó-hãi-phàⁿ(好駭怕); tshūa-nâng-ùi(𤆬人畏); tit-nâng-ùi(得人畏).

**formula**, thói-sek(體色); huap-sek(法式); tiāⁿ-sek(定色); khuán-sek(款式).

**Formosa**, Thâi-uân(臺灣); Tâi-uân(臺灣); Tang-tou(東都). *go to*, kùe-tou(過都).

**fornication**, kan-îm(姦淫); kan-îm tãu-chhiap(奸淫盜竊); kan nâng chhi-nńg(奸人妻女); thong-kan(通姦); hûa-kan(和姦); kiâⁿ-îm(行淫). *by stealth*, sai-chhêng(私情); sai-thong(私通); thau-îm(偷淫). *by force*, khiâng-kan(強姦); khiâng-îm(強淫). *by persuasion*, pek-kan(迫姦). *with a harlot*, phiâu-chhiang(嫖娼). *fornicator*, kan-hu(姦夫). *fornicatress*, kan-hũ(姦婦); îm-hũ(淫婦). *fornicatress (unmarried)*, îm-nńg(淫女).

**forsake**, lī-khui(離開); pàng-tiāu(放掉).

**fort**, phàu-thâi(炮臺); sìn-tī(信地); iâⁿ-pûaⁿ(營盤).

**forth**, *come*, tshut--lâi(出來). *from this time*, tshông-kim íⁿ-ãu(從今以後).

**forthwith**, sûi-chiet(隨即); sûi-sî(隨時); chiet-khek(即刻); chiet-sok(即速).

**fortitude**, táⁿ-liãng(膽量). *a man of*, ũ-táⁿ-liãng(有膽量).

**fortuitous**, ngóu-jiên(偶然); ngóu-ngõ ì-gūa(偶遇意外); siẽⁿ-m̄-kàu(想毋到).

**fortunate**, tsãu-hùe(造化); ũ-tshâi-khì(有財氣); hẽng-tit(幸得).

**fortune**, miāⁿ(命); ūn-khì(運氣); khì-ūn(氣運). *good*, hó-miāⁿ(好命). *bad*, khiap-miāⁿ〔〕; khóu-miāⁿ(苦命); po̍h-miāⁿ(薄命). *to tell one's*, khùaⁿ-miāⁿ(看命); sǹg-miāⁿ(算命); chhê-sì-thiãu(查四柱); sǹg-poih-jī(算八字); pok-khùe(卜卦). *teller*, lo̍h ngóu-chheⁿ sin-seⁿ(落五星先生); khùaⁿ-miāⁿ sin-seⁿ(看命先生); chheⁿ-mêⁿ sin-seⁿ(青盲先生). *to make one's*, huat-tshâi(發財).

**forty**, sì-tsa̍p(四十).

**forward**, hiàng-tsôiⁿ(向前). *go*, chìn-tsôiⁿ(進前); kṳ̃n-tsôiⁿ(近前). *bent*, hâu-ie(豪腰). *a letter*, thòi-kià-sìn(代寄信). *disposition*, tōa-táⁿ(大膽); bô-kui-kṳ́(無規矩).

**foster**, iáng(養); iáng-io̍k(養育); bú-iáng(撫養); chhī-tōa(飼大). *foster mother*, iáng-bó(養母). *foster mother (wet-nurse)*, nîⁿ-bó(年母). *foster son*, iáng-kiáⁿ(養囝). *foster son (the last three expressions must not be used in addressing the parties)*, mêng-lêng-kiáⁿ(明靈囝).

**foul**, u-ùe(污穢); nah-sap(垃圾); nah-sap-sièⁿ(垃圾相). *wind*, nge̍k-huang(逆風); m̄-sũn-huang(毋順風); tùi-thâu-huang(對頭風); tng-thâu-huang(當頭風); thêⁿ-thâu-huang(庭頭風). *mouthed*, tshou-tshùi(粗碎); tshou-tshò(粗錯); ak-tshùi(惡碎); ta̍k-tshùi(毒碎); tshùi ak-ta̍k(碎惡毒).

**found**, *a dynasty*, khai-kok(開國); tshàng-kok(創國); li̍p-chhiâu(立朝). *metal*, tsù-kim(鑄金). *iron-foundry*, tsù-thih-lôu(鑄鐵爐).

**foundation**, *of house*, tī-kha(地骹); ki-chí(地骹); tī-ki(地骹). *to lay*, pàng-tī-kha(放地骹); kiẽn-tī-kha(建地骹).

**founder**, tîm-tsûn(沉船); huang phah-tiāu-tsûn(風拍掉船); sái-khap--lo̍h-khṳ̀(使磕落去).

**foundling**, *hospital*, io̍k-eng-tn̂g(育嬰堂).

**fountain**, tsûaⁿ(泉); tsúi-tsûaⁿ(水泉); tsûaⁿ-tsúi(泉水); ngûan-tsûaⁿ(源泉); suaⁿ-tsûaⁿ(山泉); kheⁿ-tsûaⁿ(坑泉); ngûan-thâu(源頭); pńg-ngûan(本源).

**four**, sì(四). *four-cornered*, sì-kak(四角). *four-square*, sì-pang(四方). *four-fold*, sì-pũe(四倍).

**fowl**, koi(雞); chiáu(鳥). *water*, tsúi-chiáu(水鳥). *domestic*, koi. *to*, lia̍h-chiáu(掠鳥); phah-chiáu(拍鳥); thi-chiáu(治鳥); iap-chiáu(壓鳥); siā-chiáu(射鳥). *fowling-piece*, chiáu-chhèng(鳥銃).

**fox**, hôu-lâi(猴來); suaⁿ-káu(山狗).

**fraction**, lân-ló〔〕; lân-tshùi(零碎); tshàm-tshùi(纖碎).

**fracture**, chi̍h(折). *bone*, chi̍h-kut(折骨).

**fragile**, nńg-jia̍k(軟弱); kōi-phùa(易破); sou-sou(酥酥).

**fragrant**, phang(香); õi-phang(會香); chheng-hiang(清香). *sandal wood*, hieⁿ-tshâ(香柴). *plants*, hieⁿ-tsháu(香草). *fragrance*, hiang-khì(香氣).

**frail**, iêⁿ-hue tsúi-sèⁿ(楊花水性); nńg-jia̍k(軟弱); m̄-tōiⁿ(毋𠕆); m̄-kien-kù(毋堅固).

**frame**, kè(架). *door*, mn̂g-táu(門斗); mn̂g-khuan(門框); mn̂g-khuang(門框).

**France**, Tãi-huap-kok(大法國); Huat-lân-se(法蘭西).

**frankincense**, zú-hieⁿ(乳香).

**frantic**, siáu(少); tien-khûang(顛狂).

**fraternal**, zû-hiaⁿ zû-tĩ(如兄如弟). *a fraternity*, hũe(會). *fraternise*, pài-hũe(拜會); kau-tshap(交插).

**fraud**, sai-chiàm(使占); khi-phièn(欺騙); kuang-phièn(誆騙); tsà(詐); ngũi(偽); ké(假).

**fray**, tshàu-nãuⁿ(吵鬧); sie-jiáng(相嚷); jiáng-lāu-jie̍t(嚷鬧熱).

**freak**, thèng-tsò thèng-ûi(聽做聽爲).

**freckle**, seⁿ-tiám(生點); seⁿ-hue-tiám(生花點).

**free**, tsṳ̃-iû(自由); tsṳ̃-tsú(自主); ka-kī õi-tsú-ì(家己會主意); tsṳ̃-tsãi(自在). *from crime*, bô-tsũe(無罪). *choice*, sûi-ì tsṳ̃-piẽn(隨意自便). *bond and*, tsú-po̍k(主僕). *to set*, kiù(救); sek-pàng(釋放); pàng-tshut(放出); pàng--nâng tsṳ̃-iû(放人自由). *to set (ransom)*, so̍k-tshut(贖出). *freely (willingly)*, kam-sim(甘心); chhêng-ngũan(情願); huaⁿ-hí(歡喜); kam-ngũan(甘願). *drink freely*, sûi-piẽn chia̍h-chiú(隨便食酒). *gratuitously*, mién-chîⁿ(免錢); mín-ēng-chîⁿ(免用錢).

**freebooter**, tãu-tsha̍t(盜賊); tsha̍t-bé(賊馬).

**freeze**, kit-piaⁿ(結冰); kit-piaⁿ-sng(結冰霜); sêng-piaⁿ(成冰). *as gravy or oil*, kṳ̂n-tàng(凍檔). *to death*, tàng-sí(凍死); kûaⁿ-sí(寒死).

**freight**, tsûn-tsou(船租). *a*, che̍k-tsāi-hùe(一儎貨). *to*, tah-hùe(搭貨).

**frequently**, ke-ke-hãng(加加項); tsōi-tsōi-tshṳ̀(㩼㩼次); ē-ē(下下); lú-lú(屢屢); lú-tshṳ̀(屢次); siêⁿ-siêⁿ(常常); sî-sî(時時); kú-kú(久久); chhiâng-chhiâng(常常); múeⁿ-múeⁿ(每每).

**fresh**, *water*, chiáⁿ-tsúi(䭕水). *fish*, chhiⁿ-hṳ̂(鮮魚); hṳ̂-chhiⁿ(魚鮮). *new*, sin(新). *lively*, ũ-sin-khì(有新氣). *taste*, chhiⁿ-bī(鮮味); chiáⁿ-bī(䭕味).

**fret**, *fret (intransitive)*, iu-ut(憂鬱); tsṳ̃-thàng(自歎); tshoih〔〕; pui-tshoih〔〕; uàn-tshoih(怨嘈). *fret (child) (intransitive)*, e̍hⁿ-e̍hⁿ-kiè(軛軛叫). *fret (transitive)*, kek-sèⁿ(激性); kek-khì(激氣).

**friction**, chhiù(漱); bûa(磨).

**Friday**, lói-pài-ngõu(禮拜五); pài-ngõu(拜五).

**friend**, *(only used of men, never of women, except in bad sense)*, phêng-iú(朋友). *an old*, kū-iú(故友); kū-jîn(故人). *very close*, chì-iú(摯友); ba̍t-iú(密友); hó-iú(好友). *bosom-friend*, sim-pak phêng-iú(心腹朋友); ti-sim phêng-iú(知心朋友); ti-kí(知己). *acquaintance (but not intimate)*, kháu-thâu-iú(口頭友). *school or college friend*, tâng-theng phêng-iú(同窗朋友); theng-iú(窗友). *companion*, tâng-phũaⁿ(同伴). *on friendly terms*, siang-hó(相好). *friendly treatment*, kãu-thãi(厚待). *break off friendship*, tso̍h-kau(絕交).

**frighten**, phièn-nâng-kiaⁿ(騙人驚); kiaⁿ-tie̍h-nâng(驚着人). *by threats*, kiaⁿ-heh(驚嚇). *frightened*, kiaⁿ(驚). *to death*, kiaⁿ-kàu-sí(驚到死). *to death (also means very much frightened)*, kiaⁿ-sí(驚死). *frightful*, tshūa-nâng-kiaⁿ(𤆬人驚); kiaⁿ-sí-nâng(驚死人).

**frigid**, chhìn(凊). *heart*, sim néⁿ(心冷); néⁿ-ì(冷意). *manner*, néⁿ-tãⁿ(冷淡).

**fringe**, chhiu(鬚).

**frisk**, *thiàu-iak; kha thiàu*, chhiú mõng(手舞).

**fritter**, *away time*, tak-nn̄g-tiāu sî-hāu〔〕.

**frivolous**, khin-phû(輕浮); hàuⁿ-tsò bô-siang-kan sṳ̄(好做無相干事). *matter*, khin-sṳ̄(輕事); sòi-sṳ̄(細事); sié-khó-sṳ̄(小可事); bô-chhiet-iàu(無切要); bô-iàu-kín(無要緊); bô-siang-kan(無相干); bô-kàu tî-kò-khṳ̀(無到底塊去).

**frizzle**, khek(刻); khek-khek(刻刻). *cause to*, zuán-khek(轉刻).

**frog**, tsúi-koi(水雞); kap-pô(蛤婆); kap-kiú(水雞). *tadpole*, kap-kiú-kuai(蛤虯鮭).

**frolic**, sńg(耍); sie-sńg(相耍); hì-sńg kâi-sṳ̄(戲耍个事).

**from**, tsṳ̃(自); tshông(從); iû(由). *from...to*, iû...kàu(由...到); iû...chì(由...至); tsṳ̃...chì(自...至); tsṳ̃...kàu(自...到). *Swatow is over three leagues from Ching-hai*, Sùaⁿ-thâu lî Thêng-hái saⁿ-phòu-gūa lōu(線頭離澄海三舖外路). *home*, bô-tõ(無在); m̄-tõ(毋在); tshut-khṳ̀-kháu(出去口). *youth*, tsṳ̃ iùⁿ-nîⁿ(自幼年). *salute the brethren from me*, thòi-uá mn̄g-hāu chèng-ūi hiaⁿ-tĩ(代我問候眾位兄弟). *from avarice*, tshut-tõ tham-sim(出在貪心).

**front**, tsôiⁿ-mīn(前面); chiàⁿ-mīn(正面); tsôiⁿ-pôiⁿ(前爿). *door*, thâu-mn̂g(頭門); tōa-mn̂g(大門); tsóng-mn̂g(總門). *in front*, tõ-mīn-tsôiⁿ(在面前); tõ-thâu-tsôiⁿ(在頭前). *walk in front*, kiâⁿ tõ-thâu-tsôiⁿ(行在頭前); thâu-soiⁿ-kiâⁿ(頭先行). *stand opposite to*, hiàng(向); niàⁿ(領).

**frontier**, tī-kài(地界); kéng-kài(境界); kài-hãn(界限); pien-kiang(邊疆); pien-kài(邊界); piⁿ-kài(邊界); pien-thêng(邊庭). *to watch the frontier*, siú-pien(守邊).

**frontlet**, chiau-kun-ûi(招軍圍); hia̍h-tsôiⁿ-ûi(額前圍); ou-kṳn-khou(烏根箍).

**frost**, sng(霜). *and snow*, sng-soh(霜雪). *hoar-frost*, lo̍h-sng(落霜). *frost-bite*, kûaⁿ-tàng(寒凍).

**froth**, tshùi-nũaⁿ(喙涎); tshùi-phue̍h(碎沫); nũaⁿ-phue̍h(涎波); tsúi-phue̍h(水波).

**froward**, hûeⁿ-nge̍k(橫逆); nguán-nge̍k(頑逆); nguán-ngẽ(頑硬).

**frown**, náuⁿ-ma̍k(惱目); niàuⁿ-bâi(皺眉). *look at one with a*, ma̍k kàng-kàng tõ-hîm--i(目降降在熊伊). *expressing contempt and hatred by curling up the nose and frowning*, niàuⁿ-bâi niàuⁿ-phīⁿ(皺眉皺鼻), ma̍k kàng-kàng tõ-hîm--i(目降降在熊伊). *expression of anxiety*, tshok-bâi(蹙眉); ma̍k-bâi kat-kat(目眉結結); bâi-thâu tshok-tshok(眉頭蹙蹙). *to draw one's eye-brows together in a kind of frown*, bâi-thâu tièⁿ-tshok-tshok(眉頭張蹙蹙).

**frugal**, khiãm(儉); tsat-khiãm(節儉); khiãm-tsat(儉節); tsat-ēng(節用); khiãm-ēng(儉用); iak-iak(約約); séⁿ-iak(省約); séⁿ(省); khiãm-iak(儉約). *frugality is better than a large income*, khiãm-chia̍h kiêⁿ-kùe-thàn(儉食強過趁).

**fruit**, kúeⁿ(果); kúeⁿ-chí(果子). *fresh*, chheⁿ-kúeⁿ(青果). *dried*, kan-kúeⁿ(柑果). *to bear*, seⁿ-kúeⁿ(生果); kat-kúeⁿ(結果); kit-kúeⁿ(結果子); kat-si̍t(結實); kit-si̍t(結實). *to pluck*, tiah-kúeⁿ-chí(摘果子). *fruitful*, õi-seⁿ(會生); seⁿ-tsōi(生㩼); seⁿ-lâi-kãu(生來厚). *fruitful season*, nîⁿ-tang hó(年冬好). *fruitbearing*, hó-kat-si̍t(好結實). *fruitless*, bõi-seⁿ(袂生).  *fruitless (useless)*, bô-iah(無益); bô-ēng(無用).

**frustrate**, sái m̄-sêng-sṳ̄(使毋成事); hāi m̄-sêng-sṳ̄(害毋成事); gōu-sṳ̄ m̄-sêng(誤事毋成). *a plot*, phùa-kòi(破計).

**fry**, *with little or no fat (implies much stirring and turning over).*, tshá(炒). *with a little fat, and few turns*, luah(烙). *with a little water and perhaps hat*, chien(煎). *frying-pan*, tiáⁿ-kiáⁿ(鼎囝). *frying-pan (shallow)*, chien-pûaⁿ(煎盤). *frying-pan (deeper)*, tiáⁿ(鼎).

**fuel**, tshâ(柴); mue̍h-hiâⁿ(物行); tshâ-tsháu(柴草). *gather*, khieh-mue̍h-hiâⁿ(挈物燃). *add*, thiam-húe(添火); thiam-tshâ(添柴); lān-tshâ(爛柴); lān-tsháu(爛草).

**fugitive**, *from justice*, tô-tsũe(逃罪); tsáu-hũam(走犯); i̍t-hũam(逸犯). *from persecution*, pĩ-nâng to̍k-tsáu(逼人逐走).

**fulfil**, *one's expectation*, zû-mōⁿ(如望). *duty*, chĩn-pńg-hūn(盡本分); ûan-pńg-hūn(完本分); chĩn-cheh(盡節). *command*, zû-mẽng(如命). *law*, siú-huap(守法); tsun-huap(遵法). *promise*, zû-ieh(如約); siú-ieh(守約). *prediction*, èng-ngiām(應驗); hāu-ngiām(效驗); teng-ngiām(證驗). *prayer*, tsò-chiâⁿ(做成); èng-ngiām. *vows*, hôiⁿ-ngūan(還願).

**full**, múaⁿ(滿); tĩⁿ(漲); pá(飽). *full-grown*, chiáng-sêng(長成); chiáng-tōa(長大); tōa—liáu(大了). see FILL.

**fully**, tshûan(全); chĩn(盡); thàu(透); thàng(通); sêng(成); chiâⁿ(成).

**fumble**, *in one's pocket*, chiâm-tō〔〕. *about, as in the dark or blind person*, mông-at〔〕; thèng-mông, thèng-at〔〕.

**fumes**, khì(氣); bī(味).

**fumigate**, *a room*, phek-tiāu ùe-khì(癖吊穢氣); hun-tiāu tshàu-khì(熏吊臭氣).

**fun**, *to make*, sńg(耍); sie-sńg(相耍); chhiè-thâm(笑貪). *funny*, tshù-bī(趣味); hó-chhiè(好笑). *say anything in fun*, tàⁿ-sńg(等耍).

**funds**, pńg-chîⁿ(本錢); bó-thâu(母頭).

**fundamental**, pńg(本); kṳn-pńg(根本); pńg-ngûan(本元); pńg-iàu(本要); pńg-bũ(本務); tói-tsṳ́(底子).

**funeral**, sng-sṳ̄(喪事). *attend a*, sàng-tsǹg(送葬); sàng-kiũ(送求); sàng-kuaⁿ-ba̍k chiẽⁿ-suaⁿ(送官目上山).

**fungus**, kou(菇). *on trees*, chhiū-kou(樹菇); chhiū-zṳ́(樹耳); ba̍k-zṳ́(木耳). *edible*, hieⁿ-kou(香菇). *covered with*, seⁿ-kou(生菇).

**funnel**, *for pouring water*, khuah-tshùi-làu(闊喙漏). *for liquor*, chiú-hái(酒海). *of steamer*, in-tâng(煙筒); húe-hun(火薰); tâng(筒).

**fur**, môⁿ(毛). *furs*, phûe(皮). *coat*, phûe-niûⁿ(皮裘). *long fur coat*, phûe-tn̂g-niûⁿ(皮長裘).

**furbish**, bûa-kng(磨光). *as sword or knife*, bûa-pe̍h(磨白); bûa-kàu soh-soh-pe̍h(磨到雪雪白).

**furious**, hiông-méⁿ(雄猛); khì kàu kuáng-kuáng-kiè(氣到廣廣叫); khì kàu thuh-thuh-kiè(氣到腯腯叫); khuâng-pãu(狂暴).

**furl**, *as sail*, kauh(捲); kauh-bûa(捲埋); kauh-khí(捲起); kńg-khí(卷起).

**furnace**, tsàu(灶); lôu(爐); lôu-tsàu(爐灶); tsàu-lôu(灶爐); huang-lôu(風爐). *for refining gold*, kim-lôu(金爐). *for burning tiles*, sie-hiã-iê(燒瓦窯).

**furnish**, *prepare*, pĩ-phōiⁿ(備辦). *provide*, keng-kip(供給); keng-ēng(供用). *provide (by subscription)*, phài-kip(派給).

**furniture**, ke-si mue̍h-kiãⁿ(家私物件); ke-húe(家伙); tshn̂g-íⁿ(床椅). *of student*, bûn-pâng sì-pó(文房四寶).

**furrow**, lôi-tsūe(犁罪). *furrows*, che̍k-nôiⁿ che̍k-nôiⁿ(一蓮一蓮). *of the face*, mīn-phûe-jiâu(面皮嬈); mīn jiâu-jiâu(面嬈嬈); mīn seⁿ-hûn(面生魂).

**further**, khuàng-chhiáⁿ(況且); siãng-chhiáⁿ(尙且); lêng-gūa(另外); lêng-ūaⁿ(另外); huân-liáu(還了); huân-iáu(還要).

**fuse**, *metal*, khan-lôu(牽爐); khan-iêⁿ(牽洋). *fused*, iêⁿ(烊). *and cast*, tsù(鑄).

**fusee**, húe-lêng(火龍). *(tinder)*, húe-hiāⁿ(火艾).

**fuss**, *make a fuss about a small matter*, sié-sṳ̄ tãng-pò(小事動報); khin-sṳ̄ tãng-khì(輕事動氣); lo-sl(囉嗦); lo-lo so-so(囉囉嗦嗦). *fussy*, kín-kip(緊急); kip-kṳ̃(急據); huang-mâng(慌忙); huang-huang huh-huh(風風欻欻).

**future**, chiang-lâi(將來); ãu-lâi(後來); ẽ-ji̍t(下日); ãu-ji̍t(後日); ji̍t-ãu(日後). *in future*, tshông-kim íⁿ-ãu(從今以後). *the future state*, lâi-seⁿ(來生); lâi-sì(來世). *see into the future*, būe-lâi soiⁿ-tsai(未來先知).

### G

**gabble**, chiauh-chiauh-kiè(雀雀叫); kā-kā-kiè(咳咳叫).

**gable**, *of house*, pui(卑); pui-thâu(卑頭); tshù-pui(厝卑).

**gadfly**, gû-pi(牛碑).

**gag**, lêng-hâm(龍含).

**gage**, tǹg(當).

**gain**, lĩ(利); iah(益). *seek*, thû-lĩ(圖利); khiû-lĩ(求利); tshūe-lĩ(覓利). *get*, tit-lĩ(得利); thàn(趁). *a victory*, thâi-iâⁿ(刣贏).

**gainsay**, poh-khùi(駁氣); sie-à(相詏).

**gait**, kiâⁿ-pān(行辦). *slow*, kiâⁿ-pān ûn-ûn(行辦勻勻); kiâⁿ-pān mān(行辦慢); kiâⁿ-pān ûn-ûn tshāi-tshāi(行辦穩穩在在). *quick*, kiâⁿ-pān méⁿ-méⁿ hiông-hiông(行步猛猛雄雄). *uncertain: running, jumping and slow*, chhih-chhih-tshóiⁿ〔〕. *very feeble*, kiâⁿ-pān ûe-ûe jê-jê(行步微微弱弱).

**gale**, tōa-huang(大風); khuâng-huang(大風). *hurricane*, huang-thai(風颱). *blowing a*, thàu-tōa-huang(透大風); khuâng-huang tãi-tsak(狂風大作).

**gall**, táⁿ(膽). *of bear*, hîm-táⁿ(熊膽). *nuts*, ngõu-pũe-chí(五倍指).

**gallery**, lâu-thâi(樓臺).

**gallipot**, kài-au(蓋甌); khàm-au(勘甌); ie̍h-au(藥甌); kài-puah(蓋缽). *(large)*, ie̍h-puah(藥鉢).

**gallop**, pháu-bé(跑馬).

**gallows**, ká-kê(絞枷); tiàu-ãm-kê(吊頸枷).

**gambling**, pua̍h(跋); pua̍h-chîⁿ(跋錢); pua̍h-kiáu(跋繳); tóu-chîⁿ(賭錢); tú-chîⁿ(賭錢); su-iâⁿ(輸贏). *(euphemism)*, sńg-chhiè(耍笑). *with cards*, pua̍h-tsúa-pâi(跋紙牌). *lose by*, pua̍h-su(跋輸). *win by*, pua̍h-iâⁿ(跋營). *one who makes a business of*, lãu-pua̍h-kiáu(老跋繳). *public table for*, pua̍h-chîⁿ-tiêⁿ(跋錢場); pua̍h-chîⁿ-kuán(跋錢館); tóu-tiêⁿ(賭場); tóu-kuán(賭館). *to keep such a place*, khui-tiêⁿ(開場); siet-tóu(設賭); khui-tóu-tiêⁿ(開賭場).

**game**, *play (of chess)*, teh che̍k-puâⁿ-kî(壓一盤棋). *I won four games of chess from him*, uá teh-iâⁿ--i sì-pûa-kî(我壓贏伊四盤棋). *gamecock*, chhie-koi(猜個); chhie-koi-ang(猜個紅).

**gander**, gô-hêng(鵝行).

**gang**, *pan; khûn*, táng(黨); tūi(隊).

**gangrene**, sí-ne̍k(死肉); àu-ne̍k(懊肉).

**gaol**, kam(監). *put in*, kìm-kam(禁監). *to be in*, siu-kam(收監); siu-kam tsõ-lô(收監坐牢). *gaoler*, kìm-chí(禁子); kím-tsut(錦卒).

**gap**, khiah(隙); khang-khiah(空隙); làn-phāng(爛空洞). *to stop a*, póu-khiah(補隙).

**gape**, *the mouth*, tshùi thí-khuah-khuah(喙體闊闊); tièⁿ-khuah-khuah(帳闊闊). *yawn*, huah-hì(呵呬); huah-hì kàu tshùi khuah-khuah(喝戲到碎闊闊). *in wonder*, thóiⁿ-kàu ma̍k khui-khui tshùi khui-khui(睇到目開開碎開開); thóiⁿ-kàu ma̍k khuah tshùi khuah(睇到目闊碎闊).

**garble**, *a statement*, súan-chiaⁿ to̍h-pûi tàⁿ(選正擇肥呾).

**garden**, hn̂g(園); pou-hn̂g(埔園). *flower*, hue-hn̂g(花園). *vegetable*, tshài-hn̂g(菜園). *fruit*, kúeⁿ-chí-hn̂g(果子園). *gardener*, tsho-hn̂g-nâng(初園人); chèng-hn̂g-nâng(種園人); hn̂g-teng(園丁).

**gargle**, lō-tshùi(了碎); lō-âu(了喉); sok-kháu(縮口).

**garlic**, sǹg(蒜). *(fresh)*, chheⁿ-sǹg(青蒜). *(ripe roots)*, sǹg-thâu(蒜頭).

**garments**, i-ho̍k(衣服); kûn-saⁿ(裙衫); saⁿ-khòu(衫褲); ho̍k-sek(服色).

**garnish**, hún-sek(粉飾); siu-sek(修飾); tsuang-pàn(裝扮); tsuang-tshái(裝彩); pái-tshái(擺彩); tsuang-sek(裝飾).

**garrison**, siú-siâⁿ-piaⁿ(守城兵); siú-piaⁿ(守兵).

**garrulous**, tsōi-tshùi(㩼喙); tsōi-ūe(㩼話); hàuⁿ-tàⁿ-ūe(好呾話).

**garter**, bue̍h-tòa(襪帶); hû-sek(扶色).

**gash**, *to*, phoh kâi-sieⁿ-kháu(劈个傷口); le̍h(裂).

**gasp**, kip-khùi(急氣); tshuán(喘); tshuán-khì(喘氣); tshuán-kip(喘急).

**gate**, mn̂g(門); tōa-mn̂g(大門). *sity-gate*, siâⁿ-mn̂g(城門). *street-gate*, tsa̍h-mn̂g(大門); koi-tsa̍h(大門).

**gather**, siu(收); siu-si̍p(收拾); siu-bûa(收埋); siu-si̍p-bûa(收拾埋); siu-khí(收起). *as people*, tsũ-chi̍p(聚集); chi̍p-hũe(集會); hũe-chi̍p(會集); tsũ-hũe(聚會); hũe-ha̍h(會合); hũe-bûa(會埋); ha̍h-bûa(合埋). *flowers*, tiah-hue(摘花).

**gaudy**, kuang-tshái(光彩); phâi-chhiâng(排場); chheng-tshái(清彩); iām-lĩ(豔麗).

**gauze**, se(紗).

**gay**, iâu-i̍t(搖逸); kuang-tshái(光彩); phâi-chhiâng(排場); hûa-múiⁿ(華美); ngiá(雅).

**gaze**, ma̍k kim-kim thóiⁿ(目金金睇); thóiⁿ kàu ma̍k bõi-nihⁿ(睇到目袂𥍉).

**gazette**, *Peking*, kiaⁿ-pò(驚報).

**gear**, *of boat, &c*, ke-húe(家伙).

**gelatinous**, ũ-ka-liâm〔〕; ũ-tan-tah〔〕.

**gem**, ge̍k(玉); pó-ge̍k(寶玉); pó-chie̍h(寶石); pó-pùe(寶貝).

**genealogy**, tso̍k-phóu(族譜). *ranks of*, pùe-sũ(輩序).

**general (comprehensive)**, thóng(統); thong(通); tsóng(總); kong(公). *term*, tsóng-miâⁿ(總名); lóng-thóng-tàⁿ(攏統呾). *don't use general terms but be precise*, lṳ́ chhiet-si̍t lâi-tàⁿ, màiⁿ-lóng-thóng(汝切實來呾，勿攏統); chí-tiāⁿ(指定), màiⁿ-hùam-sueh(勿泛說). *use*, thong-ēng(通用). *peace*, thài-phêng(太平). *generally speaking*, tãi-khài(大慨); thóng-thóng(統統); tãi-sì(大勢); tãi-lia̍k(大略).

**general**, *in the army*, tsóng-piaⁿ(總兵); tsóng-piaⁿ-kuaⁿ(總兵官); tsóng-zông(總茸). *generalissimo*, ngûan-sùe(元帥); tsú-sùe(主帥).

**generate**, seⁿ(生).

**generation**, tō(代); sì-tō(世代). *from one, to another*, le̍h-tō(歷代). *future*, ãu-tō(後代).

**generous**, sim-heng khuah-khuah(心胸闊闊); khuang-khài(慷慨); ũ-tóu-liãng(有肚量); tóu-liãng hó(肚量好); tóu-liãng khuan-khuan(肚量寬寬); khuan-iông tãi-liãng(寬容大量). see LIBERAL.

**genial**, *(of men or weather)*, un-hûa(溫和). *(of men)*, un-jiû(溫柔). *(of the weather)*, un-lúan(溫暖). *(warm)*, chhiẽⁿ-sie(上燒).

**genii**, sien(秈); sîn-sien(辰仙). *the eight*, poih-sien(八仙). *their habitation*, sien-kéng(仙境).

**genius**, *a*, tshâi-tsṳ́(才子); ũ-tshâi-chhêng kâi-nâng(有才情个人).

**genteel**, bûn-ngiá(文雅). *(accomplished)*, sṳ-bûn(斯文).

**gentle**, un-hûa(溫和); hûa-sũn(和順); un-jiû(溫柔); liâng-siẽn(良善). see GENTLY.

**gentleman**, lãu-nâng-ke(老人家); lãu-iâ(老爺). *(father of graduate)*, thài-kong(太公). *(mandarin, but also wider use)*, lãu-tia(老爹). *young  (son of mandarin)*, siàu-iâ(少爺). *this old gentleman*, chí-ūi lãu-nâng-ke(此位老人家).

**gently**, khin-khin(輕輕); ûn-ûn(紜紜); mān-mān(慢慢); khuaⁿ-khuaⁿ(寬寬). see GENTLE.

**gentry**, hieⁿ-sin(鄉紳); sin-khim(紳襟); sin-sṳ̃(紳士).

**genuflection**, kũi(跪); kũiⁿ(跪); kiâⁿ-tōa-lói(行大禮); hẽ-tōa-lói(下大禮).

**genuine**, chin-si̍t(真實); chin(真). *not*, ké(假); m̄-chiàⁿ(毋正).

**genus**, lūi(類).

**geography**, tī-lí(地理). *book on*, tī-lí-chì(地理志); tī-lí-tsṳ(地理書).

**geomancy**, tĩ-lí(地里); thóiⁿ-suaⁿ(看山); tsáu-tī-lí(走地里); kiâⁿ-tī-lí(行地里); thóiⁿ-huang-tsúi(看風水). *geomancer*, thóiⁿ-suaⁿ sin-seⁿ(看山紳生); huang-tsúi sin-seⁿ(風水先生).

**geometry**, niêⁿ-tī-huap(年地法).

**Germany**, Tãi-Tek-kok(大德國); tsa̍p-káng-kok(十江國).

**germ**, gê(芽). *germinate*, huat-gê(發芽); mêng-gê(萌芽); pauh-gê〔〕.

**gestures**, *to use*, *in speaking*, kha mông, chhiú pí(骹摸手比).

**get**, tit(得); tit--tie̍h(得着). *up*, tsáu-khí(早起). *could not get it done*, tsò-m̄-sêng(做毋成); tsò-m̄-chiâⁿ(做毋成). *rich*, huat-tshâi(發財); tì-pù(致富). *ready*, ṳ̃-pĩ(預備); tsôi-pĩ(齊備); pĩ-phōiⁿ(備辦); pĩ-pīn〔〕. *into office*, tit-ūi(得位); tit-jĩm(得任). *advancement*, kau-seng(高升); seng-kuaⁿ(升官); seng-khip(升級). *one's wishes*, tit-ì(得意); zû-ì(如意); tit-sim kùe-ì(得心過意). *out of the way*, kiâⁿ-khui(行開); tsáu-khui(走開); kiâⁿ-bûa(行埋); khiã-khui(徛開). *angry*, seⁿ-khì(生氣); huat-náuⁿ(發惱). *hold of*, lia̍h--tie̍h(掠着). *aground (ship)*, khùa-sua(掛沙); hũam-suaⁿ〔〕. *into trouble*, lap-tie̍h-sin(套着身). *a cold*, sieⁿ-huang(傷風). *where ever did you get this*, lṳ́ tsò-ũ chí-kâi-mue̍h(汝怎有此個物).

**ghost**, kúi(鬼); siàⁿ-nâng(聖人); siàⁿ-hùe-mue̍h(聖貨物). *Holy*, Siàⁿ-Sîn(聖神).

**giant**, tōa-hān(大漢); kûiⁿ-nâng(懸人); kau-chhiâng tã-hān(高長大漢); kûiⁿ-tōa(懸大).

**giddy**, hîn(眩); thâu-khak-hîn(頭殼眩); hîn kàu-kông(眩到戇); kông-kông(戇戇); hîn kàu chiang-pua̍h(眩到將跋). *in character*, hàuⁿ-thit-thô(好佚佗).

**gift**, lói-mue̍h(禮物); sàng-lói(送禮); sie-sàng(相送). *gracious*, ṳn-sṳ̀(恩賜).

**giggle**, khih-khih-chhiè〔〕.

**gild**, tah-kim(貼金); liū-kim(鎦金); tōu-kim(鍍金); sieⁿ-kim(鑲金); tsṳ́-kim〔〕.

**gimlet**, tsǹg-kiáⁿ(鑽囝).

**gin**, *snare*, se-khou(紗箍); phùaⁿ-soh(判索); chiáu-mãng(鳥網); tieⁿ-chiáu-sùaⁿ(張鳥散). *to set a*, tieⁿ-keng siet-nãuⁿ(電經設腦).

**ginger**, kieⁿ(薑). *hard dry root (medicine)*, kieⁿ-bó(薑母). *young, tender and fresh*, chíⁿ-kieⁿ(稚薑). *sweetmeat*, thn̂g-kieⁿ(糖薑); bi̍t-chìm-kieⁿ(蜜浸薑).

**ginseng**, jîn-siam(人參). *foreign*, iêⁿ-siam(羊參). *to buy*, táu-siam(倒參).

**gird**, hâ(縖); pa̍k(縛); hâ-tòa(縖帶). *up*, kiáu-phû soih-tōa〔〕.

**girdle**, ie-tòa(腰帶); ki-tòa(肌帶); ki-ie(肌腰).

**girl**, tsṳ-niêⁿ-kiáⁿ(諸娘囝); a-niêⁿ-kiáⁿ(阿娘囝); tsáu-kiáⁿ(走囝). *boys and girls*, tsṳ́-nńg(子女). *servant-girl*, tsáu-kúi(走鬼); chhiah-kha(赤骹); hia-thâu(下頭).

**girth**, bé-tõu-tòa(馬肚帶). *what is the girth of this tree*, chí-tsâng-chhiū chiu-ûi jie̍h-tōa(指叢樹周圍若大).

**give**, pun(分); sṳ̀(賜); khṳt(乞); sàng(送); ṳ́(予). *assent*, tsún(準). *in marriage*, kè(嫁); kè--pun-nâng(嫁分人). *into one's care*, hù-thoh(付托). *way to one*, jiãng(讓); jiãng-ūi(讓位). *in*, tho(胎). *over to*, kau(交); kau-hôiⁿ(交還). *up evil*, khì-siâ kói-ak(棄邪改惡). *one's life*, siá-miāⁿ(捨命); khì-sin(棄身); siá-miāⁿ khì-sin(捨命棄身). *notice*, pò-tsai(報知). *evidence*, keng(供); kháu-keng(口供). *alms*, si-chì(施濟); chì-phîn(濟貧); chín-chì(賑濟); kiù-chì(救濟); si-siá(施捨). *trouble*, kiáu-jiáu(攪擾); lâu(流); huân-lâu(還流); bûa-lūi(磨累). *given to*, hàuⁿ(好).

**gizzard**, kṳ̃n(近).

**glad**, huaⁿ-hí(歡喜); hí-la̍k(喜樂). *very*, huaⁿ-huaⁿ hí-hí(歡歡喜喜). *to make*, sái--nâng huaⁿ-hí(使人歡喜); khṳt--nâng huaⁿ-hí(乞人歡喜).

**glance**, iáⁿ-ma̍k(影目). *to see at a*, che̍k-iáⁿ chiũ-tsai(一影就知); che̍k-thóiⁿ chiũ-tsai(一睇就知); che̍k-ma̍k liáu-jiên(一目了然). *metaph.*, che̍k-siẽⁿ chiũ-tsai(一想就知).

**glare**, *of the sun*, ji̍t-tsam chhiēⁿ-tie̍h-ma̍k(日針上着目); ji̍t-tsam tsam-tie̍h-ma̍k(日針針着目). *from water*, ji̍t-tsam tõ-tsúi-tói húan-chie--khí-lâi(日針在水底反照起來); iap-iap-sih(灼灼熠). *glare with the eyes*, ma̍k-chiu lìn-lìn-khah〔〕; ma̍k-chiu khah-khah-lìn〔〕. *too glaring*, khah-tshut-sek(較出色).

**glass**, po-lî(玻璃). *(not quite the same)*, liû-lî(琉璃). *to male*, ié-po-lî(調玻璃); pûn-po-lî(歕玻璃). *bottle*, po-lî-tsun(玻璃樽). *for drinking*, po-lî-pue(玻璃杯); po-lî-cheng(玻璃鐘).

**glaucoma**, ou-jîn pièn-chheⁿ(烏仁變青); chheⁿ-kuang hak-ngán(青光瞎眼).

**glaze**, thn̄g(搪). *to glaze*, lâm-thn̄g(藍搪).

**gleam**, kng che̍k-ē-chiè(光一下照); kng iap-che̍k-kiè(光壓一叫).

**glean**, khieh-chhek-sūi(挈測穗); to̍h-chhek-sūi(擇測穗).

**glistering**, õi-kng(會光); kng-chiè(光照); iaⁿ-chiè(影照); kng iaⁿ-iaⁿ(光影影); kng iàⁿ-iàⁿ(光映映); tāng-tāng-kng(堂堂光); ia̍p-ia̍p-sih(灼灼熠).

**globe**, kiû(球). *terrestrial*, tī-kiû(地球). *celestial*, thien-kiû(天球). *globular*, îⁿ(圓);îⁿ-thói(圓體); îⁿ-chieh(圓接); îⁿ-hêng(圓形); lòng-lòng-îⁿ(弄弄圓); îⁿ-lìn-lìn(圓輾輾).

**gloomy**, *weather*, thiⁿ ou-àm(天烏暗); thiⁿ mông-lông(天蒙朧).

**glory**, iông-kuang(榮光); iông-hûa(榮華). *gloryfy*, kui-iông-kuang(歸榮光).

**gloss**, *over a fault*, chia-buah(遮抹); iám-sek(掩飾). *commentary*, tsù-kói(註解). *glossy*, kng-kng(光光).

**gloves**, chhiú-thàu(手套). *put on*, lap-chhiú-thàu〔〕; kùa-chhiú-thàu(掛手套).

**glow**, jie̍t(熱); jie̍t-jie̍t âng-âng(熱熱紅紅). *glowing coals*, âng-húe-thòaⁿ(紅火炭); jie̍t-thòaⁿ(熱炭). *with rage*, sim jie̍t, mīn âng(心熱面紅).

**glue**, ka(膠); gû-phûe-ka(牛皮膠). *to*, ēng-ka ún-tùe(用膠穩綴). *glutinous*, ũ-ka-liâm〔〕; liâm-nîⁿ tha-thi〔〕; kṳ̍t(滑).

**glume**, tshou-khng(粗糠); chhek-khak(粟殼).

**glut**, pá-ṳ̀(飽飫); chia̍h-kàu-màiⁿ(食到勿); chia̍h-kàu-hẽng(食到行). *in the market*, hâng-chhêng pāi(行情敗); hâng-chhêng pāi nńg(行情敗軟); hâng-chhêng thûaⁿ〔〕.

**gluttonous**, tham-chia̍h(貪食); hàuⁿ-chia̍h(好食); tham-chia̍h kùe-tōu(貪食過度).

**gnash**, kã-gê(咬牙); kã khí-gê-kṳn(咬起牙根).

**gnat**, bun(蚊); bun-kiáⁿ(蚊囝).

**gnaw**, kã(咬); khòi(喫).

**go**, khṳ̀(去); kiâⁿ(行); tsáu(走); uáng(往). *down*, kàng(降); lo̍h(落); hiã(下). *up*, chiẽⁿ(上); seng(升); teng(登); khí(起). *abroad*, tshut-khṳ̀-gūa(出去外); tshut-gūa(出外); kùe-kok(過國); kùe-huan(過番); kùe-iêⁿ(過洋). *out*, khṳ̀-kháu(去口); tshut-khṳ̀-gūa(出去外); tshut-mn̂g(出門); tshut-koi(出街). *out (as fire)*, húe kùe--khṳ̀(火過去). *home*, hûe-ke(回家); tńg-khṳ̀-tshṳ̀(轉去次); kui-ke(歸家). *into the house*, khṳ̀-lãi(去內). *to*, khṳ̀-kàu(去到). *about*, uáng-lâi(往來); chiẽⁿ-lo̍h(上落); kiâⁿ-lâi kiâⁿ-khṳ̀(行來行去). *about (for amusement)*, thit-thô(佚佗); múaⁿ-kò-la̍h(滿塊臘). *about (as ship)*, kùe-phâng(過帆). *and bring*, khṳ̀-khie̍h--lâi(去挈來). *to stool*, kiâⁿ-tãng(行動); chiẽⁿ-chhè(上廁); kiâⁿ-tãi-piẽn(行大便); tshut-kiong(出恭). *to bed*, khṳ̀-gu̍t(去夗). *to market*, chiẽⁿ-chhĩ(上市); tshut-chhĩ(出市); khṳ̀-chhĩ(去市); tàu-hṳ(鬥魚). *on foot*, pōu-kiâⁿ(步行). *on foot (of a person who would ordinarily have a conveyance)*, pōu-lién(步輦). *by water*, tah-tsûn--khṳ̀(搭船去). *by land*, le̍k-lōu--khṳ̀(勒路去); tùi-lōu--khṳ̀(對路去). *on board*, lo̍h-tsûn(落船). *on shore*, chiẽⁿ-suaⁿ(上山); khí-tsúi(起水); chiẽⁿ-khàm(上勘). *upstairs*, khṳ̀-lâu-téng(去樓頂); chiẽⁿ-lâu(上樓). *to a feast*, hù-sia̍h(赴席); khṳ̀-chia̍h-toh(去食桌); èng-sia̍h(應席). *to examination*, hù-kháu(副口); èng-kháu(應口); hù-chhì(副試); èng-chhì(應試). *to heaven*, chiẽⁿ-thiⁿ(上天). *quickly*, kiâⁿ-méⁿ(行猛); tsáu-méⁿ(走猛); kúaⁿ-méⁿ(趕猛). *to visit*, khṳ̀-sie-sûn(去相巡); húang-chhin húang-iú(訪親訪友); khṳ̀-pài-hāu(去拜候). *let him*, iû-i-khṳ̀(由伊去); thèng-i-khṳ̀(亂伊去); kui-i-khṳ̀(歸伊去); sûi-i-khṳ̀(隨伊去). *where are you going*, lṳ́ àiⁿ-khṳ̀ tî-kò(汝愛去底塊). *where has he gone*, i khṳ̀-tî-kò(伊去底塊). *do not know where to go (or, where he has gone)*, m̄-tsai-tùi-tî-kò khṳ̀(毋知對底塊去). *with the tide*, kúaⁿ-lâu(趕流); sũn-lâu(順流). *all through or over*, kiâⁿ-kàu-thàu(行到透). *together*, tsò-pû-kiâⁿ(做伙行); tsò-pû-khṳ̀(做伙去); tâng-kiâⁿ(同行). *before*, soiⁿ-kiâⁿ(先行); thâu-tsôiⁿ-kiâⁿ(頭前行); kiâⁿ tõ-thâu-tsôiⁿ(行在頭前). *behind*, kiâⁿ ka-chiah-ãu(行家跡後). *go to court*, chiẽⁿ-chhiâu(上朝). *to law*, phah-kuaⁿ-si(拍官司). *halves*, sie-kāng(相共); pêⁿ-pun(平分). *and come*, lâi-lâi uáng-uáng(來來往往). *and return*, lâi-hûe(來回).

**goat**, suaⁿ-iêⁿ(山羊).

**GOD**, Siãng-tì(上帝). *to worship*, pài Siãng-tì(拜上帝). *godly*, kèng-ùi Siãng-tì(敬畏上帝). *gods*, sîn-mêng(神明).

**go-down**, tsàn-pâng(棧房).

**gold**, kim(金); n̂g-kim(黃金); chhiah-kim(赤金). *alloyed*, hún-kim(粉金); kẽ-kim(下金). *unalloyed*, tsok-siâⁿ-kim(足成金); chhiah-kim(赤金); tsok-chhiah-kim(足赤金). *gilded*, tah-kim(搭金). *gold-plated*, liū-kim(鎦金). *inlaid or covered with*, sieⁿ-kim(鑲金); pau-kim(包金). *gold-lace*, kim-pĩⁿ(金辮). *gold-thread*, kim-sùaⁿ(金線). *goldfish*, kim-lí(金理). *gold-leaf*, kim-po̍h(金薄). *gold-dust*, kim-sua(金沙). *goldsmith*, phah-kim sai-pẽ(拍金司阜).

**gong**, lô(鑼); tâng-lô(銅鑼). *with a boss*, khong(空). *one*, che̍k-mīn-lô(一面鑼). *to beat*, phah-lô(拍鑼). *stick for beating*, lô-thûi(鑼槌).

**good**, hó(好); siẽn(善). *good heart*, hó-sim(好心); liâng-sim(良心); siu-sim(修心). *good-bye*, lṳ́ chhiáⁿ(汝請); chiãm-pie̍t(暫別). *living*, chia̍h-phâng-phài(食芳派); káⁿ-chia̍h káⁿ-sái(敢食敢使). *health*, sóng-khùai(爽快); tsàng-kiẽn(壯健); phêng-an(平安). *order*, siu-si̍p-hó(收拾好); iap-thiap(壓貼); tsôi-chiáⁿ(齊整); chhî-chéng(齊整). *composition*, pit-ba̍k hó(筆墨好); bûn-khì hó(文氣好); kiâⁿ-bûn hó(行文好); ēng-pit hó(用筆好); pit-chhêng hó(筆情好). *penmanship*, jī ngiá(字雅); jī tuan-khái(字端楷). *nature*, sèⁿ-chhêng hó(性情好); tsò-nâng khuaⁿ-chiâⁿ(做人寬成); un-jiû(溫柔). *name*, miâⁿ-sek hó(名色好); hó-miâⁿ-siaⁿ(好名聲); miâⁿ-siaⁿ phang(名聲芳). *conduct*, siẽn-hẽng(善行); jîn-tek(仁德). *luck*, tsãu-hùe(造化). *good and bad*, hó-khiap〔〕; hó-tái(好痞); siẽn-ak(善惡). *a good many*, hoh-tsōi(酷㩼). *a good while*, hoh-kú(酷久). *good for nothing*, bô-ēng(無用).

**goods**, hùe(貨); hùe-mue̍h(貨物). *foreign*, iêⁿ-hùe(洋貨). *first choice of*, hùe-mīn(貨面). *remnants of*, hùe-búe(貨尾); hùe-tái(貨歹). *sample of*, hùe-mōⁿ(貨望). *mixed*, tsa̍p-hùe(雜貨). *owner of*, hùe-tsú(貨主). *invoice of*, hùe-toaⁿ(貨單). *sell*, tshut-hùe(出貨). *unload*, khí-hùe(起貨). *load*, hẽ-hùe(下貨); lo̍h-hùe(落貨). *buy*, tì-hùe(置貨). *store*, tun-hùe(囤貨). *buy on credit*, chhia-hùe(車貨). *ready-money*, hīn-chîⁿ bói-hīn-hùe(現錢買現貨). *trans-ship into smaller vessel*, poh-hùe(駁貨). *send*, tah-hùe(搭貨); kià-hùe(寄貨). *pack up*, tsuang-hùe(裝貨). *not responsible for, after they have left the shop*, tshut-mn̂g bô-jīn-hùe(出門無認貨).

**grave**, phûn(墳); phûn-mõⁿ(墳墓); suaⁿ-phûn(山墳); huang-tsúi(風水); phûn-suaⁿ(墳山). *to dig a grave*, khui-khuàng(開礦). *to dig a grave (used more of opening the grave to remove the body)*, khui-phûn(開墳). *grave-stone*, phûn-pi(墳碑); pi-chie̍h(碑石); mõⁿ-pi(墓碑); chie̍h-pi(石碑). *worship at the*, chì-phûn(祭墳); chì-mõⁿ(祭墓); sàu-mõⁿ(掃墓); chì-sàu(祭掃). *grave-clothes*, sien-i(仙衣); sien-ho̍k(仙服). *grave-yard*, phûn-tī(墳地); phûn-suaⁿ(墳山); tsa̍p-tsǹg-tī(雜葬地). *free*, ngĩ-thóng(義冢).
