**have**, ũ(有). *have you* ũ a-bô(有亞無); khá chêng-ũ--méⁿ(豈曾有咩). *I have not*, bô(無); m̄-chêng-ũ(毋曾遇). *have finished*, tsò-hó--liáu(做好了); íⁿ-keng-tsò(已經做); tsò-liáu(做了). *have you ever eaten an orange*, kaⁿ lṳ́ pat-chia̍h a-m̄-pat(敢汝別食也毋別). *I have not*, m̄-pat(毋別); tsṳ̃-liáu m̄-pat(自了毋別). *have you had dinner*, lṳ́ chia̍h-pn̄g a-būe(汝食飯也未). *I have dined*, chia̍h-pá--liáu(食飽了); chia̍h--liáu(食了); phien--liáu(便了). *have you been to the market yet*, lṳ́ chêng chiẽⁿ-chhĩ--būe(汝曾上市未). *not yet*, būe-chêng(未曾).

**hay**, pha̍k-ta-tsháu(曝灱草). *haystack*, tsháu-khṳ̂n(草芹).

**hazard**, thèng-tsãu-hùe(聽造化); phòng-tsãu-hùe(碰造悔); kiâⁿ-hiám hiau-hẽng(驚險僥倖); hiau-hẽng(僥倖). *hazardous*, huang-hiám(風險); ngûi-hiám(危險); m̄-ún-tǹg(毋穩當); m̄-thó-tàng(毋妥當).

**hazy**, mông-bū(蒙霧); mông-in(濛煙); im-bū(陰霧); in-bū(煙霧); bū-bū(霧霧); hûn-bū(雲霧); huat-bū(發霧); huat-mông(發蒙).

**he**, i(伊); hṳ́-kâi-nâng(彼個人).

**head**, thâu(陶); thâu-khak(頭殼). *head off*, tuah-tńg(咄轉). *head-dress*, thâu-tshah(頭插); tsang(莊); tá-tsang(打棕). *wind*, nge̍k-huang(逆風); thêⁿ-thâu-huang(㨨頭風); tùi-thâu-huang(對頭風). *headache*, thâu-khak thiàⁿ(頭殼痛); thâu-khak kok-kok-kiè(頭殼國國叫). *band*, hâ-jiàu-se(縖繞些); hia̍h-ûi(額圍); hia̍h-tsôiⁿ-ûi(額前圍). *head man*, thâu-nâng(頭人[訓]); tso̍k-tiéⁿ(族長); pó-chiàⁿ(保正). *of a firm*, tsō-suaⁿ(座山); hâng-tsú(行主). *heady*, thèng-tàⁿ thèng-ûi(聽呾聽爲). *headlong*, tshou-kip(粗急). *headstrong*, chip-áu(執拗); kien-phiah(堅癖). *hang down the head*, thâu hẽ-hẽ(頭下下). *lift up*, thâu iâng-iâng(頭搖搖); thâu-khak tièⁿ-phû(頭殼脹浮). *cut off*, tsám-thâu(斬頭).

**heal**, ui(醫); ui-pēⁿ(醫病); tî-pēⁿ(治病); ui-tî(醫治). *entirely*, ui-tshuân-zú(醫痊愈). *as a wound*, tshng-kháu seⁿ-bûa(瘡口生磨); sieⁿ-kháu seⁿ-bûa(傷口生磨).

**health**, phêng-an(平安); bô-iãng(無恙); uaⁿ-jiên(安然); khin-sang(輕鬆); pìn-sin zû-zuán(遍身如暖). *injure*, sieⁿ-sún--tie̍h sin-hūn(傷損着身份). *healthy appearance*, chia̍h-khṳ̀ hó(食去好).

**heap**, *a*, tun(堆); che̍k-tun(一堆); che̍k-tu(一堆). *heap up*, tun-mue̍h(堆物); tun-chek(堆積); tha̍h--khí-lâi(疊起來).

**hear**, thiaⁿ(聽); thiaⁿ-kìⁿ(聽見). *I don't hear*, thiaⁿ-m̄-kìⁿ(聽毋見). *hard of hearing*, hĩⁿ lâng(耳聾). *hearsay*, hong-bũn(風聞); zṳ́-bũn(耳聞); thiaⁿ-kìⁿ nâng-tàⁿ(聽見人呾). *hear but pay no attention*, lāu tùi-hĩⁿ--kò kùe(漏對耳塊過).

**hearken**, *hearken secretly*, tá-thèng(打聽); thàm-thiaⁿ(探聽). *hearken secretly (as eaves-dropper)*, thau-thiaⁿ(偷聽).

**heart**, sim(心); sim-kuaⁿ(心肝); sim-thâu(心頭); sim-tn̂g(心腸); sim-tī(心地); sim-tshâng(心藏). *(disposition)*, sim-sèⁿ(心性). *(the affections and desires)*, sim-chhêng(心情). *having no heart for anything*, ià-ià ien-sîn ien-sîn〔〕. *heart-ache*, sim-kuaⁿ thiàⁿ(心肝痛). *beating*, sim-kuaⁿ pok-pok-thiàu(心肝卜卜跳); sim-kuaⁿ phû-phû-tshúan(心肝浮浮喘). *with the whole*, tsuan-sim(專心). *with one*, che̍k-sim(一心); tâng-sim(同心); tsôi-sim(齊心). *heartless*, bô-sim(無心); bô-nâng-chhêng(無人情). *heartburn*, ūi-kháu m̄-siau(胃口毋消). *to affect the heart*, tõng-sim(重心). *to keep one's heart from evil thoughts*, siu-khî hùang-sim(收其渙心).

**hearth**, tsàu(灶); húe-lôu(火爐). *cricket*, tsàu-koi(灶雞).

**heat**, húe-khì(火氣); jie̍t-khì(熱氣); zua̍h-khì(熱氣). *to heat over a flame*, nãⁿ(若); hang(烘). *water*, hiâⁿ-sie-tsúi(燒相水); un-sie-tsúi(溫燒水); pû-sie(煲燒). *food*, tim-sie(燂燒). *red-heat*, sie âng-âng(燒紅紅).

**heave**, *anchor*, khí-tèng(起碇); khie̍h-tèng(挈椗); po̍ih-tèng(拔椗); chhiû-tèng(揪碇). *a sigh*, tháu-khùi(㪗氣).

**heaven**, thiⁿ(天); thien(天). *in heaven*, tõ-thiⁿ-téng(在天頂). *all under heaven(used for China)*, thiⁿ-ẽ(天下). *justice of*, thien-lí(天堂). *heaven-daring*, táⁿ pau-thiⁿ(膽包天). *swear by*, chí-thiⁿ mêng-sī(指天明誓); tng-thiⁿ chiù-tsūa(當天咒誓).

**heavy**, tãng(重). *heavy load (on shoulder)*, tãng-tàⁿ(重擔). *heavy load (in boat)*, tãng-tsāi(重儎). *heavy heart(feeling of responsibility)*, sim-kuaⁿ-thâu teh-tōa-chie̍h(心肝頭壓大石). *heavy heart(sad)*, iu-ut(憂鬱). *heavy sleep*, gu̍t tsùi-tsùi(焗睡睡); u̍t chhim-chhim(夗深深). *heavy sleep(also used for death)*, tōa-gu̍t(大夗).

**hedge**, chhì-phè(刺帕); chhì-lî(刺籬); chhì-ûi(刺圍); hn̂g-lî(園籬); hn̂g-kài(園界). *(of cactus)*, hue-uãng-lî(花旺籬).

**heed**, *take*, kṳ́n-sín(謹慎); tsṳ́-sòi(仔細); sié-sim(小心). *any one*, thiaⁿ-nâng-tàⁿ(聽人呾). *heedless*, tshou-sim(粗心); bô-ēng-sim(無用心). *heedless (careless work)*, ló-tshó(潦草).

**heel**, kha-ãu-teⁿ(骹後蹬). *of shoes*, ôi-teⁿ(鞋蹬). *on woman's shoe*, kia̍h-thô(屐桃). *down at the heels*, ta̍h-tó-teⁿ(踏倒鼎). *take to one's heels*, tsáu(走).

**heifer**, gû-kiáⁿ(牛囝); gû-eⁿ(牛嬰).

**height**, *what is the*, ũ-jie̍h-kûiⁿ(有若懸); jie̍h-kûiⁿ(若懸).

**heir**, sṳ̂-tsṳ́(嗣子); ãu-sṳ̂(後嗣). *apparent*, thài-tsṳ́(太子). *heirless*, tso̍h-sṳ̂(絕嗣); bô-ãu(無後). *heritage*, zûi-ngia̍p(瑞業). *to fall heir to one's father's property*, sêng-chiap pẽ-ngia̍p(承接父業). *fall heir to the throne*, kì-chiap sṳ̂-ūi(繼接嗣位); téng-sêng uâng-ūi(頂承王位); teng-ki(登基); chiet-ūi(即位).

**hell**, tī-ge̍k(地獄). *to go to*, tîm-lûn tī-ge̍k(沉輪地獄); lo̍h-tī-ge̍k(落地獄).

**helm**, tõa(舵); búe-tõa(尾舵). *take the*, lia̍h-tõa(掠舵); hūaⁿ-tõa(捍舵). *unship, in shallow water*, pài-tõa(拜舵). *raise higher*, chhèng-tõa(秤舵). *shaft of*, tõa-thâu(舵頭). *blade*, tõa-siám(舵閃). *put up the*, tháu(㪗). *put down the*, khan(牽). *helmsman*, tãi-kong(舵工). *tiller*, tõa-gê(舵牙). *tiller-ropes*, tõa-lêng(舵另).

**helmet**, thâu-khue(頭盔); thih-mâuⁿ(鐵帽).

**help**, pang-tsõ(幫助); sie-hũ(相輔); hũ-tsõ(輔助); pang-chhiú(幫手); tô-lông(多郎); siang-pang(相幫); pang-tsān(幫贊). *help up*, hû--i khí--lâi(扶伊起來); khan-hû(牽扶); khan-thî(牽提); khan-kũaⁿ(牽摜). *help to get office*, thî-pua̍t(提拔). *help in difficulties or dangers*, kiù-chì(救濟); chín-kiù(拯救); chín-chì(賑濟); si-chì(施濟). *help! help!*, kiù--a! kiù--a(救啊救啊); kiù-miāⁿ! kiù-miāⁿ(救命救命). *to call for*, hàm-kiè-kiù(喊叫救). *no help for it*, bô-pōu(無步). *no help but to*, bô-nãiⁿ-hô(無奈何); bô-khó nãiⁿ-hô(無可奈何); put-tit-íⁿ(不得已); bô-ta-uâ(無奈何); bô-ta i-ûa(無奈於何). *help a man to prosper*, chhiâⁿ-nâng-hó(情人好). *helpless*, bô-kiù(無救); chĩn-thâu-lêng(盡頭能).

**helter skelter**, sì-sùaⁿ(四散); lũan-tsáu(亂走); sùaⁿ-tsáu(線走); phî-phê-kiè tsáu(疲脾叫走).

**helve**, póu-thâu-pèⁿ(斧頭柄); póu-pèⁿ(斧柄).

**hem**, *to*, chih-tsūe(摺襊); chih-pòu-piⁿ(折布邊). *to (all before sewing)*, chih-pòu-tsūe(折布碎). *(to stitch very loosely)*, nn̂g-saⁿ-tsūe(䌜衫襊). *(sew finely)*, thīⁿ-saⁿ-tsūe(縫衫襊). *the (of a garment)*, saⁿ-kṳ(衫裾).

**hem**, *clear the throat*, khãm-sàu(鈸掃).

**hemp**, mûaⁿ(鰻); iû-mûaⁿ(油鰻). *seed*, mûaⁿ-chí(鰻子); mûaⁿ-jîn(鰻仁). *hemp-seed oil*, mûaⁿ-iû(鰻油); phang-iû(蜂油).

**hen**, koi-bó(街母). *young*, koi-nùaⁿ(雞卵); koi-nùaⁿ-kiáⁿ(雞卵囝). *hen-house*, koi-liâu(街寮); koi-lâng(街人). *hen-roost*, koi-tiâu(雞條); koi-chhi(街棲). *henpecked*, koi-bó-thî(街母提); koi-bó phah-si̍t-thî(雞母拍翼啼).

**hence**, *gone*, bô-tõ(無在); khṳ̀--liáu(去了). *therefore*, kù-tshṳ́(故此); só-íⁿ(所以); sǹg-lâi(算來); in-tshṳ́(因此). *henceforth*, tshông-kim íⁿ-ãu(從今以後); tsṳ̃-kim íⁿ-ãu(自今以後); tshóng-tshṳ́ íⁿ-ãu(從此以後).

**herald**, sài(使); pò-sìn(報信); pò-sie-sit(報消息).

**herd**, khûn(群). *a whole*, chiâⁿ-khûn(成群). *to*, chiéⁿ-cheng-seⁿ(掌鐘牲).

**here**, tõ-chí-kò(在此塊); tõ-chí(在此); chièⁿ-thâu(此樣頭); chí-kâi ūi-tshṳ̀(此個位處); chí-kâi tī-hng(此個地方). *up here*, tõ-chí-téng(在此頂). *down here*, tõ-chí-ẽ(在此下). *hereabouts*, tõ-chí tsôiⁿ-ãu(在此前後); kṳ̃n tõ-chí-kò(近在此塊). *come here*, lâi(來); kiâⁿ-bûa--lâi(行埋來). *hereafter*, tshṳ́-ãu(此後); ãu-lâi(後來); chiang-lâi(將來); ãu-ji̍t(後日); ẽ-ji̍t(下日); ẽ-hûe(下回); tsong-su(綜須).

**hereditary**, *property*, zũi-ngia̍p(遺業); zũi-súaⁿ(遺產). *disease*, zũi-pēⁿ(遺病). *office*, sì-si̍p(世襲); si̍p-ìm(襲蔭).

**heritage**, zũi-ngia̍p(遺業); tsóu-zũi(祖遺); tsóu-thûan kâi-ngia̍p(祖傳个業). *paternal*, pẽ-zũi(父遺).

**hermit**, tãu-sṳ̃(道士). *of literary or official person, living in seclusion*, ṳ́n-kṳ(隱居). *hermitage*, tsháu-liâu(草寮).

**hernia**, thut-kṳn-thâu(脫筋頭); siáu-chhiâng-khì(小腸氣).

**hero**, hâu(豪); kie̍t(傑); eng-hiông(英雄). *heroine (military)*, nńg-chiàng(女將).

**hew**, khám(砍); lòi-khui(𠠍開); phoh(劈).

**hiccup**, phah-oh-kiáⁿ(拍呃囝); thiu-oh-kiáⁿ(抽呃囝); khou-oh-kiáⁿ(呼呃囝).

**hide**, tshâng(藏); khǹg(囥); tshâng-khǹg(藏囥); tshâng-miⁿ(藏眠); khǹg-miⁿ(囥眠); khǹg-bûa(囥埋); siu-tshâng(收藏); ṳ́n-tshâng(隱藏); khǹg-ba̍t(囥密); tshâng-ne̍k(藏匿); ṳ́n-ne̍k(隱匿). *hide oneself*, pì-ba̍t(祕密); pì-bûa(祕埋); ṳ́n-pì(隱庇); tiàm-bûa(坫埋); iám-siám(掩閃); siám-bûa(閃埋); siám-miⁿ(閃眠). *(make oneself invisible by magic)*, siám-sin(閃身). *hide one's faults*, chia-iám(遮掩); iám-kài(掩蓋); iám-sek(掩飾); khàm-bûa(蓋埋). *hide and seek*, aⁿ-ma̍k tsáu-tiàm(掩目走坫).

**hide**, *a*, phûe-sek(皮色); chheⁿ-phûe(青皮); gû-phûe(牛皮). *to dress a*, se̍k-phûe(熟皮).

**hideous**, iá-iēⁿ(野樣); khó-ùi(可畏); chhi-gî(淒疑); lõu-ak(陋惡); chhiú-ak(醜惡); chhiú-lõu(醜陋); ke̍k-lõu(極陋).

**higgle**, sṳ-niêⁿ khah-thiám(私量較諂); ngi-ngai(疑礙).

**high**, kûiⁿ(懸); kau(高). *high antiquity*, siãng-kóu(上古). *high hill*, kûiⁿ-suaⁿ(懸山); kau-suaⁿ(高山). *high station*, kau-ūi(高位); kau-kuaⁿ(高官). *high price*, kùi(貴); kau-kè(高價); kè-chîⁿ tsōi(價錢㩼). *high wind*, huang méⁿ(風猛); huang tōa(風大). *high water*, lâu-tsúi tĩⁿ(流水漲); tsúi tōa(水大); tiê tōa(潮大). *on high*, tõ-chiēⁿ(在上); tõ-téng(在頂). *the highest*, chì-siãng(至上); tõ-téng-téng(在頂頂); siãng-téng(上頂). *prize highly*, kùi-tõng(貴重); kèng-tõng(敬重); thóiⁿ-tõng(睇重). *high-spirited*, hâu-khì(豪氣). *in the highest degree*, siãng(上); chì(至); tsa̍p-hun(十分); kàu-ke̍k(到極); kàu-ke̍k--tshù(到極處).

**hill**, suaⁿ(汕). *pass*, suaⁿ-niáⁿ(山嶺). *to cross hills*, pûaⁿ-suaⁿ kùeⁿ-niáⁿ(半山過嶺). *hillock*, suaⁿ-tu-léng(山坫嶺). *hillock (gentle slope)*, suaⁿ-pou(山坡). *hilly road*, khi-khu(崎嶇).

**hiss**, si--chē-kiè(嘶坐叫); si-si-kiè(師師叫).

**historiographer**, sṳ́-kuaⁿ(史官).

**history**, kok-sṳ́(國史); sṳ́-kì(史記); sṳ́-tsṳ(史書); sṳ́-kuán(史館); kàm-sṳ́(鑑史). *of a person*, lâi-le̍h(來歷); lí-le̍h(旅歷); tshut-si̍t(出實). *historical and statistical account, e.g. of Ch'ao-chow*, Tiê-chiu-chì(潮州志).

**hive**, phang-siū(蜂岫); phang-tàu(蜂竇); phang-tû(蜂櫥).

**hoarse**, bô-siaⁿ(無聲); âu-lêng bô-siaⁿ(喉嚨無聲); sau-siaⁿ(騷聲); siaⁿ m̄-liãng(聲毋亮).

**hoary**, *head*, thâu-môⁿ soh-soh-pe̍h(頭毛雪雪白).

**hobble**, kiâⁿ-lōu chhĩm-a-chhĩm〔〕; kũai-a-kũai(拐亞拐).

**hobgoblin**, kúi(鬼); kúi-kùai(鬼怪); iau-chiaⁿ(妖精); siàⁿ-nâng-mue̍h(聖人物).

**hod**, pùn-ki(糞箕).

**hoe**, tṳ̂-thâu(鋤頭).

**hog**, tṳ(豬). *hog-sty*, tṳ-lô(豬牢). *hoggish*, o-tso(污糟); ue-tsue(穢粗); tṳ-iēⁿ káu-sièⁿ(豬樣狗像).

**hoist**, po̍ih-khí(拔起); liū(鎦). *flag*, liū-kî(㨨旗); tshah-kî(插旗). *sail*, po̍ih-phâng(拔帆); seng-phâng(升帆); liū-phâng(㨨帆); khí-phâng(起帆).

**hold**, *anything in the hand*, chhiú-khie̍h(手挈). *from going away*, lia̍h(掠). *pencil*, khiâ-pit(擎筆). *reins*, khan-bé-soh(牽馬索). *hold up (a person)*, khan(牽); hû-khí(扶起). *hold up clothes*, tsah-phû〔〕; kiáu-phû(攪浮); put-phû(不浮). *in the mouth (as dog)*, kâⁿ(銜). *in the mouth (as man)*, kam(監). *one's tongue*, tiām-tiām(恬恬); màiⁿ-tàⁿ-ūe(勿呾話). *under the arm*, ko̍ih tõ-koh-ẽ(夾在閣下). *contain*, tshō(貯). *one catty*, tshō-che̍k-kṳn(貯一根). *will not hold it*, tshō-m̄-tit(找毋得); tshō-m̄-khṳ̀(找毋去); tshō-m̄-lâi(找毋來). *this room will hold 100 people*, chí-che̍k-koiⁿ-pâng hó-tshâng che̍k-peh-nâng(只一間房好藏一百人); chí-che̍k-koiⁿ-pâng hó-iông che̍k-peh-nâng(只一間房好容一百人); chí-che̍k-koiⁿ-pâng hó-tsõ che̍k-peh-nâng(只一間房好坐一百人); chí-che̍k-koiⁿ-pâng hó-khiã che̍k-peh-nâng(只一間房好徛一百人). *of ship*, tsûn-tshng(船倉).

**hole**, khang(空). *to make a hole*, khui-khang(開空). *knock out*, phah-khang(拍空); tshuan-khan(穿牽). *dig a hole*, liú-khang(㧕空). *to chisel a hole*, tsha̍k-khang(鑿空). *bore*, uai-khang(歪空); ui-khang(醫空). *bore (with gimlet, &c)*, tsǹg-khang(鑽空). *full of holes*, tshang-tshang(蔥蔥).

**hollow**, khang(空); khang-khak(空殼) *(oppos. tsa̍t-thâu)*; khang-phàⁿ(空冇) *(opp. tsa̍t-tōiⁿ)*; *to hollow out*, liú-khang(㧕空); ui-khang-khak〔〕. *of the hand*, chhiú-sim-tói(手心底).

**Holland**, Hô-lân-kok(荷蘭國).

**holy**, siàⁿ(聖). *Spirit*, Siàⁿ-Sîn(聖神). *holiness of life*, siẽn-hẽng(善行); ngân-hẽng chheng-kiet(顏行清潔).

**holiday**, *thih-thô-ji̍t; ôiⁿ-ji̍t; iû-ôiⁿ-ji̍t*, ôiⁿ-kang-ji̍t(閒工日); chheng-ôiⁿ-ji̍t(清閒日); uaⁿ-ôiⁿ-ji̍t(安閒日).

**homage**, kiong-kèng(恭敬). *to the emperor*, chhiâu-pài(朝拜). *by tributary princes (includes tribute)*, chhiâu-kòng(朝貢).

**home**, ke(家); tshù(厝). *at home*, tõ-tshù(在厝); tõ-lãi(在內); tõ-ke-lãi(在家內); tõ(在); tõ--kò(在塊). *go home*, hûe-ke(回家); khṳ̀-tshù(去厝); tńg-khṳ̀-tshù(轉去厝); kui-ke(歸家); tńg-tshù(轉厝). *go home (if merely going inside)*, khṳ̀-lãi(去內). *home made*, pńg-tī-tsò(本地做).

**homicide**, suah-nâng(殺人); thâi-nâng(刣人). *a*, hiong-chhiú(兇手).

**hone**, bûa-to-chie̍h(磨刀石).

**honest**, *tong-kãu; láu-si̍t; tong-hõu; phok-si̍t; tong-ti̍t*, sêng-si̍t(誠實); pe̍h-ti̍t(正經); chiàⁿ-ti̍t(正直); chiàⁿ-keng(正經); kong-tãu(公道).

**honey**, phang-bi̍t(芳蜜); bi̍t(蜜). *honey-comb*, bi̍t-phoh(蜜粕); bi̍t-tsa(蜜渣); bi̍t-phièn(蜜騙).

**hong**, hâng(行); hâng-kháu(行口). *merchant*, iêⁿ-siang(洋行).

**Hongkong**, Hiang-káng(香港); kûn-tōa-lōu(裙大路).

**honour**, tsun-kùi(尊貴); thí-mīn(體面); iông-hûa(榮華). *to*, kèng(敬); tsun-kèng(尊敬); kèng-tõng(敬重); kiong-kèng(恭敬). *to obey is better than to honour*, kiong-kèng put-zû tshông-mẽng(恭敬不如從命). *honour father and mother*, hàu-sũn pẽ-bó(孝順父母); kiâⁿ-hàu pẽ-bó(行孝父母). *honoured sir*, tsun-kè(尊駕).

**honorary**, khang-hâm(空銜).

**hood**, soh-bō(雪帽).

**hoof**, tôi(蹄).

**hook**, kau(鉤). *fish-hook*, hṳ̂-kau(魚鉤); tièⁿ-kau(釣鉤). *hooked nose*, phīⁿ kau-kau(鼻鉤鉤).

**hoop**, khou(箍); tháng-khou(桶箍).

**hoot**, tuah-nâng(喝人); tuah-siaⁿ(咄聲).

**hop**, *to*, thiàu(跳).

**hope**, hi-mōⁿ(希望); mōⁿ(望); ngiáng-mōⁿ(仰望). *hopeful*, ũ-mōⁿ(有望). *hopeful (promising)*, hó-mōⁿ(好望). *hopeless*, bô-mōⁿ(無望); tso̍h-mōⁿ(絕望); mín-mōⁿ(免望). *having too high hopes*, chhia-mōⁿ(賒望).

**horary**, *characters*, *twelve*, tsa̍p-jī sî-sîn.

**horde**, che̍k-khûn-nâng(一群人); khûn-táng(群黨).

**horizon**, thiⁿ-kha(天骹). *horizontal*, hûeⁿ(橫); pêⁿ(平).

**horn**, kak(覺). *cow's horn*, gû-kak(牛角); *deer's horn*, te̍k-kak(鹿穀). *(young, used for medicine)*, te̍k-zông(鹿茸). *shoe-horn*, ôi-chhiau(鞋鍬).

**hornet**, n̂g-phang(黃蜂).

**horoscope**, sì-thiãu(勢柱); poih-jī(八二). *to look up one's*, lũn-poih-jī(論八字); thóiⁿ-sì-thiãu(看勢柱).

**horrible**, khó-ùi(可畏); khó-kiaⁿ(可驚); tshūa-nâng-kiaⁿ(𤆬人[訓]驚); kiaⁿ-ĩ(驚驚); hãi-ĩ(駭異).

**horror**, kiaⁿ-kũ kâi-hêng-mãuⁿ(驚死个形貌); kiaⁿ-kũ kâi-iēⁿ-sièⁿ(驚懼个樣像); kiaⁿ-khiū(驚硬). see HORRIBLE.

**horse**, bé(馬). *one*, che̍k-chiah-bé(一隻馬). *horse-shoe*, bé-tôi-thih(馬蹄鐵). *horse-hair*, bé-búe(馬尾). *horse-dealer*, bé-hùan(馬換). *horseman*, khiâ-bé(騎馬). *ride on horseback*, khiâ-bé(騎馬). *horse-comb*, bé-siu(馬梳); bé-pìn(馬箆). *horse-cloth*, bé-phũe(馬被).

**hospitable**, kãu-thãi nâng-kheh(厚待人[訓]客).

**hospital**, ui-kúan(醫館).

**host**, tshù-nâng(厝人); tsú-jîn(主仁).

**hostage**, *to give or take a*, ēng-nâng tsò-tǹg(用人做當).

**hostility**, uan-ke(寃家); m̄-hûa(毋和); chhiû-khiah(仇隙); hièn-khiah(憲隙). *cause of*, hũa-kṳn(禍根); hũa-in(禍因).

**hostler**, bé-hu(馬夫). *(very slighting)*, bé-tsháu-nôuⁿ(馬草奴).

**hot**, zua̍h(熱); sie(燒). *hot weather*, thiⁿ-sî zua̍h(天時熱); pek-zua̍h(迫熱); zua̍h-ta̍k(熱毒). *hot sun*, ji̍t-thâu jie̍t(日頭熱); ji̍t-thâu méⁿ(日頭猛); ji̍t-thâu âng(日頭紅); ji̍t-thâu ham-ham-âng(日頭蚶蚶紅). *hot water*, sie-tsúi(燒水). *hot water (boiling)*, kún-tsúi(滾水). *hot-headed*, ũ-sèⁿ(有性); phòng-phiẽ sim-sèⁿ(碰鰾心性); sim-sèⁿ kín-kip(心性緊急). *spell of hot weather in cold season*, khieh-sie̍h(客熱).

**hotel**, kau-lâu-kúan(高樓館); tiàm-phòu(店舖).

**hour**, *Chinese hour*, sî-sîn(時辰). *foreign hour*, che̍k-tiám-cheng(一點鐘). *half an hour*, pùaⁿ-tiám-cheng(半點鐘). *quarter*, che̍k-khek-cheng(一刻鐘). *hourglass*, tâng-hû tih-lāu(銅壺滴漏). *hourly*, múeⁿ-tiám-cheng(每點鐘); sî-sî khek-khek(時時刻刻).

**house**, tshù(厝). *a*, che̍k-koiⁿ-tshù(一間厝); che̍k-tsō-tshù(一座厝). *school-house*, tsṳ-che(書齋). *dwelling-house*, nâng-ke(人家). *your (polite)*, kùi-hú(貴府). *my (polite)*, tsháu-sià(草舍). *house-breaker*, mêng-húe phah-kiap(明火打劫); tōng-mn̂g-tsha̍t(蕩門賊); siàng-mn̂g-tsha̍t(相門賊). *house-manager*, tng-ke(當家); hūaⁿ-ke(捍家). *house-maid*, chhiah-kha(赤骹). *house-rent*, tshù-tsou(厝租); tshù-sùe(厝稅); kúan-tsou(管租). *household*, ke-so̍k(家屬). *household goods*, ke-tsṳ(家資); ke-si mue̍h-kiãⁿ(家私物件). *household servants*, ke-jîn(家人).

**hovel**, tsháu-tshù(草厝); tsháu-liâu(草寮).

**hover**, īn(暈). *(bird, ready to dart)*, khip-sin(吸身).

**how**, tsãi-seⁿ(豸生); tsò-nîⁿ(怎呢); zû-hô(如何). *how dare*, tsò-káⁿ(怎敢). *how many*, jie̍h-tsōi(若㩼); kúi-kâi(幾個); jia̍k-kan(若干); ki-to(幾多).  *how far*, jie̍h-hñg(若遠). *how many times*, jie̍h-tsōi-ē(若㩼下); kúi-hûe(幾回); kúi-pái(幾擺); kúi-tńg(幾轉); kúi-hãng(幾項); jie̍h-tsōi-tshṳ̀(若㩼次). *how large*, jie̍h-tōa(若大). *how old*, jie̍h-tsōi-hùe(若㩼歲); tshun-chhiu jie̍h-tsōi(春秋若㩼); jie̍h-tōa(若大); jie̍h-lãu(若老); kùi-keⁿ(貴庚). *how to do*, tsò-nîⁿ-mue̍h(怎呢物). *not know how to do it*, tsò m̄-pat tò-khṳ̀(做毋識倒去). *how shall I do*, zû-hô sĩ-hó(如何是好); tsò-nîⁿ chiàⁿ-hó(怎呢正好). *how is this*, sṳ̄-sĩ-tsò-nîⁿ(事是怎呢). *how did it happen*, tsò-õi(怎會). *how did it happen (also expressing incredulity)*, tsò-ũ(怎有). *how can it be otherwise*, tsò-m̄-sĩ(做毋是). *how can that be accounted filial piety*, chièⁿ seⁿ iau-hó kiè-tsò hàu(此樣生要好叫做孝). *how can this be right*, khí-ũ tshṳ́-lí(豈有此理). *how can we get it*, tsãi-tit-tie̍h(在得着). *how much more*, hô-khùang(何況). *how fast*, méⁿ-tsãi(猛在).

**however**, hûang-liáu(還了); hûan-iáu(還要).

**howl**, háuⁿ-háuⁿ-kiè(吠吠叫); háuⁿ-chē-kiè(吠齊叫).

**hubbub**, thèng-jiáng(亂嚷).

**huckster**, koiⁿ-thiau kâi-seng-lí(肩挑個生理); lōu-tàⁿ seng-lí(路擔生理); tsò seng-lí-kiáⁿ(做生理囝).

**huddled up**, sie-chìⁿ sie-ko̍ih(相擠相夾).

**hue**, sek(色). *five hues*, ngóu-sek(五色); ngóu-tshái(五彩).

**hug**, sie-phõ(相抱); sie-lám(相攬).

**huge**, tōa(舵); tōa-tsãi(大在); tōa kàu-koh-iēⁿ(大到阁樣); tōa kàu-khî(大到奇).

**hulk**, *or hull*, tsûn-khak(船殼); tsûn-sin(船身); tsûn-tháng(船桶).

**hull**, *rice*, cheng-bí(精米); lak-bí(碌米).

**hum**, *of insects*, ng-ng-kiè(哼哼叫); hng-hng-kiè(哼哼叫); hiⁿ-hng-kiè(哼哼叫).

**human**, *life*, nâng-seⁿ(人[訓]生); nâng-miāⁿ(人[訓]命). *human life is like a dream*, nâng-seⁿ jia̍k-māng(人[訓]生若夢); phû-seⁿ jia̍k-māng(浮生若夢). *relations*, jîn-lûn(人倫). *strength*, nâng-la̍t(人[訓]力). *affairs*, jîn-sṳ̄(人事). *feelings*, nâng-chhêng(人[訓]情). *kind*, nâng-lūi(人[訓]類). *the human heart is never satisfied*, nâng-sim put-tsok(人[訓]心不足).

**humane**, ũ-nâng-chhêng(有人情); õi-tsò-nâng(會做人); tshṳ̂-sim(慈心); ũ-jîn-ài(有仁愛).

**humanity**, jîn-tek(仁德); jîn-ài(仁愛).

**humble**, khiam-sùn(謙遜); khiam-sòi(謙細); tsṳ̃-khiam(自謙); tsṳ̃-pui(自卑); tho-khiam(推謙); khiam-jiãng(謙讓); khiam-tek(謙德); khiam-sim(謙心); hṳ-sim(虛心); hṳ-khiam(虛謙); khiam-hiã(謙下); khiam-pui(謙卑). *my humble opinion*, ngô-kièn(愚見); phí-kièn(鄙見).

**humbug**, la-kè〔〕; phièn-nâng(騙人); kuang-nâng(誆人).

**humid**, tâm(㴷); tâm-sip(㴷濕); sip-khì(濕氣). *humming-bird*, kim-sai-chiáu(金絲鳥).

**humour**, sèⁿ-chhêng(性情). *ill-humour*, phiah-pēⁿ(癖病); àu-àu(漚漚); ou-àu ou-àu(烏漚烏漚); pũ-pũ àu-àu(哺哺漚漚); pũ-àu pũ-àu(哺漚哺漚). *out of humour*, sim-sèⁿ pãu-pek(心性暴迫). *accommodate oneself to the humour of others*, lia̍h--tie̍h nâng kâi-phiah-pēⁿ(掠着人[訓]个癖病). *humorous*, hàuⁿ-tshu(好趨); hàuⁿ-peh-ge̍h(好伯月); hàuⁿ-chhiè-thâm(好笑談).

**humpbacked**, ku-ie(佝腰); ie hau-hau〔〕; hau-ie〔〕. *(more slight)*, ie hâu-hâu〔〕.

**hundred**, che̍k-peh(一百).

**hunger**, tóu khùn(肚困); tóu iau(肚枵). *I am hungry*, uá tóu õi-khùn(倚肚會困). *die of*, gō-sí(餓死). *endure*, nãiⁿ-gō(耐餓).

**hunt**, phah-la̍h(拍獵). *the wild boar*, phah-suaⁿ-tṳ(拍山豬).

**hurdle**, keh(隔); tiãm(簟); ôu(湖). *(bamboo fence)*, tek-lî(竹籬).

**hurl**, *a spear*, pie-chhieⁿ(鏢槍); tong-chhieⁿ(中槍). *stones*, ka̍k-chie̍h(捔石). *hurricane*, huang-thai(風颱). *(spring gale)*, pò-thâu(報頭).

**hurry**, *to*, piàⁿ-méⁿ(拚猛). *hurry up*, méⁿ--chē(猛些); piàⁿ-méⁿ--chē(拚猛些). *in a desperate*, huang-mâng(慌忙); tsò-sṳ̄ hih-huh-kiè(做事吸呼叫); mâng-kip(忙急); mâng-pek(忙迫). *do hurriedly*, tshó-lia̍k-tsò(草略做); chhìn-tshái-tsò(凊彩做). *don't be in such a*, tshāi--chē(在在); tshāi-tshāi--nē(在在呢); ûn-ûn--nē(勻勻呢).

**hurt**, sieⁿ(傷); sieⁿ-hāi(傷害). *are you hurt*, õi-sieⁿ-tie̍h, mé(會傷着咩); õi-pua̍h--tie̍h tî-kò, mé〔〕(會跋着底塊咩)〔〕. *one's feelings*, sieⁿ-chhêng(傷情); sieⁿ-chhêng sit-ngĩ(傷情失義). *hurtful*, lĩ-hāi(厲害).

**husband**, ang(翁); jî-sài(兒婿); jî-hu(兒夫); hu-sài(夫婿); hu-kun(夫君); chiãng-hu(丈夫); tōa--nâng(大人[訓]).

**husbandman**, tsoh-tshân-nâng(作田人); tshân-hu(田夫); lông-hu(農夫); tsoh-tshân-ko(作田哥). *husbandry*, lông-sṳ̄(農事); tsoh-tshân(作田); keⁿ-tsoh(耕作); chèng-tsoh(種作).

**hush**, *up*, sai-khia-hûa(私奇和); sai-ẽ-hûa(私下和); sai-hûa(私和); hún-sek(粉飾); chia-bûa(遮埋); chia-iám(遮掩); chia-sek(遮飾).

**husk**, khak(殼). *(chaff)*, tshou-khng(粗糠). *to husk rice*, oi-lâng(挨籠); oi-chhek(挨粟).

**hustle**, sie-oi sie-léng(相挨相攆); sie-chìⁿ sie-léng(相擠相攆).

**hut**, tsháu-liâu(草寮); suaⁿ-liâu(山寮).

**hymn**, sîn-si(神詩).

**hyperbole**, tàⁿ-kùe-ke(呾過家); kùe-tsōi(過㩼); tàⁿ khah-thài-kùe(呾較太過); tàⁿ khah-kùe-sĩm(呾較過甚).

**hypocrite**, ké-hó(假好); ngũi-siẽn(僞善); ngũi-kun-tsṳ́(僞君子); kháu sĩ(口是); sim hui(心非).

**hypothesis**, pí-huang kâi-ūe(比方个話); kiá-zû kâi-ūe(假如同个話).

### I

**I**, uá(我). see WE.

**ice**, piaⁿ-sng(冰霜). *box*, piaⁿ-sng-sieⁿ(冰霜箱).

**ichthyosis**, tshou-phûe(粗皮); lêng-lân-tshou(龍鱗粗).

**idea**, ì(意); ì-sṳ̀(意思); ì-kièn(意見); siẽⁿ-thâu(想頭); liãm-thâu(念頭).

**identical**, sie-tâng(相同); che̍k-iēⁿ(一樣); bô-koh-iēⁿ(無閣樣).

**idiom**, kù-huap(句法); gṳ́-kù(語句). *classical*, tsṳ-kù(之句); tién-kù(典故).

**idiot**, ngô-tshún(愚蠢); hiã-ngô(螻愚); chhi-ngâi(痴呆); m̄-hiáu jîn-sṳ̄(毋曉人事).

**idle**, *lazy*, tõaⁿ(惰); lán-tõaⁿ(懶惰); m̄-hàuⁿ tsò-kang(毋好做工). *person*, ôiⁿ-nâng(閒人[訓]); iû-chhiú hàuⁿ-ôi(遊手好閒); hàuⁿ-i̍t(好逸). *stories*, ôiⁿ-ūe(閒話). *place where idlers meet*, ôiⁿ-koiⁿ(閒間).

**idol**, ngóu-sièⁿ(偶像); phû-sat(菩薩); lãu-iâ(老爺); tshâ-sîn(柴神). *idolatry*, pài-tshâ-sîn(拜柴神); pài-ngóu-sièⁿ(拜偶像).

**if**, jia̍k(若); zû-jia̍k(如同); tháng-jia̍k(當若); kiá-sái(假使); kiá-lẽng(假令); kóu-sek(苟式); phah-tsò(拍做); kiá-zû(假如); zû-ho̍k(如同); khó-pí(可比); phì-zû(譬如); pí-huang(比方). *if you are going*, lṳ́ jia̍k-sĩ àiⁿ-khṳ̀(汝若是欲去). *but if you won't go*, nãⁿ-sĩ lṳ́ m̃-khṳ̀(若是汝毋去). *if not*, zû-m̄-sĩ(如毋是); iā-sĩ-bô(也是無). *as if(comparison)*, phì-zû(譬如); pí-zû(比如); hāi--kùe(害過); tǹg--kùe(當過); chhin-chhiẽⁿ(親像); khó-pí(可比). *even if*, tsòng(縱); tsòng-jiên(縱然); tsòng-sái(縱使).

**ignis fatuus**, kúi-húe(鬼火).

**ignite**, to̍h-húe(着火); huat-húe(發火).

**ignoble**, hiã-tsūaⁿ(下賤); hiã-tsoh(下作); hiã-pín(下品).

**ignorant**, bô-tsai(無曉); bô-kièn-sek(無見識); m̄-hiáu(毋曉); m̄-pat(毋識).

**ill**, ũ-pēⁿ(有病); m̄-sóng-khùai(毋爽快); bô-hièⁿ-hó(無向好); m̄-phêng-an(毋平安); bô-khang-kiẽn(無康健); nâng m̄-hó(人[訓]毋好).

**ill-natured**, sèⁿ-chhêng m̄-hó(性情毋好); phî-khì m̄-hó(脾氣毋好); ũ-phiah-pēⁿ(有癖病).

**ill-favoured**, mīn-mãuⁿ tshou(面貌醜); iá-iēⁿ(野樣); thóiⁿ m̄-ji̍p-ma̍k(睇毋入目); tshou-lõu(粗陋).

**ill-shaped**, iá-iēⁿ(野樣); m̄-chiâⁿ-iēⁿ(毋成樣).

**ill-treat**, m̄-kãu-thãi-nâng(毋厚待人[訓]); khek-po̍h(刻薄). *ill-treated*, siũ-khui(受虧); siũ-khì(受氣).

**illegal**, hũam-huap(犯法); m̄-ha̍h-huap(毋合法律); m̄-ha̍h-lī(毋合理); lu̍t-huap m̄-tsún--kâi(法律毋準个).

**illegible**, jī m̄-hīn(字毋現); thóiⁿ-m̄-tshut(睇毋出); thóiⁿ-m̄-hīn(睇毋現).

**illegitimate**, *child*, thau-seⁿ kâi-kiáⁿ(偷生个囝).

**illiberal**, tōu-liãng o̍ih-sòi(度量狹細); tōu-liãng o̍ih-soih(度量狹細). *(niggardly)*, kien-liẽn(慳吝). *(greedy)*, khieh-si̍p(挈拾).

**illicit**, *intercourse*, sai-thong(私通); kóu-ha̍h(苟合); thong-kan(通姦).

**illimitable**, bô-hãn-liãng(無限量); bõi-tit-liáu(袂得了).

**illiterate**, m̄-pat-jī(毋識字); bô-tha̍k-tsṳ(無讀書); bô-ha̍k-mn̄g(無學問); m̄-chêng ta̍h-ji̍p Khóng-tsṳ́-mn̂g(毋曾踏入孔子門); tóu-lãi bô-pùaⁿ-tiám ba̍k-tsúi(肚內無半點墨水); tin-tò-thâu chèng bô-pùaⁿ-tiám ba̍k-tsúi(顛倒頭正無半點墨水).

**ill-fated**, khóu-miāⁿ(苦命); miāⁿ kuai(命乖); po̍h-miāⁿ(薄命); miāⁿ khiap(命㾀); miāⁿ phí(命鄙).

**illness**, pēⁿ(病); pēⁿ-chèng(病症). *symptoms of*, pēⁿ-chhêng(病情); pēⁿ-tsuãng(病狀).

**illuminate**, tiàu-teng(吊燈); iâⁿ-teng(迎燈); tãi-nãuⁿ húe-teng(大腦火丁).

**illumine**, chiè(照); chiè-kng(照光); chiè-mêng(照明).

**illusion**, ka-kī phièn-ka-kī(家己騙家己); tsṳ̃-mûaⁿ(自瞞); tsṳ̃-khi(自欺).

**illustrate**, kói-mêng(解明); tù-mêng(著明); huat-mêng(發明).

**illustrious**, hién-miâⁿ(顯名); tshut-miâⁿ(出名); tù-miâⁿ(著名); hién-iông(顯榮).

**image**, sièⁿ(像). *to cast*, tsù-sièⁿ(鑄像). *to draw*, ūe-sièⁿ(畫像). *to carve*, khek-sièⁿ(刻像).

**imagine**, siẽⁿ(想). *I imagine it is*, iak-móⁿ-liãng(約孬量); thóu-siẽⁿ(土想). *imaginable*, siẽⁿ-tit-tshut(想得出); sǹg-tit-tshut(算得出). *it is all imagination*, phû-huang tshok-iáⁿ(浮風捉影); bô-iáⁿ-chiah(無影跡). *I imagined he would not come*, uá khue-tiāⁿ i m̃-lâi(我恢定伊毋來).

**imbecile**, tshún-jia̍k(蠢弱); ngô-jia̍k(愚弱). see IDIOT.

**imbibe**, ím(飲); chia̍h(食). *liquid, as porous substance*, sò-tsúi(疏水).

**imbue**, jiám(染); chìm(浸).

**imitate**, o̍h(學); o̍h-iēⁿ(學樣); hãu-o̍h(效學); hãu-huap(效法); chiè-iēⁿ(照樣).

**immaculate**, sûn-chẽng(純淨); pe̍h-ge̍k bô-hiâ(白玉無瑕); pe̍h-piah bô-hiâ(白璧無瑕); bô-tshṳ̂ hó-tiah(無疵好摘).

**immaterial**, bô-hêng hó-kìⁿ(無行好見); bô-hêng bô-sièⁿ(無形無像). *of no importance*, bô-siang-kan(無相干); bô-chhiet-iàu(無切要); bô-iàu-kín(無要緊).

**immature**, būe-se̍k(未熟); chheⁿ(生); būe-kàu-tsúi(未到水).

**immeasurable**, m̄-hó liãng-ta̍t(毋好量値); m̄-hó chhek-ta̍t(毋好測値); bô-hãn-liãng(無限量); lân-íⁿ tshui-chhek(零椅催測).

**immediately**, sûi-sî(隨時); sûi-chiet(隨即); chiet-khek(即刻); lîn-sî(臨時); li̍p-chiet(立即).

**immemorial**, *from time*, siãng-kóu íⁿ-lâi(上古以來); khai-phek íⁿ-lâi(開闢以來).

**immense**, tōa-tsãi(大在); ke̍k-tōa(極大); chì-tōa(至大); tōa-bô-pān(大無辦); tōa-bô-pí(大無比). *an immense quantity*, tōa-bó-mue̍h(大母物).

**immerse**, *(dip and make damp)*, ùn(揾). *(steep)*, chìm(浸). *(sink)*, tîm(沉). *(dip many times so as to wash)*, tìm(沰).

**imminent**, kṳ̃n(近); chiang-kṳ̃n àiⁿ-kàu(將近愛到); chiang-lîm(將臨). *danger*, lîm-ngûi(臨危); ngûi-kip(危急); kín-kip(緊急).

**immoderate**, kùe-hūn(過分); bô-tōu(無度); bô-pān-bó(無辦母); khah-kùe-thâu(較過頭).

**immodest**, m̄-ha̍h-lói(毋合禮); m̄-ùi siáu-lí(毋畏少禮); bô-liâm-chhí(無廉恥).

**immoral**, m̄-chiàⁿ-keng(毋正經); búang-ûi(妄爲); thèng-tsò(聽做); m̄-tuan-chiàⁿ(毋端正); hêng-ûi put-tuan(行爲不端). *immorality*, m̄-chiàⁿ-keng-sṳ̄(毋正經事); m̄-hó-sṳ̄(毋好事); hui-ûi(非爲).

**immortal**, bõi-sí(勿會死); ióng-seⁿ(養生). *immortalize*, miâⁿ phang būan-tō(名芳萬代).

**immure**, kìm(禁).

**immutable**, put-e̍k(不易); m̄-hó-kói(毋好改); bô-î-e̍k(無移易); che̍k-tiāⁿ put-e̍k(一定不易).

**impair**, sún-hāi(損害).

**impalpable**, chhiú put-lêng-lia̍h(手不能掠); bô-si̍t-mue̍h hó-lia̍h(無實物好掠).

**impart**, sṳ̀(示); pun(分); khṳt(乞). *instruction*, si-kà(施教). *news*, thûan-sie-sit(傳消息); pò-sie-sit(報消息).

**impartial**, bô-phien-sim(無偏心); bô-lia̍h khin-tãng(無掠輕重); kong-phêng thãi-nâng(公平待人[訓]); phêng-sim khúan-thãi(公平款待); kuaⁿ-chiàⁿ(官正); kong-tãu thãi-nâng(公道待人[訓]).

**impassable**, bõi-tit-kùe(勿會得過); bô-lōu hó-kiâⁿ(無路好行); khu̍t-thâu-lōu(窟頭路).

**impatient**, kip-sèⁿ(急性); bô-jím-nãiⁿ(無忍耐); húe-sèⁿ(火性); phòng-phiẽ sim-sèⁿ(碰鰾心性); bô-tōu-liãng(無度量).

**impawn**, tǹg-mue̍h(當物); khṳt--nâng tsò-àn(乞人[訓]做案).

**impeach**, kò(告). *(report an officer's misconduct)*, tsham(參).

**impede**, tsó(阻); tsó-chí(阻止); tsó-keh(阻隔); tsó-tàng(阻擋); hûang-gāi(妨礙); thua-thūi(拖墜); gōu-sṳ̄(誤事).

**impel**, kek(激); tshui-tshok(催促); tshui-pek(催迫); tshui-kín(催緊).

**impenetrable**, bô-lōu hó-ji̍p(無路好入); tsǹg-m̄-ji̍p(鑽毋入); bõi-thong(袂通).

**impenitent**, m̄-khéng hùe-kói(毋肯悔改); sim ngúan-ngẽ(心頑硬); m̃-kói-pìⁿ(毋改變); tsṳ̃-pãu tsṳ̃-khì(自暴自氣).

**imperceptible**, thóiⁿ-m̄-tshut(睇毋出).

**imperfect**, m̄-tshûan(毋全); m̄-chiâⁿ-kâi(毋成個); bô-kàu-kâi(無夠個); ũ-khueh(有缺); khiàm-khueh(欠缺); m̄-sêng-kong(毋成功).

**imperial**, hûang-tì-kâi(皇帝個); khim(欽); gṳ̄(御). *favour*, huâng-ṳn(皇恩). *will*, khim-mẽng(欽命); siãng-zũ(上諭); siàⁿ-chí(聖旨). *robes*, gṳ̄-ho̍k(御服); n̂g-phâu(黃袍). *countenance*, lêng-ngûan(龍顏). *presence*, gṳ̄-tsôiⁿ(御前). *pencil*, gṳ̄-pit tsu-phoi(御筆朱批). *family*, uâng-chhin kok-chhek(王親國戚); kok-ke(國家); uâng-ke(王家).

**imperious**, ngẽ-sèⁿ(硬性); pà(霸).

**impertinent**, bô-kui-kṳ́(無規矩); bô-tōa bô-sòi(無大無細); hùang-sṳ̀(放肆); kùe-hūn(過分); ua̍t-hūn(越分).

**impervious**, bô-lōu hó-kùe(無路好過). *to water*, tsúi thàu bõi-tit-kùe(水透袂得過); tsúi sia̍p-m̄-kùe(水涉毋過).

**impetuous**, méⁿ(猛); méⁿ-lie̍t(猛烈); kek-lie̍t(激烈); hiông-kip(雄急).

**impiety**, bô kèng-kiong kâi-sim(無恭敬個心); mēⁿ-thiⁿ chiù-tī(罵天咒地). *filial*, put-hàu(不孝); put-siàu(不肖); m̃-kiâⁿ-hàu(毋行孝).

**implacable**, m̄-hàuⁿ-hûa(毋好和); m̄-khéng-hûa(毋肯和).

**implements**, ke-húe(家伙); mue̍h-kiãⁿ(物件); khì-kũ(器具).

**implicate**, lūi(累); liên-lūi(連累); thua-lūi(拖累); po-lūi(波累).

**implicit**, *obedience*, lím-lím-tsun(凜凜尊); tsun-sûn(尊純); zûi-mẽng-sĩ-thèng(惟命是聽).

**implore**, khṳ́n-khiû(懇求); koh-lô(閣羅).

**impolite**, m̄-hiáu-lí(毋曉理); m̄-hiáu chhêng-lí(毋曉情理); chhêng-lí m̄-thong(情理毋通); bô-lói(無禮); sit-lói(失禮); m̄-ha̍h-ngî(毋合宜).

**important**, kín-iàu(緊要); chhiet-iàu(切要); iàu-kín(要緊); tãng(重); tõng-tãi(重大). *of no importance*, bô-siang-kan(無相干); bô-kai-tsài(無該載); bô-chhiet-iàu(無切要); bô kàu tî-tò-khṳ̀(無到底倒去); bô-tá-kín(無打緊).

**imports**, ji̍p-kháu kâi-hùe(入口个貨).

**importune**, khṳ́n-khiû(懇求); chhiet-khiû(切求). *importunate*, kau-tîⁿ chhiet-khiû(交纏切求).

**impose**, *a fine*, hua̍t-ngṳ̂n(罰銀). *upon*, phièn(騙); tshuah-nâng〔〕; kuang-phièn(誆騙); khi-phièn(欺騙). *impostor*, láu-kiáⁿ(漏囝); ké-kha ké-chhiú(假骹假手).

**impossible**, tsò-m̄-lâi(做毋來); lân(攔). *to describe*, khó-ì-hũe(可意會), put-khó ngân thûan(不可言傳); tàⁿ-m̄-tshut(呾毋出); o̍h iā-bõi-siãu(學也袂曉).

**impost**, hiàng(餉); niêⁿ-sùe(糧稅).

**impotent**, bô-khûan(無權); bô-ta i-ûa(無奈於何); bô-sì-la̍t(無四力); phu̍h(薄); bô-la̍t(無力). *impotence (as a medical term)*, iâng úi(陽萎); bõi-iâng(袂陽).

**impracticable**, tsò-m̄-tit(做毋得); tsò-m̄-lâi(做毋來).

**imprecate**, chiù-tsūa(咒誓).

**impress**, *on the mind*, mêng-khek tõ-sim(明刻在心). *a seal*, kài-ìn(蓋印); khap-ìn(蓋印); teh-ìn(壓印).

**imprison**, kìm(禁); siu-kam(收監); siu-kìm(收禁); khu-kìm(拘禁); kìm-kam(禁監); ki-kam(機監); kam-ah(監押). *false imprisonment*, uan-ge̍k(冤獄); lãm-kìm(濫禁). *to be imprisoned*, siu-kam tsõ-ge̍k(收監坐獄); tsõ-lô(坐牢).

**improbable**, ke-hun sĩ-bô-iáⁿ(家分是無影); tōa-mīn bô-iáⁿ(大面無影); iak-liãng sĩ-bô(約量是無); bô kèng-tōa-mīn(無敬大面).

**improper**, m̄-ha̍h-sek(毋合適); m̄-ha̍h-ngî(毋合宜); m̄-eng-kai(毋應該); m̄-sĩ-sṳ̄(毋是事); bô-chhêng-lí(無情理).

**improve**, *in character*, chìn-tek(進德). *the time*, sieh-hun-im(惜分陰).

**improvident**, m̄-siẽⁿ-tn̂g(毋想長); bô-ién-lṳ̃(無遠慮); bô-ṳ̃-pĩ(無預備); bô-chhiâng-kú tsṳ-kòi(無長久知己); bõi-kòi-siẽⁿ(袂計想); chí-kù ma̍k-tsôiⁿ(只顧目前); ma̍k-tsôiⁿ liám-húe ma̍k-tsôiⁿ-kng(目前斂火目前光).

**imprudent**, bô-kièn-sek(無見識); bõi-phah-sǹg(勿會打算); bõi-tá-sǹg(袂打算); bô-tì-hũi(無智慧).

**impudent**, m̄-ùi siáu-lí(毋畏少禮); mīn-phûe kãu(面皮厚); bô-liâm-chhí(無廉恥).

**impunity**, thut-hêng(脫刑); mién-hua̍t(免罰); lāu-mãng(老罔).

**impure**, m̄-chheng(毋清); m̄-chheng-khih(毋清潔); m̄-chheng-kiet(毋清潔); u-ùe(污穢); siâ(斜); nah-sap(垃圾). *water*, tsúi lô-lô(水羅羅). *conversation*, phue̍h phien-siâ-ūe(白偏斜話); kìⁿ-m̄-tit-nâng kâi-ūe(見毋得人[訓]个話).

**in**, tõ(在). *the heart*, sim-lãi(心內); sim-tang(心中); sim-tói(心底); sim-khám(心坎). *order*, sûn-sũ(順序); chiè tshṳ̀-sũ(制次序); chiè-tsôiⁿ-ãu(照前後). *truth*, khî-si̍t(其實). *this manner*, àn-chièⁿ-seⁿ(按此樣生). *front*, tõ-tsôiⁿ(在前). *a dream*, māng--tang(夢中). *short*, tsóng zṳ̂-ngân--tsṳ(總而言之); lũn-khî tãi-iàu(論其大要). *in order to*, ín-tì-kàu(因致到); sái(使); tì-sái(致使).

**inability**, bô-lêng-ûi(無能爲); bô-pún-sṳ̄(無本事); bô-pún-niáⁿ(無本領); bô-pōu(無步); tsò-m̄-lâi(做毋來).

**inaccessible**, bõi-tit-kàu(袂得到).

**inaccurate**, ũ-tshò(有錯); ũ-m̄-tùi(有毋對); ũ-tsha-tshak(有差錯); ũ-tsáu-tsua̍h(有走絀); ũ-tshò-niũⁿ〔〕; õi-m̄-tie̍h(會毋着); õi-tāⁿ(會賺).

**inactive**, bô-tõng-chhiú(無動手); m̄-tshut-sin(毋出身); ôiⁿ-kṳ(閒龜); ôiⁿ-khiã(閒行); ôiⁿ-tsũ(閒坐).

**inadequate**, put-tsok(不足); m̄-kàu(毋夠). *to any task*, put-seng khî-jĩm(不勝其任). see INABILITY.

**inadvertently**, put-tsai put-kak(不知不覺); bô-ì(無意); hut-jiên(忽然); m̄-tsai-thâu(毋知頭).

**inanimate**, sí-mue̍h(死物); bõi-ua̍h(袂活).

**inapplicable**, m̄-ha̍h(毋合).

**inarticulate**, *sounds*, siaⁿ bô-hun-mêng(聲無分明).

**inasmuch as**, kì-jiên(既然); in-ũi(因爲). see BECAUSE.

**inattentive**, sim bô-tõ(心無在); m̄-tsuan-sim(毋專心); sim hùang-i̍t(心放逸).

**inaudible**, thiaⁿ-m̄-kìⁿ(聽毋見).

**inauspicious**, put-kit(不吉); put-siâng(不祥); hiong(凶).

**inborn**, seⁿ-sêng(生成); seⁿ-chieh(生質); só-seⁿ(所生). *wisdom*, seⁿ-tsai(生知).

**incalculable**, sǹg m̄-pat tò-khṳ̀(算毋識倒去); bû-sù(無數); m̄-hó-siàu(毋好數); bô-pān(無辦); lân-íⁿ tshui-chhek(零椅催測); lân-íⁿ chheng-chhê(零椅清查).

**incapable**, bô-lêng-ûi(無能爲); bô-pōu(無步); bô-tshâi-chhêng(無才情); bô-pún-sṳ̄(無本事). see INABILITY.

**incarnate**, kàng-seⁿ(降生); kàng-hûam(降凡); kàng-sì(降世); kàng-seⁿ tsò-nâng(降生做人).

**incendiary**, pàng-húe(放火).

**incense**, hieⁿ(香); phang-hieⁿ(芳香). *pot*, hieⁿ-lôu(香爐). *stick*, che̍k-ki-hieⁿ(一枝香). *to burn*, ûn-hieⁿ(焚香); sie-hieⁿ(燒香); tiám-hieⁿ(點香). *to stick an incense-stick in pot*, tshah-hieⁿ(插香); chìn-hieⁿ(進香). *to incense*, kek--nâng seⁿ-khì(激人[訓]生氣); jiá--nâng seⁿ-khì(惹人[訓]生氣). *incensed*, hṳ̃n-náuⁿ(恨惱); náuⁿ-khì(惱氣).

**incentive**, kám-tõng nâng-sim(感動人心); kám-kek nâng-sim(感激人心).

**incessant**, bô-hiah(無歇); bô-kòiⁿ-tñg(無間斷); bô-làn(無限); sî-sî khek-khek(時時刻刻); bô-sî-hiah(無時歇).

**incest**, nge̍k-lûn(逆倫); lũan-lûn(亂倫); nge̍k-lûn kan-îm(逆倫姦淫).

**inch**, tshùn(寸).

**incinerate**, sie-tsò húe-hu(燒做火灰); sie-tiāu(燒掉).

**incision**, kuah-khui(割開); le̍h-khui(歷開); le̍h-che̍k-li̍h(歷一裂).

**incite**, jiá(惹); tõng(動); jiá-tõng(惹動); kek-chiàng(激將); kek-lĩ(激勵); thie-so(挑唆); kà-so(教唆); kòi-kà(戒教); kà-lā(教納); kóu-bú(鼓舞).

**incline**, *the heart*, sim hiàng(心向); chì hiàng(志向). *inclination*, sim-chì(心志); sim tsṳ-só-mōⁿ(心姿所望). *be inclined*, hàuⁿ(好); àiⁿ(愛). *incline the head*, hú-siú(府守); thâu-khak phak-kẽ(頭殼趴下). *inclined(of things)*, tshúa-kùe-lâi(歪過來); tshúa-che̍k-pôiⁿ(歪一爿); ka-lak-khi(膠落崎); siâ(斜).

**inclose**, pau-huang(包封); ûi-tsũ(圍住); ûi(圍).

**include**, pau-hâm(包含); pau-kuat(包括). *included*, tõ-lãi(在內).

**incognito**, ṳ́n-kiâⁿ(隱行); àm-húang(暗仿); àm-chẽⁿ tshut--lâi(暗靜出來).

**incoherent**, bô-thâu bô-búe(無頭無尾); bô-tshṳ̀ bô-sũ(無次無序); bô siang-liên-so̍k(無相連續); m̄-kùan-tshùan(毋慣串).

**incombustible**, bõi-to̍h-húe(袂著火); bõi-chia̍h-húe(袂食火).

**income**, só-ji̍p(所入); só-siu(所收). *official*, hóng-lo̍k(俸祿); iáng-liâm(養廉). *from all quarters*, tsa̍p-bũ-chîⁿ(雜務錢).

**incommode**, hûan-lâu(煩勞); lâu-kè(勞駕); lūi(累); lâu-tõng(勞動); hũn(混); hũn-jiáu(混擾); kiáu-jiáu(攪擾); jiáu-tõng(擾動); kùe-jiãu(過擾).

**incomparable**, bô-hó-pí(無好比); bô-hó pí-pẽng(無好比並); lân-íⁿ siang-pí(難以相比); bô-sang(無雙).

**incompetent**, see INCAPABLE.

**incomplete**, m̄-tshûan(毋全); m̄-kàu(毋夠); tsua̍h(絀); khueh(缺); khiàm-khueh(欠缺); khih-khiàm(缺欠).

**inconceivable**, lân-íⁿ chhek-ta̍t(難以測達); siẽⁿ m̄-pat tò-khṳ̀(想毋識倒去).

**incongruous**, see INCONSISTENT.

**inconsiderate**, m̄-kṳ́n-sín(毋謹慎); bô-sòi-jī(無細字).

**inconsistent**, m̄-tùi(毋對); siang-húan(相反); pũe-lí(悖理); pũe-tãu(悖道); m̄-ha̍h(毋合).

**inconstant**, bô-siêⁿ-sim(無常心); bô-siêⁿ(無常); ũ-thâu bô-búe(有頭無尾); húan-ho̍k put-chhek(反覆不測); bô-hêng-sim(無恆心); húan-húan ho̍k-ho̍k(反反覆覆); póiⁿ-póiⁿ-tńg(反反轉).

**incontinent**, put-lêng khiok-kí(不能克己); bô-pín-tsat(無品節); bô-tsat-chì(無節制); put-lêng kuán-hat ka-kī(不能管轄家己).

**inconvenient**, put-piẽn(不便).

**incorporeal**, bô-hêng(無形); bô-thói(無體); bô-tsuãng(無狀); bô-hêng bô-tsuãng(無形無狀).

**incorrect**, see INACCURATE.

**incorrigible**, m̄-khéng kói-pìⁿ(毋肯改變); m̃-hùe-kói(毋悔改); ngẽ-sim(硬心); nguán-ngẽ(頑硬).

**incorruptible**, bô-hùi-huãi(無毀壞); tshoiⁿ-kóu put-hiùⁿ(千古不臭); buān-nîⁿ put-hiùⁿ(萬年不朽). *of character, sim kien*, ì kù(意故); put-lêng tsang-chîⁿ-ngṳ̂n iú-ho̍k--i(不能將金銀誘惑伊); kien-chip put-tshông(堅執不從).

**increase**, kia(加); thiⁿ-ke(天加); thiam-ke(添加); cheng-ke(增加); kia-cheng(加增); kia-thiam(加添); heng-sẽng(興盛); mõng-sẽng(茂盛).

**incredible**, put-tsok-sìn(不足信); lân-íⁿ siang-sìn(難以相信); lân-sìn(難信); miáu-mâng oh-sìn(渺茫僫信).

**incredulous**, bô-siang-sìn(無相信); m̄-hàuⁿ-sìn(毋好信); m̃-sìn(毋信); ũ-tshai-gî(有猜疑). *(half believing)*, gî-sìn tsham-pùaⁿ(疑信參半); pùaⁿ-sìn pùaⁿ-gî(半信半疑).

**inculcate**, hun-hù(吩咐); teng-lêng tsok-hù(叮嚀囑咐).

**incur**, *one's anger*, tshok--tie̍h i-khì(觸着伊氣).

**incurable**, m̄-hó-ui(毋好醫); lân-ui(難醫). *disease*, hùi-chi̍t(廢疾).

**indebted**, khiàm--nâng(欠人[訓]); khiàm-chè(欠債); khiàm-chîⁿ(欠錢); khiàm-siàu(欠數). *to feel under obligations for kindness received*, kám-nâng-ṳn(感人[訓]恩); kám-ṳn tài-tek(感恩戴德).

**indecent**, m̄-ha̍h-lí(毋合理); m̄-hó-thóiⁿ(毋好睇); bô-ngî(無義); bô-lói-ngî(無禮儀); hui-lói(非禮); bô-thí-mīn sṳ̄(無體面事); m̄-kuan-ngiá(毋觀雅).

**indeed**, kúaⁿ-jiên(果然); si̍t-tsãi(實在); tiāⁿ-tie̍h(定着). *indeed!*, õ(噢).

**indefatigable**, put-kuãn(不倦); bô-phî-kuãn(不疲倦); tsong-ji̍t bô-hiah(終日無歇); khṳ̂n-tsãi(肯在); khṳ̂n-la̍t(勤力).

**indefinite**, bô-tiāⁿ-tie̍h(無定着); bô-hãn-tiāⁿ(無限定).

**indelible**, put-lêng bûa-mi̍t(不能磨滅); put-lêng mi̍t-chiah(不能滅跡); jī-chiah put-mi̍t(二字不滅); hú-m̄-khṳ̀(府毋去).

**indemnify**, pûe(賠); póu(保); pûe-siêⁿ(賠償); siêⁿ-póu(償保).

**indented**, seⁿ-kṳ̀-khí(生鋸起); nap-uh(凹扼); nap-khang(肭空).

**indenture**, ha̍p-tâng(合同); ha̍p-ieh(合約); thiap(帖); kuan-thiap(官帖).

**independent**, tsṳ̃-tsú(自主); chia̍h ka-kī-pn̄g(食家己飯).

**index**, ma̍k-lo̍k(目錄); tôi-thâu(題頭).

**India**, Iǹ-tōu-kok(印度國); Thien-tsok-kok(天竺國); Thien-tek-kok(天德國). *Indian corn*, íⁿ-bí-jîn(椅米仁); iùⁿ-múiⁿ-jîn(幼麵仁).

**indict**, kò-tsn̄g(告狀); ji̍p-pín(入稟); ji̍p-tiâⁿ(入呈). *indictment*, tsn̄g-sṳ̂(狀詞); tiâⁿ-sṳ̂(呈詞).

**indicate**, chí(指); chí-sī(指示); kí-tiám(指點).

**indifferent**, bô-chhiet-iàu(無切要); put-lũn(不論); sûi-piẽn(隨便).

**indigestion**, tóu m̄-siau(肚毋消); m̄-siau-chia̍h(毋消食); bõi-siau-hùe(勿會消化).

**indignation**, khì(氣); hún-khì(憤氣). *at wrong done to another*, put-phêng(不平); ũi-put-phêng(謂不平).

**indigo**, thóu-tōiⁿ(土靛); lâm-tōiⁿ(藍靛). *(growing)*, chheⁿ(青). *(the dye)*, chheⁿ-tōiⁿ(青靛). *foreign*, iêⁿ-tōiⁿ(洋靛). *vat*, chheⁿ-tháng(青桶).

**indirect**, m̃-ti̍t-tàⁿ(毋直呾); uan-tuân(冤團); uan-khek(冤屈); úi-khiok(委屈); tshúa(惹); uai-tshúa(歪歪).

**indiscreet**, bô-tsṳ́-sòi(無仔細); bô-tì-hũi(無智慧); phû-tshàu(浮草); khin-phû(輕浮).

**indiscriminate**, bô-lũn(無論); bô-hun-pie̍t(無分別); put-khu(不拘); sûi-piẽn(隨便); thèng(聽). *statements*, khài-lũn(概論); tsò-che̍k-khài tàⁿ(做概開呾); che̍k-kù thek-lṳ̂ mēⁿ-thong-am(一故剔驢罵通庵).

**indispensable**, m̄-hó-bô(毋好無); bõi-tit-mién(袂得免); put-lêng hó-mién(不能好免); mín-put-tit(免不得); bũ-pit tie̍h-ũ(務必着有); tiāⁿ-tie̍h-àiⁿ(定着愛); ngẽ-hóuⁿ tie̍h-ũ(硬虎着有).

**indisposed**, m̄-sóng-khùai(毋爽快); m̄-tsṳ̃-tsãi(毋自在); m̄-phêng-an(毋平安); cheng-sîn kù-m̄-kàu(精神顧毋到); ien-siên〔〕. *unwilling*, bô-siẽⁿ-àiⁿ-tsò(無想愛做); ùi-ùi(畏畏); m̄-nguãn(毋願).

**indisputable**, m̄-hó poh-khùi(毋好駁氣); piẽn-poh m̄-kùe(辯駁毋過); à-m̄-khṳ̀(亞毋去); chin--kâi bõi-lêng à-tit-ké(真个袂能亞得假).

**indistinct**, m̄-hīn(毋現); mông-hũn(朦渾); bū-bū(霧霧); mông-bū(蒙霧); bô-mêng-pe̍h(無明白); hun-hun(昏昏); m̄-chheng-tshó(毋清楚); tàⁿ-ūe kâm-kôu(呾話含糊); lú-lú(魯魯).

**indivisible**, m̄-hó pun-khui(毋好分開).

**individual**, che̍k-kâi-nâng(一個人); che̍k-ūi(一位). *individually*, che̍k-nâng che̍k-nâng(一人一人); kak-nâng(各人).

**indubitable**, tiāⁿ-tie̍h(定着); mién-gî(免疑).

**induce**, khan-ín(牽引); ín-tshūa(引𤆬); ín-iú(引誘); sái(使); chie(招). *(by persuasion)*, khǹg-kòi(勸戒).

**indulge**, *oneself*, jîm-ì(任意); tsòng-ì(縱意). *indulgent*, khuan-thãi(寬待); pàng-khuan(放寬); pàng-sang(放鬆); pàng-làng-sang(放零鬆); khuan-tshṳ̂(寬慈), tshṳ̂-ài(慈愛); bô-ngiâm(無嚴). *(forgiving)*, khuan-sù(寬恕).

**indurated**, pièn-ngẽ(變硬); pièn-tōiⁿ(變靛). *(callosity)*, seⁿ-ngẽ-lan(生硬爛). *hands*, chhiú seⁿ-lan(手生爛).

**industrious**, khṳ̂n-kang(勤工); gia̍p-tsoh(業作).

**inefficacious**, bô-kong-hāu(無功效); bô-hāu-ngiām(無效驗).

**inequality**, m̄-tsôi(毋齊); m̄-tsâu(毋齊); m̄-pêⁿ(毋平); tsham-tsha(參差); tn̂g-tó(長短); kûiⁿ-kẽ(懸下).

**inestimable**, bô-kè-pó(無價寶); bô-pān-siàu(無辦數).

**inevitable**, bô-nãiⁿ-hô(無奈何); bô-khó nãiⁿ-hô(無可奈何); mién-put-tit(免不得); m̄-hó tô-pī(毋好逃避).

**inexcusable**, *bô-hó hun-sù; lí khut*, sṳ̂ khiông(辭窮).

**inexperienced**, chheⁿ-hūn(生分); chheⁿ-chhiú(生手); m̄-se̍k-chhiú(毋熟手); bô-liēn(無練); m̄-pat liēn-si̍p(毋識練習).

**inexpressible**, tàⁿ bõi-tit-liáu(呾袂得了); ngân tsṳ put-chĩn(言之不盡); tshoiⁿ-ngân būan-ngân tàⁿ-m̄-liáu(千言萬言呾毋了).

**inextricable**, kói-m̄-thut(改毋脫); kiù bõi-tit-tshut(救袂得出).

**infamous**, miâⁿ-siaⁿ tshàu(名聲臭); tshàu-miâⁿ(臭名); hiùⁿ-miâⁿ(臭名). *for ever*, būan-tō hiùⁿ-miâⁿ(萬代臭名).

**infant**, sòi-kiáⁿ(細囝); eng-jî(嬰兒); hâi-jî(孩兒); a-nôuⁿ(阿孥); siàu-tsṳ́(少子). *infanticide*, phah-sí a-nôuⁿ(拍死阿孥); ne̍k-nńg(溺女); phah-sí tsáu-kiáⁿ(拍死走囝).

**infantry**, pōu-piaⁿ(步兵).

**infect**, ùe-tie̍h-pēⁿ(穢着病). *infectious*, õi-ùe-nâng(會穢人); õi-thûan-jiám(會傳染); õi-jiám-nâng(會染人).

**infelicitous**, put-kit(不吉); put-siâng(不詳); hiong(凶); m̄-tsãu-hùe(毋造化); ūn-khì m̄-sũn(運氣毋順).

**infer**, tshui(推); tshui-sǹg(推算); tshui-siẽⁿ(推想); lūi-tshui(類推); tshui-lũn(推論); tshui-tshut(推出); tshui-siẽⁿ phan-sǹg(推想攀算).

**inferior**, su(輸); kẽ-pín(下品). *inferiors*, chhiú-ẽ kâi-nâng(手下个人).

**infested**, *with*, ûi-huãm(爲患). *with tigers*, ũ-hóuⁿ-huãm(有虎患).

**infinite**, bô-hãn bô-liãng(無限無量); bô-sí bô-tsong(無死無終).

**infirm**, sin-hūn lám〔〕; sin-hūn phàⁿ(身分冇). *of purpose*, sim-chì m̄-kien-kù(心智毋堅固); sim m̄-kien(心毋堅); sim kōi-iâu-i̍t(心易搖逸); iêⁿ-hue tsúi-sèⁿ(楊花水性). *an infirmity*, mâuⁿ-pēⁿ(毛病).

**inflammation**, húe(火); jie̍t(熱); âng-jie̍t(紅熱). *of eyes*, ma̍k-chiu jie̍t-thiàⁿ(目睭熱痛); pãu-thiàⁿ(暴痛). *remove*, thò-húe(退火).

**inflate**, pûn-huang(歕風).

**inflexible**, chip-huap(執法); chip-lūt(執律); kien-ngẽ(堅硬); thih-chie̍h sim-kuaⁿ(鐵石心肝); thih-mīn bô-chhêng(鐵面無情).

**inflict**, *punishment*, kiâⁿ-hêng-hua̍t(行刑罰).

**influence**, khuân(權); khì-la̍t(氣力); khuân-kì(權紀); sì(勢); sì-thâu(勢頭); sì-mīn(勢面); khuân-sì(權勢); khuân-kùi(權貴). *trust in others' influence*, chiã-sì(藉勢); chiã-sì-la̍t(藉勢力); sái-pa̍t-nâng kâi-sin-sì(使別人[訓]个身勢). *to influence people*, kám-tõng(感動); kám-kek(感激); kám-hùe(感化).

**inform**, thong-tsai(通知); pò-tsai(報知); thuân-tsai(通知); pín(稟); tàⁿ(呾); tàⁿ-tsai(呾知); kàu-tsai(告知); hiáu-zũ(曉諭). *informer*, sùaⁿ-soh(線索).

**infrequent**, chié-ū(少有); chié-tit(少得); chié-só-ũ(少所有); hán--tit(罕得).

**infringe**, *laws*, huãm-huap(犯法).

**infuse**, *tea*, tshong-tê(沖茶). *of good tea several infusions can be made*, hó-tê-bí nãiⁿ-tshong(好茶米耐沖).

**ingenious**, khá(巧); khi-kká(崎巧); ki-khá(機巧); sin-khá(新巧); khá-ĩ(巧耳); kuai-khá(乖巧); kuai-khiáu(乖巧).

**ingot**, *of sycee*, nguân-pó(元寶); uâng-pó(黃寶). *(chiefly of paper imitations)*, ngṳ̂n-tiã(銀錠).

**ingratitude**, buâng-ṳn hũ-ngĩ(忘恩負義); siũ-ṳn put-pò(受恩不報); hiau-chhêng tso̍h-ngĩ(僥情絕義); bô-jîn-ngĩ(無仁義); put-jîn put-ngĩ(不仁不義); chiang-ṳn chhiû-pò(將恩仇報). *beastly*, tṳ-káu buâng-chhêng(豬狗忘情).

**inhabit**, kṳ-tsũ(居住); khiã-khí(徛起). *inhabitants*, kṳ-mîn(居民); pńg-tī-nâng(本地人).

**inhale**, khip(吸); kuh(呵). *injured by inhaling cold air*, sah-tie̍h-huang(吸着風).

**inherit**, sêng-zũi-ngia̍p(承遺業). *inheritance*, zũi-ngia̍p(遺業); ke-ngia̍p(家業); mu̍eh-ngia̍p(物業); sûi-ngia̍p(隨業).

**inhospitable**, po̍h-thãi nâng-kheh(薄待人[訓]客); hut-lia̍k nâng-kheh(忽略人客).

**inhuman**, put-jîn(不仁); bô-nâng-chhêng(無人情); tshâng-pãu(殘暴); hiong-ak(兇惡); m̄-sĩ-nâng(毋是人[訓]).

**iniquitous**, m̄-kong-tãu(毋公道); m̄-kong-phêng(毋公平); put-ngĩ(不義); m̄-chiàⁿ(毋正); m̄-kuaⁿ-chiàⁿ(毋官正). *iniquity*, tsũe-ak(罪惡); tsũe-kùe(罪過).

**inject**, *as water with syringe*, ēng-thiu lâi kùan-tsúi(用抽來灌水).

**injure**, sún(損); sún-hāi(損害); sieⁿ-hāi(傷害); sún-sieⁿ(損傷); hām-hāi(陷害); sún-phùa(損破); tshâng-hāi(殘害); sieⁿ-tshâng(傷殘); khui-sún(虧損). *injurious*, hāi-nâng(害人[訓]); lĩ-hāi(利害); ũ-sún bô-iah(有損無益); hām-hāi(陷害).

**injustice**, hui-ngĩ(非義); put-ngĩ(不義). *indignant at injustice done to another*, put-phêng(不平); ũi-put-phêng(謂不平).

**inner**, lãi-mīn(內面); tói-mīn(底面); lãi-tói(內底).

**innocent**, bô-tsũe(無罪); bô-kùe(無罪); bô-kou(無罪). *harmless*, láu-si̍t(老實).

**innumerable**, bû-sù(無數); put-lêng hó-siàu(不能好數); lân-íⁿ chĩn-sǹg(攔已盡算); lân-íⁿ sǹg-kòi(攔已算計); sǹg-kòi m̄-chĩn(算計毋盡); sǹg-m̄-liáu(算毋了); sǹg m̄-pat tò-khṳ̀(算毋識倒去); bô-hãn-tsōi(無限㩼); bô-pān(無辦).

**inquisitive**, kṳn-kiù(根究); kiù kàu-tói-sòi(究到底細); múeⁿ-sṳ̄-mn̄g(每事問); kiãⁿ-kiãⁿ tou-àiⁿ-mn̄g(件件都愛問); hàuⁿ-mn̄g(好問); mn̄g-ūe lo-so(問話囉嗦); mn̄g-ūe so-siak(問話疏屑).

**insane**, siáu(瘋); huat-tien(發癲); huat-khuâng(發狂); sim-sîn m̄-tiāⁿ(心神毋定); sim m̄-tiāⁿ(心毋定); tien-khuâng(癲狂); sit-sim(失心).

**insatiable**, *m̄-tsai-tsok; tham-sim bô-iam; chéⁿ-tsúi pìⁿ-tsò-chiú*, iũ-hiâm tṳ bô-tsau(又嫌豬無糟).

**inscription**, pi-kì(碑記); pâi-pín(牌匾); pín-hia̍h(匾額).

**insensible**, m̄-tsai-nâng(毋知人[訓]). *to pain*, m̄-tsai-thiàⁿ(毋知痛). *to shame*, m̄-tsai siáu-lí(毋知少禮).

**insert**, tshah-ji̍p(插入); lōng-ji̍p(弄入); lāng-ji̍p(攪入); thn̄g--ji̍p-khṳ̀(捅入去). *in an account book*, chiẽⁿ-siàu(上數); teng-phóu(登譜); kì-siàu(記數). *in a book*, kì-lo̍k(記錄).

**inside**, lãi(內); lãi-mīn(內面); lãi-tói(內底); tói(底); tói-pôiⁿ(底爿); tói-mīn(底面).

**insidious**, àm-hāi(暗害); àm-chìⁿ(暗箭); kan-tsà(奸詐).

**inspect**, thóiⁿ(睇); kàm-tshat(監察); sûn-siú(巡守); sûn-sĩ(巡視); sûn-thóiⁿ(巡睇). *examination essays*, thóiⁿ-kńg(睇管); luat-kńg(閱管). *inspector*, kam-tok(監督).

**inspiration**, *of breath*, che̍k-khip(一吸). *inspired by the Spirit*, kám--tie̍h Siàⁿ-Sîn(感着聖神).

**instal**, *into office*, kau-ìn(交印); kau-pûaⁿ(交盤); kau-sià(交卸).

**instant**, *an*, che̍k-khùn-kiáⁿ(一頃囝); che̍k-ma̍k-nihⁿ(一目忍); che̍k-sek-kú(一色久); che̍k-siap-sî(一霎時); che̍k-khek(一刻). *instantly*, chiet-khek(即刻); sûi-chiet(隨即); sûi-sî(隨時); lîm-sî(臨時).

**insure**, *goods (of insurance compaby)*, pó-ke(保家). *goods (of the insurer)*, pa̍k-pó-ke-jī(縛保家字). *insurance office*, pó-ke(保家). *policy*, pó-ke-jī(保家字); pó-ke-toaⁿ(保家單); pó-ke-tsúa(保家紙).

**insurrection**, tsak-luãn(作亂); huán(反); mông-huán(蒙反); puãn-luãn(叛亂); huán-puãn(反叛); húan-lũan(反亂); puãn-nge̍k(叛逆).

**interpret**, hûe-ūe(會話); thûan-ūe(傳話); huan-e̍k(翻譯). *explain*, kói-mêng(解明). *interpreter*, thong-sṳ(通知). *interpreter (in court)*, thûan-keng(傳經). *interpret dreams*, piẽn-māng(辨夢); kói-māng(解夢).

**inure**, tsò-kùiⁿ-sìⁿ(做慣性); kuàn-si̍p(慣習); si̍p-kuàn ûi-siêⁿ(習慣爲常).

**invalid**, būe-ho̍k nguân-iēⁿ(未服原樣); chia̍h-khṳ̀ būe-ho̍k(食去未服); pēⁿ-thói būe-ho̍k(病體未服).

**invert**, póiⁿ-tńg(反轉); póiⁿ--kùe-lâi(反過來). *inverted*, tò(倒); tin-tò(顛倒); tin-tò-thâu(顛倒頭); tò-khap(倒恰); chèng-tńg(正轉); tin-tò-thâu chèng(顛倒頭正).

**investigate**, tshat-kiù(察究); chhê(查); chhê-mêng(查明); káng-kiù(講究); siâng-tshat(詳察); sím-mn̄g(審問); séng-tshat(省察); séⁿ-tshat(省察); ki-kháu(稽考); ki-chhê(稽查); phûan-chhê(判查); sòi-siâng-mn̄g(細詳問); kháu-kiù(考究).

**inveterate**, khah-kú oh-kói(較久惡改); kùiⁿ-sìⁿ(慣勢); tùe-ngẽ(綴硬). *disease*, kù-chi̍t(故疾).

**invigorate**, póu-la̍t(補力); tsàng-sin(壯身); póu-iáng(補養); iáng-la̍t(養力); iáng-cheng-sîn(養精神); phûe-iáng khì-la̍t(培養氣力).

**invincible**, thâi-m̄-iâⁿ(敗毋贏); thâi-m̄-kùe(敗毋過).

**invisible**, bô-hó thóiⁿ--kìⁿ(無好睇見); ma̍k só-lân-tshat(目所難察); bô-hêng hó-thóiⁿ(無形好睇); bô-chiah hó-chhîm(無跡好尋).

**invite**, chhiáⁿ(請). *guests*, chhiáⁿ-nâng-kheh(請人[訓]客); chhiáⁿ-chiú(請酒); hũe-kheh(會客); chhiáⁿ-sia̍h(請席). *invitation card*, chhiáⁿ-thiap(請帖).

**invoke**, pín-khiû(稟求); khiû(求); táu-kàu(禱告). *heaven*, táu-thiⁿ(禱天); táu-tsok Siãng-thien(禱囑上天).

**invoice**, hùe-toaⁿ(貨單); hùe-mue̍h-toaⁿ(貨物單).

**involve**, lūi(累); liên-lūi(連累); thua-lūi(拖累); thùa-lūi(退累); po-lūi(波累); hām-hāi(陷害). *involved*, siũ-lūi(受累); lap--tie̍h(拉着).

**involuntary**, bô-sim bô-ì(無心無意); put-tsai put-kak(不知不覺); tshut-tõ bô-ì(出在無意).

**irksome**, hûan-jiáu(煩擾); kiáu-jiáu(攪擾); kan-khóu(艱苦); ùi(畏); iàm-khóu(厭苦).

**iron**, thih(鐵). *cast-iron*, seⁿ(生). *unwrought*, chheⁿ-thih(生鐵). *malleable*, jiû-nńg-thih(揉軟鐵); nńg-thih(軟鐵); se̍k-thih(熟鐵). *to temper*, chhih-tsúi(彳水). *an iron for clothes*, ut-táu(熨斗). *to iron*, ut(熨). *iron-filings*, thih-sut(鐵屑); thih-tshùi(鐵碎); thih-hu(鐵夫); thih-sua(鐵沙). *iron-wire*, thih-sùaⁿ(鐵線).

**ironical**, húan-ngân(反言); húan-ngân ki-chhiáu(反言機俏); tsuan tin-tò-tàⁿ lâi-ki-chhiáu(專顛倒呾來譏誚); khõ-nâng〔〕.

**irrational**, m̄-mêng-lí(毋明理); bô-lêng-hûn(無靈魂).

**irrelevant**, u-khuah(迂闊); khuah-lok thâu-kṳn(闊漉頭跟); huàm(泛).

**irresistible**, tsó-m̄-tit(阻毋得); tí-tng m̄-tsũ(抵當毋住).

**irreverence**, put-kèng(不敬); khin-bũan(輕慢); siet-to̍k(褻瀆).

**irresolute**, thiû-thû(躊躇); thiû-siẽⁿ(躊想); tsú-ì m̄-tiāⁿ(主意毋定); būe-ũ kuatⁿì(未有決意); thiû-thû put-lêng che̍k-kuat(躊躇不能一決); chìn-chìn thò-thò(進進退退).

**irrevocable**, tui-m̄-tńg(追毋轉); che̍k-ngân kì-tshut sì-bé lân-tui(一言既出駟馬難追).

**irrigate**, pàng-tsúi lo̍h-tshân(放水落田); hòu-tsúi(戽水); ak-tsúi(沃水).

**is**, sĩ(是). *is it so*, sĩ a-m̄-sĩ(是亞毋是). *is he come*, i ũ-lâi a-būe(伊有來亞未). *is the water deep*, tsúi õi-chhim(水會深), mé(猛).

**isinglass**, hṳ̂-ka(魚膠); kim-lêng-ka(金靈膠).

**Islamism**, hûe-hûe-kà(回回教).

**island**, hái-suaⁿ(海山); hái-táu(海島); hái-sṳ̃(海嶼). *in river*, chiu(洲).

**issue**, *forth*, huat-tshut(發出). *decree*, huat-mẽng(發命). *proclamation*, tshut-kò-sī(出告示).

**isthmus**, suaⁿ-ie(山腰); sok-ie(束腰); sok-ãm(束頷); suaⁿ-ãm(山頷).

**itch**, *the*, kòi(疥). *to have*, seⁿ-kòi(生疥). *itchy*, chiẽⁿ(癢). *scratch*, pê-chiẽⁿ(爬癢).

**item**, *an*, che̍k-kiãⁿ(一件); che̍k-tiâu(一條).

**itinerate**, chiu-liû(周遊); chiu-sûn(周巡). *itinerary*, lōu-thiâⁿ-chheh(路條冊); lōu-ín(路引).

**ivory**, gê(牙); chhiẽⁿ-gê(象牙).

**ivy**, tîn(藤).

### J

**jack-fruit**, po-lô-bi̍t(菠蘿蜜).

**jade**, ge̍k(玉).

**jaded**, khùn(困); he̍k(赫); khùn-kuãn(困倦); phî-khùn(疲倦); hẽng(恨).

**jail**, kam(監); lô(牢); kam-ge̍k(監獄). *jailer*, kìm-chí(禁止); kìm-tsut(禁卒).

**jam**, ko(膏); tiâm-ko(甜膏).

**Japan**, Ji̍t-pńg-kok(日本國); Tang-iêⁿ(東洋).

**jasmine**, ba̍k-lĩ-hue(茉莉花).

**jaundice**, n̂g-sua-pēⁿ(黃痧病).

**Java**, Ka-la-pa(加拉吧).

**javelin**, chhiú-chìⁿ(手掌).

**jaw**, ẽ-hâi(下頦). *jaw-bones*, gê-tshn̂g(牙床); gê-tsô-kut(牙槽骨).

**jay**, kheh-chiáu(客鳥).

**jealous**, kòu-kĩ(妒忌); chi̍t-kòu(嫉妒).

**jeer**, ki-chhiáu(譏笑).

**jest**, tàⁿ-sńg(呾耍); tàⁿ tshù-bī-ūe(呾趣味話).

**jet**, ou-ge̍k(烏玉).

**jetty**, bé-thâu(碼頭).

**Jew**, Iû-thài-nâng(猶太人).

**jewel**, tien-pó(珠寶); pó-ge̍k(寶玉); pó-chie̍h(寶石). *jeweller*, chhia-ge̍k sai-pẽ(車玉司阜).

**jingling**, tiang-tiang-kiè(叮叮嘰).

**job**, khang-khùe(工課). *take on contract*, mãuⁿ-kang(冒工).

**join**, siang-ha̍h(相合); tsò-pû(做包); kap-bûa(合埋). *joined in succession*, chiap(接); sie-chiap(相接); chiap-liên(接連); siang-liên(相連); sie-sùa(相紲); sie-thùa(相退). *accompany*, tsò-pû-kiâⁿ(做煲行). *a partnership*, tsò-húe-kì(做火記). *an association*, pài-hũe(拜會). *hands*, siang-khan-chhiú(相牽手). *battle*, ha̍h-chièn(合戰).

**joiner**, ba̍k-kang sai-pẽ(木工司阜).

**joint**, chiap-hûn(接痕); chiap-tsūe(接罪). *of finger*, chek-tsat(積節). *of bone*, ku̍t-ngám(滑眼). *out of*, tshut-khũ(出臼). *of bamboo*, tek-tsat(竹節).

**joist**, lâu-lēng(樓柃).

**joke**, sie-sńg-ūe(相耍話); tàⁿ-sńg(呾耍); hì-sńg kâi-ūe(戲耍个話); hì-ngân(戲言); tshù-bī-ūe(趣味話); tàⁿ-khá-ūe(呾巧話).

**jolt**, chhia tiē(車地); tiē-thôu(地塗); iau-i̍t(搖曳).

**jostle**, iòng-chìⁿ(擁擠); ói-ói léng-léng〔〕.

**jot**, tiám(點). *one jot or tittle*, che̍k-hâu che̍k-lî(一毫一厘).

**journal**, kì-sṳ̄-phõu(記事簿). *newspaper*, sin-bûn-tsúa(新聞紙); ji̍t-pò(日報).

**journey**, lōu-thêng(路程); lōu-thiâⁿ(路呈). *long*, hñg kâi-lōu-thiâⁿ(遠个路程); ién-thiâⁿ(遠呈); tn̂g-thiâⁿ(長呈). *begin*, khí-thiâⁿ(起呈); khí-kiâⁿ(起行); khí-sin(起身). *to journey*, kiâⁿ-lōu(行路).

**joy**, hí-la̍k(喜樂); khùai-la̍k(快樂); huaⁿ-hí(歡喜); hí-sim(喜心).

**judge**, sím-phùan(審判); sím-sṳ̄(審事); phōiⁿ-ùaⁿ(辦案). *a judge*, thî-hêng-kuaⁿ(提刑官). *a judge (provincial)*, àn-tshat-si(按察司). *day of judgement*, sím-phùan-ji̍t(審判日). *heaven's judgements*, thiⁿ kàng-tsai(天降災). *one's judgement of anything*, ì-kièn(意見).

**jug**, *water*, tsúi-kũaⁿ(水罐); tsúi-pân(水瓶); tsúi-kùan(水罐).

**juggler**, tsò-pa-hì(做把戲); tsò-pá-hì(做飽戲).

**juice**, tsap(汁); nîⁿ(泥).

**jumbled**, hũn-tsa̍p(混雜); zṳ̂-luãn(挐亂); hũn-luãn(混亂); tsa̍p-luãn(雜亂).

**jump**, thiàu(跳); thiàu-iak(跳躍); thiàu-bú(跳舞). *over*, thiàu--kùe-khṳ̀(跳過去). *up*, thiàu--khí-lâi(跳起來).

**jungle**, chhì-nâⁿ-tà(刺林打); chhì-phè(刺帕); chhiū-ba̍k im-ùe(樹木陰穢).

**junior**, sòi(細); kiám-hùe(減歲); chié-hùe(少歲).

**junk**, tsûn(船); tōa-tsûn(大船); iêⁿ-tsûn(洋船).

**Jupiter**, ba̍k-chheⁿ(木星).

**jurisdiction**, khuân-pèⁿ(權柄).

**just**, kong-ngĩ(公義); kong-tãu(公道); kuaⁿ-chiàⁿ(官正); kong-phêng(公平). *now*, chí-tsûn(此陣); chiàⁿ(正); hīn-kim(現今); hīn-tsãi(現在). *a little ago*, thâng-kùa〔〕; siè-siè〔〕; soiⁿ che̍k-khùn-kiáⁿ(先一頃囝); tsá--tsûn(早陣). *about*, lím-lím(凜凜); kah-kah(合合); siè-siè〔〕. *like*, nẽⁿ pêⁿ-pêⁿ-iēⁿ〔〕; siãu-tsãi(肖在). *just so*, chiũ-sĩ(就是); sĩ--nōⁿ(是也); ũ-tõ-lí(有道理).

**justify**, chheng-ngĩ(稱義); sǹg-tsò-ngĩ(算做義).

**jut**, *out*, tshun--tshut-lâi(伸出來); thóu--tshut-lâi(凸出來).

**juvenile**, hãu-sêⁿ(後生); siàu-nîⁿ(少年).

### K

**keep**, siú(守); thóiⁿ-siú(睇守); thóiⁿ-kù(睇顧); khùaⁿ-kù(看顧); lâu(留); tshûn(賰); lâu--pàng-kò(留放塊); sīn--pàng-kò(剩放塊). *off the sun*, chia-ji̍t(遮日). *silence*, khiâm-kháu(緘口); m̄-khui-tshùi(毋開喙); tshùi kueⁿ-miⁿ(喙關麵); tiām-tiām(恬恬); chẽⁿ-chẽⁿ(靜靜); tiām-tiām mi̍t-mi̍t(恬恬密密). *in order*, kúan(管); kúan-sok(管束); iak-sok(約束). *rules*, siú-huap(守法); ha̍h-huap(合法). *the watch*, siú-keⁿ(守更). *the new year*, kùe-nîⁿ(過年); tsò-kùe-nîⁿ(做過年). *a feast*, tsò-tsoih(做節). *for oneself*, ka-kī-ēng(家己用). *one's word*, siú-ieh(守約); chiè-ieh(照約); zû-ieh(如約). *keepsake*, lâu-ì(留意); kìⁿ-mue̍h sṳ-nâng(見物思人[訓]); piáu-chhêng tshûn-kì(表情存記).

**kernel**, hu̍t(核); jîn(仁); chí(子). *of grain*, chhek-lia̍p(粟粒).

**kettle**, thih-ue(鐵鍋); seⁿ-ue(鍟鍋). *tea*, tê-ue(茶鍋).

**key**, só-sî(鎖匙). *hole*, só-sî-mn̂g(鎖匙門); só-sî-khang(鎖匙空).

**kick**, that(踢).

**kid**, suaⁿ-iêⁿ-kiáⁿ(山羊囝).

**kidnap**, kúai-tô(偷逃); thau-kúai-tô(偷拐逃); thau-tshūa(偷𤆬); thau-kiau(偷邀); thau-phõ(偷抱); thau-kāng〔〕.

**kidney**, lãi-siẽn(內腎); siẽn-chí(腎子); ie-chí(腰子).

**kill**, suah(殺); thâi(刣); phah-sí(拍死); suah-hāi(殺害).

**kiln**, *brick*, sie-tsng-iê(燒磚窯).

**kin**, chhin-chiâⁿ(親情); chhin-chhek(親戚); chhin-nâng(親人).

**kind**, hó-sim(好心); tshṳ̂(慈); un-hûa(溫和); khuan-kãu(寬厚); chhin-kãu(親厚); chhin-jie̍t(親熱); ũ-ṳn-chhêng(有恩情); ũ-jîn-ài(有仁愛). *kindness*, ṳn-hũi(恩惠); nâng-chhêng(人情). *receive*, niáⁿ-nâng-chhêng(領人[訓]情). *bestow*, tsò-nâng-chhêng(做人[訓]情). *beseech*, khí-nâng-chhêng(起人[訓]情); khṳ́n-nâng-chhêng(懇人[訓]情). *a kind*, lūi(類); iēⁿ(樣); sek(式); khí(起); chéng(種); so̍k(屬); téng(等); hō(號).

**kindle**, *fire*, khí-húe(起火); to̍h-húe(着火); niám-to̍h-húe(黏着火); tiám-to̍h(點着). *kindlings (tinder)*, húe-hiāⁿ(火艾).

**king**, uâng(王); kun-uâng(君王); kok-kun(國君); jîn-kun(仁君). *kingfisher*, kim-sai-chiáu(金絲鳥). *king-crab*, hāu(侯). *kingdom*, kok(國); pang-kok(邦國); pang(邦).

**kiss**, chim(斟); sie-chim(相斟). *(the mouth)*, chim-tshùi(斟喙). *(the cheek)*, chim-kih-kau(斟頰交).

**kitchen**, húe-si̍t-pâng(伙食房); húe-si̍t-koiⁿ(伙食間); tôu-pâng(廚房). *garden*, tshài-hn̂g(菜園).

**kite**, huang-khîm(風禽); tsúa-iē(紙鳶). *to fly a*, pàng-huang-khîm(放風禽).

**kitten**, ngiau-kiáⁿ(貓囝).

**knave**, láu-kiáⁿ(老囝); kuang-kùn(光棍); kùn-thû(棍徒); tsha̍t-kiáⁿ(賊囝); àu-nâng〔〕; nâng-tái(人歹).

**knead**, chhi̍p-mīⁿ〔〕. *kneading-trough*, chhi̍p-mīⁿ-tsô〔〕.

**knee**, kha-thâu-u(骹頭趺). *bend*, kha khek(骹曲); khek-kha(屈骹); kũiⁿ kha-thâu-u(跪骹頭宇); tá-chhiam(打韱). *knee-cap*, kha-thâu-u-chîⁿ(骹頭烏錢).

**kneel**, kũiⁿ(跪); kũi(跪); kũi--lo̍h-khṳ̀(跪落去); kiâⁿ-tōa-lói(行大禮). *with one knee*, kũi che̍k-chiah-kha(跪一隻骹).

**knife**, to(刀). *small*, to-kiáⁿ(刀囝). *one*, che̍k-ki-to(一刀刀). *knives and forks*, to-chhe(刀叉). *mincing-knife*, pang-to(板刀).

**knit**, *stockings*, chit-bu̍eh(織襪); kit-bu̍eh(結襪). *the eyebrows*, niàuⁿ-bâi(釀眉); bâi-thâu kat-kat(眉頭結結); bâi-thâu tièⁿ-tshok-tshok(眉頭張蹙蹙).

**knob**, *a*, che̍k-lia̍p-tsu(一粒珠).

**knock**, *at door*, phah-mn̂g(拍門); khà-mn̂g(扣門). *the head on ground*, khàu-thâu(叩頭); kha̍p-thâu(磕頭). *one down*, phah i pua̍h-lo̍h thôu-ẽ(拍伊跋落塗下). *knocker*, mn̂g-huân(門環).

**knot**, *in wood*, tshâ-ma̍k(柴目). *on rope*, khat-thâu(結頭). *to tie*, thám-khat〔〕; kat kâi-khat(結个刻). *two kinds of knot*, sí-khat(死結); ua̍h-khat(活結). *unloose*, kói-khat(解結).

**know**, tsai(知); pat(捌); hiáu(曉); thong(通). *I know him*, uá pat i(我捌伊). *do you know (recognize) me*, lṳ́ pat-tò-jīn uá, mé(汝識倒認我咩). *knowledge*, kièn-sek(見識); tì-hũi(智慧). *knowledge (learning)*, ha̍k-mn̄g(學問).

**knuckle**, tsóiⁿ-tsat(指節); tsóiⁿ-ma̍k(指目).

### L

**label**, hō-phiâu(號票); jī-hō(字號); gūa-phiâu(外票); thiap-ma̍k(貼目).

**labour**, lâu-sim(勞心); lâu-la̍t(勞力); ēng-kang(用工); bûa-lâu(磨勞); bûa-la̍t(磨力); lâu-khóu(勞苦). *day-labourer*, chhiẽⁿ-kòu(上僱). *in labour*, lîm-phûn(臨盆); àiⁿ-seⁿ-kiáⁿ(愛生囝); hun-mién(分娩). *difficult*, seⁿ-m̄-tshut(生毋出); lân-súaⁿ(難產); nge̍k-súaⁿ(逆產).

**lace**, mãng-se(網紗). *gold*, kim-si-tòa(金絲帶).

**lacquer**, iû-tshat(油漆); tshat(漆).

**lad**, nôuⁿ-kiáⁿ(孥囝); hãu-seⁿ-kiáⁿ(後生囝).

**ladder**, thui(梯); lâu-thui(樓梯). *one*, che̍k-tieⁿ-thui(一張梯). *steps of*, thui-chí(梯指); thui-kèⁿ(梯勁). *go up*, chiẽⁿ-thui(上梯); peh-chiẽⁿ-thui(百上梯).

**ladle**, tsúi-kóng(水管); khat-kóng(刻管). *use*, ēng-kóng lâi-ié-tsúi(用管來舀水).

**lady**, a-niêⁿ(阿娘); niêⁿ-niêⁿ(阿奶); a-náiⁿ(阿奶). *(wife of mandarin)*, thài-thài(阿奶). *(still higher)*, hu-jîn(夫人).

**lag**, *behind*, lo̍h-ãu(落後); tùe-m̄-tie̍h(綴毋着); m̄-chìn-tsôiⁿ(毋進前).

**lake**, ôu(湖); chek-tsúi-ôu(澤水湖).

**lamb**, iêⁿ-kiáⁿ(羊囝); mîⁿ-iêⁿ-kiáⁿ(棉羊囝). *unborn lambs, sometimes eaten*, iêⁿ-tho(羊胎).

**lame**, kuái-kha(拐骹). *(less severe)*, hièn-kha(獻骹). *walk*, kiâⁿ-lōu kuái-a-kuái(行路拐阿拐).

**lament**, khàu(哭); ai-khàu(哀哭); tháu-khùi(㪗氣); hûan-ló(煩惱). *lamentable*, khó-sieh(可惜); khó-liên(可憐); chhi-tshám(淒慘); chhi-liâng(淒凉).

**lamp**, teng(燈); teng-chhiū(燈樹); teng-khêng(燈檠); teng-húe(燈火). *hanging*, tiàu-teng(吊燈). *hand-lamp*, chhiú-teng(手燈). *lamp-light*, teng-ẽ(燈下). *lamp-wick*, teng-sim(燈心). *to light*, tiám-teng(點燈); liám-teng(斂燈); chiẽⁿ-teng(上燈); khui-teng(開燈). *blow out*, pûn-kùe(歕過); tshue--kùe(吹過); lâu--khí(留起).

**lampoon**, bô-thâu-thiap(無頭帖); ki-chhiáu(機俏).

**lance**, chhieⁿ(槍). *lancet*, khui-tshng-to(開倉刀).

**land**, tī(地); suaⁿ(山); tshân-hn̂g(田園). *land from a boat*, chiẽⁿ-suaⁿ(上山); khí-tsúi(起水). *on land*, suaⁿ-téng(山頂). *pay land tax*, uân-niêⁿ(完糧); na̍p-niêⁿ(納糧). *owner of*, tshân-tsú(田主). *landing-place*, lōu-thâu(路頭).

**landlord**, tshâi-tsú(財主). *(of house)*, tshù-tsú(厝主). *(of land)*, tshân-tsú(田主). *(of inn)*, tiàm-tsú(厝主); tiàm-ke(厝主).

**landmark**, tī-kài(地界); kài-chie̍h(界石); chie̍h-pi(石碑); tī-kài-pi(地界碑). *to look out for landmarks when at sea*, thóiⁿ-suaⁿ-mn̂g(睇山門); kam-suaⁿ-mn̂g(監山門); jīn-suaⁿ-thâu(認山頭).

**landscape**, kuang-kéng(光景). *to paint*, ūe-kéng-tī(畫景緻); ūe-suaⁿ-tsúi(畫山水).

**lane**, hāng(巷). *a*, che̍k-tiâu-hāng(一條巷).

**language**, ūe(話); ūe-kù(話句); ngân-gṳ́(言語); thóu-thâm(土談); im-gṳ́(音語). *written*, bûn-jī(文字). see COLLOQUIAL.

**languid**, khùn-tõaⁿ(睏緩); phî-kũan(疲倦); bô-cheng-sîn(無精神); bô-sîn-khì(無神氣).

**lank**, bô-mih-ne̍k(無乜肉); sán(㾪); kut-thâu khià-khià(骨頭騎騎).

**lantern**, teng-lâng(燈籠); po-lî-teng(玻璃燈). *to carry (with rod attached)*, khiâ-teng-lâng(擎燈籠). *to carry (hanging from the hand)* ,kũaⁿ-teng-lâng(摜燈籠). *hang many lanterns for congratulation*, tiàu-teng(吊燈). *on high bamboos, when in trouble*, chiẽⁿ-thiⁿ-teng(上天燈). *ornamental, in street*, chiẽⁿ-teng-tû(上燈櫥). *carry after the idols*, iâⁿ-teng(迎燈). *feast of lanterns*, ngûan-siau-mêⁿ(元宵夜).

**lap**, *sit in one's*, tsõ tõ-kha--thâu(坐在骹頭).

**lard**, tṳ-lâ(豬朥); tṳ-iû(豬油). *to melt*, luah-lâ(烙朥). *to fry in lard*, chien-lâ(煎朥).

**large**, tōa(舵); khuah-tōa(闊大); kûiⁿ-tōa(懸大); tōa-bó-kâi(大母个); lō-ho〔〕. *large-hearted*, hái-liãng(海量); liãng-tōu khuan-khuah(度量寬闊).

**largess**, siéⁿ-mue̍h(賞物); khèng-siéⁿ(慶賞); tãi-siéⁿ(大賞); pù-si(佈施); pù-sì(佈施). *(to soldiers)*, khàu-siéⁿ(犒賞).

**lark**, peh-lêng-chiáu(百靈鳥).

**larva**, thâng-nñg(蟲卵); thâng-kóiⁿ(蟲捲); tshṳ(蛆).

**larynx**, âu-lêng(喉嚨); ngẽ-âu(硬喉); âu-lâng-kńg(喉籠管).

**lascivious**, tham-sek(貪色); phiâu(嫖); tham-îm(貪淫).

**lash**, piⁿ(鞭). *to*, tsang-piⁿ phah(將鞭拍); piⁿ-phah(鞭拍).

**lassitude**, khùn-tõaⁿ(睏惰); kũan-tõaⁿ(倦惰); phî-kũan(疲倦); bô-cheng-sîn(無精神).

**last**, suah-búe(煞尾); kiáu-búe(繳尾); mua̍t(末). *night*, tsa-mêⁿ(昨夜); tsa-mêⁿ-àm(昨夜暗). *month*, chiēⁿ-kâi-gue̍h(上個月). *year*, kū-nîⁿ(舊年); khṳ̀-nîⁿ(去年); úang-nîⁿ(往年). *month*, chiēⁿ-kâi-gue̍h(上個月). *at last*, kiáu-búe(繳尾); búe-búe(尾尾). *from first to last*, tsṳ̃-sí kàu-tsong(自始到終); tshông-thâu kàu-búe(從頭到尾). *first and last the same*, sí-tsong zû-it(始終如一). *the last day*, mua̍t-ji̍t(末日). *breathe one's last*, khùi tñg(氣斷).

**last**, *to*, nãiⁿ(耐); nãiⁿ-kú(耐久); tōiⁿ(𠕆). *lasting well*, õi-nãiⁿ(會耐).

**last**, *shoe*, ôi-hùn(鞋楦).

**lastings**, ú-lêng(有綾); ú-môⁿ(羽毛); ú-tn̄g(有長); ú-se(羽紗).

**latch**, ie̍h-kúi(藥鬼).

**latchet**, ôi-tòa(鞋帶).

**late**, mān(慢); ùaⁿ(晏); chhî(遲). *too*, khah-mān(較慢); kùe-ùaⁿ(過晏). *in day*, ji̍t ùaⁿ(日晏); ji̍t àm(日暗). *in the night*, keⁿ chhim(更深). *my late father*, uá kâi-soiⁿ-kháu(我个先考); uá kâi-soiⁿ-hũ(我个先父). *my late grandfather*, uá kâi-tsóu-kháu(我个祖考). *your late father*, soiⁿ-tsun(先尊). *too late for dinner*, hù-m̄-tie̍h chia̍h(赴毋着食).

**lately**, chí-kṳ̃n-sî(此近時); chí-kṳ̃n-ji̍t(此近日); kṳ̃n-ji̍t(近日); kúi-ji̍t-tsôiⁿ(幾日前); sù-ji̍t-tsôiⁿ(數日前); soiⁿ sù-ji̍t(先數日); būe-kú(未久); soiⁿ-bô-kú(先無久).

**lathe**, chhia-pûaⁿ(車盤); chhia-tshn̂g(車廠).

**latitude**, tī-hūi-tōu(地緯度).

**lattice**, hõng-ngán-theng(鳳眼窗).

**laudable**, hó-o-ló(好呵咾); kham-kai hó-o-ló(堪該好呵咾).

**laugh**, chhiè(笑). *laugh aloud*, hā-hā-chhiè(哈哈笑); chhiè kàu hā-hā-kiè(笑到哈哈叫). *with mouth wide open*, chhiè kàu tshùi li̍h-li̍h(笑到喙裂裂). *laugh till one can laugh no more*, tâng-õi-chhiè(同會笑), chhiè kàu-bõi-chhiè(笑到袂笑). *pot laughing at kettle (literally, bed-bug laughing at tree-bug)*, ba̍t-sat chhiè chie̍h-pūi(密虱笑石吠). *laughable*, hó-chhiè(好笑); khó-chhiè(可笑).

**launch**, tsûn pàng-lo̍h-tsúi(船放落水). *steam-launch*, húe-tsûn-kiáⁿ(火船囝).

**lavender**, *water*, hue-lōu-tsúi(花露水).

**lavish**, lâng-hùi(浪費); hṳ̂-hùi(魚費); phah-phún-sái(拍糞使); chhia-chhíⁿ(奢侈); chhia-hûa(奢華).

**law**, huap(法); lu̍t-huap(法律); lu̍t-lī(律例); huap-tōu(法度). *keep*, siú-huap(守法). *break*, huãm-huap(犯法). *lawful*, ha̍h-huap(合法). *lawless*, bô-huap(無法); nge̍k-huap(逆法).

**lawsuit**, kuaⁿ-si(官司). *to have a*, phah-kuaⁿ-si(拍官司); sie-kò(相告).

**lawyer**, *(confidential adviser of mandarin)*, sṳ-iâ(師爺). *(one who writes legal documents)*, sõng-sṳ(訟師).

**lawn**, *a*, tsháu-tiêⁿ(草場); tsháu-pou(草埔).

**lax**, khah-khuan(較寬); thài-khuan(太寬); pàng-sang(放鬆); khah-khuaⁿ(較款).

**lay**, *down*, pàng(放). *oneself down*, tó(倒); khùa-ie(掛腰); khiau-ie(翹腰); gu̍t--lo̍h-khṳ̀(夗落去). *on top*, tha̍h-tõ-téng(疊在頂); thia̍p-tõ-téng(叠在頂). *by*, khǹg-bûa(囥埋); siu-bûa(收埋); siu-khṳ̀-khǹg(收去囥). *aside*, pàng-khui(放開); tṳ̂-khṳ̀(除去). *out*, phou-pâi(鋪排); pâi-pí(排比). *eggs*, seⁿ-nñg(生卵). *the table*, pâi-toh(排桌); pái-tshn̂g(擺床); pái-ti̍h toh-sia̍h(擺碟桌席). *on colour*, tsng-sek(裝飾); tsuang-sek(裝飾). *lay out money*, sái-chîⁿ(使錢). *hands on*, àn-chhiú(按手); hūaⁿ-chhiú(焊手). *hands on (seize)*, lia̍h(掠).

**layer**, *three*, saⁿ-têng(三重); saⁿ-în(三鉛). *in layers*, che̍k-têng che̍k-têng(一重一重).

**lazy**, tõaⁿ(惰); lán-tõaⁿ(懶惰); iû-chhiú hàuⁿ-ôiⁿ(遊手好閒).

**lead**, în(鉛). *pencil*, în-pit(鉛筆). *weights*, tô-chí(逃此); în-thūi(鉛墜). *white*, în-hún(鉛粉). *pour in lead*, kùan-în(罐鉛).

**lead**, *to*, ín(引); khan(牽); tshūa(𤆬); kiau(嬌); tòa(住). *leader*, niáⁿ-thâu(領頭); thâu-ma̍k(頭目); tsóng-tòa(總帶).

**leaf**, *of tree*, chhiū-hie̍h(樹葉). *book*, chheh-hie̍h(冊頁). *turn over leaves of book*, chheh-hie̍h iãuⁿ--kùe-lâi(冊頁掀過來); chheh-hie̍h hien--kùe-lâi(冊頁掀過來). *of door*, sìⁿ(扇); pôiⁿ(爿); phìⁿ(片). *double leaved door*, sang-phìⁿ-mn̂g(雙片門). *gold-leaf*, kim-po̍h(金薄).

**league**, mêng-ieh(盟約).

**leak**, lāu(漏). *mend a*, lia̍h-lāu(掠漏); póu-lāu(補漏).

**lean**, *to*, úa(倚); khùa(掛).

**lean**, sán(㾪); sòu(瘦); sán-sòu(㾪瘦); bô-ne̍k(無肉).

**leap**, thiàu(跳); thiàu--khí-lâi(跳起來). *on one, as tiger*, tà--khí-lâi(打起來); teng--khí-lâi(燈起來). *leap-frog*, thiàu-it-tshṳ́(跳一此).

**learn**, o̍h(學); ha̍k-si̍p(學習); liēn-si̍p(練習). *by heart*, tha̍k kàu-õi-liām(讀到會唸); tha̍k kàu-pat-liām(讀到識唸); tha̍k-se̍k(讀熟). *writing*, o̍h-siá-jī(學寫字). *learned*, phak-ha̍k(伏學); ũ-ha̍k-mn̄g(有學問); ha̍k-mn̄g chhim(學問深); chhim-phak(深伏); pá-ha̍k(飽學). *learning*, ha̍k-mn̄g(學問).

**lease**, *to*, sùe(稅); tsou-sùe(租稅). *a written*, khòi(契).

**least**, siãng-sòi(上細); tsùe-sòi(最細); tsùe-mûiⁿ(最微). *in the least*, hâu-lî(毫厘); sut-kiáⁿ(屑囝); se-su-kiáⁿ(些須囝). *not in the least*, pẽng-bô(並無); bô che̍k-sut-kiáⁿ(無一屑囝). *at the very least*, siãng-kiám(上減).

**leather**, phûe(皮); se̍k-phûe(熟皮). *to dress*, se̍k-phûe(熟皮). *shoes*, phûe-ôi(皮鞋).

**leave**, lī(離); lī-khui(離開); lī-pie̍t(離別); sie-pie̍t(相別). *off*, kài(戒); keh(隔); kói(改); hiah(歇). *to take*, sî-pie̍t(辭別); chiãm-pie̍t(暫別). *behind*, pàng-tiāu(放掉); ka-lau̍h(交落); khì-tiāu(棄掉). *behind (at death)*, zũi-lo̍h(遺落). *loath to leave*, siá-m̄-tit(捨毋得); siá put-tit-khṳ̀(捨不得去). *leavings*, só-tshûn(所賰).

**leaven**, kàⁿ-bó(酵母). *to leaven*, lo̍h-kàⁿ(落酵); khí-kàⁿ(起酵); phû-kàⁿ(浮酵); huat-kàⁿ(發酵).

**lecture**, sueh-tsṳ(說書); káng-tsṳ(講書); káng-tãu(講道).

**ledger**, tsóng-phõu(總簿).

**lee**, *side*, huang-ẽ-pôiⁿ(風下爿). *make leeway under sail*, kài(界).

**lees**, tsau(糟); tái(歹).

**leech**, hôu-khî(蜈蜞).

**leek**, kú-tshài(韭菜). *flowers of*, kú-tshài-hue(韭菜花).

**left**, *side*, tsó-pôiⁿ(左爿). *hand*, tsó-chhiú(左手); tò-chhiú(倒手). *over*, tshûn(賰); sīn(剩).

**leg**, kha(骹). *one*, che̍k-chiah-kha(一隻骹). *of mutton*, iêⁿ-thúi(羊腿).

**legacy**, zũi-ngia̍p(遺業); zũi-chîⁿ(遺錢).

**legal**, ha̍h-huap(合法); lu̍t-huap só-tsún(法律所準).

**legend**, kóu-thûan(古傳). *(written)*, kóu-tn̄g(古傳). *fabulous*, huang-thâng(荒唐).

**legerdemain**, tsò-pá-hì(做飽戲); tsò-pa-hì(做爸戲); tsò-hì-su̍t(做戲術); tién-chhiú-huap(典手法); chia-ngán-huap(遮眼法).

**leggings**, khòu-thúi(褲腿); khòu-thàu(褲套).

**legible**, hó-tha̍k(好讀); jī hīn-hīn(字現現); jī thóiⁿ-tit-tshut(字睇得出).

**legume**, tāu(豆).

**leisure**, ôiⁿ(閒); bô-sṳ̄(無事); chheng-ôiⁿ(清閒). *leisurely*, mān-mān(慢慢).

**lend**, chieh(借); chieh--pun-nâng(借分人[訓]). *money on interest*, seⁿ-chîⁿ(生錢). *lender*, tièⁿ-tsú(帳主); pàng-tièⁿ(放帳).

**leopard**, pà(豹).

**leprosy**, thái-ko(癩哥); tōa-huang(大風); mûaⁿ-huang(麻風).

**less**, kiám(減); kèng-chié(更少); m̄-kàu(毋夠). *make*, tṳ̂-kiám(除減). *become*, siau-si̍h(消蝕).

**lesson**, *say*, liām che̍k-hûe-tsṳ(念冊會書). *take a lesson from anything*, tsṳ̄-kéng(事境).

**lest**, mién(免); sái-kàu-mín(使到免); khióng-ùi(恐畏); khióng-phàⁿ(恐怕); kiaⁿ-ùi(驚畏); ṳ̃-hûang(預防); ṳ̃-mín(預免).

**let**, hṳ́(許); ṳ́(予); hàuⁿ(好); tsún(準). *a house*, sùe-tshù pun nâng(稅厝分人). *into*, ji̍p(入). *down*, pàng-lo̍h(放落). *go*, pàng(放). *me see*, pun-uá-thóiⁿ(分我睇). *let us go*, lâi-khṳ̀(來去). *let him do it*, thèng-i khṳ̀-tsò(聽伊去做); kui-i khṳ̀-tsò(歸伊去做); thãi-i khṳ̀-tsò(待伊去做). *off a gun*, pàng-phàu(放砲); khui-chhèng(開銃). *off crackers*, phah-phòng-phiẽ(拍碰鰾). *let not one remain*, màiⁿ-tshûn che̍k-kâi(勿賰一個). *let the request be granted*, tsún i-só-khiû(准伊所求). *let alone*, chhiú màiⁿ-thãng(手勿動); kṳ̀-i-khṳ̀〔〕.

**letter**, sìn(信); tsṳ-sìn(書信); phoi-sìn(批信). *one*, che̍k-tieⁿ-jī(冊張字); che̍k-kò-sìn(冊個信); che̍k-huang-sìn(冊方信). *to send*, kià-phoi(寄批); kià-sìn(寄信). *letters*, jī(字). *of alphabet*, jī-bó(字母). *a man of*, ũ-ha̍k-mn̄g(有學問).

**lettuce**, chheⁿ-tshài(生菜).

**leucorrhoea**, pāi-pe̍h(敗白); pe̍h-tòa(白帶).

**levee**, chhiâu-kìⁿ(朝見).

**lever**, thih-chhiâng(鐵鍁); phûe-chhiâng〔〕.

**levy**, *taxes*, thiu-sùe(抽稅); siu-niêⁿ(收糧); tui-niêⁿ(催糧). *troops*, khí-piaⁿ(起兵); tiãu-piaⁿ(調兵); teng-piaⁿ(徵兵).

**lewd**, siâ(畲); îm(淫); hàuⁿ-sek(好色).

**lexicon**, jī-tién(字典). *(small)*, jī-lūi(字類).

**libation**, kuàn-tī(灌地).

**libel**, bô-thâu-thiap(無頭帖). *to*, ka̍k-thiap-kiáⁿ(覺帖囝); tah-thiap-kiáⁿ(貼帖囝).

**liberal**, khuan-hông tãi-liãng(寬宏大量); lêng-iông-nâng(能容人); ũ-tōu-liãng(有度量). *with money*, khang-khài(慷慨); tōa-khang tōa-khài(大慷大慨); khuang-khài(慷慨).

**liberate**, pàng(放); sek-pàng(釋放); pàng-i-khṳ̀(放伊去). *liberty*, tsṳ̃-tsú(自主); tsṳ̃-lí(自理); tsṳ̃-iû(自由). *you are at liberty*, sûi-lṳ́ tsú-ì(隨汝主意); bô-nâng khu-sok(無人約束).

**libidinous**, tham-sek(貪色); hàuⁿ-phiâu(好嫖); îm-io̍k(淫慾).

**library**, tsṳ-pâng(書房).

**license**, *give a*, tshut-pâi(出牌). *take out*, niáⁿ-pâi(領牌); sùe-pâi(歲牌).

**licentious**, kùe-tōu(過度); siâ-phiah(邪僻); bô-huap-tōu(無法度); huàng-ûi zuãn-tsò(放違任做).

**lichen**, chheⁿ-thî(青苔); chheⁿ-thai(青苔); chhiêⁿ-thai(牆苔); chhiêⁿ-i(牆衣).

**lichi**, nôiⁿ-kúeⁿ(荔卷). *dried*, nôiⁿ-kúeⁿ-kuaⁿ(荔卷官).

**lick**, chĩ(舐). *the old cow licks its calf*, lãu-gû chĩ-tok(老牛舐督).

**lid**, khàm(蓋). *of pot*, ue-kùa(鍋蓋). *of frying-pan*, tiáⁿ-khàm(鼎蓋).

**lie**, tàⁿ-ké-ūe(呾假話); tàⁿ-ké(呾假); pe̍h-chia̍h pe̍h-tàⁿ(白食白呾); sueh-huáng(說謊); tàⁿ hṳ-ké kai-ūe(呾虛假該話). *a lie*, pe̍h-chiáⁿ-ūe(白䭕話); tōa-ūe(大話); hṳ-ké(虛假); huang-thâng(荒唐); bô-iáⁿ-ūe(無影話); bô-iaⁿ bô-chiah kâi-ūe(無影無跡个話).

**lie**, *down*, tó--loo̍h-khṳ̀ gu̍t(倒落去夗). *with*, tsò-pû-gu̍t(做包夗). *in ambush*, mâiⁿ-ho̍k(埋伏); bih-tiām(覕恬); bih-bûa(覕埋).

**lieutenant**, *lieutenant-governor*, bú-īⁿ(撫院); bú-thâi(武臺).

**life**, miāⁿ(命); sèⁿ-miāⁿ(性命). *present*, kim-sì(今世); tõ-seⁿ(在生); seⁿ-tsôiⁿ(生前). *future*, lâi-seⁿ(來生); sí-ãu(死後). *life and death*, seⁿ-sí(生死). *life-time*, che̍k-sì-nâng(一世人[訓]); che̍k-seⁿ-nâng(一生人[訓]); tsong-sin(終身). *all one's life-time*, chĩn-che̍k-sì(盡一世). *regardless of life*, m̄-kù-miāⁿ(毋顧命); m̄-kù sèⁿ-miāⁿ(毋顧性命). *lifeless*, bõi-ua̍h(袂活); sí--liáu(死了); pùaⁿ-seⁿ pùaⁿ-sí(半生半死). *to see life*, kìⁿ--kùe sì-chhêng(見過四情). *take life*, suah-miāⁿ(殺命). *long*, tn̂g-miāⁿ(長命); tn̂g-siū(長壽).

**lift**, khie̍h-khí(挈起); khie̍h-phû(挈浮); hû-phû(扶浮); hû-khí(扶起); kng-phû(扛浮); kiah(揭). *a screen*, hien-liâm(掀帘); kiah-liâm(揭帘). *one's clothes*, piáu-phû〔〕; tsah-phû〔〕; túi-phû(拖浮). *the head*, thâu-khak tièⁿ-taⁿ(頭殼脹擔). *with lever*, kiãu-phû(撬浮); kiãu-khí(撬起). *off a lid*, iãuⁿ-khàm〔〕; khàm iãuⁿ-phû〔〕. *up a child*, phõ--khí-lâi(抱起來).

**light**, kng(光); kuang(光); kuang-mêng(光明). *of sun*, ji̍t-kng(日光). *a lamp*, liám-húe(斂火); tiám-húe(點火), liám-teng(斂燈); tiám-teng(點燈); chiẽⁿ-teng(上燈). *a fire*, khí-húe(起火); to̍h-húe(着火). *light-house*, teng-lâu(燈樓); teng-thah(燈塔). *come to light*, huat-tsoh(發作).

**light**, *in weight*, khin(輕). *light and easy*, khin-kōi(輕易). *clothing*, chhēng-po̍h(穿薄). *wind*, huang khin(風輕); huang-kiáⁿ li-li(風囝哩哩). *in colour*, chhién-sek(淺色); sek chhién-tãⁿ(色淺淡). *light-fingered*, saⁿ-chiah-chhiú(三隻手). *lighten*, pûaⁿ-khin(盤輕); phêⁿ-kiám(彭減). *to lighter*, poh-hùe(駁貨). *make light of anyone*, thóiⁿ-khin(睇輕); thóiⁿ-m̄-chiẽⁿ-ma̍k(睇毋上目); lia̍h-tsūaⁿ(掠賤); khin-buãn(輕慢); bú-buãn(侮慢).

**lightning**, tiẽn-húe(電火); lûi-húe(雷火). *it lightens*, lûi-kong nihⁿ-ma̍k(雷公忍目); tiẽn-húe ia̍p-ia̍p-sih(電火爍爍熠).

**like**, chhin-chhiẽⁿ(親像); húang-sṳ̃(仿似); siang-sṳ̃(相似); kṳ̃n-sṳ(近似); siãu(肖); tâng(同); tshah-chhi̍h chhin-chhiẽⁿ〔〕. *it is like(simile)*, chhin-chhiẽⁿ(親像); khó-pí(可比); phì-zû(譬如); tǹg--kùe(當過); hāi--kùe(害過). *do like him*, o̍h i-kâi-iēⁿ(學伊个樣); uàⁿ i-kâi-iēⁿ(換伊个樣); hãu i-kâi-iēⁿ(效伊个樣). *make, it like this*, chiè chí-kâi-iēⁿ tsò(照此個樣做).

**like**, *to*, hàuⁿ(好); ngũan(願); kam-ngũan(甘願); chhêng-ngũan(情願); tèng-ì(中意); ha̍h-ì(合意); zûi-ì(隨意); sieh(惜).

**lounge**, ôiⁿ-iû(閒游); ôiⁿ-sin(閒身); ôiⁿ-u̍t(閒夗); chheng-sũi(清閒); ôiⁿ-mîn(閒眠); tham-tõaⁿ(貪惰).

**love**, *to love*, ài(愛); ài-sieh(愛惜); thóng-ài(寵愛); siang-ài(相愛). *to love (and respect)*, kèng-ài(敬愛). *(substantive)*, jîn-ài(仁愛); chhêng-ài(情愛); ṳn-ài(恩愛). *love blindly and over-indulge*, ne̍k-ài(肉愛). *beloved*, tit-nâng-sieh(得人[訓]惜); tit-tóng(得懂). *lovely*, khó-ài(可愛). *love-letter (bad meaning)*, chhêng-tsṳ(情姿). *love-sick*, chie-si-pēⁿ(蕉司病); siang-sṳ-pēⁿ(相思病); siang-sṳ-pĩn(相思品); ou-âng-pēⁿ(烏紅病). *love virtue*, hàuⁿ-siẽn(好善); la̍k-siẽn hàuⁿ-tek(六善好德).

**low**, kẽ(下). *low in stature*, ói(矮); kẽ-kẽ(下下); ói-sòi(矮細). *high and low*, kûiⁿ-kẽ(懸下); kau-ti(高低). *low water*, tsúi khó(水可); tsúi ta(水灱); lâu khó-ta-ta(流可灱灱). *low people*, hiã-pín(下品); hiã-tsūaⁿ(下賤). *low people (very mean)*, hiã-liû(下流). *voice*, sòi-siaⁿ(細聲). *reading in a low voice*, thiâm-ngîm chẽⁿ-tha̍k(恬吟靜讀).

**lower**, *to*, lo̍h(落); pàng-lo̍h(放落). *(as with rope)*, tūi-lo̍h(隊落). *sail*, hẽ-phâng(下帆); lo̍h-phâng(落帆); heh-phâng〔〕.

**lowly**, *in mind*, khiam-sùn(謙遜). *in rank*, pui-tsūaⁿ(卑賤). *lowlands*, phêng-nguân(平原).

**loyal**, tong-sim(中心); tong-ngĩ(忠義). *minister*, tong-chhîn(忠臣).

**luck**, tsãu-hùe(造化); hó-sî-ūn(好時運); huang-tsúi hó(風水好). *what luck of late*, kṳ̃n-sî kuang-kéng tsãi-seⁿ(近時光景在生). *lucky day*, kit-ji̍t(吉日); hó-ji̍t-chí(好日子); siãng-kit ji̍t(上吉日). *to choose such*, thóiⁿ-ji̍t(睇日); to̍h-ji̍t(擇日); siâng-to̍h kit-ji̍t(詳擇吉日). *how lucky*, tsãu-hùe(造化); hiau-hẽng(僥倖); hó-tshái(好彩).

**ludicrous**, hó-chhiè(好笑).

**luggage**, hêng-lí(行李); hêng-tsuang(行裝); pau-kó sieⁿ-láng(包稿傷囊).

**lukewarm**, lā-lûn-sie〔〕; un-un(溫溫). *in mind*, bô-néⁿ bô-zua̍h(無冷無熱); sim tãⁿ-tãⁿ(心淡淡).

**lumber**, tshâ-sāi(柴放); sam-sāi(杉放); tshâ-liāu(柴料). *to lumber up a place*, tìn-tiāu tī-hng(鎮掉地方); hũn-tsa̍p tī-hng(混雜地方).

**luminous**, õi-kng(會光); huat-kng(發光); hâu-kng(豪光); tâng-tâng-kng(銅銅光).

**lump**, *a*, che̍k-kò(一塊). *to lump or take together*, tsò-che̍k-ē(做蜀下). *in lumps*, chiâⁿ-kò(成塊); kit-chiâⁿ-kò(結成塊).

**lunatic**, tien-khuâng(癲狂); siáu(少); tùe-gu̍eh-siáu(綴月少). *(quiet)*, huat-tien(發癲). *(violent)*, huat-khuâng(發狂). 

**lunch**, tiám-sim(點心); chia̍h-ji̍t-tàu(食日晝); chia̍h-pùaⁿ-kùa(食半旰); chia̍h-tǹg-kiáⁿ(食當囝).

**lungs**, hùi(肺); phàⁿ-kuaⁿ(怕肝). *disease of*, hùi-pēⁿ(肺病); sieⁿ-hùi(傷肺); lãi-siang(內相); hṳ-sún(虛損). *inflammation of*, hùi-húe(肺火).

**lurk**, tiàm(坫); mâiⁿ-ho̍k tiàm-miⁿ(埋伏坫面); bih(覕); bih-bûa(覕埋).

**lust**, io̍k(慾); sṳ-io̍k(私慾); ne̍k-io̍k(肉慾); mu̍eh-io̍k(物慾); îm-io̍k(淫慾); sek-io̍h(色藥). *(fire of)*, io̍k-húe(慾火). *arouse lustful desire*, khí-io̍k(起慾); to̍h-io̍k(着慾). *lustful*, tham-io̍k(貪慾); tsòng-io̍k(縱慾); hàuⁿ-sek(好色); tham-îm(貪淫).

**lustre**, hâu-kng(豪光); ia̍p-ia̍p-sih(燿燿爍).

**lustring**, kìn(錦). *flowered*, hue-kìn(花錦).

**lute**, khîm(琴).

**luxuriant**, mõng-sẽng(茂盛); phò-phò〔〕; ap-ap〔〕.

**luxurious**, chhia-tsòng(奢縱); chhia-míⁿ(車麵); îm-i̍t(淫佚); kiau-la̍k(驕樂); chhia-îm(奢淫); hàuⁿ-chhia-hûa(好奢華).

**lye**, kiⁿ(鹼); kiⁿ-tsúi(鹼水).

### M

**Macao**, Má-káu(媽閣); ò-mn̂g(澳門).

**mace**, *one*, che̍k-chîⁿ-ngṳ̂n(冊錢銀). *one mace has ten candareens*, che̍k-chîⁿ ũ-tsa̍p-hun(冊錢有十分).

**macerate**, au(嘔); au-kauh(漚捲); lo̍h-khṳ̀-au(落去嘔); ùn-àu(醃嘔); chìm-kàu-àu(浸到嘔).

**mad**, siáu(少); tien-khûang(癲狂); huat-siáu(發痟); huat-tien(發癲); huat-khûang(發狂); sit-sim(失心); sim m̄-tiāⁿ(心毋定). *feign to be*, tèⁿ-tien tèⁿ-siáu(鎮癲鎮少). *dog*, siáu-káu(𤞚狗).

**madam**, a-niêⁿ(阿娘); a-náiⁿ(阿奶); thài-thài(太太); hu-jîn(夫人); niêⁿ-niêⁿ(娘娘).

**magazine**, khòu(庫); tshng-khòu(倉庫). *powder*, húe-ie̍h-ke̍k(火藥局); húe-ie̍h-khòu(火藥庫). *literary*, tsa̍p-lo̍k(雜錄).

**maggot**, thâng(蟲).

**magic**, huap-su̍t(法術); huap-la̍t(法力); siâ-su̍t(邪術); bû-su̍t(巫術). *magician*, su̍t-sṳ̃(術士); huap-sṳ̃(法士).

**magistrate**, kuaⁿ-hú(官府). *upright*, liâm-kuaⁿ(廉官); chheng-kuaⁿ(清官). *corrupt*, tham-kuaⁿ(貪官). *office of*, gê-mn̂g(衙門). *hall where he sits*, kong-tn̂g(公堂). *district magistrate*, kūiⁿ(縣); kūiⁿ-tsú(縣主).

**magnanimous**, ũ-tōu-liãng(有度量); kháng-khài(慷慨); hái-liãng(海量); liãng-tōu khuan-khuah(度量寬闊); sim-hêng khuan-khuah(心胸寬闊); sim-hêng khuah-tōa(心行闊大). *(long-suffering)*, khuan-iông(寬容).

**magnet**, hiap-chie̍h(恰石).

**magnificent**, tsun-iông(尊崇); tsun-tõng(尊重). *scenery*, khî-kéng(奇景).

**magnifying glass**, hién-mûiⁿ-kiàⁿ(顯微鏡).

**magpie**, kheh-chiáu(客鳥); hí-chiáu(喜鳥); hí-chhiak(喜雀).

**maid**, tsṳ-niêⁿ-kiáⁿ(諸娘囝); a-niêⁿ-kiáⁿ(阿娘囝). *house-maid*, chhiah-kha(赤骹). *house-maid (common term, but objectionable)*, tsáu-kúi(走鬼).

**mail**, *coat of*, chièn-kah(戰甲); thih-kah(鐵甲).

**main**, *in the*, tãi-lia̍k(大略); tãi-khài(大概); tãi-sì(大事). *mainland*, tōa-tī(大地). *mainmast*, tōa-ûi(大圍).

**maintain**, siú(守); tshûn(存); iáng(養); keng-kip nâng-chia̍h(供給人[訓]食); chhī(飼).

**maize**, i-bí-jîn(伊米仁); iùⁿ-múiⁿ-jîn(幼麵仁).

**majesty**, *his*, uâng-siãng(皇上); hûang-siãng(皇上). *your majesty*, pĩ-ẽ(被下). *of appearance*, ui-hong(威風); ui-ngiâm(威嚴); ui-hong lím-lím(威風凜凜); ui-lêng hek-hek(威靈赫赫). *put on majestic appearance*, tsak-ui(作威).

**majority**, tōa-pùaⁿ(大半); che̍k-tōa-ûe(一大半).

**make**, tsò(做); tsak(作); tsãu(造); tsõ(做). *one afraid*, phièn-i-kiaⁿ(騙伊驚); heh-i-kiaⁿ(嚇伊驚); hé-i-kiaⁿ(赫伊驚). *out a bill*, khui-toaⁿ(開單). *of wood*, tsang-tshâ tsò(將柴做); ēng-tshâ tsò(用柴做). *a bed*, siu-si̍p phou-kài(收拾鋪蓋); siu-si̍p mîn-tshn̂g(收拾民床). *up a deficiency*, póu-khueh(補缺). *a loss*, pûe(賠). *known*, thong-tsai(通知); pò-tsai(報知). *clothes*, thīⁿ-saⁿ(縫衫); tsò-saⁿ(做衫). *up one's mind*, li̍p-tsú-ì(立主意); li̍p-tiāⁿ tsú-ì(立定主意). *a bargain*, kat-ieh(結約); tiāⁿ-ieh(定約). *the mind easy*, pàng-sim(放心); uaⁿ-sim(安心). *verses*, tsò-si(做司). *music*, tsak-gau̍h(作樂). *a row*, kã-kã bó-jiáng(咬咬母讓); ki-kã-la-kiè(枝咬啦叫). *haste*, méⁿ--chē(猛些).

**Malacca**, Mûaⁿ-la̍k-kah(麻六甲).

**malady**, see DISEASE.

**male**, lâm(男); nâm(男); ta-pou(丈夫). *(beasts)*, kóu(牯). *(birds)*, kak(角); hiông(雄). *male and female*, nâm-nńg(男女); ta-pou tsṳ-niêⁿ(丈夫諸娘). *female and male*, im-iâng(陰陽). *female and male (beasts)*, phín-móuⁿ(牝牡). *female and male (birds)*, thsṳ̂-hiông(雌雄).

**malediction**, chiù-tsūa(咒誓); chiù-mēⁿ(咒罵).

**malevolent**, sim-kuaⁿ ak-ta̍k(心肝惡毒); sim-tn̂g ak-ta̍k(心腸惡毒); ta̍k-sim(毒心); ta̍k-tn̂g(毒腸); ak-ta̍k(惡毒); hiong-ak(兇惡); hiau-ak(梟惡).

**mamma**, *one's*, a-bó(阿母); bó-chhin(母親); a-âi〔〕; a-neⁿ(阿嬭). *in addressing*, a-neⁿ(阿嬭); a-bó(阿母); a-niêⁿ(阿娘). *Chinese often call their parents uncle and aunt when speaking of them.*

**mammon**, tshâi-sîn-iâ(財神爺); chiáu-tshâi-iâ(鳥財爺); tshâi-pe̍h(財白).

**man**, nâng(人). *a*, kâi-nâng(個人). *mankind*, nâng-lūi(人類); sì-jîn(四仁); sì-kan-nâng(四干人); sì--chiēⁿ kâi-nâng(世上个人[訓]). *an old*, lãu-nâng-ke(老人家). *bad*, ak-nâng(惡人); pháiⁿ-nâng(痞人[訓]). *reach manhood*, sêng-teng(成丁). *men (not including women)*, nâng-teng(人丁); lâm-teng(男丁). *how many men (or males)*, kúi-teng(鬼丁). *man-of-war*, piaⁿ-tsûn(兵船); chièn-tsûn(戰船). *manslaughter*, tshò-suah(錯殺); gōu-suah(誤殺).

**manacles**, chhiú-khàu(手銬); chhiú-kê(手枷).

**manage**, *a matter*, lí(理); phōiⁿ(辦); kuán-lí(管理); liāu-lí(料理); thiâu-lí(調理); thiâu-thiap(調貼). *a family*, tî-ke(治家); hūaⁿ-ke(捍家). *manager*, thâu-nâng(頭人); chiáng-sṳ̄(掌事); tsú-sṳ̄(主事); tsóng-lí(總理); tsóng-náuⁿ(總腦).
