**market**, chhĩ(市); hṳ(墟). *go to*, khṳ̀-chhĩ(去市); chiẽⁿ-chhĩ(上市); tàu-hṳ(鬥墟). *no market for it*, bōi-m̄-khṳ̀(賣毋去); bô-nâng khie̍h-tsáu(無人[訓]挈走); siau-m̄-khṳ̀(消毋去); sià-m̄-tshut(卸毋出). *dull*, chhĩ-chhêng néⁿ-tãⁿ(市情冷淡). *price*, chhĩ-kè(市價). *street*, koi-chhĩ(街市). *place*, hṳ-tiêⁿ(墟場). *town*, pou-thâu(埠頭); hṳ(墟). *basket*, chhĩ-nâⁿ(市籃). *boats*, hṳ-tsûn(墟船).

**marry**, tshūa(娶); tshūa-bóu(娶婦); tshūa-chhin(娶親); tshú-chhi(娶妻); tshūa-chhi(娶妻); tshūa-sin-niêⁿ(娶新娘); sin-hun(新婚); tì-ke(嫁家). *of woman*, kè(嫁); tshut-kè(出嫁); tshut-mn̂g(出門). *of woman (widow asking another husband)*, chie-jī-sài(招二婿). *of woman (parents of girl taking a husband for her into their own family)*, iáng-láu-sài(養老婿). *marriage*, hun-in(婚姻); sin-hun(新婚); ha̍h-hun(合婚); sêng-hun(成婚); kat-hun(結婚). *feast*, ha̍h-hun-toh(合婚桌). *portion*, tsng-liâm(妝奩); kè-tsng(嫁妝). *contract*, hun-tsṳ(婚書); hun-tsṳ-thiap(婚書帖). *give one's daughter in marriage*, kè--pun-nâng(嫁分人). *engage to be married*, see BETROTH. *marriageable*, kàu-kṳn-niéⁿ hó-kè--liáu(到斤兩好嫁了); kàu-lâu-tsúi(到流水); tá-tsang(打鬃); siu-thâu(梳頭). *not yet married (man)*, būe-chêng-tshūa(未曾娶). *not yet married (woman)*, būe-kùe-mn̂g(未過門).

**marrow**, kut-tshúe(骨髓).

**Mars**, húe-chheⁿ(火星).

**marsh**, kẽ-sip〔〕; tsúi-che̍k(水澤); làm-che̍k(坔澤); làm-sip(坔濕).

**martial**, *appearance*, bú-mãuⁿ(武貌); hó-han(好鼾). *exercises*, bú-gōi(武藝).

**martyr**, ũi-tãu tì-sí(謂道帝死); ũi-tãu tì-miāⁿ(謂道帝命); ũi-tãu siá-sin(謂道寫身).

**mask**, mīn-khak(面殼); mīn-bôu(面模); kúi-khak(鬼殼). *to put on an ugly mask*, kùa siáu-kúi-khak(掛小鬼殼).

**mason**, hue-kang sai-pẽ(花工司阜); thôu-kang sai-pẽ(塗工司阜); tsò-nîⁿ-tsúi(作灰工); nîⁿ-tsúi(作灰工).

**mass**, *of people*, nâng-mue̍h lāu-jie̍t(人[訓]物鬧熱).

**massacre**, tôu-lo̍k(屠戮); suah-lo̍k(殺戮); chĩn-tôu(盡屠); tshám-suah(慘殺); tshûng-kiâⁿ tu-lo̍k(存行豬戮).

**mast**, tsûn-ûi(船桅). *mainmast*, tōa-ûi(大圍). *foremast*, thâu-ûi(頭桅). *mizzen-mast*, búe-ûi(尾桅). *cut away*, tsám-tiāu-ûi(斬掉桅). *put up*, khiâ-ûi(騎桅). *take down*, siâ-ûi(斜桅); lo̍h-ûi(落桅).

**master**, tsú(主); tsú-jîn(主人); tshù-nâng(厝人); tong-ke(東家); tshâi-tsú(財主). *(used in Ch'ao-chow-foo only in bad sense)*, thâu-ke(頭家).

**mat**, chhie̍h(蓆). *rush*, tsháu-chhie̍h(草蓆). *bamboo*, bi̍h-chhie̍h(篾蓆); tek-chhie̍h(竹蓆). *rattan*, tîn-chhie̍h(藤蓆). *for sails*, chhie̍h-pau(蓆包). *cover of a boat*, phâng-kám(帆䃭). *shed*, phâng-chhiáng(帆廠). *spread a*, tshṳ-tsháu-chhie̍h(舒草蓆).

**match**, húe-lêng(火龍); húe-hiāⁿ〔〕. *matches*, tsṳ̃-lâi-húe(自來火); húe-tshâ(火柴).

**match**, *to*, phùe(配). *no match for you*, kāng-lṳ́ phit-phùe m̄-kùe(共汝匹配毋過). *matchless*, bô-sang(無雙); bô-hó-pí(無好比); bô-mue̍h hó-pí-pẽng(無物好比並); a-it(阿一); tõiⁿ-it(第一).

**mate (of foreign ship)**, tōa-hu(大夫); jī-hu(字夫).

**materials**, tshâi-liāu(材料); pín-liāu(品料); mue̍h-liāu(物料). *prepare, as for building*, phōiⁿ-liāu(辦料). *of various kinds*, sam-liāu(杉料); ie̍h-liāu(藥料); sek-liāu(色料).

**mathematics**, sǹg-huap(算法); sǹg-si(算司); cheng-mûiⁿ kâi-sǹg-huap(精微个算法).

**matrix**, bôu(模). *for type*, tâng-póiⁿ-bôu(銅反模); în-póiⁿ-bôu(鉛反模).

**matter**, mue̍h(物); chieh(借); thói(體). *great*, tōa-sṳ̄(大事). *what is the matter*, sĩ-mih-sṳ̄(是乜事). *matter of course*, tsṳ̃-jiên(自然); thien-jiên(天然); tou-tie̍h chièⁿ-seⁿ(都着此樣生). *no matter*, bô-siang-kan(無相干); bô-chhiet-iàu(無切要); bô-iàu-kín(無要緊); bô-kàu tî-tò-khṳ̀(無到底倒去). *does it matter*, sṳ̄ ũ-tāi a-bô(事有大亞無). *no matter of mine*, m̄-sĩ úa--kâi-sṳ̄(毋是我个事); ṳ́-uá bô-kan(予我無干); kāng-úa bô-kan-sia̍p(共我無干涉). *matter (pus)*, lâng(郎); n̂g-sûaⁿ-tsúi(黃腺水).

**mattock**, tṳ̂-thâu(鋤頭).

**mattress**, zo̍k(褥); tshn̂g-zo̍k(床褥); phou-zo̍k(鋪褥).

**mature**, se̍k(熟); kàu-tsúi(夠水). *by experience*, kùan-se̍k(慣熟); si̍p-se̍k(習熟); liẽn-se̍k(練熟); o̍h-se̍k(學熟). *maturity(manhood)*, sêng-teng(成丁).

**maxim**, keh-ngân(格言); huap-ngân(法言); siàⁿ-hùn(聖訓); so̍k-gṳ́(俗語).

**may**, *do it*, khó(可); khó-íⁿ(可以); tsò-tit(做得). *may I go*, uá lâi-khṳ̀, hó--mé(我來去，好咩). *may it be done*, chièⁿ-seⁿ hó--mé(此樣生好咩).

**meadows**, tsháu-pou(草埔); tsháu-tiêⁿ(草場).

**meagre**, sán(㾪); sòu(瘦). *ground*, sán-tī(㾪地).

**meal**, *a*, che̍k-tǹg-pn̄g(一當飯). *full*, chia̍h-kàu-pá(食到飽).

**meal**, be̍h-hún(麥粉); be̍h-tshōi(麥齊).

**mean**, tsūaⁿ(賤); hiã-tsūaⁿ(下賤); hiã-pín(下品); kẽ-pín(下品); hiã-liû(下流). *man*, siáu-jîn-nâng(小人人[訓]).

**mean**, *to*, ũ-ì(有意); ũ-sim(有心). *meaning*, ì-sṳ̀(意思). *of written character*, jī-ngĩ(字義).

**means**, huang-huap(方法); huap-tsat(法節); huap-tõu(法度). *no*, bô-huap(無法); bô-pōu(無步); bô-lêng-ûi(無能爲); bõi-tit ji̍p-chhiú(袂得入手). *capital*, tsṳ-pńg(資本); pńg-chîⁿ(本錢).

**meantime**, tng-sî(當時); hṳ́-sî(彼時).

**measles**, mûeⁿ-chèng(糜症). *to have*, chia̍h-mûeⁿ(食糜); tshut-mûeⁿ(出糜).

**measure**, tōu(度); tōu-liãng(度量); liãng-tōu(量度); tshùn-chhieh(寸尺); tshùn-tōu(寸度); chhieh-tōu(尺度). *to*, niêⁿ(量); chhek(測); chhek-ta̍t(測值); phit(匹); pí(比). *depth of water*, thàm-tsúi(探水).

**meat**, *(flesh)*, ne̍k(肉). *meat and drink*, ím-chia̍h(飲食).

**mechanic**, sai-pẽ(司阜); kang-chhiēⁿ(工匠). *art*, ki-gōi(技藝); chhiú-gōi(手藝). *mechanism*, ie̍h-kúi(藥機).

**meddle**, tshap(插); tshap-ji̍p(插入); lóng-sṳ̄(攏事). *meddlesome*, hàuⁿ-tshūe-sṳ̄(好覓事); hàuⁿ-phùaⁿ-sṳ̄(好判事).

**mediate**, *to*, tsò-kong-chhin(做公親); kiâⁿ-hûa(行和). *mediator*, kong-chhin(公親); tong-nâng(中人); tong-pó(中保).

**medical**, *man*, sin-seⁿ(先生); ui-seng(醫生). *science*, ui-ha̍k(醫學). *college*, thài-ui-īⁿ(太醫院); thài-ui(太醫). *books*, ie̍h-chheh(藥冊). *hospital*, ui-kuán(醫館).

**medicine**, ie̍h(藥); ie̍h-tshâi(藥材); ie̍h-liāu(藥料). *powder*, ie̍h-súaⁿ(藥散); ie̍h-hún(藥粉). *pills*, ie̍h-îⁿ(藥丸). *liquid*, ie̍h-tsúi(藥水); ie̍h-chiú(藥酒); ie̍h-tê(藥茶). *plaster*, ko-ie̍h(膏藥). *a dose*, che̍k-thiap-ie̍h(一帖藥); che̍k-ho̍k-ie̍h(一服藥). *prescription*, ie̍h-hng(藥方); ie̍h-toaⁿ(藥單). *to write ditto*, khui-ie̍h-hng(開藥方). *take*, chia̍h-ie̍h(食藥). *apply*, buah-ie̍h(抹藥); tah-ie̍h(搭藥); chhiù-ie̍h(漱藥). *prepare medicine acc. to prescription*, kap-ie̍h(合藥). *properties of*, ie̍h-sèⁿ(藥性). *buy*, thiah-ie̍h(拆藥); kap-ie̍h(合藥). *secret in medicine handed down*, pì-thuân kâi-ie̍h(祕傳个藥).

**meditate**, àm-chẽⁿ-siẽⁿ(暗靜想); àm-sṳ(暗思); àm-siẽⁿ(暗想); chẽⁿ-siẽⁿ(靜想); to̍k-sṳ(讀思); to̍k-siẽⁿ(讀想); sṳ-siẽⁿ(思想). *sit in a state of deep meditation, as Buddhist priest*, ji̍p-tẽng(入定); tsõ-siên(坐仙).

**medium**, *of the idol*, tâng-ki(童乩); lo̍h-sîn(落神); tia̍p-tâng(接童).

**medusa**, *or jelly-fish*, thē(地).

**meek**, un-jiû(溫柔); khiam-sùn(謙遜).

**meet**, sie-ngõ(相遇); ngõ--tie̍h(遇着); hũe-mīn(會面); siang-hũe(相會); siang-kìⁿ-mīn(相見面); siang-phòng(相碰). *(unexpectedly)*, phòng--tie̍h(碰着). *together*, tsũ-chi̍p(聚集); tsũ-hũe(聚會); hũe-chi̍p(會集); chi̍p-bûa(集埋); kiâⁿ-bûa(行埋). *go to*, ngêng-chih(迎接).

**melancholy**, iu-būn(憂悶); tshôu-sṳ(愁思); tshôu-būn(愁悶); iu-tshôu(憂愁); ut-kak(鬱角); ut-ì(鬱意); iu-ut(憂鬱). *affair*, hó-huân-ló(好煩惱); khó-liên(可憐).

**melodious**, ha̍h-im-ūn(合音韻); im-ūn thiâu-hûa(音韻調和); thiâu-hûa; siaⁿ-im thiâu-hûa(聲音調和).

**melon**, kue(瓜). *seeds*, kue-chí(瓜子).

**melt**, iêⁿ(烊); siau-iêⁿ(消烊).

**members**, *of the body*, sì-chiⁿ(四筋); peh-thói(百體).

**membrane**, mo̍hⁿ(膜); pau-mo̍hⁿ(包膜).

**memorable**, ióng-kú put-buâng(永久不忘); put-hiú(不朽).

**memorial**, *to the throne*, pńg-chieⁿ(本奏); tsàu-chieⁿ(奏奏); piáu-chieⁿ(表奏). *memorialize the throne*, chiẽⁿ-pńg(奏本); tsàu-pńg(奏本). *archway*, têng(亭); hō-piáu(號表); têng-piáu(亭表); hûa-piáu(華表).

**memory**, kì-sèⁿ(記性); kì-tshâi(記才); kì-tî(記池). *commit to*, tha̍k-se̍k(讀熟). *recite from*, pe̍h-tshùi-liām(白喙唸); liām-tsṳ(唸書). *good*, hó-kì-sèⁿ(好記性).

**menace**, heh(嚇); heh-nâng-kiaⁿ(嚇人驚); kiaⁿ-heh(驚嚇); háⁿ-nâng(驚人[訓]).

**Mencius**, Mẽng-tsṳ́(孟子); à-siàⁿ(亞聖).

**mend**, póu(補); póu-tùe(補綴); siu-chiáⁿ(修整); chiáⁿ-lí(整理); siu-si̍p(收拾). *clothes*, póu-saⁿ(補衫). *a house*, pa-lói-tshù(巴禮厝). *a pen or pencil*, phoi-pit(批筆). *faults*, kói-kùe(改過).

**mendicant**, khṳt-chia̍h(乞食); kiâⁿ-bí(行米); thó-chia̍h(討食).

**menial**, po̍k-hia̍h(僕役); sái-huàn(使喚); huàn-hia̍h(犯役). *low*, pui-tsūaⁿ(卑賤).

**menses**, gue̍h-keng(月經); gue̍h-sṳ̄(月事); kiâⁿ-keng(行經); keng-pái(經拜); gue̍h-sìn(月信). *suppression of*, pī-gue̍h(避月); pī-keng(避經). *profuse*, hueh-pang(血崩). *irregular*, gue̍h-keng m̄-thiâu(月經毋調). *menopause*, gue̍h-tsúi tso̍h(月水絕).

**mention**, tàⁿ(呾); thî-phû(提浮). *need not*, mín-tàⁿ(免呾).

**mercantile**, *house*, hâng(行); hâng-kháu(行口). *firm*, kong-si(公司).

**mercer**, khui tiû-tn̄g-phòu(開綢緞舖); bōi-si-tsháu kheh(賣絲草客).

**merchandise**, hùe(貨); hùe-mue̍h(貨物).

**merchant**, siang-jîn(商人); kheh-siang(客商); siang-kheh(商客); tsò-seng-lí-nâng(做生理人). *ship*, hùe-tsûn(貨船); seng-lí-tsûn(生理船).

**mercury**, tsúi-ngṳ̂n(水銀).

**mercy**, tshṳ̂-pui(慈悲); liên-mién(憐憫); khó-liên(可憐); tshṳ̂-sim(慈心). *merciless*, thih-chie̍h sim-kuaⁿ(鐵石心肝); kang-ngẽ(工硬).

**merely**, put-kùe(不過); kṳ́n-kṳ́n(僅僅); toaⁿ-toaⁿ(單單); tiāⁿ-tiāⁿ(定定); to̍k-to̍k(獨獨); chheng-chheng(清清). *not merely*, put-chí(不止); put-to̍k(不獨); m̄-chheng(毋清).

**meridian**, keⁿ-sùaⁿ(經線); tsṳ́-ngóu-sùaⁿ(子午線). *in the*, chiàⁿ-ngóu(正午); tong-ngóu(中午).

**merino**, ú-siâ(羽斜).

**merit**, kong(功); kong-lâu(功勞); kong-tek(功德). *accumulate*, chek-kong(積功). *meritorious*, ũ-kong(有功); siu-kong(修功). *and demerit*, kong-kùe(功過).

**merry**, huaⁿ-hí(歡喜); ko-le(哥哩); lo-li lo-le(囉哩囉哩). *merry-thought of a fowl*, koi-heng-kut(雞興骨).

**meshes**, *of net*, mãng-ma̍k(網目). *wide and narrow*, lang-ba̍t(籠密).

**mess**, *together*, tâng-húe-si̍t(銅伙食); tsò-pû-chia̍h(做煲食). *alone*, ka-kī-chia̍h(家己食).

**message**, pò-sìn(報信). *messenger*, chhe(差); só-sái kâi-nâng(所使个人[訓]); sài-chiá(使者); sài(使); tsáu-chhe(走差); lâi-nâng(來人[訓]); lâi-sài(來使).

**metals**, ngóu-kim(五金); kim(金), ngṳ̂n(銀), tâng(銅), thih(鐵), siah(錫).

**metamorphosis**, pièn-hùe(變化); tshoiⁿ-pièn būan-hùe(千變萬化).

**metropolis**, kiaⁿ-siâⁿ(京城); kiaⁿ-sṳ(京師); kiaⁿ-tou(京都).

**middle**, tong(中); tong-sim(中心); tong-iang(中央); tong-kan(中間); tìn-tang(鎮中); chiàⁿ-tong(正中); chiàⁿ-tang(正中). *middle-aged*, tong-nîⁿ(中年). *middling*, tit-tong(得中); tong-pān(中辦); tong-phêng(中平); tong-téng(中等); bô-thang-siãng(無通上); sì-put-siãng(四不上). *middling (size)*, thûn-thûn〔〕. *midnight*, pùaⁿ-mêⁿ(半夜); saⁿ-keⁿ pùaⁿ-mêⁿ(三更半夜); tong-mêⁿ(中夜); tong-siau(中宵). *midway*, pùaⁿ-thû(半途); pùaⁿ-lōu(半路). *middle-man*, tong-nâng(中人). *middle-man (in arranging a marriage)*, bûe-nâng(媒人). *midrib of leaf*, hie̍h-kṳn(葉筋). *mid-summer day*, hē-chì(夏至). *mid-winter*, tang-chì(冬至).

**midwife**, tsâi-bó(臍母); seⁿ-phûa(生婆); siu-seⁿ-phûa(收生婆); seⁿ-kiáⁿ-bó(生囝母); ún-phûa(穩婆). *book on midwifery*, ta̍t-seⁿ-phien(生囝母); pó-seⁿ-phien(生囝母).

**might**, khuân(權); khûan-sì(權勢); khûan-la̍t(權力); khûan-lêng(權能).

**mildew**, *to*, chhiẽⁿ-bûe(上梅); chhiẽⁿ-tiám(上點); chhiẽⁿ-hue-tiám(上花點); chhiẽⁿ-poiⁿ(上班). *to mildew (mould)*, seⁿ-kou(生菇). *of plants*, chhiẽⁿ-în(上鉛).

**mile**, *(approximately)*, saⁿ-lí(三里). *three miles*, che̍k-phòu(一舖).

**military**, bú(武). *station*, iâⁿ-pûaⁿ(營盤); sìn-tī(信地); iâⁿ-sìn(營信). *profession*, bú-gōi(武藝). *officers*, bú-kuaⁿ(武官). *laws*, kun-huap(軍法); kun-lẽng(軍令); kun-lu̍t(軍律). *examination*, kháu-bú(考武); bú-khue(武科). *graduate*, bú-siù-tsâi(武秀才); bú-kṳ́-jîn(武舉人); bú-chìn-sṳ̃(武進士). *civil and*, bûn-bú(文武).

**militia**, hieⁿ-ióng(鄉勇); ióng-tsàn(勇壯); mîn-tsàn(民壯). *to raise*, mi̍t-ióng(密勇); chie-ióng(招勇); kòu-ióng(僱勇).

**milk**, nĩⁿ(奶). *cow's*, gû-nĩⁿ(牛奶). *to milk*, liū-gû-nĩⁿ(鎦牛奶). *milk-nurse*, nĩⁿ-bó(奶母). *milky-way*, thien-hô(天和).

**mill**, *(for removing the husk)*, lâng〔〕. *(for grinding)*, bō(磨). *mill-stone*, bō-chie̍h(磨石). *turn a mill*, oi-bō(挨磨). *upper mill-stone*, chiēⁿ-tún-bō(上盾磨).

**millet**, sú(黍); siú(黍).

**million**, che̍k-peh-būan(一百万); che̍k-tiãu(一兆).

**mimic**, tieⁿ-iēⁿ(張樣); tsuang-iēⁿ(裝樣); tsò-sièⁿ(做像); tsuan-o̍h i-kâi-iēⁿ(專學伊个樣); tieⁿ-siaⁿ(張聲); tieⁿ-sueh(張說); tsuang-siaⁿ(裝聲).

**mince**, tso̍ih-tshùi-tshùi(截碎碎); tok-tshùi(剁碎); tok-iùⁿ(剁幼). *(substantive)*, ne̍k-tshò(肉銼); ne̍k-nîⁿ(肉泥). *(substantive) (less fine)*, ne̍k-sám(肉糝).

**mind**, sim(心); sim-sîn(心神); sim-chì(心志); sim-tn̂g(心腸); sim-ì(心意). *intelligent*, tóu-lãi mêng-pe̍h(肚內明白). *large*, tōu-liãng khuan-tōa(度量寬大); tōu-liãng khuan-khuah(度量寬闊); khuan-hông tãi-liãng(寬宏大量); hái-liãng(海量). *narrow*, bô-tōu-liãng(無度量); ti̍h-kiáⁿ-liãng(滴囝量); koi-tn̂g múaⁿ-chiah-tóu(雞腸滿隻肚); sim o̍ih-sòi(心狹細); sim-heng o̍ih-sòi(心胸狹細); chhién-kièn(淺見). *of one*, tâng-sim(同心). *just to my mind*, chiàⁿ-ha̍h úa-kâi-sim(正合我个心); zû-ngũan(如願); zû-ì(如意); tèng-ì(中意); ha̍h-siẽⁿ(合想). *have something on the mind*, sim-lãi ũ-sṳ̄(心內有事); sim m̄-chheng(心不清); sim m̄-ôiⁿ(心不閒); sim-lãi kãu-ue̍h(心內垢穢). *mind made up*, tsú-ì íⁿ-tiāⁿ(主意已定); li̍p-tiāⁿ tsú-ì(立定主意); íⁿ-keng kuat-ì(已經決意). *to mind*, liû-sim(留心); tì-ì(在意). *with one's whole mind*, tsuan-sim tì-ì(專心致意); chĩn-sim chĩn-ì(真心真意). *never mind*, bô-siang-kan(無相干); chhìn-tshái(凊彩); màiⁿ-khṳ̀-tshái(勿去睬); màiⁿ-khṳ̀ kài-ì(勿去介意); màiⁿ-pàng tõ-sim(勿放在心); tì-tsṳ tōu-gūa(置之度外); màiⁿ-kúan(勿管). *never mind him*, màiⁿ kāng-i kòi-kà(勿共伊計較); màiⁿ-tshái--i(勿睬伊); kṳ̀-i-khṳ̀〔〕. *keep in mind*, kì-tit(記得); kì-liãm(記念).

**mine**, *gold*, kim-suaⁿ(金山). *miner*, liú-suaⁿ-hām(㧕山陷). *in war*, tī-lûi(地雷); tī-lûi húe-phàu(地雷火砲). *to lay*, tâi-tī-lûi(抬地雷). *to explode*, kún-tī-lûi(滾地雷).

**mineralogy**, chie̍h-tsóng-lũn(石總論).

**mingle**, sie-tsham(相摻); sie-chhiau〔〕.

**miniature**, siáu-ngiá(小雅); hí-sîn(喜神).

**minister**, chhîn(臣); tãi-chhîn(大臣); tãi-láu(大老); kok-láu(國老). *prime*, tsái-siàng(宰相).

**minstrel**, chhiè-khek(唱曲); tshue-siau(吹簫); pûn-siau(歕簫); tsak-gau̍h(作樂). *(travelling)*, tsáu-chhiàng(走唱).

**mint**, *a*, tsù-chîⁿ-ke̍k(鑄錢局). *master of the*, chîⁿ-ke̍k-kuaⁿ(錢局官).

**mint**, pô-hò(薄荷); po̍h-hò(薄荷).

**minute (small)**, sòi-mûiⁿ(細微); iùⁿ-mûiⁿ(幼微); siâng-sòi(詳細); sòi-siâng(細詳); cheng-mûiⁿ(精微). *explain minutely*, hun-thiah sòi-siâng(分拆細詳).

**minute**, *a*, che̍k-hun(一分); che̍k-hun-cheng(一分鐘). *wait a minute*, tán--khùn-kiáⁿ(等頃囝); tán--siap-sî(等霎時); khiã-tiām--chē(徛恬些); chhiáⁿ-thẽng--chē(請等些).

**miracle**, ĩ-chiah(異蹟); sîn-chiah(神蹟); lêng-chiah(靈蹟); lêng-ĩ(靈異). *to perform*, kiâⁿ-ĩ-chiah(行異蹟).

**mire**, thôu-nîⁿ(土泥); nîⁿ-thôu(泥土). *(thin)*, thôu-mûeⁿ(土糜). *(sticky)*, thôu-ko(土膏).

**mirror**, mīn-kiàⁿ(面鏡); siu-tsng-kiàⁿ(梳妝鏡). *(hand)*, chhiú-kiàⁿ(手鏡). *(hanging)*, tiàu-kiàⁿ(吊鏡). *(full-length)*, chiè-sin pó-kiàⁿ(照身寶鏡). *(metallic)*, tâng-kiàⁿ(銅鏡). *look in*, chiè-kiàⁿ(照鏡). *polish metallic mirror*, bûa-kiàⁿ(磨鏡).

**misanthropic**, put-jîn(不仁); m̄-kṳ̃n nâng-chhêng(毋近人情); sèⁿ-chhêng kou-ta̍k(性情孤獨); kou-phiah(孤僻).

**misapprehend**, siẽⁿ-tāⁿ(想賺); siẽⁿ-tshò(想錯); gōu-siẽⁿ(誤想); thiaⁿ-tāⁿ(聽賺); thiaⁿ-tshò(聽錯).

**misbehave**, bô-kui-kṳ́(無規矩); bô-sũn huap-tōu(無順法度).

**miscall**, tàⁿ-tāⁿ(呟擔); kiè-tāⁿ(叫擔).

**miscarry**, sié-súaⁿ(徙算); lo̍h-tho(落胎); lo̍h-súaⁿ(落產); tho tak-nn̄g〔〕; tũi-tho(落產). *(accidental)*, a-nôuⁿ lo̍h-tiāu(阿孥落掉). *(intentional)*, lo̍h-tiāu a-nôuⁿ(落掉阿孥).

**miscellaneous**, tsa̍p(雜); tsa̍p-mue̍h(什物); tsa̍p-kiáu-liãu(雜交料); tshàm-tshùi-mue̍h(懺碎物); lo̍k-lo̍k so̍k-so̍k(碌碌俗俗); liau̍h-liau̍h chiau̍h-chiau̍h(略略雀雀).

**mischance**, m̄-tsãu-hùe(毋造化).

**mischief**, *to do*, hāi-nâng(害人). *mischievous*, lĩ-hāi(厲害); kha-chhiú m̄-hó(跤手不好); kha-chhiú tsōi(骹手㩼).

**misconduct**, kùe-sit(過失); m̄-tùi-nâng(毋對人); sàng-hẽng(送行); sàng-pín(送品).

**misdemeamour**, ũ-m̄-tie̍h--tshù(有毋着處). *slight*, siáu-kùe mûiⁿ-sit(小過微失).

**miser**, sieh-chîⁿ(鹹澀); kien-liẽn(鹹澀); liẽn-sieh chîⁿ-ngṳ̂n(憐惜錢銀); thih-koi-ang che̍k-môⁿ put-po̍ih(鐵雞翁一毛不拔); chiéⁿ-chîⁿ-nôu(掌錢奴); siú-chîⁿ-nôuⁿ(守錢奴).

**moserable**, chhi-tshám(淒慘); khóu-lān(苦卵); kan-khóu(艱苦); chhi-liâng(淒凉). *misery*, hũa(禍); hũa-hũam(禍患); kan-khóu(艱苦).

**misfortune**, bô-tsãu-hùe(無造化); put-hẽng(不幸); bô-miāⁿ-ūn(無命運); khiap-miāⁿ(㾀命); khóu-miāⁿ(苦命); po̍h-miāⁿ(薄命).

**misgiving**, khùa-sim(掛心); khùa-lṳ̃(掛慮).

**misgovern**, tshâng-hāi liâng-mîn(殘害良民); lũan-chèng(亂政).

**misinterpret**, e̍k-tshò(譯錯); e̍k-tāⁿ(譯賺); kói-tāⁿ(改賺).

**mislay**, pàng m̄-kui-ūi(放毋歸位). *mislaid*, buâng-kìⁿ(忘見); tshūe-m̄-kìⁿ(覓毋見).

**mislead**, tshūa-tāⁿ-lōu(𤆬賺路); iú-ho̍k(誘惑); ín-iú(引誘).

**mismanage**, phōiⁿ-sṳ̄ m̄-hó(辦事不好); lí-sṳ̄ m̄-chheng-tshó(理事不清楚); sṳ̄-lí m̄-pat-tò-khṳ̀(料理毋別倒去).

**misrepresent**, íⁿ-sĩ ûi-hui(以是爲非); íⁿ-ti̍t ûi-khiok(以直爲曲); piẽn-luãn sĩ-hui(辯亂是非); bû-kò(誣告); bû-lūa(誣賴); pù-lũ〔〕; iâu-pãng(謠謗).

**misrule**, sit-chèng(失政); bô-tãu(無道).

**miss**, m̄-tie̍h(毋着); m̄-tòng(毋當); sit-chìⁿ(失箭); sit-gōu(失誤). *opportunity*, sit-ki(失機). *way*, sit-lōu(失路). *lose*, m̄-kìⁿ(毋見).

**misshapen**, m̄-chiâⁿ-iēⁿ(毋成樣); iá-iēⁿ(野樣).

**misspend**, *time*, hṳ-tōu sùe-gu̍eh(虛度稅月); sit-sî(失時); hùi-sî(費時); tak-nn̄g-tiāu sî-hāu〔〕; khang-hùi kuang-im(空費光陰).

**mist**, in-bū(煙霧); in(煙); mông-in(濛煙); mông-bū(朦霧); huat-mông(發蒙); huat-bū(發霧); bū-bū(霧霧).

**mistake**, tshò(錯); tsha-tshò(差錯); tsha-niũⁿ〔〕; m̄-tie̍h(毋着); tshng m̄-tùi-phīⁿ(穿毋對鼻). *no*, bô-tsáu-tsu̍ah(無走絀); bô-tshò(無錯); put-tshò(差錯). *a person*, gōu-jīn(誤認); tshò-jīn(錯認); jīn-tāⁿ(認差); thóiⁿ-tāⁿ(睇差). *well arranged so that no*, chiu-ba̍t(差錯).

**mistress**, tsú-bó(主母); hu-jîn(夫人); ke-tsú-má(家主媽). *(thâu-ke has bad meaning in Ch'ao-chow-foo, but is commonly used in Swatow)*, thâu-ke-niêⁿ(頭家娘).

**mistrust**, gî(疑); m̄-sìn(毋信).

**misunderstand**, gōu-hũe-ì(誤會意); liáng-gōu(兩誤); jī-ke tshò-kòi(字家錯計); jī-ke tshò-siẽⁿ(自家錯想). *(in hearing)*, thiaⁿ-tāⁿ(聽賺).

**mites**, tâi(臺). *to breed*, seⁿ-tâi(生臺).

**mitigate**, *punishment*, khin-séⁿ hêng-hu̍at(輕省刑罰). *sickness*, ui-khin-pēⁿ(醫輕病); sái-pēⁿ chiãm-khin(使病暫輕). *one's wrath*, khǹg-sek(勸息). *pain*, chí-thiàⁿ(止痛).

**mix**, tsham(摻); sie-tsham(相摻); sie-chhiau〔〕; sie-chhiau sie-liãu〔〕. *mixed*, tsham-tsa̍p(摻雜); hũn-tsa̍p(混雜).

**moan**, thàn-sek(歎息); tshan(餐); tsáu-khùi(走氣); tsa-thàn(查歎); ai-thàn(哀歎); pui-thàn(悲歎).

**moist**, sip(濕); tâm(㴷); ĩm(蔭); lùn-lùn(嫩嫩); zũn-sip(潤濕). *moisten*, ùn-tsúi(煴水). *moisten (melt)*, iêⁿ(烊).

**mole**, tshân-tshṳ́(田鼠). *hill*, tshṳ́-èng(鼠應). *hole*, tshṳ́-khang(鼠空). *trap*, tshṳ́-keng(鼠經). *cricket*, thôu-káu(塗狗).

**molest**, lâu(勞); jiáu-to̍k(擾毒); kiáu-jiáu(攪擾); bûa-lūi(磨累).

**Monday**, lói-pài-it(禮拜一); pài-it(拜一).

**money**, chîⁿ(錢); chîⁿ-ngṳ̂n(錢銀). *(wealth)*, chîⁿ-tshâi(錢財). *bag*, chîⁿ-tō(錢袋); ngṳ̂n-tō(銀袋). *box*, chîⁿ-tâng(錢銅); chîⁿ-kóng(錢管); chîⁿ-kūiⁿ(錢櫃). *box (safe)*, kap-būan(甲萬). *box (earthenware)*, chîⁿ-kuh(錢嗝). *money-changer*, khui-chîⁿ-phòu(開錢舖); khui táu-toh-kūiⁿ(開倒桌櫃). *money-lender*, pàng-chè(放債); pàng-chè kâi-nâng(放債个人); pàng-lāi(放利); pàng-tièⁿ(放帳); pàng-siàu(放數); seⁿ-pàng(生放); seⁿ-ngṳ̂n(生銀). *lend on heavy interest*, pàng-tãng-chè(放重債). *moneyless*, bô-chîⁿ(無錢). *to pass bad money*, sái pe̍h-tâng-ngṳ̂n(使白銅銀).

**Mongolia**, Mông-kóu(蒙古).

**month**, gu̍eh(月). *one*, che̍k-kâi-gu̍eh(一個月). *the first*, chiaⁿ-gu̍eh(正月); chiaⁿ--gu̍eh(正月). *first day of*, chhiu-it(初一). *intercalary*, zūn-gu̍eh(閏月). *monthly*, múeⁿ-gue̍h(每月).

**more**, ke(加). *a little*, ke--lân-ló(加利老). *is there more*, huân-ũ a-bô(還有亞無). *no more of this*, pã--liáu(罷了). *more than ten*, tsa̍p-gūa(雜外); tsa̍p-tshut(雜出). *the more you plead the less he heeds you*, zú-koh-lô zú-m̄-tshái(愈閣羅愈毋睬). *more or less*, ke-kiám(加減).

**moreover**, lêng-gūa(另外); siãng-chhiáⁿ(尙且); huân-liáu(還了); khuàng-chhiáⁿ(況且); iũ-tsài(又再); kèng-chhiáⁿ(竟且); huân-iáu(還要).

**morning**, mn̂g-khí(眠起). *every*, pâi-mn̂g-khí(排眠起). *early in the*, mn̂g-khí tsá-tsá(眠起早早). *this*, mn̂g-khí(眠起). *next*, mùaⁿ-mn̂g-khí(明眠起). *and evening*, mêⁿ-hng tsá-khí(夜昏早起); mêⁿ-hng mn̂g-khí(夜昏眠起). *star*, khí-mêng-chheⁿ(啓明星). *long for (as sick person)*, thãi bõi-tit thiⁿ kng(待袂得天光).

**morose**, pũ-àu(哺懊); àu pũ-pũ(懊哺哺); mīn hìm-hìm(面念念).

**mortar**, hue(灰); hue-thôu(灰塗); thôu-sua(灰塗).

**mortgage**, tǹg(當); tóiⁿ(典). *deed*, tóiⁿ-khòi(典契). *mortgager*, tóiⁿ-tsú(典主); tshù-tsú(厝主).

**mortify**, *as flesh*, ne̍k àu--khṳ̀(肉懊去); ne̍k mîⁿ(肉糜); hiùⁿ-ne̍k(臭肉); hu-ne̍k(腐肉); ne̍k hu-hiùⁿ(肉腐臭); ne̍k hu-hiúⁿ(肉夫朽); ne̍k nūaⁿ-nūaⁿ(肉軟軟); sí-ne̍k(死肉).

**mortise**, sún-khang(損空); sún-ngám(笋眼). *to fit tenon snd mortice*, chiap-sún(接笋).

**mosquito**, máng(蚊). *numerous*, máng kãu(蚊厚). *bite*, máng kã(蚊咬). *swelling from bite*, lâu(樓). *net or curtain*, máng-tièⁿ(蠓帳); máng-tà(蚊蟲).

**moss**, thî(苔); chheⁿ-thî(青苔). *to grow*, seⁿ-thî(生苔); chhiẽⁿ-chheⁿ-thî(上青苔).

**most**, chì(至); tsãi(在); tsùe(最); sĩm(甚); tsa̍p-hun(十分). *(all signs of superlative degree)*, chì(至). *mostly*, tãi-sì(大勢); tãi-khài(大概); tsōi-siâⁿ(㩼成); tōa-mĩn(大面); tōa-pùaⁿ(大半).

**moth**, tsù(蛀); tsù-thâng(蛀蟲); teng-ngô(燈蛾); tsam-teng-ia̍h(針燈蝶).

**mother**, a-bó(阿母); bó-chhin(母親); lãu-bó(老母); a-âi〔〕; a-neⁿ(阿嬭); a-niⁿ(阿奶); a-niêⁿ(阿娘). *your*, lẽng-thâng(令堂). *your late mother*, lẽng-soiⁿ-thâng(令先堂); lẽng-soiⁿ-tshṳ̂(令先慈). *my*, ke-bó(家母); ke-tshṳ̂(家慈). *my late mother*, ke-soiⁿ-tshṳ̂(家先慈); ke-soiⁿ-bó(家先母). *sister of one's*, bó-î(母姨). *brother of*, bó-kũ(母舅). *wife's mother*, tiẽⁿ-m-phûa(丈毋婆); nga̍k-bó(岳母). *husband's mother*, ta-ke(大家). *step-mother*, kì-bó(繼母); ãu-bó(後母). *real mother*, seⁿ-bó(生母); chhin-bó(親母). *adoptive*, iáng-bó(養母). *motherless child*, bô-âi-kiáⁿ(無愛囝). *mother-of-pearl*, ô-kiàⁿ-khak(蠔囝殼).

**motion**, see MOVE.

**motive**, sim(心); ì-sṳ̀(意思); sim-ì(心意); khí-tuan(起端); in-tuan(因端); pńg-sim(本心); pńg-ì(本意).

**motley**, tsa̍p-sek(雜色).

**Moukden**, Sẽng-kiaⁿ(盛京).

**mould**, *for casting*, bôu(模); ìn(印).

**mouldy**, huat-môⁿ(發毛); seⁿ-kou(生菇); seⁿ-kou-mo̍hⁿ(生菇毛); huat-kou(發菇); chhiẽⁿ-mo̍hⁿ(上毛); chhiẽⁿ-kou(上菇).

**moulder**, *away, like wall*, huân(還); chiãm-chiãm-siau(漸漸消); kauh-tiāu(捲掉).

**moult**, thǹg-môⁿ(褪毛); phah-thǹg(拍褪); ūaⁿ-môⁿ(換毛).

**mound**, suaⁿ(山); suaⁿ-kiáⁿ(山囝); che̍k-tun(一堆); che̍k-tu-long(一堆壟); hūaⁿ(捍).

**mount**, seng(升); seng-chiẽⁿ(升上); chiẽⁿ(上); seng-kûiⁿ(升懸). *a horse*, chiẽⁿ-bé(上馬); peh-chiẽⁿ-bé(百上馬); pe̍h-chiẽⁿ bé-sin(白上馬身). *mounted on a horse*, khiâ-bé(騎馬). *as pictures*, piè-jī-ūe(表字話).

**mountain**, suaⁿ(山); kûiⁿ-suaⁿ(懸山); kau-suaⁿ(高山); suaⁿ-nga̍k(山岳). *top of*, suaⁿ-niáⁿ(山嶺); suaⁿ-téng(山頂). *chain of*, suaⁿ-lêng(山嶺). *mountainous*, kan chẽng sĩ-suaⁿ(乾淨是山).

**mourn**, khàu(哭); ai-chhek(哀惻); ai-khàu(哀哭); khàu-tshoih(哭嘈). *mournful*, iu-tshôu(憂愁); iu-būn(憂悶); pui-ai(悲哀).

**mourning**, *apparel*, hà-saⁿ(孝衫); hà-ho̍k(孝服); sng-ho̍k(喪服); sng-hà(喪孝). *to wear*, tòa-hà(帶孝). *put off*, thut-hà(脫孝); thut-ho̍k(脫服); tṳ̂-mûaⁿ(除麻). *in*, kṳ-sng(居喪); ũ-pe̍h-sṳ̄(有白事). *perform the ceremony of weeping*, lêng-tsôiⁿ khàu(另前哭); tsò-hà(做孝); teng-iu(燈憂).

**mouse**, niáuⁿ-tshṳ́(鳥鼠); chip-tshṳ́〔〕. *trap*, niáuⁿ-tshṳ́-keng(鳥鼠弓); niáuⁿ-tshṳ́-tak(鳥鼠觸). *white*, pe̍h-niáuⁿ-tshṳ́(白鳥鼠); ngṳ̂n-tshṳ́(銀鼠).

**moustache**, see MUSTACHE.

**mouth**, tshùi(喙); kháu(口). *of river*, káng-kháu(港口). *open*, khui-tshùi(開喙). *shut*, tshùi kâm-miⁿ(喙含棉); ha̍p-miⁿ(合棉). *corners of*, tshùi-piⁿ(喙邊). *mouthful*, che̍k-tshùi(一喙). *of tobacco smoke*, che̍k-kháu-hun(一口分).

**move**, tõng(動); tín-tãng(振動); iê-tõng(搖動); iâu-tõng(搖動); iê-tãng(搖重); pù-pái(佈擺). *things*, puaⁿ-mu̍eh(搬物). *as chair or table, backwards or forwards*, tshâu(移). *lodging*, puaⁿ-tshù(搬厝); súa-the̍h(徙宅); î-kṳ(移居); chhien-kṳ(遷居); chhien-súa(遷徙); puaⁿ-súa(搬徙). *a grave*, chhien-suaⁿ(遷山); khí-tsàng(起壯). *the heart*, kám-tõng(感動). *movable*, õi-tín-tãng(會振動); ua̍h(活). *movables*, ke-húe(家伙); ke-si mu̍eh-kiãⁿ(家私物件).

**much**, *ke; to*, tsōi(㩼). *not*, ũ-hãn(有限); bô-hièⁿ-tsōi(無向㩼); bô-mih-tsōi(無乜㩼). *very much*, tōa-bó-mu̍eh(大母物); tsōi-tsãi(㩼在). *as much again*, ke-che̍k-pũe(加一倍); ke-che̍k-ûe(加一半).

**mud**, nîⁿ(呢); nîⁿ-thôu(泥塗); làm-thôu(濫塗); nap-thôu(濕塗); thôu-ko(土膏). *muddy water*, lô-tsúi(濁水).

**mulberry**, *tree*, sng-sûi-chhiu(桑垂樹).

**mule**, lô-bé(騾馬).

**muller**, lûi-au(雷毬); lûi-sek-īⁿ(雷石院).

**multiplication**, sêng-siàu(乘數); sêng-huap(乘法). *table*, sêng-toaⁿ(乘單). *multiply by*, ēng-lâi-sêng(用來乘).

**multitude**, khûn-chèng(群眾); chiâⁿ-khûn(成群); sêng-khûn(成群). *the*, chèng-nâng(眾人[訓]); sù-mîn(庶民).

**mumble**, tàⁿ-ūe kâm-kôu(呾話含糊).

**munch**, chia̍h tōa-tshùi tōa-au̍hⁿ(食大喙大噢); pōu(步).

**murder**, suah-nâng(殺人); kù-suah(故殺); suah-sí-nâng(殺死人); kiâⁿ-hiong(驚兇); thâi-nâng(刣人[訓]). *of parent or king*, chhì-suah kun-pẽ(弒殺君父). *murderer*, hiong-chhiú(兇手); hiong-huãm(兇犯); hiong-thû(兇仇); tsũe-hiong(罪兇).

**murmur**, kauh-kauh-kiè(捲捲叫); liām-lōu(念路). *against*, uàn(怨); uàn-hṳ̃n(怨恨).

**muscle**, ne̍k(肉); ne̍k-si(肉絲). *(tendons of)*, ne̍k-kṳn(肉筋).

**mushroom**, kou(菇). *edible*, hieⁿ-kou(香菇).

**music**, *instrumental*, gau̍h(樂); gau̍h-im(樂音); gau̍h-siaⁿ(樂聲). *make*, tsak-gau̍h(作樂); tsàu-gau̍h(奏樂). *instruments of*, gau̍h-khì(樂器). *box*, poih-im-cheng(八音鐘). *musician*, gau̍h-sṳ(樂師).

**musk**, siâ-hieⁿ(麝香). *deer*, siâ-káu(麝狗).

**musket**, chhèng(銃); chiáu-chhèng(鳥銃); chiáu-chhieⁿ(鳥槍). *musketeer*, chhèng-chhiú(銃手). see GUN.

**muslin**, se(紗); mîⁿ-se(棉紗).

**must**, *bũ-pit*, eng-kai(應該); tie̍h(着); bõi-tit-mién(袂得免); put-tit-íⁿ(不得已). *why must*, hô-pit(何必). *must not*, m̄-hó(不好).

**mustache**, chhiu(鬚); tshùi-chhiu(喙鬚); nõⁿ-phuah-chhiu(軟拔鬚). *to grow a*, lâu-chhiu(留鬚).

**mustard**, *seed*, kài-chí(芥子); kài-lua̍h-chí(芥辣子); pe̍h-kài-chí(白芥子). *powder*, kài-lua̍h-hún(芥辣粉).

**musty**, chhiẽⁿ-ĩm〔〕; seⁿ-sip-khì(生濕氣); seⁿ-ip-chi̍p〔〕; tshàu-kou-hièn(臭菇羶).

**mute**, *(dumb)*, é(啞); bõi-tàⁿ-ūe(袂呾話). *silent*, tiām-tiām(恬恬); bô-khui-tshùi(無開喙).

**mutable**, õi-kói-pièn(會改變); õi-kói-piⁿ(會改邊).

**mutiny**, pũe-pũan(倍叛); pũe-nge̍k(背逆).

**mutter**, tàⁿ-ūe hâm-hâm hû-hû(呾話含含扶扶); chih-tsuh-kiè(拮撮計).

**mutton**, iêⁿ-ne̍k(羊肉).

**mutual**, siang(相); sie(相); jī-ke(二家); hû-siang(互相). *mutual consent*, liáng-ngũan(兩願); jī-ke hàuⁿ(二家好); liáng-ke huaⁿ-hí(兩家歡喜); pí-tshṳ́ huaⁿ-hí(彼此歡喜). *affection*, siang-ài(相愛).

**muzzle**, lâng-tshùi(籠喙); kùa-tshùi-lâng(掛喙籠); lap-gû-tshùi(套牛喙).

**my**, uá--kâi(我个). *name*, pĩ-sèⁿ(被姓); sié-miâⁿ(小名). *house*, pĩ-sià(被捨); tsháu-sià(草舍). *son*, úa siáu-jî-kiáⁿ(我小兒囝). *daughter*, sié-nńg(小女). *wife*, úa kâi-lãi-tsuat(我個內拙). *self*, ka-kī(家己); pńg-sin(本身). *I saw it with my own eyes*, úa chhin-ma̍k thóiⁿ-kìⁿ(我親目睇見).

**myrrh**, mu̍t-ie̍h(沒藥).

**mysterious**, *abstruse*, àu-biāu(奧妙); mûiⁿ-biāu(微妙); chhim-biāu(深妙). *strange and inexplicable*, hãi-ĩ lân-chhek(駭異難測). *secret*, pi-ba̍t(碑密).

**mystical**, *(having a hidden meaning)*, ṳ́n-gṳ́(隱語).

### N

**nail**, teng(釘). *iron*, thih-teng(鐵釘). *to nail*, tèng-teng(釘釘). *finger*, chhiú-tsóiⁿ-kah(手指甲); tsńg-kah(指甲). *toe*, kha-chí-kah(骹指甲).

**naked**, chhiah-sin(赤身); lòu-thói(赤身); chhiah-tiâu-tiâu(赤條條). *strip*, thn̍g-chhiah-sin(褪赤身); pak-chhiah ka-lit(膊赤交落); tshut-sin lòu-thói(出身露體); thong-sin bô-pùaⁿ-tiâu se-sùaⁿ(通身無半條紗線). *strip (without a thread of clothing)*, tñg-tiâu se-sùaⁿ(斷條紗線). 

**name**, *family*, sèⁿ(姓). *own*, miâⁿ(名); zú-miâⁿ(乳名); hãu(號); tso̍k-hãu(族號); tsṳ-miâⁿ(之名); pie̍t-hãu(別號). *what is your name*, kùi-sèⁿ(貴姓); tōa-miâⁿ(大名); *my*, pĩⁿ-sèⁿ(辨姓); sié-miâⁿ(小名). *a good*, hó-miâⁿ-sek(好名色); hó-miâⁿ-siaⁿ(好名聲). *namely*, chiũ-sĩ(就是); chiet-sĩ(即是); tsu-zû(朱如).

**Namoa**, Lâm-ò(南澳).

**nankeen**, chhiah-pòu(赤布).

**napkin**, chhiú-pòu(手布); chhiú-kṳn(手巾); kūaⁿ-kṳn(汗巾).

**narcissus**, tsúi-sien-hue(水仙花).

**narrative**, o̍h che̍k-kiãⁿ-sṳ̄(學一件事); o̍h-sṳ̄-chhêng(學事情); o̍h-sṳ̄-si̍t(學事實); o̍h-nâng-thiaⁿ(學人聽); thûan-su̍t(傳述); kóu-tn̄g(古傳).

**narrow**, o̍ih(狹); o̍ih-soih(狹細); o̍ih-to̍ih(狹窄). *minded*, sim o̍ih-soih(心狹細); bô-tōu-liãng(無度量). *watch narrowly*, ba̍t-hûang(密皇); chiéⁿ-kín(掌緊); kín-hûang(緊皇); kṳ́n-hûang(謹皇); chhim-hûang(深皇).

**nasty**, u-ùe(污穢); nah-sap(垃圾); lâm-sap〔〕; chhi-gî(淒疑).

**nation**, kok(國).

**native**, *a*, pńg-tī-nâng(本地人); pńg-thóu pńg-tī-nâng(本土本地人). *place*, pńg-hieⁿ(本鄉); pńg-tī(本地); kū-hieⁿ(舊鄉); kū-thóu(舊土); ke-hieⁿ(家鄉).

**natural**, thiⁿ-seⁿ(天生); tsṳ̃-jiên(自然); thien-jiên(天然); só-seⁿ(所生); pńg-seⁿ(本生). *disposition*, sèⁿ(性); sèⁿ-chhêng(性情); pín-sèⁿ(品性); pín-chieh(品質).

**nausea**, àiⁿ-thòu(愛吐); àiⁿ-áu(愛吐); áu-ueh(嘔噦); ueh-ueh-thòu(噦噦吐). *nauseated*, chia̍h--liáu ià(食了厭).

**naval**, *officer*, tsúi-sṳ(水師).

**navel**, tóu-tsâi(肚臍). *string*, tsâi-tòa(臍帶). *to cut it*, tńg-tsâi(轉臍).

**navigable**, hó-sái-tsûn(好使船). *navigate*, kiâⁿ-tsûn(行船). *navy*, che̍k-tūi chièn-tsûn(一隊戰船).

**near**, kṳ̃n(近); siang-kṳ̃n(相近). *sighted*, kṳ̃n-sĩ-ma̍k(近視目). *nearly*, tsha-m̄-to(差毋多); tsua̍h-m̄-tsōi(絀毋㩼); tsáu-tsua̍h ũ-hãn(走絀有限). *come near*, kṳ̃n-bûa(近埋).

**neat**, tsôi-chiáⁿ(齊整); chhî-chéng(齊整); chiám-tso̍ih(斬截); iap-thiap〔〕; kiau-kiah(矯捷).

**necessary**, iàu-ēng(要用); chhiet-ēng(切用); chhiet-iàu(切要); te̍k-àiⁿ(的愛). *daily*, ji̍t-ēng(日用). *a*, tang-si(東司); chhè-tî(廁池); chhè-koiⁿ(廁間). *of necessity*, put-tit-íⁿ(不得已). *necessitous*, phîn-khiông(貧窮); khueh-hua̍t(缺乏); phîn-kip(貧急); kip-chhiú(急手).

**neck**, ãm(頷). *back of*, ãm-ãu(頷後); ãu-táu(後斗). *front of*, ãm-ẽ(頷下). *band*, ãm-niáⁿ(頷領). *necklace*, ãm-liēn(頷鍊).

**necromancer**, thóiⁿ-siàⁿ(睇聲); lo̍h-sîn-phûa(落神婆).

**need**, see NECESSARY. *need not*, mién(免); mín-ēng(免用). *the needy*, phîn-mîn(貧民); phîn-khiông-nâng(貧窮人).

**needle**, tsam(針). *eye of*, tsam-phīⁿ(針鼻). *to thread a*, tshng-tsam(倉針). *case*, tsam-tō(針袋). *of the Chinese compass*, chí-lâm-tsam(指南針).

**needless**, *expenditure*, hṳ-hùi(虛費); hua-hùi(花費); khang-hùi(空費).

**neglect**, khin-buãn(輕慢); khin-hut(輕忽); miáuⁿ-hut(妙忽); bô-kuan-kù(無關顧); bô-chiàu-kù(無照顧); bô-thóiⁿ-kù(無睇顧); bô-kù-sím(無顧審). *(treat disrespectfully)*, tãi-buãn(大慢). *(slight)*, hut-lia̍k(忽略). *(not take care of)*, put-kù(不顧).  *(not attend to, as business)*, bô-lí(無理). *negligent*, lak-thak(落塌); lak-lṳ́(落汝). *negligent (putting off)*, lua-thûa(魯拖).

**negotiations**, *for peace*, kiâⁿ-hûa(行和); káng-hûa(講和).

**negro**, ou-mīn-nâng(烏面人); ou-huan(烏番).

**neigh**, bé kiè(馬叫).

**neighbour**, tshù-piⁿ(厝邊); tshù-piⁿ lîn-iũ(厝邊鄰右); tshù-lîn(厝邊); lîn-kṳ(厝邊). *neighbourhood*, lîn-kṳ̃n(鄰近). *neighbouring(village; kingdom)*, lîn-hieⁿ(厝邊); lîn-kok(厝邊).

**neither**, *more nor less*, bô-ke bô-kiám(無家無減). *neither he not I went*, i iā bô-khṳ̀(伊也無去), uá iā bô-khṳ̀(我也無去); pí-tshṳ́ lóng-tsóng bô-khṳ̀(彼此攏總無去).

**nephew**, tie̍t(姪). *(sister's son)*, gūa-seng(外甥). *(generally called)*, tau-sun(姪孫).

**Neptune**, hái-lêng-uâng(海靈王).

**nerve**, náuⁿ-kṳn(腦筋); náuⁿ-si(腦絲); náuⁿ-kṳn-si(腦筋絲).

**nest**, tshâu(巢); tàu(竇). *(with young birds)*, siū(岫). *make a*, tsoh-siū(作岫). *of thieves*, tsha̍t-tàu(賊竇); tsha̍t-hua̍t(賊穴); tsha̍t-tshâu(賊巢); tsha̍t-o(賊窩). *of articles of larger and smaller size, with smaller lying inside larger*, chek-thun(叔吞).

**net**, mãng(網); tsan(曾); nôiⁿ(荔). *weave*, kit-mãng(結網); phah-mãng(拍網). *cast*, pha-mãng(拋網). *set*, hē-mãng(下網); lo̍h-mãng(落網). *catch fish in*, mãng-hṳ̂(網魚).

**never**, tsóng-bô(總無); būan-bô(萬無). *yet*, tshông-tsôiⁿ būe-ũ(從前未有); tsṳ̃-liáu m̄-pat(自了毋識). *mind*, bô-siang-kan(無相干); chhìn-tshái(凊彩); m̄-kàu tî-kò-khṳ̀(毋到底塊去); bô-tì-chhiet(無知切); bò-chhiet-iàu(毋切要); bô-kai-tsài(無該載). *he will never come*, ióng-kú bô-lâi(永久無來). *this will never do*, chièⁿ-seⁿ m̄-tsò-tit(此樣生毋做得). *nevertheless*, hûan-liáu(還了).

**new**, sin(新). *style*, sin-khúan(新款); sin-siãng(新上). *your*, sin-nîⁿ(新年). *new year's eve*, kùe-nîⁿ(過年); ji̍h-káu saⁿ-tsa̍p mêⁿ(廿九三十夜). *new year's day*, chiaⁿ--gue̍h chhiu-it(正月秋一). *newly made*, sin-tsò(新做). *news*, sin-bũn(新聞); sie-sit(消息). *newspaper*, sin-bũn-tsúa(新聞紙).

**next**, *after another*, sie-sùa(相紲); tõiⁿ-jī(等二). *month*, ẽ-kâi-gue̍h(下個月); ãu-kâi-gue̍h(後個月). *day*, mêng-ji̍t(明日); mùaⁿ-khí(閩起); mùaⁿ-tsá(閩早). *year*, mêⁿ-nîⁿ(明年); mêng-nîⁿ(明年). *time*, ẽ-hûe(下回); ãu-pái(後擺).

**nice**, hó(好); ngiá(雅); tshù-bī(趣味); chhèng-ì(稱意); ha̍h-ì(合意); zû-ì(如意).

**niche**, chhiêⁿ-kham(牆龕); piah-kham(壁龕); chhiêⁿ-khang(牆龕); chhiêⁿ-keh(牆格); chhiêⁿ-tû(牆櫥).

**nickname**, nâng tsũan kâi-miâⁿ(人撰个名); phì-sièⁿ kâi-miâⁿ(譬像个名).

**niece**, tie̍t-nńg(姪女); nńg-tie̍t(女姪). *(sister's daughter)*, gūa-seng-nńg(外甥女).

**niggardly**, kiâm-siap(鹹澀); kiâm(鹹); liẽn-siap(吝嗇); kien-liẽn(慳吝); chhiú-thâu tōiⁿ(手頭𠕇); siáu-khièn〔〕; niauh-siauh〔〕.

**night**, mêⁿ(夜). *last*, tsà-mêⁿ(昨夜). *to-night*, kim-mêⁿ(今夜); mêⁿ-hng(夜昏). *journey by*, kiâⁿ-mêⁿ-lōu(行夜路). *time*, mêⁿ--kùa(夜旰); mêⁿ--tsṳ́(夜鼠). *late at*, mêⁿ-âm(夜暗); keⁿ chhim(更深); àm(暗). *dress*, gu̍t-saⁿ(夗衫). *night-mare*, māng-kìⁿ-kúi(夢見鬼); chin-kìⁿ-kúi(真見鬼); bái-kúi teh(壓鬼壓). *nightly*, pâi-mêⁿ(排夜); pâi-mêⁿ-àm(排夜暗). *first half of night*, chiēⁿ-pùaⁿ-mêⁿ(上半夜).

**nimble**, *kha khin-khiáu; kha khin*, chhiú khùe(手課).

**nine**, káu(九); khùai(快). *nineteen*, tsa̍p-káu(十九).

**nip**, nihⁿ(捏). *(more severely)*, liàm(捻). *with nippers*, khîⁿ(鉗); koih(夾). *nippers*, thih-khîⁿ(鐵鉗); thih-kîⁿ(鐵鉗); niap-kiáⁿ(挾繭); nihⁿ-kiáⁿ(捏囝); kia̍p-kiáⁿ(夾囝); koih-kiáⁿ(夾囝).

**nipples**, nîⁿ-thâu(奶頭).

**nitre**, siau(硝).

**no**, m̄-sĩ(毋是); bô(無); màiⁿ(勿). *matter*, bô-lũn(無論); bô-chhiet-iàu(無切要); bô-huâng(無妨). *help for it*, bô-nãiⁿ-hô(無奈何); bô-pōu(無步). *nobody*, bô-nâng(無人). *nothing to eat*, bô-thang-chia̍h(無通食).

**noble**, tsun(尊); kùi(貴); tsun-kùi(尊貴).

**noble family**, tōa-ke(大家). *noble man*, ũ-chiak-ūi(有爵位); tãi-láu(大佬). *minded*, kháng-khài(慷慨).

**nod**, tak-thâu(點頭). *sleeping*, tak-sut-gu̍t(觸蟀夗).

**noise**, siaⁿ(聲); hiáng(響); kiè(叫). *make a great*, tshàu-nãuⁿ(吵鬧); hā-hā-kiè(下下叫); kā-kā-kiè(咳咳叫); kā-kā-jiáng(咬咬嚷).

**noisome**, õi-hāi-nâng(會害人). *(smell)*, tshàu-hièn(臭憲).

**nominal**, *merely*, ũ-miâⁿ bô-si̍t(有名無實); ũ-khî-miâⁿ bô-khî-si̍t(有其名無其實). *rank (brevet rank)*, khang-hâm(空銜).

**none**, bô(無); bô-che̍k-kâi(無一個); kâi-kâi-bô(個個無); tsǹg-kâi-bô〔〕.

**nonsense**, thèng-tàⁿ(聽呾); bô-sueh(無說); bô-chhêng bô-lí(無影無跡); hû-sueh(胡說).

**noon**, ji̍t tàu(日晝); ngõu-sî(午時); tng-ngóu(當午); chiàⁿ-ngóu(正午).

**noose**, *to make a*, thám-seⁿ-khou(毯生箍).

**north**, pak(北). *wind*, pak-huang(北方). *star*, pak-ke̍k(北極) (pak-táu(北斗) is Ursa Major). *N. E.*, tang-pak(東北). *of China*, pak-thâu(北頭).

**nose**, phīⁿ(鼻). *nostrils*, phīⁿ-khang(鼻空). *bridge*, phīⁿ-lêng-kut(鼻龍骨); phīⁿ-uaⁿ-kut(鼻鞍骨). *bleeding*, lâu phīⁿ-khang-hueh(流鼻空血). *stuffed*, phīⁿ sat(鼻塞). *running (coryza)*, chhek-tsúi(測水). *nosegay*, hue-kiû(花球); che̍k-pé-hue(一把花).

**notable**, hui-siêⁿ(非常); ũ-miâⁿ-siaⁿ(有名聲); tshut-thoh ĩ-siêⁿ(出脫異常); thiau-so̍k(挑俗); tshut-so̍k(出色); tshut-chèng(出众); tshut-lūi(出類); théng-pua̍t(挺拔).

**notch**, khih(缺). *in arrow*, hâm(含); ngám(眼).

**note**, *written*, kò-jī(告字). *musical*, ngóu-im la̍k-lu̍t(五音六律). *commentary*, tsù-kói(注解). *note down*, kì(記); kì-lo̍k(記錄). *notebook*, kì-phõu(記簿); tshûn-phõu(存簿); tsài-phõu(載簿). *money*, chîⁿ-phiè(錢票); ngṳ̂n-toaⁿ(銀單).

**notice**, *to*, tsai-thóiⁿ(知睇); tsai-kuan(知觀); kak-tshat(覺察). *when one is not noticing; unawares*, put-kak(不覺). *a public (advertisement)*, kàu-pe̍h(到白). *a public (proclamation)*, kò-sī(告示). *notify*, ta̍t-tsai(達知); thong-tsai(通知); pò-tsai(報知).

**notion**, ì-kièn(意見); î-sṳ̀(意思); siẽⁿ-thâu(想頭).

**notorious**, chèng-nâng só-tsai--kâi(众人所知个); tshàu-miâⁿ(臭名).

**nourish**, iáng(養); iáng-io̍k(養育); bú-iáng(撫養); chhī(飼).

**novel**, *a*, siáu-sueh(小說); gūa-tsṳ(外之); kóu-tn̄g(古傳).

**novice**, chheⁿ-chhiú(生手); o̍h-būe-se̍k(學未熟). *in religion*, tsho-ji̍p-kà(初入教).

**now**, hīn-kim(現今); chí-tsûn(此陣); chí-hûe(此回); taⁿ(今); hīn-tsãi(現在); tshṳ́-tsãi(此在); hīn-sî(現時); tshṳ́-sî(此時); ngán-tsôiⁿ(眼前); ngán-kim(眼今).

**nowhere**, múaⁿ-kò-bô(滿塊無); sì-tshù tshūe-bô(四厝覓無).

**nowise**, pẽng-bô(並無); tshûan-bô(全無); tuàn-bô(斷無).

**noxious**, ta̍k(毒); ak(惡); õi-hāi-nâng(會害人); lĩ-hāi(厲害).

**nuisance**, o-tso nah-sap-sièⁿ(污糟垃圾像); tshàu-mu̍eh(臭物); jiáu-luãn(擾亂); jiáu-tsak(擾作).

**nullify**, kui-bô(歸無); kui-tsò bô-ũ(歸做無有); hùe-ûi ou-ũ(化爲烏有).

**numb**, pì(痹); ngûi(危); ngûi-pì(危痹); hiâ-pì(霞痹); ngûi-ne̍k bõi-thiàⁿ(懸肉袂痛); hueh-khì kuàn-m̄-kàu(血氣慣毋到).

**number**, siàu(數). *even*, sang-siàu(雙數). *odd*, khia-siàu(奇數). *to*, sǹg-siàu(算數). *which*, tõiⁿ-kúi(第幾). *numberless*, sǹg-m̄-liáu(算毋了); m̄-pat-tò-sǹg(毋識倒算). *number ten*, tõiⁿ-tsa̍p(第十).

**numerals**, siàu-ma̍k-jī(數目字). *capital form*, tōa-siá(大寫). *common*, séⁿ-siá(省寫); sié-siá(小寫). *contracted*, bé-kiáⁿ(碼囝).

**numerous**, tsōi(㩼); tsa̍t(實). *like bees and ants*, zû-phang zû-hiã(如蜂如蟻).

**nun**, nîⁿ-kou(尼姑); hûe-siēⁿ-phûa(和尚婆). *nunnery*, nîⁿ-kou-am(尼姑庵); nńg-am(女庵); chẽⁿ-tn̂g(靜長).

**nuptials**, sêng-chhin(成親); sêng-hun(成婚); kat-hun(結婚); ha̍h-chhin(合親); phùe-chhin(配親); sin-hun(新婚). see MARRIAGE.

**nurse**, kan-ma(乳母); kan-bó(乳母); a-bó(阿母). *(in Swatow)*, a-má(阿媽). *milk-nurse*, niⁿ-bó(奶母). *nursling*, chia̍h-nĩⁿ-kiáⁿ(食奶囝).

**nut**, *walnut*, hu̍t-thô(核桃); khut-thô(屈桃). *ground-nut*, tī-tāu(地豆). *cocoa-nut*, gê-chí(牙子); iâ-chí(椰子). *shell*, khak(殼). *meat inside*, jîn(仁); ne̍k(肉). *nutmeg*, tāu-khòu(豆庫); lãu-hàu-chí(老孝子).

**nymph**, sien-nńg(仙女).

### O

**oak**, siãng-chhiū(上樹).

**oar**, chiéⁿ(槳). *one*, che̍k-pèⁿ-chiéⁿ(一柄槳); che̍k-ki-chiéⁿ(一枝槳). *blade of*, chiéⁿ-búe(槳尾); chiéⁿ-hie̍h(槳葉). *handle*, chiéⁿ-pèⁿ(槳柄); chiéⁿ-chhiú(槳手); chiéⁿ-thâu(槳頭). *cross pieee on handle*, chiéⁿ-tiah(槳摘). *pin (thole)*, chiéⁿ-tiam(槳砧). *loop fixing oar to pin*, chiéⁿ-khau(槳摳). *to row with*, kò-chiéⁿ(划槳). *to ship, for rowing*, kah-chiéⁿ(甲槳).

**oath**, sī(誓). *to take*, li̍p-sī(立誓); huat-sī(發誓); tùi-thiⁿ mêng-sī(對天明誓). *to take (solemn covenant between persons)*, mêng-sī(明誓). *an imprecation*, chiù-tsūa(咒誓).

**oatmeal**, be̍h-hún(麥粉).

**obdurate**, sim-tn̂g ngẽ(心腸硬); ngẽ-sèⁿ(硬性); ngẽ-chip(硬執); chip-phiah(執癖); chip-áu(執拗); chip-it(執一); chip-mîⁿ put-ngõ(執糜不悟); chip-thì(執滯).

**obeisance**, *pài-lói; kũi*, kũiⁿ(跪); khàu-thâu(叩頭); pài-kũiⁿ(拜跪).

**obey**, sũn(順); sũn-mẽng(順命); tsun-mẽng(遵命); thiaⁿ(聽); thiaⁿ-mẽng(聽命); tshông-mẽng(從命); hõng-mẽng(奉命). *the law*, tsun-huap(遵法); tsun-lu̍t(遵律). *obedient*, sũn; sũn-sũn(順順); sũn-tshông(順從); thiaⁿ-nâng-tàⁿ(聽人呾).

**object**, *an*, mu̍eh-kiãⁿ(物件). *or purpose*, sim-só-hiàng(心所向); sim-só-àiⁿ(心所愛); sim-só-nguãn(心所願); sim-chì(心志); chì-nguãn(志願); ì-hiàng(意向).

**object**, *to*, m̄-nguãn(毋願); tsó-chí(阻止). *to (altercation)*, poh-khùi(駁氣). *to (in argument)*, piẽn-poh(辯駁). *what objection can there be*, ũ-sĩ-mih huâng-gāi(有是乜妨礙). *I have no objection*, uá na̍p-ì(我合意); uá hàuⁿ(我好).

**oblation**, hõng-sîn kâi-mu̍eh-kiãⁿ(奉神个物件).

**obligation**, pńg-hūn(本分); pńg-téng(本等).

**oblige (force)**, mién-kiáng(勉強); ngẽ-lia̍h(硬掠); khiâng-àiⁿ(強愛); khiâng-pek(強迫). *obliged to do*, put-tit-íⁿ(不得已); bõi-tit-mién(袂得免); m̄-káⁿ m̃-tsò(毋敢毋做); khut-tshông(屈從). *obliging*, õi-tsò-nâng(會做人); ũ-nâng-chhêng(有人情); nâng-chiâⁿ hó(人成好); hó-chhêng hó-ì(好情好意). *he conferred an obligation on me*, i ũ-nâng-chhêng tõ-uá-kò(伊有人情到我股); i ũ-ṳn-hũi tõ-uá-kò(伊有恩惠在我塊). *I am much obliged to you*, kám-ṳn put-chhién(感恩不淺); to-siā(多謝); kám-siā(感謝); tsōi-siā(㩼謝); chhim-liãm(深念); m̄-káⁿ buâng-chhêng(毋敢忘情).

**oblique**, siâ(邪); tshúa(歪); uai-tshúa(歪斜); uai-siâ(歪斜); khi(欺); m̄-chiàⁿ(毋正); m̄-ti̍t(毋直).

**obliterate**, hú-tiāu〔〕; tiám-tiāu(點掉); kôu-tiāu(糊掉); buah-tiāu(抹掉).

**oblong**, tn̂g-huang(長方).

**obloquy**, mak--tie̍h nâng-miâⁿ-siaⁿ(衊着人名聲); húiⁿ-pãng(誹謗); iâu-pãng(謠謗); lêng-zo̍k(凌辱).

**obscene**, siâ-îm(邪淫). *language*, tshou-siaⁿ(粗聲); káng-tshou lô-tshò(講粗老草). *books*, îm-tsṳ(淫書). *plays*, îm-hì(淫戲).

**obscure**, mông(摸); hiu-miáuⁿ(休妙); m̄-hīn(毋現); m̄-mêng(毋明); m̄-tshut-sek(毋出色). *dwell in obscurity*, ṳ́n-kṳ(隱居). *(much greater degree)*, mi̍t-chiah(密跡).

**obsequies**, sng-sṳ̄(喪事); pe̍h-sṳ̄(白事). see FUNERAL.

**obsequious**, hông-ngêng(逢迎); hõng-sêng(奉承); pui-thiám(陪諂); thiám-mĩⁿ(諂媚); khá-mĩⁿ(巧謎).

**observatory**, huan-chheⁿ-thâi(觀星臺).

**observe**, thóiⁿ(看); kuan(關). *law*, siú-huap(守法).

**obsolete**, kū--liáu bô-ēng(舊了無用); hùi(費). *characters*, kòu-jī(舊字); phiah-jī(僻字).

**obstacle**, hûang-gāi(妨礙); tsó-keh(阻隔). *there is no*, bô-hûang(無妨).

**obstinate**, kù-chip(固執); chip-thì(執滯); kien-chip(堅執); chip-phiah(執癖); chip-áu(執拗); ke̍h-phiah(逆僻); áu-phiah(拗僻); kuài-phiah(怪僻); chip-ì(執意); khu-thì(拘滯); thì-nĩⁿ〔〕.

**obstruct**, tsa̍h(閘); nôaⁿ(閙); nôaⁿ-tsó(阻左); tso̍ih(截); tsó-keh(阻隔); kòiⁿ-keh(間隔). *a road*, tsa̍h-lōu(閘路); nôaⁿ-lōu(阻路); tso̍ih-lōu(截路). *wind*, tsa̍h-huang(閘防). *view*, chia-tsa̍h(遮閘); tsa̍h thóiⁿ-m̄-kìⁿ(遮睇毋見).

**obtain**, tit(得); tit--tie̍h(得着); tshú(取); na̍p(納); tshūe--tie̍h(覓着).

**obtrusive**, thèng-ji̍p(聽入); zũan-ji̍p(任入); thèng-tiaⁿ thèng-tsũang(聽撞聽撞); tshàm-ngân(讖言).

**obtuse**, lú-tũn(魯鈍); ngûi-phûe(危皮).

**obviate**, mién(免); pī(避); tṳ̂(除); ṳ̃-pī(預避).

**obvious**, mêng-pe̍h(明白).

**occasion**, *no*, mién(免); mín-ēng(免用); khó-íⁿ put-pit(可以不必). *what*, ũ sĩ-mih kù-sṳ̄(有乜故何事); sĩ-mih uân-kù(是乜緣故). *this*, chí-hûe(此回); chí-pái(只擺); chí-tshṳ̀(只次); tshṳ́-tshṳ̀(此次). *on every occasion*, pâi-sî(排時); pâi-hûe(排回); sî-put-sî(時不時); sam-put-sî(三不時); múeⁿ-sî(每時). *take*, chiã-sì(藉勢); sêng-ki(乘機); sêng-ki-hũe(乘機會); chiã-kù(藉故); chieh-tuan(借端); sêng-khiah(承隙); sêng-sì(乘勢); sêng chí-kâi sṳ̄-kù(成此個事故); chiã-tuan(藉端). *occasionally*, ũ-tiâng-sî(有當時); ũ-sî(有時); che̍k-ē pùaⁿ-ē(一下半下).

**occiput**, aũ-táu(後斗); chím-kut(枕骨).

**occult**, pì-bāt(祕密); pì-mi̍t(祕密).

**occupation**, pńg-ngia̍p(本業); chhiú-ngia̍p(手業); sṳ̄-ngia̍p(事業); chhiú-gōi(手藝); gōi-ngia̍p(藝業). *literary*, bûn-gōi(文藝). *military*, bú-gōi(武藝).

**ocean**, tōa-iêⁿ(大洋); tōa-hái(大海). *cross*, kùe-hái(過海); kùe-ou-tsúi(過烏水).

**occurrence**, che̍k-tsuang-sṳ̄(一桩事); che̍k-kiãⁿ-sṳ̄(一件事).

**octagonal**, poih-kak-hêng(八角形).

**oculist**, ngán-khue sin-seⁿ(眼科先生); ma̍k-khue sin-seⁿ(目科先生); ui-ma̍k sin-seⁿ(醫目先生).

**odd**, *seventy and odd*, chhit-tsa̍p-gūa(七雜外); chhit-tsa̍p-tshut(七雜出). *not even*, khia(奇). *an odd shoe*, kou-chiah-ôi(孤隻鞋); to̍k-chiah(獨隻); toaⁿ-chiah(單隻); khia-chiah(奇隻). *peculiar*, tshut-khî(出奇); koh-iēⁿ(各樣). *odds and ends*, lân-san(零些); lân-ló(零些); tshàm-tshùi mu̍eh-kiãⁿ(懺碎物件).

**ode**, si(詩); ko(歌). *Book of Odes*, si-kiaⁿ(詩經).

**odious**, khó-ù(可惡); tshūa-nâng-lóu(惹人惱).

**odour**, bī(味); khì-bī(氣味); phang(芳); hiang(香).

**of**, *the water of the sea*, hái-tsúi(海水); hái kâi-tsúi(海个水); hái-tói kâi-tsúi(海底个水). *a man of wealth*, ũ-chîⁿ-tshâi kâi-nâng(有錢財个人). *of course*, tsṳ̃-jiên(自然); thien-jiên(天然).

**off**, *cut*, kuah-tñg(割斷). *far*, hñg-hñg(遠遠). *run*, tsáu--khṳ́(走去).

**offend**, tit-tsũe(得罪); tit-tsõ--tie̍h(得坐着); huãm-tsũe(犯罪); tshok-huãm(觸犯). *offended*, m̄-hàuⁿ(毋好); m̄-huaⁿ-hí(毋歡喜); kièn-kuài(見怪). *offensive smell*, tshàu-hièn(臭憲); ùe-khì(穢氣). *far too easily offended*, chheⁿ-mīn(青面); chheⁿ-mīn-hóuⁿ(青面虎).

**offer**, *as price*, tshut-kè(出嫁). *as reward*, hṳ́(許); tshut-siéⁿ-keh(出賞隔); tshut-hue-âng(出花紅). *a present*, sàng-lói(送禮). *tribute*, chìn-kòng(進貢); chìn-hièn(進獻). *offer it to him*, mn̄g i àiⁿ--mé(問伊愛么). *make an offering*, hõng(奉); hièn(獻); hièn-hõng(獻奉); keng-hõng(供奉); keng-hièn(供獻); kèng-hõng(敬奉); kèng-hièn(敬獻).

**office**, cheh-hūn(職分); kuaⁿ-cheh(官職); cheh-jĩm(職任); cheh-sṳ̄(職事). *enter*, chiẽⁿ-jīm(上任). *one term of*, che̍k-jīm(一任). *continue for another term*, liên-jīm(連任); ngûan-jīm(原任). *degrade but retain in office*, keh-cheh lâu-jīm(隔職留任). *put out of*, keh-jīm(隔任). *go out of*, lī-jīm(離任). *waiting for a vacant*, hāu-jīm-khueh(候任缺).

**office (counting-house)**, siá-jī-pâng(寫字房). *a public office (building)*, gê-mn̂g(衙門).

**officer**, kuaⁿ(官); kuaⁿ-hú(官府). *fellow*, tâng-liâu(銅僚). *military*, bú-kuaⁿ(武官).

**official**, *document*, bûn-tsṳ(文書). *reply*, phoi-hûe(批回).

**officiate**, lí-sṳ̄(理事); phōiⁿ-sṳ̄(辦事). *officious*, hàuⁿ-tshap-sṳ̄(好插事).

**often**, ē-ē(下下); lú-lú(屢屢); tshṳ̀-tshṳ̀(次次); múeⁿ-múeⁿ(每每); sî-sî(時時); siêⁿ-siêⁿ(常常); tsōi-hûe(㩼回); tsōi-pái(㩼擺); tsōi-tiâng-sî(㩼當時); ke-ke-hãng(加加項).

**ogle**, siâ-ma̍k-chìⁿ(斜目箭); su̍t-ma̍k(術目).

**oh**, *indeed!*, *õ*, sĩ àn-chièⁿ-seⁿ(是按此樣生). *in grief or pain*, ai-a(哀啊).

**oil**, iû(油). *bottle*, iû-pân(瓶). *press*, iû-chhia(油車). *to oil*, buah-iû(抹油); chhit-iû(漆油); iû(油). *kerosene*, húe-tsúi(火水); húe-tsúi-iû(火水油).

**ointment**, ko-ie̍h(膏藥). *apply*, tah-ko-ie̍h(搭膏藥); buah-ko-ie̍h(抹膏藥).

**old**, kū(舊). *in years*, lãu(老). *from of old*, tsṳ̃-kóu(自古). *how old are you*, jie̍h-tsōi-hùe(若㩼歲); kùi-keⁿ(貴庚); tshun-chhiu jie̍h-kau(春秋幾交). *which is older*, tî-nâng-tōa(底人大). *one year older*, tōa che̍k-hùe(大一歲). *an old friend*, kū-iú(舊友); lãu-iú(老友); kū-kau(舊交). *old gentleman*, lãu-nâng-tek(老人德).

**oleander**, tsõ-ngûan-tek(橡皮竹).

**olives**, káⁿ-náⁿ(橄欖).

**omelet**, koi-nñg luah chiâⁿ-tieⁿ(雞卵烙成張); koi-nñg-piáⁿ(雞卵餅).

**omen**, tiãu(兆); ki-tiãu(機兆). *good*, kit-tiãu(吉兆). *bad*, hiong-tiãu(凶兆).

**omit**, sit(失); lāu-tiāu(漏掉); làng-tiāu(朗掉); kau-lau̍h-tiāu(交落掉).

**omnipotent**, bô-só put-lêng(無所不能); tshûan-lêng(全能).

**omnipresent**, bô-só put-tõ(無所不在).

**omniscience**, bô-só put-tsai(無所不知); bô-só put-tshat(無所不察).

**on**, *the house top*, tõ tshù-téng(在厝頂). *the road*, tõ-lōu-chiēⁿ(在路上). *the water*, tõ-tsúi-mīn(在水面). *his arrival*, tsho-kàu(初到); che̍k-ē-kàu(一下到). *purpose*, tiãu-tsuan(掉專); ũ-ì(有意); tsuan-àiⁿ(專愛). *the contrary*, tin-tò(顛倒); húan-tńg(反轉). *horseback*, khiâ-bé(騎馬).

**once**, che̍k-tshṳ̀(一次); che̍k-tńg(一轉); che̍k-pái(一遍); che̍k-hûe(一回). *once upon a time*, soiⁿ-tiâng-sî(先當時); tng-sî(當時). *all at*, che̍k-ē(一下); tsò-che̍k-ē(做一下); tsôi-tsôi(齊齊). *at once*, sûi-sî(隨時); sûi-chiet(隨即).

**one**, che̍k(一). *one by one*, it-it(一一); ta̍k-it(逐一). *third*, saⁿ-hūn tshú-che̍k(三分取一). *eyed*, to̍k-ma̍k(獨目). *handed*, toaⁿ-chiah-chhiú(單隻手). *one's own*, ka-kī-kâi(家己个). *oneself*, ka-kī(家己); pńg-sin(本身); chhin-sin(親身). *to take upon oneself without authority*, tsṳ̃-tsuan(自專).

**onion**, tshang-thâu(蔥頭).

**only**, chí(只); put-kùe(不過); put-gūa(不外); kan-kan(剛剛); to̍k-to̍k(獨獨); toaⁿ-toaⁿ(單單); tiāⁿ-tiāⁿ(定定). *son*, toaⁿ-kâi-kiáⁿ(單個囝); toaⁿ-toaⁿ seⁿ chí-kâi-kiáⁿ tiāⁿ(單單生此個囝定).

**onset**, thâu-tīn(頭陣); tng-thâu-tīn(當頭陣); sien-hong(先鋒); ke-húe sie-chih(家伙相助).

**onward**, *to go*, chìn-tsôiⁿ(進前); tsôiⁿ-chìn(前進); chìn-pōu(進步).

**ooze**, sia̍p-lāu(洩漏).

**opaque**, m̄-siũ-chiè(毋受照); kng thàu-m̄-kùe(光透毋過); àm-chieh thàu-m̄-kùe(暗遮透毋過).

**open**, khui(開). *a letter*, thiah-sìn(拆信); thiah-khui(拆開). *out*, tháu-khui(㪗開). *eyes*, peh-khui-ma̍k(掰開目); ma̍k-chiu peh-kim(目睭掰金). *a bood*, iãuⁿ-khui〔〕; hien-khui(顯開); tién-khui(展開). *burst, as door*, léng-khui(推開); phùa-khui(破開). *a cover*, iãuⁿ-kùa〔〕. *the bowels*, lĩ-tãi-piẽn(利大辯); chia̍h-lĩ-ie̍h(食利藥); chia̍h liâng-sià kâi-ie̍h(食凉瀉个藥). *openwork*, lang-lang(朗朗). *handed*, chhiú-phāng lang(手縫朗); chhiú-phāng khùaⁿ(手縫寬). *an opening*, khang(空); khiah(隙); phāng(縫); phāng-khiah(縫隙); mn̂g-lōu(門路); tshùi(喙). *openly*, hién-mêng(顯明); tng-mīn(當面); tõ-pe̍h-ji̍t(在白日); kng-kng mêng-mêng(光光明明).

**opera**, tsò-hì chhiè-khek(做戲唱曲).

**ophthalmia**, ma̍k-chiu âng-thiàⁿ(目睭紅痛); ma̍k pãu-thiàⁿ(目曝痛).

**opinionative**, chip ka-kī kâi-ì(執家己个意); chip-phiah(執癖).

**opinion**, ì-kièn(意見). *your*, kau-kièn(高見). *my*, ngô-kièn(愚見); phí-kièn(鄙見); pĩ-kièn(敝見). *assent to one's*, hũ-hõ(互和).

**opium**, a-phièn(鴉片). *crude*, a-phièn-thôu(鴉片塗). *prepared*, a-phièn-ko(鴉片糕). *small pellet*, a-phièn-phã(鴉片泡). *to smoke*, chia̍h-a-phièn-hun(食鴉片薰). *shop*, a-phièn-phã(鴉片泡). *miserable confirmed opium smoker*, a-phièn-kúi(鴉片鬼). *craving for*, a-phièn-ngièn(鴉片癮); a-phièn-ín(鴉片引). *give up smoking*, keh-a-phièn(格鴉片).

**opponent**, tùi-thâu(對頭); chhiû-te̍k(仇敵).

**opportunity**, ki-hũe(機會). *to embrace an*, sêng-ki-hũe(乘機會); sêng-sì(乘勢). *opportunely*, sũn-piẽn(順便); huang-piẽn(方便); sêng-piẽn(乘便).

**oppose**, ûi-nge̍k(違逆); khàng-kṳ̃(抗拒); tí-tng(抵當); tí-te̍k(抵敵); tùi-te̍k(對敵).

**opposite**, siang-huán(相反); tùi-mīn(對面); sie-tùi(相對).

**oppress**, khiâng-iap(強壓); ngẽ-iap(硬壓); khi-iap(欺壓); khi-hũ(欺負); uan-uáng(冤枉). *oppressive*, khóu-to̍k(苦毒); khóu-ngia̍k(苦虐). *oppressive (extortion)*, khek-pak(刻剝).

**opprobrium**, lêng-zo̍k(凌辱); sit-zo̍k(失辱).

**or**, ho̍k(或); ho̍k-sĩ(或是); at-ho̍k(抑或). *is it or not*, sĩ a-m̄-sĩ(是抑毋是). *either you or I must go*, lṳ́-uá nõⁿ-nâng tie̍h-ũ che̍k-nâng-khṳ̀(汝我二人着有一人去); lṳ́ m̃-khṳ̍ uà chiũ-tie̍h-khṳ̀(汝毋去我就着去).

**opulent**, ũ-chîⁿ(有錢); huat-tshâi(發財); pù(富); pù-ũ(富有); pù-kãu(富厚); pù-tsok(富足).

**orange**, kaⁿ(柑); tãi-kit(大桔). *common*, soh-kaⁿ(雪柑). *loose-skinned*, phàⁿ-tháng-kaⁿ(怕桶柑); bi̍t-tháng-kaⁿ(蜜桶柑); phòng-tháng-kaⁿ(碰桶柑). *peel*, kaⁿ-phûe(柑皮). *jam*, chhêng-ko(橙糕). *very small orange*, kit(桔); kit-kiáⁿ(桔囝); tiâm-kit(甜桔); sng-kit(酸桔).

**orb**, *of moon*, gu̍eh-lûn(月輪); gu̍eh-îⁿ(月圓).

**orchard**, kúeⁿ-chí-hn̂g(果子園).

**order**, tsôiⁿ-ãu(前後); thâu-búe(頭尾); tshṳ̀-sũ(次序); tshṳ̀-tõiⁿ(次第); tsâng-tshṳ̀(層次). *put in*, an-pâi(安排); uaⁿ-pâi(鞍排); pái-hó(擺好); uaⁿ-pái-hó(安擺好); an-tùn-hó(安頓好); chèng-tũn(整頓); chiáⁿ-tũn(整頓); chiáⁿ-lí(整理); siu-si̍p(收拾); siu-chiáⁿ(修整); sṳ̃-lí(伺理); siu-si̍p iap-thiap kui-ūi(收拾壓貼規位). *in order*, tsôi-chiáⁿ(齊整).

**order**, *to*, mẽng(命); lẽng(令); hun-hù(吩咐); hàm(喊); sái(使); kiè(叫). *an order for money*, ngṳ̂n-toaⁿ(銀單).

**ordure**, pùn(糞); sái(屎).

**organ**, khîm(琴); tōa-khîm(大琴).

**origin**, pńg(本); pńg-nguân(本原); kṳn-pńg(根本); ngûan-iû(原由); ngûan-kù(原故); ngûan-in(原因). *originally*, pńg-lâi(本來); ngûan-lâi(原來); ngûan-sí(原是); tsho-thâu(初頭). *originate*, tì-khí(底氣). *with you*, iû-lṳ́ tì-khí(由汝致起).

**ornament**, siu-sek(修飾); bûn-sek(文飾); tsuang-sek(裝飾). *ornamental*, hó-thóiⁿ(好睇); hó-thóiⁿ-ngiá(好體雅); múiⁿ-kuan(美冠); ngiá-kuan(雅冠).

**orphan**, bô-pẽ-âi(無父無母); kou-jî(孤兒); kou-tsṳ́(孤子).

**orthodox**, chiàⁿ-kà(正教).

**oscillate**, *as pendulum*, hit-lâi hit-khṳ̀(許來許去).

**ostentatious**, hàuⁿ-thâng-huang(好蟲風); hàuⁿ-iâng-khì(好揚氣); hàuⁿ-sái phài-thâu(好使派頭); hàuⁿ-pái(好擺); hàuⁿ-tsuang-pái(好裝擺); tsuang-khiang(裝腔). *(of one's walk)*, hàuⁿ-iê-pái(好搖擺).

**ostrich**, thô-chiáu(鴕鳥).

**other**, pa̍t(別). *others*, pa̍t-nâng(別人). *any others*, huân-ũ a-bô(還有亞無). *the others*, khî-ṳ̂(其餘); liáu--kâi(了个). *otherwise*, pa̍t-iēⁿ(別樣); m̄-sĩ chièⁿ-seⁿ(毋是此樣生); iā-m̄-sĩ(也毋是).

**otter**, thuah(獺); hái-thuah(海獺); tsúi-thuah(水獺).

**ought**, eng-kai(應該); tie̍h(着); eng-tng(應當); pńg-téng tie̍h(本等着).

**ounce**, niéⁿ(兩).

**our**, uán--kâi(阮个); nán--kâi(咱个). see WE.

**out**, gūa(外); tshut(出). *go*, tshut--khṳ̀(出去). *go outside*, tshut-khṳ̀-kháu(出去口). *of order*, zṳ̂-zṳ̂(挐挐); hũn-tsa̍p(混雜); hũn-luãn(混亂). *outdo*, iâⁿ(贏). *outside*, gūa-mīn(外面); gūa-kháu(外口); gūa-thâu(外頭).

**outrage**, pũe-lí huãm-hūn(倍理犯分); sún-hāi(損害). *outrageous*, bô-huap-tōu(無法度); hùi-lí hūn-gūa(費理分外).

**oval**, siẽn-chí-iēⁿ(腎子樣); tn̂g-siēn(長善).

**oven**, húe-lôu(火爐); pek-lôu(焙爐); pue-lôu(焙爐).

**over**, kùe(過); gūa(外); tshut(出); ṳ̂(予); tshûn(存); tṳ̂(除). *and above*, lêng-gūa(另外); huân-liáu(還了). *all over with mud*, che̍k-sin-thôu(一身塗). *night*, kùe-mêⁿ(過夜). *ripe*, khah-se̍k(恰熟); khah-kùe-se̍k(恰過熟); khah-kùe-lâu(恰過老). *fall overboard*, pua̍h-lo̍h-tsúi(跋落水). *overbearing*, kiau-ngãu(驕傲); ̂khiâng-iap(磯壓). *overcast sky*, thiⁿ chhiẽⁿ-hûn(天上昏); thiⁿ-sek hun-àm(天色昏暗); thiⁿ khàm-khàm(天暗暗); thiⁿ so-tô(天色塗). *overdone*, pû khah-mîⁿ(曝恰綿); khah-kùe-húe(恰過火). *overflow*, iah--tshut(溢出); lâu--tshut(流出); múaⁿ--tshut(滿出). *overflow (to spout up)*, chhèng--khí-lâi(衝起來). *overhanging wall*, ngâm-chhiêⁿ(巖牆); chhiêⁿ hiám àiⁿ-tó(牆險愛倒). *overhear*, chẽⁿ-thiaⁿ(靜聽). *overshadow*, chia-ìm(遮蔭); pì-ìm(庇蔭). *overtake*, jiāu--tie̍h(擾着); tui-tie̍h(追着); kúaⁿ--tie̍h(趕着). *overthrow*, léng-tó(推倒); tó-khap(倒蓋).

**owe**, khiàm(欠); khiàm-chîⁿ(欠錢); khiàm-chè(欠債).

**owl**, ngiau-thâu-chiáu(貓頭鳥).

**own**, ka-kī-kâi(家己个); pńg(本); chhin(親). *with one's own hand*, chhin-chhiú(親手). *in one's own person*, pńg-sin(本身); chhin-sin(親身).

**own**, *to*, jīn(認).

**ox**, iam-gû(閹牛); iam-gû-kóu(閹牛牯).

### P

**pace**, pōu(步); hua̍h(伐). *large*, tōa-hua̍h(大步).

**pacify**, khn̍g-nâng màiⁿ-khì(勸人勿去); kiâⁿ-hûa(行和); khng-hûa(勸和); khǹg-tshú〔〕. *Pacific ocean*, thài-phêng-iêⁿ(太平洋).

**pack**, pau(包); phah-pau(打包); tsuang(裝); siu-sip-bûa(收拾抹). *tea*, tsuang-tê(裝茶). *in a box*, tsuang-lo̍h-sieⁿ(裝落箱). *packing box*, tsuang-sieⁿ(裝箱).

**paddle**, jiê(漿). *to*, phẽ-tsûn(扒船). *a dragon-boat*, phẽ-lêng-tsûn(扒龍船).

**paddy**, chhek(粟). *growing*, ng(秧); tiũ(稻); tâ(禾). *fields*, tshân(田). *bird*, pe̍h-liãu-si(白鷺絲).

**padlock**, só-thâu(鎖頭).

**page**, *of book*, che̍k-mīn(一面). *on the block*, che̍k-póiⁿ(一半), che̍k-kò-póiⁿ(一块半).

**pagoda**, thah(塔). *literary*, khue-chheⁿ-koh(科青閣); khue-chheⁿ-lâu(科青樓); bûn-chiang-koh(文昌閣); bûn-chhiang-koh(文昌閣)

**pail**, tsúi-tháng(水桶); tiàu-tháng(吊桶).

**pain**, thiàⁿ(痛). *to ease*, chí-thìaⁿ(指痛). *painful*, õi-thìaⁿ(會痛); kan-khóu(艱苦); chhi-tshám(淒慘); chhi-liâng(淒凉).

**paint**, iû(油); tshat(漆). *to*, sái-iû(使油); iû(油); tshat(漆). *painter*, iû-tshat sai-pẽ(油漆西父); sái-iû sai-pẽ(使油司阜); iû-mu̍eh sai-pẽ(油物司阜). *an artist*, ūe-ūe sin-seⁿ(畫畫先生).

**pair**, *a*, che̍k-sang(一雙); che̍k-tùi(一對). *to*, phùe(配); phùe-ha̍h(配合); phit-phùe(匹配).

**palace**, uâng-keng(王宮).

**palanauin**, kīe(轎).

**palataole**, hó-chia̍h(好食); ha̍h-tshùi(合喙); suah-tshùi〔〕; suáng-kháu(爽口).

**pale**, mīn pe̍h-siauh(面白削); mīn chheⁿ-liau(面青了); n̂g-mīn(黃面). *turn*, mīn pièn-chheⁿ(面變青) .

**palette**, thiâu-sek-ti̍h(調色碟).

**paling**, lân-kan(欄杆); lân-kan-chí(欄杆子); ba̍k-tsa̍h(木閘); lî-tsa̍h(籬閘); ûi-lî(圍籬); ûi-tsa̍h(圍閘).

**pall**, kài-kuaⁿ-phũe(蓋官被).

**palm**, tsang-chhiū(棕樹); tsó-chhiū(棗樹). *(cocoa-nut)*, kuang-lâng-chhiū(桄榔樹); iâ-chhiū(椰樹).

**palm**, *of hand*, chhiú-tói(手底); chhiú-sim(手心); chhiú-chiéⁿ(手掌). *palmistry*, sièⁿ-chhiú-hûn(上手痕).

**palpitate**, sim thiàu(心跳); sim-kuaⁿ pok-pok-thiàu(心肝卜卜跳); sim-kuaⁿ-thâu pok-pok-thiàu(心肝頭卜卜跳).

**palsy**, nńg-nîⁿ(軟疕); nńg-huang(軟風); tòng-huang(凍風). *(one side)*, kuàn-pien(痒癲).

**pan**, tiáⁿ(鼎); thih-ue(鐵鍋); seⁿ-ue(鍟鍋).

**perspiration**, kūaⁿ(汗). *bad smelling, of hand or foot*, kha-sie̍h(骹液); chhìu-sie̍h(漱石). *cold*, chhìn-kūaⁿ(凊汗). *to absorb*, sò-kūaⁿ(疏汗); tsṳ̀-kūaⁿ(滋汗). *bad smell of*, kūaⁿ-sng(汗酸); tshàu-kūaⁿ-sng(臭汗酸). *to encourage*, huat-kūaⁿ(發汗). *to encourage (by warm drink or medicine)*, piáu-kūaⁿ(表汗). *to encourage (by warm covering)*, hip-kūaⁿ(翕汗). *perspire*, lâu-kūaⁿ(流汗); tshut-kūaⁿ(出汗).

**poem**, si(詩). *a*, che̍k-síu-si(一首詩); che̍k-phien-si(一篇詩). *to compose a*, tsò-si(作詩). *poet*, si-ong(詩翁); si-jîn(詩人); si-kheh(詩客); tshâi-tsṳ́(才子).

**point**, chiam(尖); hong(鋒); búe(尾); tshùi(喙). *cut to a*, phoi-chiam(批尖); siah-chiam(削尖). *of a knife*, to-chiam(刀尖); to-hong(刀鋒); to-búe(刀尾). *pointed*, chiam-chiam(尖尖).

**point**, *to*, chí(指); kí(指); kí-thóiⁿ(指看); chí-tiāⁿ(指定); kí-tiāⁿ(紀定). *a book*, tiám-tsṳ. tiám-tsṳ-chheh(點書點書冊). *out an error*, chí-mîⁿ(指爛); kí-phùa(指破).

**poison**, ta̍k(毒); ta̍k-ie̍h(毒藥). *to*, lo̍h-ta̍k-ie̍h(落毒藥); ie̍h-sí-nâng(藥死人). *fish*, ie̍h-hṳ̂(藥魚). *calculated to prove fatal in a certain time*, hãn-ie̍h(限藥).

**poker**, húe-chhe(火叉).

**pole**, *for carrying*, phoi-taⁿ(批擔); pêⁿ-taⁿ(扁擔); khat-taⁿ(刻擔); chiam-taⁿ(尖擔). *(bamboo)*, tek-thûi(竹槌). *long bamboo*, tek-ko(竹篙). *to pole a boat*, theⁿ-tsûn(撐船).

**pole**, *North*, Pak-ke̍k(北極). *star*, pak-sîn(北辰).

**polecat**, hôu-lâi-ngiau(狐狸貓); tshàu-ngiau(臭貓).

**police**, chhe-hia̍h(差役); ngûan-chhe(員差); a-tsóng(阿總); pan-thâu(班頭).

**polish**, bûa-kng(磨光); chhiù-kng(漱光). *polished*, kng-ku̍t(光滑).

**polite**, hiáu-lí(曉理); ũ-lói-mãuⁿ(有禮貌); ũ-lói-ngî(有禮儀); ũ-lói(有禮). *as phrase*, bûn-ngiá(文雅). *to fail in politeness*, sit-lói(失禮).

**politics**, kok-chèng(國政); chèng-sṳ̃(政事).

**pollen**, hue-hún(花粉).

**pollute**, mak--tie̍h nah-sap(衊着垃圾); u-jiám(污染); jiám-u(染污); jiám--tie̍h nah-sap(染着垃圾); u-ùe--tie̍h(污穢着).

**polypus**, *in the nose*, phīⁿ-lêng(鼻能); phīⁿ-tsûa(鼻蛇).

**pomatum**, hiang-iû(香油); buah-thâu-iû(撥頭油); tê-iû(茶油); lêng-hieⁿ-iû(靈香油).

**pomegranate**, sie̍h-liû(石榴).

**pomp**, hûan-hua(繁華); iông-hûa(榮華); iông-kùi(榮貴).

**pond**, tì(池). *for fish*, hṳ̂-tî(魚池).

**ponder**, tóu-lãi-siẽⁿ(肚內想); àm-chẽⁿ-siẽⁿ(暗靜想); chẽⁿ-siẽⁿ(靜想); mi̍t-siẽⁿ(密想); tîm-ngîm(沉吟); tîm-sṳ chẽⁿ-siẽⁿ(沉思靜想); chim-chiak(斟酌).

**pony**, bé(馬); sòi-chiah-bé(細隻馬).

**pool**, khut(窟); tî(池).

**poop**, *of ship*, tsûn-búe-lâu(船尾樓).

**poor**, phîn(貧); khiông(窮); kêng(窮); khiau(磽); bô-chîⁿ(無錢); phîn-khiông(貧窮); khiau-kêng(磽窮). *to help the poor*, chín-chi phîn-khiông(賑濟貧窮). *in spirit*, hṳ-sim(虛心). *poorhouse*, phóu-chì-īⁿ(普濟院).

**poppy**, eng-chhek-hue(鶯測花). *pods*, eng-chhek-khak(鶯測麴)..

**populace**, sù-mîn(庶民); peh-sèⁿ(百姓). *popular*, so̍k(俗); tong-thâu(東頭); sî-kiâⁿ(時行); ha̍h-sî-chèng(合時政).

**population**, nâng-teng(人丁). *what is the*, jie̍h-tsōi húe-tsàu(若㩼火灶); pńg-hieⁿ nâng-mue̍h jie̍h-tsōi(本鄉人物若㩼); kùi-tī nâng-mue̍h jie̍h-tsōi(貴地人物若㩼). *populous*, nâng-mue̍h tsōi(人物㩼); tsa̍t(實).

**porcelain**, hûi(缶); jiâu-khùi(窯器); jiâu-khì(窯器).

**porch**, thap-tóu mn̂g-lâu(塌肚門樓); liáng-lâng(兩廊).

**porcupine**, hô-tṳ(荷豬).

**pork**, tṳ-ne̍k(豬肉); tṳ-bah(豬肉). *fat of*, pe̍h-ne̍k(白肉). *lean of*, chiàⁿ-ne̍k(豬肉).

**pores**, môⁿ-kńg-tshng(毛管瘡); môⁿ-khang(毛空); môⁿ-kńg-khang(毛管空).

**porpoise**, thûn-hṳ̂(豚魚); pe̍h-gôu-hṳ̂(白吳魚).

**porridge**, be̍h-kho̍h(麥殼).

**port**, káng-kháu(港口); pou-thâu(埠頭). *port-holes*, phàu-khang(炮空).

**portal**, *honorary*, têng(亭); têng-piáu(亭表).

**portentous**, hiong-tiãu(凶兆); kuài-ĩ(怪異).

**porter**, pé-mn̂g(把門); thóiⁿ-mn̂g(睇門); siú-mn̂g(守門); chiéⁿ-mn̂g(掌門). *carrier of burdens,* taⁿ-kang(擔工); taⁿ-tàⁿ-nâng(擔擔人); thiau-hu(挑夫); taⁿ-kieh(擔腳).

**portico**, mn̂g-lâu(門樓).

**portion**, hūn(份). *what belongs to one's*, hūn-tsôiⁿ kâi-mue̍h(份前个物).

**portrait**, hí-sîn(喜神); siáu-ngiá(小雅); sièⁿ(像). *to paint*, ūe-sièⁿ(畫像); thûan-sîn(傳神). *by photography,* hoh-sièⁿ(酷像); hoh-iáⁿ(酷影); hoh-siáu-ngiá(酷小雅). *painter*, ūe-sièⁿ sin-seⁿ(畫像先生).

**Portugal**, Phû-thô-giâ(葡萄牙).

**position**, tī-ūi(地位); ūi-tshṳ̍(位處).

**positive**, tuàn(斷); tiāⁿ(定); tuàn-tiāⁿ(斷定).

**possess**, ũ(有). *to be possessed*, phah-tang(拍童); phah-ki(拍乩); lo̍h-sîn(落神); pun-kúi tùe--tie̍h(分鬼綴着); siáu-sîn--phû(小神浮); siáu-kûi(小鬼). *possessions*, ngia̍p(業); mu̍eh-ngia̍p(物業); ke-ngia̍p(家業); ke-sṳ̄(家事); ke-tsṳ(家資); súaⁿ-ngia̍p(產業); mu̍eh-súaⁿ(物產).

**possible**, tsò-tit-lâi(做得來); lêng-tit-tsò kâi-sṳ̄(能做得个事). *can it be possible*, káⁿ-bô-iáⁿ(敢無影).

**post**, *a*, thiãu(柱); khṳ̍t〔〕.

**post**, *a letter*, kià-sìn(寄信). *post-office*, bûn-tsṳ-kuán(文資管); tsṳ-sìn-kuán(資信管). *post-station* , ia̍h-ku´¯n(驛官); ia̍h-tsãm(驛站); kuan-ia̍h(關驛). *post-runner*, bé-sìn(馬信); tshoiⁿ-lí-bé(千里馬); tsáu-bûn-tsṳ(走文書); tî-bûn-tsṳ(池文資).

**posterity**, ãu(後); ãu-ĩ(後裔); kiáⁿ-sun(囝孫); ãu-tō(後裔). *descend to*, thuân-pun ãu-ĩ(傳分後裔); thuân-pun ãu-pùe(傳分後輩).

**posthumous**, *child*, zūi-pak-kiáⁿ(墜背囝).

**postpone**, lâu-mān(留慢); chhî-mān(遲慢).

**pot**, *for cooking*, tũn-puah(燉鉢); chien-puah(煎鉢); chien-pûaⁿ(煎盤); sua-ue(沙鍋). *(deeper)*, ue(鍋). *(iron)*, seⁿ-ue(鍟鍋). *flower*, puah(缽); hue-puah(花缽). *water*, kuàn(罐); tsúi-kuàn(水罐); tsúi-kng(水缸). *chamber*, hû(壺); mêⁿ-hû(盲壺); jiē-hû(尿壺). *lid*, khàm〔〕; kùa(掛); khòiⁿ(蓋).

**potash**, kiⁿ(梔).

**potato**, hô-lan-tsṳ̂(荷蘭薯). *sweet*, huan-tsṳ̂(番薯); huan-kuah(番葛); tī-kue(地瓜).

**pot-bellied**, tōa-tóu-tháng(大肚桶); tōa-tóu-lak(大肚落); tóu kuai-kuai(肚鮭鮭).

**potter**, tsò-hûi sai-pẽ(做缶司阜). *pottery*, hûi-khì(缶器); tshou-hûi(粗缶). *a pottery*, hûi-iê(缶窯).

**pouch**, lâng(籠); tō(袋); ie-tõu(腰肚).

**poultry**, koi-ah(雞鴨).

**pounce**, *on chicken, as hawk*, liáu-eng-pô tiàu-koi-kiáⁿ(了英婆吊雞囝).

**pound**, *Chinese*, kṳn(斤). *English*, pong(磅).

**pound**, *to*, cheng(舂); tûi(捶).

**pour**, *out*, tò(倒). *out (as useless)*, tò-tiāu(倒掉). *tea*, sai-tê(司茶). *wine*, sai-chiú(司酒). *in*, tò--lo̍h-khṳ̍(倒落去). *as down the throat*, kùan(灌).

**pout**, tshùi khiàu-khiàu(喙翹翹); tshùi tu-tu(喙嘟嘟).

**powder**, hún(粉). *cosmetic*, tsúi-hún(水粉); sang-hún(雙粉); ìn-chí-hún(印子粉); tōa-pe̍h-hún(大白粉). *use this*, buah-hún(抹粉). *medicinal*, ie̍h-súaⁿ(藥散); ie̍h-bua̍h(藥末). *gun-powder*, húe-ie̍h(火藥); chhèng-ie̍h(銃藥). *horn*, gû-kak-tâng(牛角銅). *to powder by grinding*, gnóiⁿ-bua̍h(研磨); lûi-iùⁿ(擂幼).

**power**, khûan(權); khûan-lêng(權能); khûan-sì(權勢); khûan-la̍t(權力); khûan-pèⁿ(權柄); lêng-la̍t(能力); sì-la̍t(勢力); sì-thâu(勢頭); tshâi-lêng(財能). *to be in his power*, tõ i chhiú-ẽ(在伊手下); tõ i chhiú-sim-tói(在伊手心底); tõ i kúan-ẽ(在伊管下). *powerful*, ũ-khûan(有權); ũ-khì-la̍t(有氣力). *powerless*, bô-la̍t(無力); bô-khûan(無權); bô-ta-uâ(無奈何). *powerless against any one*, bô-ta i-uâ(無大伊話); bô-nãiⁿ i-hô(無奈伊何); sì-la̍t put-te̍k(勢力不敵).

**pox**, *chicken*, tsúi-tsu(水珠); tsúi-tāu(水豆). *small-*, tshut-tsu(出珠); gâu-a-niêⁿ(賢阿娘); sún-tsái〔〕; thien-hue(天花). *inoculate for (by the nostrils)*, pûn-tsu(歕珠). *vaccinate for*, chèng-tsu(種珠); chèng-tāu(種豆); chèng-iêⁿ-tāu(症羊豆). *scab of*, tsu-phí(珠痞). *pock-marked*, poiⁿ(斑).

**practice**, si̍p-liēn(習練); ha̍k-si̍p(學習); liēn-si̍p(練習); kiâⁿ-ûi(行爲).

**prance**, thìau(跳); pháu(跑); pháu-lâi pháu-khṳ̀(跑來跑去).

**prawn**, hê(蝦). *very small, dried*, hê-bí(蝦米).

**pray**, khî-táu(祈禱); táu-kàu(禱告); khî-khiû(祈求); khiû(求); táu-khiû(禱求); khî-mōⁿ(祈望); táu-tsok(禱祝); khî-tsok(祈祝). *a written prayer*, khî-táu-bûn(祈禱文). *repeat prayers*, liām-keng(唸經). *book of prayers*, keng-chheh(經冊).

**preach**, káng-tãu(講道); káng-tãu-lí(講道理); thûan-tãu(傳道); lũn-tãu(論道); lũn-káng(論講); káng-sueh(講說); sueh-tsṳ(說書); káng-mêng tõ-lí(講明道理). *the Gospel*, suang-thûan hok-im(宣傳福音); suang-mêng hok-im-tãu(宣明福音道).

**precarious**, m̄-ún-tǹg(毋穩當); m̄-thêng-tǹg(毋停當); m̄-thó-tàng(毋妥當); m̄-tek-tàng(毋得當).

**precaution**, ṳ̃-pĩ(預備); ṳ̃-hûang(預防); hûang-lṳ̃(防慮); hûang-ṳ̃(防預).

**precede**, soiⁿ(先); soiⁿ-kîaⁿ(先行); thiàu-thut(超脫).

**precious**, pó(寶); pó-pùe(寶貝); kùi-khì(貴器); kùi-tõng(貴重); tien-tõng(珍重).

**precipice**, suaⁿ kiã(山崎); kiã-sià(崎瀉); suaⁿ-khàm(山冚); kiã-hiám(崎險).

**precipitate**, mâng-kip(忙急); huang-mâng kip-chhiet(芳忙急切).

**precipitate**, *to*, léng-pua̍h(推跋). *oneself*, tsṳ̃-thiàu(自跳).

**precisely**, tùi-tùi(對對); chìaⁿ-chiàⁿ(正正); tú-tú(堵堵); bô-tshò(無錯).

**precocious**, siàu-nîⁿ láu-sêng(少年老成); nîⁿ siàu tshâi kau(年少才高).

**precursor**, soiⁿ-khu(先驅); tsôiⁿ-khu(前驅).

**predict**, ṳ̃-ngân(預言); ṳ̃-soiⁿ-tàⁿ(預先呾); thâu-soiⁿ-tàⁿ(頭先呾).

**pre-eminent**, tshut-chèng(出眾); thiàu-khûn(超群); tshut-lūi(出類); tshut-thoh(出脫); kùe-nâng(過人).

**preface**, sũ(序); sũ-thâu(序頭); siáu-ín(紹引).

**prefect**, ti-hú(知府); hú-thài-iâ(府太爺); hú-hièn(府憲). *prefecture*, hú(府).

**prefer**, kèng-hàuⁿ(敬好); zú-kèng huaⁿ-hí(愈敬歡喜). *I prefer Swatow to Shanghai*, ṳ́-khî khiã-khí Siãng-hái uá lêng-tsò khiã-khí Sùaⁿ-thâu(予其徛起上海我寧做徛起汕頭); pí khiã-khí Siãng-hái uá lêng-ngũan khiã-khí Sùaⁿ-thâu(比徛起上海我寧願徛起汕頭). *do you prefer living in Swatow or in Shanghai*, lṳ́ sĩ khiã-khí Sùaⁿ-thâu--hó(汝是徛起汕頭好), a-sĩ khiã-khí Siãng-hái--hó(阿是徛起上海好).

**pregnant**, ũ-sin-hūn(有身分); ũ-tho(有胎); ũ-ẽng(有孕); ũ-a-nôuⁿ(有阿孥); huâi-tho(懷胎); ũ-la̍k-kah(有六甲); ũ-hí-sṳ̄(有喜事).

**prejudice**, ì-kièn phien-sṳ(意見偏私); chip-it(執一); chip-thì(執滯). *to my prejudice*, uá chia̍h-khui(我食虧); uá siũ-khui(我受虧).

**premature**, būe-se̍k(未熟); sî-hāu būe-kàu(時候未到); khah-soiⁿ(較先); khah-tsá(較早). *birth*, chíⁿ-gue̍h seⁿ(稚月生); būe-tsok-gue̍h seⁿ(未足月生). *(abortion)*, pùaⁿ-súaⁿ(半產).

**premeditate**, soiⁿ-pheⁿ-phah(先斟拍); ṳ̃-siẽⁿ(預想). *premeditated*, kù-ì(故意).

**premier**, tsái-siàng(仔相).

**premium**, siéⁿ(賞); khàu-siéⁿ(犒賞).

**prepare**, ṳ̃-pĩ(預備); pĩ-phōiⁿ(備辦); an-pâi(安排); uaⁿ-pâi(安排); siu-sip(收拾). *prepared*, tsôi-pĩ(齊備); chhî-pĩ(遲備); tshuân-pĩ(全備); pĩn-chiàⁿ(並正).

**presage**, ṳ̃-tiãu(預兆); tiãu-thâu(兆頭); ki-tiãu(機兆). *felicitous*, siang-sũi(相瑞); kit-tiãu(吉兆); sũi-khì(瑞氣).

**prescription**, ie̍h-hng(藥方); ie̍h-toaⁿ(藥單). *prescribe*, khui-hng(開方).

**presence**, *in one's*, tõ-mīn-tsôiⁿ(在面前); tng-mīn(當面). *of mind*, lêng-ki èng-pièn(靈機應變); lêng-ua̍h(靈活); soiⁿ-kak(先覺); ũ-kip-tì(有急智). *of the emperor*, gṳ̄-tsôiⁿ(御前).

**present**, lói-mu̍eh(禮物); chì-kìⁿ(致見); sie-sàng(相送). *to give as a*, sàng(送).

**present**, *to, at court*, ín-kìⁿ(引見). *to present tribute*, chìn-kòng(進貢).

**present**, *time*, hīn-kim(現金); hīn-tsãi(現在); tshṳ́-tsãi(此在); chí-hûe(此回); ngán-tsôiⁿ(眼前); ngán-tsãi-kim(眼在金); chí-tsûn(此陣); hīn-jiên(現然). *dynasty*, pńg-chhiâu(本朝). *I will come presently*, uá chiũ-lâi(我就來).

**presentiment**, sim-ki(心機); sim-tang ki-tiãu(心當機兆); àm-tiãu(暗兆).

**preserve**, pó(保); pó-tshûan(保全); pó-tshûn(保存); tshûn(存). *her virtue, as widow remaining unmarried*, pó-siú tshûan-tsat(保守全節); siú-tsat(守節). *preserves*, thn̂g-kúeⁿ(糖柑); bit-chìm(蜜浸); tiâm-ko(甜糕).

**preside**, *over*, kúan-lí(管理); keng-kúan(經管). *president of board*, siēⁿ-tsṳ(尚資).

**press**, *to*, teh(壓); teh-sit(壓失); kui(規). *to urge*, tshui(催); tshui-pek(催迫). *matter from a boil*, liū-lâng(餾籠); liū-thûe(餾㿗). *a press*, kui(規). *book-binder's*, chheh-kui(冊規). *printing*, ìn-chheh-kui(印冊規). *pressed by circumstances*, khiông-kip(窮急). *pressing*, kín-kín(緊緊); kín-chhiet(緊切); kip-chhiet(急切); pek-chhiet(迫切).

**prestige**, lién(臉); thí-mīn(體面); sì-mīn(勢面). *to lose*, sit-lién(失臉); sàu-lién(掃臉).

**presume**, káⁿ(敢); tsṳ̃-tsuan(自專). *presumptuous*, tōa-tsú tōa-ì(大主大意). *I would not presume*, m̄-káⁿ(毋敢); tsò-káⁿ-tng(做敢當); hô-káⁿ-tng(何敢當); tsò-káⁿ(做敢); khí-káⁿ(起敢);

**pretend**, *not to know a thing*, tho-m̄-tsai(推毋知); tèⁿ-m̄-tsai(詐毋知); tsuang-hû-thû(裝糊塗). *to be deaf*, tèⁿ-tsò hĩⁿ lâng(詐做耳聾); tsuang-tsò hĩⁿ lâng(裝做耳聾); ké-tsò hĩⁿ lâng(假做耳聾). *pretender*, ké-kha ké-chhiú(假骹假手); ngũi-phièn(僞騙). *pretend friendliness while plotting an injury*, tshùi tõ-tàⁿ-ūe kha tõ-koih ōu-chéng(喙在呾話骹在夾芋種).

**pretext**, chiã-kù(藉故); chiã-sì(藉勢); chieh-sì(借勢); chieh-tuan(借端); chieh-miâⁿ(借名).

**pretty**, hó-thóiⁿ(好睇); ngiá(雅); zû(儒); chhiàu-kè〔〕; piáu-chì(標緻). *good*, õi-tsò-tit(會做得); khó-íⁿ(可以); hoh-hó(酷好); ũ--pan-bó(有班母).

**prevail**, iâⁿ(贏). *prevailing*, múaⁿ-tshù-ũ(滿處有).

**prevaricate**, chiau-saⁿ mõⁿ-sì(招三慕四); tsôiⁿ saⁿ(前三); ãu sì(後四); tàⁿ-ūe m̄-pe̍h-ti̍t(呾話毋白直).

**prevent**, tsó-chí(阻止); nûaⁿ-chí〔〕; nûaⁿ-tsó〔〕; nûaⁿ-tsũ〔〕; tsó-keh(阻隔); tsó-khiē(阻撓). *one from speaking*, bô i khui-tshùi(無伊開喙). *one from entering*, bô-i-ji̍p(無伊入). *trouble*, mién-hũa(免禍); mién tì-kàu kan-khóu(免致到艱苦). *falling*, màiⁿ-pua̍h-lo̍h(勿跋落).

**previously**, soiⁿ(先); ṳ̃-soiⁿ(預先).

**price**, kè(價); kè-chîⁿ(價錢). *current*, sî-kè(時價). *real*, si̍t-kè(實價). *high*, kùi-kè(貴價); kûiⁿ-kè(懸價); kau-kè(高價). *rising*, chiẽⁿ-kè(上價); chiáng-kè(掌價). *falling*, lo̍h-kè(落價); tie̍t-kè(跌價). *fixed*, put-zṳ̃-kè(不自如價); bô-nõⁿ-kè(無二價). *to ask*, mn̄g-kè(問價). *to estimate*, kóu-kè(估價); kóu jie̍h-tsōi-chîⁿ(估若㩼錢). *wait for rise in*, thãi-kè(待價). *priceless*, bô-kè-pó(無價寶).

**pride**, kiau-ngãu(驕傲); tsṳ̃-tōa(自大); tsṳ̃-tsun(自尊).
