**punctual**, èng-khî(應期); i-khî(依期); zû-khî(如期); chiè-khî(照期); tùi-khî(對期); put-sit-khî(不失期).

**pungent**, hiam(薟); lua̍h(辣); hiam-lua̍h(薟辣).

**punish**, hua̍t(罰); hêng-hua̍t(刑罰); phōiⁿ-tsũe(辦罪). *severely*, ngiâm-hêng(嚴刑); tãng-hêng(重刑). *capital punishment*, sí-miāⁿ(死命); tsám-thâu(斬頭). *by strangling*, ká-sí(絞死). *cutting to pieces*, lêng-chhî(凌遲); tshùi-si(碎絲). *with heavy bamboo*, phah-tōa-póiⁿ(拍大板). *with light one*, phah-póiⁿ-kiáⁿ(拍板囝); phah-kha-tshng(拍尻川). *by slapping on the mouth*, siak-tshùi-phói(削碎板).

**punkah**, huang-sìⁿ(風扇). *to pull*, túi-huang(拖風).

**pupil**, *of the eye*, thông-jîn(瞳人); sien-nâng(仙人).

**pupil**, *or scholar*, ha̍k-seng(學生); mn̂g-seng(門生); tĩ-tsṳ́(弟子).

**purchase**, bói(買); hak(喝); kiẽn-tì(建置).

**pure**, chheng(清); chheng-khih(清潔); chheng-kiet(清潔); chheng-chẽng(清淨); kiet-chẽng(潔淨). *silver*, tsok-siâⁿ(足成); chẽng-tsok(淨足); ngṳ̂n-tī kûiⁿ(銀地懸).

**purgative**, sià-ie̍h(瀉藥); sià-tóu ie̍h(瀉肚藥); liâng-sià-ie̍h(凉瀉藥); thong-tãi-piên-ie̍h(通大便藥).

**purloin**, thau-khie̍h(偷挈).

**purple**, phû-thô-chheⁿ(葡萄青); thien-chheⁿ(天青).

**purpose**, tsú-ì(主意); ì-sṳ̀(意思). *purposely*, ũ-ì(有意); tshut-tõ ũ-ì(出在有意); kù-ì(故意); tsuan-tsuan(專專); te̍k-te̍k(特特).

**purse**, ngṳ̂n-tō(銀袋); hô-pau(荷包); ie-tõu(腰肚).

**pursue**, tui(追); jiāu(尿); kúaⁿ(趕); tui-kúaⁿ(追趕); tui-jiāu(追擾).

**pus**, lâng(膿). *secreting pus*, pũ-lâng(胕膿); kâm-lâng(含膿).

**push**, léng(攆). *away*, léng-khui(推開). *over*, léng-tó(推倒); léng-pua̍h(推跋). *in a crowd*, sie-chìⁿ(相擠); iòng-chìⁿ(擁擠). *a boat in the mud*, sat-tsûn(虱船); oi-tsûn(挨船).

**pustule**, sié-tshng(小瘡).

**put**, pàng(放); hẽ(下); an-tì(安置); an-tùn(安頓). *away*, pàng-khui(放開). *away a servant*, sî(時). *by* khǹg(囥); khǹg-búa(囥埋). *in mind*, thî-chhéⁿ(提醒); that-chhéⁿ(踢醒); sái i kì-tit(使伊記得). *in order*, pái-hó(擺好); siu-si̍p-hó(收拾好); phou-tì-hó(鋪置好); an-pâi(安排); siu-si̍p kui-ūi(收拾歸位); siu-si̍p tsôi-chiáⁿ(收拾齊整). *into*, tshō--lo̍h-khṳ̀(放落去); ji̍p(入). *on clothes*, chhēng-saⁿ(穿衫). *on a cap*, tì-bō(戴帽). *off clothes and cap*, thǹg-saⁿ pak-bō(褪衫剝帽). *out a fire*, phah-kùe-húe(拍熄火); ìm--khí húe(蔭起火). *out a lamp*, pûn-kùe-teng(歕熄燈); lâu-kùe-teng(留熄燈); lâu--khí(留起). *the hand on*, àn-chhiú(按手); chhiú àn--pàng-kò(手按放塊); hūaⁿ-chhiú(焊手); chhiú teh(手壓). *together*, tàu(鬥); tàu-bûa(鬥埋); ha̍h-bûa(合埋). *up with*, lún(忍); nãiⁿ(耐). *to shame*, khṳt-nâng sit-lién(乞人失臉); peh-phùa mīn-phûe(掰破面皮).

**putchuk**, ba̍k-hieⁿ(木鄉).

**putrid**, hu(腐); hu-hiúⁿ(腐朽); àu(漚).

**putty**, thâng-iû-hue(蟲油花).

**puzzle**, *a*, chhit-khá-tôu(七巧圖). *puzzling*, hũn-tie̍h-sim(混着心); siẽⁿ-m̄-pat tò-khṳ̀(想毋識倒去).

**pyramid**, thah(塔); kim--jī thah(金字塔).

### Q

**quack**, *a*, uãng-lo̍k(王錄); kuang-kùn(光棍).

**quack**, *to*, ah-siaⁿ(鴨聲); ah-ah-kiè(鴨鴨叫).

**quadrant**, *(or sextant)*, niêⁿ-thiⁿ-chhieh(量天尺).

**quadrupeds**, tsáu-siù(走獸).

**quadruple**, sì-pũe(四倍); sì-têng(四重).

**quagmire**, làm-thôu(濫塗); làm().

**quail**, *a*, lōu-thûn(路豚); liãu-thûn(鹋吞); ang-tshun(翁春). *fight with*, phah-chiáu(拍鳥); phah-ang-tshun(拍翁春).

**quake**, chín-tõng(震動). *with fear*, kiaⁿ kàu-tõ-tòng(驚到在凍).

**quality**, téng(等); pín(品); hō(號); thie(挑). *best*, siãng-téng(上頂); thiàu-téng(超等); it-pín(一品). *second*, jī-téng(二等); jī-hō(二號).

**quantity**, *what*, jie̍h-tsōi(若㩼). *great*, tsōi-tsōi(㩼㩼); ke-ke(加加); tōa-bó-mue̍h(大母物). *estimate*, pān jie̍h-tsōi(辦若㩼); kóu jie̍h-tsōi(估若㩼).

**quarrel**, sie-à(相詏); seⁿ-ūe(生話); ũ-ūe(有話); sie-cheⁿ(相爭); sie-tũ〔〕; sie-mēⁿ(相罵); poh-khùi(駁氣); sĩ-hui(是非). *quarrelsome*, lãu-à(鬧詏); hàuⁿ-seⁿ-sṳ̄(好生事).

**quarry**, chie̍h-suaⁿ(石山); phah-chie̍h-suaⁿ(拍石山).

**quarter**, sì-hūn tsṳ-che̍k(四分之一). *to*, pun-tsò sì-hūn(分怎四分). *of an hour*, che̍k-khek(一刻). *a region*, tī-hng(地方).

**quartz**, pe̍h-chie̍h(白石).

**quash**, *an affair*, teh-tiāu(壓掉); hìm-tiāu(禁掉).

**quaver**, siaⁿ tiē(聲迭).

**queen**, nńg-uâng(女王); uâng-hõu(王后); huâng-hõu(皇后). *of heaven*, thien-hõu(天后).

**quell**, cheng-hua̍t(征伐); hua̍t-tsha̍t(伐賊); phêng-luãn(平亂); phêng-tī-hng(平地方).

**quench**, *fire*, kiù-húe(救火). *(fire with water)*, tsâng-kùe-húe〔〕. *thirst*, kói-khuah(解渴); chí aû ta(止喉灱).

**question**, mn̄g(問); poh-mn̄g(駁問); chhê-mn̄g(查問); kiù-mn̄g(究問); huáng-mn̄g(訪問); thèng-mn̄g(聽問). *and answer*, mn̄g-tap(問答).

**queue**, *the*, piⁿ(辮). *to plait*, pĩⁿ-piⁿ(編辮). *to comb*, siu-piⁿ(收辮). *cut off*, kuah-tiāu-piⁿ(割掉辮). *to join*, chiap-piⁿ(接邊); chiap-tsáng(接攥).

**quick**, méⁿ(猛); khùe(快); kín(緊). *walk a little more quickly*, kiâⁿ-mé--chē(行猛些). *in intelligence*, tshong-mêng(匆忙); lêng-lāi(伶俐).

**quicksilver**, tsúi-ngṳ̂n(水銀).

**quiet**, chẽⁿ(靜); tiām-chẽⁿ(恬靜); thiâm-chẽⁿ(恬靜).

**quill**, môⁿ-kńg(毛管); gô-môⁿ-kńg(鵝毛管). *pen*, gô-môⁿ-pit(鵝毛筆).

**quilt**, *to*, *a garment*, ji̍p-mîⁿ(入棉); hâng-niûⁿ(夯裘).

**quinsy**, aû-lêng jie̍t-thiàⁿ(喉嚨熱痛); âu thiàⁿ(喉痛); âu seⁿ-sang-ngô(喉生雙蛾).

**quire**, che̍k-to-tsúa(一刀紙).

**quit**, khṳ̀(去); sî(辭); siá(寫); khì(棄); lī-khui(離開).

**quite**, *the same*, pêⁿ-pêⁿ-iēⁿ(平平樣). *certain*, tiāⁿ-tie̍h(定着). *right*, chiũ-sĩ(就是); tie̍h(着); put-tshò(不錯); bõi-tāⁿ(袂賺); tùi-tùi(對對). *not quite up to*, bô-hièⁿ-chiẽⁿ(無向上); bô-hièⁿ-kàu(無向到); tsua̍h se-su(絀些須).

**quiver**, *a*, chìⁿ-tō(箭袋).

**quiver**, *to*, khiū〔〕; tòng(凍); tùn(頓). *with rage*, khì kàu kha sih chhiú sih〔〕.

**quoin**, chiⁿ(錢).

**quote**, ín-tsṳ(引資); ín-kiaⁿ kṳ̃-tién(引經據典).

### R

**rabbit**, pe̍h-thòu(石鼠); gue̍h-tshṳ́(石鼠); chie̍h-tshṳ́(石鼠).

**rabble**, kẽ-pín-nâng(下品人); hiã-liû-nâng(下流人); thóu-húiⁿ(土匪).

**rabid**, *dog*, siáu-káu(𤞚狗); khûang-káu(狂狗).

**race**, *human*, nâng-lūi(人類). *exterminate the*, mi̍t-tso̍h chéng-lūi(滅絕種類).

**race**, *a*, sie-tàu tsáu-iâⁿ(相鬥走贏); tàu-tsáu(鬥走). *horse-race*, sie-tàu pháu-bé(相鬥跑馬); tòu-bé(鬥馬). *boat-race*, sie-tàu kò-tsûn(相鬥划船).

**rack**, *a*, kè(架); tû(櫥); tãng-kè(筒架). *engine of punishment*, hêng-kũ(桁舅).

**radiate**, kuang-mâng sì-siā(光茫四射); kuang-siā(光射); huat-kng(發光); hâu-kng(豪光).

**radiant**, *countenance*, mīn ũ-kuang-tshái(面有光彩); múaⁿ-mīn hí-iông(滿面喜容).

**radical**, kṳn-pún(根本). *the radicals*, jī-bó(字母); jī-bó-põu(字母部). *this character belongs to the radical "nang"*, chí-kâi-jī sĩ-so̍k "nâng"-põu(此個字是屬人部).

**radius**, pùaⁿ-keⁿ-sùaⁿ(半經線).

**raft**, sam-pâi(杉排); tek-pâi(竹排).

**rafter**, êⁿ(楹).

**rag**, pòu-tshùi(布碎). *ragged clothes*, phùa-saⁿ-khòu(破衫褲).

**rage**, khì(氣); náuⁿ-khì(惱氣); náuⁿ-khì tshong-tshong(惱氣衝衝); huat-náuⁿ(發惱).

**rail**, *at*, mēⁿ(罵); chiù(咒); chiù-mēⁿ(咒罵); poih-mēⁿ(捌罵).

**railing**, *a*, lâng-kan(廊干); lâng-kan-chí(廊干子).

**railway**, húe-chhia(火車); húe-chhia-lōu(火車路).

**raiment**, kûn-saⁿ(裙衫); i-ho̍k(衣服); sin-chhēng(身穿). *food and*, chia̍h-chhēng(食穿).

**rain**, hõu(雨). *it rains*, lo̍h-hõu(落雨); hõu--lâi(雨來). *water*, hõu-tsúi(雨水). *rainy weather*, thiⁿ-sî lo̍h-hõu(天時落雨). *cleared up*, hõu chêⁿ(雨晴). *wetted by*, ak-tie̍h-hõu(沃着雨). *driving into a place*, hõu phuah--ji̍p-lâi(雨潑入來).

**rainbow**, khẽng(虹). *there is a*, tshut-khẽng(出虹).

**raise**, khí(起); khie̍h-khí(挈起); khie̍h-phû(挈浮); hû-khí(扶起); hû-phû(扶浮); kṳ́(舉); kṳ́-khí(舉起); kṳ́-phû(舉浮). *soldiers*, khí-piaⁿ(起兵). *the head*, tièⁿ-phû-thâu(脹浮頭); tièⁿ-khí-thâu(脹起頭); kṳ́-khí-thâu(舉起頭). *the eyes*, kṳ́-ma̍k(舉目); tièⁿ-phû-ma̍k(脹浮目). *money, by subscription*, tôi-chîⁿ(題錢). *dust*, khí-sua-mûiⁿ(起沙微); khí-sua-tîn(起沙藤); phi-phi-eng(披披英). *cattle*, chhī-cheng-seⁿ(飼眾生). *wheat*, chèng-be̍h(種麥). *a subject*, thî-phû(提浮); thî-khí(提起). *raised letters*, kuah-phû-jī(割浮字); khek-jī(刻字).

**raisins**, phû-thô-kuaⁿ(葡萄干).

**rake**, *a*, pê(耙); khau-pê(摳耙); chhek-pê(測耙). *to*, pê(耙).

**rally**, *soldiers*, piaⁿ tsài-ho̍k-tsũ(兵再復聚); piaⁿ tsài-kap-tīn(兵再合陣); piaⁿ tsài-ha̍h-bûa(兵再合埋).

**ram**, *a*, iêⁿ-kóu(羊牯).

**ramble**, thit-thô(佚佗); iû-kiâⁿ(遊行); ôiⁿ-iû(閒遊); múaⁿ-kò-la̍h(滿塊獵).

**ramify**, pun-ki pun-iẽⁿ(分枝分樣).

**rampart**, kau-lúi(高壘); siâⁿ-chhiêⁿ(城牆).

**rancid**, hu-bī(腐味); ip-bī(邑味); ha-bī(哈味).

**rancorous**, *abuse*, mēⁿ kàu-chhi-gî(罵到凄疑).

**random**, *talk*, thèng-tàⁿ(聽呾); thèng-tsãu-hùe tàⁿ(聽造化呾).

**range**, hâng-lie̍t(行列). *beyond, of gun*, chhèng phah-m̄-kàu(銃拍毋夠).

**rank**, pín-khip(品級). *the nine ranks*, káu-pín(九品). *the first*, it-pín(一品);; téng-khip(頂級); thâu-téng(頭等). *and file*, tūi-ngóu(隊伍). *place in*, pâi-tīn(擺陣). *ranks of nobility*, ngóu-chiak(五爵): kong(公), hôu(侯), pek(伯), tsṳ́(子), lâm(男).

**rank**, *to*, *with anyone*, tâng-lie̍t(職銜); pêⁿ-tōa(平大); phùe-tit-kùe(配得過).

**ransack**, chhîm-kàu-thàu(侵到套). *(looking for things in a heap)*, púe(撥). *a city*, sàu-chĩn(掃盡); sàu-chẽng(掃淨).

**ransom**, so̍k(贖); so̍k-tńg(贖轉); chhiú(取); chhiú-so̍k(取贖). *for sin*, so̍k-tsũe(贖罪).

**rap**, khà(扣).

**rapacious**, lãm-thun(濫吞); hiau-thun(驍吞); khiâng-thun(強吞); tham-sim(貪心).

**rape**, khiâng-kan(強姦).

**rapid**, méⁿ(猛). *rapids*, kip-tsúi(急水); thoaⁿ(灘).

**rapture**, huaⁿ-hí kàu-kông(歡喜到狂); huaⁿ-hí kàu-ngo̍h-ngo̍h(歡喜到愕愕).

**rare**, hán-ũ(罕有); chié-ũ(少有); hán-hông(罕逢); oh-tshūe(惡覓); hi-chié(稀少); kṳ́n-kièn(僅見). *rarely*, hán--tit(罕得); chié(少); bô-hièⁿ pat-thóiⁿ--kìⁿ(無向識睇見).

**rascal**, àu-nâng(杇人); pháiⁿ-nâng(痞人); láu-kiáⁿ(老囝); tōa-láu(大老); húiⁿ-thû(匪徒); nâng-tái(人痞). *(the rascality)*, nâng-tshṳ(人蛆).

**rase**, *as writing*, kueh-tiāu(刮掉); khoi-tiāu(溪掉). *to the ground*, húiⁿ-chiâⁿ pêⁿ-tī(毀情平地).

**rash**, káⁿ-tsò káⁿ-ûi(敢做敢爲); tshau-tsut(草率); mãuⁿ-mũeⁿ(冒昧); máng-liáng(孟浪); bô-sié-sim(無小心); khin-phû(輕浮); hṳ-phû(虛浮). *do not be*, màiⁿ-thèng-tsò(勿聽做); màiⁿ hih-huh-kiè〔〕; màiⁿ thih-thuh-kiè〔〕.

**raspberry**, hóuⁿ-m̄(虎莓).

**rat**, niáuⁿ-tshṳ́(鳥鼠).

**rather**, *nice*, lia̍k-lia̍k(略略); õi-tsò-tit(會做得); chiang-chiũ(將就). *I would rather have this one*, uá zú-àiⁿ chí-kâi(我愈愛此個); uá thóiⁿ sĩ chí--kâi hó(我睇是此個好); chiè uá kâi-ì-kièn chí-kâi kèng-hó(照我个意見此個更好). *I would rather be beaten by you than do this*, uá m̄-ngũan tsò chí-kâi-sṳ̄, uá ngũan khṳt-lṳ́-phah(我毋愿做此個事，我愿乞汝拍); uá lẽng-tsò khṳt-lṳ́-phah--hó, chí-kâi-sṳ̄ uá-m̃-tsò(我寧做乞汝拍好，此個事我毋做); uá lẽng-khó khṳt-lṳ́-phah--hó, chí-kâi-sṳ̄ uá-m̃-tsò(我寧可乞汝拍好，此個事我毋做). *I would rather have given you a thousand dollars than have had you break this*, che̍k-tshoiⁿ-ngṳ̂n khṳt-lṳ́ uá kèng-ngũan(一千銀乞汝我敬愿), chí-kiãⁿ-mue̍h khṳt lṳ́ khà-phùa úa zú-m̄-ngũan(此件物乞汝扣破我愈毋愿); che̍k-tshoiⁿ-ngṳ̂n khṳt-lṳ́ uá kōi-siá-khí(一千銀乞汝我易寫起), chí-kiãⁿ-mue̍h khṳt-lṳ́ khà-phùa uá siá-m̄-khí(此件物乞汝扣破我寫毋起). *rather too big*, khah-tōa se-su(較大些須). *rather better*, iáu-hó(要好); iáu-tsua̍h(要絀).

**rations**, *soldiers'*, piaⁿ-niêⁿ(兵糧); hóng-bí(俸米); ji̍t-niêⁿ(日糧); kan-niêⁿ(乾糧).

**rattan**, tîn(藤); khue-tîn(科藤); tîn-tiâu(藤條). *mats*, tîn-chhie̍h(藤席). *chair*, tîn-íⁿ(藤椅).

**rattle**, *a*, pa-lan-kóu(叭啷鼓); iê-kóu(搖鼓). *(hollow, wooden or bamboo)*, khok(柝). *watchman's*, keⁿ-khok(更柝).

**ravelled**, zṳ̂-zṳ̂(挐挐). *edges of dress*, sui-pôu(蓑醅); sàm-pôu(慘舖). *a coat with such edges*, sui-pôu-saⁿ(蓑醅衫).

**raven**, ou-a(烏阿); ou-a-chiáu(烏阿鳥).

**ravenous**, *appetite*, tōa-chia̍h(大食).

**ravine**, suaⁿ-kàn(山澗); kheⁿ(坑); kheⁿ-kàn(坑澗); suaⁿ-hak(山壑).

**ravish**, khiâng-kan(強姦); khiâng-to̍h(強奪). *ravishing*, lêng-î uá-chhêng(靈異我情); õi-î-súa nâng kâi-chhêng-ì(會移徙人个情意).

**raw**, chheⁿ(生); m̄-se̍k(毋熟).

**ray**, ji̍t-tsam(日針); ji̍t-kuang-siā(日光射).

**razor**, thì-to(剃刀); thì-thâu-to(剃頭刀); mīn-to(面刀). *razor-strop*, huah-to-phûe(喝刀皮); huah-thì-to-phûe(喝剃刀皮).

**reach**, kàu(到); ki̍p(及); thùa-kàu(拖到). *out*, tshun(春). *unable to*, m̄-tie̍h(毋着); m̄-kàu(毋到).

**read**, *(aloud)*, tha̍k(讀). *(silently)*, thóiⁿ(睇). *(in a low voice)*, mi̍t-sõng(密訟). *a book*, tha̍k-tsṳ(讀書); thóiⁿ-tsṳ(睇書); thóiⁿ-chheh(睇冊). *all that he reads he knows*, kìⁿ-tha̍k kìⁿ-pat(見讀見識). *prayers*, liām-keng(唸經). *to read in a hesitating manner*, tak-tak têⁿ-têⁿ(讀讀挺挺).

**ready**, pīn(牝); pĩ-pīn(備辦); pĩ-piēn(備便); tsôi-pĩ(齊備); chhî-pĩ(遲備). *money*, hīn-chîⁿ(現錢). *buy for ready money*, hīn-chîⁿ bói(現錢買); hīn-chîⁿ kau-e̍k(現錢交易); hīn-bói(現買).

**real**, chin(真); chin-si̍t(真實). *gold*, chin-kim(真金).

**really**, si̍t-tsãi(實在); kúaⁿ-chin(果真); chin-kúaⁿ(真果); kúaⁿ-jiên(果然).

**ream**, che̍k-kiû-tsúa(一球紙).

**reap**, kuah(割); kuah-tiũ(割稻). *reaping hook*, liâm-to(鐮刀); uan-liâm(彎鐮); liâm-kau(鐮鈎).

**rear**, *fowls*, chhī-koi(飼雞). *up*, khiã--khí-lâi(徛起來). *the*, ãu-mīn(後面).

**reason**, tãu(道); lí(理). *a*, uân-kù(緣故); uân-in(緣故); sṳ̄-kù(緣故). *to*, káng-kiù(講究); tshiu-lũn(緣故); lũn-lí(緣故); tshui-lí(緣故). *reasonable*, ũ-lí(緣故); ũ-tõ-lí(有道里); ũ-chhêng-lí(有情理).

**rebel**, *a*, huán-tsha̍t(反賊); kok-tsha̍t(國賊). *to*, huán(反); tsak-luãn(作亂). *rebellious*, puãn-luãn(叛亂); pũe-nge̍k(悖逆); m̃-sũn-ho̍k(毋順服).

**rebound**, tiē-tńg--lâi(迭轉來); tò-tsuãng-tńg--lâi(倒撞轉來); tò-thiàu(倒跳).

**rebuild**, lêng-ūaⁿ-khí(另換起); tsài-khí(再起).

**rebuke**, hiâm(嫌); cheh(責); cheh-hiâm(責嫌); cheh-pĩ(責備).

**recall**, kiè-tńg(叫轉); huán tiãu-i-tńg--lâi(反兆伊轉來). *to mind*, tui-siẽⁿ(追想); siẽⁿ-tshut(想出).

**recant**, *evidence*, húan-keng(反供). *a confession*, húan-chiau(反招); m̃-jīn-chiau(毋認招).

**recede**, thò-sok(退縮); thò-pōu(退步); tò-thò(倒退); thò-ãu(退後).

**receipt**, *money-receipt*, siu-toaⁿ(收單); chip-chiè(執照); chiè-toaⁿ(借單). *tax-receipt*, niêⁿ-tshùan(糧串).

**receive**, siu(收); siũ(受); sêng-siũ(承受); niáⁿ(領); chiap(接); na̍p(納). *a command*, hõng-mẽng(奉命); niáⁿ-mẽng(領命); sêng-mẽng(承命). *guests*, chiap-na̍p(接納); chih(接); sêng-chih(承接).

**receiver**, *of stolen goods*, tun-ke(囤家); o-ke(窩家); tsõ-tī pun-pûi(坐地分肥).

**recently**, kṳ̃n-sî(近時); kṳ̃n-ji̍t(近日); kṳ̃n-lâi(近來); soiⁿ bô-kú(先無久).

**reciprocal**, jī-ke(二家); siang(相). *affection*, jī-ke siang-ài(二家相愛).

**recite**, *a lesson*, liām-tsṳ(唸書).

**reckless**, káⁿ-sí(敢死); m̄-ùi-sí(毋畏死); mãuⁿ-sí(冒死). see RASH.

**reckon**, sǹg(算); sǹg-siàu(算數). *anything to be so & so*, sǹg-tsò(算做).

**reclaim**, *from evil*, khǹg-kòi kui-chiàⁿ(勸戒規正).

**recline**, khùa-ie(掛腰); uá-ie(倚腰); gu̍t--lo̍h-khṳ̀(夗落去).

**recluse**, ṳ́n-kṳ(隱居); tiàm-bûa(坫埋).

**recognize**, jīn(認); pat-tò-jīn(識倒認); jīn-tshut(認出). *slightly*, pùaⁿ-mīn sie-pat(半面相識). *not to*, m̄-pat tò-jīn(毋識倒認); jīn m̄-pat(認毋識); jīn m̄-pat tò-khṳ̀(認毋識倒去). *not to(acknowledge)*, m̃-jīn(毋認).

**recoil**, *as gun*, tò-cheng-tńg(倒爭轉). *as bow*, póiⁿ-tńg(反轉); húan-tńg(反轉).

**recommend**, ín-chìn(引薦); chìn-kṳ́(薦舉); kṳ́-chìn(舉薦); kṳ́-ín(舉引); tshue-hṳ(吹噓); o-ló(呵咾).

**recompense**, pò(報); siéⁿ(賞); pò-siéⁿ(報賞); pò-èng(報應); chhiû-tap(酬答); chhiû-siā(酬謝); tap-siā(答謝).

**reconcile**, kiâⁿ-hûa(行和); khǹg-hûa(勸和); lêng-ūaⁿ tsài-hó(另換再好); i-kū hûa-hó(伊故和好); sek-uàn hûa-hó(釋怨和好); lêng-ūaⁿ ho̍k-tńg lâi-chhin-kṳ̃n(另換復轉來親近).

**record**, *to*, kì(記); kì-lo̍k(記錄). *a*, tn̄g(傳); chì(誌); kang-kàm(工鑑); sṳ́-kì(史記).

**recover**, tshú-tńg(取轉); khie̍h-tńg(挈轉); tshūe--tie̍h(覓着); chhîm--tie̍h(尋着). *from sickness*, pēⁿ hó(病好); pēⁿ phêng(病平); ho̍k-zú(復癒); tshûan-zú(全癒); khì-thói phêng-ho̍k(氣體平復).

**recreation**, tshut--lâi sùaⁿ-sîn(出來散神); siau-iâu(逍遙); thit-thô(佚佗); iû-kuan(遊觀); kîn-kiâⁿ〔〕; iáu-tõng khì-thói〔〕.

**recruit**, *one's strength*, póu-la̍t(補力); póu-sîn-khì(補神氣); iáng-sîn-khì(養神氣); tsõ-kṳn-la̍t(坐斤力); tsõ-iáng kṳn-la̍t(坐養筋力).

**rectify**, kói-chiàⁿ(改正); chhiâⁿ-kói(正改).

**rectitude**, chiàⁿ-ti̍t(正直); mêng-chiàⁿ(明正); kuaⁿ-chiàⁿ(官正).

**red**, âng(紅). *whitish*, hún-âng(粉紅). *as of card paper*, thô-âng(桃紅). *rich bright(vermilion)*, tsu-âng(朱紅). *very red, as eyes of drunk man*, ham-ham-âng(憨憨紅). *to paint*, iû-âng(油紅).

**redeem**, so̍k-tsũe(贖罪). *from pawn or mortgage*, chhiú(取); chhiú-so̍k(取贖); so̍k-tńg(贖轉); so̍k-hûe(贖回).

**redress**, sin-uan(申冤); póu-hôiⁿ(補還); pûe(陪).

**reduce**, *the price*, khà-kiám(扣減); tṳ̂-kiám(除減). *a dislocation*, á-lo̍h-ngám(拗落眼); tshâu-lo̍h-ngám(移落眼); tshut-khũ túi-hó(出臼縋好). *a fracture*, ah-chi̍h-kut(拗折骨). *to dollars*, chiet-tsò-ngṳ̂n(節做銀); sīn-tsò-ngṳ̂n(剩做銀).

**redundant**, tshong-tsok ũ-ṳ̂(充足有餘); ũ-tshûn(有賰).

**reed**, lû-tia̍h(蘆笛); kuaⁿ-mâng(秆芒).

**reel**, pháng-chhia(紡車). *to*, pháng-se(紡紗); khuãng-se(紡紗). *to stagger*, kiâⁿ kàu kha-phõng-pheng〔〕.

**refer**, chí(指). *(to a passage)*, ín-tsṳ(引書).

**refine**, *gold*, liēn-kim(煉金). *the heart*, liēn-sím(煉審). *sugar*, se̍k-thn̂g(熟糖); lāu-thn̂g(漏糖); pak-pe̍h-thn̂g(八白糖). *lacking refinement*, tshou-lõu(粗陋).

**reflect**, tui-siẽⁿ(追想); chhim-siẽⁿ(深想); sṳ-siẽⁿ(思想). *light*, húan-chiè(反照).

**reflections**, liãm-thâu(念頭); siẽⁿ-thâu(想頭).

**reform**, kói-kùe(改過); hûe-thâu(回頭); pìⁿ-hó(變好); pièn-hùe(變化); hùe-kói(化改); kói-ak tshông-siẽn(改惡從善).

**refraction**, ji̍t-iáⁿ siâ-chiè(日影斜照); tsúan-siâ(轉斜).

**refractory**, pũe-nge̍k(悖逆); m̃-sũn-ho̍k(毋順服).

**refrain**, *from, e.g. wine*, kài(戒); ke̍h(逆).

**refreshment**, *to take some*, chia̍h-tiám-sim(食點心).

**refuge**, tiàm-sin kâi-ūi-tshṳ̀(坫身个位處); tô-pī(逃避); pī-sin(避身). *to run for*, tsáu-khṳ̀-tiàm(走去坫); pī-lān(避難); siám-lān(閃難); siám-pī(閃避).

**refund**, pûe-hôiⁿ(賠還).

**refuse**, *to*, tho-sî(毋好); m̄-khéng(毋肯); m̄-hàuⁿ(毋好); m̄-tsún(毋準); m̄-ngũan(毋愿).

**refuse**, nahⁿ-sap(垃圾). *of wine*, chiú-tsau(酒糟); tsau-phoh(糟粕). *of tea*, tê-hu(茶烌). *of sugar cane*, chià-phoh(蔗粕).

**refute**, piẽn-iâⁿ(辯贏); piẽn-tó(辯倒); poh-tó(駁倒); piẽn-tiāu(辯掉). *refuted*, piẽn-su(辯輸); à m̄-kùe-chhiú(詏毋過手).

**regain**, tsài-tit(再得); lêng-ūaⁿ tit--tie̍h(另換得着).

**regard**, kù(顧); kèng-tõng(敬重); thóiⁿ-tõng(睇重). *not to*, put-kù(不顧); m̄-tshái(毋睬); bô-kài-ì(無介意); bô-tshûn-liãm(無存念). *regards to friends*, mn̄g-hāu(問候); chhiáⁿ-uaⁿ(請安).

**regatta**, tàu-tsûn(鬥船); tsûn-kiáⁿ sie-tàu-sái(船囝相鬥駛); tsûn-kiáⁿ sie-tàu-kò(船囝相鬥划).

**regenerate**, têng-seⁿ(重生); kói-sin(改新); ūaⁿ-sin(換身); têng-sin(重新); tsãu-sin(造新).

**regent**, thòi-lí kok-chèng(代理國政).

**regicide**, chhì-kun(弒君).

**regimen**, khiēⁿ-tshùi(疆喙); kài-kháu(戒口).

**regiment**, che̍k-ki-piaⁿ(一支兵); che̍k-ki-kun(一支軍).

**region**, tī-hng(地方). *the whole*, che̍k-phài tī-hng(一派地方); pìn-tī-hng(遍地方面).

**register**, *to*, kì(記); kì-lo̍k(記錄); teng-chiã(登籍); lo̍k-chiã(錄籍). *a*, phõu(簿); lo̍k-chiã(錄籍); chheh-chiã(冊籍). *genealogical*, tso̍k-phóu(族譜); hieⁿ-phóu(鄉譜).

**regret**, huân-ló(煩惱); iu-būn(憂悶); siẽⁿ-siú-hùe(想守悔). *to*, liên-sieh(憐惜); thiàⁿ-sieh(痛惜). *matter for*, khó-sieh(可惜); khó-liên(可憐).

**regular**, ũ-tshùn-chhieh(有寸尺); ũ-tshṳ̀-tõiⁿ(有次第); ũ-tshôiⁿ-ãu(有蠶後); chiàⁿ(正). *conduct*, tuan-chiàⁿ(端正); chiàⁿ-keng(正經); kuaⁿ-chiàⁿ(官正).

**regulate**, *a watch*, tshâu-chiàⁿ(移正); tshâu-méⁿ-mān(移猛慢).

**regulations**, kui-lī(規例); kui-tiâu(規條); chiang-thiâⁿ(章程); tiâu-kui(條規); huap-tōu(法度); kui-kṳ́(規矩); tsún-sîn(準神).

**rehearse**, *to one*, o̍h pun-i-thiaⁿ(學分伊聽).

**reign**, tsò-huâng-tì(做皇帝); tî-kok(坐位); tsõ-ūi(坐位); lí-kok-chèng(理國政); lí-chhiâu-chèng(理朝政). *in the reign of Tao-Kwang*, Tãu-kuang nîⁿ--kan(道光年間); Tãu-kuang tsõ-ūi(道光坐位).

**reins**, bé-soh(馬索). *to hold*, khan-bé-soh(牽馬索).

**reiterate**, têng-tàⁿ(重呾); tàⁿ-liáu tsài-tàⁿ(呾了再呾); tàⁿ-ūe têng-têng tha̍h-tha̍h(呾話重重疊疊); têng-tha̍h-tàⁿ(重疊呾). *teaching*, teng-lêng kàu-kài(叮嚀告誡); tsài-saⁿ teng-lêng(再三叮嚀); teng-lêng tsok-hù(叮嚀囑咐).

**reject**, màiⁿ(勿); khì-tso̍h(棄絕); khì-hiâm(棄嫌); tiu-tiāu(丟掉); khì-tiāu(棄掉); ka̍k-tiāu(角掉); phau-tiāu(拋掉); hám-tiāu(撼掉); sek-tiāu(釋掉). *with disgust*, iàm-khì(厭棄).

**rejoice**, huaⁿ-hí(歡喜); hí-la̍k(喜樂); hí-zua̍t(喜悅). *others*, khṳt-nâng huaⁿ-hí(乞人歡喜). *rejoicings*, hí-sṳ̄(喜事); âng-sṳ̄(紅事); hí-la̍k(喜樂); lāu-jie̍t(鬧熱).

**relapse**, huán-pēⁿ(反病); pēⁿ tò-huán(病倒反); têng-kám(重感). *frequent*, che̍k-huán che̍k-oh(一反一惡); huán-huán ho̍k-ho̍k(反反復復).

**relate**, o̍h(學); tui-su̍t(追述); káng(講); tàⁿ(呾). *old stories*, o̍h-kóu(學古). *relating to*, ũ-siang-kuan(有相關); ũ-kuan-hĩ(有關係); ũ-kan-sia̍p(有干涉); so̍k(屬).

**relations**, chhin-nâng(親人); chhin-chhek(親戚). *by marriage*, chhin-chiâⁿ(親情). *by blood*, tah-ne̍k-chhin(搭肉親). *distant*, ién-chhin(親戚); só-ién(親戚).

**relax**, pàng-sang(放鬆); pàng-lēng(放冗). see RECREATION.

**release**, pàng(放); sek-pàng(釋放); kói-pàng(解放); kói-pa̍k(解縛); sek-pa̍k(釋縛); kói-thut(解脫).

**relent**, sek-náuⁿ(息惱); sim lo̍h(心落); siẽⁿ-tńg(想轉).

**relieve**, *the poor*, chín-chì phîn-khiông(賑濟貧窮); chiu-chì(周濟); chì-kip(濟急); chiu-kip(周急); kiù-khùn(救困); kiù-phîn(救貧); si-chì(施濟). *pain*, chí-thiàⁿ(止痛).

**relief**, *in*, phû(浮).

**religion**, kà(教); kà-tãu(教導). *the three religions*, saⁿ-kà(三教): Zû(儒), Sek(釋), Tãu(道). *Protestant*, Iâ-sou-kà(耶穌教). *R. Cath.*, Thien-tsú-kà(天主教).

**relinquish**, pàng-tiāu(放掉); zũi-sit(遺失); siá-khì(捨棄). *(to another)*, thò-jiãng(退讓).

**relish**, hàuⁿ(好); hàuⁿ-chia̍h(好食); zua̍t-kháu(悅口); súang-kháu(爽口); ha̍h-chia̍h(合食); ha̍h-tshùi(合喙); hó-bī-sòu(好味素); hó-bī(好味); hó-chia̍h(好食).

**rely**, *on*, íⁿ-kõu(依靠); i-kõu(依靠); uá(倚); uá-kõu(倚靠); íⁿ-nãiⁿ(依賴); khùa-kõu(掛靠); kõu(靠); thoh-kõu(託靠); chiã(藉); kõu-chiã(靠藉).

**remain**, nāⁿ(在). *here*, nāⁿ--kò〔〕; nāⁿ chí-kò〔〕. *over*, tshûn(存); sīn(剩); ũ-tshûn(有存); ũ-sīn(有剩); ũ-iông-ṳ̂(有容餘); ũ-iẽn-ṳ̂(有延餘); ũ-ṳ̂-sīn(有餘剩).

**remarkable**, hui-siêⁿ(奇巧); koh-iēⁿ(各樣). *remarkably expensive*, koh-iēⁿ-kùi(閣樣貴).

**remedy**, ui-huap(醫法); tî-pēⁿ kâi-huap(治病个法). *no*, bô-kiù(無救); bô-pōu(無步); bô-pièn(無變).

**remember**, kì-tit(記得); it-tit(憶得); kì-liãm(記念); sṳ-liãm(憶得). *do not*, m̄-it-tit(毋一得); m̄-kì-tit(毋記得).

**remind**, *me*, lṳ́ thói-úa it-tit(汝體我一得); lṳ́ kāng-úa sie-hũ it-tit(汝共我相扶一得).

**remiss**, tũaⁿ(惰); hân-hẽ〔〕; chhìn-tshái(凊彩); kóu-chhiáⁿ(姑且). *(as one in authority)*, pàng-làng-sang(放零鬆).

**remit**, sià(赦); sià-mién(赦免). *taxes*, sià-niêⁿ(赦糧). *rent*, sià-tsou(赦租); kien-tsou(減租); mién-tsou(免租).

**remonstrate**, khǹg-kòi(勸戒); khǹg-kàn(勸諫); cheh-lũn(責論).

**remote**, hñg(遠); iâu-ién(遙遠).

**remorse**, siẽⁿ-siú-hùe(想守悔); thiàⁿ-hùe(痛悔).

**remove**, puaⁿ-khui(搬開); khie̍h-khui(挈開); súa-khui(徙開); î-súa(移徙); chhien-î(遷移); chhien-súa(遷徙). *bad influences*, khṳ́-siâ to̍k-mu̍t(去斜毒沒); khu-siâ to̍k-mu̍t(區斜毒沒).

**remuneration**, pò-siéⁿ(報賞). *to a teacher*, sok-kim(束金); sok-siu(束收); tsṳ-kim(束金). *for work done*, kang-chîⁿ(工錢).

**rend**, li̍h(裂); lì(攦); li̍h-phùa(裂破); lì-li̍h(攦裂); túi-li̍h(扯裂).

**renew**, tsò-sin(做新); sin-tsãu(新舊); kói-sin(改新). *(change)* ūaⁿ(換).

**renounce**, khì-tiāu(棄掉); khì-tso̍h(棄絕); m̃-jīn(毋認). *one's company*, tso̍h-kau(絕交).

**renowned**, ũ hó-miâⁿ-siaⁿ(有好名聲); miâⁿ iâng sì-hái(名揚四海); tshut-miâⁿ(出名); thuân-miâⁿ(傳名); chhî-miâⁿ(馳名).

**rent**, *to, a house, *&c*, sùe(稅); tsou(租); pa̍k(縛). *house rent*, tshù-tsou(厝租); tshù-sùe(厝稅).

**repair**, siu-si̍p(收拾); pa-lói(巴禮); chiáⁿ-lí(整理); siu-chiáⁿ(修整); póu(補).

**repay**, hôiⁿ(還); hâiⁿ(還); kau-hôiⁿ(交還); pûe-hôiⁿ(賠還). see RECOMPENSE.

**repeal**, hùi-huap(廢法); phah-tiāu-lī(拍掉例).

**ridiculous**, hó-chhiè(好笑); khó-chhiè(可笑); bô-tõ-lí(無道理).

**right**, tie̍h(着); chiàⁿ(正); sĩ(侍); bô-tshò(無錯); *a wrong*, sin-uan(申冤). *and wrong*, sĩ-hui(是非); tn̂g-tó(長短). *do*, tshông-chiàⁿ(衝正). *hit the right method*, tie̍h-huap(着法). *it is my*, sĩ uá hūn-tsôiⁿ só-eng-kai(是我分前所應該); sĩ úa pńg-téng só-tit(是我本等所得). *hand*, chiàⁿ-chhiú(正手); iũ-chhiú(右手). *put to rights*, chiáⁿ-lí(整理); siu-chiáⁿ(修整); tshâu-sì-chiàⁿ(移四正). *how can this be right*, khí-ũ tshṳ́-lí(豈有此理).

**righteous**, ngĩ(義); kong-ngĩ(公義). *to declare*, chheng-ngĩ(稱義).

**rigid**, ngẽ(硬); kien-ngẽ(堅硬); ngiâm(嚴).

**rigorous**, ngiâm(嚴); ngiâm-sok(嚴肅); ngiâm-tiâu(嚴條).

**rim**, kîⁿ(墘); tshùi(喙). *of wheel*, chhia-lûn-kîⁿ(車輪墘).

**ring**, *a*, huân(環); khuan(圈); khou(箍). *arm*, chhiú-huân(手環). *finger*, chhiú-tsat(手節); chhiú-chí(手指); kài-chí(戒指).

**ring**, *to*, *a bell*, iẽ-leng(搖鈴); lõng-leng(弄鈴); khà-cheng(扣鐘); phah-cheng(拍鐘). *ringing in the ears*, hĩⁿ-khang ōng-ōng-kiè(耳空訇訇叫); hĩⁿ-khang-kúi kî-kî-kiè(耳空鬼棋棋叫).

**ringleader**, thâu-nâng(頭人). *of thieves or rebels*, tsha̍t-thâu(做頭).

**ring-worm**, sién(癬); pe̍h-sién(白癬); âng-sién(紅癬); gue̍h-īn-sién(月暈癬); gû-phûe-sién(牛皮癬); sip-sién(濕癬).

**rinse**, tñg(盪). *the mouth*, tñg-tshùi(盪喙).

**riot**, tshàu-nãuⁿ(噪鬧); lũan-nãuⁿ(亂鬧). *stir up*, kek-lũan(激亂).

**rip**, *up*, le̍h(裂); le̍h-khui(裂開); le̍h-phùa(礫破).

**ripe**, se̍k(熟); kàu-tsúi(夠水).

**ripple**, tsúi-hûn(水痕); tsúi-mīn niàuⁿ-niàuⁿ(水面鳥鳥).

**rise**, khí(起); tsáu-khí(早起). *up*, khí-sin(起身); tsáu-khí(早起); khiã--khí-lâi(徛起來). *in price*, kè chiãm-chiãm-kûiⁿ(價漸漸懸). *in rank*, kau-seng(高升); seng-khueh(升缺). *the rise(origin)*, kṳn-iû(根由); ngûan-iû(原由); ngûan-thâu(原頭); ngûan-in(原因). *and fall*, heng-sue(興衰); heng-sẽng sue-mûiⁿ(興盛衰微). *of sun*, ji̍t-thâu tshut(日頭出); ji̍t tshut(日出); ji̍t chiẽⁿ(日上). *of moon*, gue̍h chiẽⁿ(月上); gue̍h phû(月浮); gue̍h seng(月生). *of tide*, lâu-tsúi tōa(流水大); tsúi tĩⁿ(水漲); lâu tĩⁿ(流漲).

**risk**, mãuⁿ-hiám(貌險); hiám--tang khiã(險當徛). *one's life*, piàⁿ-miāⁿ(拚命); piàⁿ-sèⁿ-miāⁿ(拚性命); pheng-miāⁿ(拼命); pheng-sèⁿ-miāⁿ(拼性命); mãuⁿ-miāⁿ(冒命); mãuⁿ-sí(冒死); tì-miāⁿ(致命).

**rite**, lói(禮); lói-siàu(禮數); lói-ngî(禮儀); lói-bûn(禮文). *Book of Rites*, lí-kì(禮記).

**rivalry**, sie-tàu(相鬥); cheⁿ-iâⁿ(爭贏); cheⁿ-sèng(爭勝).

**rive**, phùa(破); phùa-khui(破開); phùa-pôiⁿ(破爿); phùa-li̍h(破裂).

**river**, hô(河); khoi(溪); kang(江). *one*, che̍k-tiâu-hô(一條河).

**rivet**, hôu-khî-tah〔〕; teng-búe phah-pêⁿ(釘尾拍平).

**rivulet**, khoi-kiáⁿ(溪囝); sié-khoi(小溪); suaⁿ-kheⁿ(山坑).

**road**, lōu(路); lōu-thâu(路頭). *highroad*, kuaⁿ-lōu(官路); tōa-lōu(大路). *roadside*, lōu-kîⁿ(路墘). *on the road*, tõ-lōu--chiēⁿ(在路上).

**roar**, háu(吼); kiè-tōa-siaⁿ(叫大聲). *roar as waves*, hái-éng ho-ho-háu(海湧呵呵吼). *roar as lion*, sai háu(獅吼).

**roast**, *to*, pek(煏). *meat*, sie-ne̍k(燒肉); pek-gû-ne̍k(煏牛肉). *to parch, as coffee beans*, tshá(炒).

**rob**, phah-kiap(拍劫); chhiéⁿ-pak(搶剝); khiâng-chhiéⁿ(強搶). *robbers*, tsha̍t(賊); tsha̍t-bé(賊馬).

**robe**, tōa-phâu(大袍); tn̂g-phâu(長袍); phâu-kùa(袍褂); lói-ho̍k(禮服); lí-ho̍k(禮服). *royal*, chhiâu-ho̍k(朝服); uâng-ho̍k(皇服). *(of mandarin, embroidered with dragons)*, máng-phâu(蟒袍).

**robust**, tsàng(壯); tsàng-kiẽn(壯健); kiẽn-tsàng(健壯); khin-kiāⁿ(輕健); khang-kiẽn(康健); khiâng-tsâng(強叢).

**rock**, chie̍h(石); chie̍h-pûaⁿ(石盤); tōa-chie̍h(大石). *strike on a rock*, tsûn lṳ̂-chie̍h(船驢石); tsûn ta̍k--tie̍h chie̍h(船泊着石). *rockery*, ke-suaⁿ(加山); ké-suaⁿ(假山).

**rock**, *to*, iê(搖); iẽ(搖). *rocking basket(cradle)*, iê-nâⁿ(搖籃).

**rocket**, húe-su̍h〔〕. *to fire a*, pàng-húe-su̍h〔〕.

**rod**, tshûe(槌); ko(戈); tek-póiⁿ(竹板). *fishing-rod*, tièⁿ-ko(電戈).

**rodomontade**, la-kè〔〕; sueh-húang(說謊); la-húang(拉謊); huah-sì(喝勢).

**roe**, *a*, te̍k-bó(鹿母).

**roe**, *of fish*, hṳ̂-tshun(魚春).

**rogue**, láu-kiáⁿ(老囝); kuang-kùn(光棍); láu-kuang-kùn(老光棍).

**roll**, lín(輪); khah(磕). *about*, khah-lâi khah-khṳ̀(籗來籗去); lín-lâi lín-khṳ̀(輦來輦去). *up*, kauh(捲); kauh--khí(捲起). *as boat*, bái(擺). *dough*, khoih-mīⁿ(挾麵). *the eyes*, ma̍k-chiu lìn-lâi lìn-khṳ̀(目睭輾來輾去). *thread*, in-sùaⁿ(引線); tîⁿ-sùaⁿ(填線); khûan-sùaⁿ(圈線). *a*, che̍k-kauh(一捲).

**roller**, chie̍h-lín(石輪); chie̍h-khah〔〕. *for cloth*, ta̍h-pòu-chie̍h(踏布石). *for dough*, mīⁿ-thûi(麵槌).

**roof**, tshù-téng(厝頂).

**room**, *pâng; koiⁿ; pâng-koiⁿ; one*, che̍k-koiⁿ-pâng(一間房). *no*, bô-ūi-tshṳ̀(無位處); bô-khang-tī(無空地); bô-khang-tshù(無空厝); bô-tī-hng(無地方). *a bed-room*, u̍t-pâng(夗房). *drawing-room*, khah-thiaⁿ(客廳); kheh-thiaⁿ(客廳).

**roost**, *for fowls*, koi-tiâu(雞條). *to*, koi chiẽⁿ-tiâu(雞上條); chhi-tiâu(棲條).

**root**, kṳn(根); kṳn-thâu(根頭). *of tree*, chhiū-kṳn(樹根). *origin*, kṳn-pún(根本); ngûan-thâu(源頭). *to root up*, po̍ih-kṳn(拔根); pi̍t-po̍ih-tiāu(畢拔掉).

**rope**, soh(索). *to make*, phah-soh(拍索); ká-soh(絞索). *walk on a*, kiâⁿ-soh(行索). *six-fold*, la̍k-kóu-soh(六股索).

**rosary**, liām-tsu(唸珠).

**rose**, gue̍h-kì-hue(月季花).

**rotten**, àu(腐); hu-hu(腐腐); mîⁿ(綿); hûan(桓); hiúⁿ(朽); nūaⁿ(軟); nūaⁿ hiúⁿ-hiúⁿ(軟朽朽). *wood*, hiúⁿ-ba̍k(朽目); thûaⁿ-tshâ(拖柴). *tooth*, tsù-khí(蛀起); khí tsù-tiāu(起蛀掉).

**rouge**, in-chi(胭脂); in-nîⁿ(胭泥). *to use*, tiám-in-chi(點胭脂); bua̍h-in-chi(抹胭脂).

**rough**, siap(澀); tshou(粗); tshou-siap(粗澀). *copy*, kó(稿). *road*, khi-khu(崎嶇). *roughly done, as outline*, tsháu-tsut(草卒). *rough unfinished article*, phue-tho(胚胎); phue-bôu(坯模).

**round**, îⁿ(圓). *to turn*, huiⁿ-lìn-tńg(翻輾轉); ut-tńg-thâu(屈轉頭).

**rouse**, *out of sleep*, hàm-chhéⁿ(喊醒); kiè-chhéⁿ(叫醒). *one's attention to anything*, that-chhéⁿ(踢醒). *incite*, kóu-bú(鼓舞); thie-so(挑梳); kà-so(教唆). *roused*, chhéⁿ-ngõ(醒悟); kéng-chhéⁿ(警醒).

**rout**, *to*, phah-tsáu(拍走); phah-sùaⁿ(拍散). *to be routed*, pāi-tsáu(敗走); pāi-tīn(敗陣). *a rout*, luãn-tsáu(亂走).

**route**, lōu(路).

**row**, hâng(行); lie̍t(列); tsūe(行). *in rows*, che̍k-hâng che̍k-hâng(一行一行); che̍k-lie̍t che̍k-lie̍t(一列一列).

**row**, *to make a*, kî-kâ bó-jiáng〔〕; tshàu-nãuⁿ(噪鬧).

**row**, *to*, kò-tsûn(划船); kò-chiéⁿ(划槳).

**rub**, bûa(磨); chhiù(漱); chhit(拭); zûe(挼); buah(抹); kueh(刮). *ink*, bûa-ba̍k(磨墨). *with salt*, lõu-iâm(陋鹽); sa-iâm(沙鹽); na̍k-iâm(捺鹽). *the hands*, zûe-chhiú(挼手). *clean*, bûa-kng(磨光); chhiù-kng(漱光). *clean (with dry cloth)*, chhit-chheng-khih(拭清潔). *clean (with damp cloth)*, zṳ̂(挐).

**rubbish**, nah-sap(垃圾); bô-ēng-mu̍eh(無用物).

**ruby**, âng-pó-chie̍h(紅寶石).

**rudder**, tõa(舵); tsûn-tõa(船舵). see HELM.

**rude**, tshou-nâng(粗人); bô-lói(無禮); bô-kui-kṳ́(無規矩); m̄-hiáu chhêng-lí(毋曉情理). *behave rudely to one*, tshong-tsuãng(衝撞).

**rue**, *to*, siẽⁿ-tie̍h huân-ló(想着煩惱); siẽⁿ-hùe(想悔); huân-ló(煩惱); siẽⁿ-siú-hùe〔〕. *rueful countenance*, mīn tshôu-tshôu(面愁愁); mīn-sek huân-ló(面色煩惱); niàuⁿ-bâi(鳥眉毛).

**ruffian**, khiâng-thû(強徒); húiⁿ-lūi(匪類); húiⁿ-thû(匪徒).

**ruffled**, *water*, tsúi-mīn jiâu-jiâu(水面縐縐); tsúi-mīn niàuⁿ-niàuⁿ(水面鳥鳥). *mind*, sim iâu-tõng(心搖動).

**rug**, *hearth*, húe-lôu-chiⁿ(火爐氈).

**rugged**, tshou-siap(粗澀); khi-khu(崎嶇).

**ruin**, pāi(敗); pāi-hāi(敗害); pāi-hũai(敗壞); hùi(廢); hùi-hāi(毀害); hùi-hũai(毀壞); phùa-hāi(破害); húiⁿ(毀); húiⁿ-hāi(毀害). *to cause*, tì-kàu-hāi(置到害). *of house*, phùa-tshù(破厝); phùa-tshù-táu(破厝倒); tó-tshù(倒厝). *ruinous*, hāi-sṳ̄(害事). *ruined, of a person*, phùa-ke(破家).

**rule**, *to*, kuán(管); kuán-lí(管理); tsú-kuán(主管); tsú-tī(主治); kuán-hat(管轄). *a ruler*, tsú(主); tsú-tsái(主宰); kuaⁿ-hú(官府).

**rule**, *a*, huap(法); kui(規); huap-tōu(法度); kui-tiâu(規條); huap-tsat(法節); kui-kṳ́(規矩); tsún-sîn(準神). *(programme)*, chiang-thiâⁿ(章程); chiang-thêng(章程). *for measuring*, chhieh(尺).

**rule**, *to*, *or draw lines on*, *paper*, phah-keh(拍格); phah-tsūe(拍襊); ūe-hûn(畫痕); ūe-keh(畫格). *a ruler for paper*, kài-chhieh(戒尺).

**ruminate**, *as cow*, huan-tsháu(反草). *mentally*, sṳ-siẽⁿ(思想); huán-ho̍k sṳ-siẽⁿ(反覆思想).

**rumour**, hong-siaⁿ(風聲); hong-bũn(風聞); iâu-ngân(謠言); hong-iâu(風謠); iâu-thûan(謠傳); koi-chhĩ-ūe(街市話).

**rumpled**, jiâu(皺); jiâu-jiâu(皺皺); niàuⁿ-niàuⁿ〔〕; póu-póu〔〕; seⁿ-hûn(生痕); chhi̍p kàu-póu-póu〔〕. *don't rumple it*, màiⁿ-chhi̍p-jiâu〔〕.

**run**, tsáu(走); pháu-tsáu(跑走); phun-tsáu(奔走); liãu-tsáu(了走); tsáu-méⁿ(走猛). *away secretly*, thua-tsáu(拖走). *from danger*, pī-tsáu(避走); tô-tsáu(逃走). *round and round*, khuan-tsáu(寬走); hui-tsáu(飛走). *over, as liquid*, lâu--tshut(流出); iah-tshut(溢出); múaⁿ--tshut(滿出); kài--tshut(界出). *out, as liquid*, lāu(漏); lāu-tiāu(漏掉). *after*, jiāu(繞); tui-jiāu(追擾); kúaⁿ-jiāu(趕擾). *into harbour*, sái-tsûn ji̍p-káng(駛船入港). *run into (collide with)*, lṳ̂(勞); lôi(犁); tsũang(撞); sie-khãm(相鈸). *run into (collide with) (lightly)*, sie-tiaⁿ(相撞).

**running**, *water*, ua̍h-tsúi(活水). *sore*, sia̍p n̂g-sûaⁿ-tsúi kâi-tshng-kháu(涉黃腺水个村口). *hand of writing*, tshó-jī(草字).

**rupture**, see HERNIA.

**rural**, hieⁿ-ẽ(鄉下). *occupations*, tsoh-tshân khang-khùe(作田工課); lông-sṳ̄(農事).

**rush**, *against*, tshong-tsũang(衝撞); tshuang-tsũang(窗撞). *an enemy*, tshong-tīn(衝陣). *of water*, tsúi lâu kā-kā-kiè(水流咳咳叫); tsúi kip(水急).

**rushes**, kiâm-tsháu(鹹草); teng-sim-tsháu(燈心草).

**Russia**, Ngô-lô-sṳ kok(俄羅斯國).

**rust**, san(銹). *rusty*, seⁿ-san(生銹). *worn away with*, kuah-tiāu(割掉).

**rustic**, hieⁿ-ẽ-nâng(鄉下人); hieⁿ-ngô(鄉愚).

**rustling**, *of wind*, huang sā-sā-kiè(風灑灑叫).

**rut**, *of wheel*, chhia-lûn-lōu(車輪路); chhia-lûn-kau(車輪溝).

**rutting**, *time, of animals*, khí-khûn(起群).

### S

**Sabbath**, an-sek-ji̍t(安息日); lói-pài-ji̍t(禮拜日).

**sack**, pòu-tō(布袋); mûaⁿ-tō(麻袋); mûaⁿ-phûe-tō(麻皮袋).

**sackcloth**, mûaⁿ-pòu(麻布); tshou-mûaⁿ-pòu(粗麻布). *to wear*, chhēng-mûaⁿ(穿麻); chhēng-mûaⁿ-pòu(穿麻布).

**sacred**, siàⁿ(聖).

**sacrifice**, chì(祭); chì-mue̍h(祭物). *to*, hièn-chì(獻祭); chì; siet-chì(設祭); kiâⁿ-chì(行祭); chì-sṳ̂(祭祠). *a lamb*, thâi-iêⁿ ûi-chì(刣羊爲祭). *one's life*, siá-miāⁿ(捨命).

**sacrilege**, siet-to̍k siàⁿ-mue̍h(褻瀆聖物).

**sad**, iu-tshôu(憂愁); iu-būn(憂悶); tshôu-būn(愁悶); hûan-sim(煩心); hûan-ló(煩惱).

**saddle**, bé-uaⁿ(馬鞍). *to*, kùa-bé-uaⁿ(掛馬鞍).

**safe**, ún-tǹg(穩當); thêng-tǹg(停當); thêng-ún(停穩); thó-tàng(妥當); ún-ún(穩穩).

**safe**, *a*, *or strong box*, kap-būan(甲萬). *iron*, thih-kap-būan(鐵甲萬). *for meat*, se-tû(西櫥); chia̍h-tû(食櫥).

**sagacious**, tshong-mêng(聰明); ũ-sim-sṳ̄(有心事); õi-siẽⁿ(會想); lêng-lāi(伶俐).

**safe**, *a*, siàⁿ-nâng(聖人); siàⁿ-hiên(聖賢).

**sago**, sai-kok-îⁿ(西谷圓).

**sail**, *a*, phâng(帆); huang-phâng(風帆). *to set*, khí-phâng(起帆); chiẽⁿ-phâng(上帆); po̍ih-phâng(拔帆); iâng-phâng(揚帆). *to take in*, phâng heh-sòi〔〕; heh-phâng〔〕. *to sail*, sái-tsûn(駛船); sái-huang(駛風); khui-tsûn(開船). *sailor*, kiâⁿ-tsûn-nâng(行船人); tsúi-siú(水手). *sailing vessel(foreign)*, kap-pán-tsûn(甲板船). *twenty sail*, jī-tsa̍p-chiah-tsûn(二十隻船).

**sake**, *for the sake of*, in-ũi(因爲); uân-in(原因); ũi-tie̍h(爲着).

**salad**, chheⁿ-tshài(生菜); phang-tshài(芳菜).

**salary**, kang-chîⁿ(工錢); kang-tsṳ(工資). *(official)*, hóng-lo̍k(俸祿); iáng-liâm-ngṳ̂n(養廉銀). *of teacher*, tsṳ-kim(書金); sok-kim(束金); sok-siu(束收).

**sale**, *on*, tah-bōi(搭賣); tshut-bōi(出賣). *deed of*, khòi(契).

**saliva**, nũaⁿ(涎); tshùi-nũaⁿ(喙涎). *flowing*, lâu-nũaⁿ(流涎).

**sallow**, mīn n̂g-n̂g(面黃黃).

**sally**, tshong-tshut(衝出).

**salt**, iâm(鹽). *(adjective)*, kiâm(鹹). *to*, lõu-kiâm(滷鹹); seh-iâm(瀉鹽); suah-iâm(撒鹽). *salt-cellar*, iâm-ti̍h(鹽碟); iâm-cheng(鹽精). *salt-pans*, iâm-tiâⁿ(鹽埕); iâm-khu(鹽區); iâm-tiêⁿ(鹽場). *to make salt in these*, pha̍k-iâm(曝鹽); sài-iâm(曬鹽). *medicinal salts*, phok-siau(樸硝); gê-siau(牙硝).

**saltpetre**, siau(硝); iâm-siau(鹽硝).

**salubrious**, tsúi-thóu hó(水土好); tī-khì hûa-phêng(地氣和平).

**salute**, pài(拜); mn̄g-hāu(問候); kióng-chhiú(拱手); ip-tsã〔〕; siang-chieh-mn̄g(相借問).

**seduce**, iú-ho̍k(誘惑); ín-iú(引誘); mîⁿ-ho̍k(迷惑); kóu-ho̍k(蠱惑); thiâu-hì(調戲).

**sedulous**, ēng-kang(用功); khṳ̂n(勤); khṳ̂n-kang(勤工); siêⁿ-sim(上心).

**see**, *to*, thóiⁿ(睇); kièn(見); kìⁿ(見); thóiⁿ-kìⁿ(睇見). *not to*, thóiⁿ-m̄-kìⁿ(睇毋見). *through*, thóiⁿ-phùa(睇破); thóiⁿ-kàu-thàu(睇到透); thóiⁿ-thàng(睇通). *go to see one*, khṳ̀-kìⁿ(去見); khṳ̀ kāng-nâng sie-kìⁿ(去共人相見); khṳ̀ kāng-nâng hũe--che̍k-mīn(去共人會一面). *one's reflection, as in mirror*, chiè-kìⁿ nâng-mīn(照見人面). *seeing that*, kì-jiên(既然); kì-sĩ(既是).

**seed**, chéng(種); chéng-chí(種子). *to sow*, iā-chéng(播種); lo̍h-chéng(落種). *seedling*, tsai(栽); chhiū-tsai(樹栽); hue-tsai(花栽). *of rice*, ng(秧).

**seek**, tshūe(揣); chhê(查); khiû(求); thû(圖); thó(討); chhîm(尋). *an opportunity to injure one*, tshūe-phāng(覓縫); tshūe-khiah(覓隙).

**seem**, *to*, chhin-chhiẽⁿ(親像); siang-sṳ̃(像是); húang-sṳ̃(仿似). *how does it seem to you*, lṳ́ thóiⁿ-tie̍h tsãi-seⁿ(汝睇着在生). *as if dead*, kâi-iēⁿ àn-sí hièⁿ-seⁿ(個樣按死向生).

**seemly**, ha̍h-ngî(合宜); ha̍h-sek(合適).

**seize**, lia̍h(掠); lû-lia̍h(虜掠); chhiéⁿ-lia̍h(搶掠); khîm-lia̍h(擒掠); túi-lia̍h(縋掠). *a thief*, lia̍h-tsha̍t(掠賊). *an opportunity*, sêng-ki-hũe(乘機會); sêng-kòiⁿ(乘計). *lie in wait to*, tng-tán-lia̍h(當等掠); biê-lia̍h〔〕.

**seldom**, chié(少); hán--tit(罕得); hán(罕). *met with*, hán-hông(罕逢).

**select**, súan(選); súan-to̍h(選擇); to̍h(擇); kóiⁿ(揀); kóiⁿ-to̍h(揀擇); to̍h--tshut-lâi(擇出來).

**self**, ka-kī(家己); tsṳ̃-kí(自己); pńg-sin(本身); chhin-sin(親身). *self-examination*, tsṳ̃-séng(自省); tsṳ̃-sṳ(自私); tsṳ̃-siẽⁿ(自想); tsṳ̃-tshat(自察); tsṳ̃-mn̄g(自問); tsṳ̃-àn(自按); séⁿ-tshat ka-kī(省察家己); mn̄g-sim chẽⁿ-àn(問心靜案). *self-satisfied*, tsṳ̃-tsok(自囑). *self-conceit*, tsṳ̃-múaⁿ(自滿); tsṳ̃-sĩ(自是). *injure oneself*, tshâng-hāi ka-kī(殘害家己); tsṳ̃-pãu(自暴); tsṳ̃-khì(自棄); tsṳ̃-tshú khî-hũa(自取奇禍).

**selfish**, sṳ-sim(私心); tsṳ̃-sim ũi-kí(自心謂己); lĩ-kí(私心); kù-kí(私心). *unselfish*, chì-kong bô-sṳ(至公無私); thãi-nâng zû-kí(待人如己); kãu-nâng po̍h-kí(厚人薄己).

**sell**, bōi(賣); phùaⁿ(判). *rice*, thiè-chhek(糶粟); thiè-bí(糶米). *on credit*, chhia-bōi(賒賣). *for ready money*, hīn-bōi(現賣); hīn-chîⁿ kau-kuan(現錢交關). *by weight*, lũn-kṳn-bōi(論根賣). *by auction*, khà-lõi-lang(扣黎郎); khà-lang(扣郎).

**semen**, cheng(精).

**semicircle**, pùaⁿ-khou(半箍); îⁿ-che̍k-pùaⁿ(圓一半).

**send**, sái(駛); chhe(差); khién(遣); huat(發); kià(寄). *back*, kià-tńg(寄轉); sái-tńg(駛轉); huat-hûe(發回). *for one*, hám-nâng-lâi(撼人來); kiè-nâng-lâi(叫人來). *under custody*, kòi-ah(計鴨); kòi-sàng(計送). *a letter*, kià-sìn(寄信).

**seniot**, chiáng-chiá(長者); lãu-pùe(老輩). *he is my*, i tōa--úa(伊大我); i kâi nîⁿ-kí tōa--úa(伊个年紀大我).

**sense**, *of*, ì(意); ì-sṳ̀(意思); ì-ngĩ(意義). *the five senses*, ngóu-kuaⁿ(五官). *senseless*, bô-sueh(無說); hû-thû(糊塗); kông-kông(戇戇). *sensible*, thong-chhêng ta̍t-lí(通情達理); ũ-tsai-kak(有知覺); hiáu-sṳ̄ hiáu-lí(曉事曉理); chhêng-lí thong-thiet(情理通徹).

**sensitive**, *plant*, niauⁿ-tsháu(鳥草); siáu-lí-tsháu(少禮草).

**sensual**, chiú-sek tsṳ-thû(酒色之徒); tham-hue luãn-chiú(貪花亂酒); tham-sek-io̍k(貪色慾); hàuⁿ-chiú-sek(好酒色).

**sentence**, che̍k-kù-ūe(一句話). *sentence to death*, tiāⁿ-sí-tsũe(定死罪).

**sentinel**, sûn-sàu-piaⁿ(巡哨兵); sûn-huâng-piaⁿ(巡航兵); siú-keⁿ-piaⁿ(守更兵); sûn-siâⁿ-piaⁿ(巡城兵).

**separate**, lî-khui(離開); pun-lî(分離); pun-pie̍t(分別); hun-pie̍t(分別); keh-pie̍t(隔別). *separated by the sea*, keh-hái(隔海). *by a wall*, keh-chhiêⁿ(隔牆); keh-piah(隔壁).

**sepulchre**, phûn(墳); phûn-mõⁿ(墳墓). *imperial*, uâng-lêng(王陵).

**seraglio**, lãi-keng(內宮). *the inmates of*, keng-ngô múiⁿ-nńg(宮娥美軟).

**serene**, uaⁿ-chẽⁿ(安靜). *sky*, thiⁿ chêⁿ(天晴).

**series**, tshṳ̀-sũ(次序); tshṳ̀-tõiⁿ(次第); téng-lie̍t(等列); téng-khip(等級); pín-lie̍t pín-tõiⁿ(品列品第). *of years*, le̍h-nîⁿ(曆年).

**serious**, tãng(重); tōa(舵). *matter*, tōa-sṳ̄(大事). *disease*, pēⁿ tãng(病重). *in manner*, ngiâm-chiàⁿ(嚴正); kṳ́n-ngiâm(謹嚴).

**serpent**, tsûa(蛇). *one*, che̍k-tiâu-tsûa(一條蛇). *to creep as a*, so(蛇); kuãn(倦).

**serrate**, seⁿ-kṳ̀-khí(生鋸齒).

**servant**, kang-jîn(工人); ēng-jîn(用人); sái-hùan kâi-nâng(使喚个人); sái-tãng kâi kang-jîn(使重个工人); iông-kang kâi-nâng(傭工个人). *(applied to servants of foreigners)*, sĩ-tsái(侍仔). *(slave)*, nôuⁿ-po̍k(奴僕). *in a family*, ke-jîn(家人). *to be one's*, kāng-nâng tsò-kang(共人做工). *servants of mandarin*, kṳn-pan(跟班); kṳn-súi(跟隨).

**serve**, ho̍k-sṳ̃(服事); ho̍k-sĩ(服侍); ho̍k-hia̍h(服役); phōiⁿ-sṳ̄(辦事).

**server**, *a*, tháng-pûaⁿ(桶盤); tshâ-pûaⁿ(柴盤).

**serviceable**, hó-ēng(好用); ēng-tit-lâi(用得來).

**servile**, pui-khut(卑屈); kùe-khiam(過謙); tsù-kiong〔〕.

**set**, *a*, che̍k-hù(一副); che̍k-thàu(一套); che̍k-kah(一甲). *of books, a whole work*, che̍k-pang(一方). *changing sets of men several times a day*, che̍k-ji̍t ūaⁿ ke-sek-nâng(一日換家色人). *a mean set*, hiã-liû-pùe(下流輩).

**set**, *to*, *as gems*, sieⁿ-ge̍k(鑲玉). *as fruit*, kat-si̍t(結實); kit-chí(結子). *as sun*, ji̍t lo̍h(日落); ji̍t-thâu lo̍h-suaⁿ(日頭落山). *a watch*, sî-pie tshâu-chiàⁿ(時標移正). *to set about*, khui-chhiú(開手); khí-kang(起工). *at rest*, pàng-uaⁿ(放安). *bones*, chiap-kut(接骨). *eggs*, khṳt koi-bó pū-nñg(乞雞母孵卵). *down*, pàng--tõ-kò(放在塊); hẽ--lo̍h-khṳ̀(下落去). *fire to*, pàng-húe(放火); to̍h-húe(着火). *fire to (accidentally)*, sit-húe(失火). *one's heart on*, liû-sim(留心); tsuan-sim(專心); tsù-liãm(注念); tsù-ì(注意); kù-sim kù-ì(顧心顧意). *out on a journey*, khí-sin(起身); khí-kiâⁿ(起行); khí-thêng(起程); tõng-sin(動身). *the teeth on edge*, khí nńg(起軟). *out trees*, chèng-chhiū-tsai(種樹栽). *the table*, pái-toh(擺桌); pái-tshn̂g(擺床); pái-siet(擺設). *up*, li̍p(立); siet-li̍p(設立). *a shop*, sin-khui-phòu(新開舖). *sail*, khí-phâng(起帆). *an example*, piáu-iēⁿ(表樣); tsò-iēⁿ khṳt-nâng-o̍h(做樣乞人學).

**settle**, *an offair*, lí-chheng-tshó(理清楚); lí-tiāⁿ-tie̍h(理定着); tiāⁿ-tie̍h(定着). *how are you going to settle this*, àiⁿ-tsò-nîⁿ huat-lo̍h(愛怎呢發落). *settled*, tieh-lo̍h(着落); tàⁿ-theng-thó(呾停妥). *accounts*, ap-siàu(押數); chheng-siàu(清數); siàu-ba̍k chheng-tshó(數目清楚). *as muddy water*, tsõ-chheng(坐清). *a bargain*, bói-sêng(買成). *a quarrel*, hûa-sek(和息).

**seven**, chhit(七). *seventeen*, tsa̍p-chhit(十七).

**several**, kúi-kâi(幾個); sù-kâi(四五個); kúi-ūa-kâi(幾外個). *months*, sù-kâi-gu̍eh(四個月). *tens*, sù-tsa̍p-kâi(四十個).

**severe**, ngiâm(嚴); ngẽ(硬). *beating*, tãng-phah(重拍); phah-thiám-thiám(拍恬恬). *wound*, tãng-sieⁿ(重傷).

**sew**, *to*, thīⁿ(縫); thīⁿ-saⁿ(縫衫). *can you sew*, lṳ́ pat sái-tsam, mé(汝曉使針咩); õi-thīⁿ-saⁿ, mé(會縫衫咩). *sewing machine*, tsam-kui(針機).

**sewer**, tsúi-kau(水溝); sái-kau(屎溝).

**sex**, nâm-nńg tsṳ-hun-pie̍t(男女之分別).

**sextant**, *(or quadrant)*, niêⁿ-thiⁿ-chhieh(量天尺).

**shabby**, *mean*, phí-lõu(鄙陋); liẽn-siap(吝嗇); siáu-jîn(小人). *in dress*, chhēng-khah-khiãm(穿較儉); phok-lõu(樸陋).

**shackles**, kha-khàu chhiú-khàu(骹銬手銬); só-kha só-chhiú(鎖骹鎖手); tshâ-gô(柴鵝).

**shaddock**, iū(柚); táu-iū(豆柚); bi̍t-iū(蜜柚); hiang-iū(香柚).

**shade**, chia(遮). *of tree*, chhiū pì-ìm(樹庇蔭); chhiū ìm-liâng(樹蔭涼). *clouds shading sun*, hûn chia-ji̍t(雲遮日); hûn iám-ji̍t(雲掩日); hûn kài-ji̍t(雲蓋日). *a house shading from the sun*, tshù tsa̍h-ji̍t(厝閘日). *to shade light*, chia-kng(遮光); tsa̍h-kng(遮光). *lamp-shade*, teng-chia(燈遮); teng-tsãu(燈罩); teng-tà(燈罩); teng-tû(燈廚). *glass-shade*, po-lî-khàiⁿ(波籬蓋); po-lî-khàm(玻璃嵌). *shady*, im-liâng(陰涼).

**shadow**, iáⁿ(影). *under the shadow of the trees*, chhiū-im-ẽ(樹陰下).

**shaft**, pèⁿ(柄). *of spear*, chhieⁿ-pèⁿ(槍柄). *of arrow*, chìⁿ-kuaⁿ(箭桿). *of column*, thiãu-sin(兆身).

**shaggy**, phòng-môⁿ(蓬毛); phòng-môⁿ-sai(蓬毛獅); môⁿ jiàng-jiàng(毛茸茸); thâu-môⁿ phông-song(頭毛蓬松).

**shake**, iê(搖); iê-tõng(搖動); iê-lóu(搖櫓); iâu-tõng(搖動); chín-tõng(震動); tín-tãng(振動); chhĩm(沁); léng(冷). *hands*, siang-tùn-chhiú(相頓手). *off, as dust*, pũaⁿ-tiāu(拂掉); hìⁿ-tiāu(搖掉). *shaky, as when socket too wide*, lok-khok〔〕. *tremble*, khiū〔〕; tòng(凍).

**shall**, chiang-àiⁿ(將愛); pit(必); àiⁿ(愛).

**shallow**, chhién(淺). *in mind*, kièn-sek-chhién(見色淺).

**sham**, ké(假). see PRETEND.

**shambles**, *(slaughter-house)*, gû-tôu(牛屠). *(meat-market)*, bōi-ne̍k-chhĩ(賣肉市).

**shame**, siáu-lí(少禮); siu-chhíⁿ(羞恥). *put to*, kièn-siàu(見笑). *shamefaced*, ùi-siáu-lí(畏少禮). *shameful*, chhiú-sṳ̄(醜事); siáu-lí-sṳ̄(少禮事). *shameless*, m̄-ùi siáu-lí(毋畏少禮); mīn-phûe kãu(面皮厚).

**shampoo**, tûi(捶). *the loins*, tûi-ie(捶腰).

**shank**, thúi-thâu(腿頭).

**shape**, hêng(形); iēⁿ(樣); hêng-iēⁿ(形樣); hêng-iông(形容); môⁿ-iēⁿ(毛樣); hêng-siãng(形像); hêng-tsũang(形狀); tsũang-mãuⁿ(狀貌); iēⁿ-sièⁿ(樣像).

**share**, hūn(份). *divided into three shares*, pun-tsò saⁿ-hūn(分做三分).

**shark**, sua-hṳ̂(鯊魚). *fins*, hṳ̂-chhì(魚翅).

**sharp**, lāi(利). *pointed*, chiam(尖). *sharpen*, bûa-lāi(磨利); bûa-chiam(磨尖); phoi-chiam(批尖). *the appetite*, khui-ūi-kháu(開胃口). *sharp of the tongue*, tshùi lāi(喙利). *sharp-featured*, chiam-lāi(尖利). *clever*, lêng-lāi(伶俐). *a sharper*, kuang-kùn(光棍); láu-kiáⁿ(漏囝).

**shatter**, phùa-tshùi(破碎). *shattered in health*, phùa-sieⁿ(破傷).

**shave**, thì(剃); khoi(溪). *the head*, thì-thâu(剃頭). *the beard*, khoi-chhiu(剃鬚). *shaving outfit(barber's)*, thì-thâu-tàⁿ(剃頭呾).

**shavings**, *of hair*, thâu-môⁿ-kiáⁿ(頭毛囝). *of wood*, tshâ-phùe-thiu(柴杮抽). *of rattan*, tîn-si(藤絲).

**shawl**, muaⁿ(幔); muaⁿ-koiⁿ(幔肩); huan-muaⁿ(番幔).

**sheaf**, pé(把); tẽⁿ(掙); pa̍k(縛); tsáng(總); sok(束); hâ(縖).

**shear**, *to*, chién-môⁿ(剪毛); ka-môⁿ(鉸毛). *shears*, tōa-ka-to(大絞刀); chién-to(剪刀). *(kind of guillotine)*, hóuⁿ-thâu-tso̍ih(虎頭截).

**sheath**, khak(殼); sièⁿ(鞘). *of grass*, tsháu-khòu(草褲).

**sheathe**, *a sword*, to ji̍p-sièⁿ(刀入像); to ji̍p-khak(刀入殼).

**shed**, *to*, *teeth*, ūaⁿ-khí(換起); ūaⁿ-gê(換牙). *tears*, lâu-ma̍k-tsap(流目汁).

**shed**, *a*, chhiáng(廠); phâng-chhiáng(棚廠); phâng-pêⁿ(棚平).

**sheep**, iêⁿ(羊); mîⁿ-iêⁿ(棉羊). *sheep-fold*, iêⁿ-lô(羊牢); iêⁿ-lâng(羊籠); iêⁿ-liâu(羊寮); iêⁿ-tsàng(羊棧). *sheep-skin coat*, iêⁿ-phûe-niûⁿ(羊皮裘).

**sheet**, *of paper*, che̍k-tieⁿ-tsúa(一張紙). *for a bed*, phũe-toaⁿ(被單). *of sail*, liâu(寮); liâu-bó(寮母). *haul in the sheet*, sa-liâu(沙寮). *slack out*, sang-liâu(雙寮).

**shelf**, kè(架); keh(格); tsâng(叢).

**shell**, khak(殼). *egg-shell*, nñg-khak(卵殼). *of shall-fish*, ham-khak(蚶殼); lô-khak(螺殼). *to blow a*, pûn-pu(歕瓠).

**shelter**, pì-ìm(庇蔭); pau-pì(包庇). *from rain*, chia-hõu(遮雨); siám-hõu(閃雨). *to take*, tiàm-sin(坫身); tshâng-sin(藏身); siám(閃).

**shepherd**, chiéⁿ-iêⁿ kâi-nâng(掌羊个人); chiéⁿ-mo̍k(掌牧个人[訓]); mo̍k-jîn(牧人).

**shield**, pâi(牌); tîn-pâi(藤牌); tshâ-pâi(柴牌). *to carry a*, kũaⁿ-pâi(慣牌); mõng-pâi(茂牌); chia-pâi(遮牌).

**shift**, súa(徙); súa-ūi(徙位); puaⁿ-tshù(搬厝). *several shifts of cows, in a mill*, kúi-ūa thòi-gû(幾代替牛). *shiftless*, bô-pièn(無變).

**shin**, kha-liâm(骹臁).

**shine**, chiè(照); chiè-kng(照光); huat-kng(發光); huat-kuang(發光). *shining brightly*, tâng-tâng-kng(銅銅光).

**ship**, tsûn(船). *one*, che̍k-chiah-tsûn(一隻船). *foreign*, kap-pán-tsûn(甲板船). *ship-wreck*, tsûn phùa-tiāu(船破掉); pua̍h-phùa-tsûn(跋破船); pua̍h-tiāu-tsûn(跋掉船). *ship-wright*, tsõ-tsûn sai-pẽ(坐船司阜). *ship-captain (foreign)*, tsûn-tsú(船主).

**shirt**, sin-tói-saⁿ(身底衫); lãi-saⁿ(內衫); kṳ̃n-sin-i(近身衣); kūaⁿ-saⁿ(汗衫); tsṳ̀-kūaⁿ-saⁿ(漬汗衫).

**shiver**, *from cold*, khĩu(崎); tòng(凍); chhìn kàu kha̍p-kha̍p-sih(凊到合合薛).

**shiver**, *to pieces*, phùa tshap-tshap-tshùi(破插插碎).

**shocked**, tie̍h-kiaⁿ(着驚).

**shoe**, ôi(鞋). *pair of*, che̍k-sang-ôi(一雙鞋). *one*, che̍k-chiah-ôi(一隻鞋); che̍k-kha-ôi(一骹鞋). *women's small*, keng-ôi(經鞋). *leather*, phûe-ôi(皮鞋). *shoelast*, ôi-hùn(鞋楦). *shoe-horn*, ôi-chhiau(鞋鍬). *shoes for wet weather*, tsúi-ôi(水鞋); kia̍h(屐); tshâ-kia̍h(柴屐).

**shoot**, *with gun*, phah-chhèng(拍銃); pàng-chhèng(放銃); huat-chhèng(發銃); khui-chhèng(開銃); pàng-phàu(放炮). *an arrow*, siā-chìⁿ(射箭).

**shoot**, *up, as plant*, huat--khí-lâi(發起來); huat-gê(發芽); mêng-gê(萌芽); pauh-gê〔〕; thiu-gê(抽芽). *bamboo shoot*, tek-sún(竹笋).

**shooting**, *pains*, thiu-thiàⁿ(抽痛); tùn-thiàⁿ(頓痛). *stars*, chheⁿ tūi(星墜); chheⁿ kùe-keng(星過經).

**shop**, phòu(舖); tiàm(店). *name of*, phòu-hō(舖號); tiàm-hō(店號). *keeper*, khui-phòu tshâi-tsú(開舖財主); tiàm-tsú(店主); tiàm-ke(店家). *clerk in*, chiáng-kūiⁿ(掌櫃).

**shore**, suaⁿ(山); toi-ngãi(峙岸); hái-kîⁿ(海墘); khoi-kîⁿ(溪墘). *go on*, chiẽⁿ-suaⁿ(上山). *on*, tõ-suaⁿ-téng(在山頂).

**short**, tó(短). *time*, bô-kú(無久); chiãm-sî(暫時); siap-sî(澀時); khùn-kiáⁿ(頃囝). *as cake*, sou(酥). *do it by a short method*, tshông-méⁿ--tsò(從猛做). *short-hand writing*, sié-siá(小寫); tshó-jī(草字); kiám-pit-jī(減筆字). *short-sighted*, kṳ̃n-sĩ(近視); tó-sĩ(短視). *shortcoming*, khiàm-khueh(欠缺); put-ki̍p(不及). *neither exceed nor come short*, màiⁿ-thài-kùe iā màiⁿ-put-ki̍p(勿太過也勿不及).

**shot**, în-chí(鉛子); chhèng-chí(銃子); thih-tiâu(鐵條); thâng-chí(銅子). *a good shot*, miâⁿ-ke phah-chhèng(名家拍銃).

**should**, eng-kai(應該); eng-tng(應當); tie̍h(着); pńg-téng tie̍h(本等着).

**shoulder**, koiⁿ-thâu(肩頭). *carry on*, khiâ tõ-koiⁿ-thâu(騎在肩頭); taⁿ(擔). *ride on one's*, khiâ-koiⁿ-bé(騎肩馬).

**shout**, kiè-tōa-siaⁿ(叫大聲); háu-siaⁿ(吼聲); háu-siaⁿ tōa-kiè(吼聲大叫). *of joy*, tuah-tshái(咄彩).

**shove**, léng(推); léng-khui(推開); léng-kiâⁿ(推行); oi-léng(挨推).

**shovel**, pùn-táu(糞斗).

**show**, khṳt-nâng-thóiⁿ(乞人睇); hién-tshut lâi-pun-nâng-thóiⁿ(顯出來分人睇); pái pun-nâng-thóiⁿ(擺分人睇). *point out*, kí-tiám khṳt-nâng-thóiⁿ(己點乞人睇). *the way*, kí-lōu(指路); kí-tiãm chí-tiâu-lōu(指點此條路). *to show out*, hièn-tshut(現出); huat-hièn(發現); lòu-tshut(露出). *a fine show*, hó-pâi-tiêⁿ(好排場); phâi-chhiâng(排場); lāu-jie̍t(鬧熱). *showy*, siu-sek-ngiá(收色雅); huan-hûa(歡華); hàuⁿ-phâi-chhiâng(好排場); hàuⁿ-tsuang-tshái(好裝彩); hàuⁿ-tsuang-pàng(好裝放).

**shower**, che̍k-tsūn-hõu(一陣雨); che̍k-tīn-hõu(一陣雨); phû-huang-hõu(浮風雨). *of arrows*, chìⁿ zû-hõu-lia̍p(箭如雨粒).

**shreds**, *torn in*, li̍h kàu che̍k-tiâu che̍k-tiâu(裂到一條一條); uân-sui-saⁿ, pue-lêng-khòu(莞荽衫，菠薐褲).

**shrewd**, lêng-lāi(伶俐); kuai-khá(乖巧); kuai-khiáu(乖巧); tshong-mêng(聰明).

**shrimp**, hê(蝦). *very small dried*, hê-bí(蝦米).

**shrine**, sîn-kham(神龕); sîn-lâu(神龕); sîn-tû(神龕). *in the ancestral hall*, tōa-kham(大龕).

**shrink**, kiu-thò(龜退); kiu-ji̍p(勼入); kiu-sòi(勼細); kiu-bûa(勼埋); thò-phāng(退縫).

**shrivelled**, jiâu-jiâu(縐縐); niàuⁿ-niàuⁿ(鳥鳥).

**shroff**, tshâi-hù(財副); ke-tiéⁿ(家長). *to shroff dollars*, thóiⁿ-ngṳ̂n(睇銀). *(in foreign hong)*, bói-pan(買班).

**shroud**, sien-saⁿ(仙衫); sàng-lãu kâi i-ho̍k(送老个衣服); sien-i(仙衣).

**shrouds**, *the*, chiẽⁿ-ûi kâi-soh-thui(上圍个索梯).

**shrub**, chhiū-kiáⁿ(樹囝); ói-chhiū(矮樹).

**shudder**, kiaⁿ-khiū(驚硬); kiaⁿ-kàu-khiū(驚到硬). *with disgust*, phah-tshùn-lūn(拍寸蹂).

**shuffle**, *cards*, sói-pâi(洗排).

**shun**, pī(避); siám-pī(閃避); tô-pī(逃避); pī-khûi(避開); sie-pī(相避).

**shut**, *shut the door (without fastening)*, hõiⁿ-mn̂g(闔門). *shut the door (and fasten)*, kueⁿ-mn̂g(關門); mn̂g kueⁿ-tah(門關貼). *shut the door (to bolt)*, tshùaⁿ-mn̂g(閂門). *door half-shut*, mn̂g pùaⁿ-hâm-hõiⁿ(門半含闔); pùaⁿ-iám-hõiⁿ(半掩闔). *shut out*, bô-nâng-ji̍p(無人入); bô-thang pun-nâng-ji̍p(無通分人入). *a shop*, kueⁿ-phòu(關舖); hiah-seng-lí(歇生理). *the eyes*, ma̍k-chiu ha̍p-miⁿ(目睭合眠). *the mouth*, tshùi ha̍p-bûa(喙合埋). *the water-gates*, lo̍h-tsa̍h(落閘); tsa̍h-chheng-pang(閘清枋). *one up in prison*, kìm-kam(禁監); siu-kam(收監).

**shutter**, theng-mn̂g(窗門).

**shuttle**, so-kiáⁿ(梭囝); keⁿ-pòu-so(經布梭). *to fly the*, phau-so(梭囝).

**shuttle-cock**, ìⁿ(燕); ìn(印). *to play*, phah-ìⁿ(拍燕); tiāu-ìn(掉印); phah-ìn(拍印).

**shy**, ùi-siáu-lí(毋敢見人[訓]); m̄-káⁿ kìⁿ-nâng(毋敢見人); kiu-niuⁿ(勼扭); kiu-kiu niuⁿ-niuⁿ(勼勼扭扭).

**Siam**, Siām-lô(暹羅).

**sick**, ũ-pēⁿ(有病); nâng bõi(人袂); nâng m̄-hó(人毋好); m̄-phêng-an(毋平安); sin-thói m̄-uaⁿ(身體毋安); sin-thói m̄-hûa(身體毋和); khì-thói m̄-hûa(氣體毋和); kong-tãu bô-thang-hó(公道無通好). *(slightly)*, ien-siên〔〕. *sickness*, pēⁿ(病); pēⁿ-chèng(病症); mâuⁿ-pēⁿ(毛病); chi̍t-pēⁿ(疾病); chèng-hāu(症候); pēⁿ-thiàⁿ(病痛); pēⁿ-nńg(病軟); pēⁿ-khùn(病睏). *sea-sick*, hîn-tsûn(眩船). *sickly*, sin-hūn lám〔〕; sin-hūn jia̍k(身分弱); sin-hūn phàⁿ(身分冇). *squeamish*, àiⁿ-thòu(愛吐). *to be sick (vomit)*, thòu(吐).

**sickle**, liâm(鐮); kau-liâm(鉤鐮); kuah-tsháu-to(割草刀).

**side**, pôiⁿ(旁); piⁿ(邊); kîⁿ(墘); phâng-piⁿ(旁邊). *door*, phien-mn̂g(偏門). *the side of the body*, phiaⁿ-lî(𩩍籬); hia̍p-ẽ(脅下). *right*, iũ-pôiⁿ(右爿); chiàⁿ-chhiú-pôiⁿ(正手爿). *left*, tsó-pôiⁿ(左爿); tò-chhiú-pôiⁿ(倒手爿). *turn from side to side*, huan-lâi huan-khṳ̀(翻來翻去). *turn from side to side (tossing sleeplessly)*, huan-lâi khah-khṳ̀ put-sêng-mîn〔〕. *this*, chièⁿ-pôiⁿ(上爿); chièⁿ-thâu(此樣頭). *that*, hièⁿ-pôiⁿ(向爿); hièⁿ-thâu(向頭). *at one's*, tõ i sin-piⁿ(在伊身邊).

**sieve**, *a*, thai(篩); bí-thai(米篩); bí-lô(米籮). *(rather, a shallow tray for winnowing)*, pùa-ki(簸箕).

**sift**, *to*, thai(篩).

**sigh**, tháu-khùi(㪗氣); thàng-khì(通氣); thàng-sek(通色).

**sight**, *of the eyes*, ma̍k-la̍t(目力); ma̍k-si̍t(目實). *to have one's*, ma̍k-chiu kng(目睭光); ma̍k-chiu thóiⁿ-kìⁿ(目睭睇見). *lose one's*, sit-mêng(失明); chheⁿ-mêⁿ(青盲). *lose sight of*, m̄-kìⁿ(毋見). *at first*, tsho-kìⁿ(初見); tsho-ē-kìⁿ(初下見). *know by*, pùaⁿ-mīn siang-sek(半面相色); sek-mīn(色面). *near*, kṳ̃n-sĩ(近視). *dim*, ma̍k-chiu hue(目睭花).

**sign**, hō(號); jī-hō(字號); kì-hō(記號); ìn-hō(印號); kì-tiãu(記條). *a secret sign*, àm-ieh(暗約); àm-hō(暗號). *to make such*, phah-àm-hō(打暗號). *in heaven*, thien-siãng(天象); thien-tiãu(天兆). *signs of the Zodiac*, tsa̍p-jī-keng(十二經). *sign-board*, chie-pâi(招牌); phòu-hō(舖號).

**sign**, *to*, *a paper*, chhiam-miâⁿ(簽名); tsham-miâⁿ(簽名); ūe-ap(畫押); ūe-hō(畫號).

**signal**, *flag*, kî-hō(旗號). *gun*, pàng-phàu ûi-hō(放砲爲號). *hoist a*, liū-kî(㨨旗).

**signature**, miâⁿ(名); hue-ap(花押).

**signet**, ìn(應).

**signify**, *it does not*, bô-kai-tsài(無該載); bô-kàu tî-kò-khṳ̀(無到底塊去); bô-siang-kan(無相干); bô-chhiet-iàu(無切要); bô-bī(無味). *signification*, ì-sṳ̀(意思); jī-ngĩ(字義); jī-ì(字意); ì-ngĩ(意義); sueh(刷).

**silent**, tiām-tiām(恬恬); tiām-chẽⁿ(恬靜); m̃-khui-tshùi(毋開喙); bô-tshut-siaⁿ(無出聲); mi̍t-mi̍t bô-ngân(密密無言).

**silk**, si-tiû lîn-tn̄g(絲綢綾緞). *thread*, si-sùaⁿ(絲線). *shop*, tiû-tn̄g-phòu(綢緞舖).

**silk-worm**, tshôiⁿ(蠶). *cocoon*, tshôiⁿ-kóiⁿ(蠶繭). *to rear*, chhī-tshôiⁿ(飼蠶); iáng-tshôiⁿ(養蠶). *larvoe of*, tshôiⁿ-jîn(蠶人). *silk-worm moth*, tshôiⁿ-ngô(蠶蛾).

**silly**, chhi-ko(痴哥); chhi-chhi ngâi-ngâi(痴痴呆呆).

**silver**, ngṳ̂n(銀). *silver-smith*, phah-ngṳ̂n sai-pẽ(拍銀司阜). *shop*, siu-sek-phòu(收色舖). *pure*, tsok-siâⁿ-ngṳ̂n(足成銀). *with two parts of alloy*, poih-siâⁿ-ngṳ̂n(八成銀). *fragments of*, ngṳ̂n-tshùi(銀碎). *ingots*, see INGOT.

**similar**, *húang-sṳ̃; siang-sṳ̃; chhin-chhiẽⁿ; tãi-tâng*, siáu-ĩ(小意); húang-hut(恍惚).

**simmer**, *as water*, tshang〔〕.

**simple**, láu-si̍t(老實); bô-ngũi(無偽); tong-ti̍t(忠直); phok-si̍t(樸實); phok-sù(樸素); tshún-ti̍t(蠢直); bô-hue-jī(無花字). *simpleton*, ngà-nâng(㦙人).

**simultaneous**, tâng-sî(同時); tsò-che̍k-ē(做蜀下).

**sin**, tsũe(罪); tsũe-ak(罪惡); tsũe-kùe(罪過). *to sin*, hũam-tsũe(犯罪); tit-tsũe(得罪).

**since**, *when*, tâng tiâng-sî(同當時). *olden times*, tâng-kóu-tsá kàu-chí-kò lâi(同自古到只塊來); tsṳ̃-tsá íⁿ-lâi(自早以來); tshông-kóu íⁿ-lâi(自古以來). *since it is so*, kì-sĩ chièⁿ-seⁿ(記是上生); kì-jiên sĩ chièⁿ-seⁿ(記然是上生).

**sincere**, sêng-si̍t(誠實); si̍t-sim si̍t-ì(實心實意); chin-sim chin-ì(真心真意); sêng-ì(實意); sêng-sim sêng-ì(誠心誠意).

**sinecure**, khang-hâm(空銜); chia̍h-kan-hóng(食乾俸).

**sinew**, kṳn(筋). *contraction of the sinews*, thiu-kha-kṳn(抽骹筋).

**sing**, ngîm-si(吟詩); chhiàng-ko(唱歌); ko-chhiàng(歌唱); chhiè-khek(唱曲); sõng-si(訟司). *street-singer*, tsáu-chhiàng(走唱).

**Singapore**, Si̍t-la̍t(實力); Sin-kia-po(新加坡).

**singe**, sie--tie̍h(燒着); húe sie(火燒). *as food, sticking to pot*, tie̍h-sie(着燒). *as hair*, húe sie(火燒); chhih-tie̍h(彳着); lua̍h-tie̍h(辣着).

**single**, toaⁿ(端); che̍k(一). *singly*, it-it(一一); che̍k-nâng che̍k-nâng(一人一人); ta̍k-it(逐一). *one fold*, toaⁿ-têng(單重).

**singular**, see **strange**.

**sink**, tîm(沉); tîm-lo̍h(沉落). *in water*, tîm-tsúi(沉水). *in vice*, tîm-ne̍k tõ-ak(沉肉在惡). see **sunk**.

**sip**, lim(啉); tshueh(啜).

**Sir**, tsun-kè(尊架); lãu-tia(老爹); láu-tsṳ́(老子); lãu-nâng-ke(老人家); sin-seⁿ(先生); siàng-kong(相公).

**sister**, ché-mūeⁿ(姐妹); chí-mūeⁿ(姐妹). *elder*, a-ché(阿姐). *younger*, a-mūeⁿ(阿妹). *sister-in-law*, *sister-in-law (wife of older brother)*, a-só(阿嫂). *sister-in-law (wife of younger brother)*, sié-ḿ(小姆); tĩ-hũ(弟婦). *wife's sister*, chhi-î(妻姨). *mother's*, bó-î(母姨). *husband's* a-kou(阿姑).

**sit**, *to*, tsõ(坐). *on horseback*, khiâ-bé(騎馬). *cross-legged*, phûan-khí-kha tsõ(盤起骹坐). *please sit down*, chhiáⁿ-tsõ(請坐). *on one's knee*, tsõ tõ i-kâi-kha--thâu(坐在伊个骹頭).

**situation**, tī-ūi(地位); cheh-hūn(職分); cheh-jĩm(職任).

**six**, la̍k(六). *hexagonal*, la̍k-kak(六角).

**skate**, *fish*, hang-hṳ̂(烘魚).

**sketch**, *to*, ūe(畫); ūe-kó(畫稿); ngóu-pit(五筆); phah-kó(拍稿). *(writing)*, phah-tshó(拍草).

**skewer**, sie-ne̍k-tshuàn(燒肉串).

**skill**, chhiú-gōi(手藝); chhiú-tūan(手斷); ki-khá(機巧); khá-gōi(巧藝); hó-chhiú-gōi(好手藝). *skilled*, keng-liēn(經練); se̍k-chhiú(熟手); cheng-kong(精工); cheng-khá(精巧); kong-khá(工巧); miâⁿ-ke(名家); gâu(賢); õi(會); tsò-kang kui-lōu(做工規路). *in managing*, õi-siẽⁿ sim-sṳ̄(會想心事).

**skim**, liê(撈); liê-tiāu(撈掉); liê-khí(撈起). *froth*, liê-phue̍h〔〕. *skimmer*, tâng-sî(銅匙); tâng-sie̍h(銅勺).

**skin**, phûe(皮); phûe-hu(皮膚). *to*, pak-tiāu-phûe(剝掉皮). *skin & bone*, nâng-póu(人脯); têng-phûe nêⁿ-têng-kut(重皮軟重骨). *disease*, phûe-hu-pēⁿ(皮膚病).

**skip**, thiàu(跳). *over*, thiàu-kùe(跳過). *about*, tshok-tshok-thiàu(促促跳).

**skull**, thâu-khak-úaⁿ(頭殼碗); thâu-náuⁿ-kut(頭腦骨).

**slab**, chie̍h-póiⁿ(石板); chie̍h-pi(石碑).

**slack**, sang(鬆); lēng(冗). *slacken*, pàng-sang(放鬆); pàng-lēng(放冗). *slackwater*, pêⁿ-lâu(平流); lâu tńg(流轉).

**slake**, *lime*, huat-hue(發灰); huaat-hue-pôu(發灰舖). *thirst*, kói-khuah(解渴); chí-âu(止喉).

**slam**, *a door*, khãm-tie̍h-mn̂g(鈸着門); mn̂g piãng--chē-kiè(門便砦叫).

**slander**, húiⁿ-pãng(誹謗); pù-lũ〔〕; tsàm-tsǹg(譖鑽). *(widely)*, iâu-pãng(謠謗).

**slang**, koi-chhĩ-ūe(街市話); chhĩ-chéⁿ-ūe(市井話).

**slanting**, tshúa(歪); uai(歪); siâ(斜); khi(崎); phien(偏).

**slap**, *on the cheek*, phah-tshùi-póiⁿ(拍喙板); piang-kih-kau(邊頰交); òng kih-kau-tsô(盎頰交槽). *on shoulder*, tah-koiⁿ-thâu(搭間頭).

**slate**, chie̍h-póiⁿ(石板); chie̍h-hiã(石瓦). *(for writing)*, hún-pâi-chie̍h(粉排石).

**slattern**, *lah-tah tsṳ-niêⁿ; thâu-môⁿ zû-sàu-soi*, kha-tîⁿ pũaⁿ-sí-koi(骹纏拂死雞).

**slaughter**, suah-lo̍k(殺戮); tu-lo̍k ke-nâng(豬戮家人). *an ox*, thâi-gû(刣牛).

**slave**, nôuⁿ(奴); nôuⁿ-po̍k(奴僕); po̍k-jîn(僕人); nôuⁿ-tshâi(奴才); ke-po̍k(家僕). *female*, tsáu-kúi(走鬼); nńg-pĩ(女婢); nôuⁿ-pĩ(奴婢). *slaves, male and female*, po̍k-pĩ(僕婢).

**sledge**, *for mud*, thôu-thiàu(塗跳). *to ride on*, thek-thiàu(踢跳). *for ice*, thua-kiē(拖轎). *sledge-hammer*, tōa-thih-thûi(大鐵槌).

**sleek**, kng-kng(光光); kuang-che̍k(光澤); môⁿ-tsháu kuang-che̍k(毛草光一); môⁿ-tsháu kuang-iām(毛草光焰); kng-ku̍t(光滑); ku̍t-che̍k(滑盡).

**sleep**, gu̍t(夗); u̍t(夗). *with one*, tsò-pû-gūt(做包夗). *sleepless*, bõi-gu̍t(袂夗). *(from drinking tea)*, chhéⁿ-pî(醒脾). *sleepy*, phî-phî(疲疲); ma̍k siap(目澀); ma̍k-chiu siap(目睭澀); àiⁿ-gu̍t(愛夗). *foot sleeping*, kha pì-pì(骹痹痹); kha ngûi-ngûi(骹危危).

**sleet**, lo̍h-sng-soh(落霜雪); lo̍h-pha̍k(落雹).

**sleeve**, *of coat*, saⁿ-ńg(衫䘼); siù-kháu(袖口); ńg-kháu(腕口).

**sleight**, *of hand*, tsò-pa-hì(做爸戲).

**slender**, iùⁿ-sòi(幼細); sòu-jia̍k(瘦弱); sán-sòu(㾪瘦). *waist*, ie sòi(腰細); in-iang-ie〔〕.

**slice**, che̍k-phièn(一片); che̍k-liàm(一捻). *to*, tso̍ih-chiâⁿ-phièn(截成片).

**slide**, *down*, liù-lo̍h(溜落). see SLIP.

**slight**, khin(輕); po̍h(薄); sòi(細); chhién(淺). *to*, thóiⁿ-khin(睇輕); thóiⁿ-m̄-chiẽⁿ-ma̍k(睇毋上目); po̍h-thãi(薄待); hut-lia̍k(忽略).

**slime**, thôu-nîⁿ(泥濘); thôu-mûe-chièⁿ(塗糜醬); siêⁿ(常); sûaⁿ(腺). *of snails*, lô-sûaⁿ(羅腺). *pass slimy matter from the bowels*, pàng-sûaⁿ(放腺).

**sling**, *a*, huat-chie̍h kâi-soh(發結个索). *to, the arm*, tiàu-chhiú(弔手).

**slip**, liù-kha(溜骹); sit-kha(失骹); sit-tsok(失作); thām-phiù-kha. *(on an incline)*, liù-pua̍h(溜跋). *(on level slippery surface)*, liū-pua̍h(溜跋). *out of the hand*, sit-chhiú(失手); phiù-chhiú(失手). *away*, thut-tsáu(脫走); thau-tsáu(逃走). *slips*, phièn(騙). *slips (bamboo)*, tek-chhiam(竹籤). *slips (paper)*, tsúa-tiâu(紙條). *slips of plants*, chhiū-tsai(樹栽); hue-tsai(花栽). *slip of the tongue*, sit-ngân(失言); sit-kháu(失口); kháu-kùe(口過); tàⁿ-tāⁿ(呾呾).

**slippers**, ôi-thua(鞋拖); ôi-liauh(鞋屢); piẽn-ôi(便鞋). *(all without heels)*, ìⁿ-búe-ôi(燕尾鞋).

**slippery**, liù-liù-ku̍t(溜溜滑); liū-liū-ku̍t(溜溜滑); ku̍t(滑).

**slit**, le̍h(曆); li̍h(裂).

**slope**, siâ(斜). *gentle*, suaⁿ-pou(山坡); pho-lo-sia(陂咯斜).

**slothful**, tõaⁿ(惰); lán-tõaⁿ(懶惰); hãi-tãi(懈怠); phî-tõaⁿ(疲惰); hàuⁿ-tõaⁿ(好惰); tham-tõaⁿ(貪惰).

**slovenly**, lah-tah(邋遢); láng-tháng(郎當). see **slothful**.

**slow**, mān(慢); chhî(遲). *of speech*, tshùi tun(喙鈍); tshùi-chi̍h tun(喙舌鈍). *slowly*, khuaⁿ-khuaⁿ(寬寬); ûn-ûn(勻勻); mān-mān(慢慢).

**sluice**, tsúi-tsa̍h(水閘); tsúi-chhēng(水拴).

**slur**, *over*, chhìn-tshái-tsò(凊彩做); tsò-sṳ̄ ló-ló tshó-tshó(做事潦潦草草); sûi-sûi piẽn-piẽn(隨隨便便); huh-huh tshuah-tshuah〔〕.

**smack**, *of the lips*, tap-kháu-sianh(答口笙).

**small**, sòi(細); siáu(小); iùⁿ(幼); mûiⁿ(微). *quantity*, chié(少); tiám-kiáⁿ(點囝); sut-kiáⁿ(屑囝); lân-ló(零些); se-su(些須); si-si(絲絲); su-su(須須); se-se(些些). *rain*, hõu-kiáⁿ mûiⁿ-mûiⁿ(雨囝微微).

**small-pox**, tshut-tsu(出珠); gâu-a-niêⁿ(賢阿娘); sún-tsái〔〕; thien-hue(天花). see **pox**.

**smart**, lêng-lāi(伶俐); kha-chhiú õi(骹手能); kha-chhiú khin-khùe kiau-kiah(骹手輕快矯捷).

**smart**, *to*, tshǹg-thiàⁿ(刺痛). *cause to, as the eyes*, soh--tie̍h(束着).

**smash**, phùa-tshùi(破碎); khà-phùa tshùi-tshùi(扣破碎碎).

**smattering**, chhién-ha̍k(淺學); ēng-kang m̄-kàu(用工毋夠).

**smear**, kôu(糊); kôu-buah(糊抹).

**smell**, *a*, bī(味). *pleasant*, phang-bī(香味). *offensive*, tshàu-bī(臭味); ha-bī(哈味). *sour*, sng-bī(酸味). *to*, phīⁿ-tie̍h(鼻着). *do not*, phīⁿ-m̄-tie̍h(鼻毋着). *of liquor*, chiú-bī(酒味).

**smelt**, *to*, tsù(鑄). *iron ore*, khan-kóiⁿ(牽揀); khan-lôu(牽爐).

**smile**, chhiè(笑); mûiⁿ-chhiè(貓呅笑); ba-bun-chhiè(貓呅笑).

**smith**, *black-*, phah-thih sai-pẽ(拍鐵司阜). *silver-*, phah-ngṳ̂n sai-pẽ(拍銀司阜). *smithy*, phah-thih-tiàm(拍鐵店); phah-thih-phòu(拍鐵舖).

**smoke**, in(煙); húe-in(火煙); hun(薰); húe-hun(火薰). *to smoke tobacco*, chia̍h-hun(食薰); chia̍h-se̍k-hun(食熟薰); kuh-hun(嗝薰). *opium*, chia̍h-a-phièn(食鴉片); chia̍h a-phièn-hun(食鴉片薰). *mosquitoes*, hun-máng(薰蠓).

**smooth**, ku̍t(滑); kng(光); pêⁿ(平). *smoothing iron*, ut-táu(熨斗). *smooth-tongued*, tshùi ku̍t-ku̍t(喙滑滑).

**smother**, hìm-miⁿ(禁眠); hìm-sí(禁死); hip-sí(翕死).

**smutty**, hun-ou(薰烏); mak--tie̍h húe-thûn(衊着火燂).

**snail**, lô(螺); tshân-lô(田螺).

**snake**, tsûa(蛇). *one*, che̍k-tiâu-tsûa(一條蛇).

**snarl**, *as dog*, chhèng-phīn(衝鼻); hm̄-hm̄-kiè(嗯嗯叫). *as man*, ngâu-ngâu-kiè(熬熬叫).

**snatch**, chhiéⁿ(搶); chhiéⁿ-to̍h(搶奪); chhiéⁿ-kùe-chhiú(搶過手).

**snow**, soh(雪). *to*, lo̍h-soh(落雪). *snow-white*, soh-soh-pe̍h(雪雪白).

**so**, chièⁿ-seⁿ(此樣生); àn-chièⁿ-seⁿ(按上生). *so much*, chièⁿ-tsōi(此樣㩼). *Mr so-and-so*, móng-nâng(某人).

**soak**, chìm(浸); chìm-tsúi(浸水); tsṳ̀(漬); sò(疏). *thoroughly soaked*, chìm-thàng(浸通); chìm-ji̍p-tī(浸入地); tsn̂g-kâi tsṳ̀--kùe〔〕; tsṳ̀-thàng(漬通).

**soap**, piáⁿ-ie̍h(餅藥); huân-káng(環港); hiang-khou(香箍); phang-khou(芳箍); tê-chí-khou(茶枳箍). *(foreign)*, huan-piáⁿ-ie̍h(番餅藥). *soap-stone*, tàng-chie̍h(凍石).

**soar**, pue-kûiⁿ(飛懸).

**sob**, tshoih〔〕; khàu-tshoih(哭嘈); thî-tshoih(啼嘈); pui-tshoih〔〕. *incessantly*, khàu-m̃-chẽⁿ(哭毋靜).

**sober**, tsat-ēng(節用); liâm-tsat(廉節); tsat-tōu(節度). *to become sober*, chiú chhéⁿ(酒醒).

**sociable**, sóng-khùai(爽快); õi-kau-tshap-nâng(會交插人). *social relations*, ngóu-lûn(五倫).

**society**, *a*, hũe(會). *to enter*, ji̍p-hũe(入會); pài-hũe(拜會); kat-hũe(結會). *a literary, to form*, kat-siã(結社). *to enter*, pài-siã(拜社); ji̍p-siã(入社).

**sod**, tsháu-phue̍h(草𠱀).

**sofa**, mîn-íⁿ(棉椅); khàng-íⁿ(空椅); khàng-tshn̂g(炕床).

**soil**, thôu(土); thôu-tī(塗地); thôu-ne̍k(塗肉); thôu-nîⁿ(塗泥); thôu-phûe(塗皮). *good*, pûi-thôu(肥塗); pûi-jiâu kâi-tī(肥饒个地). *poor*, sán-thôu(㾪塗); sán-tī(㾪地).

**solder**, ún(焊); ún-siah(焊錫); ún-tùe(焊綴); hūaⁿ-tùe(焊綴); tâng-hūaⁿ(同焊).

**sole**, *of foot*, kha-tói(骹底). *of shoe*, ôi-tói(鞋底). *to sole a shoe*, tah-ôi-tói(搭鞋底).

**solemn**, ngiâm-sok(嚴肅); ui-ngiâm(威嚴).

**solicit**, chhiáⁿ(請); khiû(求); thó(討); koh-lô(閣羅). *solicitous*, khùa-sim(掛心); khùa-lṳ̃(掛慮); khùa-liãm(掛念).

**solid**, si̍t(實); tōiⁿ(𠕇); tsa̍t-thâu(實頭) *(opp. of khang-khak, hollow)*; ún-tǹg(穩當).

**soliloquy**, ka-kī-tàⁿ ka-kī-hûe(家己呾家己回); tsṳ̃-ngân tsṳ̃-gṳ́(自言自語).

**solitary**, to̍k(獨); kou-to̍k(孤獨); kou-chiau(孤巢); sok-mo̍k(肅穆); kou-sok(孤寂); bô-phũaⁿ(無伴); to̍k-kṳ(獨居); to̍k-tshú(獨處); sok-chẽⁿ(寂靜); sok-liâu(寂寞).

**solstice**, *summer*, hē-chì(夏至). *winter*, tang-chì(冬至).

**soluble**, õi-iêⁿ(會烊); õi-siau-iêⁿ(會消烊).

**solve**, kói(解). *a riddle*, tshai-mĩⁿ(猜謎).

**some**, kúi-kâi(幾個); kúi-ūa-kâi(幾外個); sù-kâi(須個); ũ-nâng(有人); ũ-kâi(有个); tsōi-chié(濟少); ke-kiám(加減). *somebody*, ũ-nâng; móng-nâng(某人). *sometimes*, ũ-sî(有時); ũ-tiâng-sî(有誰時). *somewhat*, kúi-siâⁿ(幾成); kúi-hun(幾分). *something*, che̍k-kiãⁿ-mue̍h(一件物).

**somersault**, *to turn a*, pha-sa-lin(拋沙輪); pha-lìn-táu(拋輾斗); iauh-lìn-táu(腰輾斗); iauh bô-kṳn-táu(腰無近斗).

**son**, kiáⁿ(囝); tau-kiáⁿ(兜囝); ta-pou-kiáⁿ(丈夫囝). *your*, kong-nâng(公人); lẽng-nn̂g(令郎). *my*, siáu-jî-kiáⁿ(小兒囝); siáu-khién(小犬); siáu-thûn(小豚). *eldest*, tōa-tau-kiáⁿ(大兜囝). *daughter's*, gūa-sun(外孫). *son-in-law*, kiáⁿ-sài(囝婿). *emperor's son-in-law*, hũ-bé(父馬). *to receive a son-in-law into one's own family*, iáng-láu-sài(養老婿).

**song**, khek(曲); kua(歌); si(詩); ko(歌). *one*, che̍k-tiâu-khek(一條曲). *book*, khek-chheh(曲冊). *to si(詩)ng a*, chhiè-khek(唱曲); chhiàng-khek(唱曲); chhiè-kua(唱歌); ngîm-si(吟詩).

**soon**, tsá(早); bô-kú(無久). *sooner ripe*, soiⁿ-se̍k(先熟). *sooner than you*, soiⁿ-lṳ́(先汝); soiⁿ-kùe-lṳ́(先過汝). *sooner...than*, see RATHER.

**soot**, húe-thûn(火燂); húe-thûn-êng(火燂煙).

**soporific**, mîⁿ-ie̍h(棉藥); uaⁿ-sũi-ie̍h(安睡藥); uaⁿ-mîn-ie̍h(安眠藥).

**sorcery**, bû-su̍t(巫術); siâ-su̍t(邪術); iau-su̍t(妖術); iau-huap kùai-su̍t(妖法怪術); huap-su̍t(法術); su̍t-siàu(術數). *sorcerer*, ēng-bû-su̍t(用巫術); tsò-bû-su̍t(做巫術); su̍t-sṳ̃(術士); thóiⁿ-siàⁿ(睇邪). *sorceress*, lo̍h-sîn-phûa(落神婆); thóiⁿ-siàⁿ-phûa(睇聖婆).

**sore**, thiàⁿ(痛). *a*, tshng(瘡); tshng-tshùi(瘡碎); mîⁿ-tshng(棉瘡). *leg*, kha mîⁿ(骹糜).

**sorrow**, hûan-ló(煩惱); iu-būn(憂悶); tshôu-sim(愁心); tshôu-būn(愁悶); pui-tshôu(悲愁); iu-ut(憂鬱); pui-ut(悲鬱); ut-at(鬱抑); hûan-sim(煩心).

**sort**, téng(等); hãng(項); lūi(類); iēⁿ(樣); hō(號); sek(式); khí(起); khúan(款). *all sorts*, kak-sek(各色); kak-hãng(各項); kak-iēⁿ(各樣); peh-iēⁿ(百樣). *this sort*, chí-khí(此起); chí-che̍k-khí(此一起).

**soul**, lêng-hûn(靈魂).

**sound**, siaⁿ(聲); siaⁿ-im(聲音); kiè(叫). *to*, õi-hiáng(會響). *a drum*, phah-kóu(拍古). *of music*, gau̍h-im(樂音). *of knocking (every sound has its own proper designation in this form)*, khok-khok-kiè(柝柝叫).

**sound**, *doctrine*, chiàⁿ-kà(正教); chiàⁿ-lí(正理); chiàⁿ-tãu(正道); chiàⁿ-lōu(正路). *sound asleep*, gu̍t kàu-tsùi-tsãi(夗到醉在); tōa-gu̍t(大夗).

**sound**, *to*, *as water*, thàm-tsúi(探水). *a person*, chhì-thàm(試探); thàm-mn̄g(探問); kui-thàm(規探).

**soup**, thng(湯).

**sour**, sng(酸). *smell*, sng-khì(酸氣); sng-bī(酸味). *soured and spoiled*, tshàu-sng(臭酸); tshàu-sng-khùi(臭酸氣). *belch*, áu-sng-tsúi(嘔酸水). *looks*, húan-ma̍k(反目).

**south**, lâm(南); nâm(南); lâm-pôiⁿ(南爿). *S.E.*, tang-lâm(東南). *looking to the south*, niàⁿ-lâm(領南); hiàng-lâm(向南); tsõ-pak hiàng-lâm(坐北向南).

**souvenir**, piáu-kì(表記).

**sow**, *a*, tṳ-bó(豬母).

**space**, tī-hng(地方). *vacant*, khang-tī(空地); khang-ūi(空位). *large open*, khùaⁿ-tiêⁿ(寬場); khùang-tiâⁿ(寬埕). *in the space of one hour*, che̍k-tiám-cheng tsṳ-kan(一點鐘之間). *leave a*, làng(漏); làng-khang(漏空).

**spacious**, khuah(闊); khuah-khǹg(闊曠); khùaⁿ(寬); khuan-khuah(寬闊); khùaⁿ-chhēng〔〕.

**spade**, thih-chhiâng(鐵鍁); phûe-chhiâng〔〕.

**Spain**, Tōa-Lṳ̃-sòng kok(大呂宋國). *Spanish-fly*, see CANTHARIDES.

**span**, *a*, che̍k-lia̍h(一掠).

**spare**, niēⁿ(讓); sù(些). *not spare oneself*, put-sieh lâu-khóu(不惜勞苦); bô-liẽn-sieh ka-kī(無憐惜家己); m̄-káⁿ khùaⁿ-ua̍h(毋敢寬闊). *can spare some*, ũ-tshûn(有剩); ũ-ṳ̂(有餘). *ground*, khang-tī(空地); ṳ̂-tī(餘地); khiah-tī(隙地); ôiⁿ-tī(閒地).

**sparing**, khiãm(儉); sieh-ēng(惜用); sieh-mu̍eh(惜物); séⁿ-hùi(省費); séⁿ-khiãm(省儉); tsat-séⁿ(節省).

**spark**, húe-mêⁿ(火明). *sparkling*, ia̍p-ia̍p-sih(灼灼熠).

**sparrow**, mûaⁿ-chiah(麻雀); mûaⁿ-chiah-chiáu(麻雀鳥). *sparrow-hawk*, liáu-eng-pô(鷂鷹婆).

**spasm**, thiu-kṳn(抽筋); thiu-thek(抽搐).

**spatter**, phuah(潑). *as with mud*, phùn--tie̍h nah-sap(噴着垃圾).

**spatula**, khui-ie̍h-to(開藥刀); thih-poi(鐵杓); kueh-to(割刀).

**spawn**, *of fish*, hṳ̂-tshun(魚春); hṳ̂-nñg(魚卵).

**speak**, tàⁿ-ūe(呾話); káng(講); sueh-ūe(說話). *for one*, thòi-nâng káng-chhêng(代人講情). *I wish to speak a few words with you*, uá àiⁿ kāng-lṳ́-tàⁿ lân-kù-ūe(我愛共汝呾零故話). *don't speak to him*, màiⁿ-tshap i tàⁿ-ūe(勿插伊呾話). *speak plainly*, tàⁿ-mêng(呾明); tàⁿ-mêng-pe̍h(呾明白); ti̍t-tàⁿ(直呾). *at random*, thèng-tàⁿ(聽呾); thèng-tsãu-hùe tàⁿ(聽造化呾); zuãn-tàⁿ(任呾).

**spear**, chhieⁿ(槍). *to spear*, tshǹg(闖).

**special**, te̍k(特); tsuan(專).

**species**, chéng(種); lūi(類). *of the same*, tâng-lūi(同類).

**specify**, ta̍k-it káng-mêng(逐一講明); kiãⁿ-kiãⁿ kì-mêng(件件記明).

**specimen**, khuán-sek(款式); thói-sek(體式); keh-sek(格式); mōⁿ(模); iēⁿ(樣).

**specious**, *tshah-chhih chhin-chhiẽⁿ; chhin-chhiẽⁿ-sĩ*, huân-liáu m̄-sĩ(還了毋是).

**speck**, ou-tiám(烏點). *speckled*, hue-long(花瓏); che̍k-tiám che̍k-tiám(一點一點).

**spectacles**, ma̍k-kiàⁿ(目鏡). *eyes of*, ma̍k-kiàⁿ-jîn(目鏡人); ma̍k-kiàⁿ-ne̍k(目鏡肉). *to put on, or wear*, kùa-ma̍k-kiàⁿ(掛目鏡).

**spectator**, phâng-piⁿ-thóiⁿ kâi-nâng(傍邊睇个人); phâng-kuan--kâi-nâng(旁觀个人); chhin-ma̍k thóiⁿ--kìⁿ(親目睇見).

**speculate**, kòi-sǹg(計算). *a good speculation*, hó-siẽⁿ-thâu(好想頭).

**speech**, ūe(話); tàⁿ-ūe(呾話). *fluent*, tàⁿ-ūe liù-liù-ku̍t(呾話). *speechless*, bô-ūe hó-tàⁿ(無話好呾).

**speed**, khùe(快); méⁿ(猛).

**spell**, *a*, hû. hû-chiù(符。符咒); chiù-gṳ́(咒語). *to utter*, liām-chiù(念咒).

**spell**, *to*, chhiet-im(切音); húan-chhiet(反切).

**spend**, sái-chîⁿ(使錢); sái-ēng(使用); só-hùi(所費). *time idly*, siau-ôiⁿ kùe-ji̍t(消閒過日). *a night*, hiah-mêⁿ(歇夜); keh-mêⁿ(隔夜); kùe-mêⁿ(過夜).

**sphere**, îⁿ-thói(圓體); kiû(球).

**spices**, hieⁿ-liāu(香料).

**spider**, ti-tu(蜘蛛); bé-lêng-khiâ(馬龍騎); siàu-chîⁿ-ang〔〕; hôu-sîn-hóuⁿ(胡蠅虎); lâ-giâ(蟧蜈). *web*, ti-tu-si(蜘蛛絲); ti-tu-mãng(蜘蛛網).

**spill**, e̍k--tshut-lâi(溢出來); e̍k--tie̍h(拍倒); phah-tó(拍倒); kài-tiāu(拍倒); múaⁿ--tshut-lâi(滿出來); iah--tshut-lâi(溢出來).

**spin**, pháng-se(紡紗); cheh-tsòi(績碎). *spindle*, se-tsam(紗針). *spinning-wheel*, pháng-chhia(紡車).

**spin**, *to cause to (with the fingers)*, soh-hui(索飛). *to cause to (with string or whip)*, phah-hui(拍飛). *a top*, phah hâm-lâm-su̍t(拍銜瓏術).

**spinach**, pue-lêng-tshài(菠棱菜).

**spine**, ie-lêng-kut(腰龍骨); ie-chiah-kut(腰脊骨). *end of*, búe-lêng-kut(腰脊骨).

**spines**, *of porcupine*, hô-tṳ-chhì(荷豬刺).

**spirit**, sîn(神); sîn-lêng(神靈); sîn-hûn(神魂). *evil spirits*, siâ-sîn(邪神); siâ-môⁿ(邪毛); môⁿ-kúi(魔鬼). *to have no spirit, feel dull*, bô-cheng-sîn(無精神). *to get into the spirit of a thing*, huat-hèng(發興); hèng-hèng(興興); hèng-ì(興意). *spiritual*, lêng(靈).

**spit**, *to*, phùi(啐); phùi-nũaⁿ(呸涎). *blood*, phùi-hueh(呸血); phùi-âng(呸紅). *phlegm*, phùi-thâm(呸痰). *spittle*, nũaⁿ(涎); tshùi-nũaⁿ(喙涎). *spittoon*, thâm-a̍p(痰盒); thâm-tãng(痰筒); thâm-kùan(痰罐).

**spit**, *a*, húe-chhe(火叉); thih-chhe(鐵叉).

**spite**, uàn-hṳ̃n(怨恨).

**splash**, *water*, phùn-tsúi(噴水).

**spleen**, *the*, pî(脾). *enlarged*, pî tōa(脾大).

**splendour**, iông-hûa(榮華). *splendid*, kuang-mêng(光明); phâi-chhiâng(排場).

**splice**, sie-tàu(相鬥); tàu-chiap(鬥接); chiap(接).

**splinter**, tshâ-liàm(柴捻); tshâ-phièn(柴片); tshuaⁿ(閂). *to get a splinter into one's foot*, kha chhiah--tie̍h tshuaⁿ(骹刺着刺).

**splints**, *to put on*, ēng po̍h-sam lâi-kah(用薄衫來甲); ēng-sam-phûe lâi-ah(用杉皮來鴨).

**split**, phùa(破); phùa-khui(破開); lòi(𠠍); lòi-phùa(𠠍破). *to split the difference*, tùi-á(對拗); tùi-pùaⁿ-á(對半掗); jī-ke tshuang-tsua̍k(二家穿濁).

**spoil**, tak-nn̄g〔〕; mu̍eh-tiāu(物掉). *children*, ne̍k-ài(溺愛); seng-kong〔〕; iang-o〔〕. *spoiled, as things*, bô-ēng(無用); hāi--khṳ̀〔〕; khie̍h-tiāu(挈掉). *as eatables*, huán-bī(反味).

**spokes**, *of wheel*, chhia-lûn-tsam(車輪針); chhia-lûn-thek(車輪踢).

**sponge**, hái-zông(海茸).

**spontaneous**, tsṳ̃-seⁿ(自生); pe̍h-huat(白發). *confession*, tsṳ̃-jīn-tshò(自認錯).

**spool**, thĩ-khak(痔殼); hẽ-thĩ(下痔).

**spoon**, sî(匙); thng-sî(湯匙); thiâu-keⁿ(調羹). *lift with a*, ié(舀).

**sport**, sńg(耍); sie-sńg(相耍); thit-thô(佚佗); sie-pa-lói(相巴禮).

**spot**, tiám(點). *indelible, on the body*, ou-kì(烏記). *spotless*, bô-tiám(無點); bô-hiâ(無瑕). *spotted*, poiⁿ-tiám(斑點); hue-tiám(花點); seⁿ-tiám(生點); hue-long(花瓏); ũ-ìn-chiah(有印跡).

**spout**, *for water*, tsúi-tsô(水槽); tsúi-tâng(水筒). *as of teapot*, tê-kùan-sui(茶罐蓑); tê-kùan-tshùi(茶罐喙).

**sprain**, túi--tie̍h(挽着); chek--tie̍h(崱着); nãuⁿ--tie̍h(惱着); uái--tie̍h(歪着); tsua̍h--tie̍h(蚻着).

**spread**, pái-khui(排開); phi-khui(披開); tieⁿ-khui(張開); hien-khui(軒開); tién-khui(展開); phou(鋪). *news*, thuân-siaⁿ(傳聲); hong-siaⁿ(風聲); kià-siaⁿ(寄聲); pùa-iâng(播揚). *a mat*, tshṳ-tsháu-chhie̍h(舒草蓆); phi-tsháu-chhie̍h(披草蓆).

**sprightly**, ua̍h-tõng(活動); lêng-lāi(伶俐); ua̍h-phuah(活潑).

**spring**, tshun(春); tshun--thiⁿ(春天).

**spring**, *to*, *as tiger*, thiàu(跳); tà(踏). *up, as plant*, huat(發); seⁿ(生).

**spring**, *a*, tsûaⁿ(泉); tsúi-tsûaⁿ(水泉); tsúi-ngûan(水源); ngûan-thâu(源頭). *of a watch*, huap-tiâu(法條); thih-bé(鐵馬).

**sprinkle**, *water*, phùn-tsúi(噴水); hìⁿ-tsúi(搖水). *from the mouth*, bū-tsúi(霧水).

**sprout**, huat-gê(發芽); mêng-gê(萌芽); pauh-gê〔〕. *bamboo*, tek-sún(竹笋).

**spume**, tsúi-phue̍h(水沫).

**spur**, *cock's*, koi-jiáu(雞爪); koi-kṳ̃(雞距).

**spurious**, ké(假).

**spurt**, *water*, bū-tsúi(霧水).

**spy**, *to*, thàm(探); kui-thàm(規探). *a*, thàm-kiáⁿ(探囝); kan-sòi(奸細); tsò-sùaⁿ(做線).

**squabble**, sie-à(相詏); sie-mēⁿ(相罵); sie-mēⁿ sie-phah(相罵相拍).

**squadron**, che̍k-pan-tsûn(一班船).

**squall**, huang-sî(風時); phah-huang-sî(拍風時); khuâng-huang méⁿ-hõu(狂風猛雨).

**squander**, hua-hùi(花費); sái-tiāu-chîⁿ(使掉錢); tak-nn̄g-tiāu-chîⁿ〔〕; phùa-hùi-tiāu(破費掉); phùa-tiāu(破掉).

**square**, sì-pang(四方). *on chess board*, kî-ke̍k(棋格). *a workman's square*, khek-chhieh(曲尺). *to square accounts*, ap-siàu(押數); siàu-ba̍k chheng-tshó(數目清楚).

**squash**, *a*, kue(瓜).

**squash**, *to*, teh--tie̍h(壓着); teh-phùa(壓破); iap-phùa(壓破).

**squat**, *on the heels*, tshn̂g〔〕; khû(踞).

**squeak**, ki-ki-kiè(機機叫).

**squeamish**, àiⁿ-thòu(愛吐).

**squeeze**, tẽⁿ(捏); ko̍ih(夾); liū(溜). *money*, le̍k-sok(勒索).

**squint**, siâ-chiáu-ma̍k(斜朝目); tshúa-ma̍k(歪目); thuah-theng-ma̍k(拖撐目).

**squirt**, phùn-tsúi(噴水); bū-tsúi(霧水).

**stab**, tshǹg(闖); kiâⁿ-tshǹg(行剌).

**stable**, bé-pâng(馬房).

**stack**, *of straw*, tsháu-khn̂g(草囤).

**staff**, kuái-chiãng(拐杖). *(a club)*, kùn(棍). *(thin)*, tshûe(槌).

**stag**, te̍k-kóu(特股).

**stage**, *for plays*, hì-thâi(戲臺); hì-pêⁿ(戲棚). *of road*, lōu-tsãm(路站).

**stagger**, *to*, pho-lo-sia-kiâⁿ(陂咯斜行); pha-phîn-kiâⁿ(拋貧行).

**stagnant**, *water*, sí-tsúi(死水); bõi-kiâⁿ-lâu kâi-tsúi(袂行流个水).

**stain**, jiám-u(染污); mak--tie̍h nah-sap(衊着垃圾). *with ink*, ba̍k-u(捬着). *with blood*, hueh-u(捬着). see DYE.

**stair**, lâu-thui(樓梯); ta̍h-pōu-tsâng(踏步叢). *go upstairs*, teng-lâu(登樓); seng-lâu(升樓); chiẽⁿ-lâu(上樓); peh-chiẽⁿ-lâu(爬上樓); khṳ̀-lâu-téng(去樓頂).

**stake**, *for fastening cattle to*, gû-khṳ̍t〔〕. *to throw a rope over*, lap-khṳ̍t〔〕.

**stale**, sit-bī(失味). *(mouldy)*, tie̍h-kauh(着捲).

**stalk**, tiũ-kó(稻稿); be̍h-kó(麥稿).

**stall**, gû-koiⁿ(牛間); gû-tiâu(牛條); gû-nûaⁿ〔〕.

**stallion**, bé-kóu(馬牯).

**stamens**, hue-chhiu(花鬚).

**stammer**, tōa-chi̍h(大舌); tàⁿ-ūe têng-kù(呾話重句).

**stamp**, *to*, khap-jī-hō(恰字號); khap-ìn(蓋印).

**stamp**, *to*, *with the foot*, thiàm-kha(蹴骹); thiàm-tī(蹴地); thiàm-thôu-ẽ(蹴塗下); thiàm-tôi thiàm-kih(蹴題蹴砌). *when singing*, phah-pán(拍板).

**stanchion**, khiã-thiãu(徛柱); thèⁿ(撐). *in window*, theng-chí〔〕.

**stand**, khiã(徛). *up*, khiã--khí-lâi(徛起來). *erect*, khiā-khiā(徛徛). *not stand on ceremony*, put-khu lói-siàu(不區禮數); mín-tsṳ́-sòi(免子細). *stand and look passively on*, siù-chhiú phâng-kuan(袖手旁觀). *cannot stand it*, nãiⁿ-m̄-khṳ̀(奈毋去); m̄-hó-nãiⁿ(毋好奈). *a stand*, kè(架); kí-tshn̂g(几床); tê-kí(茶几). *for clothes*, ui-kè(衣架); saⁿ-kè(衫架).

**standard**, kî(旗).

**staphyloma**, ma̍k-chiu thóu-tsu(目睭土珠); ma̍k thóu-tsu(目土珠).

**staple**, *a*, thih-phīⁿ(鐵鼻); ka-sut〔〕.

**star**, chheⁿ(星); che̍k-lia̍p-chheⁿ(一粒星). *stars and constellations*, chheⁿ-siù(星宿). *falling*, pue-chheⁿ(飛星). *sun, moon and stars*, ji̍t-gue̍h chheⁿ-sîn(日月星辰).

**starch**, chieⁿ(漿). *(paste)*, kôu(糊). *to*, kùe-chieⁿ(過漿); kùe-ám(過飲).

**stare**, ma̍k kim-kim-thóiⁿ(目金金睇); ma̍k-chiu tsù-tsù tõ-thóiⁿ(目睭注注在睇). *staring about all round*, ma̍k thóiⁿ kàu-iaⁿ-iaⁿ(目睇到影影); ma̍k kok-kok-kim(目國國金). *what are you staring about for*, õ(哦), lṳ́ tsò kâu-kâu-iang(汝做猴猴央).

**starling**, liãu-ko-chiáu(鷯哥鳥).

**start**, *on a journey*, khí-sin(起身); khí-kiâⁿ(起行); khí-thêng(起程); khí-bé(起馬).

**startled**, tie̍h-kiaⁿ(着驚); he̍hⁿ--chē-kiè(赫些叫). *to startle*, phièn-nâng-kiaⁿ(騙人驚).

**starve**, gō(餓). *to death*, gō-sí(餓死).

**state**, *of a(阿) thing*, chhêng-hêng(情形); hêng-sì(形勢); sṳ̄-chhêng(事情); chhêng-iû(情由); kéng-ngõ(境遇); ngõ-ha̍h(遇合).

**state**, *to*, tàⁿ(呾); sueh(說); o̍h(學); kàu-sù(告訴).

**state**, *a*, *or kingdom*, pang(邦); kok(國).

**statesman**, tãi-chhîn(大臣).

**station**, *in life*, sin-hūn(身分); tī-ūi(地位). *of good station*, sin-hūn kãu-tãng(身分厚重); sin-ke kãu-tãng(身家厚重). *military*, sìn-tī(信地); iâⁿ-sìn(營信).

**statue**, sièⁿ(像); ngóu-sièⁿ(偶像); ngóu-siàng(偶相); khek-sièⁿ(刻像). *of stone*, chie̍h-sièⁿ(石像).

**statute**, *a*, che̍k-tiâu huap-lu̍t(一條法律); che̍k-tiâu lu̍t-kài(一條律界); che̍k-tiâu kài-mẽng(一條戒命).

**stave**, *of cask*, tháng-pang(桶枋); tháng-chhiêⁿ(桶牆).

**stay**, *with any one for a while*, khṳ̀ tsò-nâng-kheh(去做人客). *in a place*, nāⁿ(在); khiã-khí(徛起).

**steadfast**, kien-kù(堅固); thó-tàng(妥當); uaⁿ-ún(安穩).

**steak**, phah-ne̍k(拍肉).

**steal**, thau-khie̍h(偷挈); thau-tãu(偷盜); thau-chhiap(偷竊); tãu-chhiap(盜竊); thau-so〔〕. *in the daytime*, phah-pe̍h-ji̍t(拍白日); phah-pe̍h-tsuãng(拍白撞). *children*, kuái-tô tsṳ́-nńg(拐逃子女).

**stealthily**, thau(偷); àm-chẽⁿ(暗靜); sai-ẽ(私下).

**steam**, tsúi-in(水煙); tsúi-khì(水氣). *to*, tshue(炊); hip(翕); liū(鎦).

**steamer**, húe-tsûn(火船); húe-lûn-tsûn(火輪船).

**steel**, kǹg(鋼). *real*, chiàⁿ-kǹg(正鋼). *to put on a steel edge*, hẽ-kǹg(下鋼); chiap-kǹg(接鋼).

**steelyard**, chhìn(秤); tshâ-chhìn(柴秤). *weights of*, chhìn-thûi(秤錘). *beam of*, chhìn-kuaⁿ(秤竿); chhìn-ko(秤篙). *to test by comparing with another*, kah-chhìn(甲秤).

**steep**, kiã(崎); kiã-sià(崎瀉).

**steep**, *to*, chìm(浸). *in water*, chìm-tsúi(浸水).

**steer**, *to*, *a ship*, hūaⁿ-tõa(捍舵); lia̍h-tõa(掠舵); sái-tsûn(駛船); lia̍h-búe(掠尾). *steersman*, tãi-kong(舵工).

**stem**, *a*, kuaⁿ(竿); sin(身); kó(稿).

**stench**, tshàu-hièn(臭憲).

**step**, pōu(步). *(stride)*, hua̍h(伐). *step by step*, che̍k-pōu che̍k-pōu(一步一步). *steps of ladder*, thui-chí(梯子). *of stair-case*, ta̍h-pōu-tsâng(踏步叢). *stepping-stone*, pōu-chie̍h(步石); ta̍h-pōu-chie̍h(踏步石).

**step-mother**, kì-bó(繼母); ãu-bó(後母). *step-son*, kì-kiáⁿ(繼囝).

**sterile**, bõi-seⁿ(袂生). *ground*, sán-tī(㾪地).

**stern**, ngiâm(嚴).

**stern**, *of ship*, tsûn-búe(船尾).

**stew**, *to*, hip(翕); pû(煲); sa̍h(煠).

**stick**, *a*, tshûe(箠); kùn(棍).

**stick**, *to*, tah-tùe(搭綴). *stick in*, tshah(插); tàu(鬥). *sticky*, liâm-lî tha-thi(廉籬他替); kṳ̍t(結).

**stiff**, ngẽ(硬); ngẽ-ngau̍h(硬鱷). *stiff-necked*, sim ngẽ(心硬); aú-hûeⁿ(嘔橫); hûeⁿ-nge̍k(橫逆). *as with starch*, khiā-khiā(徛徛).

**stifle**, hip-sí(翕死); khàm-sí(勘死). *inquiry*, thâng-sat-tiāu(蟲虱掉); hìm-tiāu(禁掉).

**still**, huân-liáu(還了); huân-kèng(還敬); siãng-chhiáⁿ(尙且); iû-sĩ(猶是); jiông-jiên(仍然). *more*, zú-kèng-tsōi(愈敬㩼).

**still**, *adj.*, tiām-chẽⁿ(恬靜); thiâm-chẽⁿ(恬靜); chẽⁿ(靜); uaⁿ-chẽⁿ(安靜). *still-born*, sí-tho(死胎).

**still**, *a*, kek-tháng(激桶).

**stimulate**, kóu-bú(鼓舞); kám-tõng(感動); kám-kek(感激).

**sting**, *a*, chhì(刺). *to*, tàng(當). *stung by a wasp*, khṳt-phang tàng--tie̍h(乞芳當着).

**stingy**, khau-khak(扣剋); khek-po̍h(刻薄); khah-khiãm(較儉); kien-liẽn(慳吝).

**sitnk**, tshàu-hièn(臭獻); tshàu(臭). *stink-pot*, húe-kùan(火管).

**stipulations**, ieh-tiâu(約條); tiâu-ieh(條約); tiâu-khúan(條款).

**stir**, *to*, chhiau-phû(鍬浮); lã〔〕; lã-phû〔〕; ká(攪); ká-tsâu(絞吵); kiáu-tñg(攪蕩). *a stir*, lāu-jie̍t(鬧熱). *to stir up*, jiá(惹); thie-so(挑唆). *oneself*, tsṳ̃-mién(自勉); tsṳ̃-lĩ(自利); lĩ-chì mién-la̍t(勵志勉力); hùn-mién(奮勉).

**stirrup**, bé-ta̍h-tèng(馬踏䟓).

**stitch**, *to*, thīⁿ(縫). *too wide*, tsam-kha khah-hi(針骹較稀); tsam-kha hi-so(針骹稀疏). *slip-stitch*, chhiam(籤). *fine and close*, tsam-kha ba̍t-tsa̍t(針骹密實); kau-tsam ba̍t-thīⁿ(交針密縫).

**stock**, *in trade*, hùe-mue̍h(貨物); hùe-pńg(貨本); pńg-hùe(本貨).

**stocks**, *the*, tshâ-gô(柴鵝); kha-khàu(骹銬); kha-tsa̍h(骹柵).

**stomach**, tóu(肚); tõu(肚); ūi(胃); pî(脾). *pit of*, koi-tshùi-kháu(雞喙口); tsúi-khuh-kháu(水窟口). *empty*, khang-sim-tóu(空心肚); hau-pak(枵腹); khang-pak(空腹); tóu iau(肚枵); iau-tóu(枵肚).

**stone**, chie̍h(石); chie̍h-põu(石部). *of fruits*, hu̍t(核). *stone-quarry*, phah-chie̍h-suaⁿ(打石山). *to stone*, ka̍k-chie̍h(捔石); tsang-chie̍h ka̍k(將石捔).

**stool**, íⁿ-thâu(椅頭). *close*, tang-si-íⁿ(東司椅). *go to*, kiâⁿ-tãng(行動); kiâⁿ-tãi-piẽn(行大便); tshut-kiong(出恭). *foot-stool*, kha-ta̍h-íⁿ(骹踏椅).

**stoop**, khut-sin(屈身); phak-ku(趴佝).

**stop**, *a person*, nûaⁿ-tsũ(軟住); tsó-chí(阻止); tsó-tǹg(阻擋); nûaⁿ-tsó(軟阻); nûaⁿ-chí(軟止); kìm-chí(禁子); nûaⁿ-lōu(軟路). *for a minute*, hiah-tiām--chē(歇恬些); chhiáⁿ-būe(請未); chhiáⁿ-mān(請慢). *at the door and call*, chí-pōu iâng-siaⁿ(止步陽聲). *up*, sat-miⁿ(蝨眠); that-miⁿ(撻眠). *one's breath*, aⁿ phīⁿ-khang-huang(掩鼻空風). *raining*, hõu chêⁿ(雨晴). *doing anything*, hiah(歇); thêng-hiah(停歇); thêng-tiām(停恬); hiah-kang(歇工). *half-way*, pùaⁿ-thû zṳ̂-hùi(半途挐費); pùaⁿ-lōu-hiah(半路歇). *business, in protest against injustice*, pã-chhĩ(罷市).

**store**, *up*, tun-chek(屯積); chek-thiok(積蓄); chek-tsũ(積聚); tsũ-thiok(聚蓄); khǹg-bûa(囥埋); khǹg-khí(囥起); khǹg-chek(囥積). *a store-house*, tsàng(壯); tsàng-pâng(棧房); khòu-pâng(庫房).

**story**, *a (lie)*, pe̍h-chiáⁿ-ūe(白䭕話). *make up a*, niap-tsò ké-ūe(捏做假話). *story-teller*, hue-niauⁿ pe̍h-chi̍h(花鳥白舌); o̍h-kóu kâi-nâng(學古个人).

**story**, *of a house*, che̍k-tsâng(一層); che̍k-în-lâu(一沿樓); che̍k-têng-lâu(一重樓).

**straight**, ti̍t(直). *straighten*, phah-ti̍t(拍直); tshun-ti̍t(伸直); sái-ti̍t(使直). *straightforward speech*, ti̍t-tàⁿ(直呾); bô-úi-khiok(無偉曲). *straightway*, ti̍t-ti̍t(直直); sûi-sî(隨時).

**stranger**, *a*, nâng-kheh(人客); sin-kheh(新客); chheⁿ-hūn-nâng(生份人); ién-jîn(遠人).

**strength**, la̍t(力); khì-la̍t(氣力). *strengthening*, ũ-póu(有補).

**strike**, phah(拍); khà(扣); hḿ〔〕; khek(擊). *a name off list*, tṳ̂-miâⁿ(除名); khou-tiāu(箍掉); keh-tiāu(隔掉); sàng-khṳ̀(送去); khṳ́-tiāu(去掉). *the eye*, tshok-ma̍k(觸目); tú-ngõ thóiⁿ-kìⁿ(堵遇睇見). *together*, sie-tsuãng(相撞). *on a rock*, tsûn huãm-suaⁿ(船犯山); tsûn tiam-tie̍h-chie̍h(船砧着石); tsûn lṳ̂-suaⁿ(船驢山). *a striker, for a grain measure*, táu-kài(倒芥).

**string**, soh-kiáⁿ(索囝); sùaⁿ(線); pau-soh(包索). *for cash*, chîⁿ-kǹg-soh(錢鋼索). *of musical instrument*, hîⁿ-sùaⁿ(弦線). *to string cash*, tshng-chîⁿ(穿錢). *a string of cash*, che̍k-tiàu-chîⁿ(一吊錢); che̍k-kǹg-chîⁿ(一鋼錢); che̍k-tshoiⁿ-chîⁿ(一千錢). *a string of pearls or beads*, che̍k-pak-tsu(一腹珠); che̍k-tshùan-tsu(一串珠).

**strip**, *to*, pak(縛); thut(脫). *of everything*, pak-ko-kúe(剝糕粿). *the sleeves*, lu̍t-saⁿ-ńg(捋衫腕). *a*, che̍k-tiâu(一條).

**striped**, poiⁿ-bûn(斑文); hue-bûn(花紋); seⁿ-niàuⁿ-hûn(生鳥痕); liú-tiâu-hûn(柳條痕).

**strive**, sie-cheⁿ(相爭); sie-tàu(相鬥); sài(賽); cheⁿ-soiⁿ(爭想); sie-jiáng(相嚷); sie-à(相詏); m̄-hûa(毋和); seⁿ-ūe(生話).

**stroke**, *sun-stroke*, pha̍k-tie̍h-ji̍t(曝着日); chien-ji̍t(煎日). *fatal ditto*, ji̍t pha̍k-sí(日曝死). *of pen*, che̍k-ue̍h(盡劃). *give him ten strokes*, phah-i tsa̍p-ē(打伊十下). *fetch a stroke with something in the hand*, hḿ〔〕.

**stroke**, *to*, *the hair*, so-môⁿ(梳毛); chhiú-môⁿ(手毛). *to stroke a man down*, so-lu̍ah(梳撚); moⁿ-so(摩挲). *the beard*, lu̍t-chhiu(捋鬚).

**stroll**, *about*, thit-thô(佚佗); lau(流); in-iû(因由); ôiⁿ-iû(閒遊); ôiⁿ-kiâⁿ(閒行).

**strong**, ũ-la̍t(有力); khiàng(勥); tōiⁿ(𠕇); nãiⁿ(耐); tsàng(壯); tsàng-kiẽn(壯健); khin-kiāⁿ(輕健); kiāⁿ(健). *of party*, chhiàu〔〕. *of tea*, kãu(厚).
