**student**, bûn-thông(文童); tha̍k-tsṳ-nâng(讀書人[訓]). *(senior)*, tōa-ha̍k-seng(大學生). *(younger)*, iùⁿ-thông(養童). *studious*, khṳ̂n(勤); khṳ̂n-la̍t(勤力); khṳ̂n-sim(勤心).

**stumble**, pua̍h--tie̍h(跋着); kha tie̍h-that(骹着踢); that-pua̍h(踢跋); that--tia̍h(踢著); lap-pua̍h(拉跋); lau-pua̍h(流跋). *over a stone*, that-tie̍h-chie̍h(踢着石).

**stupid**, ngà(㦙); ngô-ngà(愚㦙); ngô-tshún(愚蠢); ngô-phak〔〕; ngô-lú(愚魯); lú-tũn(魯鈍); ngûi-phûe(危皮); m̄-hiáu(毋曉); móng-tóng(懵懂); chhi-ko(痴哥); chhi-ngâi(痴呆); chhi-ngà(痴㦙); chhi-tsuat(痴拙); ngōng-ngōng(戇戇); khòng-ngōng(悾戇).

**subject**, *of ruler*, peh-sèⁿ(百姓); sù-mîn(庶民); chhiú-ẽ(手下); kúan-ẽ(管下); hat-ẽ(轄下); so̍k-ẽ(屬下). *to be*, sũn-ho̍k(順服); zua̍t-ho̍k(悅服).

**succeed**, *to*, tit-sêng(得成); tit-chiâⁿ(得成); sêng-kong(成功); tit-ì(得意); zû-ngũan(如願); sûi-sim(遂心); ha̍h-siẽⁿ(合想); zû-ì(如意); buān-sṳ̄ sũn(萬事順); lĩ-ta̍t(利達).

**succeed**, *or follow*, kì-chiap(繼接); sêng-chiap(承繼); siang-chiap(相接); chiap-so̍k(接續). *in succession*, tshṳ̀-tõiⁿ(得意); che̍k-kiãⁿ che̍k-kiãⁿ(一件一件).

**successive**, siang-liên(相連); sie-sùa(相紲); siang-kì(相繼); siang-sêng(相承). *generations*, le̍h-tō(歷代). *a successor*, ãu-pùe(後輩); chih-jīm(接任); chih-ìn(接應). *a successor (heir)*, ãu-sṳ̂(後嗣).

**succour**, pang-tsõ(幫助); kiù-chì(救濟); kiù-tsõ(救助).

**such**, chièⁿ-seⁿ-kâi(此樣生个); chí-tsùaⁿ-kâi〔〕. *who ever heard of such a thing*, khá-ũ tshṳ́-lí(豈有此理); khí-ũ tshṳ́-lí(豈有此理); tuàn-bô tshṳ́-lí(斷無此理); tshông-bô tshṳ́-lí(從無此理).

**suck**, tsuh(嘬); kuh(嗝); khip(吸). *as child*, chia̍h-nĩⁿ(食奶); tsuh-nĩⁿ(嘬奶); kuh-nĩⁿ(嗝奶). *suckle*, chhī-nĩⁿ(飼奶).

**sudden**, hut-jiên(忽然); hut-jiên-kan(忽然間); ngóu-jiên-kan(偶然間); hó-sĩ-sĩ(好是是); huh--chē-kiè(欻些叫); put-kak(不覺); tsõu-jiên(驟然).

**sudorific**, piáu-kūaⁿ-ie̍h(表汗藥); huat-kūaⁿ-ie̍h(發汗藥).

**sue**, phah-kuaⁿ-si(拍官司); kò(告); thó(討); tshūe(覓).

**suet**, lâ(朥); lâ-pâng-thâu(朥房頭).

**suffer**, siũ-khóu(受苦); ũ-kan-khóu(有甘苦). *wrong*, siũ-uan(受苦); siũ-khut(受苦); siũ-uan-uáng(受冤枉); pĩ-khut(被屈); siũ-khui(受虧); chia̍h-khui(食虧). *patiently*, khat-khóu-lún(刻苦忍); jím-nãiⁿ(忍耐); kien-jím(堅忍).

**suffer (allow)**, hàuⁿ(好); khṳt(乞); iông(容); tsún(準).

**sufficient**, kàu(夠); tsok(足); kàu-tsok(到足); lã(𤰉). *to eat*, kàu-chia̍h(夠食).

**suffocate**, hip-sí(翕死). *in water*, kek-sí(激死); chìm-sí(沉死).

**sugar**, thn̂g(糖). *raw*, ou-thn̂g(烏糖). *white*, pe̍h-thn̂g(白糖). *highly refined*, kit-hún-thn̂g(結粉糖); kiet-hún-thn̂g(潔粉糖). *candy-sugar*, piaⁿ-thn̂g(冰糖). *sugar-cane*, chià(蔗). *to plant*, tshah-chià(插蔗); chèng-chià(種蔗). *to crush*, ká-chià(絞蔗). *sugar-mill*, ká-liâu(絞寮). *conical vessel for refining*, thn̂g-lāu(糖漏). *to refine*, lāu-thn̂g(漏糖). *warehouse*, thn̂g-pâng(糖房).

**suggest**, thî-phû(提浮); thî-khí(提起); kà(教); khí-ì(起意); huat-liãm(發念); khí-liãm-thâu(起念頭).

**suicide**, tsṳ̃-chĩn(自盡); tsṳ̃-suah(自殺); ka-kī khṳ̀-sí(家己去死); ka-kī-sí(家己死); tâu-tsúi(投水); thiàu-hái(跳海); chia̍h-ie̍h--sí(食藥死); thun-kim--sí(吞金死); tiàu-ãm--sí(吊頷死).

**suit**, *of clothes*, che̍k-hù saⁿ-khòu(全套衫褲); che̍k-thàu ho̍k-sek(全套服飾).

**suit**, *at law*, sõng-sṳ̄(訟事); kuaⁿ-si(官司). see SUE.

**suit**, *to*, ha̍h(合); ha̍h-ēng(合用); kah(合); kah-pān(合辦). *to suit people*, chhèng-nâng-ì(稱人意); ha̍h-nâng-ì(合人意); sũn-nâng-sim(順人心); tèng-ì(中意); kùe-ì(過意); *suit one, as clothes*, kah-sin(合身). *suitable*, kah-kah(合合); khap-chhiet(恰切); kah-pān.

**sullen**, mīn pãu-pek(面抱迫); mīn-sek ou-àm(面色烏暗); sèⁿ-chhêng m̄-hó(性情毋好); kou-ta̍k-sièⁿ(孤獨相); mīn pũ-àu pũ-àu(面浮懊浮懊); mīn hìm-hìm(面闇闇).

**sulphur**, liû-n̂g(硫磺).

**sultry**, hiap-zua̍h(狹熱); pãu-jie̍t(暴熱); pek-zua̍h(逼熱). *wind*, huang nãⁿ-nãⁿ(風若若).

**sum**, *to*, kāng-kòi(共計); ha̍h-kāng(合共); tsóng-kòi(總計); tsóng-siàu(總數); kat-tsóng-siàu(結總數). *the sum of this is that─*, tsóng zṳ̂-ngân--tsṳ─(總而言之).

**summary**, tãi-ì(大意); tãi-khài(大概); tãi-iàu(大要); tãi-tsóng-tsáng(大總帳); tãi-lia̍k(大略); iàu-ngân(要言); pau-kuat(包括).

**summer**, hē(夏); hē-thiⁿ(夏天); zua̍h--thiⁿ(熱天). *dress*, zua̍h-saⁿ(熱衫).

**summit**, téng(頂). *of hill*, suaⁿ-téng(山頂).

**summon**, tiãu(召); tiãu-hàm(召集); hàm(喊); kiè(叫). *to issue a summons*, tshut-phiè(出票).

**sumptuous**, hong-hûa(風華); phâi-chhiâng(排場). *(of feast)*, phâng-phài(滂沛).

**sun**, ji̍t(日); ji̍t-thâu(日頭); thài-iâng(太陽). *light*, ji̍t-kuang(日光). *beams*, ji̍t-tsam(日針). *heat*, ji̍t-khì(日氣). *the sun is not strong*, ji̍t-sek chíⁿ(日色正); ji̍t-tsháu chíⁿ(日草正). *sun-rise*, ji̍t tshut(日出); ji̍t-thâu tshut(日頭出); ji̍t khí(日起). *sun-set*, ji̍t lo̍h(日落); ji̍t-thâu lo̍h-suaⁿ(日頭落山). *declining Westward*, ji̍t siâ-sai(日斜西). *sun-dial*, ji̍t-kui(日規). *shadow*, ji̍t-iáⁿ(日影). *eclipse*, ji̍t si̍h(日蝕). *to sun oneself*, chieh-ji̍t(借日). *to dry in the sun*, pha̍k-ji̍t(曝日); sài-ji̍t(曬日). *sun-stroke*, tòng-sú(當暑). *sun-stroke (fatal)*, ji̍t pha̍k-sí(日曝死).

**Sunday**, lói-pài-ji̍t(禮拜日).

**sundries**, tsa̍p-hùe(什貨); tsa̍p-mu̍eh(什物).

**sunk**, *in vice*, ji̍p-gūa-sṳ̄(入外事); tshap-ji̍p gūa-sṳ̄(插入外事); jiám--tie̍h gūa-sṳ̄(染着外事). *sunken eyes*, ma̍k thap-thap(目遢遢); ma̍k-chiu chhim-au(目睭深凹).

**supercargo**, tshut-hái(出海); thâu-ma̍k(頭目).

**supercilious**, ma̍k-khang tōa(目空大); thóiⁿ--nâng m̄-khí(睇人毋起); thóiⁿ--nâng m̄-chiẽⁿ(睇人毋上); thóiⁿ-nâng m̄-tõ-ma̍k-kak(睇人毋到目角); ma̍k--tang bô-nâng(目冬無人); phâng jia̍k-bô-nâng(旁若無人).

**supererogation**, hūn-gūa tsṳ-kong(份外之功).

**superficial**, chhìn-tshái-tsò(凊彩做); sûi-piẽn-tsò(隨便做); tshó-lia̍k(草略); ma-ma-hu(馬馬虎); gūa-phûe kâi-kang-hu(外皮个工夫); phûe-môⁿ kâi-kang-hu(皮毛个工夫). *learning*, chhién-ha̍k(淺學).

**superfine**, siãng-téng-iùⁿ(上等幼); tsùe-iùⁿ-sòi(最幼細); cheng-sòi(精細).

**superfluous**, iẽn-ṳ̂(延餘); mín-ēng(免用). *talk*, lo-so(囉嗦); lo-lo so-so(囉囉嗦嗦).

**superintend**, chiáng-kuán(掌管); lí(理); chiáng-lí(掌理); chiáng-chip(掌執); chiáng-siú(掌守); chip-lí(執理); kam-tok(監督); tok-kang(督工); tiám-tok(點督).

**superior**, *to*, iâⁿ(贏); iâⁿ-kùe(贏過); kiêⁿ--kùe(強過); kèng-hó(更好). *a*, tōa--nâng(大人); tõ-chiēⁿ kâi-nâng(在上个人); chiēⁿ-pùe tsun-chiáng(上輩尊長). *officers*, chiēⁿ-si(上司). *the superior man*, kun-tsṳ́(君子).

**superlative**, *degree*, chì(至); ke̍k(極); siãng(上); sĩm(甚); kùe(過); tsa̍p-hun(十分).

**supersede**, thòi-tsò(代做); chih-jīm(接任).

**superstition**, sièn-siàⁿ(煽聖); hàuⁿ-kú-kuài(好古怪).

**supper**, mêⁿ-àm-pn̄g(夜暗飯); mńg-pn̄g(晚飯); àm-tǹg(暗頓); mńg-tǹg(晚當). *to cook*, tsṳ́-mêⁿ-hng(煮夜昏); pû-àm-pn̄g(煲暗飯). *The Lord's Supper*, Tsú kâi-siàⁿ-tshan(主个聖餐); mńg-tshan(晚餐). *to observe the*, siú-mńg-tshan(守晚餐).

**support**, iáng(養); iáng-io̍k(養育). *one's parents*, hõng-iãng pẽ-bó(奉養父母); chhī-húe-si̍t(飼伙食); chhī-húe-thâu(飼火頭).

**suppose**, *to*, siẽⁿ(想); phah-sǹg(拍算); kòi-sǹg(計算). *I supposed(erroneously)*, sah--tsò〔〕; gî--tsò(疑做); siẽⁿ--tsò(想做); gî-sĩ(疑是); kâu-kiè〔〕; khue-tiāⁿ〔〕; pān--tsò(判做). *supposing*, pí-zũ(比喻); phì-zû(譬如); kiá-zû(假如); kiá-sái(假使); zû-jia̍k(如若); tháng-jia̍k(倘若); siet-sái(設使).

**suppress**, hìm-tiāu(禁掉); chí-at(制遏); iap-chì(壓制); iap-ho̍k(壓服); teh(壓); ji̍h(揤). *a book*, tsṳ-chheh tui-ji̍p-khòu(之冊追入褲).

**suppurate**, seⁿ-lâng(生膿); pũ-lâng(胕膿); kùan-lâng(灌膿); kâm-lâng(含膿).

**Supreme**, *The*, Chì-Siãng--chiá(至上者).

**sure**, ún-kù(穩固); kien-kù(堅固); thó-tàng(妥當). *surely*, tiāⁿ-tie̍h(定着).

**surety**, tam-sêng(擔承); tam-pó(擔保); pó-niáⁿ(保領); tam-jīn(擔認); tong-pó(中保).

**surface**, mīn(面); gūa-mīn(外面); gūa-phûe(外皮); chiēⁿ-mīn(上面); téng-mīn(頂面); mīn-téng(面頂). *of the sea*, hái-mīn(海面).

**survey**, *land*, chiãng-tī(丈地); chiãng-tshân(丈田); niêⁿ-tshân(量田). *a coast*, thàm-sua-tsúi(探沙水). *troops*, thóiⁿ-tshau(睇操).

**suspect**, gî(疑); tshai-gî(猜疑); gî-tshai(疑猜); kiaⁿ-ùi(驚畏); khióng-phàⁿ(恐怕).

**suspend**, *to*, tiàu(吊); hûiⁿ(懸); kùa(掛).

**suspense**, khùa-sim(掛心); khùa-lṳ̃(掛慮); khùa-liãm(掛念); khùa-mōⁿ(掛望); hûiⁿ-mōⁿ(懸望); hûiⁿ-hûiⁿ tõ-mōⁿ(懸懸在望).

**suspicious**, khó-gî(好疑); hó-gî(好疑); móng-móng(茫茫). *person*, to-gî(多疑).

**sustain**, hû-khí(扶起); hû-tsõ(扶助); tsài(載). *can*, káⁿ-tng(敢當). *I cannot sustain it*, uá m̄-káⁿ-tng(我毋敢當); sêng-tsài m̄-khí(成載毋起).

**swallow**, *to*, thun(吞); thun--lo̍h-khṳ̀(吞落去). *with effort*, kṳ̃--lo̍h-khṳ̀(鋸落去).

**swan**, khok(鵠); thien-gô(天鵝).

**swarm**, che̍k-khûn(成群). *swarming with fish*, hṳ̂ kãu-tsãi(魚交際).

**swathe**, tîⁿ(纏); tsat(扎); pau(包).

**sway**, *to*, *in the wind*, iâu-lâi iâu-khṳ̀(搖來搖去).

**swear**, huat-sī(發誓); mêng-sī(盟誓). *before heaven*, tng-thiⁿ mêng-sī(當天盟誓).

**sweat**, kūaⁿ(汗). *to*, lâu-kūaⁿ(流汗). see PERSPIRE.

**sweep**, sàu(掃); sueh(刷); tshóiⁿ(鏟); pũaⁿ(槃). *together, with fingers*, sa-bûa〔〕.

**sweet**, tiâm(甜); kam(甘); kam-tiâm(甘甜). *sweet-meats*, tiâm-liāu(甜料); thn̂g-liāu(糖料); mu̍eh-chia̍h(物食). *words*, ki-tshùi chhî-chhî-tiâm(枝喙遲遲甜). *sweeten*, suah-thn̂g(煞糖); lo̍h-thn̂g(落糖); chhiau-thn̂g(鍬糖). *smell*, phang(芳). 

**sweet-bread**, *or pancreas (of pig)*, tṳ-chhieh(豬尺).

**swell**, *to*, chéng(腫); chéng--khí-lâi(腫起來); chéng-hap(腫合); hap(呷); chéng-tǹg(腫頓). *slightly, as from insect bites*, phûe hàng-hàng(皮夯夯).

**swift**, méⁿ(猛); khùe(快); sok(速).

**swim**, siû(泅); siû-tsúi(泅水). *(to float)*, phû-tsúi(浮水).

**swindle**, kuang-phièn(誆騙); kuang-lau(誆褸); lau-phièn-nâng(褸騙人). *swindler*, láu-kiáⁿ(漏囝).

**swing**, *a*, chheng-chhiu(清秋); chhien-chhiu(韆鞦). *to*, phah chheng-chhiu(拍清秋); sõ-lâi sõ-khṳ̀(搖來搖去).

**swine**, tṳ(豬). *to keep*, chhī-tṳ(飼豬).

**swoon**, m̄-tsai-nâng(毋知人); sit-sîn(失神); hun-kông(昏戇); hun-mîⁿ(昏糜).

**sword**, to(刀); kiàm(劍). *exercise*, bú-to mõng-kiàm(武刀猛劍). *to draw*, po̍ih-to(拔刀). *to sheath*, to ji̍p-to-khak(刀入刀殼).

**sycee**, uâng-pó(王寶); khiàu-thâu-si(翹頭絲); khò-si(鋯絲).

**sycophant**, tsù-kiong〔〕; pui-thiám(卑諂); thiám-mĩⁿ(諂媚).

**sympathy**, tâng-chhêng(體貼); tâng-sim(體貼); tâng-ì(體貼); tâng-iu tâng-la̍k(同憂同樂). *(kind consideration)*, thói-thiap(體貼). *(making allowance for another)*, thói-liãng(體貼); thí-liãng(體貼).

**syphon**, tsúi-thiu(水抽); khek-tsúi-tâng(刻水筒).

### T

**tabernacle**, pòu-phâng(布帆); tièⁿ-mõⁿ(帳幕).

**table**, tshn̂g(床). *one*, che̍k-chiah-tshn̂g(一隻床). *long and high*, kí-tshn̂g(几床). *to lay the*, pái-tshn̂g(擺床). *sit at*, tsõ-sia̍h(坐席). *to lay the table-cloth*, tshṳ-tshn̂g-pòu(舒床布). *embroidered cloth hung in front of table*, tshn̂g-kûn(床裙).

**table**, *or index*, ma̍k-lo̍k(目錄).

**tablet**, *ancestral*, sîn-tsú-pâi(神主牌); ke-sîn(家神); ba̍k-tsú(木主); sîn-tsú(神主). *setting forth any one's merit*, pín-hia̍h(匾額); pâi-pín(牌匾).

**tack**, *a*, kia̍h-teng〔〕. *to tack(sew)*, thīⁿ-tùe(縫綴).

**tack**, *to*, *as a ship*, khau-huang〔〕; hùe-phâng〔〕.

**tactics**, piaⁿ-huap(兵法); chièn-huap(戰法).

**tadpole**, kap-kiú-kuai(蛤虯鮭).

**tael**, *one*, *of silver*, che̍k-niéⁿ-ngṳ̂n(一兩銀).

**tail**, búe(尾). *peacock's tail feather*, khóng-chhieh-lêng(孔雀翎). *the peacock spreads its tail*, khóng-chhieh khui-phîn(孔雀開屏). *to wear a peacock's tail feather*, tài khóng-chhieh-lêng(戴孔雀翎); tì khóng-chhieh-lêng(置孔雀翎). see QUEUE.

**tailor**, tshâi-hông(裁縫); thīⁿ-saⁿ sai-pẽ(縫衫司阜).

**taint**, tiam-u(沾污); jiám(染); jiám-u(染污); ma̍k--tie̍h(目着). *tainted, as fish*, ien(蔫); sie̍h-bī(餿味).

**take**, khie̍h(挈); tshú(取); niⁿ(奶); lah(擸); put(不); tsang(棕). *your book*, khie̍h lṳ́-pńg-chheh(挈汝本冊). *a fort*, phah-phùa phàu-thâi(拍破炮刣). *a standard*, chhiéⁿ-kî(搶旗); to̍h-kî(擇旗). *away*, khie̍h-khṳ̀(挈去); siu-khí(收起); to̍h-tiāu(擇掉). *along with tea, &c*, phùe-tê(配茶); phùe-tê-chia̍h(配茶食). *with one*, thùa-khie̍h(退挈). *the air*, lā-liâng(納凉). *an inventory*, tiám-hùe-mue̍h(點貨物); kiám-tiám(檢點). *by lot*, khiah-khau(隙摳). *care*, tsṳ́-sòi(仔細); kṳ́n-sín(謹慎); sié-sim(小心); kṳ́n-sim(謹心); sòi-jī(細字). *care of*, thóiⁿ-siú(睇守); chiàu-kù(照顧); liāu-lí(料理). *care of oneself*, tsṳ̃-kí pó-tõng(自己保重). *down*, khie̍h--lo̍h-lâi(挈落來); pak--lo̍h-lâi(剝落來). *exercise*, khṳ̀-thit-thô(去佚佗); kiâⁿ-thit-thô(行佚佗); kiâⁿ-siau-iâu(行逍遙); ôiⁿ-pōu(閒步); kîn-kiâⁿ(巡行); kiâⁿ-lâi kiâⁿ-khṳ̀(行來行去). *one by the hand*, khan-chhiú(牽手). *leave of*, kàu-sî(告辭); sî-pie̍t(辭別); siang-pie̍t(相别); chiãm-pie̍t(暫別); kàu-pie̍t(告別). *one in (cheat)*, tshuah(撮); phièn(騙); kuang-phièn(誆騙). *medicine*, chia̍h-ie̍h(食藥). *out of the water*, liâu--tie̍h(蹽着). *off, shoes or clothes*, thǹg-tiāu(褪掉). *off, a hat*, pak-tiāu(剝掉); hien-tiāu(掀掉). *one's hat to any one*, hien-khí-bō tsò-lói-siàu(掀起帽做禮數). *off a cover*, iãuⁿ-khòiⁿ〔〕; iãuⁿ-khàm〔〕; iãuⁿ-khui〔〕. *out a splinter*, thie-tshuaⁿ(挑閂); kiah-chhì(揭試). *take snuff*, chia̍h-phīⁿ-hun(食鼻薰); hngh-phīⁿ-hun〔〕. *take snuff (out of bottle)*, thie-phīⁿ-hun(挑鼻薰). *up, with chopsticks*, koih(挾). *with two fingers*, nuehⁿ(捏); niⁿ(奶). *under the arm*, ko̍ih tõ koh-ẽ(夾在閣下). *the right hand path*, tùi-chiàⁿ-chhiú-pôiⁿ khṳ̀(對正手爿去). *a disease*, tie̍h-pēⁿ(着病); ùe-tie̍h-pēⁿ(慰着病); jiám-tie̍h-pēⁿ(染着病); thûan-jiám(傳染). *upon oneself*, ka-kī tam-sêng(家己擔承); taⁿ-tng(擔當). *take upon oneself (without authority)*, tsṳ̃-tsuan(自專). *fire*, to̍h-húe(着火). *a wife*, tshūa-chhin(娶親); tshūa-bóu(娶婦); tì-ke(置家). *hold of*, chhiú lia̍h(手掠); khie̍h-kín(挈緊); khîⁿ(纏); khîⁿ-kín(纏緊); mán-kín(挽緊); khan-kín(牽緊). *hold of one's queue*, khím-piⁿ(撳邊); tsáng-piⁿ(總邊); mán-piⁿ(挽邊).

**tale**, *a*, che̍k-tn̄g-kóu(一段古); kóu-chheh(古冊). *to tell tales*, o̍h-kóu(學古). *tale-bearer*, puaⁿ-sĩ-hui(搬是非); puaⁿ-pái(搬擺); puaⁿ-so(搬唆); kòiⁿ-so(間唆).

**talent**, tshâi-chhêng(才能); tshâi-lêng(才能); pún-sṳ̄(本事); pún-niáⁿ(本領). *a talented person*, tshâi-tsṳ́(才子); ũ-tshâi-chhêng(有才能).

**taste**, bī(味); bī-sòu(味素); khì-bī(氣味). *to*, siêⁿ-bī(嘗味); chhì-bī(試味). *tasteless*, bô-bī(無味); bô-bī-sòu(無味素); bô-khì-bī(無氣味); pe̍h-chiáⁿ pe̍h-chiáⁿ(白䭕白䭕); bī pi̍h(味闢); bī tãⁿ(味淡); chiáⁿ-tãⁿ(䭕淡); tãⁿ-po̍h(淡薄).

**tattered**, phùa(破); phùa-tshùi(破碎); i-saⁿ lâm-lú(伊衫藍縷); uân-sui-saⁿ pue-lêng-khòu(莞荽衫菠薐褲).

**tax**, *(customs dues)*, hiàng(餉). *(land-tax)*, niêⁿ(糧); tshân-niêⁿ(田糧); chîⁿ-niêⁿ(錢糧). *(likin)* lî-kim(厘金). *to pay*, uân-niêⁿ(完糧); na̍p-niêⁿ(納糧). *collectors of*, niêⁿ-chhe(糧差); tou-chhe(都差).

**tea**, tê(茶). *leaves*, tê-hie̍h(茶葉); tê-bí(茶米). *used leaves*, tê-phoh(茶粕). *tea-plant*, tê-tsâng(茶叢). *to make*, pû-tê(煲茶); pheng-tê(烹茶); phàu-tê(泡茶); tshong-tê(沖茶). *infuse in covered cup*, hìm-tê〔〕. *invite one to take*, chhiáⁿ-tê(請茶). *pour out*, sai-tê(司茶). *hand round*, khâng-tê(捧茶); khiâ-tê(擎茶). *drink*, chia̍h-tê(食茶); ím-tê(飲茶). *to fire*, pūe-tê(焙茶). *tea-taster*, tê-sṳ(茶師). *box of*, che̍k-sieⁿ-tê(一箱茶). *cup*, tê-cheng(茶盅); tê-pue(茶杯); tê-au(茶甌); kài-au(蓋甌). *canister*, te-bí-kuàn(茶米罐); siah-kuàn(錫罐). *kettle*, tê-ue(茶鍋). *pot*, tê-kuàn(茶罐); tshong-kuàn(冲罐). *tea-poy*, tê-kí(茶几). *saucer*, tê-tsûn(茶船); tê-ti̍h(茶碟); tê-pûaⁿ(茶盤). *strainer*, tê-thai(茶篩). *tea-men*, tê-kheh(茶客). *siftings*, tê-hu(茶夫); tê-ku̍eh(茶橛). *wholesale tea warehouse*, tê-hâng(茶行). *shop (for selling tea to drink)*, tê-kuán(茶館); tê-kṳ(茶居). *tea-harvest*, tê-tang(茶檔). *tea producing region*, tê-suaⁿ(茶山). *to gather*, tshái-tê(採茶); tiah-tê(摘茶).

**testimony**, chèng-kṳ̃(證據); kan-chèng(干證); chèng-ngân(證據); chí-chèng(證據).

**than**, *more*, put-chí(不止); m̄-chheng(毋清); put-to̍k(不獨); m̄-khéng(毋肯); tsōi--kùe(㩼過); ke--kùe(家過); huân-liáu-ke(還了家); huân-kèng-ke(還敬家); siãng-chhiáⁿ-ũ(上請有). *he is older than I*, i tōa--uá(伊大我); i tōa-kùe-uá(伊大過我). *no more than*, put-kùe(不過). *more than ten*, tsa̍p-gūa(十外); tsa̍p-tshut(十出); tsa̍p-ṳ̂(十餘); tsa̍p-tshûn(十賰).

**thank**, siā(謝); kám-siā(感謝). *many thanks*, tsōi-siā(㩼謝); to-siā(多謝); kám-mông(感蒙). *thank you*, lâu--lṳ́(勞汝); huân-lṳ́(煩汝); huân-lâu--lṳ́(煩勞汝); bûa-lūi--lṳ́(磨累汝); lūi--lṳ́(累汝); tōa-lãu-nâng(大勞人); chhit-lãu poih-tōa(七勞八大); siũ-hũi(受害); niáⁿ-hũi(領情); niáⁿ-chhêng(領情); kám-chhêng(感恩); hùi-sim(費心); phièn--lṳ́ hùi-sîn(騙汝費神); lâu-tõng--tie̍h lṳ́(勞動着汝); lãu-tõng--tie̍h tãi-kè(勞動着大駕). *I will thank you to come*, lūi-lṳ́-lâi(累汝來); chhiáⁿ-lṳ́-lâi(請汝來). *no need for thanks*, tàⁿ-kàu-lūi--kâi-ūe(呾到累个話); sĩ-pńg-téng(是本頂); sĩ-pńg-hūn(是本分); khí-káⁿ(起敢); huaⁿ-hí(歡喜); hó-ūe(好話); kōi-kōi(易易); kâi-ì-sṳ̀ tiāⁿ-tiāⁿ(個意思定定); mién-kám-siā(免感謝). *to return thanks*, tap-siā(答謝). *letter of thanks*, siā-thiap(謝帖). *thankful*, kám-ṳm put-buâng(感恩不忘); kám-ṳn put-chhién(感恩不淺); kám-liãm tõ-sim(感念在心); mông-ṳn tài-tek(蒙恩戴德); kám-ṳn tài-tek(感恩戴德); pò-ṳn(報恩); tsai-ṳn(知恩). *thankless*, buâng-ṳn(忘恩); buâng-ṳn hũ-ngĩ(忘恩負義); hiau-chhêng tso̍h-ngĩ(僥情絕義); bô-jîn-ngĩ(無仁義); buâng-chhêng(忘情); kùe-kèⁿ thiu-kúai(過勁抽拐). *thankworthy*, kai-siā(該謝).

**that**, hṳ́(許); hṳ́--kâi(許個). *that which he said*, i-só-tàⁿ(伊所呾). *that is to say*, ngân-khî(言其). *that night*, hṳ́-che̍k-mêⁿ(許一夜). *that side*, hièⁿ-pôiⁿ(向爿); hièⁿ-thâu(向頭). *at that time*, tng-sî(當時).

**thatch**, tshù-téng khàm-tsháu(厝頂蓋草); tshù-téng khòiⁿ-tsháu(厝頂蓋草); tiẽn-kài(墊蓋).

**thaw**, sng-soh siau-iêⁿ(霜雪消融).

**theatre**, hì(戲). *stage of*, hì-thâi(戲臺); hì-pêⁿ(戲棚). *to go to the*, thóiⁿ-hì(睇戲). *theatricals*, tsò-hì(做戲).

**theft**, thau-khie̍h-mue̍h(偷挈物); thau-tãu(偷盜); tãu-chhiap(盜竊); thau-chhiap(偷竊).

**theme**, tôi-ma̍k(題目). *to give out a*, tshut-tôi(出題); tshut-tôi-thâu(出題頭).

**then**, jiên-ãu(然後); ãu(後); chiũ(就); chiàⁿ(正). *at that time*, tng-sî(當時); hṳ́-tsûn(許陣); hṳ́-sî(彼時); hṳ́-hûe(許回); hṳ́-tsûn-mue̍h(彼陣物).

**thence**, tshông-hṳ́-kò(從許塊); iû-hṳ́-kò(由許塊).

**there**, tõ-hṳ́-kò(在許塊); tõ-hṳ́ kha--thâu(在許骹頭); tõ-hièⁿ-thâu(在向頭); tõ-hṳ́-pôiⁿ(在許爿). *there are*, ũ(有). *there are not*, bô(無); m̄-chêng-ũ(毋曾有). *thereabouts*, tõ-hṳ́ tsôiⁿ-ãu(在彼前後); tõ-hṳ́ lîn-kṳ̃n(在彼鄰近); tõ-hṳ́ tsó-iũ(在彼左右); tsha-m̄-to(差毋多); tsua̍h-m̄-ũa(絀毋活).

**therefore**, só-íⁿ(所以); kù-tshṳ́(故此); in-tshṳ́(因此); in-tì(因致); uân-tì(緣致).

**thermometer**, hân-sú-tsam(寒暑針).

**these**, chí-kâi(此個); chí-tsùaⁿ-kâi〔〕; chí-chiàⁿ-kâi〔〕; chí-che̍k-khài(此一塊).

**they**, i(伊); in(𪜶); hṳ́-chiàⁿ kâi-nâng〔〕.

**thick**, kãu(厚); ba̍t(密). *(consistency)*, kṳ̍t(朒).

**thicket**, chhì-phè(刺帕); chhì-nâⁿ-phè(刺藍帕); chhiū-nâⁿ(樹籃).

**thief**, tsha̍t(賊); tsha̍t-bé(賊馬). *thievish*, tshṳ́-tsha̍t(鼠賊); tsa̍t-kiáⁿ(賊囝). see THEFT.

**thigh**, tōa-thúi(大腿); thúi-thâu(骹腿). *bone*, thúi-thâu-kut(腿頭骨).

**thimble**, pòu-tsóiⁿ(布指); phûe-tsóiⁿ(皮指); tâng-tsóiⁿ(銅指).

**thin**, po̍h(薄); so(疏); so-po̍h(疏薄); chhieh(尺); kà(較); hi(稀); lang(郎); sán(㾪). *congee*, chhieh-mûeⁿ(淖糜); kà-mûeⁿ(漖糜).

**thing**, mue̍h(物); mue̍h-kiãⁿ(物件). *no such thing*, bô-chí-kâi chhêng-lí(無此個情理). *how many things*, jie̍h-tsōi kiãⁿ-mue̍h(若㩼件物).

**think**, siẽⁿ(想); liãm(念); sṳ-siẽⁿ(思想); sṳ-liãm(思念); phah-sǹg(拍算); pheⁿ-phah〔〕. *of one*, kì-liãm(記念). *I rather think so*, káⁿ-sĩ(敢是); iau-káⁿ-sĩ chièⁿ-seⁿ(要敢是此樣生); káⁿ-ũ(敢有). *highly of one*, thóiⁿ-tõng(睇重); kùi-tõng(貴重). *not worth thinking of*, mín-khùa-sim(免掛心). *I thought (erroneously)*, uá kâu-kiè〔〕; khue-tiāⁿ〔〕; sah-tsò〔〕.

**third**, tõiⁿ-saⁿ(第三).

**thirsty**, âu ta(喉灱). *to assuagethirst*, chí-khuah(止渴); kói-khuah(解渴); chí-âu(止喉); zũn-âu(潤喉).

**this**, chí(此); chí-kâi(此個); tshṳ́(此); chiá-kâi(者個). *year*, kin-nîⁿ(今年); kim-nîⁿ(今年); hīn-nîⁿ(現年); pńg-nîⁿ(本年); chí-nîⁿ(此年). *morning*, kim-tsá(今早); mn̂g-khí(眠起); mn̂g-khí-tsá(眠起早). *day*, kim-ji̍t(今日); kiáⁿ-ji̍t(今旦日); hīn-ji̍t(現日); pńg-ji̍t(本日).

**thong**, phûe-tòa(皮帶).

**thorax**, heng-tsôiⁿ(胸前); sim-kuaⁿ(心肝); sim-kuaⁿ-thâu(心肝頭); heng-kuaⁿ-thâu(胸肝頭).

**thorn**, chhì(刺). *thorny*, seⁿ-chhì(生刺). *to be pricked by a*, chhiah-tie̍h-chhì(赤着刺).

**thoroughfare**, thong-lōu(通路). *no (a blind alley)*, khu̍t-thâu-hāng〔〕.

**thoroughly**, tsa̍p-hun(十分); tshûan(全). *learned*, thong-thiet(通徹); thàu-thiet(透徹).

**though**, sui(雖); sui-jiên(雖然); sui-sĩ(雖是). *though...still*, sui-jiên(雖然)... huân-liáu(還了). *even though*, tsòng(縱); tsòng-jiên(縱然).

**thought**, siẽⁿ-thâu(想頭); liãm-thâu(念頭); sṳ-liãm(思念); ì-sṳ̀(意思). *thoughtful*, chhim-siẽⁿ(深想); ién-lṳ̃(遠慮); chhim-sṳ ién-lṳ̃(深思遠慮). *thoughtless*, m̄-tsai-siẽⁿ(毋知想); bõi-siẽⁿ(袂想); thien-thien(天天). see THINK.

**thousand**, tshoiⁿ(千); che̍k-tshoiⁿ(一千). *by thousands and tens of thousands*, káng-tshoiⁿ káng-būan(講千講萬).

**thread**, sùaⁿ(線). *silk*, si-sùaⁿ(絲線). *gold*, kim-sùaⁿ(金線). *to (a needle)*, tshng-tsam(川針); tshuan-tsam(川針). *to (cash)*, tshng-chîⁿ(川錢).

**threaten**, kiaⁿ-heh(驚嚇); kiaⁿ-tie̍h-nâng(驚着人); heh-kiaⁿ-nâng(嚇驚人).

**three**, saⁿ(三). *three-ply rope*, saⁿ-kóu-soh(三股索). *three-cornered*, saⁿ-kak(三角). *thrice*, saⁿ-hûe(三回); saⁿ-pái(三擺); saⁿ-tshṳ̀(三次); saⁿ-hãng(三項); saⁿ-tńg(三轉); saⁿ-ē(三下); saⁿ-tsau(三遭).

**thresh**, phah-tiũ(拍稻); phah-chhek(拍粟). *threshing tub*, sut-tháng(摔桶). *ladder of ditto*, sut-tháng-thui(摔桶梯). *mat enclosing ditto*, sut-tháng-tiãm(摔桶簟); sut-tháng-phâng(摔桶帆); sut-tháng-ûi(摔桶圍); sut-tháng-chia(摔桶遮). *threshing floor*, hue-tiâⁿ(灰埕); chhek-tiâⁿ(粟埕); chhek-tiêⁿ(粟場).

**threshold**, mn̂g-tõiⁿ(門第).

**thrifty**, séⁿ-ēng(省用); khiãm(儉); khiãm-ēng(儉用); tsat-ēng(節用); ũ-tsat-tōu(有節度).

**thrive**, heng-sẽng(興盛); mõng-sẽng(茂盛).

**throat**, âu(喉); âu-lêng(喉嚨). *cut one's*, kṳ̀-âu(鋸喉). *sore*, âu-lêng thiàⁿ(喉嚨痛).

**throne**, *imperial*, kim-lûan-tōiⁿ(金鑾殿); lêng-ūi(龍位); tãi-pó(大寶); thiⁿ-ūi(天位). *royal*, uâng-ūi(王位); tsō-ūi(座位). *to ascend the*, teng-ki(登基); teng-ūi(登位); chiet-ūi(即位); tsõ-ūi(坐位). *to usurp the*, tshùan-ūi(篡位).

**throng**, *a*, che̍k-khûn-nâng(一群人); nâng-mue̍h tsa̍t-tsa̍t(人物實實); nâng-mue̍h hun-hun(人物紛紛); lāu-jie̍t(鬧熱). *to throng*, oi-oi léng-léng(挨挨攆攆); oi-oi chìⁿ-chìⁿ(挨挨擠擠); sie-chìⁿ sie-ko̍ih(相擠相夾); sie-oi sie-léng(相挨相攆).

**throttle**, liū-âu〔〕; liū-âu tẽⁿ-chi̍h〔〕; tẽⁿ-âu(捏喉).

**through**, thong(通); thàu(透); thàng(通). *to come through the rain*, hãm-hõu-lâi〔〕; mãuⁿ-hõu-lâi(冒雨來). *to pass through a place*, tùi-hṳ́-kò keng-kùe(對許塊經過); keng tùi-hṳ́-kò-kùe(經對許塊過). *through fire and smoke*, mãuⁿ-in tu̍t-húe〔〕.

**throw**, *to*, ka̍k(捔); sek(擲); phîn(摒); tiāu(掉); tãⁿ(擔). *away*, ka̍k-tiāu(捔掉); sek-tiāu(擲掉); hám-tiāu(撼掉); khì-tiāu(棄掉); tiu-tiāu(丟掉); lòi-tiāu(𠠍掉); phau-tiāu(拋掉). *into the water*, tâu-tsúi(投水); ka̍k-lo̍h-tsúi(捔落水). *off clothes*, thǹg-tiāu(褪掉); pak-tiāu(剝掉). *one down*, léng-pua̍h〔〕; léng-nâng tie̍h-pua̍h〔〕. *the blame on others*, keng tõ-pa̍t-nâng--sin-téng(經到別人身頂). *about*, iā-sì-tshù(播四處); phuah-múaⁿ-kò(潑滿塊). *dust on head*, tsang-sua tha̍h thâu-khak〔〕; ēng-sua thãⁿ-tõ thâu-khak〔〕. *throw up things, as bricks*, tiāu-chiẽⁿ(掉些); tiāu-kûiⁿ(掉懸). *to throw a net*, pha-mãng(拋網).

**thrust**, *into*, tshǹg(插); tshah(插); chhiah(赤); kṳ̂(鋸). *thrust through with a spear*, ēng-chhieⁿ tshǹg-thàng--kùe-khṳ̀(用槍刺通過去).

**thumb**, chhiú-tsóiⁿ-thâu(手指頭); tsóiⁿ-thâu-kong(指頭公); tsńg-thâu-kong(指頭公); tōa-tsóiⁿ(大指). *thumb-ring*, pan-chí(板指).

**thump**, tshùaⁿ(串); tûi(搥); tèng(釘).

**thunder**, lûi(雷); lûi tân(雷彈); lûi hiáng(雷響); thiⁿ-lûi(天雷); lûi tân li̍h-leh-kiè(雷陳裂叻叫); lûi phah-kiã-leh(雷拍崎叻); lûi-siaⁿ phek-le̍k(雷聲霹靂). *and lightning*, lûi tân, thiⁿ sih(雷彈天爍); lûi-tiẽn tãi-tsak(雷電大仄). *great thunder-storm*, khí-ngóu-lûi(起午雷). *the thunder-god (or thunder as a destroying agency)*, lûi-kong(雷公). *killed in thunder-storm*, lûi khà-sí(雷拍死); lûi khà, húe sie(雷扣火燒). *thunder-bolt*, lûi-kong-tsãm(雷公斬).

**Thursday**, lói-pài-sì(禮拜四); pài-sì(拜四).

**thus**, chièⁿ-seⁿ(此樣生); àn-chièⁿ-seⁿ(按此樣生); àn-chièⁿ(按此樣).

**thwart**, nge̍k nâng-kâi-ì(逆人个意); nûaⁿ-tsó(軟阻); tsó-chí(阻指).

**tibia**, kha-tâng-kut(骹銅骨); kha-liâm-kut(骹臁骨).

**ticket**, *pawn*, hui(票); hui-kiáⁿ(飛囝); tǹg-phiè(當票); tǹg-hui(當飛). *passenger's*, tsûn-hui(船飛); tsûn-toaⁿ(船單); tsûn-phiè(船票).

**tickle**, niauⁿ(鳥); niauⁿ-chiẽⁿ(鳥上). *(one's side)*, niauⁿ koh-tang-ẽ(鳥閣當下). *(the soles of one's feet)*, niauⁿ-kha-tói(鳥骹底).

**tide**, tiê-tsúi(潮水); lâu-tsúi(流水). *full*, lâu-tsúi tĩⁿ(流水漲); lâu-tsúi pá(流水飽). *flood*, nâm-lâu(南流); ji̍p-lâu(入流). *ebb*, khó-lâu(洘流); pak-lâu(北流). *spring-tide*, tōa-lâu-tsúi(大流水). *neap-tide*, sié-lâu-tsúi(小流水). *turning*, lâu tńg(流轉). *go with the*, kúaⁿ-lâu-tsúi(趕流水). *favourable*, sũn-lâu(順流); kúaⁿ-lâu(趕流); ha̍h-lâu(合流). *adverse*, nge̍k-lâu(逆流); thêⁿ-lâu(坦流). *sail against*, tu-lâu(豬流).

**tidings**, sie-sit(消息); sin-bũn(新聞); sìn-sek(信色); sie-sek(消息).

**tie**, pa̍k(縛); kat(結); khún(捆); sǹg(算); khún-pa̍k(捆縛). *a knot*, thám-khat(毯刻); kat-khat(結刻). *a hard knot*, thám-sí-kat(毯死結); kat-sí-khat(結死刻). *a loop knot*, thám-ua̍h-khat(毯活刻). *very hard and fast*, sǹg-kín(算緊). *more loosely*, pa̍k-khùaⁿ(縛寬); tháu-lēng(㪗冗). *together*, pa̍k tsò-che̍k-ē(縛做蜀下).

**tier**, *one*, che̍k-tsâng(一層). *in tiers*, che̍k-tsâng che̍k-tsâng(一層一層).

**tiger**, hóuⁿ(虎); lãu-hóuⁿ(老虎); niãuⁿ-hóuⁿ(貓虎).

**tiffin**, tiám-sim(點心); chia̍h-ji̍t-tàu(食日晝).

**tight**, kín(緊); ân(緊). *to draw*, túi-ân-ân〔〕.

**tile**, hiã(瓦); tshù-hiã(厝瓦). *semi-cylindrical*, hiã-tâng(瓦銅); hiã-thâng(瓦堂). *with hole for skylight*, thiⁿ-thàng-hiã(天通瓦). *a tile-work*, hiã-iê(瓦窯). *to put on a roof*, khàm-hiã(蓋瓦). *glazed*, chheⁿ-hiã(青瓦). *for eaves (with points turned down)*, hiã-tâng-thâu(瓦銅頭).

**till**, *to (the ground)*, tsoh-tshân-hn̂g(作田園); chèng-tsoh(種作); keⁿ-tsoh(耕作); keⁿ-tshân(耕田); ku̍t-tshân(掘田). *till (until)*, kàu(到); chì(至); thãi(待); ki̍p(及). *don't you go away till he comes*, i-būe-lâi lṳ́ chhiáⁿ-būe-khṳ̀(伊未來汝請未去); lṳ́ tie̍h-tán i-lâi chiàⁿ-hó-khṳ̀(汝着等伊來正好去). *the tide will flow till the third watch*, lâu ji̍p kàu-saⁿ-keⁿ chiàⁿ-khó(流入到三更正可).

**tiller**, *of boat*, tõa-gê(大牙); tõa-pêⁿ(大平).

**timber**, sam-sāi(杉放); sam-liāu(杉料); tshâ-sāi(柴放); ba̍k-liāu(木料). *merchant*, khui-sam-phòu(開杉舖); khui-sam-chhiáng(開杉廠); khui-sam-hâng(開杉行); tshâ-sāi-phòu(柴放舖).

**time**, sî(時); sî-hāu(時候). *at that*, tng-sî(當時); hṳ́-sî(彼時); hṳ́--kâi sî-hāu(彼個時候); tng-khî-sî(當期時). *what is the*, ũ-sĩ-mih sî-sîn(有是乜時辰); kúi-tiám-cheng(幾點鐘). *at what*, tî-sî(底時); sĩ-mih sî-hāu(是乜時候). *have no*, m̄-ôiⁿ(毋閒); bô-ôiⁿ(無閒). *to fix a*, tiāⁿ-khî(定期); tiāⁿ-tie̍h ji̍t-chí(定着日子); ieh-tiāⁿ ji̍t-khî(約定日期). *at any*, put-lũn tî-sî(不論底時); m̄-lũn sĩ-mih sî-hāu(毋論是乜時候). *when the time comes*, thãi sî-hāu kàu(待時候到). *in time*, bõi-mān(袂慢); hù--tie̍h(副着). *not in time*, hù-m̄-tie̍h(副毋着). *time flies*, sî-ji̍t zû-so(時日如梭), kuang-im sṳ̃-chìⁿ(光陰似箭). *in the time of Confucius*, tng Khóng-tsṳ́ kâi-sî-hāu(當孔子个時候); Khóng-tsṳ́ tiâng-sî(孔子當時). *another*, ẽ-ji̍t(下日); ẽ-sî(下時). *a long*, kú(久). *a short*, chiãm-sî(暫時). *any time wil do*, bô-lũn tiâng-sî tou-hó(無論誰時都好); put-khu tî-kâi sî-hāu tou-hó(不拘底个時候都好); sûi-piẽn tî-kâi sî-hāu tou-hó(隨便底个時候都好). *three times*, saⁿ-pái(三擺); saⁿ-tshṳ̀(三次); saⁿ-hãng(三項); saⁿ-hûe(三回); saⁿ-tsúi(三水). *many times*, ē-ē(下下); sî-sî(時時); lú-lú(屢屢); lú-tshṳ̀(屢次). *ten times better*, iâⁿ-kùe tsa̍p-pũe(贏過十倍). *timely*, ha̍h-sî(合時); tùi-sî(對時); tng-sî(當時); tú-tiám(堵點). *time-serving*, sûi-sî-pièn(隨時變).

**timid**, bô-táⁿ(無膽); ùi-thâu ùi-búe(畏頭畏尾); tham-seⁿ phàⁿ-sí(貪生怕死); kiaⁿ-seⁿ kiaⁿ-sí(驚生驚死).

**tin**, pe̍h-thih(白鐵). *(pewter)*, siah(錫). *tin-foil*, siah-po̍h(錫薄). *tin-smith*, pe̍h-thih sai-pẽ(白鐵司阜); phah-siah sai-pẽ(拍錫司阜).

**tinder**, húe-hiàⁿ(火向); lo(咯); húe-bûe(火煤); tsúa-bûa(紙磨); tsúa-ín(紙引). *box*, húe-to-a̍p(火刀盒); húe-hiàⁿ-a̍p(火向盒).

**tinge**, jiám-sek(染色); níⁿ(染); làm(坔); î-sek(移色).

**tinkling**, tin-tiang-kiè(顛滇叫).

**tinsel**, *flowers*, kim-hue(金花).

**tip**, *of nose*, phīⁿ-thâu(鼻頭); phīⁿ-tsún(鼻準); tsún-thâu(準頭). *of finger*, chhiú-tsóiⁿ-thâu(手指頭). *of arrow*, chìⁿ-búe(箭尾); chìⁿ-ne̍k(箭肉); chìⁿ-chiam(箭尖). *to stand on tiptoe*, lèng-khí-kha khiã(冷起骹徛).

**tipsy**, tsùi(醉); chia̍h-chiú-tsùi(食酒醉); tsùi-chiú(醉酒). *slightly*, ba-bun-tsùi(貓蚊醉); mah-moh-tsùi(嬤麼醉).

**tired**, he̍k(乏); khùn(睏); khùn-tõaⁿ(睏惰); khùn-kũan(睏倦); khùn-he̍k(睏乏); phî-kũan(疲倦); phî-khùn(疲睏); phî-tõaⁿ(疲惰); kha sng*(腳痠), chhiú nńg(手軟). *very tired with walking*, kiâⁿ-kàu-hẽng(行到悻). *to be tired of*, iàm(厭); ùi(畏); lóu(惱); màiⁿ(勿). *tiresome*, khṳt--nâng seⁿ-iàm(乞人生厭); tshūa-nâng-ùi(𤆬人畏).

**tithe**, thiu tsa̍p-hūn tsṳ-che̍k(抽十分之一); tsa̍p-hūn thiu-che̍k(十分抽一); tsa̍p tshú-khî-che̍k(十取其一); tsa̍p-hūn tshú-che̍k(十分取一); ke-it-thiu(加一抽).

**title**, *official*, kuaⁿ-hâm(官銜); cheh-hâm(職銜). *to confer a*, hong-chiak(風爵). *title-page*, phiau-thâu(標頭); chheh-phiau(冊標). *to write the title on the edge of a book*, siá-chheh-kha(寫冊骹).

**tittle**, see JOT.

**to**, kàu(到). *speak to him*, kāng-i-tàⁿ(共伊呾). *bitten to death*, kã-sí(咬死). *to old age*, chì-kàu-lãu(直到老).

**toad**, kap-pô(蛤婆).

**toast**, *to*, pek(迫); pūe(焙). *bread*, pūe-mīⁿ-pau(焙麵包); pek-mīⁿ-pau(煏麵包).

**tobacco**, hun(薰). *leaves*, hun-hie̍h(薰葉). *prepared*, se̍k-hun(熟薰). *pipe*, hun-tâng(薰筒). *to smoke*, chia̍h-hun(食薰); chia̍h-se̍k-hun(食熟薰).

**today**, kim-ji̍t(今日); kiáⁿ-ji̍t(今旦日); pńg-ji̍t(本日); hīn-ji̍t(現日); tshṳ́-ji̍t(此日); chiet-ji̍t(即日).

**toe**, kha-tsóiⁿ(骹鏟). *the big*, kha-tsńg-thâu-kong(骹指頭公); kha-tsóiⁿ-thâu(骹鏟頭).

**together**, tsò-pû(做伙); tâng(同); kāng(共). *to walk*, tsò-pû-kiâⁿ(做伙行). *have anything together (or in common)*, sie-kāng(相同).

**toil**, lâu-khóu(勞苦); lâu-la̍t(勞力); bûa-lâu(磨勞); bûa(磨); bûa-la̍t(磨力); khóu-sin(苦身); sin-khṳ̂n(身勤); khṳ̂n-lâu(勤勞). *toilsome*, lân(難); kan-khóu(艱苦).

**toilet**, *to make one's*, tá-pàn(打扮); siu-tsuang(修妝); tsuang-pàn(裝扮). *table*, tsng-thâi(妝臺); kiàⁿ-thâi(鏡臺); kiàⁿ-tshn̂g(鏡床).

**token**, hō(號); piáu-kì(表記). *secret*, àm-hō(暗號).

**tolerable**, nãiⁿ-tit-khṳ̀(耐得去); nãiⁿ-tit-kùe(耐得過); lún-tit-kùe(忍得過). *tolerably good*, õi-tsò-tit(會做得); tshó-lia̍k tsò-tit(粗略做得); õi--nín tsò-tit(會恁做得); khó-íⁿ tsò-tit(可也做得); chiang-chiũ tsò-tit(將就做得).

**tolerate**, jĩm--nâng khṳ̀-tsò(忍人去做); bô-só-kìm(無所禁).

**toll**, kùe-lōu-chîⁿ(過路錢); kùe-hiàng-chîⁿ(過餉錢).

**tomato**, âng-sãi-kiáⁿ(紅柿囝).

**tomb**, phûn(墳); phûn-mõⁿ(墳墓); suaⁿ(山). *to worship at the tombs*, pài-phûn(拜墳); kùe-tsúa(過紙); chì-sàu(祭掃); chì-phûn(祭墳); teh-tsúa(壓紙).

**tomorrow**, mùaⁿ-tsá(明朝); mùaⁿ-khí(明起); màⁿ-khí(明旦起); mêng-ji̍t(明日). *day after*, ãu--ji̍t(後日). *two days after*, tōa-ãu--ji̍t(大後日).

**tone**, siaⁿ-im(聲音). *the eight tones*, poih-im(八音).

**tongs**, thih-kîⁿ(鐵鉗); thih-khîⁿ(鐵鉗); thih-tṳ̄(鐵箸).

**tongue**, chi̍h(舌). *tip of*, chi̍h-thâu(舌頭). *to put out the*, chi̍h tshun--tshut-lâi(舌伸出來). *to scrape the*, kueh-chi̍h(刮舌). *tongue scraper*, chi̍h-kueh(舌刮). *mother-tongue*, pńg-tī-ūe(本地話); pńg-thôu-ūe(本頭話); thôu-im(頭音).

**tonic**, *a*, póu-ie̍h(補藥); póu-pî-ie̍h(補脾藥); póu-khì-kueh(補氣郭).

**tonight**, kim-mêⁿ(今夜); mêⁿ-hng(夜昏); kim mńg(今晚); kim-siau(今宵).

**too**, *many*, khah-tsōi(較㩼). *large*, khah-tōa(較大); khah-kùe-tōa(較過大). *much*, khah-ke(較加); khah-kùe-thâu(較過頭). *young*, hûan-iáu-chíⁿ(還要稚); khah-chíⁿ(較稚). *ripe*, kùe-se̍k(過熟). *do not be too sad*, màiⁿ-khah kùe-lṳ̃(勿較過慮); mín-ēng hièⁿ-kùe-lṳ̃(免用向過慮).

**tools**, ke-húe(家伙); khì-kũ(器具); khì-mue̍h(器物).

**tooth**, *toothache*, khí thiàⁿ(齒痛). *toothbrush*, khí-sueh(齒刷). *toothpick*, khí-thak(齒剔). *toothpowder*, khí-hún(齒粉). see TEETH.

**top**, téng(頂); thâu(頭); mīn(面); téng-mīn(頂面); chiēⁿ-mīn(上面); mīn-chiēⁿ(面上). *of a hill*, suaⁿ-téng(山頂). *topmost*, téng-téng(頂頂); siãng-téng(上頂). *topsy-turvy*, tin-tò-thâu(顛倒頭); tin-tò-thâu-chèng(顛倒頭正).

**top**, *a*, hâm-lâm-su̍t(銜瓏術). *to spin a*, phah-hâm-lâm-su̍t(拍銜瓏術).

**torch**, húe-pé(火把); húe-nāⁿ(火爁).

**torment**, khóu-tshó(苦楚); thiàⁿ-tshó lân-tng(痛楚零當). *to*, kia-khóu(加苦).

**torrent**, kip-tsúi(急水); hûeⁿ-lâu(橫流); suaⁿ-thuaⁿ(山灘).

**tortoise**, ku(龜). *tortoise-shell*, ku-khak(玳瑁); ta-pūe(玳瑁).

**tortuous**, i-uan khih-khek(伊彎潔曲); uan-uan khek-khek(彎彎曲曲).

**torture**, *to examine with*, kháu-phah(考拍); kui(規); kui-mn̄g(規問).

**toss**, *up*, tiāu-khí(掉起). *to catch in the hand a thing that has been tossed up*, sah(接). *to toss about*, zũan-tiāu(任掉). *to toss in pain*, pūi-pua̍h(吠跋).

**total**, *the*, kāng-kòi(共計); tsóng-sǹg ha̍h-kòi(總算合計); tsóng-kat(總結); tsóng-sǹg(總算). *totally*, chĩn(盡); kan-chẽng(乾淨); liáu-liáu(了了); tsò-che̍k-ē(做蜀下); tsa̍p-hun(十分).

**totter**, *to*, bái-a-bái(擺阿擺); uái-a-uái(歪亞歪); kiâⁿ-lōu iâu-hiám(行路搖險); àiⁿ-pua̍h(愛跋); àiⁿ-tó(愛倒).

**touch**, *to*, thãng(動); mông(摸). *don't touch it*, chhiú màiⁿ-thãng(手勿動); chhiú màiⁿ-tiaⁿ--tie̍h(手勿撞着). *touch me not (flower)*, tsńg-kah-hue(指佮花). *touchstone*, chhì-kim-chie̍h(試金石). *touchhole*, húe-mn̂g(火門); chhèng-mn̂g(銃門); húe-hĩⁿ-khang(火耳空).

**touchy**, chheⁿ-mīn-hóuⁿ(青面虎).

**tough**, zūn(韌); ngẽ(硬).

**tow**, *to (as one ship another)*, tõa-tsûn(舵船); tshūa-tsûn(𤆬船). *to (as men pullling boat with rope)*, po̍ih-tsûn(拔船); khan-tsûn(牽船); thua-tsûn(拖船); mán-tsûn(挽船).

**towards**, hiàng(向); niàⁿ(向). *fled towards the city*, mōⁿ-siâⁿ tsáu(望城走).

**towel**, kṳn(巾); pòu(布); mīn-pòu(面布); e̍k-pòu(浴布).

**tower**, thah(塔); mōⁿ-lâu(望樓).

**town**, siâⁿ(城); siâⁿ-ip(城邑); pou-thâu(埠頭). *(with fixed market days)*, hṳ-chhĩ(墟市).

**toy**, ang-kiáⁿ(尪囝); thit-thô-mue̍h(佚佗物).

**trace**, *a*, tsong-chiah(蹤跡); hûn-chiah(痕跡); iáⁿ-chiah(影跡). *to trace*, chhîm-tui tsong-chiah(尋追蹤跡). *to trace writing (on thin paper)*, biê-jī(描字); biê-keh(描格); biê-thoih(描代).

**track**, *a*, lōu(路). *of a wheel*, chhia-kau-khut(車高屈); chhia-lōu(車路). *trackless*, bô-tsong bô-chiah(無蹤無跡).

**track**, *to (a boat)*, po̍ih-tsûn(拔船). see TOW.

**tract**, *or region*, tī-hng(地方).

**tract**, *or treatise*, khǹg-sì-bûn(勸世文); siẽn-tsṳ(善書); tsa̍p-chheh(雜冊).

**trade**, seng-lí(生理). *to*, tsò-seng-lí(做生理); bói-bōi(買賣). *stagnation of*, hùe-mue̍h m̄-siau(貨物毋銷).

**tradition**, kóu-thûan(古傳). *oral*, kháu-thûan(口傳).

**traffic**, seng-lí(生理). *great*, jie̍t(熱); lāu-jie̍t(鬧熱).

**tragedy**, chhiet-hì(切戲); khóu-hì(苦戲); tshám-tshut(慘出); tshám-chhêng-hì(慘情戲); khóu-tshut(苦出).

**trail**, *to*, thua(拖); thua-thôu(拖塗).

**train**, *to*, kà(教); kà-io̍k(教育). *soldiers*, tshau-piaⁿ(操兵); tshau-liēn-piaⁿ(操練兵); tshau-piaⁿ liēn-tsut(操兵練卒).

**train**, *a*, kṳn-pan(筋班); sûi-tsõng(隨從); kṳn-sûi(跟隨).

**trait**, *a good*, che̍k-tn̄g hó-sim(一段好心); che̍k-kiãⁿ-sṳ̄ hó-tshú(一件事好取).

**traitor**, bōi-kok(賣國); kōi-kun(易軍); kan-chhîn(奸臣); bōi-làn kun-uâng(賣爛君王); tsò-sùaⁿ(做線).

**trample**, *on*, tshau-ta̍h(糟蹋); lūn-ta̍h(蹂踏). *to death*, ta̍h-sí(踏死); lūn-sí(蹂死). *on the law*, ma̍k bô-uâng-chiang(目無王章).

**trance**, *to fall into a*, sim-sîn iû tõ-mu̍eh-siãng hṳ́-gūa(心神油在物上許外).

**tranquillity**, thài-phêng(太平); uaⁿ-chẽⁿ(安靜); phêng-an(平安); phêng-chẽⁿ(平靜). *tranquillize*, phêng(平); uaⁿ-ùe(安慰).

**transact**, *business*, phōiⁿ-sṳ̄(辦事); lí-sṳ̄(理事); lí-sṳ̄-bũ(理事務).

**transcribe**, tshau(抄); tshau-siá(抄寫); piâⁿ(平); piâⁿ--kùe-lâi(平過來).

**transfer**, thûan(傳); siá--khṳt-nâng(寫乞人); kau-hù(交付). *(as burden or responsibility)*, seng-thiau〔〕. *(to make a mutual exchange of office)*, seng-thiâu〔〕; thiâu-ūaⁿ(調換).

**transform**, pièn(變); pièn-hùe(變化); pièn-tńg(變轉); pièn-ūaⁿ(變換).

**transgress**, huãm-huap(犯法); kùe-huãm(過犯). *transgression*, tsũe(罪); kùe-sit(過失).

**transitory**, chiãm-sî(暫時); bô-kú(無久).

**translate**, huan-e̍k(翻譯); e̍k(譯). *from book style into colloquial*, sueh-tsṳ(說書); kói-sueh(解說); sueh-tsò pe̍h-ūe(說做白話). *a translator or interpreter (not of books)*, thong-sṳ̄(通事); hûe-ūe(會話).

**translucent**, ũ-mûiⁿ-kuang thàu-kùe-khṳ̀(有微光透過去).

**transmigration**, *of souls*, lûn-hûe(輪回); tsúan-lûn(轉輪).

**transmit**, thûan--lo̍h-lâi(傳落來); kià(寄).

**transparent**, õi-kng(光通); õi-thàu-kng(會透光); khong-mêng(光通); kng thàu-tit-kùe(光透得過).

**transplant**, súa-chèng(徙種). *rice*, pòu-tshân(布田); pòu-tiũ(布稻).

**transport**, *as a criminal*, mông-khién(朦遣); mông-tshong-kun(朦衝軍); tshong-kun mông-liû(衝軍朦流). *to condemn to transportation*, ngí-liû(議流); phōiⁿ-tshut-mn̂g(辮出門).

**transpose**, thiâu-ūaⁿ(調換); sie-ūaⁿ(相換); jī-ke î-tī(二家移地); jī-ke thiâu-e̍k(二家調易).

**transverse**, hûeⁿ(橫).

**trap**, *for rats*, niáu-tshṳ́-tat(貓鼠撻); thih-ngiau(鐵貓); tek-ngiau(竹貓); niáu-tshṳ́-lâng(溺此籠). *for tigers*, hóuⁿ-lô(虎牢). *a snare*, khou-thàu(箍透). *trap-door*, lâu-chéⁿ-mn̂g(流井門).

**travail**, seⁿ-súaⁿ(生產); seⁿ-kiáⁿ(生囝); kāng-a-nôuⁿ(共亞孥); hun-mién(分娩). *sore*, lân-súaⁿ(難產); oh-seⁿ(僫生).

**travel**, kiâⁿ(行); kiâⁿ-lōu(行路); tshut-gūa(出外); kheh-iû sì-hng(客遊四方).

**trawl**, khan-tsan(牽罾).

**tray**, tshâ-pûaⁿ(柴盤); tháng-pûaⁿ(桶盤). *for writing instruments*, īⁿ-pûaⁿ(硯盤).

**tread**, *on*, kha ta̍h(骹踏); lūn-ta̍h(蹂踏).

**treacherous**, kan-ak(奸惡); kan-hiông(奸雄); sit-sìn(失信).

**treacle**, thn̂g-tsúi(糖水).

**treason**, mông-húan(謀反). see TRAITOR.

**treasure**, tshâi-pe̍h(財帛); kim-ngṳ̂n(金銀); ngṳ̂n-niéⁿ(銀兩); chîⁿ-tshâi(錢財). *house*, khòu-pâng(庫房); ngṳ̂n-khòu(銀庫); ngṳ̂n-pâng(銀房).

**treat**, *to*, thãi(待); khúan-thãi(款待). *well*, kãu-thãi(厚待); hó-khúan-thãi(好款待). *ill*, po̍h-thãi(薄待); khin-thãi(輕待). *impartially*, bô-i bô-lṳ́ thãi-nâng(無伊無汝待人).

**treaty**, ieh(約); hûa-ieh(和約); tiâu-ieh(條約). *the terms of a*, ieh-tiâu(約條). *to make a*, li̍p-ieh(立約); sêng-ieh(成約); tiāⁿ-ieh(定約). *to discuss a*, ngí-ieh(議約). *to violate a*, pũe-ieh(背約); sit-ieh(失約).

**treble**, *(folds)*, saⁿ-têng(三重). *(strands)*, saⁿ-kóu(三股); saⁿ-pũe(三倍).

**tree**, chhiū(樹); chhiū-ba̍k(樹木). *a*, che̍k-tsâng-chhiū(一叢樹). *leaves*, chhiū-hie̍h(樹葉). *branches*, chhiū-ki(樹枝).

**tremble**, khiū〔〕; tòng(凍). *with fear*, kiaⁿ kàu-tõ-tòng(驚到在凍); kiâⁿ-kàu-khiū〔〕; kiaⁿ kàu kha-chhiú nóiⁿ-nóiⁿ-sih〔〕.

**trench**, kau(溝); tsúi-kau(水溝).

**trespass**, huãm-tsũe(犯罪); kùe-sit(過失); kùe-huãm(過犯); huãm-kùe(犯過).

**Triad**, *society*, sam-to-hũe(三合會).

**trials**, see TRY. *to undergo*, keng-chhì-liēn(經試煉).

**triangle**, saⁿ-kak-hêng(三角形).

**tribe**, tso̍k(族); tsong-phài(宗派); tsong-chiⁿ(宗支); chiⁿ-phài(支派); lūi(類); chéng(種); chéng-lūi(種類); chéng-tsa̍t(種族).

**tribunal**, *before a*, thâi-tsôiⁿ(臺前); ùaⁿ-tsôiⁿ(案前). *ascend*, chiẽⁿ-tn̂g(上堂).

**tribute**, *to pay*, chìn-kòng(進貢); na̍p-kòng(納貢). *to pay to the emperor*, kòng huâng-tì(貢皇帝). *articles of*, chìn-kòng kâi pín-mue̍h(進貢个品物).

**trick**, *a*, kòi(計); tsà-kòi(詐計); ngũi-kòi(偽計). *full of tricks*, tsōi-sim-sṳ̄(㩼心事). *juggler's tricks*, tsò-pa-hì(做把戲); chia-ngán-huap(遮眼法); sái-seⁿ-huap(使生法).

**trifle**, *to*, sńg(耍); bú-lõng(舞弄). *not to be trifled with*, m̄-hó-sńg(毋好耍). *a trifle*, sié-sṳ̄(小事); sié-khó kâi-sṳ̄(小可个事); mûiⁿ-mua̍t kâi-sṳ̄(微末个事); mûiⁿ-mua̍t kâi-mue̍h(微末个物). *(said of a present made by oneself)*, kâi-ì-sṳ̀ tiāⁿ-tiāⁿ(個意思定定).

**trigger**, chiáu-kiáⁿ(鳥囝). *to pull the*, peⁿ-chiáu-kiáⁿ(斑鳥囝).

**trim**, *to (a lamp)*, kiah-teng(揭燈); thie-teng(挑燈).

**Trinity**, Saⁿ-ūi che̍k-thói(三位一體).

**trip**, *to*, *thefoot*, that--tie̍h-kha(踢着骹); sit-kha(失骹). *and fall*, that-pua̍h(踢拔). *on a rope*, khṳt-soh kûe-pua̍h(乞索絆跋); khṳt-soh lau-pua̍h(乞索撈跋).

**tripe**, gû-tõu(牛肚); gû-chheh-peh(牛冊伯).

**triturate**, ngóiⁿ(研); ngóiⁿ-hún(研粉); ngóiⁿ-bua̍h(研末); bûa-hún(磨粉); lûi-iùⁿ(擂幼).

**triumph**, *over enemies*, thâi-iâⁿ(刣贏); chièn-sèng(戰勝); sèng-chiãng(勝仗).

**trivial**, bô-siang-kan sṳ̄(無相干事); sié-khó-sṳ̄(小可事).

**trocar**, thàu-kńg-tsam(透管針).

**troops**, kun(軍); piaⁿ(兵); piaⁿ-ióng(軍兵).

**trooper**, bé-piaⁿ(馬兵).

**tropic**, *(of Cancer)*, jie̍t-tòa kâi-pak-hãn(熱帶个北限). *(of Capricorn)*, jie̍t-tòa kâi-lâm-hãn(熱帶个南限).

**trot**, pháu-bé tsho̍k-tsho̍k-kiè(跑馬蹙蹙叫).

**trouble**, *to*, lūi--nâng(累人); kiáu-jiáu(攪擾); hûan-lâu(煩勞). *I will trouble you*, lâu-kè(勞駕). *excuse my troubling you*, lâu--lṳ́(勞汝); lūi--lṳ́(累汝); phièn-lṳ́ hùi-sîn(騙汝費神). *troubles*, kan-khóu-sṳ̄(艱苦事). *troubled in mind*, khóu-sim(苦心); hûan-ló(煩惱); iu-būn(憂悶).

**trough**, tsô(槽); tsúi-tsô(水槽); bé-tsô(馬槽); káu-tsô(狗槽); tṳ-tsô(豬槽).

**trousers**, khòu(褲). *one pair of*, che̍k-kâi-khòu(一個褲); che̍k-kiãⁿ-khòu(一件褲); che̍k-tiâu-khòu(一條褲). *short*, khòu-kue̍h(褲橛). *to roll up the legs of*, tsah-khòu-kha(塞褲骹).

**trowel**, hue-sî(花時).

**truce**, thêng-chièn(停戰); hiah-thâi(歇臺).

**true**, chin(真); si̍t(實); chin-si̍t(真實); ũ-iáⁿ(有影); si̍t-kṳ̃(實據); chin-ũ(真有). *to one's word*, chién-ngân(踐言); ngân--tshut zûi-kiâⁿ(言出維行); zû-ieh(如約). *truly*, si̍t-tsãi(實在); kúaⁿ-jiên(果然); kúaⁿ-chin(果真); chin-si̍t(真實).

**trumpet**, kak-tâng(); hō-tâng(); haⁿ-haⁿ(). *(conch)*, pûn-pu(); ti-tâ(嘀嗒); kóu-siú(鼓手). *to blow*, pûn(歕).

**trunk**, sieⁿ(箱). *one*, che̍k-kha-sieⁿ(一骹箱). *leathern*, phûe-sieⁿ(皮箱). *of a tree*, chhiū-sin(樹身). *of elephant*, chhiẽⁿ-phīⁿ(象鼻).

**trust**, *to*, sìn(信); siang-sìn(相信). *in*, sìn(信); kõu(靠); sìn-kõu(信靠); íⁿ-kõu(倚靠); íⁿ-nãiⁿ(倚賴); i-kõu(依靠); i-uá(依倚); uá-kõu(倚靠); chiã(藉); tit-pn̄g(得飯); khùa-pn̄g(掛飯); khàu-pn̄g(靠飯); thoh-kõu(託靠). *in wealth*, sĩ-tshâi(恃財). *a trust*, só-thoh kâi-sṳ̄(所託个事); só-hù-thoh kâi-sṳ̄(所付託个事). *trustworthy*, khó-sìn(可信); hó-siang-sìn(好相信); thó-tàng(妥當).

**truth**, see TRUE. *to speak the*, tàⁿ-si̍t-ūe(呾實話). *true doctrine*, chin-lí(真理); chin-tãu(真道); chiàⁿ-tãu(正道).

**try**, chhì(試); chhì-thóiⁿ(試睇); chhì-siêⁿ(試嘗); thèng-tsãu-hùe(聽造化).

**try**, *a cause*, sím-ùaⁿ(審案); sím-mn̄g(審問); mn̄g-ùaⁿ-kiãⁿ(問案件).

**tub**, tháng(桶); kha-tháng(骹桶). *bathing*, sói-e̍k-tháng(洗浴桶); e̍k-tháng(浴桶).

**tube**, tâng(筒); kóng(管).

**tuck**, *up the trousers*, tsah-khòu-kha(塞褲骹). *the sleeves*, tsah-chhiú-ńg(塞手䘼).

**Tuesday**, lói-pài-jī(禮拜二); pài-jī(拜二).

**tumble**, *to (down)*, pua̍h-lo̍h(跋落). *off a horse*, pua̍h-lo̍h-bé(跋落馬). *a tumbler on the stage*, pha-sa-lin(趴沙輪).

**tumbler**, *glass*, po-lî-pue(玻璃杯).

**tumour**, liû(瘤); ne̍k-liû(肉瘤); hueh-liû(血瘤); lâ-liû(朥瘤); kṳn-liû(筋瘤).

**tumult**, tshàu-nãuⁿ(臭鬧); tshàu-jiáng(吵嚷); kã-kã-jiáng(咬咬嚷); jiáng-kî-ka(嚷旗膠).

**tune**, si-pán(司板); si-tiāu(司調); pán-tiāu(板調); khek-tiāu(曲調). *on high key*, kûiⁿ-tiāu(懸調). *on low key*, kẽ-tiāu(下調). *out of*, ngîm-lâi m̄-lo̍h-sì(吟來毋落四). *tuning-key*, húiⁿ(毀). *to tune a harp*, húiⁿ-khîm-sùaⁿ(毀琴線).

**tunnel**, *(cave)*, suaⁿ-tāng(山洞); *(also pitfall)*, tī-hām(地陷); tī-tãu(地道); tī-tói kâi-lōu(地底个路); tī-ẽ àm-lōu(地下暗路).

**turban**, thâu-pòu(頭布). *to put on*, khûan-thâu-pòu(權頭布); phûan-thâu-pòu(盤頭布).

**turbid**, lô(濁); nah-sap(垃圾).

**turbulent**, phû-tshàu(浮臭); pãu-tshàu-sèⁿ(暴臭性); tshàu-kip(臭急).

**turf**, tsháu-phue̍h(草皮).

**Turkey**, Thóu-zṳ́-khî(土耳其).

**turkey**, *a*, húe-koi(火雞).

**turmeric**, kieⁿ-n̂g(薑黃).

**turn**, tńg(轉); tsúan(轉); póiⁿ(反); tsũn(順); huán-tńg(反轉); póiⁿ-tńg(反轉); huan(反); húiⁿ-kùe-lâi(反過來). *revolve*, húiⁿ〔〕; hui〔〕. *the head*, hûe-thâu(回頭); u̍t-tńg-thâu(夗轉頭); u̍t-tshúa(夗歪). *right round*, hui-tńg-sin(飛轉身). *round in bed*, huan-sin(翻身); huan-lâi khah-khṳ̀〔〕; huan-kùe-lâi huan-kùe-khṳ̀(反過來反過去). *back*, tńg; tńg--lâi(轉來); hûe(回); hûe-tńg(回轉); tò-tńg(倒轉); kiâⁿ-tò-tńg(行倒轉); suân-tńg(旋轉). *over (overturn)*, léng-tó(推倒). *over (invert)*, póiⁿ-tńg(反轉); póiⁿ--kùe-lâi(反過來); póiⁿ--khí-lâi(反起來); póiⁿ-khap(反恰); póiⁿ-chhiè(反且); póiⁿ-phak(反伏); póiⁿ-lìn-tńg(反輾轉); póiⁿ-kùe hièⁿ-pôiⁿ(反過向爿); tò-póiⁿ(倒反). *inside out (as pockets)*, póiⁿ-lìn-tńg. *upside down*, tien-táu(顛倒); tìn-tò-thâu-táu(顛倒頭倒). *round (as key)*, tsũn-só-sî(轉鎖匙); húiⁿ-só-sî(反鎖匙). *a horse's head*, mán-tńg bé-thâu(挽轉碼頭); mán-bé u̍t-tńg(挽馬夗轉). *towards*, hiàng(向); niàⁿ(向); tùi(對). *the heaven turns*, thiⁿ ūn-tõng(天運動). *to turn in a lathe*, chhia(車). *to take turns in doing*, sie-lûn(相輪); sie-lûn-liû(相輪流); sie-lûn-tsò(相輪做); sie-thòi-tsò(相代做); lûn-tsúan(輪轉); lûn-thòi(輪代). *it is your turn*, lûn-tie̍h-lṳ́(輪着汝). *to turn one away from service*, sî(辭). *to turn one out*, to̍k-tshut(逐出); kúaⁿ-tshut(趕出); jiāu-tshut(尿出). *out of office*, khṳ̀-kuaⁿ(去官); thut-kuaⁿ(脫官); thut-cheh(脫職); pã-cheh(罷職). *to turn into*, tńg--tsò(轉做); pìⁿ--tsò(變做); pièn--tsò(變做).

**turnip**, tshài-thâu(菜頭).

**turnkey**, kìm-chí(禁子); kìm-tsut(禁卒).

**twang**, *of bow*, keng-hîⁿ hiáng(弓絃響). *nasal*, phīⁿ-im(鼻音); sái-phīⁿ-khang-kńg(使鼻空管).

**twilled**, siâ-bûn(斜紋).

**twine**, soh-kiáⁿ(索囝). *twine about*, tsāng-soh(贈索); tîⁿ(纏); tõa(帶).

**twinge**, tshǹg-thiàⁿ(刺痛); mán-thiàⁿ(挽痛); thiu-thiàⁿ(抽痛); tshuah-thiàⁿ(掇痛).

**twinkle**, ia̍p-ia̍p-sih(灼灼熠); iap-iap-sih(灼灼熠); i kâi-kng õi-tín-tãng(伊个光會振動). *of the eye*, nihⁿ-ma̍k(眲目); ma̍k nihⁿ(目眲). *in a twinkling*, che̍k-ma̍k-nihⁿ-kú(一目眲久).

**twins**, sang-seⁿ(雙生).

**twirl**, *to (round)*, khie̍h-tõ-hui(挈在飛). *round on one leg*, khiã che̍k-chiah-kha u̍t-lâi u̍t-khṳ̀(徛一隻骹夗來夗去).

**twist**, *to*, tsũn(捘); ká(絞). *(by rubbing with the hand)*, zûe(挼). *ropes*, ká-soh(絞索); phah-soh(拍索); tsũn-soh(捘索).

**twitch**, *to*, túi(拖); mán(挽). *twitching of the muscles*, mán-kṳn(挽筋).

**twittering**, kih-kiauh-kiè(砌角叫); chi̍h-chia̍uh-kiè(舌雀叫); chia̍uh-chia̍uh-kiè(嚼嚼叫); ki-ku-lũ-kiè(枝龜呂叫).

**two**, nõⁿ(兩); liáng(兩); sang(雙). *two-edged*, sang-pôiⁿ-lāi(雙爿利). *a two edged sword*, kiàm(劍). *two-fold*, sang-têng(雙重); nõⁿ-ha̍p(兩合); liáng-pũe(兩倍); kia-pũe(加倍); ha̍p-pũe(合倍). *you two gentlemen*, nín jī-ūi(恁二位). *kill two dogs with one stone (literally break two clods with one blow of hammer)*, che̍k-thûi khà nõⁿ-phue̍h(一槌扣廿皮).

**tympanum**, hĩⁿ-kiàⁿ(耳鏡).

**type**, *metal*, ìn-póiⁿ(印板); ua̍h-póiⁿ(活版); tâng-póiⁿ(同反); în-póiⁿ(鉛反).

**typhoon**, huang-thai(風颱).

**tyrant**, pà-uâng(霸王). *tyranny*, pà-tãu(霸道). *tyrannical*, khiâng-pà(強霸); pãu-ngia̍k(暴虐).

**tyro**, tsho-o̍h(初學); chiãm-o̍h(暫學); chheⁿ-chhiú(生手); sin-sai-pẽ(新司阜).

### U

**ubiquity**, bô-só put-tõ(無所不在); bô-só put-kàu(無所不到).

**udder**, nīⁿ-phè(奶帕).

**ugly**, iá-iēⁿ(野樣); m̄-chiâⁿ-iēⁿ(毋成樣); chhi-gî(淒疑); m̄-hó-thóiⁿ(毋好睇); iá-hêng(野行); m̄-ngiáⁿ-kuan(毋雅觀); tshou-lõu(粗陋); phí-lõu(鄙陋); chhiú-lõu(醜陋).

**ulcer**, tshng(瘡); phùa-nūaⁿ(破爛). *ulcerate*, seⁿ-tshng(生瘡); seⁿ-mîⁿ(生糜).

**ultimately**, kiáu-búe(繳尾); kàu-búe(到尾); suah-búe(煞尾); pi̍t-kéng(畢竟); tsong(終). *(sooner or later)*, khùe-mān(快慢).

**umbilicus**, tóu-tsâi(肚臍).

**umbrageous**, im-ba̍t(陰密); õi-chia-ìm(會遮蔭).

**umbrella**, hõu-sùaⁿ(雨傘); hõu-chia(雨遮). *one*, che̍k-ki hõu-sùaⁿ(一枝雨傘). *a state one*, nêⁿ-sùaⁿ(軟傘). *to open an*, khui-hõu-chia(開雨遮); hõu-chia tién-khui(雨遮展開). *to close*, hõu-sùaⁿ ha̍p-bûa(雨傘合埋).

**umpire**, tsò-kong-chhin(做公親); tong-kan-nâng(中干人); tong-kìⁿ(中見).

**unable**, bõi(袂); bô-la̍t(無力); bô-pōu(無步); bô-lêng-ûi(無能爲); put-lêng(不能); tsò-m̄-lâi(做毋來). *to sustain*, tng-m̄-khí(當毋起). *to use*, ēng m̄-pat tò-khṳ̀(用毋別倒去). *to overtake*, jiāu-m̄-tie̍h(尿毋着). *to speak*, tàⁿ-m̄-tshut(呾毋出).

**unaccountable**, m̄-tsai tsò-nîⁿ(毋知怎呢); siẽⁿ m̄-pat tò-khṳ̀(想毋別倒去).

**unaccustomed**, m̄-kùiⁿ-sìⁿ(毋慣性); chheⁿ-hūn(生分); chheⁿ-chhiú(生手).

**unadorned**, phok-si̍t(樸實); bô-hua-tshái(無花彩); bô-bûn-tshái(無文彩); bô-iām-tshái(無焰彩).

**unadulterated**, bô-sie-tsham(無相參); bô-tshàm-tsa̍p(無摻雜); chẽng(淨); tsok-siâⁿ(足成).

**unalterable**, put-e̍k(不易); bô-kói-e̍k(無改易); m̄-hó-kói(毋好改); che̍k-tiāⁿ put-e̍k(一定不易).

**unanimous**, tâng-sim(同心); tsôi-sim tsôi-ì(齊心齊意); che̍k-sim che̍k-ì(一心一意); sim-chì sie-tâng(心志相同); sim-chì che̍k-it(心志一壹).

**unanswerable**, bô-ūe hó-tùi(無話好對); à-m̄-kùe(詏毋過); m̄-hó-à(毋好詏); lân-íⁿ kiáng-piẽn(難以強辯).

**unassuming**, khiam-sùn(謙遜); khiam-sòi(謙細); tho-khiam(推謙).

**unattainable**, put-ki̍p(不及); bõi-tit-kàu(袂得到).

**unavoidable**, put-tit-íⁿ(不得已); bõi-tit-mién(袂得免); lân-mín(難免); m̄-hó-tho(毋好推); tho-m̄-khṳ̀(推毋去); bô-khóu nãiⁿ-hô(無苦奈何); bô-khó nãiⁿ-hô(無可奈何); bô-nãiⁿ-hô(無奈何); pī-m̄-kùe(避毋過); tô-pī m̄-khui(逃避毋開).

**unawares**, put-kak(不覺); hut-jiên(忽然); put-tsai put-kak(不知不覺); siẽⁿ-m̄-kàu(想毋到); liāu-m̄-kàu(料毋到); bô-ṳ̃(無預); bô-ṳ̃-pĩ(無預備).

**unbecoming**, m̄-ha̍h-sek(毋合適); m̄-sĩ-sṳ̄(毋是事); m̄-hó-thóiⁿ(毋好睇); m̄-ha̍h-huap(毋合法); ua̍t-huap(越法); huãm-sek(犯色).

**unbelief**, m̄-sìn(毋信); m̄-sìn-tshông(毋信崇).

**uncertain**, bô-tiāⁿ(無定); bô-tiāⁿ-tie̍h(無定着); bô-tiāⁿ bô-tie̍h(無定無着).

**unconscious**, put-tsai nâng-sṳ̄(不知人事); put-séng nâng-sṳ̄(不省人事); zû-māng zû-tsùi(如夢如醉); bô-tsai bô-kak(無知無覺).

**ungrateful**, buâng-ṳn(忘恩); hũ-ngĩ(負義); hiau-chhêng(僥情); hiau-chhêng tso̍h-ngĩ(僥情絕義); siũ-ṳn put-pò(受恩不報); hiau-hũ-ṳn(無仁義); bô-jîn-ngĩ(無仁義).

**uniform**, che̍k-iēⁿ(一樣); sie-tâng(相同); tâng-sek(同色); tsôi-chiáⁿ(齊整); tsâu〔〕. *a soldier's*, hō-kùa(號褂); hō-i(號衣).

**unite**, *to*, hũe-ha̍h(會合); ha̍h-bûa(合埋); hũe-bûa(會埋); ha̍h tsò-che̍k-ē(合做蜀下). *in purpose or effort*, tâng-sim khòi-ha̍h(同心契合); tâng-sim hia̍p-la̍t(同心協力); tâng-sim tâng-la̍t(同心同力). *in marriage*, phit-phùe(匹配). *many in one*, ha̍h tsò-che̍k-ē(合做蜀下). *will not unite, as two surfaces or fluids*, m̃-sie-chia̍h(毋相食). *union(concord)*, hûa-mo̍k(和睦); siang-hûa(相和); phêng-hûa(平和).

**unlawful**, m̄-ha̍h-huap(毋合法); m̄-ha̍h lí-lu̍t(毋合理律); bô-lí bô-lu̍t(無理無律); bô-lí bô-huap(無理無法); lu̍t-huap só-m̄-tsún(律法所毋准).

**unmarried**, *man*, būe-tì-ke(未置家); būe-siũ-sit(未受室); būe-tshūa(未娶); būe-hun(未婚); būe-chêng chhin-ngêng(未成親迎); būe-cheng ngêng-chhin(未曾迎親). *woman*, būe-kè(未嫁); būe-tshut-mn̂g(未出家門); būe-kùe-mn̂g(未過門); būe-chêng kè-nâng(未曾嫁人).

**unprecedented**, būe-ũ kâi-sṳ̄ chièⁿ-seⁿ(未有個事此樣生); tsṳ̃-liáu m̄-pat thóiⁿ--kìⁿ(自料毋識睇見); būe-pat thiaⁿ--kìⁿ(未識聽見).

**unprofitable**, bô-iah(無益); bô-lĩ-iah(無利益); bô-ēng(無用). *as business*, bô-lĩ(無利); bô-thàn(無趁).

**unsuccessful**, m̄-chiâⁿ(毋成); m̄-sêng-kong(毋成功); sṳ̄ m̄-sêng-chiũ(事毋成就); bõi-tit uân-tshûan(袂得完全); bõi-tit îⁿ-múaⁿ(袂得圓滿). *at an examination*, kháu-m̄-tie̍h(扣毋着).

**unwearied**, put-sieh lâu-khóu(不惜勞苦); put-sî lâu-khóu(不辭勞苦).
