**unworthy**, m̄-kham-kai(毋堪該); put-kham(不堪); put-kai(不該); m̄-kai(毋該); m̄-eng-kai(毋應該); m̄-eng-tng(毋應當); m̄-kham-tng(毋堪當). *of notice*, put-tsok-kuan(不足觀); m̄-tèng hó-thóiⁿ(毋中好睇).

**unyielding**, ngẽ-sèⁿ(硬性); chip-sèⁿ(執性); m̃-ho̍k(毋服); m̃-sũn(毋順); kang-ngẽ(工硬).

**up**, chiẽⁿ(上); khí(起). *up and down*, chiẽⁿ-lo̍h(上落). *to get*, tsáu-khí(走起). *is the sun up*, ji̍t-thâu tshut a-būe(日頭出亞未). *does not come up to*, būe-ki̍p(未及); būe-kàu(未到); m̄-chhin-chhiẽⁿ(毋親像); būe-hó-pí(未好比); lân-pí(狼比); oh-pí(惡比); hûan-su(煩數). *not quite up to*, bô-hièⁿ-chiẽⁿ(無向上).

**upbraid**, cheh-pĩ(責備); hiâm(嫌); cheh-hiâm(責嫌).

**uphold**, hû-thî(扶提); hû-phû(扶扶); hû-tsõ(扶助); khan-hû(牽扶).

**upon**, tõ-chiēⁿ(在上); tõ-téng(倒頂); tõ-téng-mīn(倒頂面); tõ-mīn-chiēⁿ(在面上).

**upper**, téng--kâi(頂个). *seat*, téng-ūi(頂位); tōa-ūi(大位). *uppermost*, téng-téng(頂頂); siãng-téng(上頂); siãng-kûiⁿ(上懸).

**upright**, ti̍t(直); chiàⁿ-ti̍t(正直). *to place a thing*, pàng-ti̍t(放直); sái-khiã(徙崎); ti̍t-khiã(直徛).

**uproar**, tshàu-nãuⁿ(臭鬧); tshàu-jiáng(吵嚷).

**upset**, léng-tó(推倒); póiⁿ-lìn-tńg(反輾轉); póiⁿ-lèng-tńg(反推轉); phah-tó(拍倒); léng-tiāu(推掉).

**upshot**, kat-kúeⁿ(結果); kàu-búe(到尾).

**upside down**, tin-tò-thâu(顛倒頭); táu-tńg-thâu(鬥轉頭).

**upstairs**, lâu-téng(樓頂). *to go*, chiẽⁿ-lâu(上樓); teng-lâu(登樓); peh-chiẽⁿ lâu-téng(爬上樓頂); seng-chiẽⁿ lâu-téng(升上樓頂); chiẽⁿ-lâu-téng(上樓頂); khí--khṳ̀ lâu-téng(起去樓頂).

**upwards**, niàⁿ-khí(向起); mōⁿ-chiẽⁿ(望上). *upwards of a hundred*, peh-gūa(爬外); peh-ũ-tshut(百有出); peh-lân(百零); che̍k-peh ũ-lân(一百有零).

**urbanity**, lói-mãuⁿ(禮貌); ũ-lói-siàu(有禮數); hiáu--tit lói-ngî(曉得禮儀).

**urethra**, jiẽ-kńg(尿管). *stricture of*, jiē-kńg sat(尿管虱).

**urge**, *to*, tshui(催); tshui-pek(催逼); kek(激); piàⁿ-kín(拚緊); tshui-piàⁿ(催拼); tshui-kín(催緊). *urgent*, kín(緊); kín-iàu(緊要); iàu-kín(要緊); pek-chhiet(迫切).

**urine**, jiē(尿). *to pass*, pàng-jiē(放尿); sié-kói(小解); sié-piẽn(小便); siáu-piẽn(小便). *retention of*, sié-piẽn bõi-kiâⁿ(小便袂行); sié-piẽn m̄-thong(小便毋通); sié-piẽn m̄-lĩ(小便毋利). *incontinence of*, siàm-jiē(滲尿). *pass involuntarily, as child*, tshūa-jiē(𤆬尿). *urinal*, jiē-hû(尿壺); mêⁿ-hû(眉壺); piẽn-hû(便壺).

**urn**, *mortuary*, kim-sieⁿ(金箱); kim-pãu(金炮); húe-kim-pãu(火金暴).

**usage**, kui-kṳ́(規矩); so̍k(俗); hong-so̍k(風俗); sî-siãng(時尚).

**use**, *to*, ēng(用). *ill*, po̍h-thãi(薄待); khi-hũ(欺負); uan-khut(彎屈). *in common use*, siêⁿ-ēng(嘗用). *of use*, ũ-ēng(有用); hó-ēng(好用). *of no*, bô-ēng(無用); bô-lōu-ēng(無路用). *out of*, ēng-m̄-tie̍h(用毋着); mién-ēng(免用). *useful*, ũ-ēng(有用); ũ-iah(有益).

**usual**, phêng-siêⁿ(平常); phêng-sù(平素); pâi-tńg(排轉).

**usurp**, chiàm(佔); âⁿ(佔). *authority*, chhiàm-khûan(僭權); tsuan-khûan(專權). *the throne*, tshùan-ūi(篡位); chiàm-ūi(佔位). *a usurper*, pà-uâng(霸王); chhiàm-uâng(僭王).

**usury**, lĩ-sek khah-tãng(利息較重); tãng-lāi(重利). *to lend on heavy usury*, pàng-tãng-lāi(放重利).

**utensil**, khì-kũ(器具); ke-húe(家伙); khì(器).

**utterance**, kháu-tshâi(口才); kháu-lẽng(口令); õi-tàⁿ-ūe(會呾話).

**utterly**, ke̍k(極); chì-ke̍k(至極); kàu-ke̍k(到極); tsa̍p-hun(十分); liáu-liáu(了了); chĩn(盡); tsò-che̍k-ē(做蜀下); chheng-tshó(清楚); kan-chẽng(乾淨).

### V

**vacant**, khang(空); bô-mue̍h-tõ(無物在); khang-hṳ(空虛). *vacancy in office*, khueh-jĩm(缺任); khueh-ūi(缺位); khàng-khueh(空缺); hṳ-khueh(虛缺).

**vacation**, *of school*, pàng-kè(放假).

**vaccinate**, chèng-tāu(種豆). *vaccine matter*, tāu-chieⁿ(種珠); tāu-chéng(種珠).

**vagabond**, phiau-liû(飄流); liû-lî sit-só(流離失所).

**vagina**, im-hõu(陰雨); súaⁿ-mn̂g(產門); im-mn̂g(陰門).

**vagrant**, iû-chhiú(遊手).

**vague**, u-khuah(于闊); m̄-chhiet-lí(毋切理); m̄-chhiet sṳ̄-chhêng(毋切事情); hùam(泛).

**vail**, *to*, chia(遮). *the face*, chia-mīn(遮面); muaⁿ-mīn(幔面). *a*, chia-mīn-se(遮面紗); ou-kṳn(烏筋).

**vain**, *in*, thû-lâu bô-iah(徒勞無益); thû-lâu bô-kong(徒勞無功); thû-jiên(徒然). *labour*, uán-hùi kang-hu(枉費工夫); uáng-hùi cheng-sîn(枉費精神); thû-hùi sim-sṳ(徒費心思).

**vain**, tsṳ̃-khua(自誇); tsṳ̃-sĩ(自是); hàuⁿ-hua(好花); kiau-chhia(嬌車); hṳ-khua(虛誇).

**valiant**, ũ-táⁿ(有膽); ũ-táⁿ-lia̍k(有膽略); ũ-táⁿ-la̍t(有膽力). *valour*, káⁿ(敢); ióng-káⁿ(勇敢); kúaⁿ-káⁿ(趕敢); ióng(勇).

**valley**, suaⁿ-kok(深坑); suaⁿ-kok-lok(山谷落); suaⁿ-khang(山空); suaⁿ-phāng(深坑).

**valuable**, pó(寶); pó-pùe(寶貝); kùi-khì(貴器); pó-kùi(寶貴); kùi-tõng(貴重); tien-tõng(珍重); ta̍t-chîⁿ(值錢).

**value**, *real*, chin-kè(真價). *to value highly*, thóiⁿ-tõng(睇重); kùi-tõng(貴重); tien-tõng(珍重).

**van**, *of army*, sien-hong(先鋒); tsôiⁿ-hong(前鋒).

**vane**, *wind*, tiāⁿ-huang-tsam(定風針); sũn-huang-kî(順風旗).

**vanish**, kui-tsò-bô(規做無). *(into the sky)*, seng-khong(升空).

**vapour**, khì(氣). *cloudy*, hûn-bū(雲霧); in-bū(煙霧). *steam*, tsúi-khì(水氣); tsúi-in(水煙).

**variance**, *at*, ũ-ūe(有話); seⁿ-ūe(生話); ũ-hun-khiah(有分隙); m̄-hûa-mo̍k(毋和目); ũ-hiâm-khiah(有嫌隙).

**variegated**, ngóu-sek(五色); ngóu-tshái(五彩); hue-long(花瓏); tsa̍p-sek(十色).

**various**, ke-iēⁿ(加樣); kak-iē(各樣); kak-sek(各色); kak-hō(各號); kak-téng(各頂). *articles*, tsa̍p-mue̍h(什物).

**varnish**, tshat(漆); mêng-iû(明油). *to*, sái-tshat(使漆); tshat(漆). *the tree*, tshat-chhiū(漆樹).

**vase**, *a*, chéⁿ-kan(井缸); hue-kan(花缸).

**vast**, khuah(闊); khuah-tōa(闊大); miáuⁿ-miáuⁿ bô-pien(渺渺無邊); che̍k-mōⁿ bô-chì(一望無至).

**vat**, tōa-tháng(大桶). *for indigo*, chheⁿ-tháng(青桶).

**vault**, *the vault of heaven*, chheⁿ-thiⁿ(青天); thiⁿ uan-keng uan-keng++(天彎弓彎弓)+. *the vault of heaven (reading)*, khiong-tshan(穹蒼); tshan-khiong(蒼穹). *an underground*, tī-sit(地室). *vaulted*, keng-uan-mn̂g(弓彎門).

**vault**, *to*, thiàu-lêng-mn̂g(跳龍門).

**vegetables**, tshài(菜); chheⁿ-tshài(生菜). *vegetarian*, chia̍h-che(食齋); chia̍h-chhiâng-tshài(食長菜). *occasional vegetarian diet*, chia̍h-hue-che(食花齋).

**vehement**, kip(急); méⁿ(猛); kín-sèⁿ(緊性); pek-chhiet(迫切); huat-hún(發忿).

**veil**, see VAIL.

**vein**, hueh-kṳn(血筋); hueh-lōu(血路). *to open a*, khui-hueh-lōu(開血路); pàng-hueh-lōu(放血路). *in wood*, hue-jī(花字). *of silver (ore)*, ngṳ̂n-kúeⁿ(銀管).

**velvet**, zông(絨). *flowered*, hue-zông(花絨). *collar*, zông-niáⁿ(絨領); zông-ãm-niáⁿ(絨頷領).

**venerable**, khó-kèng(可敬); hó-tit-nâng-kèng(好得人敬). *Sir*, tsun-kè(尊駕); láu-thâi(老太).

**venerate**, kèng-ùi(敬畏); tsun-kèng(尊敬); khim-kèng(欽敬); khim-tsun(欽尊); khim-ho̍k(欽服).

**venereal**, *disease*, lap-ta̍k(納毒); huang-ta̍k(風毒). *congenital*, tho-ta̍k(胎毒).

**venetians**, hāu-peh-chheh(鱟伯策). *windows*, hāu-peh-chheh-theng(鱟伯策窗). *leaves*, chheh-hie̍h(冊頁).

**vengeance**, pò-chhiû(報仇); pò-uan(報冤).

**venison**, te̍k-ne̍k(竹肉). *dried*, te̍k-póu(竹脯).

**venomous**, ta̍k(毒).

**ventilate**, thong-huang(通風).

**venture**, káⁿ(敢). *one's life*, káⁿ-sí(敢死); mãuⁿ-sí(冒死); thû-sí(圖死); tì-miāⁿ(致命); piàⁿ-miāⁿ(拚命); mãuⁿ-miāⁿ(冒命).

**Venus**, *the planet*, kim-chheⁿ(金星).

**verandah**, bé-lâu(馬樓); tsáu-bé-lâu(走馬樓); lâng-ẽ(廊下).

**verb**, ua̍h-jī(活字).

**verbal**, *report*, kháu-thûan(口傳). *order*, tng-mīn hun-hù(當面吩咐). *verbatim*, chiè-kò-o̍h(照塊學); che̍k-kù che̍k-kù(一句一句); kù-kù siang-tâng(句句相同).

**verbose**, to-ngân(多言); ke-ūe(加話); lo-so(囉嗦); lo-lo so-so(囉囉嗦嗦); mīⁿ-sùaⁿ-ūe(麵線話); ki-hie̍h-ūe(枝葉話).

**verdict**, phoi-phùan(批判); kong-phùan(公判).

**verdigris**, tâng-chheⁿ(銅青).

**verify**, hāu-ngiām(校驗).

**vermicelli**, mīⁿ-sùaⁿ(麵線); tāu-hún(豆粉); tāu-chhiam(豆籤); hún-chhiam(粉籤).

**vermilion**, ngṳ̂n-tsu(銀朱).

**vernacular**, thóu-thâm(土談); thôu-ūe(塗話); pe̍h-ūe(白話); so̍k-ūe(俗話).

**versatile**, ũ-pièn-thong(有變通); ũ-khûan-pièn(有權變); ua̍h-pièn(活變); îⁿ-ua̍h(圓活).

**verse**, *poetry*, si(詩). *one*, che̍k-tsat(一節).

**vertebrae**, ie-kut-tsat(腰骨節). *(dorsal)*, pùe-kut-tsat(背骨節). *(sacral)*, búe-lûn-kut(尾輪骨). *(cervical)*, ãm-kut(頷骨).

**vertex**, téng(頂).

**vertical**, tùi-thâu-khak-téng(對頭殼頂); thâu-téng(頭頂); tùi-téng(對頂); chiàⁿ-téng(正頂).

**vertigo**, thâu-khak hîn(頭殼眩); hîn(眩); hîn-kông(眩戇); hîn-kông(眩戇).

**very**, sĩm(甚); chì(至); siãng(上); tsãi(在); thih(鐵); tsùe(最); tsa̍p-hun(十分); tōa-ē(大下). *sorry*, hûan-ló-tsãi(煩惱多). *important*, tsùe-iàu(最要). *many*, sĩm-tsōi(甚㩼). *different*, tōa-m̄-tâng(大毋同). *that very day*, tùi-tùi hṳ́-che̍k-ji̍t(對對彼一日); tú-tú hṳ́-che̍k-ji̍t(堵堵彼一日). *even a very clever man could not do it*, sui-sĩ thih-õi kâi-nâng hûan tsò-m̄-lâi(雖是鐵會个人還做毋來).

**vessel**, *a*, khì-kũ(器具); ke-húe(家伙). *ship*, tsûn(船); che̍k-chiah-tsûn(一隻船).

**vest**, tah-pùe(答背); kah-kiáⁿ(袷囝).

**vestige**, hûn-chiah(痕跡); kha-chiah(骹跡). *not a vestige of truth in it*, bô-iáⁿ-chiah(無影跡); bô-iáⁿ bô-chiah(無影無跡).

**veteran**, láu-chhiú(老手). *troops*, chhin-piaⁿ(親兵); liēn-piaⁿ(練兵).

**veterinary**, *surgeon*, ui-gû sin-sin(醫牛先生); gû-ui(牛醫); bé-ui(馬醫).

**vex**, lân-ûi(難爲); kan-khóu(艱苦); bûa-lān(磨難); thua-bûa(拖磨); pek(迫). *vexed*, hûan-ló(煩惱); iu-būn(憂悶); khóu-sim(苦心); ut-kak(鬱結); iu-ut(憂鬱); tshôu-ut(愁鬱).

**vial**, sòi kâi-po-lî-tsun(細个玻璃樽); po-lî-kùan(玻璃罐).

**vibrate**, *to vibrate*, tùn(頓); sih(薛). *to vibrate (as strings of harp)*, tuāiⁿ(振).

**vice**, *a*, thih-kia̍p(鐵夾).

**vice**, *bad conduct*, tsũe-ak(罪惡); ak-si̍p(惡習); khì-si̍p m̄-hó(氣習毋好); hui-ûi(非爲).

**vice-**, *or second*, hù(副); thòi(代). *vice-president of one of the supreme boards*, sĩ-nn̂g(是郎).

**vicinity**, siang-kṳ̃n(相近); lîn-kṳ̃n(鄰近); lîn-iũ(鄰右); siang-liên(相連); lîn-kṳ(鄰居); tsôiⁿ-ãu(前後).

**vicious**, man(蠻); àu-nâng(爛人); pháiⁿ-nâng(痞人); nâng-tái(人痞).

**victory**, thâi-iâⁿ(刣贏); chièn-iâⁿ(戰贏); chièn-sèng(戰勝); ua̍k-sèng(獲勝); sèng-te̍k(勝敵). *report of*, pò-chia̍p(報捷).

**victuals**, chia̍h(食); chia̍h-mu̍eh(食物); húe-si̍t(伙食); bí-niêⁿ(米糧). *dry, as for journey*, kan-niêⁿ(乾糧).

**view**, *to*, thóiⁿ(睇). *views or scenery*, kuang-kéng(光景); kéng-tī(景地); kéng-tshù(景厝).

**vigilant**, kéng-chhéⁿ(警醒); kṳ́n-sín(謹慎); kṳ́n-huâng(謹防); thî-huâng(提防).

**vigorous**, tsàng(壯); tsàng-kiẽn(壯健); khin-kiāⁿ(輕健); khang-kiẽn(康健); khiâng-tsàng(強壯); ũ-cheng-sîn(有精神); ũ-khì-la̍t(有氣力); ũ-cheng-la̍t(有精力); cheng-la̍t tsok(精力足).

**vile**, *hiã-tsūaⁿ*, chhiú-ak(醜惡). *person*, siáu-jîn(小人).

**vilify**, húiⁿ-pãng(誹謗); iâu-pãng(謠謗); pù-lũ〔〕.

**village**, hieⁿ-lí(鄉里); hieⁿ(鄉); hieⁿ-tshng(鄉里); hieⁿ-chē(鄉里); chē(寨). *villager*, kṳ-hieⁿ-nâng(居鄉人); hieⁿ-ẽ-nâng(鄉下人). *headmen*, hieⁿ-láu(鄉老); hieⁿ-sin(鄉紳); ieh-chiàⁿ(約正); pó-chiàⁿ(保正).

**villain**, ak-nâng(惡人); phái-nâng(痞人); kan-ak(奸惡); hiong-ak(兇惡); khiông-hiong pãu-ak(窮兇暴惡); kan-káu(奸狡); kan-hiám(奸險).

**vindicate**, *oneself*, *before a superior*, hun-sù(分訴). *another*, thòi-sù(代訴); thòi-piáu(代表). *a statement*, chí-chèng-kṳ̃ tshut--lâi(指證據出來); chí-tshut chèng-kṳ̃(指出證據); khie̍h-tshut chèng-kṳ̃(挈出證據).

**vindictive**, hàuⁿ-pò-chhiû(好報仇).

**vine**, phû-thô-chhiū(葡萄樹). *vineyard*, phû-thô-hn̂g(葡萄園).

**vinegar**, tshòu(醋); sng-tshòu(酸醋).

**violate**, *law*, huãm-huap(犯法). *an engagement*, sit-ieh(失約); huãm-ieh(犯約). *a woman*, khiâng-kan(強姦).

**violence**, *with*, khiâng(強). *to seize with*, khiâng-tshú(強取); khiâng-àiⁿ(強愛); chiàm(佔); pà-chiàm(霸佔); âⁿ(佔).

**violent**, méⁿ(猛); méⁿ-lie̍t(猛烈); pãu-ngia̍k(暴虐). *storm*, khûang-huang méⁿ-hõu(狂風猛雨); khûang-huang pãu-hõu(狂風暴雨).

**violin**, hîⁿ(弦). *to play the*, kṳ̀-hîⁿ(鋸弦); khan-hîⁿ(牽弦).

**viper**, ta̍k-tsûa(毒蛇); pn̄g-sî-thâu(飯匙頭).

**virago**, mân-hũ(蠻婦); iá-hũ(野婦); nńg-chiàng(女將); phuat-hũ(潑婦); phuat-tsūaⁿ++(潑賤)+.

**virgin**, kui-nńg(閨女); tshù-nńg(厝女); chhim-kui nńg-tsṳ́(深閨女子). *(remaining a virgin for life)*, cheng-nńg(精女). *(remaining a virgin for life, man or woman)*, cheng-thông(精童).

**virtue**, tek(德). *virtuous conduct*, tek-hẽng(德行). *the five virtues*, ngóu-siâng(五常): jîn(仁), ngĩ(義), lí(理), tì(智), sìn(信).

**virtue**, *or efficacy*, *kong*, kong-hāu(功效); khì-la̍t(氣力); hāu-ngiām(效驗).

**virulent**, ta̍k(毒); ak-ta̍k(惡毒).

**visage**, mīn(面); mīn-mãuⁿ(面貌); iông-mãuⁿ(容貌); mīn-sek(面色); mīn-hêng(面形).

**viscid**, ũ-ka-liâm〔〕; liâm-nîⁿ tha-thi〔〕.

**viscera**, ngóu-tsãng la̍k-hú(五臟六腑).

**visible**, ũ-hêng-siãng(有形像); ũ-hêng-siãng hó-thóiⁿ(有形象好睇).

**vision**, *dream*, mîn-māng(眠夢); mêⁿ-māng(夜夢); māng-mũeⁿ(夢寐). *to have a*, kìⁿ-mêⁿ-māng(見夜夢); māng--kìⁿ(夢見); ki-kuan--kìⁿ(機關見); ũ-māng-tiãu(有夢兆).

**visionary**, phû(pũ)-huang tshok-iáⁿ(捕風捉影); tsúi--tang lã-gue̍h(水中撈月); kiàⁿ-hue tsúi-gue̍h(鏡花水月).

**visit**, pài-kìⁿ(拜見); pài-hāu(拜候); mn̄g-hāu(問候); siê-sûn(常巡). *farewell*, sàng-pie̍t(送別); sàng-kiâⁿ(送行). *to miss a*, sit-chiap(失接). *I am sorry I missed your visit*, ãi! móng-ji̍t sit-chiap(哎!某日失接), sù--chē sù--chē!(恕些恕些) (Ans, õ! móng-ji̍t khṳ̀-kùe-jiáu(哦!某日去過擾), phòng--tie̍h lṳ́ tsun-kè gūa--tshut-khṳ̀(碰着汝尊駕外出去)). *to return a*, hûe-pài(回拜); hûe-pōu(回步). *to (a prince)*, chhiâu-kìⁿ(朝見); chhiâu-kun(朝君). *to (a friend or relative)*, thàm-iú(探友); thàm-chhim(探深). *visiting card*, pài-thiap(拜帖). *visitor*, nâng-kheh(人客); pin-kheh(賓客). *to receive*, chiap-na̍p(接納); ngêng-chih(迎接); khúan-thãi(款待). *to dismiss*, sàng-kheh(送客); sàng-pin(送賓). *to visit one and have a talk with him*, khṳ̀ kāng-i phûan-sûan--chē(去共伊盤旋些); khṳ̀ kāng-i chiu-sûan--chē(去共伊周旋些).

**vitriol**, *blue (sulphate of copper)*, táⁿ-huân(膽礬). *green (sulphate of iron; copperas)*, tsõ-huân(座礬); chheⁿ-huân(青礬).

**vivacious**, ua̍h-phuah(活潑); lêng-lāi(伶俐); ũ-sîn-khì(有神氣); ũ-cheng-sîn(有精神).

**vocabulary**, jī-lūi(字類).

**voice**, siaⁿ(聲); siaⁿ-im(聲音). *clear*, siaⁿ-im chheng-liãng(聲音清亮); liáu-liãng(嘹亮); mêng-liãng(明亮). *indistinct*, siaⁿ-im lô-lô(聲音囉囉); siaⁿ-im hâm-hû(聲音含糊); siaⁿ-im kâm-kôu(聲音含糊). *to lose one's*, sit-siaⁿ(失聲); bô-siaⁿ(無聲); sit-im(失音). *to read in a clear loud voice*, khui-siaⁿ-tha̍k(開聲讀). *to recognize one's*, jīn-siaⁿ(認聲); piẽn-siaⁿ(辯聲). *with one voice*, che̍k-kháu che̍k-sṳ̂(一口一詞).

**void**, see EMPTY.

**volcano**, húe-suaⁿ(火山); húe-iãm-suaⁿ(火焰山).

**volume**, *a*, che̍k-pńg(一本). *several volumes making one work*, che̍h-pang(冊幫); tshûan-põu(全部).

**voluntarily**, kam-sim(甘心); kam-ngũan(甘願); kam-sim chhêng-ngũan(甘心情願); chhêng-nguãn(情願); huaⁿ-hí(歡喜); kam-sim sêng-ì(甘心誠意).

**volunteer**, mîn-tsàng(民壯); ngĩ-piaⁿ(義兵).

**voluptuary**, tham-chiú-sek(貪酒色); hàuⁿ-chiú-sek(好酒色).

**vomit**, thòu(吐).

**vortex**, tsúi ká-pūn(水絞糞); suân-lâu-tsúi(旋流水).

**vote**, *for*, kṳ́(舉); kṳ́-chìn(舉薦).

**voucher**, pêng-kṳ̃(憑據); phêng-kṳ̃(憑據).

**vow**, *to*, hẽ-nguān(下愿); hṳ́-nguān(許愿). *to pay a*, hôiⁿ-nguān(還愿); kói-nguān(解愿); siā-nguān(謝愿).

**voyage**, tsúi-lōu(水路); tsúi-thiâⁿ(水庭); kiâⁿ-tsûn(行船). *next*, ẽ-tsūa-tsûn(下艘船); ẽ-pàng-tsûn(下放船).

**vulgar**, so̍k(俗); tshou(粗); tshou-so̍k(粗俗). *dialect*, so̍k-ūe(俗話); thóu-thâm(土談); pe̍h-ūe(白話). *language*, thóu-thóu(土土). *language (vile)*, tshou-ūe(粗話).

### W

**wadding**, mîⁿ(棉); mîⁿ-hue(棉花). *wadded coat*, ji̍p-mîⁿ-hiûⁿ(入棉裘). *to put in wadding*, phou-mîⁿ(鋪棉); ji̍p-mîⁿ(入棉).

**waddle**, *to*, phiáng-a-phiáng(蹣阿蹣); kûa-a-kûa(䠚阿䠚).

**wade**, *to*, ẽ-tsúi(下水). *over a river*, ẽ-kùe-khoi(下過溪).

**wag**, *to*, iê(搖). *wag-tail*, tih-tĩm-tim〔〕.

**wager**, sie-su(相輸); siang-tóu(相賭). *let us wager*, lâi-tóu--chē(來賭些). *to write a wager*, siá-tóu-tsn̄g(寫賭狀).

**wages**, kang-chîⁿ(工錢); kang-tsṳ(工資); kang-kè(工價). see SALARY.

**wagon**, chhia(車).

**wail**, khàu(哭); ai-khàu(哀哭); thî-khàu(啼哭). *for the dead*, khàu-sí-sng(哭死酸). *for death of son*, khàu-kiáⁿ(哭囝).

**waist**, ie(腰); pùaⁿ-ie(半腰); sin-ie(身腰). *to gird the*, hâ-ie(縖腰); sok-ie(束腰). *waistcoat*, tah-pùe(答背); kah-kiáⁿ(袷囝).

**wait**, tán(等); hāu(候); thẽng(停); thêng(停); thãi(待); thẽng-hāu(等候). *a little*, tán--chē(等些); hâu--chē(侯些). *we are waiting for you, Sir*, hāu-kè(候駕). *to wait on*, ho̍k-sṳ̃(服事); kṳn-sûi(跟隨); sĩ-tsái(侍仔). *waiters*, tsáu-tn̂g(走堂); chìn-tôu(進圖); kṳn-pan(斤班).

**waken**, *to (transitive)*, hàm-chhéⁿ(喊醒); kiè-chhéⁿ(叫醒); kiaⁿ-chhéⁿ(驚醒); tsak-chhéⁿ(聒醒). *(intransitive)*, gu̍t-chhéⁿ(夗醒); chhéⁿ(醒); chhéⁿ--khí-lâi(醒起來). *wakeful*, gu̍t-m̄-lo̍h(夗毋落); bõi-gu̍t(袂夗).

**walk**, kiâⁿ(行). *to and fro*, kiâⁿ-lâi kiâⁿ-khṳ̀(行來行去). *on foot*, pōu-kiâⁿ(步行); pōu-lién(步輦). *go for a*, khṳ̀-thit-thô(去佚佗); khṳ̀-kîn-kiâⁿ〔〕; khṳ̀-sùaⁿ-pōu(去散步). *walking-stick*, kuái-chiãng(拐杖); kuái-thûi(拐槌).

**wall**, chhiêⁿ(牆). *a*, che̍k-pang-chhiêⁿ(一方牆). *city-wall*, siâⁿ(城); siâⁿ-chhiêⁿ(城牆). *the great wall*, buān-lí chhiâng-siâⁿ(萬里長城). *a dividing*, keh-piah(隔壁). *to fall down as a*, pang(枋). *to build*, see BUILD.

**walnut**, hu̍t-thô(核桃).

**wand**, *a*, chhiū-pie(樹鏢); chhiū-lêng(樹靈); tek-lêng(竹龍); che̍k-ki-tshûe(一枝箠).

**wander**, iû(遊); tshut-iû(出遊); chiu-liû(周流). *far*, ién-iû(遠遊). *in poverty and distress*, liû-lî sit-só(流離失所); lâu-lî sit-só(流離失所). *out of the way*, kiâⁿ-tāⁿ-lōu(行賺路); tsáu-tshò lōu-thû(走錯路途); sit-lōu(失路). *wandering thoughts*, huàng-sim(渙心); sim tsa̍p(心雜); sim seⁿ-tsa̍p-liãm(心生雜念).

**wane**, *as moon*, gue̍h chiãm-chiãm-sòi(月漸漸細); gue̍h chiãm-khui(月漸虧); gue̍h tsho-tsho-sòi(月初初細).

**want**, *(wish)*, àiⁿ(愛). *(lack)*, khueh(缺); khiàm(欠).

**wanton**, siâ-îm(邪淫); hàuⁿ-phiâu(好嫖); hàuⁿ-sek(好色); hùang-îm(放淫).

**war**, kau-chièn(交戰); kau-piaⁿ(交戰); ke-húe kau-chiap(家伙交接); sie-thâi(相刣). *man-of-war*, piaⁿ-tsûn(交戰); chièn-tsûn(戰船); kuaⁿ-tsûn(交戰).

**ward**, *to off*, tói-tiāu(底掉); tí-tiāu(抵掉); tú-gṳ̃(堵禦); gṳ̃-chí(禦指); tú-tiām(堵恬); gṳ̃-tiām(禦恬); tháⁿ-tiāu(坦掉).

**wardrobe**, saⁿ-tû(衫櫥); saⁿ-kūiⁿ(衫櫃); i-sieⁿ(衣箱).

**warehouse**, tsàng-pâng(棧房); hùe-pâng(貨房); hùe-tshng(貨倉); tsàng-koiⁿ(棧間).

**warm**, sie(燒). *weather*, chhiẽⁿ-sie(上燒). *weather (mild)*, un-hûa(溫和); lúan-khì(暖氣); hûa-lúan(和暖). *warming-pan*, chhiú-lôu(手爐); húe-thang(火湯). *to warm oneself at the fire*, chieh-húe(借火).

**warn**, kéng-kài(警戒); khǹg-kòi(勸戒); that-chhéⁿ(踢醒); that-phùa(踢破); thàu(透). *to take warning*, na̍p-kài(納戒); tsṳ̃-kéng(住戒).

**warp**, *the*, keⁿ(經); pòu-keⁿ(布經). *and woof*, keⁿ-hūi(經緯). *to warp, as boards*, khiau〔〕; khiau-siâ〔〕.

**warrant**, *a*, phiè(票); pâi-phiè(排票); chhe-phiè(差票). *to issue*, tshut-phiè(出票). *to*, pau-niáⁿ(包領); pau-pó(包保); tam-sêng(擔承).

**warrior**, ióng-sṳ̃(勇士).

**wart**, *a*, tsùe(最); hṳ̂-lâng-tsùe(魚籠最).

**wash**, sói(洗). *wash-stand*, mīn-tháng-kè(面桶架); mīn-phûn-kè(面盆架). *a washerman*, sóiⁿ-saⁿ-nang(洗衫人). *to wash iron dust*, tôa-thih-sua(涂鐵沙); sói-thih(洗鐵). *to wash with gold*, tōu-kim(渡金); liū-kim(鎦金); tsṳ́-kim(紫金). *wash-hand basin*, mīn-phûn(面盆); mīn-tháng(面桶).

**wasp**, n̂g-phang(黃蜂); hóuⁿ-thâu-phang(虎頭蜂).

**waste**, *to*, tak-nn̄g〔〕; hùi-tiāu(費掉); hṳ-hùi(虛費). *time*, phau-hng-tiāu sî-hāu(拋荒掉時候); tak-nn̄g-tiāu sî-hāu〔〕; hṳ-iẽn ji̍t-chí(虛延日子); hṳ-tōu kuang-im(虛度光陰); sit-lo̍h sî-hāu(失落時候). *to use wastefully*, phah-phún-ēng〔〕. *a waste place*, khuàng-iá(曠野); khuàng-tī(曠地); khuàng-pou(曠埔); pou-iá(埔野); phau-hng(拋荒).

**watch**, *a*, sî-pie(時錶). *to wind a*, khui-sî-pie(開時錶).

**watch**, *of the night*, keⁿ(更); keⁿ-kóu(更狗); keⁿ-tiám(更點). *the first*, an-keⁿ(安更). *to beat the*, khà-keⁿ(拍更); sûn-keⁿ(巡更); chiéⁿ-keⁿ(掌更). *the man who does this*, keⁿ-hu(更夫). *though the thief comes only in one watch, we must be on guard all night*, tsò-tsha̍t che̍k-keⁿ(做賊一更), chiéⁿ-tsha̍t che̍k-mêⁿ(掌賊一夜).

**watch**, *to*, thóiⁿ-siú(看守); chiéⁿ(掌); siú(守). *as sentry*, sûn-hûang(巡防). *watchful*, m̄-káⁿ-gu̍t(毋敢夗); kéng-chhéⁿ(警醒). *watchword*, àm-hō(暗號). *to appoint a*, phah-àm-hō(拍暗號).

**water**, tsúi(水). *to water*, ak-tsúi(沃水). *water flowers*, ak-hue(沃花). *water-caltrops*, nôiⁿ-kak(菱角). *water-course*, tsúi-kau(水溝). *watercress*, tsúi-khṳ̂n-tshài(水芹菜). *water-engine*, tsúi-chhia(水車). *water-fall*, pak-pòu-tsúi(腹布水); pak-pòu-tsûaⁿ(腹布泉). *water-lily*, nôiⁿ-hue(蓮花). *water-mill*, tsúi-bō(水磨). *water-pail*, tsúi-tháng(水桶). *water melon*, si-kue(西瓜). *watering-pot*, sũan-tháng(旋桶); ak-tshài-tháng(沃菜桶). *waterspout*, lêng kauh-tsúi(龍捲水). *watery*, tâm-tâm lok-lok-chhieh(㴷㴷漉漉淖); kà-kà〔〕; seⁿ-tsúi(生水); lóng-lóng(朗朗).

**wattles**, tek-tsa̍h(竹柵); tek-ûi(竹圍).

**wave**, éng(湧); hái-éng(海湧); po-éng(波湧). *to wave a flag*, i̍t-kî(一旗). *the flag waves in the wind*, kî iãⁿ-huang(旗影風).

**waver**, *to*, siẽⁿ-thâu bô-tiāⁿ(想頭無定); būe-ũ kuat-ì(未有決意); būe-chêng phah-tiāⁿ tsú-ì(未成拍定主意); phah-sǹg būe-tiāⁿ(拍算未定).

**wax**, la̍h(蠟). *candle*, la̍h-chek(蠟燭). *to wax thread*, sùaⁿ kia̍p-la̍h(線夾蠟). *in the ears*, hĩⁿ-sái(耳屎).

**way**, lōu(路); tãu(道); thû(途); lōu-thû(路途); lōu-tãu(路道); lōu-thâu(路頭); lōu-kèⁿ(路徑). *on the*, lōu-chiēⁿ(路上); lōu-téng(路頂); lōu--kò(路塊). *to lead the*, tshūa-lōu(𤆬路); ín-lōu(引路); kāng-lōu(共路); kiau-lōu(邀路). *to be in one's*, hûang-gāi(妨礙). *to be in the way*, tìn-tò(鎮地); tìn-tiāu tī-hng(鎮掉地方). *half-way*, pùaⁿ-lōu(半路); lōu-pùaⁿ-kue̍h(路半橛). *do it this way*, chièⁿ-seⁿ-tsò(此樣生做). *what way*, ēng sĩ-mih huang-huap(用是乜方法). *which is the right*, tùi tî-tiâu-lōu kiâⁿ chiàⁿ-tie̍h(對底條路行正着). *get out of the*, kiâⁿ-khui(行開); kiâⁿ-bûa(行埋). *to get out of one another's*, sie-pī(相避). *lose one's*, kiâⁿ-tāⁿ-lōu(行賺路); kiâⁿ-tshò-lōu(行錯路).

**we**, *(excludingthe person addressed)*, ûn(紜). *(including person addressed)*, nán(咱).

**weak**, nńg-jia̍k(無力); bô-la̍t(無力); phu̍h(薄). *tea*, po̍h-tê(無力); tãⁿ-tê(無力). *weakening*, sún-cheng-sîn(損精神). *in weak health*, sin-hūn phàⁿ(身分冇); sin-hūn lám〔〕.

**wealth**, chîⁿ-tshâi(錢財); chîⁿ-ngṳ̂n(錢銀); tshâi-pe̍h(財白). *wealthy*, pù(富); ũ-chîⁿ(有錢). *to become*, huat-tshâi(發財).

**wean**, keh-nĩⁿ(隔奶); tñg-nĩⁿ(隔奶); pàng-nĩⁿ(隔奶).

**weapon**, piaⁿ-khì(兵器); ke-húe(家伙); kan-kho(干戈); pâi-chhieⁿ〔〕.

**wear**, *to wear clothes*, chhēng-saⁿ(穿衫). *wear a hat*, tì-bō(戴帽). *wear a ring (armlet)*, kùa-chhiú-hûan(掛手環). *wear a finger-ring*, kùa-chhiú-tsat(掛手節). *wear holes in one's clothes*, chhēng-phùa saⁿ-khòu(穿破衫褲). *as (for example) grind-stone*, siám-si̍h(閃蝕); siau-si̍h(消蝕). *worn out*, chhēng-kàu-phùa(穿到破); lau-se(褸些); thiau-se(挑些); phùa-mo̍hⁿ(破膜).

**weary**, *khùn; kha sng; kha sng*, chhiú nńg(手軟).

**weather**, thîⁿ-sî(天時); thiⁿ(天); thiⁿ-khì(天時). *mild*, thiⁿ-sî un-hûa(天氣溫和); thiⁿ-sî thiâu-hûa(天氣調和). *hot*, thiⁿ-sî zua̍h(天氣熱). *fair*, thiⁿ-sî chêⁿ(天氣晴). *weather-beaten*, mīn pha̍k-ou(面曝烏); huang khau-ou(風摳烏). *weather-cock*, sũn-huang-kî(順風旗); tiāⁿ-huang-tsam(定風針); huang-sìn-kî(風信旗).

**weave**, keⁿ-pòu(經布); chit-pòu(經布). *weaver's beam*, te̍k-sim(經布).

**web**, *of cloth*, che̍k-phit-pòu(一疋布); che̍k-kui-pòu(一規布). *spider's*, ti-tu-si(蜘蛛絲). *the spider makes his web*, ti-tu keⁿ-si(蜘蛛更絲); ti-tu kit-mãng(蜘蛛結網); ti-tu thòu-si(蜘蛛吐絲). *web-footed*, ũ-ah-tôi(有鴨題).

**wedding**, *a*, hun-in(婚姻). *wedding-chair*, sin-niêⁿ-kiē(新娘轎); hue-kiē(花轎). see MARRY.

**wedge**, chiⁿ(支); tshâ-chiⁿ(柴支); thih-chiⁿ(鐵支). *to wedge*, chiⁿ(支); chiⁿ-kín(支緊); chiⁿ-soih(支細). *to open with wedges*, chiⁿ-khui(支開).

**Wednesday**, lói-pài-saⁿ(禮拜三); pài-saⁿ(拜三).

**weed**, *a*, tsháu(草). *to*, khau-tsháu(薅草); mán-tsháu(挽草). *sea-weed*, hái-soi(海嘶).

**week**, *one*, che̍k-kâi lói-pài(一個禮拜); chhit-ji̍t(七日).

**weep**, *to*, khàu(哭); lâu-ma̍k-tsap(流目汁).

**weevils**, tsù-iêⁿ(蛀羊); tsù-kak-iêⁿ(蛀角羊).

**weigh**, *to*, téng(等). *to (with steelyard)*, chhìn(秤). *to  (with balances)*, phêng(平). *weights*, chhìn-thûi(秤錘); lî-téng-thûi(璃等槌); lî-chhìn-thûi(璃秤槌); tô-chí(桃指); phêng-chí(平指). *of a clock*, sî-cheng-thūi(時鐘墜). *what is the weight*, ũ-jie̍h-tãng(有若重); téng-jie̍h-tãng(等若重). *weighty*, tãng(重). *to weigh anything in the hand*, chhìn jie̍h-tãng(秤若重); chhìm jie̍h-tãng(沁若重). *anchor*, po̍ih-tèng(拔椗); chhia-tèng(車碇); khie̍h-tèng(挈椗). *a matter*, chim-chiak(斟酌); phah-sǹg(拍算); pheⁿ-phah(斟酌); phah-pheⁿ(拍斟).

**welcome**, *to*, hí-chiap(喜接); huan-ngêng(歡迎).

**well**, *in health*, nâng hó(人好); sin-chiēⁿ zû-zuán(身上如轉); sóng-khùai(爽快); khùaⁿ-ua̍h(寬活); uaⁿ-jiên(安然); phêng-an(平安); thiâu-hûa(調和). *written (as composition)*, pit-ba̍k hó(筆墨好); pit-tói hó(筆底好). *written (as characters)*, jī ngiáⁿ(字雅); ngiáⁿ-jī(雅字); õi-khiâ-pit(會擎筆); õi-siá-jī(會寫字); jī tuan-khái(字端楷); jī siù-se̍k(字秀熟). *made*, tsò-lâi kang-hu(做來工夫). *cooked*, sa̍h-se̍k(煠熟); pû-mîⁿ(煲糜). *known*, tshut-miâⁿ(出名); hién-miâⁿ(顯名); tù-miâⁿ(著名). *bred*, hiáu-lí(曉理); ũ-ke-kà(有家教); hiáu-kui-kṳ́(曉規矩); ũ-lói-huap(有禮法). *dressed*, chhēng-hó-saⁿ(穿好衫). *are you well*, lṳ́ ũ-phêng-an, mé(汝有平安咩). *well done*, hó-tsãi(好在). *well, well, no more of that*, pã--liáu(罷了). *quite well (after illness)*, tshûan-zú(全愈).

**well**, *a*, chéⁿ(井). *well-curb*, chéⁿ-nûaⁿ(井欄); chéⁿ-khuan(井圈). *to sink a*, khui-chéⁿ(開井); liú-chéⁿ(㧕井); tshuan-chéⁿ(穿井); ku̍t-chéⁿ(掘井). *well-rope*, pua̍h-tháng-soh(跋桶索). *mouth of well*, chéⁿ-tshùi(穿水); chéⁿ-mīn(井面). *well-sweep*, tiàu-o〔〕.

**west**, sai(西). *east and west*, tang-sai(東西). *southwest*, sai-lâm(西南).

**wet**, tâm(㴷). *wet with rain*, ak-tie̍h-hõu(沃着雨); ak kàu-lok-lok(沃到漉漉). *damp*, chhiẽⁿ-ĩm〔〕; tâm-ĩm〔〕; lùn-lùn(嫩嫩). *wet-nurse*, niⁿ-bó(奶母).

**whale**, khêng-hṳ̂(鯨魚).

**wharf**, bé-thâu(碼頭).

**what**, tî-kâi(底個); sĩ-mih-sṳ̄(是乜事); sĩ-mih-mue̍h(是乜物); tsò-nîⁿ(怎呢). *what man*, sĩ-mih-nâng(是乜人); tî-tiâng(底誰). *what cause*, sĩ-mih uân-kù(是乜緣故); in-ũi tsò-nîⁿ(因爲怎呢). *what a fool you are*, lṳ́ chièⁿ-ngà〔〕. *what is it like*, tsãi-seⁿ-iēⁿ(在生樣). *what, then, are you going to do*, taⁿ, àiⁿ tsò-nîⁿ-mue̍h(今，愛怎呢物). *what did you say*, lṳ́ tsò-nîⁿ-tàⁿ(汝怎呢呾). *what he says*, i-só-tàⁿ(伊所呾).

**whatever**, put-lũn(不論); tãi-hûam(大凡); tãi-hũam(大凡); sûi-piẽn(隨便).

**wheat**, be̍h(麥).

**wheel**, lûn(輪); lín(輪); lín-chîⁿ(輪錢); khah-chîⁿ(較錢); chhia-lûn(車輪). *rim of*, chhia-lûn-kîⁿ(車輪墘). *spokes of*, chhia-lûn-tsam(車輪針). *wheel-barrow*, chhiú-chhia(手車); léng-chhia(輦車).

**wheeze**, he(蝦); he-siaⁿ(嘿聲); hm̄-hm̄-kiè(嗯嗯叫); âu-thâu kō-kō-kiè(喉頭塊塊叫).

**when**, tiâng-sî(當時); tî-sî(底時); tî-tiâng-sî(底當時); tî-kâi sî-hāu(底个時候); sĩ-mih sî-hāu(是乜時候). *when David was king*, Tãi-phek tsò-uâng tiâng-sî(大闢做王當時); Tãi-phek tsò-uâng kâi-sî-hāu(大闢做王个時候). *when he comes we are going*, i lãi ún chiũ-àiⁿ-khṳ̀(伊來允就愛去). *when....then*, sûi-sî....sûi-sî(隨時....隨時); liên-sî....liên-sî(連時....連時). *when you confess I will let you go*, lṳ́ che̍k-ē-jīn uá chiũ-pàng lṳ́-khṳ̀(汝一下認我就放汝去).

*whence*. tshông-tî-kò-lâi; iû-tî-kò-lâi; tõ-tî-kò-lâi.

**whenever**, put-lũn tiâng-sî(不論誰時). *whenever I think of it tears come into my eyes*, sim che̍k-ē-siẽⁿ(心一下想), ma̍k-tsap chiũ-àiⁿ-lâu(目汁就愛流).

**where**, tî-kò(底處); tõ-tî-kò(到底處). *where I was born*, uá tshut-sì kâi-ūi-tshṳ̀(我出世个位處); uá tshut-sin kâi-tī(我出身个地). *wherever*, put-lũn tî-kò(不論底塊); put-lũn hô-tshù(不論何處).

**wherefore**, in-ũi tsò-nîⁿ(因爲怎呢); ũ sĩ-mih-uân-kù(有是乜緣故); sĩ-mih uân-kù(是乜緣故); sĩ-mih sṳ̄-kù(是乜事故). see THEREFORE.

**whether**, *or*, ho̍k...ho̍k(或..或). *whether he is willing or not I am going*, m̄-kuán i huaⁿ-hí m̄-huaⁿ-hí, uá tsóng-sĩ àiⁿ-khṳ̀(毋管伊歡喜毋歡喜，我總是愛去).

**whetstone**, bûa-to-chie̍h(磨刀石); bûa-chie̍h(磨石).

**which**, tî-kâi(底個); tî-che̍k-kâi(底一個). *which is it*, tî-che̍k-kiãⁿ-sĩ(底一件是). *which is he*, tî-che̍k-nâng-sĩ(底一人是). *the words which he spoke*, i só-tàⁿ kâi-ūe(伊所呾个話).

**while**, *a*, che̍k-sî(一時); khùn-kiáⁿ(頃囝); siap-sî(霎時). *while thinking*, hṳ́-tsûn tõ-siẽⁿ(彼陣在想). *while a cash remains he will gamble*, tshûn-kâi-chîⁿ siãng àiⁿ-khṳ̀-pua̍h(尚愛去跋); sui-sĩ tshûn-kâi-chîⁿ huân-liáu àiⁿ-khṳ̀-pua̍h(雖是賰个錢還了愛去跋). *while I was speaking he arrived*, uá chiàⁿ-tõ-tàⁿ-ūe kâi-sî-hāu, i chiũ-kàu(我正在呾話个時候伊就到). *while*, tng...kâi-sî-hāu(當...个時候).

**whimper**, hiuⁿ-hiuⁿ-kiè(香香叫); hngh-hngh-kiè(哼哼叫); hng-hng-kiè(哼哼叫).

**whip**, *a*, bé-piⁿ(馬鞭). *to strike with a*, pũaⁿ(拌); hiuh(喝); sut(摔); piⁿ-phah(鞭拍). *mosquito whip*, máng-pũaⁿ(蚊拂). *lash of whip*, piⁿ-soh(鞭索).

**whirlpool**, tsúi ká-tsn̄g(水絞狀); tsúi ká-pūn(水絞糞); suân-lâu-tsúi(旋流水).

**whirlwind**, káu-kâⁿ-huang(狗銜風); suân-huang(旋風).

**whiskers**, hôu-chhiu(鬍鬚).

**whisper**, *to*, phak tõ-hĩⁿ-khang-kháu tàⁿ-ūe(趴在耳空口呾話); tàⁿ àm-chẽⁿ-ūe(呾暗靜話); sî-so-kiè(時索叫).

**whistle**, *to*, tshùi pûn ki-kû(吹嘰咕). *a*, ki-kû(嘰咕). *to blow a*, pûn ki-kû(吹嘰咕).

**white**, pe̍h(白). *of an egg*, nñg-chhêng(卵清); nñg-pe̍h(卵白); nñg-phûe(卵皮). *of the eye*, ma̍k-chiu pe̍h-jîn(目睭白仁). *ants*, pe̍h-hiã(白蟻). *to whitewash*, sueh-pe̍h(雪白); hún-pe̍h(粉白); sueh-hún-tsúi(雪粉水); sói-hue-tsúi(洗花水).

**whitlow**, tsńg-kah-tsu(指佮珠); seⁿ tsóiⁿ-búe-tsu(生指尾珠).

**whizzing**, *sound*, hiuh-hiuh-kiè(颼颼叫).

**who**, tî-tiâng(底誰); sĩ-mih-nâng(是乜人). *whosoever*, put-lũn tî-tiâng(不論底誰); hũam-sĩ-mih-nâng(犯是乜人).

**whole**, tshûan(全); kàu-kâi(夠個); chiâⁿ-kâi(成個); chiâⁿ-kò(成塊); ka-nn̂g-kâi〔〕; tsn̂g-kâi(整個); hãm-kâi〔〕; kan-chẽng(乾淨); lóng-tsóng(攏總). *the whole*, che̍k-khài(一概); che̍k-chhiet(一切); tsò-che̍k-ē(做蜀下); tsn̂g-kâi(整個). *family*, ha̍p-ke(合家); ha̍h-ke(合家); tshûan-ke(全家). *life*, che̍k-seⁿ(一生); che̍k-sì-nâng(一世人[訓]); tsong-sin(終身). *day*, tsong-ji̍t(終日); thàng-ji̍t(通日). *heart*, tsuan-sim(專心); chĩn-sim(盡心). *whole body wet*, che̍k-sin tâm(一身㴷).

**wholesale**, *house*, hâng(行); bōi-chiàⁿ-khí(賣正起); tsò-chiēⁿ-pûaⁿ(做上盤). *to buy*, bói-chiēⁿ-pûaⁿ(買上盤).

**whore**, see PROSTITUTE.

**why**, tsò-nîⁿ(怎呢); sĩ-mih uân-kù(是乜緣故); sĩ-mih sṳ̄-kù(是乜事故); sĩ-mih sṳ̄-chhêng(是乜事情); ũi sĩ-mih-sṳ̄(謂是乜事).

**why so**, hô-pit chièⁿ-seⁿ(何必此樣生). *why*, hiá(彼個).

**wick**, teng-sim(燈心).

**wicked**, ak(惡); pháiⁿ(痞); siâ(邪); hiong-ak(兇惡).

**wicker**, *basket*, tîn-nâⁿ(藤籃). *basket (with divisions)*, tîn-siāⁿ(藤盛).

**wide**, khuah(闊); khuah-tōa(闊大); khuah-khǹg(闊曠); kuang-khuah(光闊); khuan-khuah(寬闊); khùaⁿ(寬); khuan-khùaⁿ(寬寬). *to widen*, liú-khuah(㧕闊); tsha̍k-khuah(鑿闊); khui-khuah(開闊); chhiâⁿ-khuah(情闊); mue̍h-khuah(物闊).

**widow**, kúa-hũ(寡婦); siú-kúa(守寡). *who refuses to marry again*, chiet-hũ(節婦); siú-chiet(守節). *widower*, sit-ngóu(失偶).

**wife**, chhi(妻); bóu(婦); hũ(婦); lãi-nâng(內人); ke-lãi(家內); ke-ãu(家後); ke-kùan(家眷). *take a wife*, see MARRY. *your wife*, lẽng-chiàⁿ(令正); tsun-só(尊嫂); lãi-tsõ(內坐); tsun-hu-jîn(尊夫人); tsun-lãi(尊內); hiên-só(賢嫂). *my wife*, lãi-nâng(內人); lãi-tsuat(內拙); tsuat-keng(拙經). *[if she has a son fer husband will call her so-and-so's mother.] my good wife(addressing her)*, hiên-chhi(賢妻). *wife and children*, chhi-tsṳ́(妻子); bóu-kiáⁿ(婦囝). *to take a second wife*, tshūa-jī-nâng(娶二人). *legal wife*, chiàⁿ-chhi(正妻); tek-chhi(嫡妻); tsháu-thâu(草頭). *first wife*, huat-chhi(發妻); ngûan-phùe(原配). *wife's brother*, chhi-kũ(妻舅). *wife's sister*, chhi-î(妻姨).

**wig**, ké-môⁿ(假毛); ké-thâu-môⁿ(假頭毛).

**wild**, iá(野). *beast*, iá-siù(野獸). *growing wild*, suaⁿ seⁿ(山生); pe̍h-huat(白發); tsṳ̃-seⁿ(自生). *fowl*, tsúi-chiáu(水鳥). *goose*, hái-gô(海鵝).

**wilderness**, khùang-iá(曠野); tsháu-iá(草野).

**will**, chì(志); sim-chì(心志); chì-khì(志氣); tsú-ì(主意). *will you or will you not*, lṳ́ àiⁿ a-màiⁿ(汝愛亞勿); lṳ́ àiⁿ--mé(汝愛咩). *I will go*, úa pit-àiⁿ-khṳ̀(我必愛去). *he will not do it*, i m̄-hàuⁿ-tsò(伊毋好做); m̄-khéng(毋肯); m̄-ngũan(毋愿). *will this do*, chí-kâi hó--mé(此個好猛). *it will do*, õi--tsò-tit(會做得); khó-íⁿ(可以).

**will**, *a*, zũi-tsṳ(銳資); zũi-tsok(銳族).

**wilful**, kù-ì(故意); chip-ì(執意).

**willing**, khéng(肯); hàuⁿ(好); huaⁿ-hí(歡喜); ngũan(願); kam-sim chhêng-ngũan(甘心情願); kam-ngũan(甘願); tshut-pńg-sim(出本心).

**willow**, liú(柳); liú-chhiū(柳樹). *weeping*, si-liú(絲柳); sûi-si-liú(垂絲柳).

**wince**, sok-bûa(縮埋); kiu-bûa(勼埋).

**wind**, huang(風). *a gust of wind*, che̍k-tsûn-huang(一陣風); che̍k-tsūn-huang(一陣風). *fair wind*, sũn-huang(順風). *gentle wind*, huang li-li(風哩哩). *adverse wind*, nge̍k-huang(逆風); thêⁿ-huang(坦風); tùi-huang(對風); phah-huang(拍風). *high wind*, huang tōa(風大). *wind lighter*, huang iáu-sie̍h(風搖席). *wind gone down*, huang tiām(風恬); huang chẽⁿ(風靜). *to catch the wind*, hâⁿ-huang(寒風). *windpipe*, ngẽ-âu(硬喉).

**wind**, *to (as thread)*, în(引); tîⁿ(纏); tsāng(縡). *wind the queue round the head*, khûan-piⁿ(卷鞭); phûan-piⁿ(絆鞭); *wind the queue round the head (at the back of the head)*, tá tsang-kiáⁿ-lô(打鬃囝腡). *a clock*, khui-sî-cheng(開時鐘). *a winding road*, lōu uan(路彎); lōu uan-khek(路彎曲); i-uan khit-khek(迂彎屈曲).

**window**, theng(窗). *a sliding one*, theng-thuah(窗托). *shutters*, theng-mn̂g(窗門). *stanchions*, theng-chí〔〕.

**wine**, *(spirituous liquor)*, chiú(酒). *(grape)*, phû-thô-chiú(葡萄酒). *flagon*, chiú-pân(酒便); chiú-tsun(酒樽). *cup*, chiú-pue(酒杯); chiú-cheng(酒鍾); chiú-tsúaⁿ(酒盞); chiú-chiak(酒酌), chiú-au(酒甌). *shop*, chiú-tiàm(酒店); chiú-phòu(酒舖). *press*, chiú-tsa̍h(酒閘).

**wings**, si̍t(翼). *to flap the*, phah-si̍t(拍翼). *to dress*, tshńg-si̍t(䟙翼); tshóiⁿ-si̍t(鏟翼). *to clip the*, chién-si̍t(剪翼).

**wink**, nihⁿ-ma̍k(眲目). *to wink at a thing*, tèⁿ-tsò m̄-tsai(打做毋知).

**winnow**, pùa-bí(簸米); pùa-chhek(簸粟). *tray used to*, pùa-ki(簸箕). *fan used to*, huang-kūiⁿ(風櫃). *to, in fan*, ká-chhek(絞粟).

**winter**, tang(冬); tang--thiⁿ(冬天); chhìn--thiⁿ(凊天). *clothing*, kûaⁿ-saⁿ(寒衫); hân-i(寒衣). *cap*, kûaⁿ-bō(寒帽). *solstice*, tang-tsoih(冬節); tang-chì(冬至).

**wipe**, *to wipe (with dry cloth)*, chhit(拭). *to wipe (with wet cloth)*, zṳ̂(挐).

**wire**, thih-sùaⁿ(鐵線); tâng-sùaⁿ(銅線); ngṳ̂n-sùaⁿ(銀線).

**wise**, hiên(賢); ũ-tì-hũi(有智慧); kau-mêng(高明); ũ-kièn-sek(有見色); ũ-tì-sek(有智色); ũ-tshâi-tì(有才智); ũ-tshâi-ha̍k(有才學).

**wish**, àiⁿ(愛); ngũan(愿); ngũan-mōⁿ(愿望); siẽⁿ-mōⁿ(想望); siẽⁿ-àiⁿ(想愛); him-iẽn(鑫延); it--tie̍h(一着). *according to one's wish*, zû-ì(如意); zû-ngũan(如愿).

**wit**, ki-khá(機巧); sim-khiàu méⁿ(心竅猛); ua̍h-phuah(活潑); lêng-ki èng-pièn(靈機應變). *frightened out of one's wits*, kiâⁿ-kàu-kông(行到戇); kiaⁿ-kàu-ngo̍h(驚到愕).

**witch**, thóiⁿ-siàⁿ-phûa(睇聖婆); loo̍h-sîn-phûa(落神婆). *(spiritualist medium)*, tshai-kou-î(猜姑姨). *witch-craft*, siâ-su̍t(邪術); bû-su̍t(巫術); huap-su̍t(法術); iau-su̍t(妖術).

**with**, *to carry with one*, tòa-tõ-sin(帶在身). *talk with you*, kāng-lṳ́ tàⁿ-ūe(共汝呾話). *walk with you*, kāng-lṳ́ tsò-pû-kiâⁿ(共汝做包行); kiau-lṳ́ tsò-pû-khṳ̀(邀汝做包去); kah-lṳ́-khṳ̀(合汝去). *agrees with this*, kāng-chí-kâi siang-ha̍h(共此個相合). *with a pen*, ēng-pit(用筆); tsang-pit(將筆); chiang-pit(將筆); khiâ-pit(擎筆). *with the hand*, tsang-chhiū(將手). *with respect to*, lũn(論); lũn-ki̍p(論及); chì-i(至於); tàⁿ-kàu(呾到); lũn-kàu(論到).

**withdraw**, *to*, thò(退); thò-sî(退辭); sî-siā(辭謝); sià-sṳ̄(謝事); thò-cheh(退職).

**wither**, *to (as flowers)*, kou-ta(枯灱); ta(灱); ta-ki(灱枝); siā(謝).

**within**, tõ-lãi(在內); lãi-mīn(內面); tói-mīn(底面); lãi--tang(內中); lãi--teng(內燈); lãi-thâu(內頭). *within a month*, m̄-chiẽⁿ kâi-gu̍eh(毋上個月); put-tshut kâi-gu̍eh(不出個月); tõ-che̍k-gu̍eh-lãi(在一月內); tõ-chí-gu̍eh-tói(在此月底). *within doors*, tõ-mn̂g-lãi(在門內); tõ-ke-lãi(在家內); tõ-tshù-lãi(在厝內). *within a step of death*, hiám-hiám-sí(險險死); tsu̍ah-se-su chiũ-sí(絀些須就死).

**without**, tõ-gūa(在外); gūa-mīn(外面); gūa-thâu(外頭). *without money*, bô-chîⁿ(無錢); khueh-chîⁿ(缺錢). *without fear*, bô-só-ùi(無所畏). *better without it*, put-zû-bô kèng-hó(不如無更好); su-kùe-bô(輸過無); lêng-tsò-bô(零做無). *cannot do without it*, bô chiũ-m̄-tsò-tit(無就毋做得); chhiet-iàu tie̍h-ũ(切要着有).

**withstand**, tí-tng(抵當); tang-tsũ(擋住); tng-tsũ(擋住); tùi-te̍k(對敵); khàng-kṳ̃(抗拒); khàng-nge̍k(抗逆); sie-káu-ke̍h(相搞逆).

**witness**, *a*, kan-chèng(干證); thih-kan-chèng(鐵干證). *an eye-witness*, chèng-kìⁿ(證見); chhin-ma̍k thóiⁿ--kìⁿ(親目睇見). *to bear*, tsò-kan-chèng(做干證); tsò-chèng-kìⁿ(做證見). *false*, buáng-chèng(妄證). *to suborn false witnesses*, bói-chèng(買證).

**wizard**, tâng-ki(童乩); tâng-sin(童身); tsò-bû-su̍t(做巫術); tsò-kuat-su̍t(做訣術); tsò-huap-su̍t(做法術).

**woe**, tsai-hũa(災禍); hũa-tsai(禍災); khiông-khóu(窮苦); hũa-huãm(禍患).

**wolf**, tshâi-lâng(豺狼).

**woman**, tsṳ-niêⁿ(諸娘); nńg(女); hũ-jîn(婦人); hũ-jîn-nâng(婦人人[訓]); a-má-nâng(阿媽人[訓]). *[tsa-bóu not used in Hoo city, and vulgar.] an old woman*, lãu-tsṳ-niêⁿ(老諸娘); lãu-ḿ(老姆); lãu-sím-pô(老嬸婆). *woman's work*, nńg-kang(女工); tsṳ-niêⁿ-kang(諸娘工); hũ-kang(婦工).

**womb**, tho(胎).

**wonder**, *to*, khî-ĩ(奇異); kuài-ĩ(怪異); thóiⁿ-khî(睇奇). *wonderful*, khî-ĩ(奇異); khî-kuài(奇怪); kuài-ĩ(怪異); tshut-khî(出奇); koh-iēⁿ(各樣); ĩ-sṳ̄(異事); khî-sṳ̄(奇事); chin-khî-sṳ̄(真奇事); kuài-sṳ̄(怪事).

**wonted**, kùiⁿ-sìⁿ(慣勢); phêng-siêⁿ(平常); siêⁿ-sṳ̄(常事); siêⁿ-so̍k(常俗).

**wood**, ba̍k(木); tshâ(柴); sam(杉); chhiū-ba̍k(樹木). *building materials of*, tshâ-sāi(柴放); sam-sāi(杉放). *a wood*, chhiū-nâⁿ(樹籃); chhiū-lîm(樹林). *wood-yard*, sam-chhiáng(杉廠); sam-phòu(杉舖); sam-hâng(杉行).

**woof**, hūi(緯). *warp and*, keⁿ-hūi(經緯).

**wool**, iêⁿ-môⁿ(羊毛). *woollen cloth*, nîⁿ(呢).

**word**, ūe(話); ngân(言); gṳ́(語). *written*, jī(字). *to speak words*, tàⁿ-ūe(呾話). *I wish to asy a word to you*, uà àiⁿ kāng-lṳ́-tàⁿ che̍k-kù-ūe(我愛共汝呾一句話). *to keep one's*, chiè i-kâi-ūe khṳ̀-kiâⁿ(照伊个話去行). *to break one's*, sit-sìn(失信); sit-ieh(失約); chia̍h-ngân(食言). *words and actions*, ngân-hẽng(言行). *in a single word*, tsóng--tsṳ(總書). *to speak a good word for one*, kṳ́-chìn che̍k-kù(舉薦一句). *the Word of God*, Siãng-tì kâi-tãu(上帝个道); Siàⁿ-tsṳ(聖書); Siàⁿ-kiaⁿ(聖經).

**work**, kang(工); kang-hu(工夫); khang-khùe(工課). *to work*, tsò-kang(做工). *at work*, ēng-kang(用工). *contract for*, mãuⁿ-kang(包工). *needle-work*, tsam-kang(針工). *to work clay*, chhip-thôu〔〕. *a scull*, iẽ-lóu(搖櫓). *to work by the day*, lũn-ji̍t tsò-kang(論日做工). *workman*, sai-pẽ(司阜); kang-jîn(工人). *workmanship*, kang-hu(工夫). *fine*, cheng-kong(精工); cheng-khá(精巧); iùⁿ-kang(幼工).

**world**, sì(世); sì-kài(世界); sì-kan(世間); âng-tîn(紅塵); thiⁿ-ẽ(天下). *(this dusty weary world)*, tîn-sì(塵世). *all the*, phóu-thiⁿ-ẽ(普天下); phóu-thiⁿ-kha-ẽ(普天骹下); thong-thiⁿ-kha-ẽ(通天骹下); buān-kok(萬國). *this*, tshṳ́-sì(此世); kim-sì(今世); iâng--kan(陽間); iâng-sì(陽世). *the next*, lâi-seⁿ(來生); lâi-sì(來世); im--kan(陰間); àm--thâu(暗頭). *the next (all mean one's next appearance in this world)*, ãu-sì(後世). *ignorant of the*, m̄-hiáu sì-bũ(毋曉事務). *this changing world*, iâm-liâng sì-kài(涼涼世界). *since the world began*, khai-phek íⁿ-lâi(開闢以來); khai-tshàng íⁿ-lâi(開創以來). *worldly affairs*, sì-bũ; sì-chhêng(事情).

**worm**, *a*, thâng(蟲). *earth-worm*, kãu-ún(蚯蚓). *in the intestines*, kam-thâng(柑蟲). *in books*, tsù-thâng(蛀蟲). *worm-eaten*, tsù-tiāu(蛀掉); khòi-tiāu(喫掉).

**wormwood**, în-tîn(茵陳); în-tîn khóu-chhì(茵陳苦刺).

**worse**, kèng-m̄-hó(更毋好); zú-m̄-hó(愈毋好); zû-kèng m̄-hó(愈更毋好); kèng-sĩm(更甚); kèng-hāi(更害); zú-sí(愈死). *sickness*, pēⁿ kèng-tãng(病更重). *daily growing worse*, che̍k-ji̍t kìⁿ-ji̍t-tãng(一日見一日重).

**worship**, *to*, pài(拜拜); kũi-pài(跪拜); kèng-pài(敬拜); kèng-hõng(敬奉). *go to worship*, khṳ̀-lói-pài(去禮拜). *to worship idols*, pài-sîn(拜神); pài-lãu-iâ(拜老爺); pài-tshâ-sîn(拜柴神); sāi-lãu-iâ(倳老爺). *ancestors*, pài-a-kong(拜阿公); pài-tsóu(拜祖); pài-ke-sîn(拜家神).

**worst**, ke̍k-ak(極惡); siãng-ak(上惡); chì-ak(至惡); siãng-téng m̄-hó(上等毋好).

**worsted**, zông-sùaⁿ(絨線). *stockings*, kãu-ún-bue̍h(蚯蚓襪); hôu-khî-bue̍h(蜈蜞襪).

**worth**, *what is it*, ta̍t jie̍h-tsōi-chîⁿ(值若㩼錢); kè-ta̍t jie̍h-tsōi(價值若㩼); sĩ-mih-kè(是乜價). *not worth a single cash*, m̄-ta̍t kâi-chîⁿ(毋值个錢); put-ta̍t che̍k-bûn(不值一文). *is it worth the trouble*, m̄-tsai póu-tit-kùe kang-la̍t, mé(毋知補得過工力咩).

**worthless**, bô-ēng(無用); bô-iah(無益); m̄-tèng-ēng(毋中用). *(of people)*, hiã-téng(下等). *fellow*, siáu-jîn(小人).

**worthy**, kham-kai(堪該). *he is worthy to receive it*, kham-kai hó-tit-tie̍h(堪該好得着); pńg-téng hó-tit--tie̍h(本等好得着).

**wound**, *to*, sieⁿ(傷); phah-sieⁿ(拍傷); sieⁿ--tie̍h(傷着); sún-sieⁿ(損傷); sieⁿ-sún(傷損). *with a knife or sword*, to-sieⁿ(刀傷). *with shot*, chhèng-sieⁿ(銃傷). *wounded*, õi-sieⁿ(會傷); siũ-sieⁿ(受傷). *a wound*, chhieⁿ-kháu(槍口); sieⁿ-kháu(傷口).

**wrangle**, sie-cheⁿ(相爭); sie-à(相詏); sie-jiáng(相嚷); jiáng kàu kî-kâ-kiè(嚷到奇佳叫); jiáng kàu kũang-kũang-kiè(嚷到逛逛叫).

**wrap**, *to wrap*, pau(包); phah-pau(拍包). *wrap round*, tîⁿ(纏); tsāng(藏); hâ(縖). *wrapper for books*, thû-su〔〕; chheh-pòu(冊布).

**wrath**, see ANGER.

**wreak**, *to*, *vengeance*, soh-hṳ̃n(索恨); sia̍p-hún(涉忿).

**wreck**, phùa-tsûn(破船); pua̍h-phùa-tsûn(跋破船); tiam-phùa-tsûn(砧破船); pua̍h-tiāu-tsûn(跋掉船).

**wren**, chheⁿ-thî(青苔); thiau-liâu(挑寮).

**wrench**, tsũn(捘); tsũn-tshúa(捘掉). *off*, tsũn-tiāu(捘掉).

**wrestle**, sie-khím sie-mán(相撳相挽); tòu-la̍t(鬥力); tòu-la̍t pí-bú(鬥力比武); lám-kau-pua̍h(攬交跋); pua̍h-kau(跋交).

**wretched**, khóu-miāⁿ(苦命); chhi-tshám(淒慘); khiông-khóu(窮苦); sin-chiēⁿ kan-khóu(身上艱苦).

**wriggle**, tsũn-a-tsũn(捘阿捘); kũan-a-kũan(倦阿倦). *(as worm)*, thâu-hìⁿ búe-hìⁿ(頭搖尾搖).

**wring**, *to*, tsũn(捘). *dry*, tsũn-ta(捘灱).

**wrinkled**, jiâu(縐). *face*, mīn-phûe kâu-jiâu(面皮猴縐); mīn jiâu-jiâu(面縐縐). *wrinkles*, niàuⁿ-hûn(縐痕); chhi̍p-niàuⁿ〔〕; chhi̍p-jiâu〔〕.

**wrist**, *the*, chhiú-uán(手腕). *bones of*, chhiú-ma̍k(手目).

**write**, *to*, siá(寫); siá-jī(寫字). *in a book*, siá(寫); kì(記). *an essay*, tsò-bûn(作文); tsò-bûn-chieⁿ(作文章). *a book*, tù-tsṳ(著書). *to write out from a copy*, tshau(抄); piâⁿ(平). *writing materials*, bûn-pâng sì-pó(文房四寶); pit-ba̍k tsúa-īⁿ(筆墨紙硯).

**writhe**, *to*, kũan-a-kũan(倦阿倦); tsũn-a-tsũn(捘阿捘); thâu-hìⁿ búe-hìⁿ(頭搖尾搖).

**wrong**, m̄-tie̍h(毋着); m̄-sĩ(毋是); put-sĩ(不是); m̄-tùi(毋對); tshò(錯); tāⁿ(賺); tsha-tshò(差錯); tsáu-tsua̍h(走絀). *to wrong one*, hāi(害); uan-khut(冤屈); uan-uáng(冤枉); uáng-khut(枉屈); khui(虧). *to receive*, siũ-khui(受虧); chia̍h-khui(食虧); siũ-uan-khut(受冤屈). *to redress a wrong for any one*, kāng--nâng sin-uan(共人申冤); thòi--nâng sin-uan(代人申冤).

**wrought**, *iron*, se̍k-thih(熟鐵).

**wry**, tshúa(歪); m̄-chiàⁿ(毋正). *yam*, tōa-tsṳ̂(大薯).

### Y

**yard**, *of a ship*, tsûn-ûi-kǹg(船圍鋼). *yard(measure)*, che̍k-bé(一馬).

**yarn**, se(紗); mîⁿ-se(棉紗).

**yawn**, *to*, huah-hì(呵呬). *and stretch*, tshun-lûn(伸輪).

**year**, *a*, che̍k-nîⁿ(一年); chiu-nîⁿ(周年). *all the year*, thàng-nîⁿ(通年); tsong-nîⁿ(終年). *end of the*, nîⁿ-búe(年尾); nîⁿ-piⁿ(年邊); nîⁿ-kha(年骹); nîⁿ-tói(年底); nîⁿ-lãi(年內). *new*, sin-nîⁿ(新年). *to keep the new year*, kùe-nîⁿ(過年); tsò-sin-nîⁿ(做新年). *this*, kin-nîⁿ(今年); hīn-nîⁿ(現年); pńg-nîⁿ(本年). *last*, kū-nîⁿ(舊年); khṳ̀-nîⁿ(去年). *year before last*, tsôiⁿ--nîⁿ(前年). *next*, mêⁿ-nîⁿ(明年); lâi-nîⁿ(來年). *six years old*, la̍k-hùe(六歲). *a year or half a year*, che̍k-nîⁿ pùaⁿ-tsái(一年半載).

**yeast**, kàⁿ(酵); kàⁿ-bó(酵母); chiú-piáⁿ(酒餅).

**yell**, tōa-siaⁿ kiè(大聲叫).

**yellow**, n̂g(黃); n̂g-sek(黃色); chhiah(赤). *yellowish*, chhién-n̂g(淺黃).

**yes**, sĩ(是); ũ(有); tie̍h(着). *is he in*, ũ-tõ a-bô(有在阿無). *yes*, tõ--kò(在塊).

**yesterday**, tsa-ji̍t(昨日). *yesterday night*, tsa-mêⁿ(昨夜).

**yet**, tàu-tí(鬥抵); siãng-chhiáⁿ(尙且); huân-liáu(還了); huân-iáu(還要). *and yet(of an unlikely circumstance)*, kèng-jiên(竟然). *not yet*, būe(未); huân-būe(還未); iáu-būe(猶未); būe-chêng(未曾).

**yield**, tâu-hâng(投降); hâng-ho̍k(降服); kui-hâng(歸降). *the way*, jiãng-lōu(讓路); sie-tho-kùe(相退過). *place*, jiãng-ūi(讓位); sie-tho-tsõ(相退坐). *yielding*, khiam-jiãng(謙讓); tho-jiãng(推讓). *to one*, jiãng--khṳt-i(讓乞伊).

**yoke**, *a*, gû-taⁿ(牛擔); gû-taⁿ-uaⁿ(牛擔安).

**yolk**, *of egg*, nñg-jîn(黃仁).

**yonder**, hièⁿ-thâu(向頭); hṳ́-kò(許塊).

**you**, *(singular)*, lṳ́(汝). *(plural)*, nín(恁). *you, Sir*, tsun-kè(尊駕). *you, Sirs*, tsu-ūi(諸位). *what is your surname*, kùi-sèⁿ(貴姓).

**young**, hãu-seⁿ(後生); siàu-nîⁿ(少年); chíⁿ(稚); iùⁿ(幼); sòi(細). *I am a year younger than he*, uá sòi--i che̍k-hùe(我細伊一歲). *younger brother*, a-tĩ(阿弟). *a young man*, hãu-seⁿ-kiáⁿ(後生囝); siàu-nîⁿ-nâng(少年人[訓]). *a young cow*, gû-kiáⁿ(牛囝).

### Z

**zealous**, jie̍t-sim(熱心); pek-chhiet(迫切); huat-hún(發忿); tshut-la̍t(出力).

**zenith**, thiⁿ-téng(天頂).

**zephyr**, huang-kiáⁿ(風囝); khin-huang(輕風); huang-kiáⁿ li-li(風囝哩哩).

**zigzag**, tshũaⁿ-kùe-lâi tshũaⁿ-kùe-khṳ̀(闖過來闖過去); in-uan khit-khek(迂彎屈曲). *to walk*, tshũaⁿ-kiâⁿ(闖行).

**zinc**, pe̍h-în(白鉛).

**zodiac**, n̂g-tãu(黃道).

**zone**, tòa-tãu(帶道); sùaⁿ-lōu(線路). *temperate*, un-tãu(溫道). *frigid*, hân-tãu(寒道).

**zoology**, seⁿ-mue̍h tsóng-lũn(生物總論).
